yuṣmadasmatpratyayagocarayor viṣayaviṣayiṇos tamaḥprakāśavadviruddhasvabhāvayor itaretarabhāvāupapattau siddhāyāṃ taddharmāṇām api sutarām itaretarabhāvāupapattiḥ ity ato asmatpratyayagocare viṣayiṇi cidātmake yuṣmatpratyayagocarasya viṣayasya taddharmāṇāṃ cādhyāsaḥ tadviparyayeṇa viṣayiṇas
taddharmāṇāṃ ca viṣaye adhyāso mithyeti bhavituṃ yuktam tathāpy ayoyasmi ayoyātmakatām ayoyadharmāṃś cādhyasyetaretarāvivekeātyataviviktayor dharmadharmiṇor mithyājñāaimittaḥ satyāṛte mithuīkṛtya ahaṃ idaṃ mamedam iti
aisārgiko ayaṃ lokavyavahāraḥ āhako ayam adhyāso āmety ucyatesmṛtirūpaḥ paratra pūrvadṛṣṭāvabhāsaḥ taṃ kecitayatrāyadharmādhyāsa iti vadati kecit tu yatra yadadhyāsas tadvivekāgrahaibadhao bhrama
iti aye tu yatra yadadhyāsas tasyaiva viparītadharmatvakalpaām ācakṣata iti sarvathāpi tv ayasyāyadharmāvabhāsatāṃ a vyabhicarati tathā ca loke aubhavaḥ śuktikā hi
rajatavad avabhāsate ekaś cadraḥ sadvitīyavad iti kathaṃ puaḥ pratyagātmay aviṣaye adhyāso viṣayataddharmāṇām sarvo hi puro avasthite viṣaye viṣayātaram adhyasyati yuṣmatpratyayāpetasya
ca pratyagātmao aviṣayatvaṃ bravīṣi ucyatea tāvad ayam ekāteāviṣayaḥ asmatpratyayaviṣayatvāt aparokṣatvāc ca pratyagātmaprasiddheḥ a cāyam asti iyamaḥpuroavasthita eva viṣaye viṣayātaram adhyasitavyam
iti apratyakṣe api hy ākāśe bālāstalamaliatādy adhyasyati evam aviruddhaḥ pratyagātmay apy aātmādhyāsaḥ tam etam evaṃlakṣaṇam adhyāsaṃ paṇḍitā avidyeti mayate tadvivekea
ca vastusvarūpāvadhāraṇaṃ vidyām āhuḥ tatraivaṃ sati yatra yadadhyāsaḥ tatkṛtea doṣeṇa guṇea vā aṇumātreṇāpi sa a sambadhyate tam etam avidyākhyam ātmāātmaor
itaretarādhyasaṃ puraskṛtya sarve pramāṇaprameyavyavahārā laukikā vaidikāś ca pravṛttāḥ sarvāṇi ca śāstrāṇi vidhipratiṣedhamokṣaparāṇi kathaṃ puar avidyāvadviṣayāṇi pratyakṣādīi pramāṇāi śāstrāṇi ceti ucyatedehedriyādiṣv
ahaṃmamābhimāarahitasya pramātṛtvāupapattau pramāṇapravṛttyaupapatteḥ a hīdriyāṇy aupādāya pratyakṣādivyavahāraḥ saṃbhavati a cādhiṣṭhāam atareṇedriyāṇāṃ vyavahāraḥ saṃbhavati a cāadhyastātmabhāvea dehea kaścid vyāpriyate a caitasmi
sarvasmi asati asaṅgasyātmaaḥ pramātṛtvam upapadyate a ca pramātṛtvam atareṇa pramāṇapravṛttir asti tasmād avidyāvadviṣayāṇy eva pratyakṣādīi pramāṇāi śāstrāṇi ca paśvādibhiś cāviśeṣāt
yathā hi paśvādayaḥ śabdādibhiḥ śrotrādīāṃ saṃbadhe sati śabdādivijñāe pratikūle jāte tato ivartate aukūle ca pravartate yathā daṇḍodyatakaraṃ puruṣam abhimukham upalabhya
gāṃ hatum ayam icchatīti palāyitum ārabhate haritatṛṇapūrṇapāṇim upalabhya taṃ praty abhimukhībhavati evaṃ puruṣā api vyutpaacittāḥ krūradṛṣṭī ākrośataḥ khaḍgodyatakarā balavata upalabhya
tato ivartate tadviparītā prati pravartate ataḥ samāaḥ paśvādibhiḥ puruṣāṇāṃ pramāṇaprameyavyavahāraḥ paśvādīāṃ ca prasiddho avivekapuraḥasaraḥ pratyakṣādivyavahāraḥ tatsāmāyadarśaād vyutpattimatām api puruṣāṇāṃ pratyakṣādivyavahāras
tatkālaḥ samāa iti iścīyate śāstrīye tu vyavahāre yady api buddhipūrvakārī āviditvātmaaḥ paralokasaṃbadham adhikriyate tathāpi a vedātavedyam aśaāyādyatītam apetabrahmakṣatrādibhedam asaṃsāryātmatattvam adhikāre
apekṣyate aupayogād adhikāravirodhāc ca prāk ca tathābhūtātmavijñāāt pravartamāaṃ śāstram avidyāvadviṣayatvaṃ ātivartate tathā hibrāhmaṇo yajeta ityādīi śāstrāṇy ātmai varṇāśramavayoavasthādiviśeṣādhyāsam āśritya pravartate
adhyāso āma atasmiṃs tadbuddhir ity avocāma tadyathāputrabhāryādiṣu vikaleṣu sakaleṣu vā aham eva vikalaḥ sakalo veti bāhyadharmā ātmay adhyasyati tathā dehadharmā
sthūlo ahaṃ kṛśo ahaṃ gaur ahaṃ tiṣṭhāmi gacchāmi laṅghayāmi ceti tathedriyadharmā mūkaḥ kāṇaḥ klībaḥ badhiraḥ adho aham iti tathātaḥkaraṇadharmā kāmasaṃkalpavicikitsādhyavasāyādī
evam ahaṃ pratyayiam aśeṣesvapracārasākṣiṇi pratyagātmay adhyasya taṃ ca pratyagātmāaṃ sarvasākṣiṇaṃ tadviparyayeṇātaḥkaraṇādiṣv adhyasyati evam ayam aādir aato aisargiko adhyāso mithyāpratyayarūpaḥ kartṛtvabhoktṛtvapravartakaḥ
sarvalokapratyakṣaḥ asyāarthahetoḥ prahāṇāya ātmaikatvavidyāpratipattaye sarve vedātā ārabhyate sic yathā cāyam arthaḥ sarveṣāṃ vedātāāṃ tathā vayam asyāṃ śārīrakamīmāṃsāyāṃ pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ vedātamīmāṃsāśāstrasya vyācikhyāsitasyedam
ādimaṃ sūtram prathamodhyāyaḥ prathamaḥ pādaḥ athāto brahmajijñāsā jijñāsādhikaraṇam atrāthaśabdaḥ āataryārthaḥ parigṛhyate ādhikārārthaḥ brahmajijñāsāyā aadhikāryatvāt maṅgalasya ca vākyārthe samavayābhāvāt arthātaraprayukta eva
hy athaśabdaḥ śrutyā maṅgalaprayojao bhavati pūrvaprakṛtāpekṣāyāś ca phalata āataryāvyatirekāt sati ca āataryārthatve yathā dharmajijñāsāpūrvavṛttaṃ vedādhyayaaṃ iyameāpekṣate evaṃ brahmajijñāsāpi yat pūrvavṛttaṃ
iyameāpekṣate tad vaktavyam svādhyāyādhyayaāataryaṃ tu samāam av iha karmāvabodhāataryaṃ viśeṣaḥ a dharmajijñāsāyāḥ prāg api adhītavedātasya brahmajijñāsopapatteḥ yathā ca hṛdayādyavadāāām āataryaiyamaḥ
kramasya vivakṣitatvāt a tatheha kramo vivakṣitaḥ śeṣaśeṣitve adhikṛtādhikāre vā pramāṇābhāvāt dharmabrahmajijñāsayoḥ phalajijñāsyabhedāc ca abhyudayaphalaṃ dharmajñāam tac cāuṣṭhāāpekṣam iḥśreyasaphalaṃ tu brahmajñāam
a cāuṣṭhāātarāpekṣam bhavyaś ca dharmo jijñāsyo a jñāakāle sti puruṣavyāpāratatratvāt iha tu bhūtaṃ brahma jijñāsyaṃ ityavṛttatvā a puruṣavyāpāratatram codaāpravṛttibhedāc ca
yā hi codaā dharmasya lakṣaṇam sā svaviṣaye iyuñjāaiva puruṣam avabodhayati brahmacodaā tu puruṣam avabodhayaty eva kevalam avabodhasya codaājayatvā a puruṣo
vabodhe iyujyate yathā akṣārthasaṃikarṣeṇārthāvabodhe tadvat tasmāt kim api vaktavyam yad aataraṃ brahmajijñāsopadiśyata iti ucyate ityāityavastuvivekaḥ ihāmutrārthabhogavirāgaḥ śamadamādisādhaasaṃpat mumukṣutvaṃ ca teṣu
hi satsu prāg api dharmajijñāsāyā ūrdhvaṃ ca śakyate brahma jijñāsituṃ jñātuṃ ca a viparyaye tasmāt athaśabdea yathoktasādhaasaṃpattyāataryam upadiśyate ataḥśabdaḥ hetvarthaḥ
yasmād veda eva agihotrādīāṃ śreyaḥsādhaāām aityaphalatāṃ darśayati tadyatheha karmacito lokaḥ kṣīyata evam evāmutra puṇyacito lokaḥ kṣīyate ityādiḥ tathā brahmajñāād api
paraṃ puruṣārthaṃ darśayati brahmavid āpoti param ityādiḥ tasmāt yathoktasādhaasaṃpattyaataraṃ brahmajijñāsā kartavyā brahmaṇo jijñāsā brahmajijñāsā brahma ca vakṣyamāṇalakṣaṇam jamādyasya yataḥ iti
ata eva a brahmaśabdasya jātyādyarthātaramāśaṅkitavyam brahmaṇa iti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī a śeṣe jijñāsyāpekṣatvāj jijñāsāyāḥ jijñāsyātarāirdeśāc ca au śeṣaṣaṣṭhīparigrahepi brahmaṇo jijñāsākarmatvaṃ a
virudhyate saṃbadhasāmāyasya viśeṣaiṣṭhatvāt evam api pratyakṣaṃ brahmaṇaḥ karmatvam utsṛjya sāmāyadvāreṇa parokṣaṃ karmatvaṃ kalpayato vyarthaḥ prayāsaḥ syāt a vyarthaḥ brahmāśritāśeṣavicārapratijñāārthatvād iti
cet a pradhāaparigrahe tadapekṣitāām apy arthākṣiptatvāt brahma hi jñāeāptum iṣṭatamatvāt pradhāam tasmi pradhāe jijñāsākarmaṇi parigṛhīte yair jijñāsitair viā brahma jijñāsitaṃ
a bhavati tāy arthākṣiptāy eveti a pṛthak sūtrayitavyāi yathā rājāsau gacchati ity ukte saparivārasya rājño gamaam uktaṃ bhavati tadvat śrutyaugamāc
ca yato vā imāi bhūtāi jāyate ityādyāḥ śrutayaḥ tad vijijñāsasva tad brahma iti pratyakṣam eva brahmaṇo jijñāsākarmatvaṃ darśayati tac ca
karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhīparigrahe sūtreṇāugataṃ bhavati tasmād brahmaṇa iti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī jñātum icchā jijñāsā avagatiparyataṃ jñāaṃ sa vācyāyā icchāyāḥ karma phalaviṣayatvād icchāyāḥ
jñāea hi pramāṇeāvagatum iṣṭaṃ brahma brahmāvagatir hi puruṣārthaḥ iḥśeṣasaṃsārabījāvidyādyaarthaibarhaṇāt tasmād brahma jijñāsitavyam tat puarbrahma prasiddham aprasiddhaṃ vā syāt yadi prasiddhaṃ
a jijñāsitavyam athāprasiddhaṃ aiva śakyaṃ jijñāsitum iti ucyate asti tāvad brahma ityaśuddhabuddhamuktasvabhāvaṃ sarvajñaṃ sarvaśaktisamavitam brahmaśabdasya hi vyutpādyamāasya ityaśuddhatvādayorthāḥ pratīyate bṛṃhater
dhātor arthāugamāt sarvasyātmatvāc ca brahmāstitvaprasiddhiḥ sarvo hy ātmāstitvaṃ pratyeti a āham asmi iti yadi hi ātmāstitvaprasiddhiḥ syāt sarvo lokaḥ āham
asmi iti pratīyāt ātmā ca brahma yadi tarhi loke brahma ātmatvea prasiddham asti tato jñātam evety ajijñāsyatvaṃ puar āpaam a
tadviśeṣaṃ prati vipratipatteḥ dehamātraṃ caitayaviśiṣṭam ātmeti prākṛtā jaā laukāyatikāśca pratipaāḥ idriyāṇy eva cetaāy ātmety apare maa ity aye vijñāamātraṃ kṣaṇikam
ity eke śūyam ity apare asti dehādivyatiriktaḥ saṃsārī kartā bhoktety apare bhoktaiva kevalaṃ a kartety eke asti tadvyatirikta īśvaraḥ sarvajñaḥ
sarvaśaktir iti kecit ātmā sa bhoktur ity apare evaṃ bahavo vipratipaā yuktivākyatadābhāsasamāśrayāḥ sataḥ tatrāvicārya yatkiṃcit pratipadyamāo iḥśreyasāt pratihayeta aarthaṃ ceyāt
tasmād brahmajijñāsopayāsamukhea vedātavākyamīmāṃsā tadavirodhitarkopakaraṇā iḥśreyasaprayojaā prastūyate brahma jijñāsitavyam ity uktam kiṃlakṣaṇaṃ puas tad brahmety ata āha bhagavāsūtrakāraḥ jamādy asya yataḥ
jamādyadhikaraṇam jama utpattiḥ ādiḥ asya iti tadguṇasaṃvijñāo bahuvrīhiḥ jamasthitibhaṅgaṃ samāsārthaḥ jamaaś cāditvaṃ śrutiirdeśāpekṣaṃ vastuvṛttāpekṣaṃ ca śrutiirdeśas tāvat yato vā imāi
bhūtāi jāyate iti asmi vākye jamasthitipralayāāṃ kramadarśaāt vastuvṛttam api jamaā labdhasattākasya dharmiṇaḥ sthitipralayasaṃbhavāt asyeti pratyakṣādisaṃidhāpitasya dharmiṇa idam ā irdeśaḥ ṣaṣṭhī
jamādidharmasaṃbadhārthā yata iti kāraṇairdeśaḥ asya jagato āmarūpābhyāṃ vyākṛtasya aekakartṛbhoktṛsaṃyuktasya pratiiyatadeśakālaimittakriyāphalāśrayasya maasāpy acityaracaārūpasya jamasthitibhaṅgaṃ yataḥ sarvajñāt sarvaśakteḥ kāraṇād bhavati tad brahmeti
vākyaśeṣaḥ ayeṣām api bhāvavikārāṇāṃ triṣv evātarbhāva iti jamasthitiāśāām iha grahaṇam yāskaparipaṭhitāāṃ tu jāyate sti ityādīāṃ grahaṇe teṣāṃ jagataḥ sthitikāle saṃbhāvyamāatvā
mūlakāraṇād utpattisthitiāś ā jagato a gṛhītāḥ syur ity āśaṅkyeta ta mā śaṅki iti yā utpattir brahmaṇaḥ kāraṇāt tatraiva sthitiḥ pralayaś
ca te gṛhyate a ca yathoktaviśeṣaṇasya jagato yathoktaviśeṣaṇam īśvaraṃ muktvā ayataḥ pradhāād acetaāt aṇubhyo vā abhāvād vā saṃsāriṇo vā utpattyādi
saṃbhāvayituṃ śakyam a ca svabhāvataḥ viśiṣṭadeśakālaimittāām ihopādāāt etad evāumāaṃ saṃsārivyatirikteśvarāstitvādisādhaaṃ mayate īśvarakāraṇavādiaḥ av ihāpi tad evopayastaṃ jamādisūtre a vedātavākyakusumagrathaārthatvāt sūtrāṇām
vedātavākyāi hi sūtrair udāhṛtya vicāryate vākyārthavicāraṇādhyavasāairvṛttā hi brahmāvagatiḥ āumāādipramāṇātarairvṛttā satsu tu vedātavākyeṣu jagato jamādikāraṇavādiṣu tadarthagrahaṇad ārḍhyāya aumāam api vedātavākyāvirodhi pramāṇaṃ
bhavat a ivāryate śrutyaiva ca sahāyatvea tarkasyāpy abhyupetatvāt tathā hi śrotavyo matavyaḥ iti śrutiḥ paṇḍito medhāvī gadhārāevopasaṃpadyetaivam evehācāryavā puruṣo veda
iti ca puruṣabuddhisāhāyyam ātmao darśayati a dharmajijñasāyām iva śrutyādaya eva pramāṇaṃ brahmajijñāsāyām kiṃtu śrutyādayo ubhavādayaś ca yathāsaṃbhavam iha pramāṇam aubhavāvasāatvād
bhūtavastuviṣayatvāc ca brahmajñāasya kartavye hi viṣaye āubhavāpekṣāstīti śrutyādīām eva prāmāṇyaṃ syāt puruṣādhīātmalābhatvāc ca kartavyasya kartum akartum ayathā vā kartuṃ śakyaṃ
laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ ca karma yathā aśvea gacchati padbhyām ayathā vā a vā gacchatīti tathā atirātre ṣoḍaśiaṃ gṛhṇāti ātirātre ṣoḍaśiaṃ gṛhṇāti
udite juhoti audite juhoti iti vidhipratiṣedhāś ca atra arthavataḥ syuḥ vikalpotsargāpavādāś ca a tu vastu evam aivam asti āsti iti
vā vikalpyate vikalpaās tu puruṣabuddhyapekṣāḥ a vastuyāthātmyajñāaṃ puruṣabuddhyapekṣam kiṃ tarhi vastutatram eva tat a hi sthāṇāv ekasmi sthāṇur vā puruṣo
yo vā iti tattvajñāaṃ bhavati tatra puruṣo yo vā iti mithyājñāam sthāṇur eva iti tattvajñāam vastutatratvāt evaṃ bhūtavastuviṣayāṇāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ vastutatram
tatraivaṃ sati brahmajñāam api vastutatram eva bhūtavastuviṣayatvāt au bhūtavastuviṣayatve brahmaṇaḥ pramāṇātaraviṣayatvam eveti vedātavākyavicāraṇā aarthikaiva prāptā a idriyāviṣayatvea saṃbadhāgrahaṇāt svabhāvato viṣayaviṣayāṇīdriyāṇi
a brahmaviṣayāṇi sati hīdriyaviṣayatve brahmaṇaḥ idaṃ brahmaṇā saṃbaddhaṃ kāryam iti gṛhyeta kāryamātram eva tu gṛhyamāṇam kiṃ brahmaṇā saṃbaddham kim ayea
keacid vā saṃbaddham iti a śakyaṃ iścetum tasmāj jamādisūtraṃ āumāopayāsārtham kiṃ tarhi vedātavākyapradarśaārtham kiṃ puas tad vedātavākyaṃ yat sūtreṇeha lilakṣayiṣitam
bhṛgur vai vāruṇiḥ varuṇaṃ pitaramupasasāra adhīhi bhagavo brahmeti ity upakramyāha yato vā imāi bhūtāi jāyate yea jātāi jīvati yat prayatyabhisaṃviśati
tadvijijñāsasva tad brahmeti tasya ca irṇayavākyam āadād dhyeva khalv imāi bhūtāi jāyate āadea jātāi jīvati āadaṃ prayaty abhisaṃviśati iti ayāy
apy evaṃjātīyakāi vākyāi ityaśuddhabuddham uktasvabhāvasarvajñasvarūpakāraṇaviṣayāṇi udāhartavyāi jagatkāraṇatvapradarśaea sarvajñaṃ brahmety upakṣiptam tad eva draḍhaya āha śāstrayoitvāt śāstrayoitvādhikaraṇam mahata ṛgvedādeḥ śāstrasya aekavidyāsthāopabṛṃhitasya
pradīpavatsarvārthāvadyotiaḥ sarvajñakalpasya yoiḥ kāraṇaṃ brahma a hīdṛśasya śāstrasya ṛgvedādilakṣaṇasya sarvajñaguṇāvitasya sarvajñādayataḥ saṃbhavosti yadyadvistarārthaṃ śāstraṃ yasmātpuruṣaviśeṣātsaṃbhavati yathā vyākaraṇādi pāṇiyādeḥ jñeyaikadeśārthamapi sa
tatopyadhikataravijñāa iti prasiddhaṃ loke kimu vaktavyam aekaśākhābhedabhiasya devatiryaṅmauṣyavarṇāśramādipravibhāgahetoḥ ṛgvedādyākhyasya sarvajñāākarasya aprayateaiva līlāyāyea puruṣaiḥśvāsavat yasmā mahato bhūtāt yoeḥ saṃbhavaḥ asya mahato
bhūtasya iḥśvasitam etat yad ṛgvedaḥ ityādiśruteḥ tasya mahato bhūtasya iratiśayaṃ sarvajñatvaṃ sarvaśaktimattvaṃ ceti athavā yathoktam ṛgvedādi śāstraṃ yoiḥ kāraṇaṃ pramāṇam
asya brahmaṇo yathāvatsvarūpādhigame śāstrād eva pramāṇāt jagato jamādikāraṇaṃ brahmādhigamyata ity abhiprāyaḥ śāstram udāhṛtaṃ pūrvasūtre yato vā imāi bhūtāi jāyate ityādi
kimarthaṃ tarhīdaṃ sūtram yāvatā pūrvasūtreṇaiva evaṃjātīyakaṃ śāstram udāharatā śāstrayoitvaṃ brahmaṇo darśitam ucyate tatra sūtrākṣareṇa spaṣṭaṃ śāstrasyāupādāāj jamādisūtreṇa kevalam aumāam upayastam
ityāśaṅkyeta tām āśaṅkāṃ ivartayitum idaṃ sūtraṃ pravavṛte śāstrayoitvāt iti kathaṃ puar brahmaṇaḥ śāstrapramāṇakatvam ucyate yāvatā āmāyasya kriyārthatvād āarthakyam atadarthāām iti
kriyāparatvaṃ śāstrasya pradarśitam ato vedātāām āarthakyam akriyārthatvāt kartṛdevatādiprakāśaārthatvea vā kriyāvidhiśeṣatvam upāsaādikriyātaravidhāārthatvaṃ vā a hi pariiṣṭhitavastusvarūpapratipādaaṃ saṃbhavati pratyakṣādiviṣayatvāt pariiṣṭhitavastuaḥ tatpratipādae ca

vyācikīrṣite iti brūmaḥ yatprasādād dhi yogiām apy atītāāgataviṣayaṃ pratyakṣaṃ jñāam icchati yogaśāstravidaḥ kim u vaktavyaṃ tasya ityasiddhasyeśvarasya sṛṣṭisthitisaṃhṛtiviṣayaṃ ityajñāaṃ bhavatīti
yad apy uktaṃ prāg utpatter brahmaṇaḥ śarīrādisaṃbadham atareṇekṣitṛtvam aupapaam iti a tac codyam avatarati savitṛprakāśavad brahmaṇo jñāasvarūpaityatve jñāasādhaāpekṣāupapatteḥ api cāvidyādimataḥ
saṃsāriṇaḥ śarīrādyapekṣā jñāotpattiḥ syāt a jñāapratibadhakāraṇarahitasyeśvarasya matrau cemāv īśvarasya śarīrādyaapekṣatām aāvaraṇajñāatāṃ ca darśayataḥ a tasya kāryaṃ karaṇaṃ ca vidyate a
tatsamaś cābhyadhikaś ca dṛśyate parāsya śaktir vividhaiva śrūyate svābhāvikī jñāabalakriyā ca iti apāṇipādo javao grahītā paśyaty acakṣuḥ sa śrṛṇoty akarṇaḥ
sa vetti vedyaṃ a ca tasyāsti vettā tam āhur agryaṃ puruṣaṃ mahātam iti ca au āsti tava jñāapratibadhakāraṇarahiteśvarād ayaḥ saṃsārī
āyo to sti draṣṭā āyo to sti vijñātā ityādiśruteḥ tatra kim idam ucyate saṃsāriṇaḥ śarīrādyapekṣā jñāotpattiḥ eśvarasyeti atrocyate satyaṃ eśvarād
ayaḥ saṃsārī tathāpi dehādisaṃghātopādhisaṃbadha iṣyata eva ghaṭakarakagiriguhādyupādhisaṃbadha iva vyomaḥ tatkṛtaś ca śabdapratyayavyavahāro lokasya dṛṣṭaḥ ghaṭacchidram karakacchidram ityādiḥ ākāśāvyatireke pi tatkṛtā
cākāśe ghaṭākāśādibhedamithyābuddhir dṛṣṭā tathehāpi dehādisaṃghātopādhisaṃbadhāvivekakṛteśvarasaṃsāribhedamithyābuddhiḥ dṛśyate cātmaa eva sato dehādisaṃghāte ātmay ātmatvābhiiveśo mithyābuddhimātreṇa pūrvapūrveṇa sati caivaṃ saṃsāritve dehādyapekṣam īkṣitṛtvam upapaaṃ
saṃsāriṇaḥ yad apy uktaṃ pradhāasyāekātmakatvā mṛdādivat kāraṇatvopapattir āsaṃhatasya brahmaṇa iti tat pradhāasyāśabdatveaiva pratyuktam yathā tu tarkeṇāpi brahmaṇa eva kāraṇatvaṃ irvoḍhuṃ
śakyate a pradhāādīām tathā prapañcayiṣyati a vilakṣaṇatvād asya ityevamādiā atrāha yad uktaṃ ācetaaṃ pradhāaṃ jagatkāraṇam īkṣitṛtvaśravaṇād iti tad ayathāpy upapadyate
acetae pi cetaavad upacāradarśaāt yathā pratyāsaapataatāṃ adyāḥ kūlasyālakṣya kūlaṃ pipatiṣati ity acetaepi kūle cetaavad upacāro dṛṣṭaḥ tadvad acetae pi pradhāe
pratyāsaasarge cetaavadupacāro bhaviṣyati tadaikṣata iti yathā loke kaścic cetaaḥ sātvā bhuktvā cāparāhṇe grāmaṃ rathea gamiṣyāmi itīkṣitvā aataraṃ tathaiva iyamea pravartate
tathā pradhāam api mahadādyākāreṇa iyamea pravartate tasmāc cetaavad upacaryate kasmāt puaḥ kāraṇāt vihāya mukhyam īkṣitṛtvam aupacārikaṃ kalpyate tat teja aikṣata
tā āpa aikṣata iti cācetaayor apy aptejasoś cetaavadupacāradarśaāt tasmāt satkartṛkam apīkṣaṇam aupacārikam iti gamyate upacāraprāye vacaāt ity evaṃ prāpte idaṃ
sūtram ārabhyate gauṇaś ce ātmaśabdāt yad uktaṃ pradhāam acetaaṃ sacchabdavācyaṃ tasmi aupacārikam īkṣitṛtvam aptejasor iveti tad asat kasmāt ātmaśabdāt sad
eva somyedam agra āsīt ity upakramya tad aikṣata tat tejo asṛjata iti ca tejobaāāṃ sṛṣṭim uktvā tad eva prakṛtaṃ sad
īkṣitṛ tāi ca tejobaāi devatāśabdea parāmṛśyāha seyaṃ devataikṣata hatāham imās tisro devatā aea jīveātmaāupraviśya āmarūpe vyākaravāṇi iti tatra yadi pradhāam
acetaaṃ guṇavṛttyekṣitṛ kalpyeta tad eva prakṛtatvāt seyaṃ devatā iti parāmṛśyeta a tadā devatā jīvam ātmaśabdeābhidadhyāt jīvo hi āma cetaaḥ śarīrādhyakṣaḥ
prāṇāāṃ dhārayitā tatprasiddher irvacaāc ca sa katham acetaasya pradhāasyātmā bhavet ātmā hi āma svarūpam ācetaasya pradhāasya cetao jīvaḥ svarūpaṃ bhavitum
arhati atha tu cetaaṃ brahma mukhyam īkṣitṛ parigṛhyeta tasya jīvaviṣaya ātmaśabdaprayoga upapadyate tathā sa ya eṣoṇimaitad ātmyam idaṃ sarvaṃ tatsatyaṃ
sa ātmā tat tvam asi śvetaketo ity atra sa ātmā iti prakṛtaṃ sadaṇimāamātmāam ātmaśabdeopadiśya tat tvam asi śvetaketo iti cetaasya
śvetaketor ātmatveopadiśati aptejasos tu viṣayatvād acetaatvam āmarūpavyākaraṇādau ca prayojyatveaiva irdeśāt a cātmaśabdavat kiṃci mukhyatve kāraṇam astīti yuktaṃ kūlavad gauṇatvam īkṣitṛtvasya
tayor api sadadhiṣṭhitatvāpekṣam evekṣitṛtvam satas tv ātmaśabdā a gauṇam īkṣitṛtvam ity uktam athocyeta acetaepi pradhāe bhavatyātmaśabdaḥ ātmaaḥ sarvārthakāritvāt yathā rājñaḥ
sarvārthakāriṇi bhṛtye bhavaty ātmaśabdaḥ mamātmā bhadraseaḥ iti pradhāaṃ hi puruṣasyātmao bhogāpavargau kurvadupakaroti rājña iva bhṛtyaḥ saṃdhivigrahādiṣu vartamāaḥ athavaika evātmaśabdaś cetaācetaaviṣayo
bhaviṣyati bhūtātmā idriyātmā iti ca prayogadarśaāt yathaika eva jyotiḥśabdaḥ kratujvalaaviṣayaḥ tatra kuta etad ātmaśabdād īkṣater agauṇatvam ity ata uttaraṃ paṭhati
taiṣṭhasya mokṣopadeśāt a pradhāamacetaamātmaśabdālambaaṃ bhavitumarhati sa ātmā iti prakṛtaṃ sadaṇimāamādāya tattvamasi śvetaketo iti cetaasya śvetaketormokṣayitavyasya taiṣṭhāmupadiśya ācāryavāpuruṣo veda tasya tāvadeva
ciraṃ yāvaa vimokṣyetha saṃpatsye iti mokṣopadeśāt yadi hyacetaaṃ pradhāaṃ sacchabdavācyam tat asi iti grāhayet mumukṣuṃ cetaaṃ satamacetaosīti tadā viparītavādi śāstraṃ
puruṣasyāarthāyetyapramāṇaṃ syāt a tu irdoṣamidaṃ śāstramapramāṇaṃ kalpayituṃ yuktam yadi cājñasya sato mumukṣoracetaamaātmāamātmetyupadiśetpramāṇabhūtaṃ śāstram sa śraddadhāatayā adhagolāṅgūlayāyea tadātmadṛṣṭiṃ a parityajet tadvyatiriktaṃ
cātmāaṃ a pratipadyeta tathā sati puruṣārthādvihayeta aarthaṃ vā ṛcchet tasmādyathā svargādyarthiogihotrādisādhaaṃ yathābhūtamupadiśati tathā mumukṣorapi sa ātmā tattvamasi śvetaketo iti yathābhūtamevātmāamupadiśatīti
yuktam evaṃ ca sati taptaparaśugrahaṇamokṣadṛṣṭātea satyābhisaṃdhasya mokṣopadeśa upapadyate ayathā hyamukhye sadātmatattvopadeśe ahamukthamasmīti vidyāt itivatsaṃpamātramidamaityaphalaṃ syāt tatra mokṣopadeśo opapadyeta tasmāa sadaṇimayātmaśabdasya
gauṇatvam bhṛtye tu svāmibhṛtyabhedasya pratyakṣatvādupapao gauṇa ātmaśabdaḥ mamātmā bhadraseaḥ iti api ca kvacidgauṇaḥ śabdo dṛṣṭa iti aitāvatā śabdapramāṇakerthe gauṇīkalpaā yāyyā
sarvatrāāśvāsaprasaṅgāt yattūktaṃ cetaācetaayoḥ sādhāraṇa ātmaśabdaḥ kratujvalaayoriva jyotiḥśabda iti taa aekārthatvasyāyāyyatvāt tasmāccetaaviṣaya eva mukhya ātmaśabdaścetaatvopacārādbhūtādiṣu prayujyate bhūtātmā idriyātmā iti ca sādhāraṇatvepyātmaśabdasya
a prakaraṇamupapadaṃ vā kiṃciiścāyakamatareṇāyataravṛttitā irdhārayituṃ śakyate a cātrācetaasya iścāyakaṃ kiṃcitkāraṇamasti prakṛtaṃ tu sadīkṣitṛ saṃihitaśca cetaaḥ śvetaketuḥ a hi cetaasya śvetaketoracetaa
ātmā saṃbhavatītyavocāma tasmāccetaaviṣaya ihātmaśabda iti iścīyate jyotiḥśabdopi laukikea prayogeṇa jvalaa eva rūḍhaḥ arthavādakalpitea tu jvalaasādṛśyea kratau pravṛtta ityadṛṣṭātaḥ athavā pūrvasūtra
evātmaśabdaṃ irastasamastagauṇatvasādhāraṇatvāśaṅkatayā vyākhyāya tataḥ svatatra eva pradhāakāraṇairākaraṇaheturvyākhyeyaḥ taiṣṭhasya mokṣopadeśāt iti tasmāācetaaṃ pradhāaṃ sacchabdavācyam kutaśca a pradhāaṃ sacchabdavācyam heyatvāvacaācca yadyaātmaiva pradhāaṃ
sacchabdavācyam sa ātmā tattvamasi itīhopadiṣṭaṃ syāt sa tadupadeśaśravaṇādaātmajñatayā taiṣṭho mā bhūditi mukhyamātmāamupadidikṣu śāstraṃ tasya heyatvaṃ brūyāt yathārudhatīṃ didarśayiṣustatsamīpasthāṃ sthūlāṃ tārāmamukhyāṃ
prathamamarudhatīti grāhayitvā tāṃ pratyākhyāya paścādarudhatīmeva grāhayati tadvaāyamātmeti brūyāt a caivamavocat samātrātmāvagatiiṣṭhaiva hi ṣaṣṭhaprapāṭhake parisamāptirdṛśyate caśabdaḥ pratijñāvirodhābhyuccayapradarśaārthaḥ satyapi heyatvavacae pratijñāvirodhaḥ prasajyeta
kāraṇavijñāāddhi sarvaṃ vijñātamiti pratijñātam uta tamādeśamaprākṣyo yeāśrutaṃ śrutaṃ bhavatyamataṃ matamavijñātaṃ vijñātamiti kathaṃ u bhagavaḥ sa ādeśo bhavatīti yathā somyaikea mṛtpiṇḍea
sarvaṃ mṛmayaṃ vijñātaṃ syādvācārambhaṇaṃ vikāro āmadheyaṃ mṛttiketyeva satyam evaṃ somya sa ādeśo bhavati iti vākyopakrame śravaṇāt a ca sacchabdavācye pradhāe
bhogyavargakāraṇe heyatveāheyatvea vā vijñāte bhoktṛvargo vijñāto bhavati apradhāavikāratvādbhoktṛvargasya tasmāa pradhāaṃ sacchabdavācyam kutaśca a pradhāaṃ sacchabdavācyam svāpyayāt tadeva sacchabdavācyaṃ kāraṇaṃ prakṛtya
śrūyate yatraitatpuruṣaḥ svapiti āma satā somya tadā saṃpao bhavati svamapīto bhavati tasmādeaṃ svapitītyācakṣate svaṃ hyapīto bhavati iti eṣā śrutiḥ svapitītyetatpuruṣasya
lokaprasiddhaṃ āma irvakti svaśabdeehātmocyate yaḥ prakṛtaḥ sacchabdavācyastamapīto bhavatyapigato bhavatītyarthaḥ apipūrvasyaiterlayārthatvaṃ prasiddham prabhavāpyayāvityutpattipralayayoḥ prayogadarśaāt maaḥpracāropādhiviśeṣasaṃbadhādidriyārthāgṛhṇaṃstadviśeṣāpao jīvo jāgarti tadvāsaāviśiṣṭaḥ svapāpaśyamaaḥśabdavācyo bhavati sa
upādhidvayoparame suṣuptāvasthāyāmupādhikṛtaviśeṣābhāvātsvātmai pralīa iveti svaṃ hyapīto bhavati ityucyate yathā hṛdayaśabdairvacaaṃ śrutyā darśitam sa vā eṣa ātmā hṛdi tasyaitadeva iruktam hṛdyayamiti
tasmāddhṛdayamiti yathā vāśaāyodayāśabdapravṛttimūlaṃ darśayati śrutiḥ āpa eva tadaśitaṃ ayate teja eva tatpītaṃ ayate iti ca evaṃ svamātmāaṃ sacchabdavācyamapīto bhavati itīmamarthaṃ
svapitiāmairvacaea darśayati a ca cetaa ātmā acetaaṃ pradhāaṃ svarūpatvea pratipadyeta yadi puaḥ pradhāamevātmīyatvātsvaśabdeaivocyeta evamapi cetaocetaamapyetīti viruddhamāpadyeta śrutyataraṃ ca prājñeātmaā saṃpariṣvakto
a bāhyaṃ kiṃcaa veda ātaram iti suṣuptāvasthāyāṃ cetae apyayaṃ darśayati ato yasmiapyayaḥ sarveṣāṃ cetaāāṃ taccetaaṃ sacchabdavācyaṃ jagataḥ kāraṇaṃ syāt ācetaaṃ
pradhāam kutaśca a pradhāaṃ jagataḥ kāraṇam gatisāmāyāt yadi tārkikasamaya iva vedāteṣvapi bhiā kāraṇāvagagatirabhaviṣyat kvaciccetaaṃ brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam kvacidacetaaṃ pradhāam kvacidayadeveti
tataḥ kadācitpradhāakāraṇavādāurodheāpīkṣatyādiśravaṇamakalpayiṣyat a tvetadasti samāaiva hi sarveṣu vedāteṣu cetaakāraṇāvagatiḥ yathāgerjvalataḥ sarvā diśo visphuliṅgā vipratiṣṭheraevamevaitasmādātmaaḥ sarve prāṇā yathāyataaṃ vipratiṣṭhate prāṇebhyo devā
devebhyo lokāḥ iti tasmād vā etasmād ātmaa ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti ātmaa evedaṃ sarvam iti ātmaa eṣa prāṇo jāyate iti ca
ātmaaḥ kāraṇatvaṃ darśayati sarve vedātāḥ ātmaśabdaśca cetaavacaa ityavocāma mahacca prāmāṇyakāraṇametat yadvedātavākyāāṃ cetaakāraṇatve samāagatitvam cakṣurādīāmiva rūpādiṣu ato gatisamāyātsarvajñaṃ brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam
kutaśca sarvajñaṃ brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam śrutatvācca svaśabdeaiva ca sarvajña īśvaro jagataḥ kāraṇamiti śrūyate śvetāśvatarāṇāṃ matropaiṣadi sarvajñam īśvaraṃ prakṛtya sa kāraṇaṃ
karaṇādhipādhipo a cāsya kaścij jaitā a cādhipaḥ iti tasmāt sarvajñaṃ brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam ācetaaṃ pradhāam ayad veti siddham jamādyasya yataḥ
ity ārabhya śrutatvāc ca ity etadataiḥ sūtrair yāy udāhṛtāi vedātavākyāi teṣāṃ sarvajñaḥ sarvaśaktir īśvaro jagato jamasthitipralayakāraṇam ity etasyārthasya pratipādakatvaṃ yāyapūrvakaṃ
pratipāditam gatisāmāyopayāsea ca sarve vedātāś cetaakāraṇavādia iti vyākhyātam ataḥ parasya grathasya kim utthāam iti ucyate dvirūpaṃ hi brahmāvagamyate āmarūpavikārabhedopādhiviśiṣṭam tadviparītaṃ
ca sarvopādhivivarjitam yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tad itara itaraṃ paśyati yatra tv asya sarvam ātmaivābhūt tat kea kaṃ paśyet
yatra āyat paśyati āyac chṛṇoti āyad vijāāti sa bhūmā atha yatrāyat paśyaty ayac chṛṇoty ayad vijāāti tad alpam yo vai
bhūmā tad amṛtam atha yad alpaṃ ta martyam sarvāṇi rūpāṇi vicitya dhīro āmāi kṛtvābhivada yad āste iṣkalaṃ iṣkriyaṃ śātaṃ iravadyaṃ
irañjaam amṛtasya paraṃ setuṃ dagdhedhaam ivāalam eti eti asthūlam aaṇv ahrasvam adīrgham iti yūam ayat sthāaṃ saṃpūrṇam ayat iti caivaṃ
sahasraśo vidyāvidyāviṣayabhedea brahmaṇo dvirūpatāṃ darśayati vedātavākyāi tatrāvidyāvasthāyāṃ brahmaṇa upāsyopāsakādilakṣaṇaḥ sarvo vyavahāraḥ tatra kāicid brahmaṇa upāsaāy abhyudayārthāi kāicit kramamuktyarthāi kāicit karmasamṛddhyarthāi
teṣāṃ guṇaviśeṣopādhibhedea bhedaḥ eka eva tu para ātmeśvaras tais tair guṇaviśeṣair viśiṣṭa upāsyo yady api bhavati tathāpi yathāguṇopāsaam eva phalāi
bhidyate taṃ yathā yathopāsate tad eva bhavati iti śruteḥ yathākraturasimalloke puruṣo bhavati tathetaḥ pretya bhavati iti ca smṛteś ca yaṃ
yaṃ vāpi smarabhāvaṃ tyajaty ate kalebaram taṃ tam evaiti kauteya sadā tadbhāvabhāvitaḥ iti yady apy eka ātmā sarvabhūteṣu sthāvarajaṅgameṣu gūḍhaḥ
tathāpi cittopādhiviśeṣatāratamyād ātmaaḥ kūṭasthaityasyaikarūpasyāpy uttarottaram āviṣkṛtasya tāratamyam aiśvaryaśaktiviśeṣaiḥ śrūyate tasya ya ātmāam āvistarāṃ veda ity atra smṛtāv api yad yad
vibhūtimat sattvaṃ śrīmad ūrjitam eva vā tat tad evāvagaccha tvaṃ mama tejoṃśasaṃbhavam iti yatra yatra vibhūtyādyatiśayaḥ sa sa īśvara ity
upāsyatayā codyate evam ihāpy ādityamaṇḍale hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣaḥ sarvapāpmodayaliṅgāt para eveti vakṣyati evam ākāśas tal liṅgāt ityādiṣu draṣṭavyam evaṃ sadyomuktikāraṇam apy
ātmajñāam upādhiviśeṣadvāreṇopadiśyamāam apy avivakṣitopādhisaṃbadhaviśeṣaṃ parāparaviṣayatvea saṃdihyamāaṃ vākyagatiparyālocaayā irṇetavyaṃ bhavati yathehaiva tāvat āadamayobhyāsāt iti evam ekam api brahmāpekṣitopādhisaṃbadhaṃ irastopādhisaṃbadhaṃ copāsyatvea jñeyatvea
ca vedāteṣūpadiśyata iti pradarśayituṃ paro gratha ārabhyate yac ca gatisāmāyāt ity acetaakāraṇairākaraṇam uktam tad api vākyātarāṇi brahmaviṣayāṇi vyācakṣāṇea brahmaviparītakāraṇaiṣedhea prapañcyate
āadamayobhyāsāt āadamayādhikaraṇam taittirīyake aamayaṃ prāṇamayaṃ maomayaṃ vijñāamayaṃ cāukramyāmāyate tasmād vā etasmād vijñāamayād ayo tara ātmāadamayaḥ iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim ihāadamayaśabdea
param eva brahmocyate yat prakṛtam satyaṃ jñāam aataṃ brahma iti kiṃ vāamayādivad brahmaṇorthātaram iti kiṃ tāvat prāptam brahmaṇo rthātaram amukhya
ātmāadamayaḥ syāt kasmāt aamayādyamukhyātmapravāhapatitatvāt athāpi syāt sarvātaratvād āadamayo mukhya evātmeti a syāt priyādyavayavayogāc chārīratvaśravaṇāc ca mukhyaś ced ātmā syā a
priyādisaṃsparśaḥ syāt iha tu tasya priyam eva śiraḥ ityādi śrūyate śārīratvaṃ ca śrūyate tasyaiṣa eva śārīra ātmā yaḥ pūrvasya iti
tasya pūrvasya vijñāamayasyaiṣa eva śārīra ātmā ya eṣa āadamaya ity arthaḥ a ca saśarīrasya sataḥ priyāpriyasaṃsparśo vārayituṃ śakyaḥ tasmāt saṃsāry
evāadamaya ātmety evaṃ prāpte idam ucyate āadamayo bhyāsāt para evātmāadamayo bhavitum arhati kutaḥ abhyāsāt parasmi eva hy ātmay āadaśabdo bahukṛtvo
bhyasyate āadamayaṃ prastutya raso vai saḥ iti tasyaiva rasatvam uktvā ucyate ras hy evāyaṃ labdhvāadī bhavati ko hy evāyāt kaḥ
prāṇyāt yad eṣa ākāśa āado a syāt eṣa hy evāadayāti saiṣāadasya mīmāsā bhavati etam āadamayam ātmāam upasaṃkrāmati āadaṃ brahmaṇo vidvā
a bibheti kutaścaa iti āado brahmeti vyajāāt iti ca śrutyatare ca vijñāam āadaṃ brahma iti brahmaṇy evāadaśabdo dṛṣṭaḥ evam āadaśabdasya
bahukṛtvo brahmaṇy abhyāsād āadamaya ātmā brahmeti gamyate yat tūktam aamayādyamukhyātmapravāhapatitatvād āadamayasyāpy amukhyatvam iti āsau doṣaḥ āadamayasya sarvātaratvāt mukhyam eva hy
ātmāam upadidikṣu śāstraṃ lokabuddhim ausarat aamayaṃ śarīram aātmāam atyatamūḍhāām ātmatvea prasiddham aūdya mūṣāiṣiktadrutatāmrādipratimāvattato taraṃ tato taram ity evaṃ pūrveṇa pūrveṇa
samāam uttaram uttaram aātmāam ātmeti grāhayat pratipattisaukaryāpekṣayā sarvātaraṃ mukhyam āadamayam ātmāam upadideśeti śliṣṭataram yathārudhatīdarśae bahvīṣv api tārāsvamukhyāsvarudhatīṣu darśitāsu yā atyā
pradarśyate sā mukhyaivārudhatī bhavati evamihāpyāadamayasya sarvātaratvāmukhyamātmatvam yat tu brūṣe priyādīāṃ śirastvādikalpaāupapaā mukhyasyātmaa iti atītāataropādhijaitā sā a svābhāvikīty adoṣaḥ śārīratvam apy
āadamayasyāamayādiśarīraparamparayā pradarśyamāatvāt a puaḥ sākṣād eva śārīratvaṃ saṃsārivat tasmād āadamayaḥ para evātmā vikāraśabdā eti ce a prācuryāt atrāha āadamayaḥ para
ātmā bhavitum arhati kasmāt vikāraśabdāt prakṛtivacaād ayam ayaḥ śabdo vikāravacaaḥ samadhigataḥ āadamayaḥ iti mayaṭo vikārārthatvāt tasmād aamayādiśabdavad vikāraviṣaya evāyam āadamayaśabda
iti cet a prācuryārthepi mayaṭaḥ smaraṇāt tatprakṛtavacae mayaṭ AA iti hi pracuratāyām api mayaṭ smaryate yathā aamayo yajñaḥ ity aapracura
ucyate evam āadapracuraṃ brahmāadamayam ucyate āadapracuratvaṃ ca brahmaṇo mauṣyatvād ārabhyottarasmi uttarasmi sthāe śataguṇa āada ity uktvā brahmāadasya iratiśayatvāvadhāraṇāt tasmāt prācuryārthe
mayaṭ taddhetuvyapadeśāc ca itaś ca prācuryārthe mayaṭ yasmād āadahetutvaṃ brahmaṇo vyapadiśati śrutiḥ eṣa hy evāadayāti iti āadayatīty arthaḥ yo hy
ayā āadayati sa pracurāada iti prasiddhaṃ bhavati yathā loke yoyeṣāṃ dhaikatvam āpādayati sa pracuradhaa iti gamyate tadvat tasmāt prācuryārthepi mayaṭaḥ
saṃbhavād āadamayaḥ para evātmā mātravarṇikam eva ca gīyate itaś cāadamayaḥ para evātmā yasmāt brahmavid āpoti param ity upakramya satyaṃ jñāam
aataṃ brahma ity asmi matre yat brahma prakṛtaṃ satyajñāāataviśeṣaṇair irdhāritam yasmād ākāśādikrameṇa sthāvarajaṅgamāi bhūtāy ajāyata yac ca bhūtāi sṛṣṭvā tāy
aupraviśya guhāyām avasthitaṃ sarvātaram yasya vijñāāya ayotara ātmā ayotara ātmā iti prakrātam tamātravarṇikameva brahmeha gīyate ayotara ātmāadamayaḥ iti matrabrāhmaṇayoś caikārthatvaṃ
yuktam avirodhāt ayathā hi prakṛtahāāprakṛtaprakriye syātām a cāamayādibhya ivāadamayād ayotara ātmābhidhīyate etaiṣṭhaiva ca bhārgavī vāruṇī vidyā āado brahmeti vyajāāt iti
tasmād āadamayaḥ para evātmā etaro upapatteḥ itaś cāadamayaḥ para evātmā etaraḥ itara īśvarād ayaḥ saṃsārī jīva ity arthaḥ a jīva
āadamayaśabdeābhidhīyate kasmāt aupapatteḥ āadamayaṃ hi prakṛtya śrūyate sokāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa tapotapyata sa tapastaptvā idsarvamasṛjata yad idaṃ kiṃca iti
tatra prākśarīrādyutpatter abhidhyāam sṛjyamāāāṃ ca vikārāṇāṃ sraṣṭur avyatirekaḥ sarvavikārasṛṣṭiś ca a parasmād ātmaoyatropapadyate bhedavyapadeśāc ca itaś ca āadamayaḥ saṃsārī yasmād
āadamayādhikāre raso vai saḥ rashyevāyaṃ labdhvāadī bhavati iti jīvāadamayau bhedea vyapadiśati a hi labdhaiva labdhavyo bhavati kathaṃ tarhi ātmāveṣṭavyaḥ ātmalābhāa
paraṃ vidyate iti śrutismṛtī yāvatā a labdhaiva labdhavyo bhavatīty uktam bāḍham tathāpy ātmaopracyutātmabhāvasyaiva satas tattvāavabodhaimitto mithyaiva dehādiṣv aātmasu ātmatvaiścayo laukiko
dṛṣṭaḥ tea dehādibhūtasyātmaopi ātmā aaviṣṭaḥ aveṣṭavyaḥ alabdhaḥ labdhavyaḥ aśrutaḥ śrotavyaḥ amataḥ matavyaḥ avijñātaḥ vijñātavyaḥ ityādibhedavyapadeśa upapadyate pratiṣidhyata eva tu paramārthataḥ
sarvajñāt parameśvarād ayo draṣṭā śrotā vā āyotosti draṣṭā ityādiā parameśvaras tu avidyākalpitāc chārīrāt kartur bhoktuḥ vijñāātmākhyāt ayaḥ yathā māyāviaścarmakhaḍgadharāt sūtreṇākāśam
adhirohataḥ sa eva māyāvī paramārtharūpo bhūmiṣṭho ayaḥ yathā vā ghaṭākāśād upādhiparicchiād aupādhiparicchia ākāśo ayaḥ īdṛśaṃ ca vijñāātmaparamātmabhedam āśritya etaro aupapatteḥ
bhedavyapadeśāc ca ity uktam kāmāc ca āumāāpekṣā āadamayādhikāre ca sokāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti iti kāmayitṛtvairdeśāc ca āumāikam api sāṃkhyaparikalpitam acetaaṃ
pradhāam āadamayatvea kāraṇatvea vā apekṣitavyam īkṣater āśabdam iti irākṛtam api pradhāaṃ pūrvasūtrodāhṛtāṃ kāmayitṛtvaśrutim āśritya prasaṅgāt puar irākriyate gatisāmāyaprapañcaāya asmi asya
ca tadyogaṃ śāsti itaś ca a pradhāe jīve vāadamayaśabdaḥ yasmād asmi āadamaye prakṛta ātmai pratibuddhasyāsya jīvasya tad yogaṃ śāsti tad
ātmaā yogas tadyogaḥ tadbhāvāpattiḥ muktir ity arthaḥ tadyogaṃ śāsti śāstram yadā hy evaiṣa etasmi adṛśyeātmyeirukteilayaebhayaṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ vidate atha sobhayaṃ gato
bhavati yadā hy evaiṣa etasmi udaram ataraṃ kurute atha tasya bhayaṃ bhavati iti etad uktaṃ bhavati yadaitasmi āadamayelpam apy ataram
atādātmyarūpaṃ paśyati tadā saṃsārabhayā a ivartate yadā tv etasmi āadamaye irataraṃ tādātmyea pratitiṣṭhati tadā saṃsārabhayā ivartata iti tac ca paramātmaparigrahe
ghaṭate a pradhāaparigrahe jīvaparigrahe vā tasmād āadamayaḥ paramātmeti siddham idaṃ tv iha vaktavyam sa vā eṣa puruṣoarasamayaḥ tasmād vā etasmād
aarasamayād ayotara ātmā prāṇamayaḥ tasmāt ayotara ātmā maomayaḥ tasmāt ayotara ātmā vijñāamayaḥ iti ca vikārārthe mayaṭpravāhe sati āadamaya evākasmād ardhajaratīyayāyea
kathamiva mayaṭaḥ prācuryārthatvaṃ brahmaviṣayatvaṃ cāśrīyata iti mātravarṇikabrahmādhikārād iti cet a aamayādīām api tarhi brahmatvaprasaṅgaḥ atrāha yuktam aamayādīām abrahmatvam tasmāt tasmād
ātarasyātarasyāyasyāyasyātmaa ucyamāatvāt āadamayāt tu a kaścid aya ātara ātmocyate teāadamayasya brahmatvam ayathā prakṛtahāāprakṛtaprakriyāprasaṅgād iti atrocyate yady apy aamayādibhya ivāadamayāt ayotara
ātmā iti a śrūyate tathāpi āadamayasya brahmatvam yata āadamayaṃ prakṛtya śrūyate tasya priyam eva śiraḥ modo dakṣiṇaḥ pakṣaḥ pramoda uttaraḥ
pakṣaḥ āada ātmā brahma pucchaṃ pratiṣṭhā iti tatra yad brahmeha matravarṇe prakṛtam satyaṃ jñāam aataṃ brahma iti tad iha brahma
pucchaṃ pratiṣṭhā ity ucyate tadvijijñāpayiṣayaivāamayādaya āadamayaparyatāḥ pañca kośāḥ kalpyate tatra kutaḥ prakṛtahāāprakṛtaprakriyāprasaṅgaḥ av āadamayasyāvayavatvea brahma pucchaṃ pratiṣṭhā ity ucyate aamayādīām
iva idaṃ pucchaṃ pratiṣṭhā ityādi tatra kathaṃ brahmaṇaḥ svapradhāatvaṃ śakyaṃ vijñātum prakṛtatvād iti brūmaḥ av āadamayāvayavatveāpi brahmaṇi vijñāyamāe a prakṛtatvaṃ
hīyate āadamayasya brahmatvād iti atrocyate tathā sati tad eva brahma āadamaya ātmā avayavī tad eva ca brahma pucchaṃ pratiṣṭhā avayava
ity asāmañjasyaṃ syāt ayataraparigrahe tu yuktam brahma pucchaṃ pratiṣṭhā ity atraiva brahmairdeśa āśrayitum brahmaśabdasaṃyogāt āadamayavākye brahmaśabdasaṃyogābhāvāditi api ca brahma pucchaṃ
pratiṣṭhety uktvedam ucyate tad apy eṣa śloko bhavati asa eva sa bhavati asad brahmeti veda cet asti brahmeti ced veda
satam eaṃ tato viduḥ iti asmiṃś ca ślokeaukṛṣyāadamayaṃ brahmaṇa eva bhāvābhāvavedaayor guṇadoṣābhidhāād gamyate brahma pucchaṃ pratiṣṭhā ity atra brahmaṇa eva
svapradhāatvam iti a cāadamayasyātmao bhāvābhāvāśaṅkā yuktā priyamodādiviśiṣṭasyāadamayasya sarvalokaprasiddhatvāt kathaṃ puaḥ svapradhāaṃ sad brahma āadamayasya pucchatvea irdiśyate brahma pucchaṃ pratiṣṭhā iti
aiṣa doṣaḥ pucchavatpuccham pratiṣṭhā parāyaṇamekaīḍaṃ laukikasyāadajātasya brahmāadaḥ ity etad aea vivakṣyate āvayavatvam etasyaivāadasyāyāi bhūtāi mātrām upajīvati iti śrutyatarāt api cāadamayasya
brahmatve priyādyavayavatvea saviśeṣaṃ brahmābhyupagatavyam irviśeṣaṃ tu brahma vākyaśeṣe śrūyate vāṅmaasayor agocaratvābhidhāāt yato vāco ivartate aprāpya maasā saha āadaṃ brahmaṇo vidvā
a bibheti kutaś caa iti api cāadapracura ity ukte duḥkhālpīyastvam api gamyate prācuryasya loke pratiyogyalpatvāpekṣatvāt tathā ca sati yatra āyat
paśyati āyac chṛṇoti āyad vijāāti sa bhūmā iti bhūmi brahmaṇi tadvyatiriktābhāvaśrutir uparudhyeta pratiśarīraṃ ca priyādibhedād āadamayasya bhiatvam brahma tu a
pratiśarīraṃ bhidyate satyaṃ jñāam aataṃ brahma ityāatyaśruteḥ eko devaḥ sarvabhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarvavyāpī sarvabhūtātarātmā iti ca śrutyatarāt a cāadamayābhyāsaḥ śrūyate prātipadikārthamātram
eva hi sarvatrābhyasyate raso vai saḥ ras hy evāyaṃ labdhvāadī bhavati ko hy evāyāt kaḥ prāṇyāt yad eṣa ākāśa āado
a syāt saiṣāadasya mīmāṃsā bhavati āadaṃ brahmaṇo vidvā a bibheti kutaś caa iti āado brahmeti vyajāāt iti ca yadi cāadamayaśabdasya
brahmaviṣayatvaṃ iścitaṃ bhavet tata uttareṣv āadamātraprayogeṣv apy āadamayābhyāsaḥ kalpyeta a tv āadamayasya brahmatvam asti priyaśirastvādibhir hetubhir ity avocāma tasmāc chrutyatare
vijñāam āadaṃ brahma ity āadapadaprātipadikasya brahmaṇi prayogadarśaāt yad eṣa ākāśa āado a syāt iti brahmaviṣayaḥ prayogo a tv āadamayābhyāsa ity
avagatavyam yas tv ayaṃ mayaḍatasyaivāadamayaśabdasyābhyāsaḥ etam āadamayam ātmāam upasaṃkrāmati iti a tasya brahmaviṣayatvam asti vikārātmaām evāamayādīām aātmaām upasaṃkramitavyāāṃ pravāhe patitatvāt
av āadamayasyopasaṃkramitavyasyāamayādivad abrahmatve sati aiva viduṣo brahmaprāptiḥ phalaṃ irdiṣṭaṃ bhavet aiṣa doṣaḥ āadamayopasaṃkramaṇairdeśeaiva viduṣaḥ pucchapratiṣṭhābhūtabrahmaprāpteḥ phalasya irdiṣṭatvāt tad apy eṣa
śloko bhavati yato vāco ivartate ityādiā ca prapañcyamāatvāt yā tv āadamayasaṃidhāe sokāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti itīyaṃ śrutir udāhṛtā sā brahma
pucchaṃ pratiṣṭhā ity aea saṃihitatareṇa brahmaṇā saṃbadhyamāā āadamayasya brahmatāṃ pratibodhayati tadapekṣatvāc cottarasya grathasya raso vai saḥ ityāder āadamayaviṣayatā au sokāmayata
iti brahmaṇi puṃliṅgairdeśo opapadyate āyaṃ doṣaḥ tasmād vā etasmād ātmaa ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ ity atra puṃliṅgeāpy ātmaśabdea brahmaṇaḥ prakṛtatvāt yat tu
bhārgavī vāruṇī vidyā āado brahmeti vyajāāt iti tasyāṃ mayaḍaśravaṇāt priyaśirastvādyaśravaṇāc ca yuktam āadasya brahmatvam tasmād aṇumātram api viśeṣam aāśritya a
svata eva priyaśirastvādi brahmaṇa upapadyate a ceha saviśeṣaṃ brahma pratipipādayiṣitam vāṅmaasagocarātikramaṇaśruteḥ tasmād aamayādiṣv ivāadamayepi vikārārtha eva mayaṭ vijñeyaḥ a prācuryārthaḥ
sūtrāṇi tv evaṃ vyākhyeyāi brahma pucchaṃ pratiṣṭhā ity atra kim āadamayāvayavatvea brahma vivakṣyate uta svapradhāatveeti pucchaśabdād avayavatveeti prāpte ucyate āadamayobhyāsāt
āadamaya ātmā ity atra brahma pucchaṃ pratiṣṭhā iti svapradhāam eva brahmopadiśyate abhyāsāt asa eva sa bhavati ity asmi igamaaśloke brahmaṇa
eva kevalasyābhyasyamāatvāt vikāraśabdā eti ce a prācuryāt vikāraśabdovayavaśabdobhipretaḥ puccham ity avayavaśabdā a svapradhāatvaṃ brahmaṇa iti yad uktam tasya parihāro vaktavyaḥ
atrocyate āyaṃ doṣaḥ prācuryād apy avayavaśabdopapatteḥ prācuryaṃ prāyāpattiḥ avayavaprāye vacaam ity arthaḥ aamayādīāṃ hi śiraādiṣu pucchāteṣv avayaveṣūkteṣv āadamayasyāpi śiraādīy avayavātarāṇy
uktvā avayavaprāyāpattyā brahma pucchaṃ pratiṣṭhā ity āha āvayavavivakṣayā yatkāraṇam abhyāsāt iti svapradhāatvaṃ brahmaṇaḥ samarthitam taddhetuvyapadeśāc ca sarvasya hi vikārajātasya sāadamayasya
kāraṇatvea brahma vyapadiśyate id sarvam asṛjata yad idaṃ kiṃca iti a ca kāraṇaṃ sad brahma svavikārasyāadamayasya mukhyayā vṛttyāvayava upapadyate aparāṇy
api sūtrāṇi yathāsaṃbhavaṃ pucchavākyairdiṣṭasyaiva brahmaṇa upapādakāi draṣṭavyāi atastaddharmopadeśāt ataradhikaraṇam idamāmāyate atha ya eṣotarāditye hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣo dṛśyate hiraṇyaśmaśrurhiraṇyakeśa ā praṇakhātsarvaeva suvarṇaḥ
tasya yathā kapyāsaṃ puṇḍarīkamevamakṣiṇī tasyoditi āma sa eṣa sarvebhyaḥ pāpmabhya udita udeti ha vai sarvebhyaḥ pāpmabhyo ya evaṃ veda ityadhidaivatam
athādhyātmamapi atha ya eṣotarakṣiṇi puruṣo dṛśyate ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ vidyākarmātiśayavaśātprāptotkarṣaḥ kaścitsaṃsārī sūryamaṇḍale cakṣuṣi copāsyatvea śrūyate kiṃ vā ityasiddhaḥ parameśvaraḥ
iti kiṃ tāvatprāptam saṃsārīti kutaḥ rūpavattvaśravaṇāt ādityapuruṣe tāvat hiraṇyaśmaśruḥ ityādi rūpamudāhṛtam akṣipuruṣepi tadevātideśea prāpyate tasyaitasya tadeva rūpaṃ yadamuṣya rūpam iti
a ca parameśvarasya rūpavattvaṃ yuktam aśabdamasparśamarūpamavyayam iti śruteḥ ādhāraśravaṇācca ya eṣotarāditye ya eṣotarakṣiṇi iti a hyaādhārasya svamahimapratiṣṭhitasya sarvavyāpiaḥ parameśvarasyādhāra upadiśyeta
sa bhagavaḥ kasmipratiṣṭhita iti sve mahimi iti ākāśavatsarvagataśca ityaḥ iti ca śrutī bhavataḥ aiśvaryamaryādāśruteśca sa eṣa ye cāmuṣmātparāñco lokāsteṣāṃ ceṣṭe
devakāmāāṃ ca ityādityapuruṣasya aiśvaryamaryādā sa eṣa ye caitasmādarvāñco lokāsteṣāṃ ceṣṭe mauṣyakāmāāṃ ca ityakṣipuruṣasya a ca parameśvarasya maryādāvadaiśvaryaṃ yuktam eṣa sarveśvara
eṣa bhūtādhipatireṣa bhūtapāla eṣa seturvidharaṇa eṣāṃ lokāāmasaṃbhedāya ityaviśeṣaśruteḥ tasmāākṣyādityayorataḥ parameśvara ityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ atastaddharmopadeśāt iti ya eṣotarāditye ya eṣotarakṣiṇi iti
ca śrūyamāṇaḥ puruṣaḥ parameśvara eva a saṃsārī kutaḥ taddharmopadeśāt tasya hi parameśvarasya dharmā ihopadiṣṭāḥ tadyathā tasyoditi āma iti śrāvayitvā tasyādityapuruṣasya
āma sa eṣa sarvebhyaḥ pāpmabhya uditaḥ iti sarvapāpmāpagamea irvakti tadeva ca kṛtairvacaaṃ āmākṣipuruṣasyāpyatidiśati yaāma taāma iti sarvapāpmāpagamaśca paramātmaa eva śrūyate
ya ātmāpahatapāpmā ityādau tathā cākṣuṣe puruṣe saiva ṛk tatsāma tadukthaṃ tadyajustadbrahma iti ṛksāmādyātmakatāṃ irdhārayati sā ca parameśvarasyopapadyate sarvakāraṇatvātsarvātmakatvopapatteḥ pṛthivyagyādyātmake cādhidaivatamṛksāme
vākprāṇādyātmake cādhyātmamaukramyāha tasyarkca sāma ca geṣṇau ityadhidaivatam tathādhyātmamapi yāvamuṣya geṣṇau tau geṣṇau iti tacca sarvātmakatve satyevopapadyate tadya ime vīṇāyāṃ gāyatyetaṃ
tveva te gāyati tasmātte dhaasaayaḥ iti ca laukikeṣvapi gāeṣvasyaiva gīyamāatvaṃ darśayati tacca parameśvaraparigraha eva ghaṭate yadyadvibhūtimatsattvaṃ śrīmadūrjitameva vā tattadevāvagaccha tvaṃ
mama tejoṃśasaṃbhavam iti bhagavadgītādarśaāt lokakāmeśitṛtvamapi iraṅkuśaṃ śrūyamāṇaṃ parameśvaraṃ gamayati yattūktaṃ hiraṇyaśmaśrutvādirūpavattvaśravaṇaṃ parameśvare opapadyata iti atra brūmaḥ syātparameśvarasyāpīcchāvaśāmāyāmayaṃ rūpaṃ sādhakāugrahārtham māyā
hyeṣā mayā sṛṣṭā yamāṃ paśyasi ārada sarvabhūtaguṇairyuktaṃ maivaṃ māṃ jñātumarhasi iti smaraṇāt api ca yatra tu irastasarvaviśeṣaṃ pārameśvaraṃ rūpamupadiśyate bhavati
tatra śāstram aśabdamasparśamarūpamavyayam ityādi sarvakāraṇatvāttu vikāradharmairapi kaiścidviśiṣṭaḥ parameśvara upāsyatvea irdiśyate sarvakarmā sarvakāmaḥ sarvagadhaḥ sarvarasaḥ ityādiā tathā hiraṇyaśmaśrutvādiirdeśopi bhaviṣyati yadapyādhāraśravaṇāa parameśvara
iti atrocyate svamahimapratiṣṭhasyāpyādhāraviśeṣopadeśa upāsaārtho bhaviṣyati sarvagatatvādbrahmaṇo vyomavatsarvātaratvopapatteḥ aiśvaryamaryādāśravaṇamapyadhyātmādhidaivatavibhāgāpekṣamupāsaārthameva tasmātparameśvara evākṣyādityayoratarupadiśyate bhedavyapadeśāc cāyaḥ asti cādityādiśarīrābhimāibhyo jīvebhyoya īśvarotaryāmī ya āditye tiṣṭhaādityādataro yamādityo
a veda yasyādityaḥ śarīraṃ ya ādityamataro yamayatyeṣa ta ātmātaryāmyamṛtaḥ iti śrutyatare bhedavyapadeśāt tatra hi ādityādataro yamādityo a veda iti vediturādityādvijñāātmaoyotaryāmī
spaṣṭaṃ irdiśyate sa evehāpyatarāditye puruṣo bhavitumarhati śrutisāmāyāt tasmātparameśvara evehopadiśyata iti siddham ākāśastalliṅgāt ākāśādhikaraṇam idamāmaati asya lokasya kā gatirityākāśa iti hovāca
sarvāṇi ha vā imāi bhūtāy ākāśād eva samutpadyata ākāśaṃ praty astaṃ yaty ākāśo hy evaibhyo jyāyā ākāśaḥ parāyaṇam iti tatra
saṃśayaḥ kim ākāśaśabdea paraṃ brahmābhidhīyate uta bhūtākāśam iti kutaḥ saṃśayaḥ ubhayatra prayogadarśaāt bhūtaviśeṣe tāvat suprasiddho lokavedayor ākāśaśabdaḥ brahmaṇy api kvacit
prayujyamāo dṛśyate yatra vākyaśeṣavaśād asādhāraṇaguṇaśravaṇād vā irdhāritaṃ brahma bhavati yathā yad eṣa ākāśa āado a syāt iti ākāśo ha vai
āma āmarūpayor irvahitā te yadatarā tad brahma iti caivamādau ataḥ saṃśayaḥ kiṃ puar atra yuktam bhūtākāśam iti kutaḥ tad dhi
prasiddhatareṇa prayogeṇa śīghraṃ buddhim ārohati a cāyam ākāśaśabda ubhayoḥ sādhāraṇaḥ śakyo vijñātum aekārthatvaprasaṅgāt tasmād brahmaṇi gauṇa eva ākāśaśabdo bhavitum arhati
vibhutvādibhir hi bahubhir dharmaiḥ sadṛśam ākāśea brahma bhavati a ca mukhyasaṃbhave gauṇo rtho grahaṇam arhati saṃbhavati ceha mukhyasyaivākāśasya grahaṇam au
bhūtākāśaparigrahe vākyaśeṣo opapadyate sarvāṇi ha vā imāi bhūtāy ākāśād eva samutpadyate ityādiḥ aiṣa doṣaḥ bhūtākāśasyāpi vāyvādikrameṇa kāraṇatvopapatteḥ vijñāyate hi tasmād
vā etasmād ātmaa ākāśaḥ saṃbhūta ākāśād vāyur vāyor agiḥ ityādi jyāyas tv aparāyaṇatve api bhūtātarāpekṣayopapadyete bhūtākāśasyāpi tasmād ākāśaśabdea bhūtākāśasya grahaṇam
ity evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ ākāśas talliṅgāt ākāśaśabdeeha brahmaṇo grahaṇaṃ yuktam kutaḥ talliṅgāt parasya hi brahmaṇa idaṃ liṅgam sarvāṇi ha vā
imāi bhūtāy ākāśād eva samutpadyate iti parasmād dhi brahmaṇo bhūtāām utpattir iti vedāteṣu maryādā au bhūtākāśasyāpi vāyvādikrameṇa kāraṇatvaṃ darśitam satyaṃ
darśitam tathāpi mūlakāraṇasya brahmaṇo parigrahāt ākāśād evety avadhāraṇaṃ sarvāṇīti ca bhūtaviśeṣaṇaṃ āukūlaṃ syāt tathākāśaṃ praty astaṃ yati iti brahmaliṅgam ākāśo
hy evaibhyo jyāyā ākāśaḥ parāyaṇam iti ca jyāyas tv aparāyaṇatve jyāyastvaṃ hy aāpekṣikaṃ paramātmay evaikasmi āmātam jyāyā pṛthivyā jyāyā atarikṣāj
jyāyā divo jyāyā ebhyo lokebhyaḥ iti tathā parāyaṇatvam api paramakāraṇatvāt paramātmay eva upapaataraṃ bhavati śrutiś ca vijñāam āadaṃ brahma rātir
dātuḥ parāyaṇam iti api cātavat tv adoṣeṇa śālāvatyasya pakṣaṃ iditvā aataṃ kiṃcid vaktukāmea jaivaliākāśaḥ parigṛhītaḥ taṃ cākāśamudgīthe saṃpādyopasaṃharati sa eṣa
parovarīyāudgīthaḥ sa eṣoataḥ iti taccāatyaṃ brahmaliṅgam yat puar uktaṃ bhūtākāśaṃ prasiddhibalea prathamataraṃ pratīyata iti atra brūmaḥ prathamataraṃ pratītam api tadvākyaśeṣagatā
brahmaguṇā dṛṣṭvā a parigṛhyate darśitaś ca brahmaṇy apy ākāśaśabdaḥ ākāśo ha vai āma āmarūpayorirvahitā ityādau tathākāśaparyāyavāciām api brahmaṇi prayogo dṛśyate
ṛco akṣare parame vyoma yasmi devā adhi viśve iṣeduḥ saiṣā bhārgavī vāruṇī vidyā parame vyoma pratiṣṭhitā kaṃ brahma khaṃ brahma
khaṃ purāṇam iti caivamādau vākyopakrame pi vartamāasyākāśaśabdasya vākyaśeṣavaśād yuktā brahmaviṣayatvāvadhāraṇā agir adhīte uvākam iti hi vākyopakramagato py agiśabdo māṇavakaviṣayo dṛśyate
tasmād ākāśaśabdaṃ brahmeti siddham ata eva prāṇaḥ prāṇādhikaraṇam udgīthe prastotaryā devatā prastāvamavāyattā ityupakramya śrūyate katamā sā devateti prāṇa iti hovāca
sarvāṇi ha vā imāi bhūtāi prāṇamevābhisaṃviśati prāṇamabhyujjihate saiṣā devatā prastāvamavāyattā iti tatra saṃśayairṇayau pūrvavadeva draṣṭavyau prāṇabadhahi somya maaḥ prāṇasya prāṇam
iti caivamādau brahmaviṣayaḥ prāṇaśabdo dṛśyate vāyuvikāre tu prasiddhataro lokavedayoḥ ata iha prāṇaśabdea katarasyopādāaṃ yuktamiti bhavati saṃśayaḥ kiṃ puaratra yuktam vāyuvikārasya
pañcavṛtteḥ prāṇasyopādāaṃ yuktam tatra hi prasiddhataraḥ prāṇaśabda ityavocāma au pūrvavadihāpi talliṅgādbrahmaṇa eva grahaṇaṃ yuktam ihāpi hi vākyaśeṣe bhūtāāṃ saṃveśaodgamaaṃ pārameśvaraṃ
karma pratīyate a mukhyepi prāṇe bhūtasaṃveśaodgamaasya darśaāt evaṃ hyāmāyate yadā vai puruṣaḥ svapiti prāṇaṃ tarhi vāgapyeti prāṇaṃ cakṣuḥ prāṇaṃ śrotraṃ
prāṇaṃ maaḥ sa yadā prabudhyate prāṇādevādhi puarjāyate iti pratyakṣaṃ caitat svāpakāle prāṇavṛttāvaparilupyamāāyāmidriyavṛttayaḥ parilupyate prabodhakāle ca puaḥ prādurbhavatīti idriyasāratvācca bhūtāāmaviruddho mukhye
prāṇepi bhūtasaṃveśaodgamaavādī vākyaśeṣaḥ api cādityoaṃ codgīthapratihārayordevate prastāvadevatāyāḥ prāṇasyāataraṃ irdiśyeta a ca tayorbrahmatvamasti tatsāmāyācca prāṇasyāpi a brahmatvamityevaṃ prāpte sūtrakāra āha ata
eva prāṇaḥ iti talliṅgāditi pūrvasūtre irdiṣṭam ata eva talliṅgātprāṇaśabdamapi paraṃ brahma bhavitumarhati prāṇasyāpi hi brahmaliṅgasaṃbadhaḥ śrūyate sarvāṇi ha vā imāi
bhūtāi prāṇamevābhisaṃviśati prāṇamabhyujjihate iti prāṇaimittau sarveṣāṃ bhūtāāmutpattipralayāvucyamāau prāṇasya brahmatāṃ gamayataḥ aūktaṃ mukhyaprāṇaparigrahepi saṃveśaodgamaadarśaamaviruddham svāpaprabodhayordarśaāditi atrocyate svāpaprabodhayoridriyāṇāmeva kevalāāṃ prāṇāśrayaṃ saṃveśaodgamaaṃ dṛśyate
a sarveṣāṃ bhūtāām iha tu sedriyāṇāṃ saśarīrāṇāṃ ca jīvāviṣṭāāṃ bhūtāām sarvāṇi ha vā imāi bhūtāi iti śruteḥ yadāpi bhūtaśrutirmahābhūtaviṣayā parigṛhyate
tadāpi brahmaliṅgatvamaviruddham au sahāpi viṣayairidriyāṇāṃ svāpaprabodhayoḥ prāṇepyayaṃ prāṇācca prabhavaṃ śrṛṇumaḥ yadā suptaḥ svapaṃ a kaṃcaa paśyatyathāsmiprāṇa evaikadhā bhavati tadaiaṃ vāksarvairāmabhiḥ
sahāpyeti iti tatrāpi talliṅgātprāṇaśabdaṃ brahmeva yat puar uktam aādityasaṃidhāāt prāṇasyābrahmatvam iti tad ayuktam vākyaśeṣabalea prāṇaśabdasya brahmaviṣayatāyāṃ pratīyamāāyāṃ saṃidhāasyākiṃcitkaratvāt yat puaḥ
prāṇaśabdasya pañcavṛttau prasiddhataratvam tad ākāśaśabdasyeva pratividheyam tasmāt siddhaṃ prastāvadevatāyāḥ prāṇasya brahmatvam atra kecid udāharati prāṇasya prāṇam prāṇabadhaaṃ hi somya maaḥ
iti ca tad ayuktam śabdabhedāt prakaraṇāc ca saṃśayāupapatteḥ yathā pituḥ piteti prayoge ayaḥ pitā ṣaṣṭhīirdiṣṭāt prathamāirdiṣṭaḥ pituḥ pitā iti gamyate
tadvat prāṇasya prāṇam iti śabdabhedāt prasiddhāt prāṇāt ayaḥ prāṇasya prāṇa iti iścīyate a hi sa eva tasyeti bhedairdeśārho bhavati yasya
ca prakaraṇe yo irdiśyate āmātareṇāpi sa eva tatra prakaraṇī irdiṣṭa iti gamyate yathā jyotiṣṭomādhikāre vasate vasate jyotiṣā yajeta ity atra
jyotiḥśabdo jyotiṣṭomaviṣayo bhavati tathā parasya brahmaṇaḥ prakaraṇe prāṇabadhaaṃ hi somya maaḥ iti śrutaḥ prāṇaśabdo vāyuvikāramātraṃ katham avagamayet ataḥ saṃśayāviṣayatvā aitad
udāharaṇaṃ yuktam prastāvadevatāyāṃ tu prāṇe saṃśayapūrvapakṣairṇayā upapāditāḥ jyotiścaraṇābhidhāāt jyotiścaraṇādhikaraṇam idam āmaati atha yad ataḥ paro divo jyotir dīpyate viśvataḥ pṛṣṭheṣu
sarvataḥ pṛṣṭheṣvauttameṣūttameṣu lokeṣvidaṃ vāva tadyadidamasmiataḥ puruṣe jyotiḥ iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha jyotiḥśabdeādityādikaṃ jyotirabhidhīyate kiṃ vā para ātmā iti arthātaraviṣayasyāpi
prāṇaśabdasya talliṅgādbrahmaviṣayatvam uktam iha tu talliṅgam evāsti āstīti vicāryate kiṃ tāvat prāptam ādityādikam eva jyotiḥśabdea parigṛhyata iti kutaḥ prasiddheḥ tamo
jyotir iti hīmau śabdau parasparapratidvadviviṣayau prasiddhau cakṣurvṛtter irodhakaṃ śārvarādikaṃ tama ucyate tasyā evāugrāhakam ādityādikaṃ jyotiḥ tathā dīpyate itīyam api śrutir
ādityādiviṣayā prasiddhā a hi rūpādihīaṃ brahma dīpyata iti mukhyāṃ śrutim arhati dyumaryādatvaśruteś ca a hi carācarabījasya brahmaṇaḥ sarvātmakasya dyaurmaryādā yuktā
kāryasya tu jyotiśaḥ paricchiasya dyaurmaryādā syāt paro divo jyotiḥ iti ca brāhmaṇam au kāryasyāpi jyotiṣaḥ sarvatra gamyamāatvād dyumaryādāvattvam asamañjasam astu
tarhy atrivṛtkṛtaṃ tejaḥ prathamajam a atrivṛtkṛtasya tejasaḥ prayojaābhāvād iti idam eva prayojaaṃ yad upāsyatvam iti cet a prayojaātaraprayuktasyaivādityāder upāsyatvadarśaāt tāsāṃ
trivṛtaṃ trivṛtam ekaikāṃ karavāṇi iti cāviśeṣaśruteḥ a cātrivṛtkṛtasyāpi tejaso dyumaryādatvaṃ prasiddham astu tarhi trivṛtkṛtameva tat tejo jyotiḥśabdam aūktamarvāg api divovagamyategyādikaṃ
jyotir iti aiṣa doṣaḥ sarvatrāpi gamyamāasya jyotiṣaḥ paro divaḥ ity upāsaārthaḥ pradeśaviśeṣaparigraho a virudhyate a tu iṣpradeśasyāpi brahmaṇaḥ pradeśaviśeṣakalpaā bhāgiī
sarvataḥ pṛṣṭheṣv auttameṣūttameṣu lokeṣu iti cādhārabahutvaśrutiḥ kārye jyotiṣy upapadyatetarām idaṃ vāva tad yad idam asmi ataḥ puruṣe jyotiḥ iti ca
kaukṣeye jyotiṣi paraṃ jyotir adhyasyamāaṃ dṛśyate sārūpyaimittāś cādhyāsā bhavati yathā tasya bhūriti śira ekhi śira ekam etad akṣaram iti kaukṣeyasya
tu jyotiṣaḥ prasiddham abrahmatvam tasyaiṣā dṛṣṭiḥ tasyaiṣā śrutiḥ iti cauṣṇyaghoṣaviśiṣṭatvasya śravaṇāt tad etad dṛṣṭaṃ ca śrutaṃ cety upāsīta iti ca
śruteḥ cakṣuṣyaś ca śruto bhavati ya evaṃ veda iti cālpaphalaśravaṇād abrahmatvam mahate hi phalāya brahmopāsaam iṣyate a cāyadapi kiṃcitsvavākye prāṇākāśavaj
jyotiṣo asti brahmatvaliṅgam a ca pūrvasmi api vākye brahma irdiṣṭamasti gāyatrī vā idaṃ sarvaṃ bhūtam iti cchadoirdeśāt athāpi kathaṃcit pūrvasmi
vākye brahma irdiṣṭaṃ syāt evam api a tasyeha pratyabhijñāam asti tatra hi tripādasyāmṛtaṃ divi iti dyauradhikaraṇatvea śrūyate atra puaḥ paro
divo jyotiḥ iti dyaurmaryādātvea tasmāt prākṛtaṃ jyotir iha grāhyam ity evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ jyotir iha brahma grāhyam kutaḥ caraṇābhidhāāt pādābhidhāādityarthaḥ
pūrvasmihi vākye catuṣpādbrahma irdiṣṭam tāvāasya mahimā tato jyāyāśca puruṣaḥ pādosya sarvā bhūtāi tripādasyāmṛtaṃ divi ityaea matreṇa tatra yaccatuṣpado brahmaṇastripādamṛtaṃ dyusaṃbadhirūpaṃ
irdiṣṭam tadeveha dyusaṃbadhāirdiṣṭamiti pratyabhijñāyate tatparityajya prākṛtaṃ jyotiḥ kalpayataḥ prakṛtahāāprakṛtaprakriye prasajyeyātām a kevalaṃ jyotirvākya eva brahmāuvṛttiḥ parasyāmapi hi śāṇḍilyavidyāyāmauvartiṣyate brahma tasmādiha
jyotiriti brahma pratipattavyam yattūktam jyotirdīpyate iti caitau śabdau kārye jyotiṣi prasiddhāviti āyaṃ doṣaḥ prakaraṇādbrahmāvagame satyaayoḥ śabdayoraviśeṣakatvāt dīpyamāakāryajyotirupalakṣite brahmaṇyapi prayogasaṃbhavāt yea
sūryastapati tejaseddhaḥ iti ca matravarṇāt yadvā āyaṃ jyotiḥśabdaścakṣurvṛtterevāugrāhake tejasi vartate ayatrāpi prayogadarśaāt vācaivāyaṃ jyotiṣāste mao jyotirjuṣatām iti ca tasmādyadyatkasyacidavabhāsakaṃ tattajjyotiḥśabdeābhidhīyate
tathā sati brahmaṇopi caitayarūpasya samastajagadavabhāsahetutvādupapao jyotiḥśabdaḥ tameva bhātamaubhāti sarvaṃ tasya bhāsā sarvamidaṃ vibhāti taddevā jyotiṣāṃ jyotirāyurhopāsatemṛtam ityādiśrutibhyaśca yadapyuktaṃ dyumaryādatvaṃ sarvagatasya
brahmaṇo opapadyata iti atrocyate sarvagatasyāpi brahmaṇa upāsaārthaḥ pradeśaviśeṣaparigraho a virudhyate aūktaṃ iṣpradeśasya brahmaṇaḥ pradeśaviśeṣakalpaā opapadyata iti āyaṃ doṣaḥ iṣpradeśasyāpi brahmaṇa
upādhiviśeṣasaṃbadhātpradeśaviśeṣakalpaopapatteḥ tathā hi āditye cakṣuṣi hṛdaye iti pradeśaviśeṣasaṃbadhīi brahmaṇaḥ upāsaāi śrūyate etea viśvataḥ pṛṣṭheṣu ityādhārabahutvamupapāditam yadapyetaduktam auṣṇyaghoṣābhyāmaumite kaukṣeye kārye jyotiṣyadhyasyamāatvātparamapi
divaḥ kāryajyotireveti tadapyayuktam parasyāpi brahmaṇo āmādipratīkatvavatkaukṣeyajyotiṣpratīkatvopapatteḥ dṛṣṭaṃ ca śrutaṃ cety upāsīta iti tu pratīkadvārakaṃ dṛṣṭatvaṃ śrutatvaṃ ca bhaviṣyati yad apy
uktam alpaphalaśravaṇāc ca a brahmeti tad aupapaam a hi iyate phalāya brahmāśrayaṇīyam iyate a iti iyame hetur asti yatra hi
irastasarvaviśeṣasaṃbadhaṃ paraṃ brahmātmatveopadiśyate tatraikarūpam eva phalaṃ mokṣa ity avagamyate yatra tu guṇaviśeṣasaṃbadhaṃ pratīkaviśeṣasaṃbadhaṃ vā brahmopadiśyate tatra saṃsāragocarāṇyevoccāvacāi phalāi dṛśyate aādo
vasudāo vidate vasu ya evaṃ veda ityādyāsu śrutiṣu yadyapi a svavākye kiṃcijjyotiṣo brahmatvaliṅgamasti tathāpi pūrvasmivākye dṛśyamāaṃ grahītavyaṃ bhavati taduktaṃ sūtrakāreṇa
jyotiścaraṇābhidhāāditi kathaṃ puarvākyātaragatea brahmasaṃidhāea jyotiḥśrutiḥ svaviṣayāt śakyā pracyāvayitum aiṣa doṣaḥ atha yadataḥ paro divo jyotiḥ iti prathamatarapaṭhitea yacchabdea sarvaāmā dyusaṃbadhātpratyabhijñāyamāe
pūrvavākyairdiṣṭe brahmaṇi svasāmarthyea parāmṛṣṭe satyarthājjyotiḥśabdasyāpi brahmaviṣayatvopapatteḥ tasmādiha jyotiriti brahma pratipattavyam chadobhidhāāeti cea tathā cetorpaṇaigadāttathā hi darśaam atha yaduktaṃ pūrvasmiapi vākye
a brahmābhihitamasti gāyatrī vā idsarvaṃ bhūtaṃ yadidaṃ kiṃca iti gāyatryākhyasya cchadasobhihitatvāditi tatparihartavyam kathaṃ puaśchadobhidhāāa brahmābhihitamiti śakyate vaktum yāvatā tāvāasya mahimā
ityetasyāmṛci catuṣpādbrahma darśitam aitadasti gāyatrī vā idsarvam iti gāyatrīmupakramya tāmeva bhūtapṛthivīśarīrahṛdayavākprāṇaprabhedairvyākhyāya saiṣā catuṣpadā ṣaḍvidhā gāyatrī tadetadṛcābhyaūktaṃ tāvāasya mahimā iti tasyāmeva
vyākhyātarūpāyāṃ gāyatryāmudāhṛto matraḥ kathamakasmādbrahma catuṣpādabhidadhyāt yopi tatra yadvai tadbrahma iti brahmaśabdaḥ sopi cchadasaḥ prakṛtatvācchadoviṣaya eva ya etāmevaṃ brahmopaiṣadaṃ veda ityatra
hi vedopaiṣadamiti vyācakṣate tasmācchadobhidhāāa brahmaṇaḥ prakṛtatvamiti cet aiṣa doṣaḥ tathā cetorpaṇaigadāt tathā gāyatryākhyacchadodvāreṇa tadaugate brahmaṇi cetasorpaṇaṃ cittasamādhāam aea brāhmaṇavākyea igadyate
gāyatrī vā idsarvam iti a hyakṣarasaṃiveśamātrāyā gāyatryāḥ sarvātmakatvaṃ saṃbhavati tasmādyadgāyatryākhyavikāreugataṃ jagatkāraṇaṃ brahma irdiṣṭam tadiha sarvamityucyate yathā sarvaṃ khalvidaṃ brahma iti
kāryaṃ ca kāraṇādavyatiriktamiti vakṣyāmaḥ tadaayatvamārambhaṇaśabdādibhyaḥ ityatra tathāyatrāpi vikāradvāreṇa brahmaṇa upāsaaṃ dṛśyate etaṃ hyeva bahvṛcā mahatyukthe mīmāṃsata etamagāvadhvaryava etaṃ mahāvrate cchadogāḥ
iti tasmādasti cchadobhidhāepi pūrvasmivākye catuṣpādbrahma irdiṣṭam tadeva jyotirvākyepi parāmṛśyata upāsaātaravidhāāya apara āha sākṣādeva gāyatrīśabdea brahma pratipādyate saṃkhyāsāmāyāt yathā gāyatrī catuṣpadā
ṣaḍakṣaraiḥ pādaiḥ tathā brahma catuṣpāt tathāyatrāpi cchadobhidhāyī śabdorthātare saṃkhyāsāmāyātprayujyamāo dṛśyate tadyathā te vā ete pañcāye pañcāye daśa satastatkṛtam ityupakramyāha saiṣā
virāḍaādī iti asmipakṣe brahmaivābhihitamiti a cchadobhidhāam sarvathāpyasti pūrvasmivākye prakṛtaṃ brahma iti bhūtādipādavyapadeśopapatteścaivam itaścaivamabhyupagatavyamasti pūrvasmivākye prakṛtaṃ brahmeti yato bhūtādīpādāvyapadiśati śrutiḥ bhūtapṛthivīśarīrahṛdayāi
hi irdiśyāha saiṣā catuṣpadā ṣaḍvidhā gāyatrī iti a hi brahmāāśrayaṇe kevalasya cchadaso bhūtādayaḥ pādā upapadyate api ca brahmāāśrayaṇe eyamṛk saṃbadhyeta
tāvāasya mahimā iti aayā hi ṛcā svarasea brahmaivābhidhīyate pādosya sarvā bhūtāi tripādasyāmṛtaṃ divi iti sarvātmatvopapatteḥ puruṣasūktepīyamṛk brahmaparatayaiva samāmāyate smṛtiśca brahmaṇa
evaṃrūpatāṃ darśayati viṣṭabhyāhamidaṃ kṛtsamekāṃśea sthito jagat iti yadvai tadbrahma iti ca irdeśaḥ evaṃ sati mukhyārtha upapadyate te vā ete pañca
brahmapuruṣāḥ iti ca hṛdayasuṣiṣu brahmapuruṣaśrutirbrahmasaṃbadhitāyāṃ vivakṣitāyāṃ saṃbhavati tasmādasti pūrvasmivākye brahma prakṛtam tadeva brahma jyotirvākye dyusaṃbadhātpratyabhijñāyamāaṃ parāmṛśyata iti sthitam upadeśabhedāeti ceobhayasmiapyavirodhāt
yadapyetaduktam pūrvatra tripādasyāmṛtaṃ divi iti saptamyā dyauḥ ādhāratveopadiṣṭā iha puaḥ atha yadataḥ paro divaḥ iti pañcamyā maryādātvea tasmādupadeśabhedāa tasyeha pratyabhijñāamastīti
tatparihartavyam atrocyate āyaṃ doṣaḥ ubhayasmiapyavirodhāt ubhayasmiapi saptamyate pañcamyate copadeśe a pratyabhijñāaṃ virudhyate yathā loke vṛkṣāgreṇa saṃbaddhopi śyea ubhayathopadiśyamāo dṛśyate vṛkṣāgre
śyeo vṛkṣāgrātparataḥ śyea iti ca evaṃ divyeva sadbrahma divaḥ paramityupadiśyate apara āha yathā loke vṛkṣāgreṇāsaṃbaddhopi śyea ubhayathopadiśyamāo dṛśyate vṛkṣāgre śyeo
vṛkṣāgrātparataḥ śyea iti ca evaṃ divaḥ paramapi sadbrahma divītyupadiśyate tasmādasti pūrvairdiṣṭasya brahmaṇa iha pratyabhijñāam ataḥ parameva brahma jyotiḥśabdamiti siddham prāṇas
tathāugamāt prātardaādhikaraṇam asti kauṣītakibrāhmaṇopaiṣadīdrapratardaākhyāyikā pratardao ha vai daivodāsiridrasya priyaṃ dhāmopajagāma yuddhea ca pauruṣeṇa ca ity ārabhyāmātā tasyāṃ śrūyate sa hovāca
prāṇosmi prajñātmā taṃ māmāyur amṛtam ity upāssva iti tathottaratrāpi atha khalu prāṇa eva prajñātmedaṃ śarīraṃ parigṛhyotthāpayati iti tathā a vācaṃ
vijijñāsīta vaktāraṃ vidyāt iti ate ca sa eṣa prāṇa eva prajñātmāadojaromṛtaḥ ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kimiha prāṇaśabdea vāyumātramabhidhīyate uta devatātmā uta
jīvaḥ athavā paraṃ brahmeti au ata eva prāṇaḥ ityatra varṇitaṃ prāṇaśabdasya brahmaparatvam ihāpi ca brahmaliṅgamasti āadojaromṛtaḥ ityādi kathamiha puaḥ saṃśayaḥ
saṃbhavati aekaliṅgadarśaāditi brūmaḥ a kevalamiha brahmaliṅgamevopalabhyate sati hītaraliṅgāyapi māmeva vijāīhi itīdrasya vacaaṃ devatātmaliṅgam idaṃ śarīraṃ parigṛhyotthāpayati iti prāṇaliṅgam a vācaṃ
vijijñāsīta vaktāraṃ vidyāt ityādi jīvaliṅgama ata upapaaḥ saṃśayaḥ tatra prasiddhervāyuḥ prāṇa iti prāpte idamucyate prāṇaśabdaṃ brahma vijñeyam kutaḥ tathāugamāt tathāhi
paurvāparyeṇa paryālocyamāe vākye padāāṃ samavayo brahmapratipādaapara upalabhyate upakrame tāvat varaṃ vṛṇīṣva itīdreṇoktaḥ pratardaaḥ paramaṃ puruṣārthaṃ varamupacikṣepa tvameva me varaṃ vṛṇīṣva
yaṃ tvaṃ mauṣyāya hitatamaṃ mayase iti tasmai hitatamatveopadiśyamāaḥ prāṇaḥ kathaṃ paramātmā a syāt a hyayatra paramātmavijñāāddhitatamaprāptirasti tameva viditvāti mṛtyumeti āyaḥ
pathā vidyateyaāya ityādiśrutibhyaḥ tathā sa yo māṃ veda a ha vai tasya keacaa karmaṇā loko mīyate a steyea a bhrūṇahatyayā
ityādi ca brahmaparigrahe ghaṭate brahmavijñāea hi sarvakarmakṣayaḥ prasiddhaḥ kṣīyate cāsya karmāṇi tasmidṛṣṭe parāvare ityādyāsu śrutiṣu prajñātmatvaṃ ca brahmapakṣa evopapadyate a
hyacetaasya vāyoḥ prajñātmatvaṃ saṃbhavati tathopasaṃhārepi āadojaromṛtaḥ ityāadatvādīi ca a brahmaṇoyatra samyak saṃbhavati sa a sādhuā karmaṇā bhūyābhavati o evāsādhuā karmaṇā
kaīyāeṣa hyeva sādhu karma kārayati taṃ yamebhyo lokebhya uiīṣate eṣa u evāsādhu karma kārayati taṃ yamebhyo lokebhyodho iīṣate iti eṣa
lokādhipatir eṣa lokapāla eṣa lokeśaḥ iti ca sarvam etat parasmi brahmaṇy āśrīyamāṇeugatuṃ śakyate a mukhye prāṇe tasmāt prāṇo brahma a
vakturātmopadeśāditi cedadhyātmasambadhabhūmā hyasmi yaduktaṃ prāṇo brahmeti tadākṣipyate a paraṃ brahma prāṇaśabdam kasmāt vakturātmopadeśāt vaktā hīdro āma kaścidvigrahavādevatāviśeṣaḥ svamātmāaṃ pratardaāyācacakṣe māmeva
vijāīhi ityupakramya prāṇosmi prajñātmā ityahaṃkāravādea sa eva vakturātmatveopadiśyamāaḥ prāṇaḥ kathaṃ brahma syāt a hi brahmaṇo vaktṛtvaṃ saṃbhavati avāgamaāḥ ityādiśrutibhyaḥ tathā
vigrahasaṃbadhibhireva brahmaṇyasaṃbhavadbhirdharmairidra ātmāaṃ tuṣṭāva triśīrṣāṇaṃ tvāṣṭramahaamarumukhāyatīñśālāvṛkebhyaḥ prāyaccham ityevamādibhiḥ prāṇatvaṃ cedrasya balavattvādupapadyate prāṇo vai balam iti hi vijñāyate balasya cedro devatā
prasiddhā yā ca kācidbalaprakṛtiḥ idrasya karmaiva taditi hi vadati prajñātmatvamapyapratihatajñāatvāddevatātmaaḥ saṃbhavati apratihatajñāā devatā iti hi vadati iścite caivaṃ devatātmopadeśe hitatamatvādivacaāi
yathāsaṃbhavaṃ tadviṣayāṇyeva yojayitavyāi tasmādvakturidrasyātmopadeśāt a prāṇo brahmetyākṣipya pratisamādhīyate adhyātmasaṃbadhabhūmā hyasmi iti adhyātmasaṃbadhaḥ pratyagātmasaṃbadhaḥ tasya bhūmā bāhulyam asmiadhyāye upalabhyate yāvaddhyasmiñśarīre prāṇo
vasati tāvadāyuḥ iti prāṇasyaiva prajñātmaaḥ pratyagbhūtasyāyuṣpradāopasaṃhārayoḥ svātatryaṃ darśayati a devatāviśeṣasya parācīasya tathāstitve ca prāṇāāṃ iḥśreyasamityadhyātmamevedriyāśrayaṃ prāṇaṃ darśayati tathā prāṇa eva
prajñātmedaṃ śarīraṃ parigṛhyotthāpayati iti a vācaṃ vijijñāsīta vaktāraṃ vidyāt iti copakramya tadyathā rathasyāreṣu emirarpitā ābhāvarā arpitā evamevaitā bhūtamātrāḥ prajñāmātrāsvarpitāḥ prajñāmātrāḥ
prāṇerpitāḥ sa eṣa prāṇa eva prajñātmāadojaromṛtaḥ iti viṣayedriyavyavahārāraābhibhūtaṃ pratyagātmāamevopasaṃharati sa ma ātmeti vidyāt iti copasaṃhāraḥ pratyagātmaparigrahe sādhuḥ a parācīaparigrahe ayamātmā
brahma sarvāubhūḥ iti ca śrutyataram tasmādadhyātmasaṃbadhabāhulyādbrahmopadeśa evāyam a devatātmopadeśaḥ kathaṃ tarhi vakturātmopadeśaḥ śāstradṛṣṭyā tūpadeśo vāmadevavat idro āma devatātmā svamātmāaṃ paramātmatvea
ahameva paraṃ brahma ityārṣeṇa darśaea yathāśāstraṃ paśya upadiśati sma māmeva vijāīhi iti yathā taddhaitatpaśyaṛṣirvāmadevaḥ pratipedehaṃ maurabhavaṃ sūryaśca iti tadvat tadyo
yo devāāṃ pratyabudhyata sa eva tadabhavat iti śruteḥ yatpuaruktam māmeva vijāīhi ityuktvā vigrahacarmairidraḥ svamātmāaṃ tuṣṭāva tvāṣṭravadhādibhiriti tatparihartavyam atrocyate a tāvat
tvāṣṭravadhādīāṃ vijñeyedrastutyarthatveopayāsaḥ yasmādevaṃkarmāham tasmāmāṃ vijāīhi iti kathaṃ tarhi vijñāastutyarthatvea yatkāraṇaṃ tvāṣṭravadhādīi sāhasāyupayasya pareṇa vijñāastutimausaṃdadhāti tasya me tatra loma ca a
mīyate sa yo māṃ veda a ha vai tasya kea ca karmaṇā loke mīyate ityādiā etaduktaṃ bhavati yasmādīdṛśāyapi krūrāṇi karmāṇi
kṛtavato mama brahmabhūtasya lomāpi a hiṃsyate sa yoyopi māṃ veda a tasya keacidapi karmaṇā loko hiṃsyata iti vijñeyaṃ tu brahmaiva
prāṇosmi prajñātmā iti vakṣyamāṇam tasmād brahmavākyam etat jīvamukhyaprāṇaliṅgā eti ce opāsātraividhyād āśritatvād iha tadyogāt yady apy adhyātmasaṃbadhabhūmadarśaā a parācīasya devatātmaa
upadeśaḥ tathāpi a brahmavākyaṃ bhavitum arhati kutaḥ jīvaliṅgāt mukhyaprāṇaliṅgāc ca jīvasya tāvad asmi vākye vispaṣṭaṃ liṅgam upalabhyate a vācaṃ vijijñāsīta
vaktāraṃ vidyāt ityādi atra hi vāgādibhiḥ karaṇairvyāpṛtasya kāryakaraṇādhyakṣasya jīvasya vijñeyatvamabhidhīyate tathā mukhyaprāṇaliṅgamapi atha khalu prāṇa eva prajñātmedaṃ śarīraṃ parigṛhyotthāpayati iti
śarīradhāraṇaṃ ca mukhyaprāṇasya dharmaḥ prāṇasaṃvāde vāgādīprāṇāprakṛtya tāvariṣṭhaḥ prāṇa uvāca mā moham āpadyathāham evaitat pañcadhātmāaṃ pravibhajyaitad bāṇam avaṣṭabhya vidhārayāmi iti śravaṇāt
ye tu imaṃ śarīraṃ parigṛhya iti paṭhati teṣām imaṃ jīvamidriyagrāmaṃ vā parigṛhya śarīramutthāpayatīti vyākhyeyam prajñātmatvam api jīve tāvac cetaatvād upapaam
mukhye pi prāṇe prajñāsādhaaprāṇātarāśrayatvād upapaam eva evaṃ jīvamukhyaprāṇaparigrahe ca prāṇaprajñātmaoḥ sahavṛttitveābhedairdeśaḥ svarūpeṇa ca bhedarideśaḥ ity ubhayathāpi irdeśa upapadyate yo vai
prāṇaḥ sā prajñā yā vai prajñā sa prāṇaḥ saha hy etāvasmiñ śarīre vasataḥ sahotkrāmataḥ iti brahmaparigrahe tu kiṃ kasmād bhidyeta
tasmād iha jīvamukhyaprāṇayor ayatara ubhau vā pratīyeyātāṃ a brahmeti cet aitad evam upāsātraividhyāt evaṃ sati trividham upāsaaṃ prasajyeta jīvopāsaaṃ mukhyaprāṇopāsaaṃ
brahmopāsaaṃ ceti a caitadekasmivākyebhyupagatuṃ yuktam upakramopasaṃhārābhyāṃ hi vākyaikavākyatvamavagamyate mām eva vijāīhi ity upakramya prāṇosmi prajñātmā taṃ mām āyur amṛtam ity
upāssva ity uktvā ate sa eṣa prāṇa eva prajñātmāadojaromṛtaḥ ity ekarūpāv upakramopasaṃhārau dṛśyete tatrārthaikatvaṃ yuktam āśrayitum a ca brahmaliṅgamayaparatvea pariṇetuṃ
śakyam daśāāṃ bhūtamātrāṇāṃ prajñāmātrāṇāṃ ca brahmaṇoyatra arpaṇāupapatteḥ āśritatvācca ayatrāpi brahmaliṅgavaśātprāṇaśabdasya brahmaṇi pravṛtteḥ ihāpi ca hitatamopayāsādibrahmaliṅgayogāt brahmopadeśa evāyamiti gamyate yattu mukhyaprāṇaliṅgaṃ
darśitam idaṃ śarīraṃ parigṛhyotthāpayati iti tadasat prāṇavyāpārasyāpi paramātmāyattatvātparamātmayupacarituṃ śakyatvāt a prāṇea āpāea martyo jīvati kaścaa itareṇa tu jīvati yasmietāvupāśritau iti
śruteḥ yadapi a vācaṃ vijijñāsīta vaktāraṃ vidyāt ityādi jīvaliṅgaṃ darśitam tadapi a brahmapakṣaṃ ivārayati a hi jīvo āmātyatabhio brahmaṇaḥ tattvamasi
ahaṃ brahmāsmi ityādiśrutibhyaḥ buddhyādyupādhikṛtaṃ tu viśeṣamāśritya brahmaiva sa jīvaḥ kartā bhoktā cetyucyate tasyopādhikṛtaviśeṣaparityāgea svarūpaṃ brahma darśayitum a vācaṃ vijijñāsīta vaktāraṃ
vidyāt ityādiā pratyagātmābhimukhīkaraṇārtha upadeśo a virudhyate yadvācāabhyuditaṃ yea vāgabhyudyate tadeva brahma tvaṃ viddhi edaṃ yadidamupāsate ityādi ca śrutyataraṃ vacaādikriyāvyāpṛtasyaivātmao brahmatvaṃ
darśayati yat puar etad uktam saha hy etāvasmiñ śarīre vasataḥ sahotkrāmataḥ iti prāṇaprajñātmaor bhedadarśaaṃ brahmavādio opapadyata iti aiṣa doṣaḥ jñāakriyāśaktidvayāśrayayor
buddhiprāṇayoḥ pratyagātmopādhibhūtayor bhedairdeśopapatteḥ upādhidvayopahitasya tu pratyagātmaaḥ svarūpeṇābheda ityataḥ prāṇa eva prajñātmā ityekīkaraṇamaviruddham athavā opāsātraividhyādāśritatvādiha tadyogāt ityasyāyamayorthaḥ a brahmavākyepi jīvamukhyaprāṇaliṅgaṃ virudhyate
katham upāsātraividhyāt trividhamiha brahmaṇa upāsaaṃ vivakṣitam prāṇadharmeṇa prajñādharmeṇa svadharmeṇa ca tatra āyuramṛtamityupāssvāyuḥ prāṇaḥ iti idaṃ śarīraṃ parigṛhyotthāpayati iti tasmādetadevokthamupāsīta iti
ca prāṇadharmaḥ atha yathāsyai prajñāyai sarvāṇi bhūtāyekībhavati tadvyākhyāsyāmaḥ ityupakramya vāgevāsyā ekamaṅgamadūduhattasyai āma parastātprativihitā bhūtamātrā prajñayā vācaṃ samāruhya vācā sarvāṇi āmāyāpoti
ityādiḥ prajñādharmaḥ tā vā etā daśaiva bhūtamātrā adhiprajñaṃ daśa prajñāmātrā adhibhūtam yadi bhūtamātrā a syura prajñāmātrāḥ syuḥ yadi prajñāmātrā a
syura bhūtamātrāḥ syuḥ a hyayatarato rūpaṃ kiṃcaa sidhyet o etaāā tadyathā rathasyāreṣu emirarpitā ābhāvarā arpitā evamevaitā bhūtamātrāḥ prajñāmātrāsvarpitāḥ prajñāmātrāḥ prāṇerpitāḥ
sa eṣa prāṇa eva prajñātmā ityādirbrahmadharmaḥ tasmādbrahmaṇa evaitadupādhidvayadharmeṇa svadharmeṇa caikamupāsaaṃ trividhaṃ vivakṣitam ayatrāpi maomayaḥ prāṇaśarīraḥ ityādāvupādhidharmeṇa brahmaṇa upāsaamāśritam ihāpi tadyujyate
vākyasyopakramopasaṃhārābhyāmekārthatvāvagamāt prāṇaprajñātmabrahmaliṅgāvagamācca tasmādbrahmavākyamevaitaditi siddham iti śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācāryasya śrīgovidabhagavatpūjyapādaśiṣyasya śrīmacchaṃkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīrakamīmāṃsāsūtrabhāṣye prathamādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ murat prathamodhyāyaḥ dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ sarvatra prasiddhopadeśāt sarvatraprasiddhyadhikaraṇam
idamāmāyate sarvaṃ khalvidaṃ brahma tajjalāiti śāta upāsīta atha khalu kratumayaḥ puruṣo yathākraturasimalloke puruṣo bhavati tathetaḥ pretya bhavati sa kratuṃ kurvīta
maomayaḥ prāṇaśarīraḥ ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kimiha maomayatvādibhirdharmaiḥ śārīra ātmopāsyatveopadiśyate āhosvitparaṃ brahmeti kiṃ tāvatprāptam śārīra iti kutaḥ tasya hi kāryakaraṇādhipateḥ prasiddho
maaādibhiḥ saṃbadhaḥ a parasya brahmaṇaḥ aprāṇo hyamaāḥ śubhraḥ ityādiśrutibhyaḥ au sarvaṃ khalvidaṃ brahma iti svaśabdeaiva brahmopāttam kathamiha śārīra ātmopāsyatveāśaṅkyate aiṣa
doṣaḥ edaṃ vākyaṃ brahmopāsaavidhiparam kiṃ tarhi śamavidhiparam yatkāraṇam sarvaṃ khalvidaṃ brahma tajjalāiti śāta upāsīta ityāha etaduktaṃ bhavati yasmātsarvamidaṃ vikārajātaṃ brahmaiva
tajjatvāt tallatvāt tadaatvācca a ca sarvasyaikātmatve rāgādayaḥ saṃbhavati tasmāt śāta upāsīteti a ca śamavidhiparatve satyaea vākyea brahmopāsaaṃ iyatuṃ śakyate upāsaaṃ
tu sa kratuṃ kurvīta ityaea vidhīyate kratuḥ saṃkalpo dhyāamityarthaḥ tasya ca viṣayatvea śrūyate maomayaḥ prāṇaśarīraḥ iti jīvaliṅgam ato brūmaḥ jīvaviṣayametadupāsaamiti
sarvakarmā sarvakāmaḥ ityādyapi śrūyamāṇaṃ paryāyeṇa jīvaviṣayamupapadyate eṣa ma ātmātarhṛdayeṇīyāvrīhervā yavādvā iti ca hṛdayāyataatvamaṇīyastvaṃ cārāgramātrasya jīvasyāvakalpate āparicchiasya brahmaṇaḥ au jyāyāpṛthivyāḥ ityādyapi
a paricchievakalpata iti atra brūmaḥ a tāvadaṇīyastvaṃ jyāyastvaṃ cobhayamekasmisamāśrayituṃ śakyam virodhāt ayatarāśrayaṇe ca prathamaśrutatvādaṇīyastvaṃ yuktamāśrayitum jyāyastvaṃ tu brahmabhāvāpekṣayā bhaviṣyatīti iścite
ca jīvaviṣayatve yadate brahmasaṃkīrtaam etadbrahma iti tadapi prakṛtaparāmarśārthatvājjīvaviṣayameva tasmāmaomayatvādibhirdharmairjīva upāsya ityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ parameva brahmeha maomayatvādibhirdharmairupāsyam kutaḥ sarvatra prasiddhopadeśāt yatsarveṣu
vedāteṣu prasiddhaṃ brahmaśabdasyālambaaṃ jagatkāraṇam iha ca sarvaṃ khalvidaṃ brahma iti vākyopakrame śrutam tadeva maomayatvādidharmairviśiṣṭamupadiśyata iti yuktam evaṃ ca sati prakṛtahāāprakṛtaprakriye
a bhaviṣyataḥ au vākyopakrame śamavidhivivakṣayā brahma irdiṣṭaṃ a svavivakṣayetyuktam atrocyate yadyapi śamavidhivivakṣayā brahma irdiṣṭam tathāpi maomayatvādiṣūpadiśyamāeṣu tadeva brahma saṃihitaṃ bhavati
jīvastu a saṃihitaḥ a ca svaśabdeopātta iti vaiṣamyam vivakṣitaguṇopapatteśca vaktumiṣṭā vivakṣitāḥ yadyapyapauruṣeye vede vakturabhāvāt ecchārthaḥ saṃbhavati tathāpyupādāea phaleopacaryate lokepi yacchabdābhihitamupādeyaṃ
bhavati tadvivakṣitamityucyate yadaupādeyaṃ tadavivakṣitamiti tadvadvedepyupādeyatveābhihitaṃ vivakṣitaṃ bhavati itaradavivakṣitam upādāāupādāe tu vedavākyatātparyātātparyābhyāmavagamyete tadiha ye vivakṣitā guṇā upāsaāyāmupādeyatveopadiṣṭāḥ satyasaṃkalpaprabhṛtayaḥ te parasmibrahmaṇyupapadyate satyasaṃkalpatvaṃ
hi sṛṣṭisthitisaṃhāreṣvapratibaddhaśaktitvātparamātmaa evāvakalpate paramātmaguṇatvea ca ya ātmāpahatapāpmā ityatra satyakāmaḥ satyasaṃkalpaḥ iti śrutam ākāśātmā iti ca ākāśavad ātmā asyety arthaḥ sarvagatatvādibhir
dharmaiḥ saṃbhavaty ākāśea sāmyaṃ brahmaṇaḥ jyāyāpṛthivyāḥ ityādiā caitad eva darśayati yad api ākāśa ātmā asyeti vyākhyāyate tad api saṃbhavati sarvajagatkāraṇasya
sarvātmao brahmaṇa ākāśātmatvam ata eva sarvakarmā ityādi evam ihopāsyatayā vivakṣitā guṇā brahmaṇy upapadyate yat tūktam maomayaḥ prāṇaśarīraḥ iti jīvaliṅgam a
tad brahmaṇy upapadyata iti tad api brahmaṇy upapadyata iti brūmaḥ sarvātmatvād dhi brahmaṇo jīvasaṃbadhīi maomayatvādīi brahmasaṃbadhīi bhavati tathā ca brahmaviṣaye
śrutismṛtī bhavataḥ tvaṃ strī tvaṃ pumāasi tvaṃ kumāra uta vā kumārī tvaṃ jīrṇo daṇḍea vañcasi tvaṃ jāto bhavasi viśvatomukhaḥ iti
sarvataḥpāṇipādaṃ tatsarvatokṣiśiromukham sarvataḥśrutimalloke sarvamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati iti ca aprāṇo hyamaāḥ śubhraḥ iti śrutiḥ śuddhabrahmaviṣayā iyaṃ tu śrutiḥ maomayaḥ prāṇaśarīraḥ iti saguṇabrahmaviṣayeti
viśeṣaḥ ato vivakṣitaguṇopapatteḥ parameva brahma ihopāsyatveopadiṣṭamiti gamyate aupapattestu a śārīraḥ pūrveṇa sūtreṇa brahmaṇi vivakṣitāāṃ guṇāāmupapattiruktā aea śārīre teṣāmaupapattirucyate tuśabdovadhāraṇārthaḥ brahmaivoktea
yāyea maomayatvādiguṇam a tu śārīro jīvo maomayatvādiguṇaḥ yatkāraṇam satyasaṃkalpaḥ ākāśātmā avākī aādaraḥ jyāyāpṛthivyāḥ iti caivaṃjātīyakā guṇā a śārīre āñjasyeopapadyate śārīra
iti śarīre bhava ityarthaḥ avīśvaropi śarīre bhavati satyam śarīre bhavati a tu śarīra eva bhavati jyāyāpṛthivyā jyāyāatarikṣāt ākāśavat sarvagataśca ityaḥ
iti ca vyāpitvaśravaṇāt jīvas tu śarīra eva bhavati tasya bhogādhiṣṭhāāc charīrād ayatra vṛttyabhāvāt karmakartṛvyapadeśācca itaśca a śārīro maomayatvādiguṇaḥ yasmātkarmakartṛvyapadeśo bhavati
etamitaḥ pretyābhisaṃbhavitāsmi iti etamiti prakṛtaṃ maomayatvādiguṇamupāsyamātmāaṃ karmatvea prāpyatvea vyapadiśati abhisaṃbhavitāsmīti śārīramupāsakaṃ kartṛtvea prāpakatvea abhisaṃbhavitāsmīti prāptāsmītyarthaḥ a ca satyāṃ gatāvekasya karmakartṛvyapadeśo
yuktaḥ tathopāsyopāsakabhāvopi bhedādhiṣṭhāa eva tasmādapi a śārīro maomayatvādiviśiṣṭaḥ śabdaviśeṣāt itaś ca śārīrād ayo maomayatvādiguṇaḥ yasmāc chabdaviśeṣo bhavati samāaprakaraṇe śrutyatare yathā
vrīhir vā yavo vā śyāmāko vā śyāmākataṇḍulo vaivamayamatarātmapuruṣo hiraṇmayaḥ iti śārīrasyātmao yaḥ śabdobhidhāyakaḥ saptamyataḥ atarātmaiti tasmādviśiṣṭoyaḥ prathamātaḥ puruṣaśabdo maomayatvādiviśiṣṭasyātmaobhidhāyakaḥ tasmāttayorbhedodhigamyate
smṛteś ca smṛtiśca śārīraparamātmaorbhedaṃ darśayati īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtāāṃ hṛddeśerjua tiṣṭhati bhrāmayasarvabhūtāi yatrārūḍhāi māyayā ityādyā atrāha kaḥ puarayaṃ śārīro āma paramātmaoyaḥ yaḥ
pratiṣidhyate aupapattestu a śārīraḥ ityādiā śrutistu āyotosti draṣṭā āyotosti śrotā ityevaṃjātīyakā paramātmaoyamātmāaṃ vārayati tathā smṛtirapi kṣetrajñaṃ cāpi māṃ viddhi sarvakṣetreṣu
bhārata ityevaṃjātīyaketi atrocyate satyamevaitat para evātmā dehedriyamaobuddhyupādhibhiḥ paricchidyamāo bālaiḥ śārīra ityupacaryate yathā ghaṭakarakādyupādhivaśādaparicchiamapi abhaḥ paricchiavadavabhāsate tadvat tadapekṣayā ca karmakartṛtvādibhedavyavahāro a
virudhyate prāk tattvamasi ity ātmaikatvopadeśagrahaṇāt gṛhīte tv ātmaikatve badhamokṣādisarvavyavahāraparisamāptireva syāt arbhakaukastvāt tadvyapadeśāc ca eti ce a icāyyatvād evaṃ vyomavac ca
arbhakamalpam oko īḍam eṣa ma ātmātarhṛdaye iti paricchiāyataatvāt svaśabdea ca aṇīyāvrīhervā yavādvā ityaṇīyastvavyapadeśāt śārīra evārāgramātro jīva ihopadiśyate a sarvagataḥ paramātmā
iti yaduktaṃ tatparihartavyam atrocyate āyaṃ doṣaḥ a tāvatparicchiadeśasya sarvagatatvavyapadeśaḥ kathamapyupapadyate sarvagatasya tu sarvadeśeṣu vidyamāatvātparicchiadeśavyapadeśopi kayācidapekṣayā saṃbhavati yathā samastavasudhādhipatirapi hi sa
ayodhyādhipatiriti vyapadiśyate kayā puarapekṣayā sarvagataḥ saīśvarorbhakaukā aṇīyāṃśca vyapadiśyata iti icāyyatvādevamiti brūmaḥ evam aṇīyastvādiguṇagaṇopeta īśvaraḥ tatra hṛdayapuṇḍarīke icāyyo draṣṭavya upadiśyate yathā
sālagrāme hariḥ tatrāsya buddhivijñāaṃ grāhakam sarvagato pīśvaras tatropāsyamāaḥ prasīdati vyomavac caitad draṣṭavyam yathā sarvagatam api sad vyoma sūcīpāśādyapekṣayārbhakauko ṇīyaś ceti
vyapadiśyate evaṃ brahmāpi tad evaṃ icāyyatvāpekṣaṃ brahmaṇo rbhakaukastvam aṇīyastvaṃ ca a pāramārthikam tatra yad āśaṅkyate hṛdayāyataatvād brahmaṇo hṛdayāāṃ ca pratiśarīraṃ
bhiatvād bhiāyataāāṃ ca śukādīām aekatvasāvayavatvāityatvādidoṣadarśaād brahmaṇo pi tadvat prasaṅga iti tad api parihṛtaṃ bhavati sambhogaprāptir iti ce a vaiśeṣyāt vyomavat
sarvagatasya brahmaṇaḥ sarvaprāṇihṛdayasaṃbadhāt cidrūpatayā ca śārīrād aviśiṣṭatvāt sukhaduḥkhādisaṃbhogo apy aviśiṣṭaḥ prasajyeta ekatvāc ca a hi parasmād ātmao ayaḥ kaścid ātmā
saṃsārī vidyate āyo ato asti vijñātā ityādiśrutibhyaḥ tasmāt parasyaiva brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhogaprāptir iti cet a vaiśeṣyāt a tāvat sarvaprāṇihṛdayasaṃbadhāt cidrūpatayā ca
śārīravad brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhogaprasaṅgaḥ vaiśeṣyāt viśeṣo hi bhavati śārīraparameśvarayoḥ ekaḥ kartā bhoktā dharmādharmādisādhaaḥ sukhaduḥkhādimāṃś ca ekas tadviparīto apahatapāpmatvādiguṇaḥ etasmād aayor viśeṣād
ekasya bhogaḥ etarasya yadi ca saṃidhāamātreṇa vastuśaktim aāśritya kāryasaṃbadho abhyupagamyeta ākāśādīām api dāhādiprasaṅgaḥ sarvagatāekātmavādiām api samāvetau codyaparihārau yad apy ekatvād
brahmaṇa ātmātarābhāvāc chārīrasya bhogea brahmaṇo bhogaprasaṅgaḥ iti atra vadāmaḥ idaṃ tāvad devāāṃ priyaḥ praṣṭavyaḥ katham ayaṃ tvayātmātarābhāvo adhyavasita iti tattvamasi
ahaṃ brahmāsmi āyo ato asti vijñātā ityādiśāstrebhya iti cet yathāśāstraṃ tarhi śāstrīyorthaḥ pratipattavyaḥ a tatrārdhajaratīyaṃ labhyam śāstraṃ ca tattvamasi ityapahatapāpmatvādiviśeṣaṇaṃ
brahma śārīrasyātmatveopadiśacchārīrasyaiva tāvadupabhoktṛtvaṃ vārayati kutastadupabhogea brahmaṇa upabhogaprasaṅgaḥ athāgṛhītaṃ śārīrasya brahmaṇaikatvam tadā mithyājñāaimittaḥ śārīrasyopabhogaḥ a tea paramārtharūpasya brahmaṇaḥ saṃsparśaḥ a hi
bālaistalamaliatādibhirvyomi vikalpyamāe talamaliatādiviśiṣṭameva paramārthato vyoma bhavati tadāha a vaiśeṣyāditi aikatvepi śārīrasyopabhogea brahmaṇa upabhogaprasaṅgaḥ vaiśeṣyāt viśeṣo hi bhavati mithyājñāasamyagjñāayoḥ mithyājñāakalpita upabhogaḥ
samyagjñāadṛṣṭamekatvam a ca mithyājñāakalpiteopabhogea samyagjñāadṛṣṭaṃ vastu saṃspṛśyate tasmāopabhogagadhopi śakya īśvarasya kalpayitum attā carācaragrahaṇāt attradhikaraṇam kaṭhavallīṣu paṭhyate yasya brahma ca kṣatraṃ
cobhe bhavata odaaḥ mṛtyuryasyopasecaaṃ ka itthā veda yatra saḥ iti atra kaścidodaopasecaasūcitottā pratīyate tatra kimagirattā syāt uta jīvaḥ athavā paramātmā
iti saṃśayaḥ viśeṣāavadhāraṇāt trayāṇāṃ cāgijīvaparamātmaāmasmigrathe praśopayāsopalabdheḥ kiṃ tāvatprāptam agiratteti kutaḥ agiraādaḥ iti śrutiprasiddhibhyām jīvo vā attā syāt tayorayaḥ pippalaṃ svādvatti
iti darśaāt a paramātmā aaścaayobhicākaśīti iti darśaādityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ attātra paramātmā bhavitumarhati kutaḥ carācaragrahaṇāt carācaraṃ hi sthāvarajaṅgamaṃ mṛtyūpasecaamihādyatvea pratīyate tādṛśasya
cādyasya a paramātmaoyaḥ kārtsyeāttā saṃbhavati paramātmā tu vikārajātamupasaṃharasarvamattītyupapadyate aviha carācaragrahaṇaṃ opalabhyate kathaṃ siddhavaccarācaragrahaṇaṃ hetutveopādīyate aiṣa doṣaḥ mṛtyūpasecaatveehādyatvea sarvasya prāṇiikāyasya pratīyamāatvāt
brahmakṣatrayośca prādhāyātpradarśaārthatvopapatteḥ yattu paramātmaopi āttṛtvaṃ saṃbhavati aaśaayobhicākaśīti iti darśaāditi atrocyate karmaphalabhogasya pratiṣedhakametaddarśaam tasya saṃihitatvāt a vikārasaṃhārasya pratiṣedhakam sarvavedāteṣu sṛṣṭisthitisaṃhārakāraṇatvea brahmaṇaḥ
prasiddhatvāt tasmātparamātmaivehāttā bhavitumarhati prakaraṇācca itaśca paramātmaivehāttā bhavitumarhati yatkāraṇaṃ prakaraṇamidaṃ paramātmaaḥ a jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit ityādi prakṛtagrahaṇaṃ ca yāyyam ka
itthā veda yatra saḥ iti ca durvijñāatvaṃ paramātmaliṅgam guhāṃ praviṣṭāv ātmāau hi taddarśaāt guhāpraviṣṭādhikaraṇam kaṭhavallīṣv eva paṭhyate ṛtaṃ pibatau sukṛtasya

uta jīvaparamātmāām iti yadi buddhijīvau tato buddhipradhāāt kāryakaraṇasaṃghātād vilakṣaṇo jīvaḥ pratipādito bhavati tad apīha pratipādayitavyam yeyaṃ prete vicikisā mauṣyestīty eke
āyam astīti caike etadvidyām auśiṣṭas tvayāhaṃ varāṇām eṣa varas tṛtīyaḥ iti pṛṣṭatvāt atha jīvaparamātmāau tato jīvād vilakṣaṇaḥ paramātmā pratipādito bhavati
tad apīha pratipādayitavyam ayatra dharmād ayatrādharmād ayatrāsmāt kṛtākṛtāt ayatra bhūtāc ca bhavyāc ca yat tat paśyasi tadvada iti pṛṣṭatvāt atrāhākṣeptā
ubhāv apy etau pakṣau a saṃbhavataḥ kasmāt ṛtapāaṃ hi karmaphalopabhogaḥ sukṛtasya loke iti liṅgāt tac ca cetaasya kṣetrajñasya saṃbhavati ācetaāyā
buddheḥ pibatau iti dvivacaea dvayoḥ pāaṃ darśayati śrutiḥ ato buddhikṣetrajñapakṣastāvaa saṃbhavati ata eva kṣetrajñaparamātmapakṣopi a saṃbhavati cetaepi paramātmai ṛtapāāsaṃbhavāt aaśa
ayobhicākaśīti iti matravarṇād iti atrocyate aiṣa doṣaḥ chatriṇo gacchatīty ekeāpi cchatriṇā bahūām acchatriṇāṃ chatritvopacāradarśaāt evam ekeāpi pibatā dvau pibatāv ucyeyātām

iti kutaḥ guhāṃ praviṣṭau iti viśeṣaṇāt yadi śarīraṃ guhā yadi vā hṛdayam ubhayathāpi buddhikṣetrajñau guhāṃ praviṣṭāv upapadyete a ca sati
