evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ vijñāātmaparamātmāāv ihocyeyātām kasmāt ātmāau hi tāv ubhāv api cetaau samāasvabhāvau saṃkhyāśravaṇe ca samāasvabhāveṣv eva loke pratītir dṛśyate
asya gor dvitīyoveṣṭavyaḥ ity ukte gaur eva dvitīyoviṣyate āśvaḥ puruṣo vā tad iha ṛtapāea liṅgea iścite vijñāātmai dvitīyāveṣaṇāyāṃ samāasvabhāvaś cetaaḥ
paramātmaiva pratīyate aūktaṃ guhāhitatvadarśaā a paramātmā pratyetavya iti guhāhitatvadarśaād eva paramātmā pratyetavya iti vadāmaḥ guhāhitatvaṃ tu śrutismṛtiṣv asakṛtparamātmaa eva dṛśyate
guhāhitaṃ gahvareṣṭhaṃ purāṇam yo veda ihitaṃ guhāyāṃ parame vyoma ātmāam aviccha guhāṃ praviṣṭam ityādyāsu sarvagatasyāpi brahmaṇa upalabdhyartho deśaviśeṣopadeśo a virudhyata
ity etad apy uktam eva sukṛtalokavartitvaṃ tu cchatritvavad ekasmi api vartamāam ubhayor aviruddham chāyātapau ity apy aviruddham chāyātapavat parasparavilakṣaṇatvāt saṃsāritvāsaṃsāritvayoḥ
avidyākṛtatvāt saṃsāritvasya pāramārthikatvāc cāsaṃsāritvasya tasmād vijñāātmaparamātmāau guhāṃ praviṣṭau gṛhyete kutaś ca vijñāātmaparamātmāau gṛhyete viśeṣaṇācca viśeṣaṇaṃ ca vijñāātmaparamātmaoreva bhavati ātmāaṃ rathiaṃ
viddhi śarīraṃ rathameva tu ityādiā pareṇa grathea rathirathādirūpakakalpaayā vijñāātmāaṃ rathiaṃ saṃsāramokṣayorgatāraṃ kalpayati sodhvaaḥ pāramāpoti tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam iti paramātmāaṃ gatavyaṃ
kalpayati tathā taṃ durdarśaṃ gūḍhamaupraviṣṭaṃ guhāhitaṃ gahvareṣṭhaṃ purāṇam adhyātmayogādhigamea devaṃ matvā dhīro harṣaśokau jahāti iti pūrvasmiapi grathe matṛmatavyatveaitāveva viśeṣitau prakaraṇaṃ
cedaṃ paramātmaaḥ brahmavido vadati Kaṭha iti ca vaktṛviśeṣopādāaṃ paramātmaparigrahe ghaṭate tasmādiha jīvaparamātmāāvucyeyātām eṣa eva yāyaḥ dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyā ityevamādiṣvapi
tatrāpi hy adhyātmādhikārā a prākṛtau suparṇāv ucyete tayor ayaḥ pippalaṃ svādv atti ity adaaliṅgād vijñāātmā bhavati aaścaayobhicākaśīti ityaaśaacetaatvābhyāṃ paramātmā aatare
ca matre tāveva draṣṭṛdraṣṭavyabhāvea viśiaṣṭi samāe vṛkṣe puruṣo imagoīśayā śocati muhyamāaḥ juṣṭaṃ yadā paśyatyayamīśamasya mahimāamiti vītaśokaḥ iti apara āha dvā
suparṇā iti eyamṛgasyādhikaraṇasya siddhātaṃ bhajate paiṅgirahasyabrāhmaṇeāyathā vyākhyātatvāt tayorayaḥ pippalaṃ svādvattīti sattvamaaścaayobhicākaśītītyaaścaayobhipaśyati jñastāvetau sattvakṣetrajñau iti sattvaśabdo jīvaḥ kṣetrajñaśabdaḥ paramātmeti yaducyate taa
sattvakṣetrajñaśabdayorataḥkaraṇaśārīraparatayā prasiddhatvāt tatraiva ca vyākhyātatvāt tadetatsattvaṃ yea svapaṃ paśyati atha yoyaṃ śārīra upadraṣṭā sa kṣetrajñastāvetau sattvakṣetrajñau iti āpyasyādhikaraṇasya pūrvapakṣabhāvaṃ bhajate
a hyatra śārīraḥ kṣetrajñaḥ kartṛtvabhoktṛtvādiā saṃsāradharmeṇopeto vivakṣyate kathaṃ tarhi sarvasaṃsāradharmātīto brahmasvabhāvaścaitayamātrasvarūpaḥ aaścaayobhicākaśītītyaaścaayobhipaśyati jñaḥ iti vacaāt tattvamasi kṣetrajñaṃ cāpi māṃ viddhi
ityādiśrutismṛtibhyaśca tāvatā ca vidyopasaṃhāradarśaamevamevāvakalpate tāvetau sattvakṣetrajñau a ha vā evaṃvidi kiṃcaa raja ādhvaṃsate ityādi kathaṃ puarasmipakṣe tayorayaḥ pippalaṃ svādvattīti sattvam
ityacetae sattve bhoktṛtvavacaamiti ucyate eyaṃ śrutiracetaasya sattvasya bhoktṛtvaṃ vakṣyāmīti pravṛttā kiṃ tarhi cetaasya kṣetrajñasyābhoktṛtvaṃ brahmasvabhāvatāṃ ca vakṣyāmīti tadarthaṃ sukhaduḥkhādivikriyāvati sattve
bhoktṛtvamadhyāropayati idaṃ hi kartṛtvaṃ bhoktṛtvaṃ ca sattvakṣetrajñayoritaretarasvabhāvāvivekakṛtaṃ kalpyate paramārthatastu āyatarasyāpi saṃbhavati acetaatvātsattvasya avikriyatvācca kṣetrajñasya avidyāpratyupasthāpitasvabhāvatvācca sattvasya sutarāṃ a saṃbhavati tathā
ca śrutiḥ yatra vā ayadiva syāttatrāyoyatpaśyet ityādiā svapadṛṣṭahastyādivyavahāravadavidyāviṣaya eva kartṛtvādivyavahāraṃ darśayati yatra tvasya sarvamātmaivābhūttatkea kaṃ paśyet ityādiā ca vivekiaḥ kartṛtvādivyavahāraṃ
ivārayati atara upapatteḥ atarādhikaraṇam ya eṣo kṣiṇi puruṣo dṛśyata eṣa ātmeti hovācaitad amṛtam abhayam etad brahmeti tad yady apy asmi
sarpir vodakaṃ vā siñcati vartmaī eva gacchati ityādi śrūyate tatra saṃśayaḥ kim ayaṃ pratibimbātmākṣyadhikaraṇo irdiśyate atha vijñāātmā uta devatātmedriyasyādhiṣṭhātā athaveśvara
iti kiṃ tāvat prāptam chāyātmā puruṣapratirūpa iti kutaḥ tasya dṛśyamāatvaprasiddheḥ ya eṣokṣiṇi puruṣo dṛśyate iti ca prasiddhavad upadeśāt vijñāātmao vāyaṃ
irdeśa iti yuktam sa hi cakṣuṣā rūpaṃ paśyaṃś cakṣuṣi saṃihito bhavati ātmaśabdaś cāsmi pakṣe ukūlo bhavati ādityapuruṣo vā cakṣuṣo ugrāhakaḥ
pratīyate raśmibhir eṣosmi pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti śruteḥ amṛtatvādīāṃ ca devatātmay api kathaṃcit saṃbhavāt eśvaraḥ sthāaviśeṣairdeśāt ity evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ parameśvara evākṣiṇy
abhyataraḥ puruṣa ihopadiṣṭa iti kasmāt upapatteḥ upapadyate hi parameśvare guṇajātam ihopadiśyamāam ātmatvaṃ tāva mukhyayā vṛttyā parameśvare upapadyate sa ātmā tat
tvam asi iti śruteḥ amṛtatvābhayatve ca tasmi asakṛcchrūyete tathā parameśvarāurūpam etad akṣisthāam yathā hi parameśvaraḥ sarvadoṣair aliptaḥ apahatapāpmatvādiśravaṇāt tathākṣisthāaṃ sarvaleparahitam
upadiṣṭam tad yady apy asmi sarpir vodakaṃ vā siñcati vartmaī eva gacchati iti śruteḥ saṃyadvāmatvādiguṇopadeśaś ca tasmi avakalpate etaṃ saṃyadvāma
ityācakṣate etaṃ hi sarvāṇi vāmāy abhisaṃyati eṣa u eva vāmaīr eṣa hi sarvāṇi vāmāi ayati eṣa u eva bhāmaīr eṣa
hi sarveṣu lokeṣu bhāti iti ca ata upapatter ataraḥ parameśvaraḥ sthāādivyapadeśācca kathaṃ puar ākāśavat sarvagatasya brahmaṇo akṣyalpaṃ sthāam upapadyata iti
atrocyate bhaved eṣāavakḷptiḥ yady etad evaikaṃ sthāam asya irdiṣṭaṃ bhavet sati hy ayāy api pṛthivyādīi sthāāy asya irdiṣṭāi yaḥ pṛthivyāṃ
tiṣṭha ityādiā teṣu hi cakṣurapi irdiṣṭam yaś cakṣuṣi tiṣṭha iti sthāādivyapadeśādityādigrahaṇeaitaddarśayati a kevalaṃ sthāamevaikamaucitaṃ brahmaṇo irdiśyate kiṃ tarhi āma rūpamityevaṃjātīyakamapyaāmarūpasya
brahmaṇoucitaṃ irdiśyamāaṃ dṛśyate tasyoditi āma hiraṇyaśmaśruḥ ityādi irguṇamapi sadbrahma āmarūpagatairguṇaiḥ saguṇamupāsaārthaṃ tatra tatropadiśyata ityetadapyuktameva sarvagatasyāpi brahmaṇa upalabdhyarthaṃ sthāaviśeṣo a virudhyate
sālagrāma iva viṣṇorityetadapyuktameva sukhaviśiṣṭābhidhāādeva ca api ca aivātra vivaditavyam kiṃ brahmāsmivāṃkyebhidhīyate a veti sukhaviśiṣṭābhidhāādeva brahmatvaṃ siddham sukhaviśiṣṭaṃ hi brahma yadvākyopakrame
prakrātam prāṇo brahma kaṃ brahma khaṃ brahma iti tadevehābhihitam prakṛtaparigrahasya yāyyatvāt ācāryastu te gatiṃ vaktā iti ca gatimātrābhidhāapratijñāāt kathaṃ puarvākyopakrame
sukhaviśiṣṭaṃ brahma vijñāyata iti ucyate prāṇo brahma kaṃ brahma khaṃ brahma ityetadagīāṃ vacaaṃ śrutvopakosala uvāca vijāāmy ahaṃ yat prāṇo brahma
kaṃ ca khaṃ ca tu a vijāāmi iti tatredaṃ prativacaam yad vāva kaṃ tad eva khaṃ yad eva khaṃ tad
eva kam iti tatra khaṃśabdo bhūtākāśe irūḍho loke yadi tasya viśeṣaṇatvea kaṃśabdaḥ sukhavācī opādīyeta tathā sati kevale bhūtākāśe brahmaśabdo āmādiṣv
iva pratīkābhiprāyeṇa prayukta iti pratītiḥ syāt tathā kaṃśabdasya viṣayedriyasaṃparkajaite sāmaye sukhe prasiddhatvāt yadi tasya khaṃśabdo viśeṣaṇatvea opādīyeta laukikaṃ sukhaṃ brahmeti
pratītiḥ syāt itaretaraviśeṣitau tu kaṃkhaṃśabdau sukhātmakaṃ brahma gamayataḥ tatra dvitīye brahmaśabdeupādīyamāe kaṃ khaṃ brahma ityevocyamāe kaṃśabdasya viśeṣaṇatveaivopayuktatvātsukhasya guṇasyādhyeyatvaṃ syāt tamā
bhūt ityubhayoḥ kaṃkhaṃśabdayorbrahmaśabdaśirastvam kaṃ brahma khaṃ brahma iti iṣṭaṃ hi sukhasyāpi guṇasya guṇivaddhyeyatvam tadevaṃ vākyopakrame sukhaviśiṣṭaṃ brahmopadiṣṭam pratyekaṃ ca gārhapatyādayogayaḥ
svaṃ svaṃ mahimāamupadiśya eṣā somya tesmadvidyātmavidyā ca ityupasaṃharataḥ pūrvatra brahma irdiṣṭamiti jñāpayati ācāryastu te gatiṃ vaktā iti ca gatimātrābhidhāapratijñāamarthātaravivakṣāṃ vārayati
yathā puṣkarapalāśa āpo a śliṣyata evamevaṃvidi pāpaṃ karma a śliṣyate iti cākṣisthāaṃ puruṣaṃ vijāataḥ pāpmaāupaghātaṃ bruvaakṣisthāasya puruṣasya brahmatvaṃ darśayati tasmātprakṛtasyaiva
brahmaṇokṣisthāatāṃ saṃyadvāmatvādiguṇatāṃ coktvā arcirādikāṃ tadvido gatiṃ vakṣyāmītyupakramate ya eṣokṣiṇi puruṣo dṛśyata eṣa ātmeti hovāca iti śrutopaiṣatkagatyabhidhāācca itaś cākṣisthāaḥ puruṣaḥ parameśvaraḥ
yasmāc chrutopaiṣatkasya śrutarahasya vijñāasya brahmavido yā gatir devayāākhyā prasiddhā śrutau athottareṇa tapasā brahmacaryeṇa śraddhayā vidyayātmāamaviṣyādityamabhijayate etadvai prāṇāāmāyataametadamṛtamabhayametatparāyaṇametasmāa puarāvartate iti smṛtāvapi
agirjyotirahaḥ śuklaḥ ṣaṇmāsā uttarāyaṇam tatra prayātā gacchati brahma brahmavido jaāḥ BhG iti saivehākṣipuruṣavidobhidhīyamāā dṛśyate atha yadu caivāsmiñśavyaṃ kurvati yadi ca
ārciṣamevābhisaṃbhavati ityupakramya ādityāccadramasaṃ cadramaso vidyutaṃ tatpuruṣomāavaḥ sa eābrahma gamayatyeṣa devapatho brahmapatha etea pratipadyamāā imaṃ māavamāvartaṃ āvartate iti tadiha brahmavidviṣayayā prasiddhayā
gatyā akṣisthāasya brahmatvaṃ iścīyate aavasthiter asambhavāc ca etaraḥ yat puar uktaṃ chāyātmā vijñāātmā devatātmā vā syād akṣisthāa iti atrocyate a
cchāyātmādir itara iha grahaṇam arhati kasmāt aavasthiteḥ a tāvac chāyātmaaś cakṣuṣi ityam avasthāaṃ saṃbhavati yadaiva hi kaścit puruṣaś cakṣur āsīdati
tadā cakṣuṣi puruṣacchāyā dṛśyate apagate tasmi a dṛśyate ya eṣokṣiṇi puruṣaḥ iti ca śrutiḥ saṃidhāāt svacakṣuṣi dṛśyamāaṃ puruṣam upāsyatveopadiśati a
copāsaākāle cchāyākaraṃ kaṃcit puruṣaṃ cakṣuḥsamīpe saṃidhāpyopāsta iti yuktaṃ kalpayitum asyaiva śarīrasya āśam aveṣa aśyati iti śrutiś chāyātmao py aavasthitatvaṃ darśayati
asaṃbhāvac ca tasmi amṛtatvādīāṃ guṇāāṃ a cchāyātmai pratītiḥ tathā vijñāātmao pi sādhāraṇe kṛtsaśarīredriyasaṃbadhe sati a cakṣuṣy evāvasthitatvaṃ śakyaṃ vaktum brahmaṇas
tu sarvavyāpio pi dṛṣṭa upalabdhyartho hṛdayādideśaviśeṣasaṃbadhaḥ samāaś ca vijñāātmay apy amṛtatvādīāṃ guṇāām asaṃbhavaḥ yady api vijñāātmā paramātmao aya eva tathāpy
avidyākām akarmakṛtaṃ tasmi martyatvam adhyāropitaṃ bhayaṃ cety amṛtatvābhayatve opapadyete saṃyadvāmatvādayaś caitasmi aaiśvaryād aupapaā eva devatātmaas tu raśmibhir eṣo smi pratiṣṭhitaḥ
iti śruteḥ yady api cakṣuṣy avasthāaṃ syāt tathāpy ātmatvaṃ tāva a saṃbhavati parāgrūpatvāt amṛtatvādayo pi a saṃbhavati utpattipralayaśravaṇāt amaratvam api
devāāṃ cirakālāvasthāāpekṣam aiśvaryam api parameśvarāyattam a svābhāvikam bhīṣāsmād vātaḥ pavate bhīṣodeti sūryaḥ bhīṣāsmād agiś cedraś ca mṛtyur dhāvati pañcamaḥ iti
matravarṇāt tasmāt parameśvara evāyam akṣisthāaḥ pratyetavyaḥ asmiṃś ca pakṣe dṛśyate iti prasiddhavad upādāaṃ śāstrādyapekṣaṃ vidvadviṣayaṃ prarocaārtham iti vyākhyeyam ataryāmyadhidaivādiṣu taddharmavyapadeśāt
ataryāmyadhikaraṇam ya imaṃ ca lokaṃ paraṃ ca lokaṃ sarvāṇi ca bhūtāyataro yamayati ityupakramya śrūyate yaḥ pṛthivyāṃ tiṣṭhapṛthivyā ataro yaṃ pṛthivī
a veda yasya pṛthivī śarīraṃ yaḥ pṛthivīmataro yamayatyeṣa ta ātmātaryāmyamṛtaḥ ityādi atrādhidaivatamadhilokamadhivedamadhiyajñamadhibhūtamadhyātmaṃ ca kaścidataravasthito yamayitā ataryāmīti śrūyate sa kimadhidaivādyabhimāī devatātmā
kaścit kiṃ vā prāptāṇimādyaiśvaryaḥ kaścidyogī kiṃ vā paramātmā kiṃ vārthātaraṃ kiṃcita ityapūrvasaṃjñādarśaātsaṃśayaḥ kiṃ tāvaaḥ pratibhāti saṃjñāyā aprasiddhatvātsaṃjñiāpyaprasiddheārthātareṇa keacidbhavitavyamiti athavā āirūpitarūpamarthātaraṃ
kiṃcidapi śakyamastītyabhyupagatum ataryāmiśabdaścātaryamaayogea pravṛtto ātyatamaprasiddhaḥ tasmātpṛthivyādyabhimāī kaściddevotaryāmī syāt tathā ca śrūyate pṛthivyeva yasyāyataamagirloko mao jyotiḥ ityādi sa ca kāryakaraṇavattvātpṛthivyādīatastiṣṭhayamayatīti yuktaṃ
devatātmao yamayitṛtvam yogio vā kasyacitsiddhasya sarvāupraveśea yamayitṛtvaṃ syāt a tu paramātmā pratīyate akāryakaraṇatvāt ityevaṃ prāpte idamucyate yotaryāmyadhidaivādiṣu śrūyate sa paramātmaiva
syāt āya iti kutaḥ taddharmavyapadeśāt tasya hi paramātmao dharmā iha irdiśyamāā dṛśyate pṛthivyādi tāvadadhidaivādibhedabhiaṃ samastaṃ vikārajātamatastiṣṭhayamayatīti paramātmao yamayitṛtvaṃ dharma upapadyate
sarvavikārakāraṇatve sati sarvaśaktyupapatteḥ eṣa ta ātmātaryāmyamṛtaḥ iti cātmatvāmṛtatve mukhye paramātmaa upapadyete yaṃ pṛthivī a veda iti ca pṛthivīdevatāyā avijñeyamataryāmiṇaṃ bruvadevatātmaoyamataryāmiṇaṃ
darśayati pṛthivī devatā hyahamasmi pṛthivītyātmāaṃ vijāīyāt tathā adṛṣṭośrutaḥ ityādivyapadeśo rūpādivihīatvātparamātmaa upapadyata iti yattvakāryakaraṇasya paramātmao yamayitṛtvaṃ opapadyata iti aiṣa doṣaḥ yāiyacchati
tatkāryakaraṇaireva tasya kāryakaraṇavattvopapatteḥ tasyāpyayo iyatetyaavasthādoṣaśca a saṃbhavati bhedābhāvāt bhede hi satyaavasthādoṣopapattiḥ tasmātparamātmaivātaryāmī a ca smārtamataddharmābhilāpāt syādetat adṛṣṭatvādayo dharmāḥ sāṃkhyasmṛtikalpitasya pradhāasyāpyupapadyate
rūpādihīatayā tasya tairabhyupagamāt apratarkyamavijñeyaṃ prasuptamiva sarvataḥ iti hi smarati tasyāpi iyatṛtvaṃ sarvavikārakāraṇatvādupapadyate tasmātpradhāamataryāmiśabdaṃ syāt īkṣaterāśabdam ityatra irākṛtamapi sat pradhāamihādṛṣṭatvādivyapadeśasaṃbhavea puarāśaṅkyate
ata uttaramucyate a ca smārtaṃ pradhāamataryāmiśabdaṃ bhavitumarhati kasmāt ataddharmābhilāpāt yadyapyadṛṣṭatvādivyapadeśaḥ pradhāasya saṃbhavati tathāpi a draṣṭṛtvādivyapadeśaḥ saṃbhavati pradhāasyācetaatvea tairabhyupagamāt adṛṣṭo draṣṭāśrutaḥ
śrotāmato matāvijñāto vijñātā iti hi vākyaśeṣa iha bhavati ātmatvamapi a pradhāasyopapadyate yadi pradhāamātmatvadraṣṭṛtvādyasaṃbhavāātaryāmyabhyupagamyate śārīrastarhyataryāmī bhavatu śārīro hi cetaatvāddraṣṭā śrotā matā
vijñātā ca bhavati ātmā ca pratyaktvāt amṛtaśca dharmādharmaphalopabhogopapatteḥ adṛṣṭatvādayaśca dharmāḥ śārīre suprasiddhāḥ darśaādikriyāyāḥ kartari pravṛttivirodhāt a dṛṣṭerdraṣṭāraṃ paśyeḥ ityādiśrutibhyaśca tasya
ca kāryakaraṇasaṃghātamataryamayituṃ śīlam bhoktṛtvāt tasmācchārīrotaryāmītyata uttaraṃ paṭhati śārīraścobhayepi hi bhedeaiamadhīyate eti pūrvasūtrādauvartate śārīraśca ātaryāmī syāt kasmāt yadyapi draṣṭṛtvādayo dharmāstasya saṃbhavati
tathāpi ghaṭākāśavadupādhiparicchiatvāa kārtsyea pṛthivyādiṣvataravasthātuṃ iyatuṃ ca śakoti api cobhayepi hi śākhiaḥ kāṇvā mādhyaṃdiāścātaryāmiṇo bhedeaiaṃ śārīraṃ pṛthivyādivadadhiṣṭhāatvea iyamyatvea cādhīyate yo vijñāe
tiṣṭha iti kāṇvāḥ ya ātmai tiṣṭha iti mādhyaṃdiāḥ ya ātmai tiṣṭha ityasmiṃstāvat pāṭhe bhavatyātmaśabdaḥ śārīrasya vācakaḥ yo vijñāe tiṣṭha ityasmiapi
pāṭhe vijñāaśabdea śārīra ucyate vijñāamayo hi śārīra iti tasmācchārīrādaya īśvarotaryāmīti siddham kathaṃ puarekasmidehe dvau draṣṭārāvupapadyete yaścāyamīśvarotaryāmī yaścāyamitaraḥ śārīraḥ kā puarihāupapattiḥ

a pāramārthikaḥ eko hi pratyagātmā bhavati a dvau pratyagātmāau saṃbhavataḥ ekasyaiva tu bhedavyavahāra upādhikṛtaḥ yathā ghaṭākāśo mahākāśa iti tataśca jñātṛjñeyādibhedaśrutayaḥ

pṛthivīpratiṣṭhitatvātam yaccādhyātmaṃ prasiddhaṃ mūrdhatvādi cubukapratiṣṭhitatvātam tatparigṛhyate ata eva a devatā bhūtaṃ ca yat puar uktaṃ bhūtāger api matravarṇe dyulokādisaṃbadhadarśsaā mūrdhaiva
sutejā ityādyavayavakalpaaṃ tasyaiva bhaviṣyatīti taccharīrāyā devatāyā vaiśvaryayogād iti tat parihartavyam atorcyateata evoktebhyo hetubhyo a devatā vaiśvāaraḥ tathā bhūtāgir api a
vaiśvāaraḥ a hi bhūtāger auṣṇyaprakāśamātrātmakasya dyumūrdhatvādikalpaopapadyate vikārasya vikārātarātmatvāsaṃbhavāt tathā devatāyāḥ saty apy aiśvaryayoge a dyumūrdhatvādikalpaā smbhavati akāraṇatvāt parameśvarādhīaiśvaryatvāc ca ātmaśabdasaṃbhavaś
ca sarveṣv pakṣeṣu sthita eva sākṣādapyavirodhaṃ jaimiiḥ pūrvaṃ jāṭharāgipratīko jāṭharāgyupādhiko vā parameśvara upāsya ityuktam ataḥpratiṣṭhitatvādyaurodhea idāīṃ tu viaiva pratīkopādhikalpaābhyāṃ sākṣādapi
parameśvaropāsaaparigrahe a kaścidvirodha iti jaimiirācāryo mayate au jāṭharāgyaparigrahetaḥpratiṣṭhitatvavacaaṃ śabdādīi ca kāraṇāi virudhyeraiti atrocyate ataḥpratiṣṭhitatvavacaaṃ tāvaa virudhyate a hīha puruṣavidhaṃ puruṣetaḥ
pratiṣṭhitaṃ veda iti jāṭharāgyabhiprāyeṇedamucyate tasyāprakṛtatvādasaṃśabditatvācca kathaṃ tarhi yatprakṛtaṃ mūrdhādicubukāteṣu puruṣāvayaveṣu puruṣavidhatvaṃ kalpitam tadabhiprāyeṇedamucyate puruṣavidhaṃ puruṣetaḥ pratiṣṭhitaṃ veda iti yathā vṛkṣe
śākhāṃ pratiṣṭhitāṃ paśyatīti tadvat athavā yaḥ prakṛtaḥ paramātmādhyātmamadhidaivataṃ ca puruṣavidhatvopādhiḥ tasya yatkevalaṃ sākṣirūpam tadabhiprāyeṇedamucyate puruṣavidhaṃ puruṣetaḥ pratiṣṭhitaṃ veda iti iścite
ca pūrvāparālocaavaśea paramātmaparigrahe tadviṣaya eva vaiśvāaraśabdaḥ keacidyogea vartiṣyate viśvaścāyaṃ araśceti viśveṣāṃ vāyaṃ araḥ viśve vā arā asyeti viśvāaraḥ paramātmā sarvātmatvāt
viśvāara eva vaiśvāaraḥ taddhitoayārthaḥ rākṣasavāyasādivat agiśabdopyagraṇītvādiyogāśrayaṇea paramātmaviṣaya eva bhaviṣyati gārhapatyādikalpaaṃ prāṇāhutyadhikaraṇatvaṃ ca paramātmaopi sarvātmatvādupapadyate kathaṃ puaḥ parameśvaraparigrahe prādeśamātraśrutir upapadyata iti
tāṃ vyākhyātum ārabhate abhivyakter ity āśmarathyaḥ atimātrasyāpi parameśvarasya prādeśamātratvamabhivyaktiimittaṃ syāt abhivyajyate kila prādeśamātraparimāṇaḥ parameśvara upāsakāāṃ kṛte pradeśaviśeṣeṣu vā hṛdayādiṣūpalabdhisthāeṣu viśeṣeṇābhivyajyate
ataḥ parameśvarepi prādeśamātraśrutirabhivyakterupapadyata ity āśmarathya ācāryo mayate ausmṛter bādariḥ prādeśamātrahṛdayapratiṣṭhitea vāyaṃ maasāusmaryate tea prādeśamātraḥ ity ucyate yathā prasthamitā yavāḥ prasthā
ity ucyate tadvat yady api ca yaveṣu svagatam eva parimāṇaṃ prasthasaṃbadhād vyajyate a ceha parameśvaragataṃ kiṃcit parimāṇam asti yad dhṛdayasaṃbadhād
vyajyeta tathāpi prayuktāyāḥ prādeśamātraśruteḥ saṃbhavati yathā kathaṃcid ausmaraṇam ālambaam ity ucyate prādeśamātratvea vāyam aprādeśamātro py ausmaraṇīyaḥ prādeśamātraśrutyarthavattāyai evam ausmṛtiimittā parameśvare
prādeśamātraśrutir iti bādarir ācāryo mayate āmaati caiam asmi ātmaati caiaṃ parameśvaram asmi mūrdhacubukātarāle jābālāḥ ya eṣo ato vyakta ātmā so
vimukte pratiṣṭhita iti so vimuktaḥ kasmi pratiṣṭhita iti varaṇāyāṃ āsyāṃ ca madhye pratiṣṭhita iti kā vai varaṇā kā ca āsīti
tatra cemām eva āsikām sarvāṇīdriyakṛtāi pāpāi vārayatīti sā varaṇā sarvāṇīdriyakṛtāi pāpāi āśayatīti sā āsī iti varaṇāāsīti irucya puar apy āmaati
katamac cāsya sthāaṃ bhavatīti bhruvor ghrāṇasya ca yaḥ saṃdhiḥ sa eṣa dyulokasya parasya ca saṃdhir bhavati iti tasmād upapaā parameśvare
prādeśamātraśrutiḥ abhivimāaśrutiḥ pratyagātmatvābhiprāyā pratyagātmatayā sarvaiḥ prāṇibhirabhivimīyata ityabhivimāaḥ abhigato vāyaṃ pratyagātmatvāt vimāaś ca māaviyogāt ity abhivimāaḥ abhivimimīte vā sarvaṃ jagat kāraṇatvād
ity abhivimāaḥ tasmāt parameśvaro vaiśvāara iti siddham iti śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācāryasya śrīgovidabhagavatpūjyapādaśiṣyasya śrīmacchaṃkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīrakamīmāṃsāsūtrabhāṣye prathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ murat prathamodhyāyaḥ tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ
dyubhvādyāyataaṃ svaśabdāt dyubhvādyadhikaraṇam idaṃ śrūyate yasmidyauḥ pṛthivī cātarikṣamotaṃ maaḥ saha prāṇaiśca sarvaiḥ tamevaikaṃ jāatha ātmāamayā vāco vimuñcathāmṛtasyaiṣa setuḥ iti atra
yadetaddyuprabhṛtīāmotatvavacaādāyataaṃ kiṃcidavagamyate tatkiṃ paraṃ brahma syāt āhosvidarthātaramiti saṃdihyate tatrārthātaraṃ kimapyāyataaṃ syāditi prāptam kasmāt amṛtasyaiṣa setuḥ iti śravaṇāt pāravāhi loke setuḥ
prakhyātaḥ a ca parasya brahmaṇaḥ pāravattvaṃ śakyamabhyupagatum aatamapāram iti śravaṇāt arthātare cāyatae parigṛhyamāṇe smṛtiprasiddhaṃ pradhāaṃ parigrahītavyam tasya kāraṇatvādāyataatvopapatteḥ śrutiprasiddho vā
vāyuḥ syāt vāyurvāva gautama tatsūtraṃ vāyuā vai gautama sūtreṇāyaṃ ca lokaḥ paraśca lokaḥ sarvāṇi ca bhūtāi saṃdṛbdhāi bhavati iti vāyorapi
vidhāraṇatvaśravaṇāt śārīro vā syāt tasyāpi bhoktṛtvāt bhogyaṃ prapañcaṃ pratyāyataatvopapatteḥ ityevaṃ prāpte idamāha dyubhvādyāyataamiti dyauśca bhūśca dyubhuvau dyubhuvau ādī yasya tadidaṃ
dyubhvādi yadetadasmivākye dyauḥ pṛthivyatarikṣaṃ maaḥ prāṇā ityevamātmakaṃ jagat otatvea irdiṣṭam tasyāyataaṃ paraṃ brahma bhavitumarhati kutaḥ svaśabdāt ātmaśabdādityarthaḥ ātmaśabdo hīha bhavati
tamevaikaṃ jāatha ātmāam iti ātmaśabdaśca paramātmaparigrahe samyagavakalpate ārthātaraparigrahe kvacicca svaśabdeaiva brahmaṇa āyataatva śrūyate samūlāḥ somyemāḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ sadāyataāḥ satpratiṣṭhāḥ iti
svaśabdeaiva ceha purastādupariṣṭācca brahma saṃkīrtyate puruṣa evedaṃ viśvaṃ karma tapo brahma parāmṛtam iti brahmaivedamamṛtaṃ purastādbrahma paścādbrahma dakṣiṇataścottareṇa iti ca tatra
tvāyataāyataavadbhāvaśravaṇāt sarvaṃ brahmeti ca sāmāādhikaraṇyāt yathā hyaekātmako vṛkṣaḥ śākhā skadho mūlaṃ ceti evaṃ āāraso vicitra ātmetyāśaṅkā saṃbhavati tāṃ ivartayituṃ sāvadhāraṇamāha
tamevaikaṃ jāatha ātmāam iti etaduktaṃ bhavati a kāryaprapañcaviśiṣṭo vicitra ātmā vijñeyaḥ kiṃ tarhi avidyākṛtaṃ kāryaprapañcaṃ vidyayā pravilāpayataḥ tamevaikamāyataabhūtamātmāaṃ jāatha ekarasamiti
yathā yasmiāste devadattastadāaya ityukte āsaamevāayati a devadattam tadvadāyataabhūtasyaivaikarasasyātmao vijñeyatvamupadiśyate vikārāṛtābhisaṃdhasya cāpavādaḥ śrūyate mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyumāpoti ya iha āeva paśyati iti
sarvaṃ brahma iti tu sāmāādhikaraṇyaṃ prapañcavilāpaārtham a aekarasatāpratipādaārtham sa yathā saidhavaghaoatarobāhyaḥ kṛtso rasaghaa evaivaṃ vā areyamātmāatarobāhyaḥ kṛtsaḥ prajñāaghaa eva ityekarasatāśravaṇāt
tasmāddyubhvādyāyataaṃ paraṃ brahma yattūktam setuśruteḥ setośca pāravattvopapatteḥ brahmaṇorthātareṇa dyubhvādyāyataea bhavitavyamiti atrocyate vidhāraṇatvamātrameva setuśrutyā vivakṣyate a pāravattvādi a hi mṛddārumayo loke
seturdṛṣṭa ityatrāpi mṛddārumaya eva seturabhyupagamyate setuśabdārthopi vidhāraṇatvamātrameva a pāravattvādi ṣiño badhaakarmaṇaḥ setuśabdavyutpatteḥ apara āha tamevaikaṃ jāatha ātmāam iti yadetatsaṃkīrtitamātmajñāam yaccaitat
ayā vāco vimuñcatha iti vāgvimocaam tat atra amṛtatvasādhaatvāt amṛtasyaiṣa setuḥ iti setuśrutyā saṃkīrtyate a tu dyubhvādyāyataam tatra yaduktam setuśruterbrahmaṇorthātareṇa dyubhvādyāyataea
bhavitavyamiti etadayuktam muktopasṛpyavyapadeśāt itaśca parameva brahma dyubhvādyāyataam yasmāmuktopasṛpyatāsya vyapadiśyamāā dṛśyate muktairupasṛpyaṃ muktopasṛpyam dehādiṣvaātmasu ahamasmītyātmabuddhiravidyā tatastatpūjaādau rāgaḥ tatparibhavādau ca dveṣaḥ taducchedadarśaādbhayaṃ
mohaśca ityevamayamaatabhedoarthavrātaḥ saṃtataḥ sarveṣāṃ aḥ pratyakṣaḥ tadviparyayeṇāvidyārāgadveṣādidoṣamuktairupasṛpyamupagamyametaditi dyubhvādyāyataaṃ prakṛtya vyapadeśo bhavati katham bhidyate hṛdayagrathiśchidyate sarvasaṃśayāḥ kṣīyate cāsya karmāṇi tasmidṛṣṭe parāvare
ityuktvā bravīti tathā vidvāāmarūpādvimuktaḥ parātparaṃ puruṣamupaiti divyam iti brahmaṇaśca muktopasṛpyatvaṃ prasiddhaṃ śāstre yadā sarve pramucyate kāmā yesya hṛdi śritāḥ atha
martyomṛto bhavatyatra brahma samaśute ityevamādau pradhāādīāṃ tu a kvacimuktopasṛpyatvamasti prasiddham api ca tamevaikaṃ jāatha ātmāamayā vāco vimuñcathāmṛtasyaiṣa setuḥ iti vāgvimokapūrvakaṃ
vijñeyatvamiha dyubhvādyāyataasyocyate tacca śrutyatare brahmaṇo dṛṣṭam tameva dhīro vijñāya prajñāṃ kurvīta brāhmaṇaḥ āudhyāyādbahūñśabdāvāco viglāpaaṃ hi tat iti tasmādapi dyubhvādyāyataaṃ paraṃ
brahma āumāamatacchabdāt yathā brahmaṇaḥ pratipādako vaiśeṣiko heturuktaḥ aivamarthātarasya vaiśeṣiko hetuḥ pratipādakostītyāha āumāaṃ sāṃkhyasmṛtiparikalpitaṃ pradhāam iha dyubhvādyāyataatvea pratipattavyam kasmāt atacchabdāt tasyācetaasya
pradhāasya pratipādakaḥ śabdaḥ tacchabdaḥ a tacchabdaḥ atacchabdaḥ a hyatrācetaasya pradhāasya pratipādakaḥ kaścicchabdosti yeācetaaṃ pradhāaṃ kāraṇatveāyataatvea vāvagamyeta tadviparītasya cetaasya pratipādakaśabdotrāsti yaḥ
sarvajñaḥ sarvavit ityādiḥ ata eva a vāyurapīha dyubhvādyāyataatveāśrīyate prāṇabhṛcca yady api prāṇabhṛto vijñāātmaa ātmatvaṃ cetaatvaṃ ca saṃbhavati tathāpy upādhiparicchiajñāasya sarvajñatvādyasaṃbhave
sati asmādevātacchabdāt prāṇabhṛd api a dyubhvādyāyataatveāśrayitavyaḥ a copādhiparicchiasyāvibhoḥ prāṇabhṛto dyubhvādyāyataatvam api samyaksaṃbhavati pṛthagyogakaraṇam uttarārtham kutaśca a prāṇabhṛt dyubhvādyāyataatveāśrayitavyaḥ bhedavyapadeśāt bhedavyapadeśaśceha
bhavati tamevaikaṃ jāatha ātmāam iti jñeyajñātṛbhāvea tatra prāṇabhṛt tāvamumukṣutvājjñātā pariśeṣādātmaśabdavācyaṃ brahma jñeyaṃ dyubhvādyāyataamiti gamyate a prāṇabhṛt kutaśca a prāṇabhṛt dyubhvādyāyataatveāśrayitavyaḥ
prakaraṇāt prakaraṇaṃ cedaṃ paramātmaaḥ kasmiu bhagavo vijñāte sarvamidaṃ vijñātaṃ bhavati ityekavijñāea sarvavijñāāpekṣaṇāt paramātmai hi sarvātmake vijñāte sarvamidaṃ vijñātaṃ syāt a
kevale prāṇabhṛti kutaśca a prāṇabhṛt dyubhvādyāyataatveāśrayitavyaḥ sthityadaābhyāṃ ca dyubhvādyāyataaṃ ca prakṛtya dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyā ityatra sthityadae irdiśyete tayorayaḥ pippalaṃ
svādvatti iti karmaphalāśaam aaścaayobhicākaśīti ityaudāsīyeāvasthāam tābhyāṃ ca sthityadaābhyāmīśvarakṣetrajñau tatra gṛhyete yadi ca īśvaro dyubhvādyāyataatvea vivakṣitaḥ tatastasya prakṛtasyeśvarasya kṣetrajñātpṛthagvacaamavakalpate ayathā hyaprakṛtavacaamākasmikamasaṃbaddhaṃ
syāt au tavāpi kṣetrajñasyeśvarātpṛthagvacaamākasmikameva prasajyeta a tasyāvivakṣitatvāt kṣetrajño hi kartṛtvea bhoktṛtvea ca pratiśarīraṃ buddhyādyupādhisaṃbaddhaḥ lokata eva prasiddhaḥ āsau śrutyā tātparyeṇa
vivakṣyate īśvarastu lokatoprasiddhatvācchrutyā tātparyeṇa vivakṣyata iti a tasyākasmikaṃ vacaaṃ yuktam guhāṃ praviṣṭāvātmāau hi ityatrāpyetaddarśitam dvā suparṇā ityasyāmṛci īśvarakṣetrajñāvucyete iti yadāpi
paiṅgyupaiṣatkṛtea vyākhyāeāsyāmṛci sattvakṣetrajñāvucyete tadāpi a virodhaḥ kaścit katham prāṇabhṛddhīha ghaṭādicchidravat sattvādyupādhyabhimāitvea pratiśarīraṃ gṛhyamāṇo dyubhvādyāyataaṃ a bhavatīti pratiṣidhyate yastu sarvaśarīreṣūpādhibhirviopalakṣyate paraeva
sa bhavati yathā ghaṭādicchidrāṇi ghaṭādibhirupādhibhirviopalakṣyamāṇāi mahākāśa eva bhavati tadvat prāṇabhṛtaḥ parasmādayatvāupapatteḥ pratiṣedho opapadyate tasmātsattvādyupādhyabhimāia eva dyubhvādyāyataatvapratiṣedhaḥ tasmātparameva brahma dyubhvādyāyataam tadetat
adṛśyatvādiguṇako dharmokteḥ ityaeaiva siddham tasyaiva hi bhūtayoivākyasya madhye idaṃ paṭhitam yasmidyauḥ pṛthivī cātarikṣam iti prapañcārthaṃ tu puarupayastam bhūmā samprasādād adhyupadeśāt
bhūmādhikaraṇam idaṃ samāmaati bhūmā tv eva vijijñāsitavya iti bhūmāaṃ bhagavo vijijñāsa ChU iti yatra āyat paśyati āyac chṛṇoti āyad vijāāti
sa bhūmā atha yatrāyat paśyaty ayacchṛṇoty ayad vijāāti tad alpam ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ prāṇo bhūmā syāt āhosvit paramātmeti kutaḥ
saṃśayaḥ bhūmeti tāvad bahutvama bhidhīyate bahor lopo bhū ca bahoḥ iti bhūmaśabdasya bhāvapratyayātatāsmaraṇāt kimātmakaṃ puas tadbahutvamiti viśeṣākāṅkṣāyām prāṇo vā āśāyā
bhūyā iti saṃidhāāt prāṇo bhūmeti pratibhāti tathā śrutaṃ hyeva me bhagavaddṛśebhyastarati śokamātmaviditi sohaṃ bhagavaḥ śocāmi taṃ mā bhagavāñśokasya pāraṃ tārayatu

asti bhagavo āmo bhūyaḥ iti vāgvāva āmo bhūyasī iti tathā asti bhagavo vāco bhūyaḥ iti mao vāva vāco bhūyaḥ iti
ca āmādibhyo hi ā prāṇāt bhūyaḥpraśaprativacaapravāhaḥ pravṛttaḥ aivaṃ prāṇātparaṃ bhūyaḥpraśaprativacaaṃ dṛśyate asti bhagavaḥ prāṇādbhūyaḥ iti ado vāva prāṇādbhūyaḥ iti prāṇameva
tu āmādibhya āśātebhyo bhūyāṃsam prāṇo vā āśāyā bhūyā ityādiā saprapañcamuktvā prāṇadarśiaścātivāditvam ativādyasītyativādyasmīti brūyāāpahuvīta ityabhyaujñāya eṣa tu vā ativadati yaḥ satyeātivadati
iti prāṇavratamativāditvamaukṛṣya aparityajyaiva prāṇaṃ satyādiparaṃparayā bhūmāamavatāraya prāṇameva bhūmāaṃ mayata iti gamyate kathaṃ puaḥ prāṇe bhūmai vyākhyāyamāe yatra āyatpaśyati ityetadbhūmo lakṣaṇaparaṃ
vacaaṃ vyākhyāyeteti ucyate suṣuptāvasthāyāṃ prāṇagrasteṣu karaṇeṣu darśaādivyavahāraivṛttidarśaātsaṃbhavati prāṇasyāpi yatra āyatpaśyatīti etallakṣaṇam tathā ca śrutiḥ a śrṛṇoti a paśyati ityādiā sarvakaraṇavyāpārapratyastamayarūpāṃ
suṣuptyavasthāmuktvā prāṇāgaya evaitasmipure jāgrati iti tasyāmevāvasthāyāṃ pañcavṛtteḥ prāṇasya jāgaraṇaṃ bruvatī prāṇapradhāāṃ suṣuptyavasthāṃ darśayati yaccaitadbhūmaḥ sukhatvaṃ śrutam yo vai bhūmā tatsukham
iti tadapyaviruddham atraiṣa devaḥ svapāa paśyatyatha yadetasmiñśarīre sukhaṃ bhavati iti suṣuptyavasthāyāmeva sukhaśravaṇāt yacca yo vai bhūmā tadamṛtam iti tadapi prāṇasyāviruddham
prāṇo vā amṛtam iti śruteḥ kathaṃ puaḥ prāṇaṃ bhūmāaṃ mayamāasya tarati śokamātmavit ityātmavividiṣayā prakaraṇasyotthāamupapadyate prāṇa evehātmā vivakṣita iti brūmaḥ tathāhi
prāṇo ha pitā prāṇo mātā prāṇo bhrātā prāṇaḥ svasā prāṇa ācāryaḥ prāṇo brāhmaṇaḥ iti prāṇameva sarvātmāaṃ karoti yathā vā arā
ābhau samarpitā evam asmi prāṇe sarvaṃ samarpitam iti ca sarvātmatvāraābhiidarśaābhyāṃ ca saṃbhavati vaipulyātmikā bhūmarūpatā prāṇasya tasmāt prāṇo bhūmety evaṃ prāptam
tata idam ucyate paramātmaiveha bhūmā bhavitum arhati a prāṇaḥ kasmāt saṃprasādādadhyupadeśāt saṃprasāda iti suṣuptaṃ sthāam ucyate samyakprasīdaty asmi iti irvacaāt
bṛhadāraṇyake ca svapajāgaritasthāābhyāṃ saha pāṭhāt tasyāṃ ca saṃprasādāvasthāyāṃ prāṇo jāgartīti prāṇotra saṃprasādobhipreyate prāṇād ūrdhvaṃ bhūma upadiśyamāatvād ity arthaḥ prāṇa eva
cedbhūmā syāt sa eva tasmād ūrdhvam upadiśyetety āśliṣṭam etat syāt a hi āmaiva āmo bhūyaḥ iti āma ūrdhvam upadiṣṭam kiṃ
tarhi āmoyad arthātaram upadiṣṭaṃ vāgākhyam vāg vāva āmo bhūyasī iti tathā vāgādibhyopi ā prāṇād arthātaram eva tatra tatrordhvam upadiṣṭam tadvat
prāṇād ūrdhvam upadiśyamāo bhūmā prāṇād arthātarabhūto bhavitum arhati av iha āsti praśaḥ asti bhagavaḥ prāṇādbhūyaḥ iti āpi prativacaamasti prāṇādvāva bhūyosti
iti kathaṃ prāṇādadhi bhūmopadiśyata ity ucyate prāṇaviṣayam eva cātivāditvam uttaratrāukṛṣyamāṇaṃ paśyāmaḥ eṣa tu vā ativadati yaḥ satyeātivadati iti tasmā āsti
prāṇād adhyupadeśa iti atrocyate a tāvat prāṇaviṣayasyaivātivāditvasyaitad aukarṣaṇam iti śakyaṃ vaktum viśeṣavādāt yaḥ satyeātivadati iti au viśeṣavādopy ayaṃ prāṇaviṣaya eva
bhaviṣyati katham yathā eṣogihotrī yaḥ satyaṃ vadati ity ukte a satyavadaeāgihotritvam kea tarhi agihotreṇaiva tatsatyavadaaṃ tv agihotriṇo viśeṣa ucyate tathā
eṣa tu vā ativadati yaḥ satyeātivadati ity ukte a satyavadaeātivāditvam kea tarhi prakṛtea prāṇavijñāeaiva satyavadaaṃ tu prāṇavido viśeṣo vivakṣyata iti
eti brūmaḥ śrutyarthaparityāgaprasaṅgāt śrutyā hy atra satyavadaeātivāditvaṃ pratīyate yaḥ satyeātivadati sotivadati iti ātra prāṇavijñāasya saṃkīrtaam asti prakaraṇāt tu prāṇavijñāaṃ saṃbadhyeta
tatra prakaraṇāurodhea śrutiḥ parityaktā syāt prakṛtavyāvṛttyarthaś ca tuśabdo a saṃgaccheta eṣa tu vā ativadati iti satyaṃ tveva vijijñāsitavyam iti ca
prayatātarakaraṇamarthātaravivakṣāṃ sūcayati tasmādyathaikavedapraśaṃsāyāṃ prakṛtāyām eṣa tu mahābrāhmaṇaḥ yaścaturo vedāadhīte ityekavedebhyorthātarabhūtaścaturvedaḥ praśasyate tādṛgetaddraṣṭavyam a ca praśaprativacaarūpayaivārthātaravivakṣayā bhavitavyamiti iyamosti prakṛtasaṃbadhāsaṃbhavakāritatvādarthātaravivakṣāyāḥ tatra prāṇātamauśāsaaṃ
śrutvā tūṣṇīṃbhūtaṃ āradaṃ svayameva saatkumāro vyutpādayati yatprāṇavijñāea vikārāṛtaviṣayeṇātivāditvamaativāditvameva tat eṣa tu vā ativadati yaḥ satyeātivadati iti tatra satyamiti paraṃ brahmocyate
paramārtharūpatvāt satyaṃ jñāamaataṃ brahma iti ca śrutyatarāt tathā vyutpātitāya āradāya sohaṃ bhagavaḥ satyeātivadāi ityevaṃ pravṛttāya vijñāādisādhaaparaṃparayā bhūmāamupadiśati tatra yatprāṇādadhi satyaṃ
vaktavyaṃ pratijñātam tadeveha bhūmetyucyata iti gamyate tasmādasti prāṇādadhi bhūma upadeśa iti ataḥ prāṇādayaḥ paramātmā bhūmā bhavitumarhatīti evaṃ cehātmavividiṣayā prakaraṇasyotthāamupapaaṃ bhaviṣyati
prāṇa evehātmā vivakṣita ityetadapi opapadyate a hi prāṇasya mukhyayā vṛttyātmatvamasti a cāyatra paramātmajñāācchokaviivṛttirasti āyaḥ pathā vidyateyaāya iti śrutyatarāt taṃ mā
bhagavāñśokasya pāraṃ tārayatu iti copakramyopasaṃharati tasmai mṛditakaṣāyāya tamasaḥ pāraṃ darśayati bhagavāsaatkumāraḥ iti tama iti śokādikāraṇamavidyocyeta prāṇāte cāuśāsae a prāṇasyāyāyattatocyate ātmataḥ
prāṇaḥ iti ca brāhmaṇam prakaraṇāte paramātmavivakṣā bhaviṣyati bhūmātra prāṇa eveti cet a sa bhagavaḥ kasmipratiṣṭhita iti sve mahimi ityādiā bhūma
eva ā prakaraṇasamāpteraukarṣaṇāt vaipulyātmikā ca bhūmarūpatā sarvakāraṇatvātparamātmaaḥ sutarāmupapadyate dharmopapatteśca api ca ye bhūmi śrūyate dharmāḥ te paramātmayupapadyate yatra āyatpaśyati āyacchṛṇoti
āyadvijāāti sa bhūmā iti darśaādivyavahārābhāvaṃ bhūmai avagamayati paramātmai cāyaṃ darśaādivyavahārābhāvovagataḥ yatra tvasya sarvamātmaivābhūttatkea kaṃ paśyet ityādiśrutyatarāt yopyasau suṣuptyavasthāyāṃ darśaādivyavahārābhāva uktaḥ
sopyātmaa evāsaṅgatvavivakṣayoktaḥ a prāṇasvabhāvavivakṣayā paramātmaprakaraṇāt yadapi tasyāmavasthāyāṃ sukhamuktam tadapyātmaa eva sukharūpatvavivakṣayoktam yata āha eṣosya parama āada etasyaivāadasyāyāi bhūtāi mātrāmupajīvati iti
ihāpi yo vai bhūmā tatsukhaṃ ālpe sukhamasti bhūmaiva sukham iti sāmayasukhairākaraṇea brahmaiva sukhaṃ bhūmāaṃ darśayati yo vai bhūmā tadamṛtam ityamṛtatvamapīha
śrūyamāṇaṃ paramakāraṇaṃ gamayati vikārāṇāmamṛtatvasyāpekṣikatvāt atoyadārtam iti ca śrutyatarāt tathā ca satyatvaṃ svamahimapratiṣṭhitatvaṃ sarvagatatvaṃ sarvātmatvamiti caite dharmāḥ śrūyamāṇāḥ paramātmayevopapadyate āyatra tasmādbhūmā
paramātmeti siddham akṣaramambarātadhṛteḥ akṣarādhikaraṇam kasmiu khalvākāśa otaśca potaśceti sa hovācaitadvai tadakṣaraṃ gārgi brāhmaṇā abhivadatyasthūlamaaṇu ityādi śrūyate tatra saṃśayaḥ kimakṣaraśabdea varṇa
ucyate kiṃ vā parameśvara iti tatrākṣarasamāmāya ityādāvakṣaraśabdasya varṇe prasiddhatvāt prasiddhyatikramya cāyuktatvāt oṃkāra evedaṃ sarvam ityādau ca śrutyatare varṇasyāpyupāsyatvea sarvātmakatvāvadhāraṇāt varṇa
evākṣaraśabda ityevaṃ prāpte ucyate para evātmākṣaraśabdavācyaḥ kasmāt ambarātadhṛteḥ pṛthivyāderākāśātasya vikārajātasya dhāraṇāt tatra hi pṛthivyādeḥ samastavikārajātasya kālatrayavibhaktasya ākāśa eva tadotaṃ ca
protaṃ ca ityākāśe pratiṣṭhitatvamuktvā kasmiu khalvākāśa otaśca protaśca ityaea praśeedamakṣaramavatāritam tathā copasaṃhṛtam etasmiu khalvakṣare gārgyākāśa otaśca protaśca iti a ceyamambarātadhṛtirbrahmaṇoyatra
saṃbhavati yadapi oṃkāra evedaṃ sarvam iti tadapi brahmapratipattisādhaatvātstutyarthaṃ draṣṭavyam tasmia kṣarati aśute ceti ityatvavyāpitvābhyāmakṣaraṃ parameva brahma syādetat kāryasya cetkāraṇādhīatvamambarātadhṛtirabhyupagamyate pradhāakāraṇavādiopīyamupapadyate
kathamambarātadhṛterbrahmatvapratipattiriti ata uttaraṃ paṭhati sā ca praśāsaāt sā ca ambarātadhṛtiḥ parameśvarasyaiva karma kasmāt praśāsaāt praśāsaaṃ hīha śrūyate etasya vā akṣarasya
praśāsae gārgi sūryācadramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ ityādi praśāsaaṃ ca pārameśvaraṃ karma a acetaasya praśāsaaṃ bhavati a hyacetaāāṃ ghaṭādikāraṇāāṃ mṛdādīāṃ ghaṭādiviṣayaṃ praśāsaamasti
ayabhāvavyāvṛtteśca ayabhāvavyāvṛtteśca kāraṇādbrahmaivākṣaraśabdavācyam tasyaivāmbarātadhṛtiḥ karma āyasya kasyacit kimidam ayabhāvavyāvṛtteriti ayasya bhāvoyabhāvaḥ tasmādvyāvṛttiḥ ayabhāvavyāvṛttiriti tasyāḥ etaduktaṃ bhavati yadayadbrahmaṇokṣaraśabdavācyamihāśaṅkyate tadbhāvāt idamambarātavidhāraṇamakṣaraṃ vyāvartayati
śrutiḥ tadvā etadakṣaraṃ gārgi adṛṣṭaṃ draṣṭṛ aśrutaṃ śrotṛ amataṃ matṛ avijñātaṃ vijñātṛ iti tatrādṛṣṭatvādivyapadeśaḥ pradhāasyāpi saṃbhavati draṣṭṛtvādivyapadeśastu a tasya saṃbhavati
acetaatvāt tathā āyadatosti draṣṭṛ āyadatosti śrotṛ āyadatosti matṛ āyadatosti vijñātṛ ityātmabhedapratiṣedhāt a śārīrasyāpyupādhimatokṣaraśabdavācyatvam acakṣuṣkamaśrotramavāgamaaḥ iti copādhimattāpratiṣedhāt a hi irupādhikaḥ śārīro
āma bhavati tasmātparameva brahmākṣaramiti iścayaḥ īkṣatikarmavyapadeśāt saḥ īkṣatikarmādhikaraṇam etad vai satyakāma paraṃ cāparaṃ ca brahma yad oṃkāras tasmād vidvā eteaivāyataeaikataram
aveti iti prakṛtya śrūyate yaḥ puar etaṃ trimātreṇom ity eteaivākṣareṇa paraṃ puruṣam abhidhyāyīta iti kim asmi vākye paraṃ brahmābhidhyātavyam upadiśyate
āhosvid aparam iti eteaivāyataea param aparaṃ vaikataram avetīti prakṛtatvāt saṃśayaḥ tatrāparam idaṃ brahmeti prāptam kasmāt sa tejasi sūrye saṃpaaḥ sa
sāmabhiruīyate brahmalokam iti ca tadvido deśaparicchiasya phalasyocyamāatvāt a hi parabrahmaviddeśaparicchiaṃ phalamaśuvīteti yuktam sarvagatatvātparasya brahmaṇaḥ avaparabrahmaparigrahe paraṃ puruṣam iti viśeṣaṇaṃ opapadyate
aiṣa doṣaḥ piṇḍāpekṣayā prāṇasya paratvopapatteḥ ity evaṃ prāpte abhidhīyate param eva brahma iha abhidhyātavyam upadiśyate kasmāt īkṣatikarmavyapadeśāt īkṣatirdarśaam darśaavyāpyamīkṣatikarma īkṣatikarmatveāsyābhidhyātavyasya
puruṣasya vākyaśeṣe vyapadeśo bhavati sa etasmājjīvaghaātparātparaṃ puriśayaṃ puruṣamīkṣate iti tatra abhidhyāyateratathābhūtamapi vastu karma bhavati maorathakalpitasyāpyabhidhyāyatikarmatvāt īkṣatestu tathābhūtameva vastu loke karma
dṛṣṭam ityataḥ paramātmaivāyaṃ samyagdarśaaviṣayabhūta īkṣatikarmatvea vyapadiṣṭa iti gamyate sa eva ceha parapuruṣaśabdābhyāmabhidhyātavyaḥ pratyabhijñāyate avabhidhyāe paraḥ puruṣa uktaḥ īkṣaṇe tu parātparaḥ
kathamitara itaratra pratyabhijñāyata iti atrocyate parapuruṣaśabdau tāvadubhayatra sādhāraṇau a cātra jīvaghaaśabdea prakṛtobhidhyātavyaḥ paraḥ puruṣaḥ parāmṛśyate yea tasmāt parātparoyamīkṣitavyaḥ puruṣoyaḥ syāt
kastarhi jīvaghaa iti ucyate ghao mūrtiḥ jīvalakṣaṇo ghaaḥ jīvaghaaḥ saidhavakhilyavat yaḥ paramātmao jīvarūpaḥ khilyabhāva upādhikṛtaḥ paraśca viṣayedriyebhyaḥ sotra jīvaghaa iti
apara āha sa sāmabhiruīyate brahmalokam ityatītāataravākyairdiṣṭo yo brahmalokaḥ paraśca lokātarebhyaḥ sotra jīvaghaa ityucyate jīvāāṃ hi sarveṣāṃ karaṇaparivṛtāāṃ sarvakaraṇātmai hiraṇyagarbhe brahmalokaivāsii
saṃghātopapatterbhavati brahmaloko jīvaghaaḥ tasmātparo yaḥ puruṣaḥ paramātmā īkṣaṇakarmabhūtaḥ sa evābhidhyāepi karmabhūta iti gamyate paraṃ puruṣam iti ca viśeṣaṇaṃ paramātmaparigraha evāvakalpate
paro hi puruṣaḥ paramātmaiva bhavati yasmātparaṃ kiṃcidayaāsti puruṣāa paraṃ kiṃcitsā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ iti ca śrutyatarāt paraṃ cāparaṃ ca
brahma yadoṃkāraḥ iti ca vibhajya aataramoṃkāreṇa paraṃ puruṣamabhidhyātavyaṃ bruva parameva brahma paraṃ puruṣaṃ gamayati yathā pādodarastvacā viirmucyata evaṃ ha vai
sa pāpmaā viirmucyate iti pāpmaviirmokaphalavacaaṃ paramātmāamihābhidhyātavyaṃ sūcayati atha yaduktaṃ paramātmābhidhyāyio a deśaparicchiaṃ phalaṃ yujyata iti atrocyate trimātreṇoṃkāreṇālambaea paramātmāamabhidhyāyataḥ phalaṃ brahmalokaprāptiḥ
krameṇa ca samyagdarśaotpattiḥ iti kramamuktyabhiprāyametadbhaviṣyatītyadoṣaḥ dahara uttarebhyaḥ daharādhikaraṇam atha yad idam asmi brahmapure daharaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ veśma daharosmi atarākāśas tasmi yad
atas tad aveṣṭavyaṃ tadvāva vijijñāsitavyam ityādi vākyaṃ samāmāyate tatra yoyaṃ dahare hṛdayapuṇḍarīke dahara ākāśaḥ śrutaḥ sa kiṃ bhūtākāśaḥ atha vijñāātmā
athavā paramātmeti saṃśayyate kutaḥ saṃśayaḥ ākāśabrahmapuraśabdābhyām ākāśaśabdo hyayaṃ bhūtākāśe parasmiṃśca brahmaṇi prayujyamāo dṛśyate tatra kiṃ bhūtākāśa eva daharaḥ syāt kiṃ
vā para iti saṃśayaḥ tathā brahmapuramiti kiṃ jīvotra brahmaāmā tasyedaṃ puraṃ śarīraṃ brahmapuram athavā parasyaiva brahmaṇaḥ puraṃ brahmapuramiti tatra jīvasya
parasya vāyatarasya purasvāmio daharākāśatve saṃśayaḥ tatrākāśaśabdasya bhūtākāśe rūḍhatvādbhūtākāśa eva daharaśabda iti prāptam tasya ca daharāyataāpekṣayā daharatvam yāvāvā ayamākāśastāvāeṣotarhṛdaya ākāśaḥ iti
ca bāhyābhyatarabhāvakṛtabhedasyopamāopameyabhāvaḥ dyāvāpṛthivyādi ca tasmiataḥ samāhitam avakāśātmaākāśasyaikatvāt athavā jīvo dahara iti prāptam brahmapuraśabdāt jīvasya hīdaṃ puraṃ sat śarīraṃ brahmapuramityucyate tasya
svakarmaṇopārjitatvāt bhaktyā ca tasya brahmaśabdavācyatvam a hi parasya brahmaṇaḥ śarīreṇa svasvāmibhāvaḥ saṃbadhosti tatra purasvāmiaḥ puraikadeśevasthāaṃ dṛṣṭam yathā rājñaḥ maaupādhikaśca jīvaḥ
maaśca prāyeṇa hṛdaye pratiṣṭhitam ityato jīvasyaivedaṃ hṛdayātaravasthāaṃ syāt daharatvamapi tasyaiva ārāgropamitatvāt avakalpate ākāśopamitatvādi ca brahmābhedavivakṣayā bhaviṣyati a cātra daharasyākāśasyāveṣṭavyatvaṃ vijijñāsitavyatvaṃ
ca śrūyate tasmiyadataḥ iti paraviśeṣaṇatveopādāāditi ata uttaraṃ brūmaḥ parameśvara evātra daharākāśo bhavitumarhati a bhūtākāśo jīvo vā kasmāt uttarebhyaḥ vākyaśeṣagatebhyo hetubhyaḥ
tathāhi aveṣṭavyatayābhihitasya daharākāśasya taṃ cedbrūyuḥ ityupakramya kiṃ tadatra vidyate yadaveṣṭavyaṃ yadvāva vijijñāsitavyam ityevamākṣepapūrvakaṃ pratisamādhāavacaaṃ bhavati sa brūyādyāvāvā ayamākāśastāvāeṣotarhṛdaya ākāśa ubhe
asmidyāvāpṛthivī atareva samāhite ityādi tatra puṇḍarīkadaharatvea prāptadaharatvasyākāśasya prasiddhākāśaupamyea daharatvaṃ ivartaya bhūtākāśatvaṃ daharasyākāśasya ivartayatīti gamyate yadyapyākāśaśabdo bhūtākāśe rūḍhaḥ tathāpi teaiva tasyopamā
opapadyata iti bhūtākāśaśaṅkā ivartitā bhavati avekasyāpyākāśasya bāhyābhyataratvakalpitea bhedeopamāopameyabhāvaḥ saṃbhavatītyuktam aivaṃ saṃbhavati agatikā hīyaṃ gatiḥ yatkālpaikabhedāśrayaṇam api ca kalpayitvā bhedamupamāopameyabhāvaṃ varṇayataḥ
paricchiatvādabhyatarākāśasya a bāhyākāśaparimāṇatvamupapadyeta au parameśvarasyāpi jyāyāākāśāt iti śrutyatarāt aivākāśaparimāṇatvamupapadyate aiṣa doṣaḥ puṇḍarīkaveṣṭaaprāptadaharatvaivṛttiparatvādvākyasya a tāvattvapratipādaaparatvam ubhayapratipādae hi vākyaṃ bhidyeta a ca
kalpitabhede puṇḍarīkaveṣṭita ākāśaikadeśe dyāvāpṛthivyādīāmataḥ samādhāamupapadyate eṣa ātmāpahatapāpmā vijaro vimṛtyurviśoko vijighatsopipāsaḥ satyakāmaḥ satyasaṃkalpaḥ iti cātmatvāpahatapāpmatvādayaśca guṇā a bhūtākāśe saṃbhavati yadyapyātmaśabdo jīve
saṃbhavati tathāpītarebhyaḥ kāraṇebhyo jīvāśaṅkāpi ivartitā bhavati a hyupādhiparicchiasyārāgropamitasya jīvasya puṇḍarīkaveṣṭaakṛtaṃ daharatvaṃ śakyaṃ ivartayitum brahmābhedavivakṣayā jīvasya sarvagatatvādi vivakṣyeteti cet yadātmatayā jīvasya
sarvagatatvādi vivakṣyeta tasyaiva brahmaṇaḥ sākṣātsarvagatatvādi vivakṣyatām iti yuktam yad apy uktam brahmapuram iti jīvea purasyopalakṣitatvād rājña iva jīvasyaivedaṃ purasvāmiaḥ puraikadeśavartitvam
astviti atra brūmaḥ parasyaivedaṃ brahmaṇaḥ puraṃ sat śarīraṃ brahmapuramityucyate brahmaśabdasya tasmimukhyatvāt tasyāpyasti pureṇāea saṃbadhaḥ upalabdhyadhiṣṭhāatvāt sa etasmājjīvaghaātparātparaṃ puriśayaṃ puruṣamīkṣate sa
vā ayaṃ puruṣaḥ sarvāsu pūrṣu puriśayaḥ ityādiśrutibhyaḥ athavā jīvapura evāsmi brahma saṃihitamupalakṣyate yathā sālagrāme viṣṇuḥ saṃihita iti tadvat tadyatheha karmacito
lokaḥ kṣīyata evamevāmutra puṇyacito lokaḥ kṣīyate iti ca karmaṇāmatavatphalatvamuktvā atha ya ihātmāamauvidya vrajatyetāṃśca satyākāmāṃsteṣāṃ sarveṣu lokeṣu kāmacāro bhavati iti prakṛtadaharākāśavijñāasyāataphalatvaṃ
vada paramātmatvamasya sūcayati yadapyetaduktam a daharasyākāśasyāveṣṭavyatvaṃ vijijñāsitavyatvaṃ ca śrutaṃ paraviśeṣaṇatveopādāāditi atra brūmaḥ yadyākāśo āveṣṭavyatveoktaḥ syāt yāvāvā ayamākāśastāvāeṣotarhṛdaya ākāśaḥ ityādyākāśasvarūpapradarśaaṃ opapadyeta
av etad apy atarvartivastusadbhāvadarśaāyaiva pradarśyate taṃ ced brūyur yad idam asmi brahmapure daharaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ veśma daharo smi atarākāśaḥ kiṃ tad
atra vidyate yad aveṣṭavyaṃ yad vāva vijijñāsitavyam ity ākṣipya parihārāvasare ākāśaupamyopakrameṇa dyāv ā pṛthivyādīām ataḥsamāhitatvapradarśaāt aitad evam evaṃ hi sati
yad ataḥ samāhitaṃ dyāvāpṛthivyādi tad aveṣṭavyaṃ vijijñāsitavyaṃ coktaṃ syāt tatra vākyaśeṣo opapadyeta asmi kāmāḥ samāhitāḥ eṣa ātmāpahatapāpmā iti hi prakṛtaṃ
dyāvāpṛthivyādisamādhāādhāram ākāśam ākṛṣya atha ya ihātmāam auvidya vrajaty etāṃś ca satyā kāmā iti samuccayārthea caśabdeātmāaṃ kāmādhāram āśritāṃś ca kāmā vijñeyā
vākyaśeṣo darśayati tasmād vākyopakrame pi dahara evākāśo hṛdayapuṇḍarīkādhiṣṭhāaḥ sahātaḥsthaiḥ samāhitaiḥ pṛthivyādibhiḥ satyaiś ca kāmair vijñeya ukta iti gamyate sa coktebhyo
hetubhyaḥ parameśvara iti sthitam gatiśabdābhyāṃ tathā hi dṛṣṭaṃ liṅgaṃ ca daharaḥ parameśvara uttarebhyo hetubhya ityuktam ta evottare hetava idāīṃ prapañcyate
itaśca parameśvara eva daharaḥ yasmāddaharavākyaśeṣe parameśvarasyaiva pratipādakau gatiśabdau bhavataḥ imāḥ sarvāḥ prajā aharahargacchatya etaṃ brahmalokaṃ a vidati iti tatra prakṛtaṃ
daharaṃ brahmalokaśabdeābhidhāya tadviṣayā gatiḥ prajāśabdavācyāāṃ jīvāāmabhidhīyamāā daharasya brahmatāṃ gamayati tathā hyaharaharjīvāāṃ suṣuptāvasthāyāṃ brahmaviṣayaṃ gamaaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śrutyatare satā somya tadā saṃpao
bhavati ityevamādau lokepi kila gāḍhaṃ suṣuptamācakṣate brahmībhūto brahmatāṃ gataḥ iti tathā brahmalokaśabdopi prakṛte dahare prayujyamāo jīvabhūtākāśāśaṅkāṃ ivartayabrahmatāmasya gamayati au kamalāsaalokamapi
brahmalokaśabdo gamayet gamayedyadi brahmaṇo loka iti ṣaṣṭhīsamāsavṛttyā vyutpādyeta sāmāādhikaraṇyavṛttyā tu vyutpādyamāo brahmaiva loko brahmaloka iti parameva brahma gamayiṣyati etadeva cāharaharbrahmalokagamaaṃ
dṛṣṭaṃ brahmalokaśabdasya sāmāādhikaraṇyavṛttiparigrahe liṅgam a hyaharaharimāḥ prajāḥ kāryabrahmalokaṃ satyalokākhyaṃ gacchatīti śakyaṃ kalpayitum dhṛteśca mahimosyāsmiupalabdheḥ dhṛteśca hetoḥ parameśvara evāyaṃ daharaḥ katham
daharosmiatarākāśaḥ iti hi prakṛtya ākāśaupamyapūrvakaṃ tasmisarvasamādhāamuktvā tasmieva cātmaśabdaṃ prayujyāpahatapāpmatvādiguṇayogaṃ copadiśya tamevāativṛttaprakaraṇaṃ irdiśati atha ya ātmā sa seturvidhṛtireṣāṃ lokāāmasaṃbhedāya iti tatra
vidhṛtirityātmaśabdasāmāādhikaraṇyādvidhārayitocyate kticaḥ kartari smaraṇāt yathodakasaṃtāasya vidhārayitā loke setuḥ kṣetrasaṃpadāmasaṃbhedāya evamayamātmā eṣāmadhyātmādibhedabhiāāṃ lokāāṃ varṇāśramādīāṃ ca vidhārayitā setuḥ asaṃbhedāya asaṃkarāyeti evamiha prakṛte
dahare vidharaṇalakṣaṇaṃ mahimāaṃ darśayati ayaṃ ca mahimā parameśvara eva śrutyatarādupalabhyate etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsae gārgi sūryācadramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ ityādeḥ tathāyatrāpi
iścite parameśvaravākye śrūyate eṣa sarveśvara eṣa bhūtādhipatireṣa bhūtapāla eṣa seturvidharaṇa eṣāṃ lokāāmasaṃbhedāya iti evaṃ dhṛteśca hetoḥ parameśvara evāyaṃ daharaḥ prasiddheś
ca itaśca parameśvara eva daharosmiatarākāśaḥ ityucyate yatkāraṇamākāśaśabdaḥ parameśvare prasiddhaḥ ākāśo vai āma āmarūpayorirvahitā sarvāṇi ha vā imāi bhūtāyākāśādeva samutpadyate ityādiprayogadarśaāt
jīve tu a kvacidākāśaśabdaḥ prayujyamāo dṛśyate bhūtākāśastu satyāmapyākāśaśabdaprasiddhau upamāopameyabhāvādyasaṃbhavāa grahītavya ityuktam itaraparāmarśātsa iti ceāsambhavāt yadi vākyaśeṣabalea dahara iti parameśvaraḥ parigṛhyeta
asti hītarasthāpi jīvasya vākyaśeṣe parāmarśaḥ atha ya eṣa saṃprasādosmāccharīrātsamutthāya paraṃ jyotirupasaṃpadya svea rūpeṇābhiiṣpadyata eṣa ātmeti hovāca iti atra hi saṃprasādaśabdaḥ
śrutyatare suṣuptāvasthāyāṃ dṛṣṭatvādavasthāvataṃ jīvaṃ śakotyupasthāpayitum ārthātaram tathā śarīravyapāśrayasyaiva jīvasya śarīrātsamutthāaṃ saṃbhavati yathākāśavyapāśrayāṇāṃ vāyvādīāmākāśātsamutthāam tadvat yathā cādṛṣṭopi loke parameśvaraviṣaya ākāśaśabdaḥ parameśvaradharmasamabhivyāhārāt
ākāśo vai āma āmarūpayorirvahitā ityevamādau parameśvaraviṣayobhyupagataḥ evaṃ jīvaviṣayopi bhaviṣyati tasmāditaraparāmarśāt daharosmiatarākāśaḥ ityatra sa eva jīva ucyata iti cet aitadevaṃ syāt
kasmāt asaṃbhavāt a hi jīvo buddhyādyupādhiparicchedābhimāī sa ākāśeopamīyeta a copādhidharmāabhimayamāasyāpahatapāpmatvādayo dharmāḥ saṃbhavati prapañcitaṃ caitatprathame sūtre atirekāśaṅkāparihārāya atra tu puarupayastam paṭhiṣyati
copariṣṭāt ayārthaśca parāmarśaḥ iti uttarāc ced āvirbhūtasvarūpas tu itaraparāmarśād yā jīvāśaṅkā jātā sā asaṃbhavā irākṛtā athedāīṃ mṛtasyevāmṛtasekāt puaḥ samutthāaṃ jīvāśaṅkāyāḥ
kriyate uttarasmāt prājāpatyād vākyāt tatra hi ya ātmāpahatapāpmā ity apahatapāpmatvādiguṇakam ātmāam aveṣṭavyaṃ vijijñāsitavyaṃ ca pratijñāya ya eṣo akṣiṇi puruṣo dṛśyata
eṣa ātmā iti bruva akṣisthaṃ draṣṭāraṃ jīvam ātmāaṃ irdiśati etaṃ tv eva te bhūyo auvyākhyāsyāmi iti ca tam eva puaḥ
puaḥ parāmṛśya ya eṣa svape mahīyamāaś caraty eṣa ātmā iti tad yatraitat suptaḥ samastaḥ saṃprasaaḥ svapaṃ a vijāāty eṣa ātmā
iti ca jīvam evāvasthātaragataṃ vyācaṣṭe tasyaiva cāpahatapāpmatvādi darśayati etad amṛtam abhayam etad brahma iti āha khalv ayam evaṃ saṃpratyātmāaṃ jāāty
ayam aham asmīti o evemāi bhūtāi iti ca suṣuptāvasthāyāṃ doṣam upalabhya etaṃ tv eva te bhūyo auvyākhyāsyāmi o evāyatraitasmāt iti
copakramya śarīrasaṃbadhaidāpūrvakam eṣa saṃprasādo asmāc charīrāt samutthāya paraṃ jyotir upasaṃpadya svea rūpeṇābhiiṣpadyate sa uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ iti jīvam eva śarīrāt samutthitam
uttamaṃ puruṣaṃ darśayati tasmād asti saṃbhavo jīve pārameśvarāṇāṃ dharmāṇām ataḥ daharo asmi atarākāśaḥ iti jīva evokta iti cet kaścid brūyāt
taṃ prati brūyāt āvirbhūtasvarūpas tu iti tuśabdaḥ pūrvapakṣavyāvṛttyarthaḥ ottarasmād api vākyād iha jīvasyāśaṅkā saṃbhavatīty arthaḥ kasmāt yatas tatrāpy āvirbhūtasvarūpo jīvo
vivakṣyate āvirbhūtaṃ svarūpam asyety āvirbhūtasvarūpaḥ bhūtapūrvagatyā jīvavacaam etad uktaṃ bhavati ya eṣo akṣiṇi ity akṣilakṣitaṃ draṣṭāraṃ irdiśya udaśarāvabrāhmaṇea eaṃ śarīrātmatayā
vyutthāpya etaṃ tv eva te iti puaḥ puas tam eva vyākhyeyatveākṛṣya svapasuṣuptopayāsakrameṇa paraṃ jyotir upasaṃpadya svea rūpeṇābhiiṣpadyate iti yad asya
pāramārthikaṃ svarūpaṃ paraṃ brahma tadrūpatayaiaṃ jīvaṃ vyācaṣṭe a jaivea rūpeṇa yat tat paraṃ jyotir upasaṃpattavyaṃ śrutam tat paraṃ brahma tac
cāpahatapāpmatvādidharmakam tad eva ca jīvasya pāramārthikaṃ svarūpam tat tvam asi ityādiśāstrebhyaḥ etarad upādhikalpitam yāvad eva hi sthāṇāv iva puruṣabuddhiṃ dvaitalakṣaṇām
avidyāṃ ivartaya kūṭasthaityadṛksvarūpam ātmāam ahaṃ brahmāsmi iti a pratipadyate tāvaj jīvasya jīvatvam yadā tu dehedriyamaobuddhisaṃghātād vyutthāpya śrutyā pratibodhyate āsi tvaṃ
dehedriyamaobuddhisaṃghātaḥ āpi saṃsārī kiṃ tarhi tad yat satyaṃ sa ātmā caitayamātrasvarūpas tat tvam asīti tadā kūṭasthaityadṛksvarūpam ātmāaṃ pratibudhya asmāc charīrādyabhimāāt
samuttiṣṭha sa eva kūṭasthaityadṛksvarūpa ātmā bhavati sa yo ha vai tat paramaṃ brahma veda brahmaiva bhavati ityādiśrutibhyaḥ tad eva cāsya
pāramārthikaṃ svarūpam yea śarīrāt samutthāya svea rūpeṇābhiiṣpadyate kathaṃ puaḥ svaṃ ca rūpaṃ sveaiva ca iṣpadyata iti saṃbhavati kūṭasthaityasya suvarṇādīāṃ tu
dravyātarasaṃparkād abhibhūtasvarūpāṇām aabhivyaktāsādhāraṇaviśeṣāṇāṃ kṣāraprakṣepādibhiḥ śodhyamāāāṃ svarūpeṇābhiiṣpattiḥ syāt tathā akṣatrādīām ahay abhibhūtaprakāśāām abhibhāvakaviyoge rātrau svarūpeṇābhiiṣpattiḥ syāt a tu tathātmacaitayajyotiṣo ityasya keacid
abhibhavaḥ saṃbhavati asaṃsargitvāt vyoma iva dṛṣṭavirodhāc ca dṛṣṭiśrutim ativijñātayo hi jīvasya svarūpam tac ca śarīrād asamutthitasyāpi jīvasya sadā iṣpaam eva
dṛśyate sarvo hi jīvaḥ paśya śrṛṇva mavāo vijāa vyavaharati ayathā vyavahārāupapatteḥ tac cet śarīrāt samutthitasya iṣpadyeta prāk samutthāād dṛṣṭo vyavahāro
virudhyeta ataḥ kimātmakam idaṃ śarīrāt samutthāam kim ātmikā vā svarūpeṇābhiiṣpattir iti atrocyate prāg vivekavijñāotpatteḥ śarīredriyamaobuddhiviṣayavedaopādhibhir aviviktam iva jīvasya dṛṣṭyādijyotiḥsvarūpaṃ bhavati
yathā śuddhasya sphaṭikasya svācchyaṃ śauklyaṃ ca svarūpaṃ prāg vivekagrahaṇād raktaīlādyupādhibhir aviviktam iva bhavati pramāṇajaitavivekagrahaṇāt tu parācīaḥ sphaṭikaḥ svācchyea śauklyea ca
svea rūpeṇābhiiṣpadyata ity ucyate prāg api tathaiva sa tathā dehādyupādhyaviviktasyaiva sato jīvasya śrutikṛtaṃ vivekavijñāaṃ śarīrāt samutthāam vivekavijñāaphalaṃ svarūpeṇābhiiṣpattiḥ kevalātmasvarūpāvagatiḥ tathā
vivekāvivekamātreṇaivātmao aśarīratvaṃ saśarīratvaṃ ca matravarṇāt aśarīraṃ śarīreṣu iti śarīrastho api kauteya a karoti a lipyate iti ca saśarīratvāśarīratvaviśeṣābhāvasmaraṇāt tasmād vivekavijñāābhāvād
aāvirbhūtasvarūpaḥ sa vivekavijñāād āvirbhūtasvarūpa ity ucyate a tv ayādṛśau āvirbhāvāāvirbhāvau svarūpasya saṃbhavataḥ svarūpatvād eva evaṃ mithyājñāakṛta eva jīvaparameśvarayor bhedaḥ a
vastukṛtaḥ vyomavad asaṅgatvāviśeṣāt kutaś caitad evaṃ pratipattavyam yataḥ ya eṣo kṣiṇi puruṣo dṛśyate ity upadiśya etad amṛtam abhayam etad brahma
ity upadiśati yo kṣiṇi prasiddho draṣṭā draṣṭṛtvea vibhāvyate so mṛtābhayalakṣaṇād brahmaṇo yaś cet syāt tato mṛtābhayabrahmasāmāādhikaraṇyaṃ a syāt āpi praticchāyātmāyam
akṣilakṣito irdiśyate prajāpater mṛṣāvāditvaprasaṅgāt tathā dvitīye pi paryāye ya eṣa svape mahīyamāaś carati iti a prathamaparyāyairdiṣṭād akṣipuruṣād draṣṭur ayo irdiṣṭaḥ
etaṃ tv eva te bhūyo uvyākhyāsyāmi ity upakramāt kiṃca aham adya svape hastiam adrākṣam edāīṃ taṃ paśyāmi iti dṛṣṭam eva
pratibuddhaḥ pratyācaṣṭe draṣṭāraṃ tu tam eva pratyabhijāāti ya evāhaṃ svapamadrākṣam sa evāhaṃ jāgaritaṃ paśyāmi iti tathā tṛtīye pi paryāye āha
khalv ayam evaṃ saṃpraty ātmāaṃ jāāty ayam aham asmīti o evemāi bhūtāi iti suṣuptāvasthāyāṃ viśeṣavijñāābhāvam eva darśayati a vijñātāraṃ pratiṣedhati
yat tu tatra viāśam evāpīto bhavati iti tad api viśeṣavijñāaviāśābhiprāyam eva a vijñātṛviāśābhiprāyam a hi vijñātur vijñāter viparilopo vidyate viāśitvāt
iti śrutyatarāt tathā caturthe pi paryāye etaṃ tv eva te bhūyo uvyākhyāsyāmi o evāyatraitasmāt ity upakramya maghava martyaṃ vā idaṃ
śarīram ityādiā prapañcea śarīrādyupādhisaṃbadhapratyākhyāea saṃprasādaśabdoditaṃ jīvam svea rūpeṇābhiiṣpadyate iti brahmasvarūpāpaaṃ darśaya a parasmād brahmaṇo mṛtābhayasvarūpād ayaṃ jīvaṃ darśayati kecit tu
paramātmavivakṣāyām etaṃ tv eva te iti jīvākarṣaṇam ayāyyaṃ mayamāā etam eva vākyopakramasūcitam apahatapāpmatvādiguṇakam ātmāaṃ te bhūyo uvyākhyāsyāmīti kalpayati teṣām etam
iti saṃihitāvalambiī sarvaāmaśrutir viprakṛṣyeta bhūyaḥ śrutiś coparudhyeta paryāyātarābhihitasya paryāyātareṇāabhidhīyamāatvāt etaṃ tv eva te iti ca pratijñāya prāk caturthāt paryāyād ayam
ayaṃ vyācakṣāṇasya prajāpateḥ pratārakatvaṃ prasajyeta tasmāt yad avidyāpratyupasthāpitam apāramārthikaṃ jaivaṃ rūpaṃ kartṛtvabhoktṛtvarāgadveṣādidoṣakaluṣitam aekāarthayogi tadvilayaea tadviparītam apahatapāpmatvādiguṇakaṃ pārameśvaraṃ svarūpaṃ vidyayā pratipadyate
sarpādivilayaeeva rajjvādī apare tu vādiaḥ pāramārthikam eva jaivaṃ rūpam iti mayate smadīyāś ca kecit teṣāṃ sarveṣām ātmaikatvasamyagdarśaapratipakṣabhūtāāṃ pratiṣedhāyedaṃ śārīrakam ārabdham
eka eva parameśvaraḥ kūṭasthaityo vijñāadhātur avidyayā māyayā māyāvivat aekadhā vibhāvyate āyo vijñāadhātur astīti yat tv idaṃ parameśvaravākye jīvam āśaṅkya pratiṣedhati
sūtrakāraḥ āsaṃbhavāt ityādiā tatrāyam abhiprāyaḥ ityaśuddhabuddhamuktasvabhāve kūṭasthaitye ekasmi asaṅge paramātmai tadviparītaṃ jaivaṃ rūpaṃ vyomīva talamalādi parikalpitam tat ātmaikatvapratipādaaparair vākyair yāyopetair
dvaitavādapratiṣedhaiś cāpaeṣyāmīti paramātmao jīvād ayatvaṃ draḍhayati jīvasya tu a parasmād ayatvaṃ pratipipādayiṣati kiṃ tv auvadaty evāvidyākalpitaṃ lokaprasiddhaṃ jīvabhedam evaṃ hi
svābhāvikakartṛtvabhoktṛtvāuvādea pravṛttāḥ karmavidhayo a virudhyata iti mayate pratipādyaṃ tu śāstrārtham ātmaikatvam eva darśayati śāstradṛṣṭyā tūpadeśo vāmadevavat ityādiā varṇitaś cāsmābhiḥ vidvadavidvadbhedea
karmavidhivirodhaparihāraḥ ayārthaśca parāmarśaḥ atha yoyaṃ daharavākyaśeṣe jīvaparāmarśo darśitaḥ atha ya eṣa saṃprasādaḥ ityādiḥ sa dahare parameśvare vyākhyāyamāe a jīvopāsaopadeśaḥ āpi
prakṛtaviśeṣopadeśaḥ ityaarthakatvaṃ prāpotītyata āha ayārthoyaṃ jīvaparāmarśo a jīvasvarūpaparyavasāyī kiṃ tarhi parameśvarasvarūpaparyavasāyī katham saṃprasādaśabdodito jīvo jāgaritavyavahāre dehedriyapañjarādhyakṣo bhūtvā tadvāsaāirmitāṃśca svapāāḍīcaroubhūya śrātaḥ
śaraṇaṃ prepsurubhayarūpādapi śarīrābhimāātsamutthāya suṣuptāvasthāyāṃ paraṃ jyotirākāśaśabditaṃ paraṃ brahmopasaṃpadya viśeṣavijñāavattvaṃ ca parityajya svea rūpeṇābhiiṣpadyate yadasyopasaṃpattavyaṃ paraṃ jyotiḥ yea svea rūpeṇāyamabhiiṣpadyate sa

ca bhūtāāṃ karmaṇāṃ ca pravartaam vedaśabdebhya evādau irmame sa maheśvaraḥ iti sarveṣāṃ tu sa āmāi karmāṇi ca pṛthak pṛthak vedaśabdebhya

pratyāyayet vyabhicārāt a ca varṇasamudāyapratyayosti kramavartitvādvarṇāām pūrvapūrvavarṇāubhavajaitasaṃskārasahitotyo varṇorthaṃ pratyāyayiṣyatīti yadyucyeta taa saṃbadhagrahaṇāpekṣo hi śabdaḥ svayaṃ pratīyamāorthaṃ pratyāyayet dhūmādivat a ca
pūrvapūrvavarṇāubhavajaitasaṃskārasahitasyātyavarṇasya pratītirasti apratyakṣatvātsaṃskārāṇām kāryapratyāyitaiḥ saṃskāraiḥ sahitotyo varṇorthaṃ pratyāyayiṣyatīti cet a saṃskārakāryasyāpi smaraṇasya kramavartitvāt tasmātsphoṭa eva śabdaḥ sa caikaikavarṇapratyayāhitasaṃskārabījetyavarṇapratyayajaitaparipāke pratyayiyekapratyayaviṣayatayā jhaṭiti
pratyavabhāsate a cāyamekapratyayo varṇaviṣayā smṛtiḥ varṇāāmaekatvādekapratyayaviṣayatvāupapatteḥ tasya ca pratyuccāraṇaṃ pratyabhijñāyamāatvāityatvam bhedapratyayasya varṇaviṣayatvāt tasmāityācchabdātsphoṭarūpādabhidhāyakātkriyākārakaphalalakṣaṇaṃ jagadabhidheyabhūtaṃ prabhavatīti varṇā eva tu śabdaḥ iti
bhagavāupavarṣaḥ aūtpaapradhvaṃsitvaṃ varṇāāmuktam taa ta eveti pratyabhijñāāt sādṛśyātpratyabhijñāaṃ keśādiṣviveti cet a pratyabhijñāasya pramāṇātareṇa bādhāupapatteḥ pratyabhijñāamākṛtiimittamiti cet a vyaktipratyabhijñāāt yadi hi
pratyuccāraṇaṃ gavādivyaktivadayā ayā varṇavyaktayaḥ pratīyera tata ākṛtiimittaṃ pratyabhijñāaṃ syāt a tvetadasti varṇavyaktaya eva hi pratyuccāraṇaṃ pratyabhijñāyate dvirgośabda uccāritaḥ iti hi
pratipattiḥ a tu dvau gośabdāviti au varṇāapyuccāraṇabhedea bhiāḥ pratīyate devadattayajñadattayor adhyayaadhvaiśravaṇād eva bhedapratīter ity uktam atrābhidhīyate sati varṇaviṣaye iścite pratyabhijñāe
saṃyogavibhāgābhivyaṅgyatvādvarṇāām abhivyañjakavaicitryaimitto yaṃ varṇaviṣayo vicitraḥ pratyayaḥ a svarūpaimittaḥ api ca varṇavyaktibhedavādiāpi pratyabhijñāasiddhaye varṇākṛtayaḥ kalpayitavyāḥ tāsu ca paropādhiko bhedapratyaya ity abhyupagatavyam
tadvaraṃ varṇavyaktiṣv eva paropādhiko bhedapratyayaḥ svarūpaimittaṃ ca pratyabhijñāam iti kalpaālāghavam eṣa eva ca varṇaviṣayasya bhedapratyayasya bādhakaḥ pratyayaḥ yat pratyabhijñāam kathaṃ
hy ekasmi kāle bahūām uccārayatām eka eva sa gakāro yugapad aekarūpaḥ syāt udāttaś cāudāttaś ca svaritaś ca sāuāsikaś ca irauāsikaś
ceti atha vā dhvaikṛto yaṃ bhedapratyayo a varṇakṛta ity adoṣaḥ kaḥ puar ayaṃ dhvair āma yo dūrād ākarṇayato varṇavivekam apratipadyamāasya
karṇapatham avatarati pratyāsītadataś ca paṭumṛdutvādibhedaṃ varṇeṣv āsañjayati taibadhaāś codāttādayo viśeṣāḥ a varṇasvarūpaibadhaāḥ varṇāāṃ pratyuccāraṇaṃ pratyabhijñāyamāatvāt evaṃ ca sati sālambaā evaite
udāttādipratyayā bhaviṣyati itarathā hi varṇāāṃ pratyabhijñāyamāāāṃ irbhedatvāt saṃyogavibhāgakṛtā udāttādiviśeṣāḥ kalpyera saṃyogavibhāgāāṃ cāpratyakṣatvāa tadāśrayā viśeṣāḥ varṇeṣvadhyavasātuṃ śakyata ityato irālambaā eva ete
udāttādipratyayāḥ syuḥ api ca aivaitad abhiiveṣṭavyam udāttādibhedea varṇāāṃ pratyabhijñāyamāāāṃ bhedo bhavediti a hy ayasya bhedeāyasyābhidyamāasya bhedo bhavitum arhati a hi
vyaktibhedea jātiṃ bhiāṃ mayate varṇebhyaś cārthapratīteḥ saṃbhavāt sphoṭakalpaāarthikā a kalpayāmy ahaṃ sphoṭam pratyakṣam eva tv eam avagacchāmi ekaikavarṇagrahaṇāhitasaṃskārāyā buddhau jhaṭiti
pratyavabhāsaād iti cet a asyā api buddher varṇaviṣayatvāt ekaikavarṇagrahaṇottarakālā hīyam ekā buddhir gaur iti samastavarṇaviṣayā ārthātaraviṣayā katham etad avagamyate yato
syām api buddhau gakārādayo varṇā auvartate a tu dakārādayaḥ yadi hy asyā buddher gakārādibhyo rthātaraṃ sphoṭo viṣayaḥ syāt tato dakārādaya
iva gakārādayo py asyā buddher vyāvartera a tu tathāsti tasmād iyam ekabuddhir varṇaviṣayaiva smṛtiḥ av aekatvād varṇāāṃ aikabuddhiviṣayatopapadyata ity uktam
tat prati brūmaḥ saṃbhavaty aekasyāpy ekabuddhiviṣayatvam paṅktiḥ vaaṃ seā daśa śataṃ sahasram ityādidarśaāt yā tu gaur ity eko yaṃ śabda
iti buddhiḥ sā bahuṣv eva varṇeṣv ekārthāvacchedaibadhaā aupacārikī vaaseādibuddhivad eva atrāha yadi varṇā eva sāmastyea ekabuddhiviṣayatām āpadyamāāḥ padaṃ syuḥ tato
jārā rājā kapiḥ pika ityādiṣu padaviśeṣapratipattir a syāt ta eva hi varṇā itaratretaratra ca pratyavabhāsata iti atra vadāmaḥ saty api
samastavarṇapratyavamarśe yathā kramāurodhiya eva pipīlikāḥ paṅktibuddhim ārohati evaṃ kramāurodhia eva hi varṇāḥ padabuddhim ārokṣyati tatra varṇāām aviśeṣe pi kramaviśeṣakṛtā padaviśeṣapratipattir

pratyāyayiṣyatīti varṇavādio laghīyasī kalpaā sphoṭavādias tu dṛṣṭahāiḥ adṛṣṭakalpaā ca varṇāś ceme krameṇa gṛhyamāṇāḥ sphoṭaṃ vyañjayati sa sphoṭo rthaṃ vyaaktīti garīyasī
kalpaā syāt athāpi āma pratyuccāraṇam aye ye varṇāḥ syuḥ tathāpi pratyabhijñālambaabhāvea varṇasāmāyāām avaśyābhyupagatavyatvāt varṇeṣv arthapratipādaaprakriyā racitā sā sāmāyeṣu saṃcārayitavyā tataś
ca ityebhyaḥ śabdebhyo devādivyaktīāṃ prabhava ity aviruddham ata eva ca ityatvam karturasmaraṇāditi sthite vedasya ityatve devādivyaktiprabhavābhyupagamea tasya virodhamāśaṅkya ataḥ prabhavāt
iti parihṛtya idāīṃ tadeva vedaityatvaṃ sthitaṃ draḍhayati ata eva ca ityatvamiti ata eva iyatākṛterdevāderjagato vedaśabdaprabhavatvāt vedaśabdaityatvamapi pratyetavyam tathā ca matravarṇaḥ
yajñea vācaḥ padavīyamāyaṃstāmavavidaṛṣiṣu praviṣṭām iti sthitāmeva vācamauviāṃ darśayati vedavyāsaścaivameva smarati yugātetarhitāvedāsetihāsāmaharṣayaḥ lebhire tapasā pūrvamaujñātāḥ svayaṃbhuvā iti samāaāmarūpatvāc cāvṛttāv apy avirodho
darśaāt smṛteś ca athāpi syāt yadi paśvādivyaktivad devādivyaktayo pi saṃtatyaivotpadyera irudhyeraṃś ca tato bhidhāābhidheyābhidhātṛvyavahārāvicchedāt saṃbadhaityatvea virodhaḥ śabde parihriyeta yadā tu
khalu sakalaṃ trailokyaṃ parityaktaāmarūpaṃ irlepaṃ pralīyate prabhavati cābhiavam iti śrutismṛtivādā vadati tadā katham avirodha iti tatredam abhidhīyate samāaāmarūpatvād iti tadāpi
saṃsārasyāāditvaṃ tāvad abhyupagatavyam pratipādayiṣyati cācāryaḥ saṃsārasyāāditvam upapadyate cāpy upalabhyate ca iti aādau ca saṃsāre yathā svāpaprabodhayoḥ pralayaprabhavaśravaṇepi pūrvaprabodhavad uttaraprabodhe pi
vyavahārā a kaścid virodhaḥ evaṃ kalpātaraprabhavapralayayor apīti draṣṭavyam svāpaprabodhayoś ca pralayaprabhavau śrūyete yadā suptaḥ svapaṃ a kaṃcaa paśyaty athāsmi prāṇa
evaikadhā bhavati tadaiaṃ vāksarvairāmabhiḥ sahāpy eti cakṣuḥ sarvai rūpaiḥ sahāpyeti śrotraṃ sarvaiḥ śabdaiḥ sahāpyeti maaḥ sarvair dhyāaiḥ sahāpyeti sa yadā
pratibudhyate yathāger jvalataḥ sarvā diśo visphuliṅgā vipratiṣṭhera evam evaitasmād ātmaaḥ sarve prāṇā yathāyataaṃ vipratiṣṭhate prāṇebhyo devā devebhyo lokāḥ iti syād
etat svāpe puruṣātaravyavahārāvicchedāt svayaṃ ca suṣuptaprabuddhasya pūrvaprabodhavyavahārāusaṃdhāasaṃbhavād aviruddham mahāpralaye tu sarvavyavahārocchedāj jamātaravyavahāravac ca kalpātaravyavahārasyāusaṃdhātum aśakyatvād vaiṣamyam iti aiṣa doṣaḥ saty
api sarvavyavahārocchedii mahāpralaye parameśvarāugrahād īśvarāṇāṃ hiraṇyagarbhādīāṃ kalpātaravyavahārāusaṃdhāopapatteḥ yady api prākṛtāḥ prāṇio a jamātaravyavahāram ausaṃdadhāā dṛśyata iti tathāpi a tatprākṛtavad īśvarāṇāṃ
bhavitavyam yathā hi prāṇitvāviśeṣe pi mauṣyādistambaparyateṣu jñāaiśvaryādipratibadhaḥ pareṇa pareṇa bhūyā bhava dṛśyate tathā mauṣyādiṣv eva hiraṇyagarbhaparyateṣu jñāaiśvaryādyabhivyaktir api pareṇa pareṇa
bhūyasī bhavatīty etacchrutismṛtivādeṣv asakṛd evāukalpādau prādurbhavatāṃ pāramaiśvaryaṃ śrūyamāṇaṃ a śakyaṃ āstīti vaditum tataś cātītakalpāuṣṭhitaprakṛṣṭajñāakarmaṇām īśvarāṇāṃ hiraṇyagarbhādīāṃ vartamāakalpādau prādurbhavatāṃ parameśvarāugṛhītāāṃ suptapratibuddhavat
kalpātaravyavahārāusaṃdhāopapattiḥ tathā ca śrutiḥ yo brahmāṇaṃ vidadhāti pūrvaṃ yo vai vaidāś ca prahiṇoti tasmai thi devam ātmabuddhiprakāśaṃ mumukṣurvai śaraṇam ahaṃ
prapadye iti smarati ca śauakādayaḥ madhucchadaḥprabhṛtibhir ṛṣibhir dāśatayyo dṛṣṭāḥ iti prativedaṃ caivam eva kāṇḍarṣyādayaḥ smaryate śrutir api ṛṣijñāapūrvakam eva matreṇāuṣṭhāaṃ
darśayati yo ha vā aviditārṣeyacchadodaivatabrāhmaṇea matreṇa yājayati vādhyāpayati vā sthāṇuṃ varcchati gartaṃ vā pratipadyate ity upakramya tasmād etāi matre matre
vidyāt iti prāṇiāṃ ca sukhaprāptaye dharmo vidhīyate duḥkhaparihārāya cādharmaḥ pratiṣidhyate dṛṣṭāuśravikasukhaduḥkhaviṣayau ca rāgadveṣau bhavataḥ a vilakṣaṇaviṣayau ityato dharmādharmaphalabhūtottarottarā sṛṣṭiriṣpadyamāā pūrvasṛṣṭisadṛśyeva

tasmāttattasya rocate iti pralīyamāamapi cedaṃ jagacchaktyavaśeṣameva pralīyate śaktimūlameva ca prabhavati itarathā ākasmikatvaprasaṅgāt a cāekākārāḥ śaktayaḥ śakyāḥ kalpayitum tataśca vicchidya vicchidyāpyudbhavatāṃ
bhūrādilokapravāhāṇām devatiryaṅmauṣyalakṣaṇāāṃ ca prāṇiikāyapravāhāṇām varṇāśramadharmaphalavyavasthāāṃ cāādau saṃsāre iyatatvamidriyaviṣayasaṃbadhaiyatatvavatpratyetavyam a hīdriyaviṣayasaṃbadhādervyavahārasya pratisargamayathātvaṃ ṣaṣṭhedriyaviṣayakalpaṃ śakyamutprekṣitum ataśca sarvakalpāāṃ tulyavyavahāratvāt kalpātaravyavahārāusaṃdhāakṣamatvācceśvarāṇāṃ samāaāmarūpā eva pratisargaṃ

yathā pūrvasmikalpe sūryācadramaḥprabhṛti jagat klṛptam tathāsmiapi kalpe parameśvarokalpayadityarthaḥ tathā agirvā akāmayata aādo devāāsyāmiti sa etamagaye kṛttikābhyaḥ puroḍāśamaṣṭākapālaṃ iravapat iti akṣatreṣṭividhau

tathā hi śrūyate subrahmaṇyārthavāde medhātither meṣa iti medhātithiṃ ha kāṇvāyaam idro meṣo bhūtvā jahāra iti smaryate ca ādityaḥ puruṣo bhūtvā

matrārthavādādiṣu vyavahārādityuktam yad apy uktam matrārthavādayor ayārthatvā a devatāvigrahādiprakāśaasāmarthyam iti atra brūmaḥ pratyayāpratyayau hi sadbhāvāsadbhāvayoḥ kāraṇam āyārthatvam aayārthatvaṃ vā tathā
hy ayārtham api prasthitaḥ pathi patitaṃ tṛṇaparṇādyastīty eva pratipadyate atrāha viṣama upayāsaḥ tatra hi tṛṇaparṇādiviṣayaṃ pratyakṣaṃ pravṛttam asti yea tadastitvaṃ
pratipadyate atra puar vidhyuddeśaikavākyabhāvea stutyarthe rthavāde a pārthagarthyea vṛttātaviṣayā pravṛttiḥ śakyādhyavasātum a hi mahāvākye rthapratyāyake vātaravākyasya pṛthakpratyāyakatvamasti yathā a surāṃ
pibet iti añvati vākye padatrayasaṃbadhātsurāpāapratiṣedha evaikorthovagamyate a puaḥ surāṃ pibediti padadvayasaṃbadhātsurāpāavidhirapīti atrocyate viṣama upayāsaḥ yuktaṃ yatsurāpāapratiṣedhe padāvayasyaikatvādavātaravākyārthasyāgrahaṇam vidhyuddeśārthavādayostvarthavādasthāi padāi pṛthagavayaṃ

kṣepiṣṭhā devatā vāyumeva svea bhāgadheyeopadhāvati sa evaiaṃ bhūtiṃ gamayati Maitrāyaṇī Saṃhitā ityeṣāmarthavādagatāāṃ padāām a hi bhavati vāyurvā ālabheta iti kṣepiṣṭhā
devatā vā ālabheta ityādi vāyusvabhāvasaṃkīrtaea tu avātaramavayaṃ pratipadya evaṃ viśiṣṭadaivatyamidaṃ karmeti vidhiṃ stuvati tadyatra yovātaravākyārthaḥ pramāṇātaragocaro bhavati tatra tadauvādeārthavādaḥ pravartate

vyākhyātaḥ api ca vidhibhirevedrādidaivatyāi havīṃṣi codayadbhirapekṣitamidrādīāṃ svarūpam a hi svarūparahitā idrādayaścetasyāropayituṃ śakyate a ca cetasyaārūḍhāyai tasyai tasyai devatāyai haviḥ pradātuṃ
śakyate śrāvayati ca yasyai devatāyai havirgṛhītaṃ syāttāṃ dhyāyedvaṣaṭ kariṣya iti a ca śabdamātramarthasvarūpaṃ saṃbhavati śabdārthayorbhedāt tatra yādṛśaṃ matrārthavādayoridrādīāṃ svarūpamavagataṃ a
tattādṛśaṃ śabdapramāṇakea pratyākhyātuṃ yuktam itihāsapurāṇamapi vyākhyātea mārgeṇa saṃbhavamatrārthavādamūlakatvāt prabhavati devatāvigrahādi sādhayitum pratyakṣādimūlamapi saṃbhavati bhavati hyasmākamapratyakṣamapi ciraṃtaāāṃ pratyakṣam tathā ca vyāsādayo
devādibhiḥ pratyakṣaṃ vyavaharatīti smaryate yastu brūyāt idāīṃtaāāmiva pūrveṣāmapi āsti devādibhirvyavahartuṃ sāmarthyamiti sa jagadvaicitryaṃ pratiṣedhet idāīmiva ca āyadāpi sārvabhaumaḥ kṣatriyostīti brūyāt
tataśca rājasūyādicodaā uparudhyāt idāīmiva ca kālātarepyavyavasthitaprāyāvarṇāśramadharmāpratijāīta tataśca vyavasthāvidhāyi śāstramaarthakaṃ kuryāt tasmāddharmotkarṣavaśācciraṃtaā devādibhiḥ pratyakṣaṃ vyavajahuriti śliṣyate api ca smarati svādhyāyād iṣṭadevatāsaṃprayogaḥ
ityādi yogopyaṇimādyaiśvaryaprāptiphalakaḥ smaryamāṇo a śakyate sāhasamātreṇa pratyākhyātum śrutiśca yogamāhātmyaṃ prakhyāpayati pṛthivyaptejoilakhe samutthite pañcātmake yogaguṇe pravṛtte a tasya rogo a jarā
a mṛtyuḥ prāptasya yogāgimayaṃ śarīram iti ṛṣīṇāmapi matrabrāhmaṇadarśiāṃ sāmarthyaṃ āsmadīyea sāmarthyeopamātuṃ yuktam tasmātsamūlamitihāsapurāṇam lokaprasiddhirapi a sati saṃbhave irālambaādhyavasātuṃ yuktā tasmādupapao
matrādibhyo devādīāṃ vigrahavattvādyavagamaḥ tataścārthitvādisaṃbhavādupapao devādīāmapi brahmavidyāyām adhikāraḥ kramamuktidarśaāyapyevamevopapadyate śugasya tadaādaraśravaṇāttadādravaṇātsūcyate hi apaśūdrādhikaraṇam yathā mauṣyādhikāraiyamamapodya devādīāmapi vidyāsvadhikāra uktaḥ tathaiva dvijātyadhikāraiyamāpavādea śūdrasyāpyadhikāraḥ
syādityetāmāśaṅkāṃ ivartayitumidamadhikaraṇamārabhyate tatra śūdrasyāpyadhikāraḥ syāditi tāvatprāptam arthitvasāmarthyayoḥ saṃbhavāt tasmācchūdro yajñeavaklṛptaḥ itivat śūdro vidyāyāmaavaklṛpta iti iṣedhāśravaṇāt yacca karmasvaadhikārakāraṇaṃ śūdrasyāagitvam a tadvidyāsvadhikārasyāpavādakam
a hyāhavaīyādirahitea vidyā vedituṃ a śakyate bhavati ca śrautaṃ liṅgaṃ śūdrādhikārasyopodbalakam saṃvargavidyāyāṃ hi jāaśrutiṃ pautrāyaṇaṃ śuśrūṣuṃ śūdraśabdea parāmṛśati aha hāre
tvā śūdra tavaiva saha gobhirastu iti viduraprabhṛtayaśca śūdrayoiprabhavā api viśiṣṭavijñāasaṃpaāḥ smaryate tasmādadhikriyate śūdro vidyāsvityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ a śūdrasyādhikāraḥ vedādhyayaābhāvāt adhītavedo
hi viditavedārtho vedārtheṣvadhikriyate a ca śūdrasya vedādhyayaamasti upaayaapūrvakatvādvedādhyayaasya upaayaasya ca varṇatrayaviṣayatvāt yattu arthitvam a tadasati sāmarthyedhikārakāraṇaṃ bhavati sāmarthyamapi a laukikaṃ
kevalamadhikārakāraṇaṃ bhavati śāstrīyerthe śāstrīyasya sāmarthyasyāpekṣitatvāt śāstrīyasya ca sāmarthyasyādhyayaairākaraṇea irākṛtatvāt yaccedam śūdro yajñeavaklṛptaḥ iti tat yāyapūrvakatvādvidyāyāmapyaavaklṛptatvaṃ dyotayati yāyasya sādhāraṇatvāt yatpuaḥ saṃvargavidyāyāṃ
śūdraśabdaśravaṇaṃ liṅgaṃ mayase a talliṅgam yāyābhāvāt yāyokte hi liṅgadarśaaṃ dyotakaṃ bhavati a cātra yāyosti kāmaṃ cāyaṃ śūdraśabdaḥ saṃvargavidyāyāmevaikasyāṃ śūdramadhikuryāt tadviṣayatvāt
a sarvāsu vidyāsu arthavādasthatvāttu a kvacidapyayaṃ śūdramadhikartumutsahate śakyate cāyaṃ śūdraśabdodhikṛtaviṣaye yojayitum kathamityucyate kamvara eametatsataṃ sayugvāamiva raikvamāttha ityasmāddhaṃsavākyādātmaoādaraṃ śrutavato jāaśruteḥ pautrāyaṇasya
śuk utpede tāmṛṣī raikvaḥ śūdraśabdeāea sūcayāṃbabhūva ātmaaḥ parokṣajñatākhyāpaāyeti gamyate jātiśūdrasyāadhikārāt kathaṃ puaḥ śūdraśabdea śugutpaā sūcyata iti ucyate tadādravaṇāt śucamabhidudrāva śucā
vā abhidudruve śucā vā raikvamabhidudrāva iti śūdraḥ avayavārthasaṃbhavāt rūḍhyarthasya cāsaṃbhavāt dṛśyate cāyamarthosyāmākhyāyikāyām kṣatriyatvagateścottaratra caitrarathea liṅgāt itaśca a jātiśūdro jāaśrutiḥ yatkāraṇaṃ

irdhārite jābālaṃ gautama upaetumauśāsituṃ ca pravavṛte aitadabrāhmaṇo vivaktumarhati samidhaṃ somyāharopa tvā eṣye a satyādagāḥ iti śrutiliṅgāt śravaṇādhyayaārthapratiṣedhātsmṛteśca itaśca a śūdrasyādhikāraḥ
yadasya smṛteḥ śravaṇādhyayaārthapratiṣedho bhavati vedaśravaṇapratiṣedhaḥ vedādhyayaapratiṣedhaḥ tadarthajñāāuṣṭhāayośca pratiṣedhaḥ śūdrasya smaryate śravaṇapratiṣedhastāvat atha hāsya vedamupaśrṛṇvatastrapujatubhyāṃ śrotrapratipūraṇam iti padyu ha vā etacchamaśāaṃ

pratipattavyaḥ ityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ brahmaivedamiha pratipattavyam kutaḥ pūrvottarālocaāt pūrvottarayorhi grathabhāgayorbrahmaiva irdiśyamāamupalabhāmahe ihaiva kathamakasmādatarāle vāyuṃ irdiśyamāaṃ pratipadyemahi pūrvatra tāvat tadeva śukraṃ
tadbrahma tadevāmṛtamucyate tasimallokāḥ śritāḥ sarve tadu ātyeti kaścaa iti brahma irdiṣṭam tadeva ihāpi saṃidhāāt jagatsarvaṃ prāṇa ejati iti ca lokāśrayatvapratyabhijñāāt
irdiṣṭamiti gamyate prāṇaśabdopyayaṃ paramātmayeva prayuktaḥ prāṇasya prāṇam iti darśaāt ejayitṛtvamapīdaṃ paramātmaa evopapadyate a vāyumātrasya tathā coktam a prāṇea āpāea martyo

savāyukasya jagato bhayahetutvābhidhāāt tadeva ihāpi saṃidhāāt mahadbhayaṃ vajramudyatam iti ca bhayahetutvaṃ pratyabhijñāāirdiṣṭamiti gamyate vajraśabdopyayaṃ bhayahetutvasāmāyātprayuktaḥ yathā hi vajramudyataṃ mamaiva śirasi

bhayāakaṃ vajropamitaṃ brahma tathā ca brahmaviṣayaṃ śrutyataram bhīṣāsmādvātaḥ pavate bhīṣodeti sūryaḥ bhīṣāsmādagiścedraśca mṛtyurdhāvati pañcamaḥ iti amṛtatvaphalaśravaṇādapi brahmaivedamiti gamyate brahmajñāāddhyamṛtatvaprāptiḥ tameva

kiṃ jyotiḥśabdaṃ cakṣurviṣayatamopahaṃ tejaḥ kiṃ vā paraṃ brahmeti kiṃ tāvatprāptam prasiddhameva tejo jyotiḥśabdamiti kutaḥ jyotiḥśabdasya rūḍhatvāt jyotiścaraṇābhidhāāt ityatra hi prakaraṇājjyotiḥśabdaḥ
svārthaṃ parityajya brahmaṇi vartate a ceha tadvatkiṃcitsvārthaparityāge kāraṇaṃ dṛśyate tathā ca āḍīkhaṇḍe atha yatraitadasmāccharīrādutkrāmatyathaitaireva raśmibhirūrdhvamākramate iti mumukṣorādityaprāptirabhihitā tasmātprasiddhameva tejo jyotiḥśabdamiti

puruṣaḥ iti ca viśeṣaṇāt yattūktaṃ mumukṣorādityaprāptirabhihiteti āsāvātyatiko mokṣaḥ gatyutkrātisaṃbadhāt a hyātyatike mokṣe gatyutkrātī sta iti vakṣyāmaḥ ākāśo arthātaratvādivyapadeśāt arthātaratvādivyapadeśādhikaraṇam ākāśo

prasiddham eva bhūtākāśam iti vicāre bhūtaparigraho yuktaḥ ākāśaśabdasya tasmi rūḍhatvāt āmarūpairvahaṇasya cāvakāśadāadvāreṇa tasmi yojayituṃ śakyatvāt sraṣṭṛtvādeś ca spaṣṭasya brahmaliṅgasyāśravaṇād ity
