arthātarabhūtam ākāśaṃ vyapadiśati a ca brahmaṇo aya āmarūpābhyām arthātaraṃ saṃbhavati sarvasya vikārajātasya āmarūpābhyām eva vyākṛtatvāt āmarūpayor api irvahaṇaṃ iraṅkuśaṃ a
brahmaṇo ayatra saṃbhavati aea jīveātmaāupraviśya āmarūpe vyākaravāṇi iti brahmakartṛkatvaśravaṇāt au jīvasyāpi pratyakṣaṃ āmarūpaviṣayaṃ irvoḍhṛtvam asti bāḍham asti abhedas tv iha
vivakṣitaḥ āmarūpairvahaṇābhidhāād eva ca sraṣṭṛtvādi brahmaliṅgam abhihitaṃ bhavati tad brahma tad amṛtaṃ sa ātmā iti ca brahmavādasya liṅgāi ākāśas talliṅgāt
ity asyaivāyaṃ prapañcaḥ suṣuptyutkrātyorbhedea suṣuptyadhikaraṇam vyapadeśādityauvartate bṛhadāraṇyake ṣaṣṭhe prapāṭhake katama ātmeti yoyaṃ vijñāamayaḥ prāṇeṣu hṛdyatarjyotiḥ puruṣaḥ ityupakramya bhūyāātmaviṣayaḥ prapañcaḥ kṛtaḥ
tatkiṃ saṃsārisvarūpamātrāvākhyāaparaṃ vākyam utāsaṃsārisvarūpapratipādaaparamiti viśayaḥ kiṃ tāvatprāptam saṃsārisvarūpamātraviṣayameveti kutaḥ upakramopasaṃhārābhyām upakrame yoyaṃ vijñāamayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti śārīraliṅgāt upasaṃhāre ca sa vā
eṣa mahāaja ātmā yoyaṃ vijñāamayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti tadaparityāgāt madhyepi buddhātādyavasthopayāsea tasyaiva prapañcaādityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ parameśvaropadeśaparamevedaṃ vākyam a śārīramātrāvākhyāaparam kasmāt suṣuptāvutkrātau
ca śārīrādbhedea parameśvarasya vyapadeśāt suṣuptau tāvat ayaṃ puruṣaḥ prājñeātmaā saṃpariṣvakto a bāhyaṃ kiṃcaa veda ātaram iti śārīrādbhedea parameśvaraṃ vyapadiśati tatra
puruṣaḥ śārīraḥ syāt tasya veditṛtvāt bāhyābhyataravedaaprasaṅge sati tatpratiṣedhasaṃbhavāt prājñaḥ parameśvaraḥ sarvajñatvalakṣaṇayā prajñayā ityamaviyogāt tathotkrātāvapi ayaṃ śārīra ātmā prājñeātmaāvārūḍha utsarjayāti iti
jīvādbhedea parameśvaraṃ vyapadiśati tatrāpi śārīro jīvaḥ syāt śarīrasvāmitvāt prājñastu sa eva parameśvaraḥ tasmātsuṣuptyutkrātyorbhedea vyapadeśātparameśvara evātra vivakṣita iti gamyate yaduktamādyatamadhyeṣu śārīraliṅgāt
tatparatvamasya vākyasyeti atra brūmaḥ upakrame tāvat yoyaṃ vijñāamayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti a saṃsārisvarūpaṃ vivakṣitam kiṃ tarhi aūdya saṃsārisvarūpaṃ pareṇa brahmaṇāsyaikatāṃ vivakṣati
yataḥ dhyāyatīva lelāyatīva ityevamādyuttaragrathapravṛttiḥ saṃsāridharmairākaraṇaparā lakṣyate tathopasaṃhārepi yathopakramamevopasaṃharati sa vā eṣa mahāaja ātmā yoyaṃ vijñāamayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti yoyaṃ vijñāamayaḥ prāṇeṣu
saṃsārī lakṣyate sa vā eṣa mahāaja ātmā parameśvara evāsmābhiḥ pratipādita ityarthaḥ yastu madhye buddhātādyavasthopayāsātsaṃsārisvarūpavivakṣāṃ mayate sa prācīmapi diśaṃ prasthāpitaḥ pratīcīmapi
diśaṃ pratiṣṭheta yato a buddhātādyavasthopayāseāvasthāvattvaṃ saṃsāritvaṃ vā vivakṣati kiṃ tarhi avasthārahitatvamasaṃsāritvaṃ ca kathametadavagamyate yat ata ūrdhvaṃ vimokṣāyaiva brūhi iti pade
pade pṛcchati yacca aavāgatastea bhavatyasaṅgo hyayaṃ puruṣaḥ iti pade pade prativakti aavāgataṃ puṇyeāavāgataṃ pāpea tīrṇo hi tadā sarvāñśokāhṛdayasya bhavati iti
ca tasmādasaṃsārisvarūpapratipādaaparamevaitadvākyamityavagatavyam patyādiśabdebhyaḥ itaścāsaṃsārisvarūpapratipādaaparamevaitadvākyamityavagatavyam yadasmivākye patyādayaḥ śabdā asaṃsārisvarūpapratipādaaparāḥ saṃsārisvabhāvapratiṣedhaāśca bhavati sarvasya vaśī sarvasyeśāaḥ sarvasyādhipatiḥ ityevaṃjātīyakā asaṃsārisvabhāvapratipādaaparāḥ sa a sādhuā karmaṇā
bhūyāo evāsādhuā kaīyā ityevaṃjātīyakāḥ saṃsārisvabhāvapratiṣedhaāḥ tasmādasaṃsārī parameśvara ihokta ityavagamyate iti śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācāryasya śrīgovidabhagavatpūjyapādaśiṣyasya śrīmacchaṃkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīrakamīmāṃsāsūtrabhāṣye prathamādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ murat prathamodhyāyaḥ
caturthaḥ pādaḥ āumāikam apy ekeṣām iti ce a śarīrarūpakaviyastagṛhīter darśayati ca āumāikādhikaraṇam āumāikam api aumāairūpitam api pradhāam ekeṣāṃ śākhiāṃ śabdavad
upalabhyate kāṭhake hi paṭhyate mahataḥ param avyaktam avyaktāt puruṣaḥ paraḥ iti tatra ya eva yaāmāo yatkramāś ca mahadavyaktapuruṣāḥ smṛtiprasiddhāḥ ta
eveha pratyabhijñāyate tatrāvyaktam iti smṛtiprasiddheḥ śabdādihīatvāc ca a vyaktam avyaktam iti vyutpattisaṃbhavāt smṛtiprasiddhaṃ pradhāam abhidhīyate atas tasya śabdavattvād aśabdatvam aupapaam
tad eva ca jagataḥ kāraṇaṃ śrutismṛtiyāyaprasiddhibhya iti cet aitad evam a hy etat kāṭhakavākyaṃ smṛtiprasiddhayor mahadavyaktayor astitvaparam a hy atra
yādṛśaṃ smṛtiprasiddhaṃ svatatraṃ kāraṇaṃ triguṇaṃ pradhāam tādṛśaṃ pratyabhijñāyate śabdamātraṃ hyatrāvyaktamiti pratyabhijñāyate sa ca śabdaḥ a vyaktamavyaktamiti yaugikatvāt ayasmiapi sūkṣme sudurlakṣye
ca prayujyate a cāyaṃ kasmiṃś cid rūḍhaḥ yā tu pradhāavādiāṃ rūḍhiḥ sā teṣām eva pāribhāṣikī satī a vedārthairūpaṇe kāraṇabhāvaṃ pratipadyate
a ca kramamātrasāmāyāt samāārthapratipattir bhavati asati tadrūpapratyabhijñāe a hyaścasthāe gāṃ paśyaaśvoyamityamūḍhodhyavasyati prakaraṇairūpaṇāyāṃ cātra a paraparikalpitaṃ pradhāaṃ pratīyate śarīrarūpakaviyastagṛhīteḥ śarīraṃ hyatra
ratharūpakaviyastamavyaktaśabdea parigṛhyate kutaḥ prakaraṇāt pariśeṣācca tathā hyaatarātīto gratha ātmaśarīrādīāṃ rathirathādirūpakaklṛptiṃ darśayati ātmāaṃ rathiaṃ viddhi śarīraṃ rathameva tu buddhiṃ tu sārathiṃ
viddhi maaḥ pragrahameva ca idriyāṇi hayāāhurviṣayāṃsteṣu gocarā ātmedriyamaoyuktaṃ bhoktetyāhurmaīṣiṇaḥ iti taiścedriyādibhirasaṃyataiḥ saṃsāramadhigacchati saṃyataistvadhvaaḥ pāraṃ tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padamāpoti iti darśayitatvā kiṃ
tadadhvaaḥ pāraṃ viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padamityasyāmākāṅkṣāyām tebhya eva prakṛtebhyaḥ idriyādibhyaḥ paratvea paramātmāamadhvaaḥ pāraṃ tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ darśayati idriyebhyaḥ parā hyarthā arthebhyaśca
paraṃ maaḥ maasastu parā buddhirbuddherātmā mahāparaḥ mahataḥ paramavyaktamavyaktātpuruṣaḥ paraḥ puruṣāa paraṃ kiṃcitsā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ iti tatra ya evedriyādayaḥ
pūrvasyāṃ ratharūpakakalpaāyām aśvādibhāvea prakṛtāḥ ta eveha parigṛhyate prakṛtahāāprakṛtaprakriyāparihārāya tatra idriyamaobuddhayas tāvat pūrvatra iha ca samāaśabdā eva arthās tu ye śabdādayo
viṣayā idriyahayagocaratvea irdiṣṭāḥ teṣāṃ cedriyebhyaḥ paratvam idriyāṇāṃ ca grahatvaṃ viṣayāṇām atigrahatvam iti śrutiprasiddheḥ viṣayebhyaś ca maasaḥ paratvam maomūlatvād viṣayedriyavyavahārasya maasas
tu parā buddhiḥ buddhiṃ hy āruhya bhogyajātaṃ bhoktāramupasarpati buddherātmā mahāparaḥ yaḥ saḥ ātmāaṃ rathiaṃ viddhi iti rathitveopakṣiptaḥ kutaḥ ātmaśabdāt bhoktuśca
bhogopakaraṇātparatvopapatteḥ mahattvaṃ cāsya svāmitvādupapaam athavā mao mahāmatirbrahmā pūrbuddhiḥ khyātirīśvaraḥ prajñā saṃviccitiścaiva smṛtiśca paripaṭhyate iti smṛteḥ yo brahmāṇaṃ vidadhāti pūrvaṃ yo
vai vedāṃśca prahiṇoti tasmai iti ca śruteḥ yā prathamajasya hiraṇyagarbhasya buddhiḥ sā sarvāsāṃ buddhīāṃ paramā pratiṣṭhā seha mahāātmetyucyate sā ca
pūrvatra buddhigrahaṇeaiva gṛhītā satī hirugihopadiśyate tasyā apyasmadīyābhyo buddhibhyaḥ paratvopapatteḥ etasmiṃstu pakṣe paramātmaviṣayeṇaiva pareṇa puruṣagrahaṇea rathia ātmao grahaṇaṃ draṣṭavyam paramārthatastu paramātmavijñāātmaorbhedābhāvāt
tadevaṃ śarīramevaikaṃ pariśiṣyate teṣvitarāṇīdriyādīi prakṛtāy eva paramapadadidarśayiṣayā samaukrāma pariśiṣyamāṇeehātyeāvyaktaśabdea pariśiṣyamāṇaṃ prakṛtaṃ śarīraṃ darśayatīti gamyate śarīredriyamaobuddhiviṣayavedaāsaṃyuktasya hyavidyāvato bhoktuḥ śarīrādīāṃ rathādirūpakakalpaayā saṃsāramokṣagatiirūpaṇea
pratyagātmabrahmāvagatiriha vivakṣitā tathā ca eṣa sarveṣu bhūteṣu gūḍhotmā a prakāśate dṛśyate tvagryayā buddhyā sūkṣmayā sūkṣmadarśibhiḥ iti vaiṣṇavasya paramapadasya duravagamatvamuktvā tadavagamārthaṃ
yogaṃ darśayati yacchedvāṅmaasī prājñastadyacchejjñāa ātmai jñāamātmai mahati iyacchettadyacchecchāta ātmai iti etaduktaṃ bhavati vācaṃ maasi saṃyacchet vāgādibāhyedriyavyāpāramutsṛjya maomātreṇāvatiṣṭheta maopi viṣayavikalpābhimukhaṃ vikalpadoṣadarśaea
jñāaśabdoditāyāṃ buddhāvadhyavasāyasvabhāvāyāṃ dhārayet tāmapi buddhiṃ mahatyātmai bhoktari agryāyāṃ vā buddhau sūkṣmatāpādaea iyacchet mahātaṃ tvātmāaṃ śāta ātmai prakaraṇavati parasmipuruṣe parasyāṃ kāṣṭhāyāṃ
pratiṣṭhāpayediti ca tadevaṃ pūrvāparālocaāyāṃ āstyatra paraparikalpitasya pradhāasyāvakāśaḥ sūkṣmaṃ tu tadarhatvāt uktam etat prakaraṇapariśeṣābhyāṃ śarīram avyaktaśabdam a pradhāam iti idam idāīm
āśaṅkyate katham avyaktaśabdārthatvaṃ śarīrasya yāvatā sthūlatvāt spaṣṭataram idaṃ śarīraṃ vyaktaśabdārtham aspaṣṭavacaas tv avyaktaśabda iti ata uttaram ucyate sūkṣmaṃ tu iha
kāraṇātmaā śarīraṃ vivakṣyate sūkṣmasyāvyaktaśabdārthatvāt yady api sthūlam idaṃ śarīraṃ a svayam avyaktaśabdam arhati tathāpi tasya tv ārambhakaṃ bhūtasūkṣmam avyaktaśabdam arhati
prakṛtiśabdaś ca vikāre dṛṣṭaḥ yathā gobhiḥ śrīṇīta matsaram iti śrutiś ca tad dhedaṃ tarhy avyākṛtam āsīt itīdam eva vyākṛtaāmarūpavibhiaṃ jagatprāgavasthāyāṃ
parityaktavyākṛtaāmarūpaṃ bījaśaktyavastham avyaktaśabdayogyaṃ darśayati tadadhīatvād arthavat atrāha yadi jagad idam aabhivyaktaāmarūpaṃ bījātmakaṃ prāg avastham avyaktaśabdārham abhyupagamyeta tadātmaā ca śarīrasyāpy avyaktaśabdārhatvaṃ
pratijñāyeta sa eva tarhi pradhāakāraṇavāda evaṃ saty āpadyeta asyaiva jagataḥ prāg avasthāyāḥ pradhāatveābhyupagamād iti atrocyate yadi vayaṃ svatatrāṃ kāṃcit prāgavasthāṃ
jagataḥ kāraṇatveābhyupagacchema prasañjayema tadā pradhāakāraṇavādam parameśvarādhīā tv iyam asmābhiḥ prāgavasthā jagato bhyupagamyate a svatatrā sā cāvaśyābhyupagatavyā arthavatī hi sā a
hi tayā viā parameśvarasya sraṣṭṛtvaṃ sidhyati śaktirahitasya tasya pravṛttyaupapatteḥ muktāāṃ ca puar autpattiḥ kutaḥ vidyayā tasyā bījaśakter dāhāt avidyātmikā hi
sā bījaśaktir avyaktaśabdairdeśyā parameśvarāśrayā māyāmayī mahāsuṣuptiḥ yasyāṃ svarūpapratibodharahitāḥ śerate saṃsāriṇo jīvāḥ tad etad avyaktaṃ kvacid ākāśaśabdairdiṣṭam etasmi u khalv akṣare
gārgyākāśa otaś ca protaś ca iti śruteḥ kvacid akṣaraśabdoditam akṣarāt parataḥ paraḥ iti śruteḥ kvaci māyeti sūcitam māyāṃ tu prakṛtiṃ
vidyāmāyiaṃ tu maheśvaram iti matravarṇāt avyaktā hi sā māyā tattvāyatvairūpaṇasyāśakyatvāt tad idaṃ mahataḥ param avyaktam ity uktam avyaktaprabhavatvāmahataḥ yadā hairaṇyagarbhī
buddhirmahā yadā tu jīvo mahā tadāpyavyaktādhīatvājjīvabhāvasya mahataḥ paramavyaktamityuktam avidyā hyavyaktam avidyāvattveaiva jīvasya sarvaḥ saṃvyavahāraḥ saṃtato vartate tacca avyaktagataṃ mahataḥ paratvamabhedopacārāttadvikāre
śarīre parikalpyate satyapi śarīravadidriyādīāṃ tadvikāratvāviśeṣe śarīrasyaivābhedopacārādavyaktaśabdea grahaṇam idriyādīāṃ svaśabdaireva gṛhītatvāt pariśiṣṭatvācca śarīrasya aye tu varṇayati dvividhaṃ hi śarīraṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ
ca sthūlam yadidamupalabhyate sūkṣmam yaduttaratra vakṣyate tadatarapratipattau raṃhati saṃpariṣvaktaḥ praśairūpaṇābhyām iti taccobhayamapi śarīramaviśeṣātpūrvatra rathatvea saṃkīrtitam iha tu sūkṣmamavyaktaśabdea parigṛhyate sūkṣmasyāvyaktaśabdārhatvāt
tadadhīatvācca badhamokṣavyavahārasya jīvāttasya paratvam yathārthādhīatvādidriyavyāpārasyedriyebhyaḥ paratvamarthāāmiti taistvetadvaktavyam aviśeṣeṇa śarīradvayasya pūrvatra rathatvea saṃkīrtitatvāt samāayoḥ prakṛtatvapariśiṣṭatvayoḥ kathaṃ sūkṣmameva śarīramiha gṛhyate a puaḥ
sthūlamapīti āmātasyārthaṃ pratipattuṃ prabhavāmaḥ āmātaṃ paryauyoktum āmātaṃ cāvyaktapadaṃ sūkṣmameva pratipādayituṃ śakoti etarat vyaktatvāttasyeti cet a ekavākyatādhīatvādarthaṃpratipatteḥ a hīme pūrvottare āmāte
ekavākyatāmaāpadya kaṃcidarthaṃ pratipādayataḥ prakṛtahāāprakṛtaprakriyāprasaṅgāt a cākāṅkṣāmatareṇaikavākyatāpratipattirasti tatrāviśiṣṭāyāṃ śarīradvayasya grāhyatvākāṅkṣāyāṃ yathākāṅkṣaṃ saṃbadheabhyupagamyamāe ekavākyataiva bādhitā bhavati kuta āmātasyārthasya pratipattiḥ a caivaṃ matavyam

vadadbhiḥ a hi guṇasvarūpamajñātvā guṇebhyaḥ puruṣasyātaraṃ śakyaṃ jñātumiti kvacicca vibhūtiviśeṣaprāptaye pradhāaṃ jñeyamiti smarati a cedamihāvyaktaṃ jñeyatveocyate padamātraṃ hyavyaktaśabdaḥ ehāvyaktaṃ jñātavyamupāsitavyaṃ
ceti vākyamasti a cāupadiṣṭaṃ padārthajñāaṃ puruṣārthamiti śakyaṃ pratipattum tasmādapi āvyaktaśabdea pradhāamabhidhīyate asmākaṃ tu ratharūpakaklṛptaśarīrādyausaraṇea viṣṇoreva paramaṃ padaṃ darśayitumayamupayāsa ityaavadyam vadatīti
ce a prājño hi prakaraṇāt atrāha sāṃkhyaḥ jñeyatvāvacaāt ity asiddham katham śrūyate hy uttaratrāvyaktaśabdoditasya pradhāasya jñeyatvavacaam aśabdam asparśam arūpam avyayaṃ
tathārasaṃ ityam agadhavac ca yat aādyaataṃ mahataḥ paraṃ dhruvaṃ icāyya taṃ mṛtyumukhāt pramucyate iti atra hi yādṛśaṃ śabdādihīaṃ pradhāaṃ mahataḥ
paraṃ smṛtau irūpitam tādṛśam eva icāyyatvea irdiṣṭam tasmāt pradhāam evedam tad eva cāvyaktaśabdairdiṣṭam iti atra brūmaḥ eha pradhāaṃ icāyyatvea irdiṣṭam
prājño hīha paramātmā icāyyatvea irdiṣṭa iti gamyate kutaḥ prakaraṇāt prājñasya hi prakaraṇaṃ vitataṃ vartate puruṣā a paraṃ kiṃcit sā kāṣṭhā
sā parā gatiḥ ityādiirdeśāt eṣa sarveṣu bhūteṣu guḍhotmā a prakāśate iti ca durjñāatvavacaea tasyaiva jñeyatvākāṅkṣaṇāt yacchedvāṅ maasī prājñaḥ iti ca
tajjñāāyaiva vāgādisaṃyamasya vihitatvāt mṛtyumukhapramokṣaṇaphalatvāc ca a hi pradhāamātraṃ icāyya mṛtyumukhāt pramucyata iti sāṃkhyair iṣyate cetaātmavijñāād dhi mṛtyumukhāt pramucyata iti teṣām
abhyupagamaḥ sarveṣu vedāteṣu prājñasyaivātmaośabdādidharmatvam abhilapyate tasmā a pradhāasyātra jñeyatvam avyaktaśabdairdiṣṭatvaṃ vā trayāṇām eva caivam upayāsaḥ praśaś ca itaś ca a
pradhāasyāvyaktaśabdavācyatvaṃ jñeyatvaṃ vā yasmāt trayāṇām eva padārthāām agijīvaparamātmaām asmi grathe kaṭhavallīṣu varapradāasāmarthyād vaktavyatayopayāso dṛśyate tadviṣaya eva ca praśaḥ ātoyasya praśa
upayāso vāsti tatra tāvat sa tvam agiṃ svargyam adhyeṣi mṛtyo prabrūhi taṃ śraddadhāāya mahyam ity agiviṣayaḥ praśaḥ yeyaṃ prete vicikitsā
mauṣyestīty eke āyam astīti caike etadvidyām auśiṣṭastvayāhaṃ varāṇām eṣa varas tṛtīyaḥ iti jīvaviṣayaḥ praśaḥ ayatra dharmād ayatrādharmād ayatrāsmāt kṛtākṛtāt ayatra
bhūtāc ca bhavyāc ca yat tat paśyasi tad vada iti paramātmaviṣayaḥ prativacaam api lokādim agiṃ tam uvāca tasmai yā iṣṭakā
yāvatīr vā yathā vā ity agiviṣayam hata ta idaṃ pravakṣyāmi guhyaṃ brahma saātaam yathā ca maraṇaṃ prāpya ātmā bhavati gautama
yoim aye prapadyate śarīratvāya dehiaḥ sthāṇum ayeusaṃyati yathākarma yathāśrutam iti vyavahitaṃ jīvaviṣayam a jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit ityādi bahuprapañcaṃ paramātmaviṣayam
aivaṃ pradhāaviṣayaḥ praśosti apṛṣṭatvāc cāupayasaīyatvaṃ tasyeti atrāha yoyam ātmaviṣayaḥ praśaḥ yeyaṃ prete vicikitsā mauṣyesti iti kiṃ sa evāyam ayatra dharmād
ayatrādharmāt iti puar aukṛṣyate kiṃ vā tatoyoyam apūrvaḥ praśa utthāpyata iti kiṃ cātaḥ sa evāyaṃ praśaḥ puar aukṛṣyata iti yady
ucyeta tadā dvayor ātmaviṣayayoḥ praśayor ekatāpatter agiviṣaya ātmaviṣayaś ca dvāv eva praśāv ity ato a vaktavyaṃ trayāṇāṃ praśopayāsāv iti athāyoyam
apūrvaḥ praśa utthāpyata ity ucyeta tato yathaiva varapradāavyatirekeṇa praśakalpaāyām adoṣaḥ evaṃ praśavyatirekeṇāpi pradhāopayāsakalpaāyām adoṣaḥ syād iti atrocyate aivaṃ vayam iha
varapradāavyatirekeṇa praśaṃ kaṃcit kalpayāmaḥ vākyopakramasāmarthyāt varapradāopakramā hi mṛtyuaciketaḥsaṃvādarūpā vākyapravṛttiḥ ā samāpteḥ kaṭhavallīāṃ lakṣyate mṛtyuḥ kila aciketase pitrā prahitāya trī varā
pradadau aciketāḥ kila teṣāṃ prathamea vareṇa pituḥ saumaasyaṃ vavre dvitīyeāgividyām tṛtīyeātmavidyām yeyaṃ prete iti varāṇām eṣa varas tṛtīyaḥ iti liṅgāt
tatra yadi ayatra dharmāt ity ayoyam apūrvaḥ praśa utthāpyeta tato varapradāavyatirekeṇāpi praśakalpaādvākyaṃ bādhyeta au praṣṭavyabhedād apūrvoyaṃ praśo bhavitum arhati apūrvo
hi praśo jīvaviṣayaḥ yeyaṃ prete vicikitsā mauṣyesti āstīti vicikitsābhidhāāt jīvaś ca dharmādigocaratvāt a ayatra dharmāt iti praśam arhati prājñas tu
dharmādyatītatvāt ayatra dharmāt iti praśam arhati praśacchāyā ca a samāā lakṣyate pūrvasyāstitvaāstitvaviṣayatvāt uttarasya dharmādyatītavastuviṣayatvāc ca tasmāt pratyabhijñāābhāvāt praśabhedaḥ a pūrvasyaivottaratrāukarṣaṇam
iti cet a jīvaprājñayor ekatvābhyupagamāt bhavet praṣṭavyabhedāt praśabhedo yady ayo jīvaḥ prājñātsyāt a tv ayatvam asti tattvamasi ityādiśrutyatarebhyaḥ iha ca
ayatra dharmāt ity asya praśasya prativacaam a jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit iti jamamaraṇapratiṣedhea pratipādyamāaṃ śārīraparameśvarayor abhedaṃ darśayati sati hi prasaṅge
pratiṣedho bhāgī bhavati prasaṅgaś ca jamamaraṇayoḥ śarīrasaṃsparśāc chārīrasya bhavati a parameśvarasya tathā svapātaṃ jāgaritātaṃ cobhau yeāupaśyati mahātaṃ vibhum ātmāaṃ matvā
dhīro a śocati iti svapajāgaritadṛśo jīvasyaiva mahattvavibhutvaviśeṣaṇasya maaea śokavicchedaṃ darśaya a prājñād ayo jīva iti darśayati prājñavijñāād dhi śokaviccheda iti
vedātasiddhātaḥ tathāgre yad eveha tad amutra yad amutra tad av iha mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpoti ya iha āeva paśyati iti
jīvaprājñabhedadṛṣṭim apavadati tathā jīvaviṣayasyāstitvaāstitvapraśasyāataram ayaṃ varaṃ aciketo vṛṇīṣva ity ārabhya mṛtyuā tais taiḥ kāmaiḥ pralobhyamāopi aciketā yadā a cacāla tadaiaṃ
mṛtyur abhyudayaiḥśreyasavibhāgapradarśaea vidyāvidyāvibhāgapradarśaea ca vidyābhīpsiaṃ aciketasaṃ maye a tvā kāmā bahavololupata iti praśasya praśam api tadīyaṃ praśaṃs ayad uvāca taṃ
durdarśaṃ gūḍham aupraviṣṭaṃ guhāhitaṃ gahvar eṣṭhaṃ purāṇam adhyātmayogādhigamea devaṃ matvā dhīro harṣaśokau jahāti iti teāpi jīvaprājñayor abheda eveha vivakṣita iti
gamyate yat praśaimittāṃ ca praśaṃsāṃ mahatīṃ mṛtyoḥ pratyapadyata aciketāḥ yadi taṃ vihāya praśaṃsāataram ayam eva praśam upakṣipet asthāa eva sā
sarvā praśaṃsā prasāritā syāt tasmāt yeyaṃ prete ity asyaiva praśasyaitad aukarṣaṇam ayatra dharmāt iti yat tu praśacchāyāvailakṣaṇyam uktam tad adūṣaṇam
tadīyasyaiva viśeṣasya puaḥ pṛcchyamāatvāt pūrvatra hi dehādivyatiriktasyātmaostitvaṃ pṛṣṭam uttaratra tu tasyaivāsaṃsāritvaṃ pṛcchayata iti yāvad dhy avidyā a ivartate tāvad dharmādigocaratvaṃ
jīvasya jīvatvaṃ ca a ivartate taivṛttau tu prājña eva tattvamasi iti śrutyā pratyāyyate a cāvidyāvattve tadapagame ca vastuaḥ kaścid viśeṣosti
yathā kaścit saṃ tamase patitāṃ kāṃcid rajjum ahiṃ mayamāo bhīto vepamāaḥ palāyate taṃ cāparo brūyāt mā bhaiṣīḥ āyam ahiḥ rajjur
eveti sa ca tadupaśrutyāhikṛtaṃ bhayam utsṛjed vepathuṃ palāyaaṃ ca a tv ahibuddhikāle tadapagamakāle ca vastuaḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ syāt tathaivaitad api
draṣṭavyam tataś ca a jāyate mriyate vā ity evamādyapi bhavaty astitvaāstitvapraśasya prativacaam sūtraṃ tv avidyākalpitajīvaprājñabhedāpekṣayā yojayitavyam ekatvepi hy ātmaviṣayasya praśasya
prāyaṇāvasthāyāṃ dehavyatiriktāstitvamātravicikitsaāt kartṛtvādisaṃsārasvabhāvāapohaāc ca pūrvasya paryāyasya jīvaviṣayatvam utprekṣyate uttarasya tu dharmādyatyayasaṃkīrtaāt prājñaviṣayatvam iti tataś ca yuktā agijīvaparamātmakalpaā pradhāakalpaāyāṃ tu a
varapradāaṃ a praśo a prativacaam iti vaiṣamyam mahadvacca yathā mahacchabdaḥ sāṃkhyaiḥ sattāmātrepi prathamaje prayuktaḥ a tameva vaidikepi prayogebhidhatte buddherātmā mahāparaḥ
mahātaṃ vibhumātmāam vedāhametaṃ puruṣaṃ mahātam ityevamādāvātmaśabdaprayogādibhyo hetubhyaḥ tathāvyaktaśabdopi a vaidike prayoge pradhāamabhidhātumarhati ataśca āstyāumāikasya śabdavattvam camasavadaviśeṣāt camasādhikaraṇam puarapi pradhāavādī aśabdatvaṃ
pradhāasyāsiddhamityāha kasmāt matravarṇāt ajāmekāṃ lohitaśuklakṛṣṇāṃ vahvīḥ prajāḥ sṛjamāāṃ sarūpāḥ ajo hyeko juṣamāṇouśete jahātyeāṃ bhuktabhogāmajoyaḥ iti atra hi matre lohitaśuklakṛṣṇaśabdaiḥ rajaḥsattvatamāṃsyabhidhīyate
lohitaṃ rajaḥ rañjaātmakatvāt śuklaṃ sattvam prakāśātmakatvāt kṛṣṇaṃ tamaḥ āvaraṇātmakatvāt teṣāṃ sāmyāvasthā avayavadharmairvyapadiśyate lohitaśuklakṛṣṇeti a jāyata iti ca ajā syāt mūlaprakṛtiravikṛtiḥ
ityabhyupagamāt avajāśabdaśchāgyāṃ rūḍhaḥ bāḍham sā tu rūḍhiriha āśrayituṃ śakyā vidyāprakaraṇāt sā ca bahvīḥ prajāstraiguṇyāvitā jaayati tāṃ prakṛtimaja ekaḥ puruṣo juṣamāṇaḥ
prīyamāṇaḥ sevamāo vā auśetetāmevāvidyayā ātmatveopagamya sukhī duḥkhī mūḍhohamityavivekitayā saṃsarati ayaḥ puarajaḥ puruṣa utpaavivekajñāo virakto jahātyeāṃ prakṛtiṃ bhuktabhogāṃ kṛtabhogāpavargāṃ parityajati mucyata
ityarthaḥ tasmācchrutimūlaiva pradhāādikalpaā kāpilāāmityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ āea matreṇa śrutimattvaṃ sāṃkhyavādasya śakyamāśrayitum a hyayaṃ matraḥ svātatryeṇa kaṃcidapi vādaṃ samarthayitumutsahate sarvatrāpi yayā
kayācitkalpaayā ajātvādisaṃpādaopapatteḥ sāṃkhyavāda evehābhipreta iti viśeṣāvadhāraṇakāraṇābhāvāt camasavat yathā hi arvāgbilaścamasa ūrdhvabudhaḥ ityasmimatre svātatryeṇāyaṃ āmāsau camasobhipreta iti a śakyate iyatum sarvatrāpi
yathākathaṃcidarvāgbilatvādikalpaopapatteḥ evamihāpyaviśeṣaḥ ajāmekām ityasya matrasya āsmimatre pradhāamevājābhipreteti śakyate iyatum tatra tu idaṃ tacchira eṣa hyarvāgbilaścamasa ūrdhvabuddhaḥ iti vākyaśeṣāccamasaviśeṣapratipattirbhavati iha puaḥ
keyamajā pratipattavyetyatra brūmaḥ jyotirupakramā tu tathā hy adhīyata eke parameśvarād utpaā jyotiḥpramukhā tejobaalakṣaṇā caturvidhasya bhūtagrāmasya prakṛtibhūteyam ajā pratipattavyā tuśabdo vadhāraṇārthaḥ
bhūtatrayalakṣaṇaiveyam ajā vijñeyā a guṇatrayalakṣaṇā kasmāt tathā hy eke śākhias tejobaāāṃ parameśvarād utpattim āmāya teṣām eva rohitādirūpatām āmaati yad age
rohitaṃ rūpaṃ tejasas tadrūpaṃ yacchuklaṃ tad apāṃ yat kṛṣṇaṃ tad aasya iti tāy eveha tejobaāi pratyabhijñāyate rohitādiśabdasāmāyāt rohitādīāṃ ca śabdāāṃ
rūpaviśeṣeṣu mukhyatvād bhāktatvāc ca guṇaviṣayatvasya asaṃdigdhea ca saṃdigdhasya igamaaṃ yāyyaṃ mayate tathehāpi brahmavādio vadati kiṃkāraṇaṃ brahma Śvet ity upakramya te
dhyāayogāugatā apaśya devātmaśaktiṃ svaguṇairigūḍhām iti pārameśvaryāḥ śakteḥ samastajagadvidhāyiyā vākyopakrame vagamāt vākyaśeṣe pi māyāṃ tu prakṛtiṃ vidyā māyiaṃ tu maheśvaram iti
yo yoiṃ yoim adhitiṣṭhaty ekaḥ iti ca tasyā evāvagamā a svatatrā kācit prakṛtiḥ pradhāaṃ āmājām atreṇāmāyata iti śakyate vaktum prakaraṇāt
tu saiva daivī śaktir avyākṛtaām arūpā āmarūpayoḥ prāg avasthā aeāpi matreṇāmāyata ity ucyate tasyāś ca svavikāraviṣayeṇa trairūpyeṇa trairūpyam uktam kathaṃ
puas tejobaātmaā trairūpyeṇa trirūpā ajā pratipattuṃ śakyate yāvatā a tāvat tejobaeṣvajākṛtir asti a ca tejobaāāṃ jātiśravaṇādajātiimitto py ajāśabdaḥ saṃbhavatīti ata
uttaraṃ paṭhati kalpaopadeśācca madhvādivadavirodhaḥ āyamajākṛtiimittojāśabdaḥ āpi yaugikaḥ kiṃ tarhi kalpaopadeśoyam ajārūpakaklṛptistejobaalakṣaṇāyāścarācarayoerupadiśyate yathā hi loke yadṛcchayā kācidajā rohitaśuklakṛṣṇavarṇā syādbahubarkarā sarūpabarkarā ca
tāṃ ca kaścidajo juṣamāṇouśayīta kaściccaiāṃ bhuktabhogāṃ jahyāt evamiyamapi tejobaalakṣaṇā bhūtaprakṛtistrivarṇā bahu sarūpaṃ carācaralakṣaṇaṃ vikārajātaṃ jaayati aviduṣā ca kṣetrajñeopabhujyate viduṣā ca
parityajyata iti a cedamāśaṅkitavyam ekaḥ kṣetrajñouśete ayo jahātītyataḥ kṣetrajñabhedaḥ pāramārthikaḥ pareṣāmiṣṭaḥ prāpotīti a hīyaṃ kṣetrajñabhedapratipipādayiṣā kiṃtu badhamokṣavyavasthāpratipipādayiṣaivaiṣā prasiddhaṃ tu bhedamaūdya
badhamokṣavyavasthā pratipādyate bhedastūpādhiimitto mithyājñāakalpitaḥ a pāramārthikaḥ eko devaḥ sarvabhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarvavyāpī sarvabhūtātarātmā ityādiśrutibhyaḥ madhvādivat yathā ādityasyāmadhuo madhutvam vācaścādheordheutvam dyulokādīāṃ cāagīāmagitvam
ityevaṃjātīyakaṃ kalpyate evamidamaajāyā ajātvaṃ kalpyata ityarthaḥ tasmādavirodhastejobaeṣvajāśabdaprayogasya a saṃkhyopasaṃgrahādapi āābhāvādatirekācca saṃkhyopasaṃgrahādhikaraṇam evaṃ parihṛtepyajāmatre puarapyayasmāmatrātsāṃkhyaḥ pratyavatiṣṭhate yasmipañca pañcajaā ākāśaśca pratiṣṭhitaḥ tameva
maya ātmāaṃ vidvābrahmāmṛtomṛtam iti asmimatre pañca pañcajaā iti pañcasaṃkhyāviṣayā aparā pañcasaṃkhyā śrūyate pañcaśabdadvayadarśaāt ta ete pañca pañcakāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ saṃpadyate tayā
ca pañcaviṃśatisaṃkhyayā yāvataḥ saṃkhyeyā ākāṅkṣyate tāvatyeva ca tattvāi sāṃkhyaiḥ saṃkhyāyate mūlaprakṛtiravikṛtirmahadādyāḥ prakṛtivikṛtayaḥ sapta ṣoḍaśakaśca vikāro a prakṛtira vikṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ iti
tayā śrutiprasiddhayā pañcaviṃśatisaṃkhyayā teṣāṃ smṛtiprasiddhāāṃ pañcaviṃśatestattvāāmupasaṃgrahātprāptaṃ puaḥ śrutimattvameva pradhāādīām tato brūmaḥ a saṃkhyopasaṃgrahādapi pradhāādīāṃ śrutimattvaṃ pratyāśā kartavyā kasmāt āābhāvāt āā
hyetāi pañcaviṃśatistattvāi aiṣāṃ pañcaśaḥ pañcaśaḥ sādhāraṇo dharmosti yea pañcaviṃśateratarāle parāḥ pañca pañca saṃkhyā iviśera a hyekaibadhaamatareṇa āābhūteṣu dvitvādikāḥ saṃkhyā iviśate
athocyeta pañcaviṃśatisaṃkhyaiveyamavayavadvāreṇa lakṣyate yathā pañca sapta ca varṣāṇi a vavarṣa śatakratuḥ iti dvādaśavārṣikīmaāvṛṣṭiṃ kathayati tadvaditi tadapi opapadyate ayamevāsmipakṣe doṣaḥ yallakṣaṇāśrayaṇīyā
syāt paraścātra pañcaśabdo jaaśabdea samastaḥ pañcajaā iti bhāṣikasvareṇaikapadatvaiścayāt prayogātare ca pañcāāṃ tvā pañcajaāām ityaikapadyaikasvaryaikavibhaktikatvāvagamāt samastatvācca a vīpsā pañca pañca iti
tea a pañcakadvayagrahaṇaṃ pañca pañceti a ca pañcasaṃkhyāyā ekasyāḥ pañcasaṃkhyayā parayā viśeṣaṇam pañca pañcakāḥ iti upasarjaasya viśeṣaṇeāsaṃyogāt avāpaapañcasaṃkhyākā jaā eva
puaḥ pañcasaṃkhyayā viśeṣyamāṇāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ pratyeṣyate yathā pañca pañcapūlya iti pañcaviṃśatiḥ pūlāḥ pratīyate tadvat eti brūmaḥ yuktaṃ yatpañcapūlīśabdasya samāhārābhiprāyatvāt katīti satyāṃ
bhedākāṅkṣāyāṃ pañca pañcapūlya iti viśeṣaṇam iha tu pañca jaā ityādita eva bhedopādāātkatītyasatyāṃ bhedākāṅkṣāyāṃ a pañca pañcajaā iti viśeṣaṇaṃ bhavet bhavadapīdaṃ
viśeṣaṇaṃ pañcasaṃkhyāyā eva bhavet tatra cokto doṣaḥ tasmātpañca pañcajaā iti a pañcaviṃśatitattvābhiprāyam atirekācca a pañcaviṃśatitattvābhiprāyam atireko hi bhavatyātmākāśābhyāṃ pañcaviṃśatisaṃkhyāyāḥ ātmā
tāvadiha pratiṣṭhāṃ pratyādhāratvea irdiṣṭaḥ yasmi iti saptamīsūcitasya tameva maya ātmāam ityātmatveāukarṣaṇāt ātmā ca cetaaḥ puruṣaḥ sa ca pañcaviṃśatāvatargata eveti a
tasyaivādhāratvamādheyatvaṃ ca yujyeta arthātaraparigrahe vā tattvasaṃkhyātirekaḥ siddhātaviruddhaḥ prasajyeta tathā ākāśaśca pratiṣṭhitaḥ ityākāśasyāpi pañcaviṃśatāvatargatasya a pṛthagupādāaṃ yāyyam arthātaraparigrahe coktaṃ dūṣaṇam kathaṃ
ca saṃkhyāmātraśravaṇe satyaśrutāāṃ pañcaviṃśatitattvāāmupasaṃgrahaḥ pratīyeta jaaśabdasya tattveṣvarūḍhatvāt arthātaropasaṃgrahepi saṃkhyopapatteḥ kathaṃ tarhi pañca pañcajaā iti ucyate diksaṃkhye saṃjñāyām iti viśeṣasmaraṇātsaṃjñāyāmeva pañcaśabdasya
jaaśabdea samāsaḥ tataśca rūḍhatvābhiprāyeṇaiva kecitpañcajaā āma vivakṣyate a sāṃkhyatattvābhiprāyeṇa te katītyasyāmākāṅkṣāyāṃ puaḥ pañceti prayujyate pañcajaā āma ye kecit te ca
pañcaivetyarthaḥ saptarṣayaḥ sapteti yathā ke puaste pañcajaā āmeti taducyate prāṇādayo vākyaśeṣāt yasmipañca pañcajaāḥ ityata uttarasmimatre brahmasvarūpairūpaṇāya prāṇādayaḥ pañca irdiṣṭāḥ prāṇasya
prāṇamuta cakṣuṣaścakṣuruta śrotrasya śrotramaasyāaṃ maaso ye mao viduḥ iti tetra vākyaśeṣagatāḥ saṃidhāātpañcajaā vivakṣyate kathaṃ puaḥ prāṇādiṣu jaaśabdaprayogaḥ tattveṣu vā kathaṃ
jaaśabdaprayogaḥ samāe tu prasiddhyatikrame vākyaśeṣavaśātprāṇādaya eva grahītavyā bhavati jaasaṃbadhācca prāṇādayo jaaśabdabhājo bhavati jaavacaaśca puruṣaśabdaḥ prāṇeṣu prayuktaḥ te vā ete pañca
brahmapuruṣāḥ ityatra prāṇo ha pitā prāṇo ha mātā ityādi ca brāhmaṇam samāsabalācca samudāyasya rūḍhatvamaviruddham kathaṃ puarasati prathamaprayoge rūḍhiḥ śakyāśrayitum śakyā
udbhidādivadityāha prasiddhārthasaṃidhāe hyaprasiddhārthaḥ śabdaḥ prayujyamāaḥ samabhivyāhārāttadviṣayo iyamyate yathā udbhidā yajeta yūpaṃ chiatti vediṃ karoti iti tathā ayamapi pañcajaaśabdaḥ samāsāvākhyāādavagatasaṃjñābhāvaḥ saṃjñyākāṅkṣī
vākyaśeṣasamabhivyāhṛteṣu prāṇādiṣu vartiṣyate kaiścittu devāḥ pitaro gadharvā asurā rakṣāṃsi ca pañca pañcajaā vyākhyātāḥ ayaiśca catvāro varṇā iṣādapañcamāḥ parigṛhītāḥ kvacicca yatpāñcajayayā
viśā iti prajāparaḥ prayogaḥ pañcajaaśabdasya dṛśyate tatparigrahepīha a kaścidvirodhaḥ ācāryastu a pañcaviṃśatestattvāāmiha pratītirastītyevaṃparatayā prāṇādayo vākyaśeṣāt iti jagāda bhaveyustāvatprāṇādayaḥ pañcajaā mādhyaṃdiāām
yeaṃ prāṇādiṣvāmaati kāṇvāāṃ tu kathaṃ prāṇādayaḥ pañcajaā bhaveyuḥ yeaṃ prāṇādiṣu āmaatīti ata uttaraṃ paṭhati jyotiṣaikeṣāmasatyae asatyapi kāṇvāāmae jyotiṣā teṣāṃ pañcasaṃkhyā
pūryeta tepi hi yasmipañca pañcajaāḥ ityataḥ pūrvasmimatre brahmasvarūpairūpaṇāyaiva jyotiradhīyate taddevā jyotiṣāṃ jyotiḥ iti kathaṃ puarubhayeṣāmapi tulyavadidaṃ jyotiḥ paṭhyamāaṃ samāamatragatayā pañcasaṃkhyayā

iti śreṣṭhatvairdhāraṇāya prajāpatigamaam tadvacaāccaikaikotkramaṇeāvayavyatirekābhyāṃ prāṇaśraiṣṭhyapratipattiḥ tasmai baliharaṇam iti caivaṃjātīyakosmadādiṣviva vyavahārougamyamāobhimāivyapadeśaṃ draḍhayati tatteja aikṣata ityapi parasyā eva devatāyā adhiṣṭhātryāḥ svavikāreṣvaugatāyā iyamīkṣā
vyapadiśyata iti draṣṭavyam tasmādvilakṣaṇamevedaṃ brahmaṇo jagat vilakṣaṇatvācca a brahmaprakṛtikamityākṣipte pratividhatte dṛśyate tu tuśabdaḥ pakṣaṃ vyāvartayati yad uktam vilakṣaṇatvā edaṃ jagad
brahmaprakṛtikam iti āyam ekātaḥ dṛśyate hi loke cetaatvea prasiddhebhyaḥ puruṣādibhyo vilakṣaṇāāṃ keśaakhādīām utpattiḥ acetaatvea ca prasiddhebhyo gomayādibhyo vṛścikādīām av acetaāy
eva puruṣādiśarīrāṇy acetaāāṃ keśaakhādīāṃ kāraṇāi acetaāy eva ca vṛścikādiśarīrāṇy acetaāāṃ gomayādīāṃ kāryāṇīti ucyate evam api kiṃcid acetaaṃ cetaasyāyataabhāvam upagacchati kiṃci
ety asty eva vailakṣaṇyam mahāṃś cāyaṃ pāriṇāmikaḥ svabhāvaviprakarṣaḥ puruṣādīāṃ keśaakhādīāṃ ca rūpādibhedāt tathā gomayādīāṃ vṛścikādīāṃ ca atyatasārūpye ca prakṛtivikārabhāva eva
pralīyeta athocyeta asti kaścit pārthivatvādisvabhāvaḥ puruṣādīāṃ keśaakhādiṣv auvartamāo gomayādīāṃ ca vṛścikādiṣv iti brahmaṇo pi tarhi sattālakṣaṇaḥ svabhāva ākāśādiṣv auvartamāo dṛśyate
vilakṣaṇatvea ca kāraṇea brahmaprakṛtikatvaṃ jagato dūṣayatā kim aśeṣasya brahmasvabhāvasyāauvartaaṃ vilakṣaṇatvam abhipreyate uta yasya kasyacit atha caitayasyeti vaktavyam prathame vikalpe samastaprakṛtivikārabhāvocchedaprasaṅgaḥ
a hyasatyatiśaye prakṛtivikārabhāva iti bhavati dvitīye cāsiddhatvam dṛśyate hi sattālakṣaṇo brahmasvabhāva ākāśādiṣvauvartamāa ityuktam tṛtīye tu dṛṣṭātābhāvaḥ kiṃ hi yaccaitayeāavitaṃ tadabrahmaprakṛtikaṃ
dṛṣṭamiti brahmakāraṇavādiaṃ pratyudāhriyeta samastasyāsya vastujātasya brahmaprakṛtikatvābhyupagamāt āgamavirodhas tu prasiddha eva cetaaṃ brahma jagataḥ kāraṇaṃ prakṛtiścetyāgamatātparyasya prasādhitatvāt yat tūktaṃ pariiṣpaatvād brahmaṇi
pramāṇātarāṇi saṃbhaveyur iti tad api maorathamātram rūpādyabhāvād dhi āyam arthaḥ pratyakṣasya gocaraḥ liṅgādyabhāvāc ca āumāādīām āgamamātrasamadhigamya eva tv ayam artho
dharmavat tathā ca śrutiḥ aiṣā tarkeṇa matirāpaeyā proktāyeaiva sujñāāya preṣṭha iti ko addhā veda ka iha pravocat iyaṃ visṛṣṭir yata
ābabhūva iti caite ṛcau ijasiddhāām apīśvarāṇāṃ durbodhatāṃ jagatkāraṇasya darśayataḥ smṛtir api bhavati acityāḥ khalu ye bhāvā a tāṃs tarkeṇa yojayet
iti avyakto yam acityo yam avikāryo yam ucyate iti ca a me viduḥ suragaṇāḥ prabhavaṃ a maharṣayaḥ ahamādir hi devāāṃ
maharṣīṇāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ iti caivaṃjātīyakā yad api śravaṇavyatirekeṇa maaaṃ vidadhac chabda eva tarkam apy ādartavyaṃ darśayatīty uktam āea miṣeṇa śuṣkatarkasyātrātmalābhaḥ
saṃbhavati śrutyaugṛhīta eva hy atra tarko ubhavāṅgatveāśrīyate svapātabuddhātayor ubhayor itaretaravyabhicārād ātmao avāgatatvam saṃprasāde ca prapañcaparityāgea sadātmaā saṃpatter iṣprapañcasadātmakatvam prapañcasya brahmaprabhavatvāt
kāryakāraṇāayatvayāyea brahmāvyatirekaḥ ity evaṃjātīyakaḥ tarkāpratiṣṭhāād iti ca kevalasya tarkasya vipralambhakatvaṃ darśayiṣyati yo pi cetaakāraṇaśravaṇabaleaiva samastasya jagataś cetaatām utprekṣeta tasyāpi vijñāaṃ
cāvijñāaṃ ca iti cetaācetaavibhāgaśravaṇaṃ vibhāvaāvibhāvaābhyāṃ caitayasya śakyata eva yojayitum parasyaiva tv idam api vibhāgaśravaṇaṃ a yujyate katham paramakāraṇasya hy atra
samastajagadātmaā samavasthāaṃ śrāvyate vijñāaṃ cāvijñāaṃ cābhavat iti tatra yathā cetaasyācetaabhāvo opapadyate vilakṣaṇatvāt evam acetaasyāpi cetaabhāvo opapadyate pratyuktatvāt tu vilakṣaṇatvasya yathā
śrutyaiva cetaaṃ kāraṇaṃ grahītavyaṃ bhavati asad iti ce a pratiṣedhamātratvāt yadi cetaaṃ śuddhaṃ śabdādihīaṃ ca brahma tadviparītasyācetaasyāśuddhasya śabdādimataśca kāryasya kāraṇamiṣyeta
asattarhi kāryaṃ prāgutpatteriti prasajyeta aiṣṭaṃ caitatsatkāryavādiastaveti cet aiṣa doṣaḥ pratiṣedhamātratvāt pratiṣedhamātraṃ hīdam āsya pratiṣedhasya pratiṣedhyamasti a hyayaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ prāgutpatteḥ sattvaṃ
kāryasya pratiṣeddhuṃ śakoti katham yathaiva hīdāīmapīdaṃ kāryaṃ kāraṇātmaā sat evaṃ prāgutpatterapīti gamyate a hīdāīmapīdaṃ kāryaṃ kāraṇātmāamatareṇa svatatramevāsti sarvaṃ taṃ parādādyoyatrātmaaḥ
sarvaṃ veda ityādiśravaṇāt kāraṇātmaā tu sattvaṃ kāryasya prāgutpatteraviśiṣṭam au śabdādihīaṃ brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam bāḍham a tu śabdādimatkāryaṃ kāraṇātmaā hīaṃ prāgutpatteridāīṃ
vā asti tea a śakyate vaktuṃ prāgutpatterasatkāryamiti vistareṇa caitat kāryakāraṇāayatvavāde vakṣyāmaḥ apītau tadvat prasaṅgād asamañjasam atrāha yadi sthaulyasāvayavattvācetaatvaparicchiatvāśuddhyādidharmakaṃ kāryaṃ brahmakāraṇakamabhyupagamyeta
tadāpītau pralaye pratisaṃsṛjyamāaṃ kāryaṃ kāraṇāvibhāgamāpadyamāaṃ kāraṇamātmīyea dharmeṇa dūṣayediti apītau kāraṇasyāpi brahmaṇaḥ kāryasyevāśuddhyādirūpatāprasaṅgāt sarvajñaṃ brahma jagataḥ kāraṇamityasamañjasamidamaupaiṣadaṃ darśaam api ca samastasya
vibhāgasyāvibhāgaprāpteḥ puarutpattau iyamakāraṇābhāvādbhoktṛbhogyādivibhāgeotpattira prāpotītyasamañjasam api ca bhoktṛṇāṃ pareṇa brahmaṇā avibhāgaṃ gatāāṃ karmādiimittapralayepi puarutpattāvabhyupagamyamāāyāṃ muktāāmapi puarutpattiprasaṅgādasamañjasam athedaṃ jagadapītāvapi vibhaktameva pareṇa brahmaṇāvatiṣṭheta
evamapyapītiśca a saṃbhavati kāraṇāvyatiriktaṃ ca kāryaṃ a saṃbhavatītyasamañjasameveti atrocyate a tu dṛṣṭātabhāvāt aivāsmadīye darśae kiṃcid asāmañjasyam asti yat tāvad abhihitam
kāraṇam api gacchat kāryaṃ kāraṇam ātmīyea dharmeṇa dūṣayed iti a tad dūṣaṇam kasmāt dṛṣṭātabhāvāt sati hi dṛṣṭātāḥ yathā kāraṇamapigacchatkāryaṃ kāraṇamātmīyea
dharmeṇa a dūṣayati tadyathā śarāvādayo mṛtprakṛtikā vikārā vibhāgāvasthāyāmuccāvacamadhyamaprabhedāḥ sataḥ puaḥ prakṛtimapigacchato a tāmātmīyea dharmeṇa saṃsṛjati rucakādayaśca suvarṇavikārā apītau a puaḥ
suvarṇamātmīyea dharmeṇa saṃsṛjati pṛthivīvikāraścaturvidho bhūtagrāmo a pṛthivīmapītāvātmīyea dharmeṇa saṃsṛjati tvatpakṣasya tu a kaściddṛṣṭātosti apītireva hi a saṃbhavet yadi kāraṇe kāryaṃ
svadharmeṇaivāvatiṣṭheta aayatvepi kāryakāraṇayoḥ kāryasya kāraṇātmatvam a tu kāraṇasya kāryātmatvam ārambhaṇaśabdādibhyaḥ ityatra vakṣyāmaḥ atyalpaṃ cedam ucyate kāryamapītāvātmīyea dharmeṇa kāraṇaṃ saṃsṛjediti sthitāvapi
hi samāoyaṃ prasaṅgaḥ kāryakāraṇayoraayatvābhyupagamāt idaṃ sarvaṃ yadayamātmā ātmaivedaṃ sarvam brahmaivedamamṛtaṃ purastāt sarvaṃ khalvidaṃ brahma ityevamādyābhir hi śrutibhir aviśeṣeṇa triṣv api

yathā svayaṃ prasāritayā māyayā māyāvī triṣv api kāleṣu a saṃspṛśyate avastutvāt evaṃ paramātmāpi saṃsāramāyayā a saṃspṛśyata iti yathā ca svapadṛgekaḥ

svapavadavyāhataḥ sthitau dṛśyate evamapītāvapi mithyājñāapratibaddhaiva vibhāgaśaktiraumāsyate etea muktāāṃ puarutpattiprasaṅgaḥ pratyuktaḥ samyagjñāea mithyājñāasyāpoditatvāt yaḥ puarayamateparo vikalpa utprekṣitaḥ athedaṃ jagadapītāvapi vibhaktameva pareṇa
brahmaṇāvatiṣṭheteti sopyaabhyupagamādeva pratiṣiddhaḥ tasmāt samañjasam idam aupaiṣadaṃ darśaam svapakṣadoṣāc ca svapakṣe caite prativādiaḥ sādhāraṇā doṣāḥ prāduḥṣyuḥ katham ity ucyate yattāvad

abhīpsatā iti ārṣaṃ dharmopadeśaṃ ca vedaśāstrāvirodhiā yas tarkeṇāusaṃdhatte sa dharmaṃ veda etaraḥ iti ca Mau bruva ayam eva ca tarkasyālaṃkāraḥ

pi tarhi svayaṃ saṃbadharūpatvād aapekṣyaivāparaṃ samavāyaṃ saṃbadhyeta tādātmyapratīteś ca dravyaguṇādīāṃ samavāyakalpaāarthakyam kathaṃ ca kāryam avayavidravyaṃ kāraṇeṣv avayavadravyeṣu vartamāaṃ vartate kiṃ

babhūva bhavati bhaviṣyatīti vā viśeṣyate yadi ca vadhyāputro pi kārakavyāpārād ūrdhvam abhaviṣyat tata idam apy upāpatsyata kāryabhāvo pi kārakavyāpārād ūrdhvaṃ

a tasmihitākaraṇādayo doṣāḥ prasajyate a hi tasya hitaṃ kiṃcitkartavyamasti ahitaṃ vā parihartavyam ityamuktasvabhāvatvāt a ca tasya jñāapratibadhaḥ śaktipratibadho vā kvacidapyasti

tapyatāpakayorjātyatarabhāvāabhyupagamāt ekaṃ hi brahma sarvātmakaṃ sarvasya prapañcasya kāraṇamabhyupagacchatām ekasyaivātmao viśeṣau tapyatāpakau a jātyatarabhūtau ityabhyupagatavyaṃ syāt yadi caitau tapyatāpakāvekasyātmao viśeṣau syātām
sa tābhyāṃ tapyatāpakābhyāṃ a irmucyeta iti tāpopaśātaye samyagdarśaamupadiśacchāstramaarthakaṃ syāt a hyauṣṇyaprakāśadharmasya pradīpasya tadavasthasyaiva tābhyāṃ irmokṣa upapadyate yopi jalataraṅgavīcīpheādyupayāsaḥ tatrāpi jalātmaa
ekasya vīcyādayo viśeṣā āvirbhāvatirobhāvarūpeṇa ityā eva iti samāo jalātmao vīcyādibhirairmokṣaḥ prasiddhaścāyaṃ tapyatāpakayorjātyatarabhāvo loke tathā hi arthī cārthaścāyoyabhiau lakṣyete yadyarthiaḥ svatoyortho
a syāt yasyārthio yadviṣayamarthitvaṃ sa tasyārtho ityasiddha eveti a tasya tadviṣayamarthitvaṃ syāt yathā prakāśātmaaḥ pradīpasya prakāśākhyortho ityasiddha eveti a tasya
tadviṣayamarthitvaṃ bhavati aprāpte hyartherthiorthitvaṃ syāditi tathārthasyāpyarthatvaṃ a syāt yadi syāt svārthatvameva syāt a caitadasti saṃbadhiśabdau hyetāvarthī cārthaśceti dvayoś ca saṃbadhioḥ
saṃbadhaḥ syāt aikasyaiva tasmādbhiāvetāvarthārthiau tathāarthāarthiāvapi arthioukūlaḥ arthaḥ pratikūlaḥ aarthaḥ tābhyāmekaḥ paryāyeṇobhābhyāṃ saṃbadhyate tatrārthasyālpīyastvāt bhūyastvāccāarthasya ubhāvapyarthāarthau aartha eveti tāpakaḥ sa ucyate
tapyastu puruṣaḥ ya ekaḥ paryāyeṇobhābhyāṃ saṃbadhyate iti tayostapyatāpakayorekātmatāyāṃ mokṣāupapattiḥ jātyatarabhāve tu tatsaṃyogahetuparihārāt syād api kadāci mokṣopapattir iti atrocyate a ekatvād
eva tapyatāpakabhāvāupapatteḥ bhaved eṣa doṣaḥ yady ekātmatāyāṃ tapyatāpakāv ayoyasya viṣayaviṣayibhāvaṃ pratipadyeyātām a tv etad asti ekatvād eva a hy agir
ekaḥ sa svam ātmāaṃ dahati prakāśayati vā saty apy auṣṇyaprakāśādidharmabhede pariṇāmitve ca kim u kūṭasthe brahmaṇy ekasmiṃs tapyatāpakabhāvaḥ saṃbhavet kva
puar ayaṃ tapyatāpakabhāvaḥ syād iti ucyate kiṃ a paśyasi karmabhūto jīvaddehastapyaḥ tāpakaḥ saviteti au taptirāma duḥkham sā cetayituḥ ācetaasya dehasya
yadi hi dehasyaiva taptiḥ syāt sā dehaāśe svayameva aśyatīti taāśāya sādhaaṃ aiṣitavyaṃ syāditi ucyate dehābhāvepi kevalasya cetaasya taptir a dṛṣṭā
a ca tvayāpi taptirāma vikriyā cetayituḥ kevalasyeṣyate āpi dehacetaayoḥ saṃhatatvam aśuddhyādidoṣaprasaṅgāt a ca taptereva taptimabhyupagacchasi kathaṃ tavāpi tapyatāpakabhāvaḥ sattvaṃ tapyam
tāpakaṃ rajaḥ iti cet a tābhyāṃ cetaasya saṃhatatvāupapatteḥ sattvāurodhitvāccetaopi tapyata iveti cet paramārthatastarhi aiva tapyata ityāpatati ivaśabdaprayogāt a cettapyate evaśabdo
doṣāya a hi ḍuṇḍubhaḥ sarpa iva ityetāvatā saviṣo bhavati sarpo vā ḍuṇḍubha sarpa iva ityetāvatā irviṣo bhavati ataścāvidyākṛtoyaṃ tapyatāpakabhāvaḥ a
pāramārthikaḥ ityabhyupagatavyamiti aivaṃ sati mamāpi kiṃcid duṣyati atha pāramārthikameva cetaasya tapyatvamabhyupagacchasi tavaiva sutarāmairmokṣaḥ prasajyeta ityatvābhyupagamācca tāpakasya tapyatāpakaśaktyorityatvepi saimittasaṃyogāpekṣatvāttapteḥ saṃyogaimittādarśaaivṛttau ātyatikaḥ
saṃyogoparamaḥ tataścātyatiko mokṣa upapaaḥ iti cet a adarśaasya tamaso ityatvābhyupagamāt guṇāāṃ codbhavābhibhavayoraiyatatvādaiyataḥ saṃyogaimittoparama iti viyogasyāpyaiyatatvātsāṃkhyasyaivāirmokṣoparihāryaḥ syāt aupaiṣadasya tu ātmaikatvābhyupagamāt ekasya

bhavati pradhāakāraṇavādo irākṛtaḥ paramāṇukāraṇavāda idāīṃ irākartavyaḥ tatrādau tāvat yo ṇuvādiā brahmavādii doṣa utprekṣyate sa pratisamādhīyate tatrāyaṃ vaiśeṣikāṇām abhyupagamaḥ kāraṇadravyasamavāyio guṇāḥ
kāryadravye samāajātīyaṃ guṇātaramārabhate śuklebhyastatubhyaḥ śuklasya paṭasya prasavadarśaāt tadviparyayādarśaācca tasmāccetaasya brahmaṇo jagatkāraṇatvebhyupagamyamāe kāryepi jagati caitayaṃ samaveyāt tadadarśaāttu a cetaaṃ brahma jagatkāraṇaṃ
bhavitumarhatīti imamabhyupagamaṃ tadīyayaiva prakriyayā vyabhicārayati mahaddīrghavad vā hrasvaparimaṇḍalābhyām mahaddīrghādhikaraṇam eṣā teṣāṃ prakriyā paramāṇavaḥ kila kaṃcitkālamaārabdhakāryā yathāyogaṃ rūpādimataḥ pārimāṇḍalyaparimāṇāśca tiṣṭhati te
ca paścādadṛṣṭādipuraḥsarāḥ saṃyogasacivāśca sato dvyaṇukādikrameṇa kṛtsaṃ kāryajātamārabhate kāraṇaguṇāśca kārye guṇātaram yadā dvau paramāṇū dvyaṇukamārabhete tadā paramāṇugatā rūpādiguṇaviśeṣāḥ śuklādayo dvyaṇuke śuklādīaparāārabhate
paramāṇuguṇaviśeṣastu pārimāṇḍalyaṃ a dvyaṇuke pārimāṇḍalyamaparamārabhate dvyaṇukasya parimāṇātarayogābhyupagamāt aṇutvahrasvatve hi dvyaṇukavartiī parimāṇe varṇayati yadāpi dve dvyaṇuke caturaṇukamārabhete tadāpi samāaṃ dvyaṇukasamavāyiāṃ śuklādīāmārambhakatvam
aṇutvahrasvatve tu dvyaṇukasamavāyiī api aivārabhete caturaṇukasya mahattvadīrghatvaparimāṇayogābhyupagamāt yadāpi bahavaḥ paramāṇavaḥ bahūi vā dvyaṇukāi dvyaṇukasahito vā paramāṇuḥ kāryamārabhate tadāpi samāaiṣā yojaā
tadevaṃ yathā paramāṇoḥ parimaṇḍalātsatoṇu hrasvaṃ ca dvyaṇukaṃ jāyate mahad dīrghaṃ ca tryaṇukādi a parimaṇḍalam yathā vā dvyaṇukādaṇorhrasvācca sato mahaddīrghaṃ ca
tryaṇukaṃ jāyate āṇu o hrasvam evaṃ cetaādbrahmaṇocetaaṃ jagajjaiṣyate ity abhyupagame kiṃ tava cchiam atha mayase virodhiā parimāṇātareṇākrātaṃ kāryadravyaṃ dvyaṇukādi ityato
ārambhakāṇi kāraṇagatāi pārimāṇḍalyādīi ityabhyupagacchāmi a tu cetaāvirodhiā guṇātareṇa jagata ākrātatvamasti yea kāraṇagatā cetaā kārye cetaātaraṃ ārabheta a hyacetaā āma cetaāvirodhī
kaścidguṇosti cetaāpratiṣedhamātratvāt tasmātpārimāṇḍalyādivaiṣamyātprāpoti cetaāyā ārambhakatvamiti maivaṃ maṃsthāḥ yathā kāraṇe vidyamāāāmapi pārimāṇḍalyādīāmaārambhakatvam evaṃ caitayasyāpi ity asyāṃśasya samāatvāt a ca parimāṇātarākrātatvaṃ pārimāṇḍalyādīāmaārambhakatve
kāraṇam prākparimāṇātarārambhātpārimāṇḍalyādīāmārambhakatvopapatteḥ ārabdhamapi kāryadravyaṃ prāgguṇārambhātkṣaṇamātramaguṇaṃ tiṣṭhatītyabhyupagamāt a ca parimāṇātarārambhe vyagrāṇi pārimāṇḍalyādīītyataḥ svasamāajātīyaṃ parimāṇātaraṃ ārabhate parimāṇātarasyāyahetutvābhyupagamāt kāraṇabahutvātkāraṇamahattvātpracayaviśeṣācca mahat tadviparītamaṇu etea dīrghatvahrasvatve
vyākhyāte iti hi kāṇabhujāi sūtrāṇi a ca saṃidhāaviśeṣātkutaścitkāraṇabahutvādīyevārabhate a pārimāṇḍalyādīīti ucyeta dravyātare guṇātare vā ārabhyamāṇe sarveṣāmeva kāraṇaguṇāāṃ svāśrayasamavāyāviśeṣāt tasmātsvabhāvādeva pārimāṇḍalyādīāmaārambhakatvam
tathā cetaāyā apīti draṣṭavyam saṃyogāc ca dravyādīāṃ vilakṣaṇāām utpattidarśaāt samāajātīyotpattivyabhicāraḥ dravye prakṛte guṇodāharaṇam ayuktam iti cet a dṛṣṭātea vilakṣaṇārambhamātrasya vivakṣitatvāt
a ca dravyasya dravyam evodāhartavyam guṇasya vā guṇa eveti kaści iyame hetur asti sūtrakāropi bhavatāṃ dravyasya guṇam udājahāra pratyakṣāpratyakṣāṇām apratyakṣatvāt
saṃyogasya pañcātmakaṃ a vidyate VS Cadrāad iti yathā pratyakṣāpratyakṣayor bhūmyākāśayoḥ samavaya saṃyogo pratyakṣaḥ evaṃ pratyakṣāpratyakṣeṣu pañcasu bhūteṣu samavayac charīram apratyakṣaṃ
syāt pratyakṣaṃ hi śarīram tasmā a pāñcabhautikam iti etad uktaṃ bhavati guṇaś ca saṃyogo dravyaṃ śarīram dṛśyate tu iti cātrāpi
vilakṣaṇotpattiḥ prapañcitā av evaṃ sati teaivaitad gatam eti brūmaḥ tat sāṃkhyaṃ pratyuktam etat tu vaiśeṣikaṃ prati av atideśo pi samāayāyatayā
kṛtaḥ etea śiṣṭāparigrahā api vyākhyātāḥ iti satyam etat tasyaiva tv ayaṃ vaiśeṣikaparīkṣārambhe tat prakriyāugatea idarśaea prapañcaḥ kṛtaḥ ubhayathā pi a
karmātas tadabhāvaḥ paramāṇujagadakāraṇatvādhikaraṇam idāīṃ paramāṇukāraṇavādaṃ irākaroti sa ca vāda itthaṃ samuttiṣṭhati paṭādīi hi loke sāvayavāi dravyāṇi svāugatair eva saṃyogasacivais tatvādibhir
dravyair ārabhyamāṇāi dṛṣṭāi tatsāmāyea yāvat kiṃcit sāvayavam tat sarvaṃ svāugatair eva saṃyogasacivais tais tair dravyair ārabdham iti gamyate sa cāyam
avayavāvayavivibhāgo yato ivartate so pakarṣaparyatagataḥ paramāṇuḥ sarvaṃ cedaṃ girisamudrādikaṃ jagat sāvayavam sāvayatvāc cādyatavat a cākāraṇea kāryeṇa bhavitavyam ity ataḥ paramāṇavo
jagataḥ kāraṇam iti kaṇabhugabhiprāyaḥ tāīmāi catvāri bhūtāi bhūmyudakatejaḥpavaākhyāi sāvayavāy upalabhya caturvidhāḥ paramāṇavaḥ parikalpyate teṣāṃ cāpakarṣaparyatagatatvea parato vibhāgāsaṃbhavād viaśyatāṃ pṛthivyādīāṃ paramāṇuparyato
vibhāgo bhavati sa pralayakālaḥ tataḥ sargakāle ca vāyavīyeṣv aṇuṣv adṛṣṭāpekṣaṃ karmotpadyate tat karma svāśrayam aṇum aṇvatareṇa saṃyuakti tato dvyaṇukādikrameṇa vāyur
utpadyate evam agiḥ evam āpaḥ evaṃ pṛthivī evam eva śarīraṃ sedriyam ity evaṃ sarvam idaṃ jagat aṇubhyaḥ saṃbhavati aṇugatebhyaś ca
rūpādibhyo dvyaṇukādigatāi rūpādīi saṃbhavati tatupaṭayāyea iti kāṇādā mayate tatredam abhidhīyate vibhāgāvasthāāṃ tāvadaṇūāṃ saṃyogaḥ karmāpekṣobhyupagatavyaḥ karmavatāṃ tatvādīāṃ saṃyogadarśaāt karmaṇaśca kāryatvāimittaṃ kimapyabhyupagatavyam
aabhyupagame imittābhāvāāṇuṣvādyaṃ karma syāt abhyupagamepi yadi prayatobhighātādirvā yathā dṛṣṭaṃ kimapi karmaṇo imittamabhyupagamyeta tasyāsaṃbhavāaivāṇuṣvādyaṃ karma syāt a hi tasyāmavasthāyāmātmaguṇaḥ prayataḥ saṃbhavati
śarīrābhāvāt śarīrapratiṣṭhe hi maasyātmaaḥ saṃyoge sati ātmaguṇaḥ prayato jāyate eteābhighātādyapi dṛṣṭaṃ imittaṃ pratyākhyātavyam sargottarakālaṃ hi tatsarvaṃ ādyasya karmaṇo imittaṃ saṃbhavati
athādṛṣṭamādyasya karmaṇo imittamityucyeta tatpuarātmasamavāyi vā syāt aṇusamavāyi vā ubhayathāpi ādṛṣṭaimittamaṇuṣu karmāvakalpeta adṛṣṭasyācetaatvāt a hyacetaaṃ cetaeāadhiṣṭhitaṃ svatatraṃ pravartate pravartayati veti sāṃkhyaparīkṣāyāmabhihitam
ātmaaścāutpaacaitayasya tasyāmavasthāyāmacetaatvāt ātmasamavāyitvābhyupagamācca ādṛṣṭamaṇuṣu karmaṇo imittaṃ syāt asaṃbadhāt adṛṣṭavatā puruṣeṇāstyaṇūāṃ saṃbadha iti cet saṃbadhasātatyātpravṛttisātatyaprasaṅgaḥ iyāmakātarābhāvāt tadevaṃ iyatasya kasyacitkarmaimittasyābhāvāāṇuṣvādyaṃ karma syāt
karmābhāvāttaibadhaaḥ saṃyogo a syāt saṃyogābhāvāc ca taibadhaaṃ dvyauṇakādi kāryajātaṃ a syāt saṃyogaś cāṇor aṇvatareṇa sarvātmaā vā syāt ekadeśea vā sarvātmaā
cet upacayāupapatter aṇumātratvaprasaṅgaḥ dṛṣṭaviparyayaprasaṅgaś ca pradeśavato dravyasya pradeśavatā dravyātareṇa saṃyogasya dṛṣṭatvāt ekadeśea cet sāvayavatvaprasaṅgaḥ paramāṇūāṃ kalpitāḥ pradeśāḥ syur iti cet
kalpitāām avastutvād avastv eva saṃyoga iti vastuaḥ kāryasyāsamavāyikāraṇaṃ a syāt asati cāsamavāyikāraṇe dvyaṇukādi kāryadravyaṃ otpadyeta yathā cādisarge imittābhāvāt saṃyogotpattyarthaṃ karma
āṇūāṃ saṃbhavati evaṃ mahāpralayepi vibhāgotpattyarthaṃ karma aivāṇūāṃ saṃbhavet a hi tatrāpi kiṃci iyataṃ taimittaṃ dṛṣṭam asti adṛṣṭam api bhogaprasiddhyartham a
pralayaprasiddhyartham ity ato imittābhāvā a syād aṇūāṃ saṃyogotpattyarthaṃ vibhāgotpattyarthaṃ vā karma ataś ca saṃyogavibhāgābhāvāt tadāyattayoḥ sargapralayayor abhāvaḥ prasajyeta tasmād aupapao
yaṃ paramāṇukāraṇavādaḥ samavāyābhyupagamāc ca sāmyād aavasthiteḥ samavāyābhyupagamāc ca tadabhāva iti prakṛteāṇuvādairākaraṇea saṃbadhyate dvābhyāṃ cāṇubhyāṃ dvyaṇukam utpadyamāam atyatabhiam aṇubhyām aṇvoḥ samavaitīty
abhyupagamyate bhavatā a caivam abhyupagacchatā śakyate ṇukāraṇatā samarthayitum kutaḥ sāmyād aavasthiteḥ yathaiva hy aṇubhyām atyatabhiaṃ sat dvyaṇukaṃ samavāyalakṣaṇea saṃbadhea tābhyāṃ
saṃbadhyate evaṃ samavāyo pi samavāyibhyo tyatabhiaḥ sa samavāyalakṣaṇeāyeaiva saṃbadhea samavāyibhiḥ saṃbadhyeta atyatabhedasāmyāt tataś ca tasya tasyāyo yaḥ saṃbadhaḥ kalpayitavya ity
aavasthaiva prasajyeta au iha pratyayagrāhyaḥ samavāyo ityasaṃbaddha eva samavāyibhir gṛhyate āsaṃbaddhaḥ saṃbadhātarāpekṣo vā tataś ca a tasyāyaḥ saṃbadhaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ yeāavasthā
prasajyeteti ety ucyate saṃyogopy evaṃ sati saṃyogibhir ityasaṃbaddha eveti samavāyava āyaṃ saṃbadham apekṣeta athārthātaratvāt saṃyogaḥ saṃbadhātaram apekṣeta samavāyo pi tarhy
arthātaratvāt saṃbadhātaram apekṣeta a ca guṇatvāt saṃyogaḥ saṃbadhātaram apekṣate a samavāyaḥ aguṇatvād iti yujyate vaktum apekṣākāraṇasya tulyatvāt guṇaparibhāṣāyāś cātatratvāt tasmād
arthātaraṃ samavāyam abhyupagacchataḥ prasajyetaivāavasthā prasajyamāāyāṃ cāavasthāyām ekāsiddhau sarvāsiddher dvābhyām aṇubhyāṃ dvyaṇukaṃ aivotpadyeta tasmād apy aupapaaḥ paramāṇukāraṇavādaḥ ityam eva ca bhāvāt
api cāṇavaḥ pravṛttisvabhāvā vā ivṛttisvabhāvā vā ubhayasvabhāvā vā aubhayasvabhāvā vā abhyupagamyate gatyatarābhāvāt caturdhāpi opapadyate pravṛttisvabhāvatve ityam eva pravṛtter bhāvāt pralayābhāvaprasaṅgaḥ
ivṛttisvabhāvatve pi ityam eva ivṛtter bhāvāt sargābhāvaprasaṅgaḥ ubhayasvabhāvatvaṃ ca virodhād asamañjasam aubhayasvabhāvatve tu imittavaśāt pravṛttiivṛttyor abhyupagamyamāayor adṛṣṭāder imittasya ityasaṃidhāā ityapravṛttiprasaṅgaḥ
atatratve py adṛṣṭāder ityāpravṛttiprasaṅgaḥ tasmād apy aupapaaḥ paramāṇukāraṇavādaḥ rūpādimattvāc ca viparyayo darśaāt sāvayavāāṃ dravyāṇām avayavaśo vibhajyamāāāṃ yataḥ paro vibhāgo a
saṃbhavati te caturvidhā rūpādimataḥ paramāṇavaś caturvidhasya rūpādimato bhūtabhautikasyārambhakā ityāś ceti yad vaiśeṣikā abhyupagacchati sa teṣām abhyupagamo irālambaa eva yato rūpādimattvāt
paramāṇūām aṇutvaityatvaviparyayaḥ prasajyeta paramakāraṇāpekṣayā sthūlatvam aityatvaṃ ca teṣām abhipretaviparītam āpadyetety arthaḥ kutaḥ evaṃ loke dṛṣṭatvāt yad dhi loke rūpādimad vastu
tat svakāraṇāpekṣayā sthūlam aityaṃ ca dṛṣṭam tad yathā paṭas tatū apekṣya sthūlo ityaś ca bhavati tatavaś cāṃśū apekṣya sthūlā aityāś
ca bhavati tathā cāmī paramāṇavo rūpādimatas tair abhyupagamyate tasmāt te pi kāraṇavatas tadapekṣayā sthūlā aityāś ca prāpuvati yac ca ityatve
kāraṇaṃ tair uktam sad akāraṇava ityam iti tad apy evaṃ sati aṇuṣu a saṃbhavati uktea prakāreṇāṇūām api kāraṇavattvopapatteḥ yad api
ityatve dvitīyaṃ kāraṇam uktam aityam iti ca viśeṣataḥ pratiṣedhābhāvaḥ iti tad api āvaśyaṃ paramāṇūāṃ ityatvaṃ sādhayati asati hi yasmi kasmiṃś
ci itye vastui ityaśabdea añaḥ samāso opapadyate a puaḥ paramāṇuityatvam evāpekṣyate tac cāsty eva ityaṃ paramakāraṇaṃ brahma a ca śabdārthavyavahāramātreṇa

satāṃ paridṛśyamāakāryāṇāṃ kāraṇāāṃ pratyakṣeṇāgrahaṇam avidyeti tato dvyaṇukaityatāpy āpadyeta athādravyatve satīti viśeṣyeta tathāpy akāraṇavattvam eva ityatāimittam āpadyeta tasya ca prāg evoktatvāt
avidyā ca iti puaruktaṃ syāt athāpi kāraṇavibhāgāt kāraṇaviāśāc cāyasya tṛtīyasya viāśahetor asaṃbhavo vidyā sā paramāṇūāṃ ityatvaṃ khyāpayati iti vyākhyāyeta āvaśyaṃ

tv apāstaviśeṣaṃ sāmāyātmakaṃ kāraṇaṃ viśeṣavad avasthātaram āpadyamāam ārambhakam abhyupagamyate tadā ghṛtakāṭhiyavilayaavamūrtyavasthāvilayaeāpi viāśa upapadyate tasmād rūpādimattvāt syād abhipretaviparyayaḥ paramāṇūām tasmād apy
aupapaaḥ paramāṇukāraṇavādaḥ ubhayathā ca doṣāt gadharasarūpasparśaguṇā sthūlā pṛthivī rūparasasparśaguṇāḥ sūkṣmā āpaḥ rūpasparśaguṇaṃ sūkṣmataraṃ tejaḥ sparśaguṇaḥ sūkṣmatamo vāyuḥ ityevametāi catvāri bhūtāyupacitāpacitaguṇāi
sthūlasūkṣmasūkṣmatarasūkṣmatamatāratamyopetāi ca loke lakṣyate tadvatparamāṇavopyupacitāpacitaguṇāḥ kalpera a vā ubhayathāpi ca doṣāuṣaṅgoparihārya eva syāt kalpyamāe tāvadupacitāpacitaguṇatve upacitaguṇāāṃ mūrtyupacayādaparamāṇutvaprasaṅgaḥ a cātareṇāpi mūrtyupacayaṃ
guṇopacayo bhavatītyucyeta kāryeṣu bhūteṣu guṇopacaye mūrtyupacayadarśaāt akalpyamāe tūpacitāpacitaguṇatve paramāṇutvasāmyaprasiddhaye yadi tāvatsarva ekaikaguṇā eva kalpyera tatastejasi sparśasyopalabdhira syāt apsu rūpasparśayoḥ pṛthivyāṃ
ca rasarūpasparśāām kāraṇaguṇapūrvakatvātkāryaguṇāām atha sarve caturguṇā eva kalpyera tatopsvapi gadhasyopalabdhiḥ syāt tejasi gadharasayoḥ vāyau ca gadharūparasāām a caivaṃ dṛśyate tasmādapyaupapaaḥ

parigṛhīta ity atyatam evāādaraṇīyo vedavādibhiḥ api ca vaiśeṣikās tatrārthabhūtā ṣaṭpadārthā dravyaguṇakarmasāmāyaviśeṣasamavāyākhyā atyatabhiā bhialakṣaṇā abhyupagacchati yathā mauṣyo śvaḥ śaśa iti tathātvaṃ
cābhyupagamya tadviruddhaṃ dravyādhīatvaṃ śeṣāṇām abhyupagacchati ta opapadyate katham yathā hi loke śaśakuśapalāśaprabhṛtīām atyatabhiāāṃ satāṃ etaretarādhīatvaṃ bhavati evaṃ dravyādīām apy atyatabhiatvāt
aiva dravyādhīatvaṃ guṇādīāṃ bhavitum arhati atha bhavati dravyādhīatvaṃ guṇādīām tato dravyabhāve bhāvād dravyābhāve bhāvād dravyam eva saṃsthāādibhedād aekaśabdapratyayabhāg bhavati yathā
devadatta eka eva sa avasthātarayogād aekaśabdapratyayabhāg bhavati tadvat tathā sati sāṃkhyasiddhātaprasaṅgaḥ svasiddhātavirodhaś cāpadyeyātām av ager ayasyāpi sato dhūmasyāgyadhīatvaṃ dṛśyate satyaṃ
dṛśyate bhedapratītestu tatrāgidhūmayor ayatvaṃ iścīyate iha tu śuklaḥ kambalaḥ rohiṇī dheuḥ īlam utpalam iti dravyasyaiva tasya tasya tea tea viśeṣaṇea
pratīyamāatvāt aiva dravyaguṇayor agidhūmayor iva bhedapratītir asti tasmād dravyātmakatā guṇasya etea karmasāmāyaviśeṣasamavāyāāṃ dravyātmakatā vyākhyātā guṇāāṃ dravyādhīatvaṃ dravyaguṇayor ayutasiddhatvād iti yady
ucyeta tat puar ayutasiddhatvam apṛthagdeśatvaṃ vā syāt apṛthakkālatvaṃ vā apṛthaksvabhāvatvaṃ vā sarvathāpi opapadyate apṛthagdeśatve tāvat svābhyupagamo virudhyeta katham tatvārabdho hi
paṭas tatudeśo bhyupagamyate a paṭadeśaḥ paṭasya tu guṇāḥ śuklatvādayaḥ paṭadeśā abhyupagamyate a tatudeśāḥ tathā cāhuḥ dravyāṇi dravyātaram ārabhate guṇāś ca
guṇātaram VS iti tatavo hi kāraṇadravyāṇi kāryadravyaṃ paṭam ārabhate tatugatāś ca guṇāḥ śuklādayaḥ kāryadravye paṭe śuklādiguṇātaram ārabhate iti hi te
bhyupagacchati so bhyupagamo dravyaguṇayor apṛthagdeśatve bhyupagamyamāe bādhyeta atha apṛthakkālatvam ayutasiddhatvam ucyeta savyadakṣiṇayor api goviṣāṇayor ayutasiddhatvaṃ prasajyeta tathā apṛthaksvabhāvatve tv ayutasiddhatve
a dravyaguṇayor ātmabhedaḥ saṃbhavati tasya tādātmyeaiva pratīyamāatvāt yutasiddhayoḥ saṃbadhaḥ saṃyogaḥ ayutasiddhayos tu samavāyaḥ ity ayam abhyupagamo mṛṣaiva teṣām prāksiddhasya kāryāt
kāraṇasyāyutasiddhatvāupapatteḥ athāyatarāpekṣa evāyam abhyupagamaḥ syāt ayutasiddhasya kāryasya kāraṇea saṃbadhaḥ samavāya iti evam api prāgasiddhasyālabdhātmakasya kāryasya kāraṇea saṃbadho opapadyate dvayāyattatvāt saṃbadhasya
siddhaṃ bhūtvā saṃbadhyata iti cet prāk kāraṇasaṃbadhāt kāryasya siddhāv abhyupagamyamāāyām ayutasiddhyabhāvāt kāryakāraṇayoḥ saṃyogavibhāgau a vidyete VS or itīdam uktaṃ duruktaṃ
syāt yathā cotpaamātrasyākriyasya kāryadravyasya vibhubhir ākāśādibhir dravyātaraiḥ saṃbadhaḥ saṃyoga evābhyupagamyate a samavāyaḥ evaṃ kāraṇadravyeṇāpi saṃbadhaḥ saṃyoga eva syāt a samavāyaḥ
āpi saṃyogasya samavāyasya vā saṃbadhasya saṃbadhivyatirekeṇāstitve kiṃcit pramāṇam asti saṃbadhiśabdapratyayavyatirekeṇa saṃyogasamavāyaśabdapratyayadarśaāt tayor astitvam iti cet a ekatve pi svarūpabāhyarūpāpekṣayā aekaśabdapratyayadarśaāt
yathaiko pi sa devadatto loke svarūpaṃ saṃbadhirūpaṃ cāpekṣya aekaśabdapratyayabhāg bhavati mauṣyo brāhmaṇaḥ śrotriyo vadāyo bālo yuvā sthaviraḥ pitā putraḥ pautro
bhrātā jāmāteti yathā caikāpi satī rekhā sthāāyatvea iviśamāā ekadaśaśatasahasrādiśabdapratyayabhedam aubhavati tathā saṃbadhior eva saṃbadhiśabdapratyayavyatirekeṇa saṃyogasamavāyaśabdapratyayārhatvam a vyatiriktavastvastitvea ity upalabdhilakṣaṇaprāptasyāupalabdheḥ abhāvaḥ
vastvatarasya āpi saṃbadhiviṣayatve saṃbadhaśabdapratyayayoḥ saṃtatabhāvaprasaṅgaḥ svarūpabāhyarūpāpekṣayeti uktottaratvāt tathāṇvātmamaasām apradeśatvā a saṃyogaḥ saṃbhavati pradeśavato dravyasya pradeśavatā dravyātareṇa saṃyogadarśaāt kalpitāḥ pradeśā aṇvātmamaasāṃ
bhaviṣyatīti cet a avidyamāārthakalpaāyāṃ sarvārthasiddhiprasaṅgāt iyā evāvidyamāo viruddho viruddho vā arthaḥ kalpaīyaḥ ātodhikaḥ iti iyamahetvabhāvāt kalpaāyāś ca svāyattatvāt prabhūtatvasaṃbhavāc ca
a ca vaiśeṣikaiḥ kalpitebhyaḥ ṣaḍbhyaḥ padārthebhyo yedhikāḥ śataṃ sahasraṃ vā arthā a kalpayitavyā iti ivārako hetur asti tasmād yasmai yasmai

tayor bhedasiddhiḥ kuṇḍabadaravat itītaretarāśrayatā syāt a hi kāryakāraṇayor bheda āśritāśrayabhāvo vā vedātavādibhir abhyupagamyate kāraṇasyaiva saṃsthāamātraṃ kāryam ity abhyupagamāt kiṃcāyat paramāṇūāṃ
paricchiatvāt yāvatyo diśaḥ ṣaṭ aṣṭau daśa vā tāvadbhir avayavaiḥ sāvayavās te syuḥ sāvayavatvād aityāś ca iti ityatvairavayavatvābhyupagamo bādhyeta yāṃs tvaṃ

kāryā āryaiḥ śreyorthibhir iti vākyaśeṣaḥ samudāya ubhayahetuke pi tadaprāptiḥ samudāyādhikaraṇam vaiśeṣikarāddhāto duryuktiyogād vedavirodhāc chiṣṭāparigrahāc ca āpekṣitavya ity uktam sordhavaiāśika iti
vaiāśikatvasāmyāt sarvavaiāśikarāddhāto atarām apekṣitavya itīdam idāīm upapādayāmaḥ sa ca bahuprakāraḥ pratipattibhedād vieyabhedād vā tatraite trayo vādio bhavati kecit sarvāstitvavādiaḥ kecidvijñāāstitvamātravādiaḥ
aye puaḥ sarvaśūyatvavādia iti tatra ye sarvāstitvavādio bāhyam ātaraṃ ca vastvabhyupagacchati bhūtaṃ bhautikaṃ ca cittaṃ caittaṃ ca tāṃs tāvat pratibrūmaḥ
tatra bhūtaṃ pṛthivīdhātvādayaḥ bhautikaṃ rūpādayaś cakṣurādayaś ca catuṣṭaye ca pṛthivyādiparamāṇavaḥ kharasehoṣṇeraṇasvabhāvāḥ te pṛthivyādibhāvea saṃhayate iti mayate tathā rūpavijñāavedaāsaṃjñāsaṃskārasaṃjñakāḥ pañcas kadhāḥ
te py ādhyātmaṃ sarvavyavahārāspadabhāvea saṃhayate iti mayate tatredam abhidhīyate yo yam ubhayahetuka ubhayaprakāraḥ samudāyaḥ pareṣām abhipretaḥ aṇuhetukaś ca bhūtabhautikasaṃhatirūpaḥ skadhahetukaś
ca pañcaskadhīrūpaḥ tasmi ubhayahetuke pi samudāye bhipreyamāṇe tadaprāptiḥ syāt samudāyāprāptiḥ samudāyabhāvāupapattir ity arthaḥ kutaḥ samudāyiām acetaatvāt cittābhijvalaasya ca samudāyasiddhyadhīatvāt ayasya
ca kasyacic cetaasya bhoktuḥ praśāsitur vā sthirasya saṃhatur aabhyupagamāt irapekṣapravṛttyabhyupagame ca pravṛttyauparamaprasaṅgāt āśayasyāpy ayatvāayatvābhyām airūpyatvāt kṣaṇikatvābhyupagamāc ca irvyāpāratvāt pravṛttyaupapatteḥ tasmāt

sparśaḥ vedaā tṛṣṇā upādāaṃ bhavaḥ jātiḥ jarā maraṇaṃ śokaḥ paridevaā duḥkhaṃ durmaastā ity evaṃjātīyakā itaretarahetukāḥ saugate samaye kvacit saṃkṣiptā irdiṣṭāḥ

a kasmāt utpattimātraimittatvāt bhaved upapaaḥ saṃghātaḥ yadi saṃghātasya kiṃci imittam avagamyeta a tv avagamyate yata itaretarapratyayatve py avidyādīāṃ pūrvapūrvam uttarottarasyotpattimātraimittaṃ
bhavat bhavet a tu saṃghātotpatteḥ kiṃci imittaṃ saṃbhavati av avidyādibhir arthād ākṣipyate saṃghāta ity uktam atrocyate yadi tāvad ayam abhiprāyaḥ
avidyādayaḥ saṃghātam atareṇātmāam alabhamāā apekṣate saṃghātam iti tatas tasya saṃghātasya kiṃci imittaṃ vaktavyam tacca ityeṣv apy aṇuṣv abhyugamyamāeṣv āśrayāśrayibhūteṣu ca
bhoktṛṣu satsu a saṃbhavatīty uktaṃ vaiśeṣikaparīkṣāyām kimaṅga puaḥ kṣaṇikeṣv apy aṇuṣu bhoktṛ rahiteṣv āśrayāśrayiśūyeṣu vābhyupagamyamāeṣu saṃbhavet athāyam abhiprāyaḥ avidyādaya eva
saṃghātasya imittam iti kathaṃ tam evāśrityātmāaṃ labhamāās tasyaiva imittaṃ syuḥ atha mayase saṃghātā evāādau saṃsāre saṃtatyāuvartate tadāśrayāś cāvidyādaya iti tadāpi
saṃghātāt saṃghātātaram utpadyamāaṃ iyamea vā sadṛśam evotpadyeta aiyamea vā sadṛśaṃ visadṛśaṃ votpadyeta iyamābhyupagame mauṣyapudgalasya devatiryagyoiārakaprāptyabhāvaḥ prāpuyāt aiyamābhyupagamepi mauṣyapudgalaḥ kadācit kṣaṇea

uttarotpāde ca pūrvairodhāt uktam etat avidyādīām utpattimātraimittatvā a saṃghātasiddhir astīti tad api tu utpattimātraimittatvaṃ a saṃbhavatītīdam idāīm upapādyate kṣaṇabhaṅgavādio yam
abhyupagamaḥ uttarasmi kṣaṇe utpadyamāe pūrvaḥ kṣaṇo irudhyata iti a caivam abhyupagacchatā pūrvottarayoḥ kṣaṇayor hetuphalabhāvaḥ śakyate saṃpādayitum irudhyamāasya iruddhasya vā pūrvakṣaṇasyābhāvagrastatvād
uttarakṣaṇahetutvāupapatteḥ atha bhāvabhūtaḥ pariiṣpaāvasthaḥ pūrvakṣaṇa uttarakṣaṇasya hetur ity abhiprāyaḥ tathāpi opapadyate bhāvabhūtasya puar vyāpārakalpaāyāṃ kṣaṇātarasaṃbadhaprasaṅgāt atha bhāva evāsya vyāpāra ity

cotpādairodhau āma vastuaḥ svarūpam eva vā syātām avasthātaraṃ vā vastvataram eva vā sarvathāpi opapadyate yadi tāvad vastuaḥ svarūpam evotpādairodhau syātām
tato vastuśabda utpādairodhaśabdau ca paryāyāḥ prāpuyuḥ athāsti kaścid viśeṣa iti mayeta utpādairodhaśabdābhyāṃ madhyavartio vastua ādyatākhye avasthe abhilapyete iti evam apy
ādyatamadhyakṣaṇatrayasaṃbadhitvād vastuaḥ kṣaṇikatvābhyupagamahāiḥ athātyatavyatiriktāv evotpādairodhau vastuaḥ syātām aśvamahiṣavat tato vastu utpādairodhābhyām asaṃspṛṣṭam iti vastuaḥ śāśvatatvaprasaṅgaḥ yadi ca darśaādarśae vastua utpādairodhau
syātām evam api draṣṭṛdharmau tau a vastudharmāv iti vastuaḥ śāśvatatvaprasaṅga eva tasmād apy asaṃgataṃ saugataṃ matam asati pratijñoparodho yaugapadyam ayathā
kṣaṇabhaṅgavāde pūrvakṣaṇo irodhagrastatvā ottarasya kṣaṇasya hetur bhavatīty uktam athāsaty eva hetau phalotpattiṃ brūyāt tataḥ pratijñoparodhaḥ syāt caturvidhāhetūpratītya cittacaittā utpadyata itīyaṃ
pratijñā hīyeta irhetukāyāṃ cotpattāvapratibadhātsarvaṃ sarvatrotpadyeta athottarakṣaṇotpattiryāvattāvadavatiṣṭhate pūrvakṣaṇa iti brūyāt tato yaugapadyaṃ hetuphalayoḥ syāt tathāpi pratijñoparodha eva syāt kṣaṇikāḥ sarve saṃskārā
itīyaṃ pratijñoparudhyeta pratisaṃkhyāpratisaṃkhyāirodhāprāptiravicchedāt api ca vaiāśikāḥ kalpayati buddhibodhyaṃ trayādayatsaṃskṛtaṃ kṣaṇikaṃ ceti tadapi ca trayam pratisaṃkhyāpratisaṃkhyāirodhau ākāśaṃ cetyācakṣate trayamapi caitat avastu
abhāvamātraṃ irupākhyamiti mayate buddhipūrvakaḥ kila viāśo bhāvāāṃ pratisaṃkhyāirodho āma bhāṣyate tadviparītopratisaṃkhyāirodhaḥ āvaraṇābhāvamātramākāśamiti teṣāmākāśaṃ parastātpratyākhyāsyati irodhadvayamidāīṃ pratyācaṣṭe pratisaṃkhyāpratisaṃkhyāirodhayoḥ aprāptirasaṃbhava ityarthaḥ kasmāt
avicchedāt etau hi pratisaṃkhyāpratisaṃkhyāirodhau saṃtāagocarau vā syātām bhāvagocarau vā a tāvatsaṃtāagocarau saṃbhavataḥ sarveṣvapi saṃtāeṣu saṃtāiāmavicchiea hetuphalabhāvea saṃtāavicchedasyāsaṃbhavāt āpi bhāvagocarau saṃbhavataḥ
a hi bhāvāāṃ iravayo irupākhyo viāśaḥ saṃbhavati sarvāsvapyavasthāsu pratyabhijñāabaleāvayyavicchedadarśaāt aspaṣṭapratyabhijñāāsvapyavasthāsu kvaciddṛṣṭeāvayyavicchedeāyatrāpi tadaumāāt tasmātparaparikalpitasya irodhadvayasyāupapattiḥ ubhayathā ca doṣāt yoyamavidyādiirodhaḥ pratisaṃkhyāirodhātaḥpātī paraparikalpitaḥ
sa samyagjñāādvā saparikarātsyāt svayameva vā pūrvasmivikalpe irhetukaviāśābhyupagamahāiprasaṅgaḥ uttarasmiṃstu mārgopadeśāarthakyaprasaṅgaḥ evamubhayathāpi doṣaprasaṅgādasamañjasamidaṃ darśaam ākāśe cāviśeṣāt yac ca teṣām evābhipretaṃ irodhadvayam ākāśaṃ
ca irupākhyam iti tatra irodhadvayasya irupākhyatvaṃ purastā irākṛtam ākāśasyedāīṃ irākriyate ākāśe cāyukto irupākhyatvābhyupagamaḥ pratisaṃkhyāpratisaṃkhyāirodhayor iva vastutvapratipatter aviśeṣāt āgamaprāmāṇyāt tāvat ātmaa
ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ ityādiśrutibhya ākāśasya ca vastutvaprasiddhiḥ vipratipaāprati tu śabdaguṇāumeyatvaṃ vaktavyam gadhādīāṃ guṇāāṃ pṛthivyādivastvāśrayatvadarśaāt api ca āvaraṇābhāvamātram ākāśam icchatām ekasmi suparṇe
patatyāvaraṇasya vidyamāatvāt suparṇātarasyotpitsato avakāśatvaprasaṅgaḥ yatrāvaraṇābhāvas tatra patiṣyatīti cet yeāvaraṇābhāvo viśeṣyate tat tarhi vastubhūtam evākāśaṃ syāt a āvaraṇābhāvamātram api ca āvaraṇābhāvamātram
ākaśaṃ mayamāasya saugatasya svābhyupagamavirodhaḥ prasajyeta saugate hi samaye pṛthivī bhagava kiṃsaṃiśrayā ity asmi praśaprativacaapravāhe pṛthivyādīām ate vāyuḥ kiṃsaṃiśrayaḥ ityasya praśasya
prativacaaṃ bhavati vāyur ākāśasaṃiśrayaḥ iti tadākāśasyāvastutve a samañjasaṃ syāt tasmād apy ayuktam ākāśasyāvastutvam api ca irodhadvayamākāśaṃ ca trayamapyetairupākhyamavastu ityaṃ ceti
vipratiṣiddham a hyavastuo ityatvamaityatvaṃ vā saṃbhavati vastvāśrayatvād dharmadharmivyavahārasya dharmadharmibhāve hi ghaṭādivad vastutvam eva syāt a irupākhyatvam ausmṛteś ca api ca
vaiāśikaḥ sarvasya vastuaḥ kṣaṇikatāmabhyupaya upalabdhurapi kṣaṇikatāmabhyupeyāt a ca sā saṃbhavati ausmṛteḥ aubhavam upalabdhimaūtpadyamāaṃ smaraṇameva ausmṛtiḥ sā copalabdhyekakartṛkā satī saṃbhavati puruṣātaropalabdhiviṣaye
puruṣātarasya smṛtyadarśaāt kathaṃ hi ahamadodrākṣam idamidāīṃ paśyāmi iti ca pūrvottaradarśiyekasmiasati pratyayaḥ syāt api ca darśaasmaraṇayoḥ kartaryekasmipratyakṣaḥ pratyabhijñāpratyayaḥ sarvasya lokasya prasiddhaḥ
ahamadodrākṣam idaṃ paśyāmi iti yadi hi tayorbhiaḥ kartā syāt tataḥ ahaṃ smarāmi adrākṣīdayaḥ iti pratīyāt a tvevaṃ pratyeti kaścit yatraivaṃ
pratyayastatra darśaasmaraṇayorbhiameva kartāraṃ sarvalokovagacchati smarāmyaham asāvadodrākṣīt iti iha tu ahamadodrākṣam iti darśaasmaraṇayorvaiāśikopyātmāamevaikaṃ kartāramavagacchati a āham ityātmao darśaaṃ irvṛttaṃ ihute yathā
agirauṣṇoprakāśa iti vā tatraivaṃ satyekasya darśaasmaraṇalakṣaṇakṣaṇadvayasaṃbadhe kṣaṇikatvābhyupagamahāiraparihāryā vaiāśikasya syāt tathā aatarāmaatarāmātmaa eva pratipattiṃ pratyabhijāaekakartṛkām ā uttamāducchvāsāt atītāśca pratipattīḥ ā jamaa
ātmaikakartṛkāḥ pratisaṃdadhāaḥ kathaṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgavādī vaiāśiko āpatrapeta sa yadi brūyāt sādṛśyādetatsaṃpatsyata iti taṃ pratibrūyāt teedaṃ sadṛśamiti dvayāyattatvātsādṛśyasya kṣaṇabhaṅgavādiaḥ sadṛśayordvayorvastuorgrahīturekasyābhāvāt sādṛśyaimittaṃ pratisaṃdhāamiti
mithyāpralāpa eva syāt syāccetpūrvottarayoḥ kṣaṇayoḥ sādṛśyasya grahītaikaḥ tathā satyekasya kṣaṇadvayāvasthāātkṣaṇikatvapratijñā pīḍyeta teedaṃ sadṛśam iti pratyayātaramevedam a pūrvottarakṣaṇadvayagrahaṇaimittamiti cet a tea
idam iti bhiapadārthopādāāt pratyayātarameva cetsādṛśyaviṣayaṃ syāt teedaṃ sadṛśam iti vākyaprayogoarthakaḥ syāt sādṛśyam ityeva prayogaḥ prāpuyāt yadā hi loke prasiddhaḥ padārthaḥ
parīkṣakaira parigṛhyate tadā svapakṣasiddhiḥ parapakṣadoṣo vā ubhayamapyucyamāaṃ parīkṣakāṇāmātmaaśca yathārthatvea a buddhisaṃtāamārohati evamevaiṣorthaḥ iti iścitaṃ yat tadeva vaktavyam tatoyaducyamāaṃ bahupralāpitvamātmaaḥ kevalaṃ
prakhyāpayet a cāyaṃ sādṛśyātsaṃvyavahāro yuktaḥ tadbhāvāvagamāt tatsadṛśabhāvāavagamācca bhavedapi kadācidbāhyavastui vipralambhasaṃbhavāt tadevedaṃ syāt tatsadṛśaṃ vā iti saṃdehaḥ upalabdhari tu saṃdehopi a
kadācidbhavati sa evāhaṃ syāṃ tatsadṛśo vā iti ya evāhaṃ pūrvedyuradrākṣaṃ sa evāhamadya smarāmi iti iścitatadbhāvopalambhāt tasmādapyaupapao vaiāśikasamayaḥ āsatodṛṣṭatvāt itaś cāupapao
vaiāśikasamayaḥ yataḥ sthiram auyāyikāraṇam aabhyupagacchatām abhāvād bhāvotpattir ity etad āpadyeta darśayati cābhāvād bhāvotpattim āupamṛdya prādurbhāvāt iti viaṣṭād dhi kila bījād
aṅkura utpadyate tathā viaṣṭāt kṣīrād dadhi mṛtpiṇḍāc ca ghaṭaḥ kūṭasthāc cet kāraṇāt kāryam utpadyeta aviśeṣāt sarvaṃ sarvata utpadyeta tasmād abhāvagrastebhyo
bījādibhyo ṅkurādīām utpadyamāatvād abhāvād bhāvotpattiḥ iti mayate tatredam ucyate āsato dṛṣṭatvāt iti ābhāvād bhāva utpadyate yady abhāvād bhāva utpadyeta abhāvatvāviśeṣāt
kāraṇaviśeṣābhyupagamo arthakaḥ syāt a hi bījādīām upamṛditāāṃ yo bhāvas tasyābhāvasya śaśaviṣāṇādīāṃ ca iḥsvabhāvatvāviśeṣād abhāvatve kaścid viśeṣo sti yea bījād evāṅkuro
jāyate kṣīrād eva dadhi ity evaṃjātīyakaḥ kāraṇaviśeṣābhyupagamo rthavāsyāt irviśeṣasya tv abhāvasya kāraṇatvābhyupagame śaśaviṣāṇādibhyo py aṅkurādayo jāyera a caivaṃ dṛśyate yadi
puar abhāvasyāpi viśeṣo bhyupagamyeta utpalādīāmiva īlatvādiḥ tato viśeṣavattvād evābhāvasya bhāvatvam utpalādivat prasajyeta āpy abhāvaḥ kasyacid utpattihetuḥ syāt abhāvatvād evaśaśaviṣāṇādivat abhāvāc
ca bhāvotpattāv abhāvāvitam eva sarvaṃ kāryaṃ syāt a caivaṃ dṛśyate sarvasya ca vastuaḥ svea svea rūpeṇa bhāvātmaaivopalabhyamāatvāt a ca mṛdavitāḥ
śarāvādayo bhāvās tatvādivikārāḥ keacid abhyupagamyate mṛdvikārāeva tu mṛdavitā bhāvā lokaḥ pratyeti yat tūktam svarūpopamardam atareṇa kasyacit kūṭasthasya vastuaḥ kāraṇatvāupapatter abhāvād
bhāvotpattir bhavitum arhatīti tad duruktam sthirasvabhāvāām eva suvarṇādīāṃ pratyabhijñāyamāāāṃ rucakādikāraṇabhāvadarśaāt yeṣv api bījādiṣu svarūpopamardo lakṣyate teṣv api āsāv upamṛdyamāā pūrvāvasthā
uttarāvasthāyāḥ kāraṇam abhyupagamyate aupamṛdyamāāām evāuyāyiāṃ bījādyavayavāām aṅkurādikāraṇabhāvābhyupagamāt tasmād asadbhyaḥ śaśaviṣāṇādibhyaḥ sad utpattyadarśaāt sadbhyaś ca suvarṇādibhyaḥ sad utpattidarśaāt aupapao yam abhāvād
bhāvotpattyabhyupagamaḥ api ca caturbhiś cittacaittā utpadyate paramāṇubhyaś ca bhūtabhautikalakṣaṇaḥ samudāya utpadyate ity abhyupagamya puarabhāvād bhāvotpattiṃ kalpayadbhir abhyupagamam apahuvāair vaiāśikaiḥ sarvo
loka ākulīkriyate udīsīāāmapi caivaṃ siddhiḥ yadi cābhāvādbhāvotpattirabhyupagamyeta evaṃ satyudāsīāāmaīhamāāāmapi jaāāmabhimatasiddhiḥ syāt abhāvasya sulabhatvāt kṛṣīvalasya kṣetrakarmaṇyaprayatamāasyāpi sasyaiṣpattiḥ syāt kulālasya ca mṛtsaṃskriyāyāmaprayatamāasyāpi
amatrotpattiḥ tatuvāyasyāpi tatūatavāasyāpi tavāasyeva vastralābhaḥ svargāpavargayośca a kaścitkathaṃcitsamīheta a caitadyujyate abhyupagamyate vā keacit tasmādaupapaoyamabhāvādbhāvotpattyabhyupagamaḥ ābhāva upalabdheḥ ābhāvādhikaraṇam evaṃ bāhyārthavādam āśritya
samudāyāprāptyādiṣu dūṣaṇeṣūdbhāviteṣu vijñāavādī bauddha idāīṃ pratyavatiṣṭhate keṣāṃcit kila vieyāāṃ bāhye vastuy abhiiveśam ālakṣya tadaurodhea bāhyārthavādaprakriyeyaṃ viracitā āsau sugatābhiprāyaḥ tasya tu
vijñāaikaskadhavāda evābhipretaḥ tasmiṃś ca vijñāavāde buddhyārūḍhea rūpeṇātastha eva pramāṇaprameyaphalavyavahāraḥ sarva upapadyate saty api bāhyārthe buddhyāroham atareṇa pramāṇādivyavahārāavatārāt kathaṃ puar avagamyate
atastha evāyaṃ sarvavyavahāraḥ a vijñāavyatirikto bāhyorthostīti tadasaṃbhavād ity āha sa hi bāhyorthobhyupagamyamāaḥ paramāṇavo vā syuḥ tatsamūhā vā stambhādayaḥ syuḥ tatra
a tāvat paramāṇavaḥ stambhādipratyayaparicchedyā bhavitum arhati paramāṇvābhāsajñāāupapatteḥ āpi tatsamūhāḥ stambhādayaḥ teṣāṃ paramāṇubhyoyatvāayatvābhyāṃ irūpayitum aśakyatvāt evaṃ jātyādī api pratyācakṣīta api ca
aubhavamātreṇa sādhāraṇātmao jñāasya jāyamāasya yoyaṃ prativiṣayaṃ pakṣapātaḥ stambhajñāaṃ kuḍyajñāaṃ ghaṭajñāaṃ paṭajñāam iti āsau jñāagataviśeṣam atareṇopapadyata ity avaśyaṃ viṣayasārūpyaṃ jñāasyāṅgīkartavyam aṅgīkṛte
ca tasmi viṣayākārasya jñāeaivāvaruddhatvād apārthikā bāhyārthasadbhāvakalpaā api ca sahopalambhaiyamād abhedo viṣayavijñāayor āpatati a hy aayor ekasyāupalambheyasyopalambhosti a caitat svabhāvaviveke yuktam
pratibadhakāraṇābhāvāt tasmād apy arthābhāvaḥ svapādivac cedaṃ draṣṭavyam yathā hi svapamāyāmarīcyudakagadharvaagarādipratyayā viaiva bāhyeārthea grāhyagrāhakākārā bhavati evaṃ jāgaritagocarā api stambhādipratyayā bhavitum arhatīty
avagamyate pratyayatvāviśeṣāt kathaṃ puar asati bāhyārthe pratyayavaicitryam upapadyate vāsaāvaicitryād ity āha aādau hi saṃsāre bījāṅkuravad vijñāāāṃ vāsaāāṃ cāyoyaimittaaimittikabhāvea vaicitryaṃ a
vipratiṣidhyate api ca avayavyatirekābhyāṃ vāsaāimittam eva jñāavaicitryam ity avagamyate svapādiṣv atareṇāpy arthaṃ vāsaāimittasya jñāavaicitryasya ubhābhyām apy āvābhyām abhyupagamyamāatvāt atareṇa tu
vāsaām arthaimittasya jñāavaicitryasya mayā aabhyupagamyamāatvāt tasmād apy abhāvo bāhyārthasyeti evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ ābhāva upalabdher iti a khalv abhāvo bāhyasyārthasyādhyavasātuṃ śakyate
kasmāt upalabdheḥ upalabhyate hi pratipratyayaṃ bāhyorthaḥ stambhaḥ kuḍyaṃ ghaṭaḥ paṭa iti a copalabhyamāasyaivābhāvo bhavitum arhati yathā hi kaścid bhuñjāo bhuji
sādhyāyāṃ tṛptau svayam aubhūyamāāyām evaṃ brūyāt āhaṃ bhuñje a vā tṛpyāmi iti tadvad idriyasaṃikarṣeṇa svayam upalabhamāa eva bāhyam artham āhamupalabhe
a ca sosti iti bruva katham upādeyavacaaḥ syāt au āham evaṃ bravīmi a kaṃcid artham upalabhe iti kiṃ tu upalabdhivyatiriktaṃ
opalabhe iti bravīmi bāḍham evaṃ bravīṣi iraṅkuśatvāt te tuṇḍasya a tu yuktyupetaṃ bravīṣi yata upalabdhivyatirekopi balād arthasyābhyupagatavyaḥ upalabdher eva a
hi kaścid upalabdhim eva stambhaḥ kuḍyaṃ cety upalabhate upalabdhiviṣayatveaiva tu stambhakuḍyādī sarve laukikā upalabhate ataś ca evam eva sarve laukikā
upalabhate yat pratyācakṣāṇā api bāhyam artham evam ācakṣate yad atarjñeyarūpaṃ tad bahirvad avabhāsate iti tepi hi sarvalokaprasiddhāṃ bahiravabhāsamāāṃ saṃvidaṃ pratilabhamāāḥ
pratyākhyātukāmāś ca bāhyam artham bahirvat iti vatkāraṃ kurvati itarathā hi kasmāt bahirvat iti brūyuḥ a hi viṣṇumitro vadhyāputravad avabhāsate iti
kaścid ācakṣīta tasmāt yathāubhavaṃ tattvam abhyupagacchadbhiḥ bahir evāvabhāsate iti yuktam abhyupagatum a tu bahirvat avabhāsata iti au bāhyasyārthasyāsaṃbhavāt bahirvad avabhāsate
ity adhyavasitam āyaṃ sādhur adhyavasāyaḥ yataḥ pramāṇapravṛttyapravṛttipūrvakau saṃbhavāsaṃbhavāv avadhāryete a puaḥ saṃbhavāsaṃbhavapūrvake pramāṇapravṛttyapravṛttī yad dhi pratyakṣādīām ayatameāpi pramāṇeopalabhyate tatsaṃbhavati yat
tu a keacid api pramāṇeopalabhyate ta a saṃbhavati iha tu yathāsvaṃ sarvair eva pramāṇair bāhyortha upalabhyamāaḥ kathaṃ vyatirekāvyatirekādivikalpair a saṃbhavatīty
ucyeta upalabdher eva a ca jñāasya viṣayasārūpyād viṣayaāśo bhavati asati viṣaye viṣayasārūpyāupapatteḥ bahirupalabdheś ca viṣayasya ata eva sahopalambhaiyamopi pratyayaviṣayayor upāyopeyabhāvahetukaḥ
a abhedahetukaḥ ity abhyupagatavyam api ca ghaṭajñāaṃ paṭajñāam iti viśeṣaṇayor eve ghaṭapaṭayor bhedaḥ a viśeṣyasya jñāasya yathā śuklo gauḥ kṛṣṇo
gaur iti śauklyakārṣṇyayor eva bhedaḥ a gotvasya dvābhyāṃ ca bheda ekasya siddho bhavati ekasmāc ca dvayoḥ tasmād arthajñāayor bhedaḥ tathā
ghaṭadarśaaṃ ghaṭasmaraṇam ity atrāpi pratipattavyam atrāpi hi viśeṣyayor eva darśaasmaraṇayor bhedaḥ a viśeṣaṇasya ghaṭasya yathā kṣīragadhaḥ kṣīrarasa iti viśeṣyayor eva
gadharasayor bhedaḥ a viśeṣaṇasya kṣīrasya tadvat api ca dvayor vijñāayoḥ pūrvottarakālayoḥ svasaṃvedaeaiva upakṣīṇayoḥ itaretaragrāhyagrāhakatvāupapattiḥ tataś ca vijñāabhedapratijñā kṣaṇikatvādidharmapratijñā svalakṣaṇasāmāyalakṣaṇavāsyavāsakatvāvidyopaplavasadasaddharmabadhamokṣādipratijñāś ca
svaśāstragatāḥ tā hīyera kiṃcāyat vijñāaṃ vijñāam ity abhyupagacchatā bāhyārthaḥ stambhaḥ kuḍyam ity evaṃjātīyakaḥ kasmā ābhyupagamyata iti vaktavyam vijñāam aubhūyata iti
cet bāhyopy arthoubhūyata eveti yuktam abhyupagatum atha vijñāaṃ prakāśātmakatvāt pradīpavat svayam evāubhūyate a tathā bāhyopy artha iti cet atyataviruddhāṃ svātmai
