vedabāhyāsv īśvarakalpaāsu yathāsaṃbhavam asāmañjasyaṃ yojayitavyam adhiṣṭhāāupapatteśca itaścāupapattistārkikaparikalpitasyeśvarasya sa hi parikalpyamāaḥ kumbhakāra iva mṛdādīi pradhāādīyadhiṣṭhāya pravartayet a caivamupapadyate a hyapratyakṣaṃ rūpādihīaṃ
ca pradhāamīśvarasyādhiṣṭheyaṃ saṃbhavati mṛdādivailakṣaṇyāt karaṇavaccea bhogādibhyaḥ syād etat yathā karaṇagrāmaṃ cakṣurādikamapratyakṣaṃ rūpādihīaṃ ca puruṣodhitiṣṭhati evaṃ pradhāam īśvarodhiṣṭhāsyatīti tathāpi opapadyate bhogādidarśaāddhi
karaṇagrāmasya adhiṣṭhitatvaṃ gamyate a cātra bhogādayo dṛśyate karaṇagrāmasāmye ca abhyupagamyamāe saṃsāriṇāmiva īśvarasyāpi bhogādayaḥ prasajyera ayathā vā sūtradvayaṃ vyākhyāyate adhiṣṭhāāupapatteśca itaścāupapattistārkikaparikalpitasyeśvarasya
sādhiṣṭhāo hi loke saśarīro rājā rāṣṭrasyeśvaro dṛśyate a iradhiṣṭhāaḥ ataśca taddṛṣṭātavaśeādṛṣṭamīśvaraṃ kalpayitumicchataḥ īśvarasyāpi kiṃciccharīraṃ karaṇāyataaṃ varṇayitavyaṃ syāt a ca tadvarṇayituṃ
śakyate sṛṣṭyuttarakālabhāvitvāccharīrasya prāksṛṣṭestadaupapatteḥ iradhiṣṭhāatve ceśvarasya pravartakatvāupapattiḥ evaṃ loke dṛṣṭatvāt karaṇavaccea bhogādibhyaḥ atha lokadarśaāusāreṇa īśvarasyāpi kiṃcitkaraṇāāmāyataaṃ śarīraṃ kāmea kalpyeta evamapi opapadyate
saśarīratve hi sati saṃsārivadbhogādiprasaṅgāt īśvarasyāpyaīśvaratvaṃ prasajyeta atavattvam asarvajñatā vā itaś cāupapattis tārkikaparikalpitasyeśvarasya sa hi sarvajñas tair abhyupagamyate ataś ca aataṃ
ca pradhāam aatāś ca puruṣā mitho bhiā abhyupagamyate tatra sarvajñeeśvareṇa pradhāasya puruṣāṇāmātmaaśceyattā paricchidyeta vā a vā paricchidyeta ubhayathāpi doṣouṣakta eva
katham pūrvasmiṃstāvadvikalpe iyattāparicchiatvāt pradhāapuruṣeśvarāṇām atavattvam avaśyaṃbhāvi evaṃ loke dṛṣṭatvāt yaddhi loke iyattāparicchiaṃ vastu ghaṭādi tadatavaddṛṣṭam tathā pradhāapuruṣeśvaratrayam apīyattāparicchiatvād atavat syāt
saṃkhyāparimāṇaṃ tāvat pradhāapuruṣeśvaratrayarūpeṇa paricchiam svarūpaparimāṇamapi tadgatamīśvareṇa paricchidyeta puruṣagatā ca mahāsaṃkhyā tataśceyattāparicchiāāṃ madhye ye saṃsārāmucyate teṣāṃ saṃsārotavā saṃsāritvaṃ ca teṣāmatavat evamitareṣvapi
krameṇa mucyamāeṣu saṃsārasya saṃsāriṇāṃ ca atavattvaṃ syāt pradhāaṃ ca savikāraṃ puruṣārthamīśvarasya adhiṣṭheyaṃ saṃsāratveābhimatam tacchūyatāyām īśvaraḥ kimadhitiṣṭhet kiṃviṣaye vā sarvajñateśvarate syātām
pradhāapuruṣeśvarāṇām caivamatavattve sati ādimattvaprasaṅgaḥ ādyatavattve ca śūyavādaprasaṅgaḥ atha mā bhūdeṣa doṣa ityuttaro vikalpobhyupagamyeta a pradhāasya puruṣāṇāmātmaaśca iyattā īśvareṇa paricchidyata iti
tata īśvarasya sarvajñatvābhyupagamahāiraparo doṣaḥ prasajyeta tasmād apy asaṃgatas tārkikaparigṛhīta īśvarakāraṇavādaḥ utpattyasambhavāt utpattyasaṃbhavādhikaraṇam yeṣām aprakṛtir adhiṣṭhātā kevalaimittakāraṇam īśvaro bhimataḥ teṣāṃ pakṣaḥ
pratyākhyātaḥ yeṣāṃ puaḥ prakṛtiścādhiṣṭhātā ca ubhayātmakaṃ kāraṇamīśvarobhimataḥ teṣāṃ pakṣaḥ pratyākhyāyate au śrutisamāśrayaṇeāpyevaṃrūpa eveśvaraḥ prāṅirdhāritaḥ prakṛtiścādhiṣṭhātā ceti śrutyausāriṇī ca smṛtiḥ pramāṇamiti
sthitiḥ tatkasya hetoreṣa pakṣaḥ pratyācikhyāsita iti ucyate yady apy evaṃjātīyakoṃśaḥ samāatvāa visaṃvādagocaro bhavati asti tvaṃśātaraṃ visaṃvādasthāamityatastatpratyākhyāāyārambhaḥ tatra bhāgavatā mayate bhagavāevaiko
vāsudevo irañjaajñāasvarūpaḥ paramārthatattvam sa caturdhātmāaṃ pravibhajya pratiṣṭhitaḥ vāsudevavyūharūpeṇa saṃkarṣaṇavyūharūpeṇa pradyumavyūharūpeṇa airuddhavyūharūpeṇa ca vāsudevo āma paramātmā ucyate saṃkarṣaṇo āma jīvaḥ pradyumo
āma maaḥ airuddho āma ahaṃkāraḥ teṣāṃ vāsudevaḥ parā prakṛtiḥ itare saṃkarṣaṇādayaḥ kāryam tamitthaṃbhūtaṃ parameśvaraṃ bhagavatamabhigamaopādāejyāsvādhyāyayogairvarṣaśatamiṣṭvā kṣīṇakleśo bhagavatameva pratipadyata iti tatra
yattāvaducyate yosau ārāyaṇaḥ paro vyaktāt prasiddhaḥ paramātmā sarvātmā sa ātmaātmāam aekadhā vyūhyāvasthita iti ta a irākriyate sa ekadhā bhavati tridhā
bhavati ityādiśrutibhyaḥ paramātmao ekadhābhāvasyādhigatatvāt yad api tasya bhagavato bhigamaādilakṣaṇam ārādhaam ajasram aayacittatayābhipreyate tadapi a pratiṣidhyate śrutismṛtyorīśvarapraṇidhāasya prasiddhatvāt yatpuaridamucyate vāsudevātsaṃkarṣaṇa utpadyate
saṃkarṣaṇācca pradyumaḥ pradyumāccāiruddha iti atra brūmaḥ a vāsudevasaṃjñakātparamātmaaḥ saṃkarṣaṇasaṃjñakasya jīvasyotpattiḥ saṃbhavati aityatvādidoṣaprasaṅgāt utpattimattve hi jīvasya aityatvādayo doṣāḥ prasajyera tataśca aivāsya
bhagavatprāptirmokṣaḥ syāt kāraṇaprāptau kāryasya pravilayaprasaṅgāt pratiṣedhiṣyati ca ācāryo jīvasyotpattim ātmāśruterityatvācca tābhyaḥ iti tasmādasaṃgataiṣā kalpaā a ca kartuḥ karaṇam itaś cāsaṃgataiṣā
kalpaā yasmāa hi loke karturdevadattādeḥ karaṇaṃ paraśvādyutpadyamāaṃ dṛśyate varṇayati ca bhāgavatāḥ karturjīvātsaṃkarṣaṇasaṃjñakātkaraṇaṃ maaḥ pradyumasaṃjñakamutpadyate kartṛjācca tasmādairuddhasaṃjñakohaṃkāra utpadyata iti a caitaddṛṣṭātamatareṇādhyavasātuṃ
śakumaḥ a caivaṃbhūtāṃ śrutimupalabhāmahe vijñāādibhāve vā tadapratiṣedhaḥ athāpi syāt a caite saṃkarṣaṇādayo jīvādibhāveābhipreyate kiṃ tarhi īśvarā evaite sarve jñāaiśvaryaśaktibalavīryatejobhiraiśvaryadharmairavitā abhyupagamyate
vāsudevā evaite sarve irdoṣā iradhiṣṭhāā iravadyāśceti tasmāāyaṃ yathāvarṇita utpattyasaṃbhavo doṣaḥ prāpotīti atrocyate evamapi tadapratiṣedhaḥ utpattyasaṃbhavasyāpratiṣedhaḥ prāpotyevāyamutpattyasaṃbhavo doṣaḥ prakārātareṇetyabhiprāyaḥ katham yadi
tāvadayamabhiprāyaḥ parasparabhiā evaite vāsudevādayaścatvāra īśvarāstulyadharmāṇaḥ aiṣāmekātmakatvamastīti tatoekeśvarakalpaāarthakyam ekeaiveśvareṇeśvarakāryasiddheḥ siddhātahāiśca bhagavāevaiko vāsudevaḥ paramārthatattvamityabhyupagamāt athāyamabhiprāyaḥ ekasyaiva bhagavata ete catvāro vyūhāstulyadharmāṇa iti tathāpi
tadavastha evotpattyasaṃbhavaḥ a hi vāsudevātsaṃkarṣaṇasyotpattiḥ saṃbhavati saṃkarṣaṇācca pradyumasya pradyumāccāiruddhasya atiśayābhāvāt bhavitavyaṃ hi kāryakāraṇayoratiśayea yathā mṛddhaṭayoḥ a hyasatyatiśaye kāryaṃ kāraṇamityavakalpate a
ca pañcarātrasiddhātibhirvāsudevādiṣu ekasmisarveṣu vā jñāaiśvaryāditāratamyakṛtaḥ kaścidbhedobhyupagamyate vāsudevā eva hi sarve vyūhā irviśeṣā iṣyate a caite bhagavadvyūhāścatuḥsaṃkhyāyāmevāvatiṣṭhera brahmādistambaparyatasya samastasyaiva jagato bhagavadvyūhatvāvagamāt
vipratiṣedhāc ca vipratiṣedhaśca asmi śāstre bahuvidha upalabhyate guṇaguṇitvakalpaādilakṣaṇaḥ jñāaiśvaryaśaktibalavīryatejāṃsi guṇāḥ ātmāa evaite bhagavato vāsudevā ityādidarśaāt vedavipratiṣedhaśca bhavati caturṣu vedeṣu paraṃ
śreyolabdhvā śāṇḍilya idaṃ śāstramadhigatavāityādivedaidādarśaāt tasmāt asaṃgataiṣā kalpaeti siddham iti śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācāryasya śrīgovidabhagavatpūjyapādaśiṣyasya śrīmacchaṃkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīrakamīmāṃsāsūtrabhāṣye dvitīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ murat dvitīyodhyāyaḥ tṛtīyaḥ
pādaḥ a viyadaśruteḥ viyadadhikaraṇam kimasyākāśasyotpattirasti uta āstīti tatra tāvatpratipadyate a viyadaśruteriti a khalvākāśamutpadyate kasmāt aśruteḥ a hyasyotpattiprakaraṇe śravaṇamasti chādogye hi
sadeva somyedamagra āsīdekamevādvitīyam iti sacchabdavācyaṃ brahma prakṛtya tadaikṣata tattejosṛjata iti ca pañcāāṃ mahābhūtāāṃ madhyamaṃ teja ādi kṛtvā trayāṇāṃ tejobaāāmutpattiḥ śrāvyate
śrutiśca aḥ pramāṇamatīdriyārthavijñāotpattau a ca atra śrutirastyākāśasyotpattipratipādiī tasmāākāśasyotpattiriti asti tu tuśabdaḥ pakṣātaraparigrahe mā āmākāśasya chādogye bhūdutpattiḥ śrutyatare tv asti taittirīyakā
hi samāmaati satyaṃ jñāam aataṃ brahma iti prakṛtya tasmād vā etasmād ātmaa ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti tataś ca śrutyor vipratiṣedhaḥ kvacit
tejaḥpramukhā sṛṣṭiḥ kvacidākāśapramukheti av ekavākyatā aayoḥ śrutyoryuktā satyaṃ sā yuktā a tu sā avagatuṃ śakyate kutaḥ tattejosṛjata iti sakṛcchrutasya sraṣṭuḥ
sraṣṭavyadvayea saṃbadhāupapatteḥ tattejosṛjata tadākāśamasṛjata iti au sakṛcchrutasyāpi kartuḥ kartavyadvayea saṃbadho dṛśyate yathā saḥ sūpaṃ paktvā odaaṃ pacatīti evaṃ tadākāśaṃ sṛṣṭvā
tattejosṛjata iti yojayiṣyāmi aivaṃ yujyate prathamajatvaṃ hi chādogye tejasovagamyate taittirīyake ca ākāśasya a ca ubhayoḥ prathamajatvaṃ saṃbhavati etea itaraśrutyakṣaravirodhopi vyākhyātaḥ
tasmādvā etasmādātmaa ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ ityatrāpi tasmādākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ tasmāttejaḥ saṃbhūtam iti sakṛcchrutasyāpādāasya saṃbhavaasya ca viyattejobhyāṃ yugapatsaṃbadhāupapatteḥ vāyoragiḥ iti ca pṛthagāmāāt asmivipratiṣedhe
kaścidāha goṇyasambhavāt āsti viyata utpattiḥ aśrutereva yā tvitarā viyadutpattivādiī śrutirudāhṛtā sā gauṇī bhavitumarhati kasmāt asaṃbhavāt a hyākāśasyotpattiḥ saṃbhāvayituṃ śakyā śrīmatkaṇabhugabhiprāyāusāripu
jīvatsu te hi kāraṇasāmagryasaṃbhavādākāśasyotpattiṃ vārayati samavāyyasamavāyiimittakāraṇebhyo hi kila sarvamutpadyamāaṃ samutpadyate dravyasya caikajātīyakamaekaṃ ca dravyaṃ samavāyikāraṇaṃ bhavati a cākāśasyaikajātīyakamaekaṃ ca dravyamārambhakamasti
yasmisamavāyikāraṇe sati asamavāyikāraṇe ca tatsaṃyoge ākāśa utpadyeta tadabhāvāttu tadaugrahapravṛttaṃ imittakāraṇaṃ dūrāpetameva ākāśasya bhavati utpattimatāṃ ca tejaḥprabhṛtīāṃ pūrvottarakālayorviśeṣaḥ saṃbhāvyate prāgutpatteḥ prakāśādikāryaṃ
a babhūva paścācca bhavatīti ākāśasya puara pūrvottarakālayorviśeṣaḥ saṃbhāvayituṃ śakyate kiṃ hi prāgutpatteraavakāśamasuṣiramacchidraṃ babhūveti śakyatedhyavasātum pṛthivyādivaidharmyācca vibhutvādilakṣaṇāt ākāśasya ajatvasiddhiḥ tasmādyathā loke
ākāśaṃ kuru ākāśo jātaḥ ityevaṃjātīyako gauṇaḥ prayogo bhavati yathā caghaṭākāśaḥ karakākāśaḥ gṛhākāśaḥ ityekasyāpyākāśasya evaṃjātīyako bhedavyapadeśo gauṇo bhavati vedepi āraṇyāākāśeṣvālabhera iti
evamutpattiśrutirapi gauṇī draṣṭavyā śabdācca śabdaḥ khalvapyākāśasya ajatvaṃ khyāpayati yata āha vāyuścātarikṣaṃ caitadamṛtam iti a hyamṛtasyotpattirupapadyate ākāśavatsarvagataśca ityaḥ iti ca ākāśea
brahma sarvagatatvaityatvābhyāṃ dharmābhyāmupamimāaḥ ākāśasyāpi tau dharmau sūcayati a ca tādṛśasyotpattirupapadyate sa yathāatoyamākāśa evamaata ātmā veditavyaḥ iti ca udāharaṇ ākāśaśarīraṃ brahma
ākāśa ātmā iti ca a hyākāśasyotpattimattve brahmaṇastea viśeṣaṇaṃ saṃbhavati īleevotpalasya tasmāityamevākāśea sādhāraṇaṃ brahmeti gamyate syāccaikasya brahmaśabdavat idaṃ padottaraṃ sūtram syādetat
kathaṃ puarekasya saṃbhūtaśabdasya tasmādvā etasmādātmaa ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ ityasmiadhikāre pareṣu tejaḥprabhṛtiṣvauvartamāasya mukhyatvaṃ saṃbhavati ākāśe ca gauṇatvamiti ata uttaramucyate syāccaikasyāpi saṃbhūtaśabdasya viṣayaviśeṣavaśādgauṇo
mukhyaśca prayogaḥ brahmaśabdavat yathaikasyāpi brahmaśabdasya tapasā brahma vijijñāsasva tapo brahma ityasmiadhikāreādiṣu gauṇaḥ prayogaḥ āade ca mukhyaḥ yathā ca tapasi brahmavijñāasādhae
brahmaśabdo bhaktyā prayujyate añjasā tu vijñeye brahmaṇi tadvat kathaṃ puarautpattau abhasaḥ ekamevādvitīyam itīyaṃ pratijñā samarthyate au abhasā dvitīyea sadvitīyaṃ brahma
prāpoti kathaṃ ca brahmaṇi vidite sarvaṃ viditaṃ syāditi taducyate ekameva iti tāvatsvakāryāpekṣayopapadyate yathā loke kaścitkumbhakārakule pūrvedyurmṛddaṇḍacakrādīi ca upalabhya aparedyuśca āāvidhāyamatrāṇi
prasāritāyupalabhya brūyāt mṛdevaikākiī pūrvedyurāsīt iti sa ca tayāvadhāraṇayā mṛtkāryajātameva pūrvedyurāsīdityabhipreyāt a daṇḍacakrādi tadvadadvitīyaśrutiradhiṣṭhātrataraṃ vārayati yathā mṛdomatraprakṛteḥ kumbhakārodhiṣṭhātā dṛśyate aivaṃ brahmaṇo
jagatprakṛterayodhiṣṭhātā astīti a ca abhasāpi dvitīyea sadvitīyaṃ brahma prasajyate lakṣaṇāyatvaimittaṃ hi āātvam a ca prāgutpatterbrahmaabhasorlakṣaṇāyatvamasti kṣīrodakayoriva saṃsṛṣṭayoḥ vyāpitvāmūrtatvādidharmasāmāyāt sargakāle tu
brahma jagadutpādayituṃ yatate stimitamitarattiṣṭhati teāyatvamavasīyate tathā ca ākāśaśarīraṃ brahma ityādiśrutibhyopi brahmākāśayorabhedopacārasiddhiḥ ata eva ca brahmavijñāea sarvavijñāasiddhiḥ api ca sarvaṃ kāryamutpadyamāamākāśeāvyatiriktadeśakālamevotpadyate
brahmaṇā ca avyatiriktadeśakālamevākāśaṃ bhavatīti ato brahmaṇā tatkāryeṇa ca vijñātea sahavijñātamevākāśaṃ bhavati yathā kṣīrapūrṇe ghaṭe katicidabbidavaḥ prakṣiptāḥ sataḥ kṣīragrahaṇeaiva gṛhītā bhavati
a hi kṣīragrahaṇādabbidugrahaṇaṃ pariśiṣyate evaṃ brahmaṇā tatkāryaiścāvyatiriktadeśakālatvāt gṛhītameva brahmagrahaṇea abho bhavati tasmādbhāktaṃ abhasaḥ saṃbhavaśravaṇamiti evaṃ prāpte idamāha pratijñāhāiravyatirekācchabdebhyaḥ yeāśrutśrutaṃ bhavatyamataṃ
matamavijñātaṃ vijñātam iti ātmai khalvare dṛṣṭe śrute mate vijñāte idaṃ sarvaṃ viditam iti kasmiu bhagavo vijñāte sarvamidaṃ vijñātaṃ bhavati iti
a kācaa madbahirdhā vidyāsti iti caivaṃrūpā prativedātaṃ pratijñā vijñāyate tasyāḥ pratijñāyā evamahāirauparodhaḥ syāt yadyavyatirekaḥ kṛtsasya vastujātasya vijñeyādbrahmaṇaḥ syāt vyatireke hi
sati ekavijñāāea sarvaṃ vijñāyata itīyaṃ pratijñā hīyeta sa cāvyatireka evamupapadyate yadi kṛtsaṃ vastujātamekasmādbrahmaṇa utpadyeta śabdebhyaśca prakṛtivikārāvyatirekayāyeaiva pratijñāsiddhiravagamyate tathā hi yeāśrutśrutaṃ
bhavati iti pratijñāya mṛdādidṛṣṭātaiḥ kāryakāraṇābhedapratipādaaparaiḥ pratijñaiṣā samarthyate tatsādhaāyaiva cottare śabdāḥ sadeva somyedamagra āsīdekamevādvitīyam tadaikṣata tattejosṛjata ityevaṃ kāryajātaṃ brahmaṇaḥ pradarśya avyatirekaṃ
pradarśayati aitadātmyamidsarvam ityārabhya ā prapāṭhakaparisamāpteḥ tadyadyākāśaṃ a brahmakāryaṃ syāt a brahmaṇi vijñāte ākāśaṃ vijñāyeta tataśca pratijñāhāiḥ syāt a ca pratijñāhāyā
vedasyāprāmāṇyaṃ yuktaṃ kartum tathā hi prativedātaṃ te te śabdāstea tea dṛṣṭātea tāmeva pratijñāṃ jñāpayati idaṃ sarvaṃ yadayamātmā brahmaivedamamṛtaṃ purastāt ityevamādayaḥ
tasmājjvalaādivadeva gagaamapyutpadyate yaduktam aśrutera viyadutpadyata iti tadayuktam viyadutpattiviṣayaśrutyatarasya darśitatvāt tasmādvā etasmādātmaa ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti satyaṃ darśitam viruddhaṃ tu tattejosṛjata ityaea
śrutyatareṇa a ekavākyatvātsarvaśrutīām bhavatvekavākyatvamaviruddhāām iha tu virodha uktaḥ sakṛcchrutasya sraṣṭuḥ sraṣṭavyadvayasaṃbadhāsaṃbhavāddvayośca prathamajatvāsaṃbhavādvikalpāsaṃbhavācceti aiṣa doṣaḥ tejaḥsargasya taittirīyake tṛtīyatvaśravaṇāt tasmādvā etasmādātmaa ākāśaḥ
saṃbhūtaḥ ākāśādvāyuḥ vāyoragiḥ iti aśakyā hīyaṃ śrutirayathā pariṇetum śakyā tu pariṇetuṃ chādogyaśrutiḥ tadākāśaṃ vāyuṃ ca sṛṣṭvā tattejosṛjata iti a hīyaṃ
śrutistejojaipradhāā satī śrutyataraprasiddhāmākāśasyotpattiṃ vārayituṃ śakoti ekasya vākyasya vyāpāradvayāsaṃbhavāt sraṣṭā tvekopi krameṇāekaṃ sraṣṭavyaṃ sṛjet ityekavākyatvakalpaāyāṃ saṃbhavatyāṃ a viruddhārthatvea śrutirhātavyā a cāsmābhiḥ
sakṛcchrutasya sraṣṭuḥ sraṣṭavyadvayasaṃbadhobhipreyate śrutyataravaśea sraṣṭavyātaropasaṃgrahāt yathā ca sarvaṃ khalvidaṃ brahma tajjalā ityatra sākṣādeva sarvasya vastujātasya brahmajatvaṃ śrūyamāṇaṃ a pradeśātaravihitaṃ tejaḥpramukhamutpattikramaṃ
vārayati evaṃ tejasopi brahmajatvaṃ śrūyamāṇaṃ a śrutyataravihitaṃ abhaḥpramukhamutpattikramaṃ vārayitumarhati au śamavidhāārthametadvākyam tajjalāiti śāta upāsīta iti śruteḥ aitatsṛṣṭivākyam tasmādetaa pradeśātaraprasiddhaṃ kramamauroddhumarhatīti
tattejosṛjata ityetatsṛṣṭivākyam tasmādatra yathāśruti kramo grahītavya iti etyucyate a hi tejaḥprāthamyāurodhea śrutyataraprasiddho viyatpadārthaḥ parityaktavyo bhavati padārthadharmatvātkramasya api ca tattejosṛjata iti
ātra kramasya vācakaḥ kaścicchabdosti arthāttu kramo gamyate sa ca vāyoragiḥ ityaea śrutyataraprasiddhea krameṇa ivāryate vikalpasamuccayau tu viyattejasoḥ prathamajatvaviṣayāvasaṃbhavāabhyupagamābhyāṃ ivārito tasmāāsti
śrutyorvipratiṣedhaḥ api ca chādogye yeāśrutaṃ śrutaṃ bhavati ityetāṃ pratijñāṃ vākyopakrame śrutāṃ samarthayitumasamāmātamapi viyat utpattāvupasaṃkhyātavyam kimaṅga puastaittirīyake samāmātaṃ abho a saṃgṛhyate
yaccoktam ākāśasya sarveṇāayadeśakālatvādbrahmaṇā tatkāryaiśca saha viditameva tadbhavati ato a pratijñā hīyate a ca ekamevādvitīyam iti śrutikopo bhavati kṣīrodakavadbrahmaabhasoravyatirekopapatteriti atrocyate a
kṣīrodakayāyeedamekavijñāea sarvavijñāaṃ etavyam mṛdādidṛṣṭātapraṇayaāddhi prakṛtivikārayāyeaivedaṃ sarvavijñāaṃ etavyamiti gamyate kṣīrodakayāyea ca sarvavijñāaṃ kalpyamāaṃ a samyagvijñāaṃ syāt a hi kṣīrajñāagṛhītasyodakasya samyagvijñāagṛhītatvamasti a
ca vedasya puruṣāṇāmiva māyālīkavañcaādibhirarthāvadhāraṇamupapadyate sāvadhāraṇā ceyam ekamevādvitīyam iti śrutiḥ kṣīrodakayāyea īyamāā pīḍyeta a ca svakāryāpekṣayedaṃ vastvekadeśaviṣayaṃ sarvavijñāamevādvitīyatāvadhāraṇaṃ ceti yāyyam mṛdādiṣvapi
hi tatsaṃbhavāt a tadapūrvavadupayasitavyaṃ bhavati śvetaketo yau somyedaṃ mahāmaā aūcāamāī stabdhosyuta tamādeśamaprākṣyaḥ yeāśrutaṃ śrutaṃ bhavati ityādiā tasmādaśeṣavastuviṣayamevedaṃ sarvavijñāaṃ sarvasya brahmakāryatāpekṣayopayasyata
iti draṣṭavyam yatpuaretaduktam asaṃbhavādgauṇī gagaasyotpattiśrutiriti atra brūmaḥ yāvadvikāraṃ tu vibhāgo lokavat tuśabdosaṃbhavāśaṅkāvyāvṛttyarthaḥ a khalvākāśotpattāvasaṃbhavāśaṅkā kartavyā yato yāvatkiṃcidvikārajātaṃ dṛśyate ghaṭaghaṭikodañcaādi vā
kaṭakakeyūrakuṇḍalādi vā sūcīārācaistriṃśādi vā tāvāeva vibhāgo loke lakṣyate a tvavikṛtaṃ kiṃcitkutaścidvibhaktamupalabhyate vibhāgaścākāśasya pṛthivyādibhyovagamyate tasmātsopi vikāro bhavitumarhati etea dikkālamaaḥparamāṇvādīāṃ kāryatvaṃ vyākhyātam
avātmāpyākāśādibhyo vibhakta iti tasyāpi kāryatvaṃ ghaṭādivatprāpoti a ātmaa ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti śruteḥ yadi hyātmāpi vikāraḥ syāt tasmātparamayaa śrutamityākāśādi sarvaṃ kāryaṃ
irātmakamātmaaḥ kāryatve syāt tathā ca śūyavādaḥ prasajyeta ātmatvāccātmao irākaraṇaśaṅkāupapattiḥ a hyātmāgatukaḥ kasyacit svayaṃsiddhatvāt a hyātmā ātmaaḥ pramāṇamapekṣya sidhyati tasya hi
pratyakṣādīi pramāṇāyasiddhaprameyasiddhaye upādīyate a hyākāśādayaḥ padārthāḥ pramāṇairapekṣāḥ svayaṃ siddhāḥ keacidabhyupagamyate ātmā tu pramāṇādivyavahārāśrayatvātprāgeva pramāṇādivyavahārātsidhyati a cedṛśasya irākaraṇaṃ saṃbhavati āgatukaṃ hi
vastu irākriyate a svarūpam ya eva hi irākartā tadeva tasya svarūpam a hyagerauṣṇyamagiā irākriyate tathā ahamevedāīṃ jāāmi vartamāaṃ vastu ahamevātītamatītataraṃ
cājñāsiṣam ahamevāāgatamaāgatataraṃ ca jñāsyāmi ityatītāāgatavartamāabhāveāyathābhavatyapi jñātavye a jñāturayathābhāvosti sarvadā vartamāasvabhāvatvāt tathā bhasmībhavatyapi dehe ātmaa ucchedaḥ vartamāasvabhāvādayasvabhāvatvaṃ vā a saṃbhāvayituṃ śakyam
evamapratyākhyeyasvabhāvatvādakāryatvamātmāaḥ kāryatvaṃ ca ākāśasya yattūktaṃ samāajātīyamaekaṃ kāraṇadravyaṃ vyomo āstīti tatpratyucyate a tāvatsamāajātīyamevārabhate a bhiajātīyamiti iyamosti a hi tatūāṃ tatsaṃyogāāṃ ca
samāajātīyatvamasti dravyaguṇatvābhyupagamāt a ca imittakāraṇāāmapi turīvemādīāṃ samāajātīyatvaiyamosti syādetat samavāyikāraṇaviṣaya eva samāajātīyatvābhyupagamaḥ a kāraṇātaraviṣaya iti tadapyaaikātikam sūtragovālairhyaekajātīyairekā rajjuḥ sṛjyamāā dṛśyate tathā
sūtrairūrṇādibhiśca vicitrākambalāvitavate sattvadravyatvādyapekṣayā vā samāajātīyatve kalpyamāe iyamāarthakyam sarvasya sarveṇa samāajātīyakatvāt āpyaekamevārabhate aikam iti iyamosti aṇumaasorādyakarmārambhābhyupagamāt ekaiko hi paramāṇurmaaścādyaṃ karmārabhate a
dravyātaraiḥ saṃhatya ityabhyupagamyate dravyārambha evāekārambhakatvaiyama iti cet a pariṇāmābhyupagamāt bhavedeṣa iyamaḥ yadi saṃyogasacivaṃ dravyaṃ dravyātarasyārambhakamabhyupagamyeta tadeva tu dravyaṃ viśeṣavadavasthātaramāpadyamāaṃ kāryaṃ
āmābhyupagamyate tacca kvacidaekaṃ pariṇamate mṛdbījādi aṅkurādibhāvea kvacidekaṃ pariṇamate kṣīrādi dadhyādibhāvea eśvaraśāsaamiti aekameva kāraṇaṃ kāryaṃ jaayatīti ataḥ śrutiprāmāṇyādekasmādbrahmaṇa ākāśādimahābhūtotpattikrameṇa jagajjātamiti iścīyate
tathā coktam upasaṃhāradarśaāeti cea kṣīravaddhi iti yaccoktam ākāśasyotpattau a pūrvottarakālayorviśeṣaḥ saṃbhāvayituṃ śakyata iti tadayuktam yeaiva viśeṣeṇa pṛthivyādibhyo vyatiricyamāaṃ abhaḥ svarūpavadidāīmadhyavasīyate
sa eva viśeṣaḥ prāgutpatterāsīditi gamyate yathā ca brahma a sthūlādibhiḥ pṛthivyādisvabhāvaiḥ svabhāvavat asthūlamaaṇu ityādiśrutibhyaḥ evamākāśasvabhāveāpi a svabhāvavadaākāśamiti śruteravagamyate tasmātprāgutpatteraākāśamiti sthitam
yadapyuktaṃ pṛthivyādivaidharmyādākāśasyājatvamiti tadapyasat śrutivirodhe satyutpattyasaṃbhavāumāasyābhāsatvopapatteḥ utpattyaumāasya ca darśitatvāt aityamākāśam aityaguṇāśrayatvāt ghaṭādivadityādiprayogasaṃbhavācca ātmayaaikātikamiti cet a tasyaupaiṣadaṃ pratyaityaguṇāśrayatvāsiddheḥ vibhutvādīāṃ ca ākāśasyotpattivādiaṃ pratyasiddhatvāt
yaccoktametat śabdācceti tatrāmṛtatvaśrutistāvadviyati amṛtā divaukasaḥ itivaddraṣṭavyā utpattipralayayorupapāditatvāt ākāśavatsarvagataśca ityaḥ ityapi prasiddhamahattveākāśopamāaṃ kriyate iratiśayamahattvāya a ākāśasamatvāya yathā iṣuriva savitā dhāvati iti
kṣipragatitvāyocyate a iṣutulyagatitvāya tadvat eteāatatvopamāaśrutirvyākhyātā jyāyāākāśāt ityādiśrutibhyaśca brahmaṇaḥ sakāśādākāśasyoaparimāṇatvasiddhiḥ a tasya pratimāsti iti ca brahmaṇoupamāatvaṃ darśayati atoyadārtam iti ca brahmaṇoyeṣāmākāśādīāmārtatvaṃ
darśayati tapasi brahmaśabdavadākāśasya jamaśrutergauṇatvamityetadākāśasaṃbhavaśrutyaumāābhyāṃ parihṛtam tasmādbrahmakāryaṃ viyaditi siddham etea mātariśvā vyākhyātaḥ mātariśvādhikaraṇam atideśoyam etea viyadvyākhyāea mātariśvāpi viyadāśrayo vāyurvyākhyātaḥ tatrāpyete yathāyogaṃ
pakṣā racayitavyāḥ a vāyurutpadyate chadogāāmutpattiprakaraṇeāmāādityekaḥ pakṣaḥ asti tu taittirīyāṇāmutpattiprakaraṇe āmāam ākāśādvāyuḥ iti pakṣātaram tataśca śrutyorvipratiṣedhe sati gauṇī vāyorutpattiśrutiḥ asaṃbhavāt ityaparobhiprāyaḥ
asaṃbhavaśca saiṣāastamitā devatā yadvāyuḥ ityastamayapratiṣedhādamṛtatvādiśravaṇācca pratijñāuparodhādyāvadvikāraṃ ca vibhāgābhyupagamādutpadyate vāyuriti siddhātaḥ astamayapratiṣedhoparavidyāviṣaya āpekṣikaḥ agyādīāmiva vāyorastamayābhāvāt kṛtapratividhāaṃ ca amṛtatvādiśravaṇam au vāyorākāśasya ca
tulyayorutpattiprakaraṇe śravaṇāśravaṇayorekamevādhikaraṇamubhayaviṣayamastu kimatideśeāsati viśeṣa iti ucyate satyamevametat tathāpi madadhiyāṃ śabdamātrakṛtāśaṅkāivṛttyarthoyamatideśaḥ kriyate saṃvargavidyādiṣu hyupāsyata vāyormahābhāgatvaśravaṇāt astamayapratiṣedhādibhyaśca bhavati ityatvāśaṅkā kasyaciditi asambhavastu satoupapatteḥ
asaṃbhavādhikaraṇam viyatpavaayorasaṃbhāvyamāajamaorapyutpattimupaśrutya brahmaṇopi bhavetkutaścidutpattiriti syātkasyacimatiḥ tathā vikārebhya evākāśādibhya uttareṣāṃ vikārāṇāmutpattimupaśrutya ākāśasyāpi vikārādeva brahmaṇa utpattiriti kaścimayeta tāmāśaṅkāmapaetumidaṃ sūtram asaṃbhavastviti a khalu
brahmaṇaḥ sadātmakasya kutaścidayataḥ saṃbhava utpattirāśaṅkitavyā kasmāt aupapatteḥ samātraṃ hi brahma a tasya samātrādevotpattiḥ saṃbhavati asatyatiśaye prakṛtivikārabhāvāupapatteḥ āpi sadviśeṣāt dṛṣṭaviparyayāt sāmāyādviśeṣā
utpadyamāā dṛśyate mṛdāderghaṭādayaḥ a tu viśeṣebhyaḥ sāmāyam āpyasataḥ irātmakatvāt kathamasataḥ sajjāyeta iti ca ākṣepaśravaṇāt sa kāraṇaṃ karaṇādhipādhipo a cāsya kaścijjaitā
a cādhipaḥ iti ca brahmaṇo jaayitāraṃ vārayati viyatpavaayoḥ puarutpattiḥ pradarśitā a tu brahmaṇaḥ sā astīti vaiṣamyam a ca vikārebhyo vikārātarotpattidarśaādbrahmaṇopi
vikāratvaṃ bhavitumarhati mūlaprakṛtyaabhyupagameavasthāprasaṅgāt yā mūlaprakṛtirabhyupagamyate tadeva ca o brahmetyavirodhaḥ tejotastathāhyāha tejodhikaraṇam chādogye samūlatvaṃ tejasaḥ śrāvitam taittirīyake tu vāyumūlatvam tatra tejoyoiṃ
prati śrutivipratipattau satyām prāptaṃ tāvadbrahmayoikaṃ teja iti kutaḥ sadeva ityupakramya tattejosṛjata ityupadeśāt sarvavijñāapratijñāyāśca brahmaprabhavatve sarvasya saṃbhavāt tajjalā iti ca aviśeṣaśruteḥ
etasmājjāyate prāṇaḥ iti ca upakramya śrutyatare sarvasyāviśeṣeṇa brahmajatvopadeśāt taittirīyake ca sa tapastaptvā idaṃ sarvamasṛjata yadidaṃ kiṃca ityaviśeṣaśravaṇāt tasmāt vāyoragiḥ iti
kramopadeśo draṣṭavyaḥ vāyoraataramagiḥ saṃbhūta iti evaṃ prāpte ucyate tejaḥ ataḥ mātariśvaaḥ jāyata iti kasmāt tathā hyāha vāyoragiḥ iti avyavahite hi
tejaso brahmajatve sati asati vāyujatve vāyoragiḥ itīyaṃ śrutiḥ kadarthitā syāt au kramārthaiṣā bhaviṣyatītyuktam eti brūmaḥ tasmādvā etasmādātmaa ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti
purastāt saṃbhavatyapādāasya ātmaaḥ pañcamīirdeśāt tasyaiva ca saṃbhavaterihādhikārāt parastādapi tadadhikāre pṛthivyā oṣadhayaḥ ityapādāapañcamīdarśaāt vāyoragiḥ ityapādāapañcamyevaiṣeti gamyate api ca vāyorūrdhvamagiḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti
kalpyaḥ upapadārthayogaḥ klṛptastu kārakārthayogaḥ vāyoragiḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti tasmādeṣā śrutirvāyuyoitvaṃ tejasovagamayati avitarāpi śrutirbrahmayoitvaṃ tejasovagamayati tattejosṛjata iti a tasyāḥ pāraṃparyajatvepyavirodhāt yadāpi hyākāśaṃ
vāyuṃ ca sṛṣṭvā vāyubhāvāpaaṃ brahma tejosṛjateti kalpyate tadāpi brahmajatvaṃ tejaso a virudhyate yathā tasyāḥ śrṛtam tasyā dadhi tasyā āmikṣetyādi darśayati
ca brahmaṇo vikārātmaāvasthāam tadātmāsvayamakuruta iti tathā ca īśvarasmaraṇaṃ bhavati buddhirjñāamasaṃmohaḥ ityādyaukramya bhavati bhāvā bhūtāāṃ matta eva pṛthagvidhāḥ iti yadyapi buddhyādayaḥ
svakāraṇebhyaḥ pratyakṣaṃ bhavato dṛśyate tathāpi sarvasya bhāvajātasya sākṣātpraṇāḍyā vā īśvaravaṃśyatvāt eteākramasṛṣṭivādiyaḥ śrutayo vyākhyātāḥ tāsāṃ sarvathopapatteḥ kramavatsṛṣṭivādiīāṃ tvayathāupapatteḥ pratijñāpi sadvaṃśyatvamātramapekṣate a
avyavahitajayatvam ityavirodhaḥ āpaḥ abadhikaraṇam atastathā hyāha ityauvartate āpaḥ ataḥ tejasaḥ jāyate kasmāt tathā hyāha tadaposṛjata iti agerāpaḥ iti ca sati
vacae āsti saṃśayaḥ tejasastu sṛṣṭiṃ vyākhyāya pṛthivyā vyākhyāsya apotariyāmiti āpaḥ iti sūtrayāṃbabhūva pṛthivyadhikārarūpaśabdātarebhyaḥ pṛthivyadhikārādhikaraṇam tā āpa aikṣata bahvyaḥ syāma prajāyemahīti
tā aam asṛjata iti śrūyate tatra saṃśayaḥ kim aeāaśabdea vrīhiyavādy abhyavahāryaṃ vā odaādy ucyate kiṃ vā pṛthivīti tatra prāptaṃ tāvat
vrīhiyavādi odaādi vā parigrahītavyam iti tatra hy aaśabdaḥ prasiddho loke vākyaśeṣo py etam artham upodbalayati tasmād yatra kvacaa varṣati tad
eva bhūyiṣṭham aaṃ bhavati iti vrīhiyavādy eva hi sati varṣaṇe bahu bhavati a pṛthivīti evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ pṛthivy eveyam aaśabdeādbhyo
jāyamāā vivakṣyata iti kasmāt adhikārāt rūpāt śabdātarāc ca adhikāras tāvat tat tejo sṛjata tadapo sṛjata iti mahābhūtaviṣayo vartate tatra kramaprāptāṃ
pṛthivīṃ mahābhūtaṃ vilaṅghya ākasmād vrīhyādiparigraho yāyyaḥ tathā rūpam api vākyaśeṣe pṛthivyauguṇaṃ dṛśyate yat kṛṣṇaṃ tad aasya iti a hy odaāder
abhyavahāryasya kṛṣṇatvaiyamo sti āpi vrīhyādīām au pṛthivyā api aiva kṛṣṇatvaiyamo sti payaḥpāṇḍurasyāṅgārarohitasya ca kṣetrasya darśaāt āyaṃ doṣaḥ bāhulyāpekṣatvāt bhūyiṣṭhaṃ hi
pṛthivyāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ rūpam a tathā śvetarohite paurāṇikā api pṛthivīcchāyāṃ śarvarīm upadiśati sā ca kṛṣṇābhāsā ity ataḥ kṛṣṇaṃ rūpaṃ pṛthivyā iti
śliṣyate śrutyataram api samāādhikāram adabhyaḥ pṛthivī iti bhavati tad yad apāṃ śara āsīt tat samahayata sā pṛthivy abhavat iti ca
pṛthivyās tu vrīhyāder utpattiṃ darśayati pṛthivyā oṣadhaya oṣadhībhyo am iti ca evam adhikārādiṣu pṛthivyāḥ pratipādakeṣu satsu kuto vrīhyādipratipattiḥ prasiddhir apy
adhikārādibhir eva bādhyate vākyaśeṣo pi pārthivatvād aādy asya taddvāreṇa pṛthivyā evādbhyaḥ prabhavatvaṃ sūcayatīti draṣṭavyam tasmāt pṛthivīyam aaśabda iti tadabhidhyāādeva tu
talliṅgātsaḥ tadabhidhyāādhikaraṇam kimimāi viyadādīi bhūtāi svayameva svavikārāsṛjati āhosvitparameśvara eva tea tea ātmaāvatiṣṭhamāobhidhyāya taṃ taṃ vikāraṃ sṛjatīti saṃdehe sati prāptaṃ tāvat
svayameva sṛjatīti kutaḥ ākāśādvāyurvāyoragiḥ ityādisvātatryaśravaṇāt au acetaāāṃ svatatrāṇāṃ pravṛttiḥ pratiṣiddhā aiṣa doṣaḥ tatteja aikṣata tā āpa aikṣata iti ca bhūtāāmapi
cetaatvaśravaṇāditi evaṃ prāpte abhidhīyate sa eva parameśvarastea tea ātmaā avatiṣṭhamāobhidhyāya taṃ taṃ vikāraṃ sṛjatīti kutaḥ talliṅgāt tathā hi śāstram yaḥ
pṛthivyāṃ tiṣṭhayaḥ pṛthivyā ataro yaṃ pṛthivī a veda yasya pṛthivī śarīraṃ yaḥ pṛthivīmataro yamayati ityevaṃjātīyakam sādhyakṣāṇāmeva bhūtāāṃ pravṛttiṃ darśayati tathā

śarīraikadeśasaṃbaddhopi sa sakaladehavyāpiamāhlādaṃ karoti evamātmāpi dehaikadeśasthaḥ sakaladehavyāpiīmupalabdhiṃ kariṣyati tvaksaṃbadhāccāsya sakalaśarīragatā vedaā a virudhyate tvagātmaorhi saṃbadhaḥ kṛtsāyāṃ tvaci vartate tvakca kṛtsaśarīravyāpiīti
avasthitivaiśeṣyāditi ceābhyupagamāddhṛdi hi atrāha yaduktamavirodhaścadaavaditi tadayuktam dṛṣṭātadārṣṭātikayoratulyatvāt siddhe hi ātmao dehaikadeśasthatve cadaadṛṣṭāto bhavati pratyakṣaṃ tu cadaasyāvasthitivaiśeṣyamekadeśasthatvaṃ sakaladehāhlādaaṃ ca ātmaaḥ puaḥ
sakaladehopalabdhimātraṃ pratyakṣam aikadeśavartitvam aumeyaṃ tu taditi yadapyucyeta a ca atrāumāaṃ saṃbhavati kimātmaaḥ sakalaśarīragatā vedaā tvagidriyasyeva sakaladehavyāpiaḥ sataḥ kiṃ vā vibhorabhasa
iva āhosviccadaabidorivāṇorekadeśasthasya iti saṃśayāativṛtteriti atrocyate āyaṃ doṣaḥ kasmāt abhyupagamāt abhyupagamyate hi ātmaopi cadaasyeva dehaikadeśavṛttitvamavasthitivaiśeṣyam kathamiti ucyate hṛdi hyeṣa ātmā paṭhyate
vedāteṣu hṛdi hyeṣa ātmā sa vā eṣa ātmā hṛdi katama ātmeti yoyaṃ vijñāamayaḥ prāṇeṣu hṛdyatarjyotiḥ puruṣaḥ ityādyupadeśebhyaḥ tasmāddṛṣṭātadārṣṭātikayoravaiṣamyāt yuktamevaitat avirodhaścadaavat
iti guṇādvā lokavat caitayaguṇavyāptervā aṇorapi sato jīvasya sakaladehavyāpi kāryaṃ a virudhyate yathā loke maṇipradīpaprabhṛtīāmapavarakaikadeśavartiāmapi prabhā apavarakavyāpiī satī kṛtsepavarake kāryaṃ karoti
tadvat syāt kadāciccadaasya sāvayavatvātsūkṣmāvayavavisarpaṇeāpi sakaladeha āhlādayitṛtvam a tvaṇorjīvasyāvayavāḥ sati yairayaṃ sakaladehaṃ visarpet ityāśaṅkya guṇādvā lokavat ityuktam kathaṃ puarguṇo guṇivyatirekeṇāyatra varteta
a hi paṭasya śuklo guṇaḥ paṭavyatirekeṇāyatra vartamāo dṛśyate pradīpaprabhāvadbhavediti cet a tasyā api dravyatvābhyupagamāt ibiḍāvayavaṃ hi tejodravyaṃ pradīpaḥ praviralāvayavaṃ tu
tejodravyameva prabhā iti ata uttaraṃ paṭhati vyatireko gadhavat yathā guṇasyāpi sato gadhasya gadhavaddravyavyatirekeṇa vṛttirbhavati aprāpteṣvapi kusumādiṣu gadhavatsu kusumagadhopalabdheḥ evamaṇorapi sato
jīvasya caitayaguṇavyatireko bhaviṣyati ataścāaikātikametat guṇatvādrūpādivadāśrayaviśleṣāupapattiriti guṇasyaiva sato gadhasya āśrayaviśleṣadarśaāt gadhasyāpi sahaivāśrayeṇa viśleṣa iti cet a yasmāmūladravyādviśleṣaḥ tasya kṣayaprasaṅgāt akṣīyamāṇamapi tatpūrvāvasthāto
gamyate ayathā tatpūrvāvasthairgurutvādibhirhīyeta syādetat gadhāśrayāṇāṃ viśliṣṭāāmavayavāāmalpatvāt saapi viśleṣo opalakṣyate sūkṣmā hi gadhaparamāṇavaḥ sarvato viprasṛtā gadhabuddhimutpādayati āsikāpuṭamaupraviśata iti cet a atīdriyatvātparamāṇūām
sphuṭagadhopalabdheśca āgakesarādiṣu a ca loke pratītiḥ gadhavaddravyamāghrātamiti gadha eva āghrāta iti tu laukikāḥ pratiyati rūpādiṣvāśrayavyatirekāupalabdhergadhasyāpyayukta āśrayavyatireka iti cet a pratyakṣatvādaumāāpravṛtteḥ
tasmāt yat yathā loke dṛṣṭam tat tathaiva aumatavyaṃ irūpakaiḥ āyathā a hi raso guṇo jihvayopalabhyata ityato rūpādayopi guṇā jihvayaivopalabhyeraiti iyatuṃ
śakyate tathā ca darśayati hṛdayāyataatvamaṇuparimāṇatvaṃ ca ātmaaḥ abhidhāya tasyaiva ā lomabhya ā akhāgrebhyaḥ iti caitayea guṇea samastaśarīravyāpitvaṃ darśayati pṛthagupadeśāt prajñayā
śarīraṃ samāruhya iti ca ātmaprajñayoḥ kartṛkaraṇabhāvea pṛthagupadeśāt caitayaguṇeaiva asya śarīravyāpitā gamyate tadeṣāṃ prāṇāāṃ vijñāea vijñāamādāya iti ca kartuḥ śārīrātpṛthagvijñāasyopadeśaḥ etamevābhiprāyamupodbalayati
tasmādaṇurātmeti evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ tadguṇasāratvāttu tadvyapadeśaḥ prājñavat tuśabdaḥ pakṣaṃ vyāvartayati aitadasti aṇurātmeti utpattyaśravaṇāt parasyaiva tu brahmaṇaḥ praveśaśravaṇāt tādātmyopadeśācca parameva brahma
jīva ityuktam parameva cedbrahma jīvaḥ tasmādyāvatparaṃ brahma tāvāeva jīvo bhavitumarhati parasya ca brahmaṇo vibhutvamāmātam tasmādvibhurjīvaḥ tathā ca sa vā eṣa
mahāaja ātmā yoyaṃ vijñāamayaḥ prāṇeṣu ityevaṃjātīyakā jīvaviṣayā vibhutvavādāḥ śrautāḥ smārtāśca samarthitā bhavati a ca aṇorjīvasya sakalaśarīragatā vedaopapadyate tvaksaṃbadhātsyāditi cet a
kaṇṭakatodaepi sakalaśarīragataiva vedaā prasajyeta tvakkaṇṭakayorhi saṃyogaḥ kṛtsāyāṃ tvaci vartate tvakca kṛtsaśarīravyāpiīti pādatala eva tu kaṇṭakauo vedaāṃ pratilabhate a ca aṇorguṇavyāptirupapadyate
guṇasya guṇideśatvāt guṇatvameva hi guṇiamaāśritya guṇasya hīyeta pradīpaprabhāyāśca dravyātaratvaṃ vyākhyātam gadhopi guṇatvābhyupagamātsāśraya eva saṃcaritumarhati ayathā guṇatvahāiprasaṅgāt tathā coktaṃ bhagavatā dvaipāyaea
upalabhyāpsu cedgadhaṃ kecidbrūyuraaipuṇāḥ pṛthivyāmeva taṃ vidyādapo vāyuṃ ca saṃśritam iti yadi ca caitayaṃ jīvasya samastaśarīraṃ vyāpuyāt āṇurjīvaḥ syāt caitayameva hi
asya svarūpam agerivauṣṇyaprakāśau ātra guṇaguṇivibhāgo vidyata iti śarīraparimāṇatvaṃ ca pratyākhyātam pariśeṣādvibhurjīvaḥ kathaṃ tarhi aṇutvādivyapadeśa ityata āha tadguṇasāratvāttu tadvyapadeśa iti tasyā
buddheḥ guṇāstadguṇāḥ icchā dveṣaḥ sukhaṃ duḥkhamityevamādayaḥ tadguṇāḥ sāraḥ pradhāaṃ yasyātmaaḥ saṃsāritve saṃbhavati sa tadguṇasāraḥ tasya bhāvastadguṇasāratvam a hi buddherguṇairviā kevalasya
ātmaaḥ saṃsāritvamasti buddhyupādhidharmādhyāsaimittaṃ hi kartṛtvabhoktṛtvādilakṣaṇaṃ saṃsāritvam akarturabhoktuścāsaṃsāriṇo ityamuktasya sata ātmaaḥ tasmāttadguṇasāratvādbuddhiparimāṇeāsya parimāṇavyapadeśaḥ tadutkrātyādibhiśca asyotkrātyādivyapadeśaḥ a svataḥ tathā ca vālāgraśatabhāgasya śatadhā
kalpitasya ca bhāgo jīvaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ sa cāatyāya kalpate ityaṇutvaṃ jīvasyoktvā tasyaiva puarāatyamāha taccaivameva samañjasaṃ syāt yadyaupacārikamaṇutvaṃ jīvasya bhavet pāramārthikaṃ
ca āatyam a hi ubhayaṃ mukhyamavakalpeta a ca āatyamaupacārikamiti śakyaṃ vijñātum sarvopaiṣatsu brahmātmabhāvasya pratipipādayiṣitatvāt tathetarasmiapyumāe buddherguṇeātmaguṇea caiva ārāgramātro hyavaropi dṛṣṭaḥ
iti ca buddhiguṇasaṃbadheaiva ārāgramātratāṃ śāsti a sveaivātmaā eṣoṇurātmā cetasā veditavyaḥ ityatrāpi a jīvasya aṇuparimāṇatvaṃ śiṣyate parasyaivātmaaścakṣurādyaavagrāhyatvea jñāaprasādagamyatvea ca prakṛtatvāt jīvasyāpi
ca mukhyāṇuparimāṇatvāupapatteḥ tasmāddurjñāatvābhiprāyamidamaṇutvavacaam upādhyabhiprāyaṃ vā draṣṭavyam tathā prajñayā śarīraṃ samāruhya ityevaṃjātīyakeṣvapi bhedopadeśeṣu buddhyaivopādhibhūtayā jīvaḥ śarīraṃ samāruhya ityevaṃ yojayitavyam vyapadeśamātraṃ vā
śilāputrakasya śarīramityādivat a hyatra guṇaguṇivibhāgopi vidyata ityuktam hṛdayāyataatvavacaamapi buddhereva tadāyataatvāt tathā utkrātyādīāmapyupādhyāyattatāṃ darśayati kasmiu ahamutkrāta utkrāto bhaviṣyāmi kasmivā pratiṣṭhite pratiṣṭhāsyāmīti
sa prāṇamasṛjata iti utkrātyabhāve hi gatyāgatyorapyabhāvo vijñāyate a hi aapasṛptasya dehādgatyāgatī syātām evamupādhiguṇasāratvājjīvasyāṇutvādivyapadeśaḥ prājñavat yathā prājñasya paramātmaaḥ saguṇeṣūpāsaeṣu upādhiguṇasāratvādaṇīyastvādivyapadeśaḥ aṇīyāvrīhervā
yavādvā maomayaḥ prāṇamayaḥ prāṇaśarīraḥ sarvagadhaḥ sarvarasaḥ satyakāmaḥ satyasaṃkalpaḥ ityevaṃprakāraḥ tadvat syādetat yadi buddhiguṇasāratvādātmaaḥ saṃsāritvaṃ kalpyeta tato buddhyātmaorbhiayoḥ saṃyogāvasāamavaśyaṃbhāvītyato buddhiviyoge sati
ātmao vibhaktasyāālakṣyatvādasattvamasaṃsāritvaṃ vā prasajyeteti ata uttaraṃ paṭhati yāvadātmabhāvitvācca a doṣastaddarśaāt eyamaatarairdiṣṭadoṣaprāptirāśaṅkaīyā kasmāt yāvadātmabhāvitvādbuddhisaṃyogasya yāvadayamātmā saṃsārī bhavati yāvadasya samyagdarśaea saṃsāritvaṃ a
ivartate tāvadasya buddhyā saṃyogo a śāmyati yāvadeva cāyaṃ buddhyupādhisaṃbadhaḥ tāvadevāsya jīvatvaṃ saṃsāritvaṃ ca paramārthatastu a jīvo āma buddhyupādhiparikalpitasvarūpavyatirekeṇāsti a hi
ityamuktasvarūpātsarvajñādīśvarādayaścetao dhāturdvitīyo vedātārthairūpaṇāyāmupalabhyate āyotosti draṣṭā śrotā matā vijñātā āyadatosti draṣṭṛ śrotṛ matṛ vijñātṛ tattvamasi ahaṃ brahmāsmi ityādiśrutiśatebhyaḥ kathaṃ puaravagamyate yāvadātmabhāvī
buddhisaṃyoga iti taddarśaādityāha tathā hi śāstraṃ darśayati yoyaṃ vijñāamayaḥ prāṇeṣu hṛdyatarjyotiḥ puruṣaḥ sa samāaḥ saubhau lokāvausaṃcarati dhyāyatīva lelāyatīva ityādi tatra
vijñāamaya iti buddhimaya ityetaduktaṃ bhavati pradeśātare vijñāamayo maomayaḥ prāṇamayaścakṣurmayaḥ śrotramayaḥ iti vijñāamayasya maaādibhiḥ saha pāṭhāt buddhimayatvaṃ ca tadguṇasāratvamevābhipreyate yathā loke
strīmayo devadatta iti strīrāgādipradhāobhidhīyate tadvat sa samāaḥ saubhau lokāvausaṃcarati iti ca lokātaragamaepyaviyogaṃ buddhyā darśayati kea samāaḥ tayaiva buddhyeti gamyate saṃidhāāt
tacca darśayati dhyāyatīva lelāyatīva iti etaduktaṃ bhavati āyaṃ svato dhyāyati āpi calati dhyāyatyāṃ buddhau dhyāyatīva calatyāṃ buddhau calatīveti api ca
mithyājñāapuraḥsaroyamātmao buddhyupādhisaṃbadhaḥ a ca mithyājñāasya samyagjñāādayatra ivṛttirastītyato yāvadbrahmātmatāavabodhaḥ tāvadayaṃ buddhyupādhisaṃbadho a śāmyati darśayati ca vedāhametaṃ puruṣaṃ mahātamādityavarṇaṃ tamasaḥ parastāt tameva
viditvāti mṛtyumeti āyaḥ pathā vidyateyaāya iti au suṣuptapralayayora śakyate buddhisaṃbadha ātmaobhyupagatum satā somya tadā saṃpao bhavati svamapīto bhavati iti vacaāt
kṛtsavikārapralayābhyupagamācca tatkathaṃ yāvadātmabhāvitvaṃ buddhisaṃbadhasyeti atrocyate puṃstvādivattvasya satobhivyaktiyogāt yathā loke puṃstvādīi bījātmaā vidyamāāyeva bālyādiṣvaupalabhyamāāyavidyamāavadabhipreyamāṇāi yauvaādiṣvāvirbhavati a avidyamāāyutpadyate ṣaṇḍādīāmapi tadutpattiprasaṅgāt evamayamapi buddhisaṃbadhaḥ
śaktyātmaā vidyamāa eva suṣuptapralayayoḥ puaḥ prabodhaprasavayorāvirbhavati evaṃ hi etadyujyate a hi ākasmikī kasyacidutpattiḥ saṃbhavati atiprasaṅgāt darśayati ca suṣuptādutthāamavidyātmakabījasadbhāvakāritam sati saṃpadya
a viduḥ sati saṃpadyāmaha iti ta iha vyāghro vā siṃho vā ityādiā tasmātsiddhametat yāvadātmabhāvī buddhyādyupādhisaṃbadha iti ityopalabdhyaupalabdhiprasaṅgoyataraiyamo vāyathā taccātmaa upādhibhūtam
ataḥkaraṇaṃ mao buddhirvijñāaṃ cittamiti ca aekadhā tatra tatrābhilapyate kvacicca vṛttivibhāgea saṃśayādivṛttikaṃ maa ityucyate iścayādivṛttikaṃ buddhiriti taccaivaṃ bhūtamataḥkaraṇamavaśyamastītyabhyupagatavyam ayathā hyaabhyupagamyamāe tasmiityopalabdhyaupalabdhiprasaṅgaḥ
syāt ātmedriyaviṣayāṇāmupalabdhisādhaāāṃ saṃidhāe sati ityamevopalabdhiḥ prasajyeta atha satyapi hetusamavadhāe phalābhāvaḥ tato ityamevāupalabdhiḥ prasajyeta a caivaṃ dṛśyate athavā ayatarasyātmaa idriyasya vā
śaktipratibadhobhyupagatavyaḥ a ca ātmaaḥ śaktipratibadhaḥ saṃbhavati avikriyatvāt āpi idriyasya a hi tasya pūrvottarayoḥ kṣaṇayorapratibaddhaśaktikasya satokasmācchaktiḥ pratibadhyeta tasmāt yasyāvadhāāavadhāābhyāmupalabdhyaupalabdhī bhavataḥ tamaaḥ
tathā ca śrutiḥ ayatramaā abhūvaṃ ādarśamayatramaā abhūvaṃ āśrauṣam iti maasā hyeva paśyati maasā śrṛṇoti iti ca kāmādayaścāsya vṛttaya iti darśayati
kāmaḥ saṃkalpo vicikitsā śraddhāśraddhā dhṛtiradhṛtirhrīrdhīrbhīrityetatsarvaṃ maa eva iti tasmādyuktametat tadguṇasāratvāttadvyapadeśa iti kartā śāstrārthavattvāt kartradhikaraṇam tadguṇasāratvādhikāreṇaivāparopi jīvadharmaḥ prapañcyate kartā ca ayaṃ
jīvaḥ syāt kasmāt śāstrārthavattvāt evaṃ ca yajeta juhuyāt dadyāt ityevaṃvidhaṃ vidhiśāstramarthavad vihāropadeśāt itaśca jīvasya kartṛtvam yajjīvaprakriyāyāṃ saṃdhye sthāe vihāramupadiśati sa
īyatemṛto yatra kāmam iti sve śarīre yathākāmaṃ parivartate iti ca upādāāt itaścāsya kartṛtvam yajjīvaprakriyāyāmeva karaṇāāmupādāaṃ saṃkīrtayati tadeṣāṃ prāṇāāṃ vijñāea vijñāamādāya
iti prāṇāgṛhītvā iti ca vyapadeśācca kriyāyāṃ a ceirdeśaviparyayaḥ itaśca jīvasya kartṛtvam yadasya laukikīṣu vaidikīṣu ca kriyāsu kartṛtvaṃ vyapadiśati śāstram vijñāaṃ
yajñaṃ taute karmāṇi tautepi ca iti au vijñāaśabdo buddhau samadhigataḥ kathamaea jīvasya kartṛtvaṃ sūcyata iti etyucyate jīvasyaivaiṣa irdeśaḥ a buddheḥ
a cejjīvasya syāt irdeśaviparyayaḥ syāt vijñāeetyevaṃ iradekṣyat tathā hi ayatra buddhivivakṣāyāṃ vijñāaśabdasya karaṇavibhaktiirdeśo dṛśyate tadeṣāṃ prāṇāāṃ vijñāea vijñāamādāya iti iha
tu vijñāaṃ yajñaṃ taute iti kartṛsāmāādhikaraṇyairdeśādbuddhivyatiriktasyaivātmaaḥ kartṛtvaṃ sūcyata ityadoṣaḥ atrāha yadi buddhivyatirikto jīvaḥ kartā syāt sa svatatraḥ sa priyaṃ hitaṃ
caiva ātmao iyamea saṃpādayet a viparītam viparītamapi tu saṃpādayaupalabhyate a ca svatatrasyātmaaḥ īdṛśī pravṛttiraiyameopapadyata iti ata uttaraṃ paṭhati upalabdhivadaiyamaḥ yathāyamātmopalabdhiṃ
prati svatatropi aiyameeṣṭamaiṣṭaṃ ca upalabhate evamaiyameaiveṣṭamaiṣṭaṃ ca saṃpādayiṣyati upalabdhāvapyasvātatryam upalabdhihetūpādāopalambhāditi cet a viṣayaprakalpaāmātraprayojaatvādupalabdhihetūām upalabdhau tu aayāpekṣatvamātmaaḥ caitayayogāt api ca arthakriyāyāmapi
ātyatamātmaaḥ svātatryamasti deśakālaimittaviśeṣāpekṣatvāt a ca sahāyāpekṣasya kartuḥ kartṛtvaṃ ivartate bhavati hyedhodakādyapekṣasyāpi paktuḥ paktṛtvam sahakārivaicitryācca iṣṭāiṣṭārthakriyāyāmaiyamea pravṛttirātmao a virudhyate śaktiviparyayāt itaśca
vijñāavyatirikto jīvaḥ kartā bhavitumarhati yadi puarvijñāaśabdavācyā buddhireva kartrī syāt tataḥ śaktiviparyayaḥ syāt karaṇaśaktirbuddherhīyeta kartṛśaktiścāpadyeta satyāṃ ca buddheḥ kartṛśaktau tasyā eva
ahaṃpratyayaviṣayatvamabhyupagatavyam ahaṃkārapūrvikāyā eva pravṛtteḥ sarvatra darśaāt ahaṃ gacchāmi ahamāgacchāmi ahaṃ bhuñje ahaṃ pibāmi iti ca tasyāśca kartṛśaktiyuktāyāḥ sarvārthakāri karaṇamayatkalpayitavyam śaktopi
hi sa kartā karaṇamupādāya kriyāsu pravartamāo dṛśyate tataśca saṃjñāmātre vivādaḥ syāt a vastubhedaḥ kaścit karaṇavyatiriktasya kartṛtvābhyupagamāt samādhyabhāvāc ca yopy ayam
aupaiṣadātmapratipattiprayojaaḥ samādhir upadiṣṭo vedāteṣu ātmā vā are draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyo matavyo ididhyāsitavyaḥ so veṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ om ity evaṃ dhyāyatha ātmāam
ity evaṃlakṣaṇaḥ sopy asaty ātmaaḥ kartṛtve opapadyeta tasmād apy asya kartṛtvasiddhiḥ yathā ca takṣobhayathā takṣādhikaraṇam evaṃ tāvac chāstrārthavattvādibhir hetubhiḥ kartṛtvaṃ
śārīrasya pradarśitam tat puaḥ svābhāvikaṃ vā syāt upādhiimittaṃ veti cityate tatraitair eva śāstrārthavattvādibhir hetubhiḥ svābhāvikaṃ kartṛtvam apavādahetvabhāvād iti evaṃ prāpte
brūmaḥ a svābhāvikaṃ kartṛtvam ātmaaḥ saṃbhavati airmokṣaprasaṅgāt kartṛtvasvabhāvatve hy ātmao a kartṛtvā irmokṣaḥ saṃbhavati ager ivauṣṇyāt a ca kartṛtvādairmuktasyāsti puruṣārthasiddhiḥ
kartṛtvasya duḥkharūpatvāt au sthitāyām api kartṛtvaśaktau kartṛtvakāryaparihārāt puruṣārthaḥ setsyati tatparihāraś ca imittaparihārāt yathāger dahaaśaktiyuktasyāpi kāṣṭhaviyogād dahaakāryābhāvaḥ tadvat a imittāām api
śaktilakṣaṇea saṃbadhea saṃbaddhāām atyataparihārāsaṃbhāvāt au mokṣasādhaavidhāā mokṣaḥ setsyati a sādhaāyattasya aityatvāt api ca ityaśuddhamuktātmapratipādaāt mokṣasiddhir abhimatā tādṛg ātmapratipādaaṃ ca a
svābhāvike kartṛtvevakalpeta tasmāt upādhidharmādhyāseaivātmaaḥ kartṛtvam a svābhāvikam tathā ca śrutiḥ dhyāyatīva lelāyatīva iti ātmedriyamaoyuktaṃ bhoktety āhur maīṣiṇaḥ iti ca upādhisaṃpṛktasyaivātmao
bhoktṛtvādiviśeṣalābhaṃ darśayati a hi vivekiāṃ parasmād ayo jīvo āma kartā bhoktā vā vidyate āyotosti draṣṭā ityādiśravaṇāt para eva tarhi saṃsārī
kartā bhoktā ca prasajyeta parasmād ayaś cec citimāñ jīvaḥ kartā buddhyādisaṃghātavyatirikto a syāt a avidyāpratyupasthāpitatvāt kartṛtvabhoktṛtvayoḥ tathā ca śāstram yatra
hi dvaitam iva bhavati tad itara itaraṃ paśyati ity avidyāvasthāyāṃ kartṛtvabhoktṛtve darśayitvā vidyāvasthāyāṃ te eva kartṛtvabhoktṛtve ivārayati yatra tv asya
sarvam ātmaivābhūt tat kea kaṃ paśyet iti tathā svapajāgaritayor ātmaa upādhisaṃparkakṛtaṃ śramaṃ śyeasyevākāśe viparipatataḥ śrāvayitvā tadabhāvaṃ suṣuptau prājñeātmaā saṃpariṣvaktasya śrāvayati
tadvā asyaitad āptakāmam ātmakāmam akāmaṃ rūpaṃ śokātaram ity ārabhya eṣāsya paramā gatir eṣāsya paramā saṃpad eṣosya paramo loka eṣosya parama
āadaḥ ity upasaṃhārāt tad etad āhācāryaḥ yathā ca takṣobhayathā iti tvarthe ca ayaṃ caḥ paṭhitaḥ aivaṃ matavyam svābhāvikam evātmaaḥ kartṛtvam
ager ivauṣṇyamiti yathā tu takṣā loke vāsyādikaraṇahastaḥ kartā duḥkhī bhavati sa eva svagṛhaṃ prāpto vimuktavāsyādikaraṇaḥ svastho irvṛto irvyāpāraḥ sukhī bhavati
evam avidyāpratyupasthāpitadvaitasaṃpṛkta ātmā svapajāgaritāvasthayoḥ kartā duḥkhī bhavati saḥ tacchramāpauttaye svam ātmāaṃ paraṃ brahma praviśya vimuktakāryakaraṇasaṃghātokartā sukhī bhavati saṃprasādāvasthāyām tathā muktyavasthāyām
apy avidyādhvātaṃ vidyāpradīpea vidhūya ātmaiva kevalo irvṛttaḥ sukhī bhavati takṣadṛṣṭātaś caitāvatāṃśea draṣṭavyaḥ takṣā hi viśiṣṭeṣu takṣaṇādivyāpāreṣv apekṣyaiva pratiiyatāi karaṇāi vāsyādīi
kartā bhavati svaśarīreṇa tu akartaiva evam ayam ātmā sarvavyāpāreṣv apekṣyaiva maaādīi karaṇāi kartā bhavati svātmaā tu kartaiveti a tu ātmaas
takṣṇa ivāvayavāḥ sati yaiḥ hastādibhir iva vāsyādīi takṣā maaādīi karaṇāy ātmopādadīta yasyed vā yat tūktam śāstrārthavattvādibhir hetubhiḥ svābhāvikam ātmaaḥ kartṛtvam
iti ta a vidhiśāstraṃ tāvad yathāprāptaṃ kartṛtvam upādāya kartavyaviśeṣam upadiśati a kartṛtvam ātmaaḥ pratipādayati a ca svābhāvikam asya kartṛtvam asti
brahmātmatvopadeśāt ity avocāma tasmād avidyākṛtaṃ kartṛtvam upādāya vidhiśāstraṃ pravartiṣyate kartā vijñāātmā puruṣaḥ ity evaṃjātīyakam api śāstram auvādarūpatvād yathāprāptam evāvidyākṛtaṃ kartṛtvam
auvadiṣyati etea vihāropādāe parihṛte tayor apy auvādarūpatvāt au saṃdhye sthāe prasupteṣu karaṇeṣu sve śarīre yathākāmaṃ parivartate iti vihāra upadiśyamāaḥ kevalasyātmaaḥ
kartṛtvam āvahati tathopādāepi tad eṣāṃ prāṇāāṃ vijñāea vijñāam ādāya iti karaṇeṣu karmakaraṇavibhaktī śrūyamāṇe kevalasyātmaaḥ kartṛtvaṃ gamayata iti atrocyate a tāvat
saṃdhye sthāetyatam ātmaaḥ karaṇaviramaṇamasti sadhīḥ svapo bhūtvemaṃ lokamatikrāmati iti tatrāpi dhīsaṃbadhaśravaṇāt tathā ca smarati idriyāṇāmuparame maouparataṃ yadi sevate viṣayāeva tadvidyātsvapadarśaam
iti kāmādayaśca maaso vṛttayaḥ iti śrutiḥ tāśca svape dṛśyate tasmātsamaā eva svapte viharati vihāropi ca tatratyo vāsaāmaya eva a tu
pāramārthikosti tathā ca śrutiḥ ivakārāubaddhameva svapavyāpāraṃ varṇayati uteva strībhiḥ saha modamāo jakṣadutevāpi bhayāi paśya iti laukikā api tathaiva svapaṃ kathayati
ārukṣamiva giriśrṛṅgam adrākṣamiva vaarājimiti tathopādāepi yadyapi karaṇeṣu karmakaraṇavibhaktiirdeśaḥ tathāpi tatsaṃpṛktasyaivātmaaḥ kartṛtvaṃ draṣṭavyam kevale kartṛtvāsaṃbhavasya darśitatvāt bhavati ca lokeekaprakārā vivakṣā yodhā
yudhyate yodhai rājā yudhyata iti api ca asmi upādāe karaṇavyāpāroparamamātraṃ vivakṣyate a svātatryaṃ kasyacit abuddhipūrvakasyāpi svāpe karaṇavyāpāroparam asya dṛṣṭatvāt yas
tvayaṃ vyapadeśo darśitaḥ vijñāaṃ yajñaṃ taute iti sa buddher eva kartṛtvaṃ prāpayati vijñāaśabdasya tatra prasiddhatvāt maoataraṃ pāṭhāc ca tasya śraddhaiva
śiraḥ iti ca vijñāamayasyātmaaḥ śraddhādyavayavatvasaṃkīrtaāt śraddhādīāṃ ca buddhidharmatvaprasiddheḥ vijñāaṃ devāḥ sarve brahma jyeṣṭhamupāsate iti ca vākyaśeṣāt jyeṣṭhatvasya ca prathamajatvasya buddhau
prasiddhatvāt sa eṣa vācaś cittasyottarottarakramo yad yajñaḥ iti ca śrutyatare yajñasya vāgbuddhisādhyatvāvadhāraṇāt a ca buddheḥ śaktiviparyayaḥ karaṇāāṃ kartṛtvābhyupagame bhavati sarvakārakāṇām
eva svasvavyāpāreṣu kartṛtvasyāvaśyaṃbhāvitvāt upalabdhyapekṣaṃ tveṣāṃ karaṇāāṃ karaṇatvam sā cātmaaḥ a ca tasyām apy asya kartṛtvam asti ityopalabdhisvarūpatvāt ahaṃkārapūrvakam api kartṛtvaṃ
opalabdhur bhavitum arhati ahaṃkārasyāpy upalabhyamāatvāt a caivaṃ sati karaṇātarakalpaāprasaṅgaḥ buddheḥ karaṇatvābhyupagamāt samādhyabhāvas tu śāstrārthavattveaiva parihṛtaḥ yathāprāptam eva kartṛtvam upādāya samādhividhāāt
tasmāt kartṛtvam apy ātmaa upādhiimittam eveti sthitam parāttu tacchruteḥ parāyattādhikaraṇam yadidamavidyāvasthāyāmupādhiibadhaaṃ kartṛtvaṃ jīvasyābhihitam tatkimaapekṣyeśvaraṃ bhavati āhosvidīśvarāpekṣamiti bhavati vicāraṇā tatra prāptaṃ
tāvat eśvaramapekṣate jīvaḥ kartṛtva iti kasmāt apekṣāprayojaābhāvāt ayaṃ hi jīvaḥ svayameva rāgadveṣādidoṣaprayuktaḥ kārakātarasāmagrīsaṃpaaḥ kartṛtvamaubhavituṃ śakoti tasya kimīśvaraḥ kariṣyati a ca
loke prasiddharasti kṛṣyādikāsu kriyāsvaaḍuhādivat īśvaroparopekṣitavya iti kleśātmakea ca kartṛtvea jatūsaṃsṛjata īśvarasya airghṛṇyaṃ prasajyeta viṣamaphalaṃ ca eṣāṃ kartṛtvaṃ vidadhato vaiṣamyam au
vaiṣamyaairghṛṇye a sāpekṣatvāt ityuktam satyamuktam sati tu īśvarasya sāpekṣatvasaṃbhave sāpekṣatvaṃ ca īśvarasya saṃbhavati satorjatūāṃ dharmādharmayoḥ tayośca sadbhāvaḥ sati jīvasya kartṛtve
tadeva cetkartṛtvamīśvarāpekṣaṃ syāt kiṃviṣayamīśvarasya sāpekṣatvamucyeta akṛtābhyāgamaścaivaṃ jīvasya prasajyeta tasmātsvata evāsya kartṛtvamiti etāṃ prāptiṃ tuśabdea vyāvartya pratijāīte parāditi avidyāvasthāyāṃ kāryakaraṇasaṃghātāvivekadarśio jīvasyāvidyātimirādhasya
sataḥ parasmādātmaaḥ karmādhyakṣātsarvabhūtādhivāsātsākṣiṇaścetayiturīśvarāttadaujñayā kartṛtvabhoktṛtvalakṣaṇasya saṃsārasya siddhiḥ tadaugrahahetukeaiva ca vijñāea mokṣasiddhirbhavitumarhati kutaḥ tacchruteḥ yadyapi doṣaprayuktaḥ sāmagrīsaṃpaaśca jīvaḥ yadyapi ca loke kṛṣyādiṣu
karmasu eśvarakāraṇatvaṃ prasiddham tathāpi sarvāsveva pravṛttiṣvīśvaro hetukarteti śruteravasīyate tathā hi śrutirbhavati eṣa hyeva sādhu karma kārayati taṃ yamebhyo lokebhya uiīṣate
eṣa hyevāsādhu karma kārayati taṃ yamadho iīṣate iti ya ātmai tiṣṭhaātmāamataro yamayati iti ca evaṃjātīyakā au evamīśvarasya kārayitṛtve sati vaiṣamyaairghṛṇye
syātām akṛtābhyāgamaśca jīvasyeti etyucyata kṛtaprayatāpekṣastu vihitapratiṣiddhāvaiyarthyādibhyaḥ tuśabdaścoditadoṣavyāvartaārthaḥ kṛto yaḥ prayato jīvasya dharmādharmalakṣaṇaḥ tadapekṣa evaiamīśvaraḥ kārayati ataścaite coditā doṣā a prasajyate
jīvakṛtadharmādharmavaiṣamyāpekṣa eva tattatphalāi viṣamaṃ vibhajetparjayavat īśvaro imittatvamātreṇa yathā loke āāvidhāāṃ gucchagulmādīāṃ vrīhiyavādīāṃ ca asādhāraṇebhyaḥ svasvabījebhyo jāyamāāāṃ sādhāraṇaṃ imittaṃ bhavati parjayaḥ
a hi asati parjaye rasapuṣpaphalapalāśādivaiṣamyaṃ teṣāṃ jāyate āpyasatsu svasvabījeṣu evaṃ jīvakṛtaprayatāpekṣa īśvaraḥ teṣāṃ śubhāśubhaṃ vidadhyāditi śliṣyate au kṛtaprayatāpekṣatvameva jīvasya parāyatte
kartṛtve opapadyate aiṣa doṣaḥ parāyattepi hi kartṛtve karotyeva jīvaḥ kurvataṃ hi tamīśvaraḥ kārayati api ca pūrvaprayatamapekṣya idāīṃ kārayati pūrvataraṃ ca
prayatamapekṣya pūrvamakārayaditi aāditvātsaṃsārasyeti aavadyam kathaṃ puaravagamyate kṛtaprayatāpekṣa īśvara iti vihitapratiṣiddhāvaiyarthyādibhyaḥ ityāha evaṃ hi svargakāmo yajeta brāhmaṇo a hatavyaḥ ityevaṃjātīyakasya vihitasya
pratiṣiddhasya ca avaiyarthyaṃ bhavati ayathā tadaarthakaṃ syāt īśvara eva vidhipratiṣedhayoriyujyeta atyataparatatratvājjīvasya tathā vihitakāriṇamapyaarthea saṃsṛjet pratiṣiddhakāriṇamapyarthea tataśca prāmāṇyaṃ vedasyāstamiyāt īśvarasya ca
atyatāapekṣatve laukikasyāpi puruṣakārasya vaiyarthyam tathā deśakālaimittāām pūrvoktadoṣaprasaṅgaśca ityevaṃjātīyakaṃ doṣajātamādigrahaṇea darśayati aṃśo āāvyapadeśādayathā cāpi dāśakitavāditvamadhīyata eke aśādhikaraṇam jīveśvarayorupakāryopakārakabhāva uktaḥ sa ca
saṃbaddhayoreva loke dṛṣṭaḥ yathā svāmibhṛtyayoḥ yathā vā agivisphuliṅgayoḥ tataśca jīveśvarayorapyupakāryopakārakabhāvābhyupagamāt kiṃ svāmibhṛtyavatsaṃbadhaḥ āhosvidagivisphuliṅgavat ityasyāṃ vicikitsāyām aiyamo vā prāpoti athavā svāmibhṛtyaprakāreṣveva
īśitrīśitavyabhāvasya prasiddhatvāttadvidha eva saṃbadha iti prāpoti ato bravīti aṃśa iti jīva īśvarasyāṃśo bhavitumarhati yathāgervisphuliṅgaḥ aṃśa ivāṃśaḥ a hi iravayavasya mukhyoṃśaḥ
saṃbhavati kasmātpuaḥ iravayavatvāt sa eva a bhavati āāvyapadeśāt soveṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ etameva viditvā muirbhavati ya ātmai tiṣṭhaātmāamataro yamayati iti ca
evaṃjātīyako bhedairdeśo āsati bhede yujyate au ca ayaṃ āāvyapadeśaḥ sutarāṃ svāmibhṛtyasārūpye yujyata iti ata āha ayathā cāpīti a ca āāvyapadeśādeva
kevalādaṃśatvapratipattiḥ kiṃ tarhi ayathā cāpi vyapadeśo bhavatyaāātvasya pratipādakaḥ tathā hyeke śākhio dāśakitavādibhāvaṃ brahmaṇa āmaatyātharvaṇikā brahmasūkte brahma dāśā brahma dāsā brahmaiveme
kitavāḥ ityādiā dāśā ya ete kaivartāḥ prasiddhāḥ ye ca amīdāsāḥ svāmiṣvātmāamupakṣapayati ye ca aye kitavā dyūtakṛtaḥ te sarve brahmaiva iti
hīajatūdāharaṇea sarveṣāmeva āmarūpakṛtakāryakaraṇasaṃghātapraviṣṭāāṃ jīvāāṃ brahmatvamāha tathā ayatrāpi brahmaprakriyāyāmevāyamarthaḥ prapañcyate tvaṃ strī tvaṃ pumāasi tvaṃ kumāra uta vā kumārī tvaṃ jīrṇo
daṇḍea vañcasi tvaṃ jāto bhavati viśvatomukhaḥ iti sarvāṇi rūpāṇi vicitya dhīro āmāi kṛtvābhivadayadāste iti ca āyotosti draṣṭā ityādiśrutibhyaśca asyārthasya siddhiḥ
caitayaṃ ca aviśiṣṭaṃ jīveśvarayoḥ yathāgivisphuliṅgayorauṣṇyam ato bhedābhedāvagamābhyāmaṃśatvāvagamaḥ kutaśca aṃśatvāvagamaḥ matravarṇācca matravarṇaścaitamarthamavagamayati tāvāasya mahimā tato jyāyāśca puruṣaḥ pādosya sarvā bhūtāi tripādasyāmṛtaṃ
divi iti atra bhūtaśabdea jīvapradhāāi sthāvarajaṅgamāi irdiśati ahiṃsasarvabhūtāyayatra tīrthebhyaḥ iti prayogāt aṃśaḥ pādo bhāga ityaarthātaram tasmādapyaṃśatvāvagamaḥ kutaśca aṃśatvāvagamaḥ api ca
smaryate īśvaragītāsvapi ca īśvarāṃśatvaṃ jīvasya smaryate mamaivāṃśo jīvaloke jīvabhūtaḥ saātaaḥ iti tasmādapyaṃśatvāvagamaḥ yattūktam svāmibhṛtyādiṣveva īśitrīśitavyabhāvo loke prasiddha iti yadyapyeṣā loke
prasiddhiḥ tathāpi śāstrāttu atra aṃśāṃśitvamīśitrīśitavyabhāvaśca iścīyate iratiśayopādhisaṃpaaśceśvaro ihīopādhisaṃpaāñjīvā praśāstīti a kiṃcidvipratiṣidhyate atrāha au jīvasyeśvarāṃśatvābhyupagame tadīyea saṃsāraduḥkhopabhogeāṃśia īśvarasyāpi duḥkhitvaṃ syāt yathā
loke hastapādādyayatamāṅgatea duḥkhea aṅgio devadattasya duḥkhitvam tadvat tataśca tatprāptāāṃ mahattaraṃ duḥkhaṃ prāpuyāt ato varaṃ pūrvāvasthaḥ saṃsāra evāstu iti samyagdarśaāarthakyaprasaṅgaḥ syāt
iti atrocyate prakāśādiva aivaṃ paraḥ yathā jīvaḥ saṃsāraduḥkhama ubhavati aivaṃ para īśvaroubhavatīti pratijāīmahe jīvo hi avidyāveśavaśāt dehādyātmabhāvam iva gatvā tatkṛtea
duḥkhea duḥkhī aham iti avidyayā kṛtaṃ duḥkhopabhogam abhimayate aivaṃ parameśvarasya dehādyātmabhāvo duḥkhābhimāo vā asti jīvasyāpy avidyākṛtaāmarūpairvṛttadehedriyādyupādhyavivekabhramaimitta eva duḥkhābhimāaḥ a tu
pāramārthiko sti yathā ca svadehagatadāhacchedādiimittaṃ duḥkhaṃ tadabhimāabhrātyāubhavati tathā putramitrādigocaram api duḥkhaṃ tadabhimāabhrātyaivāubhavati aham eva putraḥ aham eva mitram ity evaṃ
sehavaśea putramitrādiṣv abhiiviśamāaḥ tataś ca iścitam etad avagamyate mithyābhimāabhramaimitta eva duḥkhāubhava iti vyatirekadarśaāc ca evam avagamyate tathā hi putramitrādimatsu bahuṣūpaviṣṭeṣu
tatsaṃbadhābhimāiṣv itareṣu ca putro mṛto mitraṃ mṛtam ity evam āghoṣite yeṣām eva putramitrādimattvābhimāas teṣām eva taimittaṃ duḥkham utpadyate a abhimāahīāāṃ
parivrājakādīām ataś ca laukikasyāpi puṃsaḥ samyagdaśaārthavattvaṃ dṛṣṭam kim uta viṣayaśūyād ātmao yadvastvataramapaśyato ityacaitayamātrasvarūpasyeti tasmāāsti samyagdarśaāarthakyaprasaṅgaḥ prakāśādivaditi idarśaopayāsaḥ prakāśaḥ sauraścādramaso vā
viyadvyāpya avatiṣṭhamāaḥ aṅgulyādyupādhisaṃbadhāt teṣu ṛjuvakrādibhāvaṃ pratipadyamāeṣu tattadbhāvamiva pratipadyamāopi a paramārthatastadbhāvaṃ pratipadyate yathā ca ākāśo ghaṭādiṣu gacchatsu gacchaiva vibhāvyamāopi a paramārthato
gacchati yathā ca udaśarāvādikampaāttadgate sūryapratibimbe kampamāepi a tadvāsūryaḥ kampate evamavidyāpratyupasthāpite buddhyādyupahite jīvākhye aṃśe duḥkhāyamāepi a tadvāīśvaro duḥkhāyate jīvasyāpi duḥkhaprāptiravidyāimittaivetyuktam tathā
ca avidyāimittajīvabhāvavyudāsea brahmabhāvameva jīvasya pratipādayati vedātāḥ tattvamasi ityevamādayaḥ tasmāāsti jaivea duḥkhea paramātmao duḥkhitvaprasaṅgaḥ smarati ca smarati ca vyāsādayaḥ yathā jaivea
duḥkhea a paramātmā duḥkhāyata iti tatra yaḥ paramātmā hi sa ityo irguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ a lipyate phalaiścāpi padmapatramivāmbhasā karmātmā tvaparo yosau
mokṣabadhaiḥ sa yujyate sa saptadaśakeāpi rāśiā yujyate puaḥ iti caśabdāt samāmaati ca iti vākyaśeṣaḥ tayorayaḥ pippalaṃ svādvattyaaśaayo abhicākaśīti iti ekastathā
sarvabhūtātarātmā a lipyate lokaduḥkhea bāhyaḥ iti ca atrāha yadi tarhyeka eva sarveṣāṃ bhūtāāmatarātmā syāt kathamaujñāparihārau syātāṃ laukikau vaidikau ceti au
ca aṃśo jīva īśvarasya ityuktam tadbhedāccāujñāparihārau tadāśrayāvavyatikīrṇāvupapadyete kimatra codyata iti ucyate aitadevam aaṃśatvamapi hi jīvasyābhedavādiyaḥ śrutayaḥ pratipādayati tatsṛṣṭvā tadevāuprāviśat āyotosti
draṣṭā mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyumāpoti ya iha āeva paśyati tattvamasi ahaṃ brahmāsmi ityevaṃjātīyakāḥ au bhedābhedāvagamābhyāmaṃśatvaṃ sidhyatītyuktam syādetadevam yadyubhāvapi bhedābhedau pratipipādayiṣitau syātām
abheda eva tvatra pratipipādayiṣitaḥ brahmātmatvapratipattau puruṣārthasiddheḥ svabhāvaprāptastu bhedoūdyate a ca iravayavasya brahmaṇo mukhyoṃśo jīvaḥ saṃbhavatītyuktam tasmātpara evaikaḥ sarveṣāṃ bhūtāāmatarātmā jīvabhāveāvasthita
ityato vaktavyā aujñāparihāropapattiḥ tāṃ brūmaḥ aujñāparihārau dehasambadhājjyotirādivat ṛtau bhāryāmupeyāt ityaujñā gurvaṅgaāṃ opagacchet iti parihāraḥ tathā agīṣomīyaṃ paśuṃ saṃjñapayet ityaujñā a
hiṃsyātsarvā bhūtāi iti parihāraḥ evaṃ lokepi mitram upasevitavyam ity aujñā śatruḥ parihartavya iti parihāraḥ evaṃprakārāv aujñāparihārau ekatve py ātmaaḥ dehasaṃbadhāt
syāt dehaiḥ saṃbadho dehasaṃbadhaḥ kaḥ puardehasaṃbadhaḥ dehādir ayaṃ saṃghāto ham eva ity ātmai viparītapratyayotpattiḥ dṛṣṭā ca sā sarvaprāṇiām ahaṃ gacchāmi
aham āgacchāmi aham adhaḥ aham aadhaḥ ahaṃ mūḍhaḥ aham amūḍhaḥ ityevamātmikā a hi asyāḥ samyagdarśaād aya ivārakam asti prāk tu
samyagdarśaāt pratataiṣā bhrātiḥ sarvajatuṣu tad evam avidyāimittadehādyupādhisaṃbadhakṛtād viśeṣād aikātmyābhyupagame py aujñāparihārāv avakalpete samyagdarśias tarhy aujñāparihārāarthakyaṃ prāptam a tasya kṛtārthatvā iyojyatvāupapatteḥ
heyopādeyayor hi iyojyo iyoktavyaḥ syāt ātmaas tv atiriktaṃ heyam upādeyaṃ vā vastv apaśya kathaṃ iyujyeta a ca ātmā ātmay eva
iyojyaḥ syāt śarīravyatirekadarśia eva iyojyatvam iti cet a tatsaṃhatatvābhimāāt satyaṃ vyatirekadarśio iyojyatvam tathāpi vyomādivaddehādyasaṃhatatvam apaśyata eva ātmao iyojyatvābhimāaḥ a hi
dehādyasaṃhatatvadarśiaḥ kasyacid api iyogo dṛṣṭaḥ kimutaikātmyadarśiaḥ a ca iyogābhāvāt samyagdarśio yatheṣṭaceṣṭāprasaṅgaḥ sarvatrābhimāasyaiva pravartakatvāt abhimāābhāvācca samyagdarśiaḥ tasmāddehasaṃbadhādevāujñāparihārau jyotirādivat yathā jyotiṣa ekatvepyagiḥ
kravyātparihriyate etaraḥ yathā ca prakāśa ekasyāpi savituramedhyadeśasaṃbaddhaḥ parihriyate etaraḥ śucibhūmiṣṭhaḥ tathā bhaumāḥ pradeśā vajravaiḍūryādaya upādīyate bhaumā api sato arakalebarādayaḥ parihriyate
tathā mūtrapurīṣaṃ gavāṃ pavitratayā parigṛhyate tadeva jātyatare parivarjyate tadvat asatateścāvyatikaraḥ syātāṃ āma aujñāparihārāvekasyātmao dehaviśeṣayogāt yastvayaṃ karmaphalasaṃbadhaḥ sa ca aikātmyābhyupagame vyatikīryeta
svāmyekatvāditi cet aitadevam asaṃtateḥ a hi karturbhoktuścātmaaḥ saṃtataḥ sarvaiḥ śarīraiḥ saṃbadhosti upādhitatro hi jīva ityuktam upādhyasaṃtāācca āsti jīvasaṃtāaḥ tataśca karmavyatikaraḥ
phalavyatikaro vā a bhaviṣyati ābhāsa eva ca ābhāsa eva ca eṣa jīvaḥ parasyātmao jalasūryakādivatpratipattavyaḥ a sa eva sākṣāt āpi vastvataram
ataśca yathā aikasmiñjalasūryake kampamāe jalasūryakātaraṃ kampate evaṃ aikasmiñjīve karmaphalasaṃbadhii jīvātarasya tatsaṃbadhaḥ evamavyatikara eva karmaphalayoḥ ābhāsasya ca avidyākṛtatvāttadāśrayasya saṃsārasyāvidyākṛtatvopapattiriti tadvyudāsea ca
pāramārthikasya brahmātmabhāvasyopadeśopapattiḥ yeṣāṃ tu bahava ātmāaḥ te ca sarve sarvagatāḥ teṣāmevaiṣa vyatikaraḥ prāpoti katham bahavo vibhavaścātmāaścaitayamātrasvarūpā irguṇā iratiśayāśca tadarthaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ
pradhāam taimittaiṣāṃ bhogāpavargasiddhiriti sāṃkhyāḥ sati bahutve vibhutve ca ghaṭakuḍyādisamāā dravyamātrasvarūpāḥ svato acetaā ātmāaḥ tadupakaraṇāi ca aṇūi maāṃsy acetaāi tatra ātmadravyāṇāṃ
maodravyāṇāṃ ca saṃyogāt ava icchādayo vaiśeṣikā ātmaguṇā utpadyate te ca avyatirekeṇa pratyekamātmasu samavayati sa saṃsāraḥ teṣāṃ avāāmātmaguṇāāmatyatāutpādo mokṣa iti kāṇādāḥ
tatra sāṃkhyāāṃ tāvaccaitayasvarūpatvātsarvātmaāṃ saṃidhāādyaviśeṣācca ekasya sukhaduḥkhasaṃbadhe sarveṣāṃ sukhaduḥkhasaṃbadhaḥ prāpoti syādetat pradhāapravṛtteḥ puruṣakaivalyārthatvādvyavasthā bhaviṣyati ayathā hi svavibhūtikhyāpaārthā pradhāapravṛttiḥ syāt tathā ca
airmokṣaḥ prasajyeteti aitatsāram a hi abhilaṣitasiddhiibadhaā vyavasthā śakyā vijñātum upapattyā tu kayācidvyavasthocyeta asatyāṃ puarupapattau kāmaṃ mā bhūdabhilaṣitaṃ puruṣakaivalyam prāpoti tu
vyavasthāhetvabhāvādvyatikaraḥ kāṇādāāmapi yadā ekeātmaā maaḥ saṃyujyate tadā ātmātarairapi ātarīyakaḥ saṃyogaḥ syāt saṃidhāādyaviśeṣāt tataśca hetvaviśeṣātphalāviśeṣa ityekasyātmaaḥ sukhaduḥkhayoge sarvātmaāmapi samāaṃ sukhaduḥkhitvaṃ prasajyeta
syādetat adṛṣṭaimitto iyamo bhaviṣyatīti etyāha adṛṣṭāiyamāt bahuṣvātmasvākāśavatsarvagateṣu pratiśarīraṃ bāhyābhyatarāviśeṣeṇa saṃihiteṣu maovākkāyairdharmādharmalakṣaṇamadṛṣṭamupārjyate sāṃkhyāāṃ tāvat tad aātmasamavāyi pradhāavarti pradhāasādhāraṇyā a pratyātmaṃ sukhaduḥkhopabhogasya
iyāmakam upapadyate kāṇādāām api pūrvavat sādhāraṇeātmamaaḥsaṃyogea irvartitasyādṛṣṭasyāpi asyaivātmaa idam adṛṣṭam iti iyame hetvabhāvādeṣa eva doṣaḥ syādetat ahamidaṃ phalaṃ prāpavāi idaṃ
pariharāṇi itthaṃ prayatai itthaṃ karavāṇi ityevaṃvidhā abhisaṃdhyādayaḥ pratyātmaṃ pravartamāā adṛṣṭasyātmaāṃ ca svasvāmibhāvaṃ iyaṃsyatīti etyāha abhisadhyādiṣvapi caivam amisaṃdhyādīāmapi sādhāraṇeaivātmamaaḥsaṃyogea sarvātmasaṃidhau kriyamāṇāāṃ
iyamahetutvāupapatteruktadoṣāuṣaṅga eva pradeśād iti ce ātarbhāvāt athocyeta vibhutve py ātmaaḥ śarīrapratiṣṭhea maasā saṃyogaḥ śarīrāvacchia eva ātmapradeśe bhaviṣyati ataḥ pradeśakṛtā vyavasthā
abhisaṃdhyādīām adṛṣṭasya sukhaduḥkhayoś ca bhaviṣyatīti tad api opapadyate kasmāt atarbhāvāt vibhutvāviśeṣād dhi sarva evātmāaḥ sarvaśarīreṣv atarbhavati tatra a vaiśeṣikaiḥ śarīrāvacchio
py ātmaaḥ pradeśaḥ kalpayituṃ śakyaḥ kalpyamāo py ayaṃ iṣpradeśasyātmaaḥ pradeśaḥ kālpaikatvād eva a pāramārthikaṃ kāryaṃ iyatuṃ śakoti śarīram api sarvātmasaṃidhāv
utpadyamāam asyaiva ātmaaḥ etareṣām iti a iyatuṃ śakyam pradeśaviśeṣābhyupagame pi ca dvayor ātmaoḥ samāasukhaduḥkhabhājoḥ kadācid ekeaiva tāvac charīreṇopabhogasiddhiḥ syāt samāapradeśasyāpi
dvayor ātmaor adṛṣṭasya saṃbhavāt tathā hi devadatto yasmi pradeśe sukhaduḥkham avabhūt tasmāt pradeśād apakrāte taccharīre yajñadattaśarīre ca taṃ pradeśam auprāpte
tasyāpi itareṇa samāaḥ sukhaduḥkhāubhavo dṛśyate sa a syāt yadi devadattayajñadattayoḥ samāapradeśam adṛṣṭaṃ a syāt svargādyaupabhogaprasaṅgaśca pradeśavādiaḥ syāt brāhmaṇādiśarīrapradeśeṣv adṛṣṭaiṣpatteḥ pradeśātaravartitvāc
ca svargādyupabhogasya sarvagatatvāupapattiś ca bahūām ātmaām dṛṣṭātābhāvāt vada tāvat tvam ke bahavaḥ samāadeśāś ceti rūpādaya iti cet a teṣām api
dharmyaṃśeābhedāt lakṣaṇabhedāc ca a tu bahūām ātmaāṃ lakṣaṇabhedo sti atyaviśeṣavaśād bhedopapattir iti cet a bhedakalpaāyā atyaviśeṣakalpaāyāś ca itaretarāśrayatvāt ākāśādīām api
vibhutvaṃ brahmavādio siddham kāryatvābhyupagamāt tasmād ātmaikatvapakṣa eva sarvadoṣābhāva iti siddham iti śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācāryasya śrīgovidabhagavatpūjyapādaśiṣyasya śrīmacchaṃkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīrakamīmāṃsāsūtrabhāṣye dvitīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ murat
dvitīyodhyāyaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ tathā prāṇāḥ prāṇotpattyadhikaraṇam tathā prāṇā iti kathaṃ puaratra tathā ityakṣarāulomyam prakṛtopamāābhāvāt sarvagatātmabahutvavādidūṣaṇam atītāatarapādāte prakṛtam tattāvaopamāaṃ saṃbhavati sādṛśyābhāvāt
sādṛśye hi sati upamāaṃ syāt yathā siṃhas tathā balavarmeti adṛṣṭasāmyapratipādaārthamiti yadyucyeta yathā adṛṣṭasya sarvātmasaṃidhāvutpadyamāasyāiyatatvam evaṃ prāṇāāmapi sarvātmaaḥ pratyaiyatatvamiti tadapi dehāiyameaivoktatvātpuaruktaṃ
bhavet a ca jīvea prāṇā upamīyera siddhātavirodhāt jīvasya hi autpattirākhyātā prāṇāāṃ tu utpattirācikhyāsitā tasmāttathā ityasaṃbaddhamiva pratibhāti a udāharaṇopātteāpyupamāea saṃbadhopapatteḥ atra
prāṇotpattivādivākyajātamudāharaṇam etasmādātmaaḥ sarve prāṇāḥ sarve lokāḥ sarve devāḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāi vyuccarati ityevaṃjātīyakam tatra yathā lokādayaḥ parasmādbrahmaṇa utpadyate tathā prāṇā apītyarthaḥ
tathā etasmājjāyate prāṇo maaḥ sarvedriyāṇi ca khaṃ vāyurjyotirāpaḥ pṛthivī viśvasya dhāriṇī ityevamādiṣvapi khādivatprāṇāāmutpattiriti draṣṭavyam athavā pāavyāpacca tadvat ityevamādiṣu vyavahitopamāasaṃbadhasyāpyāśritatvāt yathā
atītāatarapādādāvuktā viyadādayaḥ parasya brahmaṇo vikārāḥ samadhigatāḥ tathā prāṇā api parasya brahmaṇo vikārā iti yojayitavyam kaḥ puaḥ prāṇāāṃ vikāratve hetuḥ śrutatvameva
au keṣucitpradeśeṣu a prāṇāāmutpattiḥ śrūyata ityuktam tadayuktam pradeśātareṣu śravaṇāt a hi kvacidaśravaṇamayatra śrutaṃ ivārayitumutsahate tasmācchrutatvāviśeṣādākāśādivatprāṇā apyutpadyata iti sūktam gauṇyasambhavāt yatpuaruktaṃ
prāgutpatteḥ sadbhāvaśravaṇādgauṇī prāṇāāmutpattiśrutiriti tatpratyāha gauṇyasaṃbhavāditi gauṇyā asaṃbhavo gauṇyasaṃbhavaḥ a hi prāṇāāmutpattiśrutirgauṇī saṃbhavati pratijñāhāiprasaṅgāt kasmiu bhagavo vijñāte sarvamidaṃ vijñātaṃ bhavati iti
hi ekavijñāea sarvavijñāaṃ pratijñāya tatsādhaāyedamāmāyate etasmājjāyate prāṇaḥ ityādi sā ca pratijñā prāṇādeḥ samastasya jagato brahmavikāratve sati prakṛtivyatirekeṇa vikārābhāvātsidhyati gauṇyāṃ tu
prāṇāāmutpattiśrutau pratijñā iyaṃ hīyeta tathā ca pratijñātārthamupasaṃharati puruṣa evedaṃ viśvaṃ karma tapo brahma parāmṛtam iti brahmaivedaṃ viśvamidaṃ variṣṭham iti ca
tathā ātmao vā are darśaea śravaṇea matyā vijñāeedaṃ sarvaṃ viditam ityevaṃjātīyakāsu śrutiṣu eṣaiva pratijñā yojayitavyā kathaṃ puaḥ prāgutpatteḥ prāṇāāṃ sadbhāvaśravaṇam
aitamūlaprakṛtiviṣayam aprāṇo hyamaāḥ śubhro hyakṣarātparataḥ paraḥ iti mūlaprakṛteḥ prāṇādisamastaviśeṣarahitatvāvadhāraṇāt avātaraprakṛtiviṣayaṃ tvetat svavikārāpekṣaṃ prāgutpatteḥ prāṇāāṃ sadbhāvāvadhāraṇamiti draṣṭavyam vyākṛtaviṣayāṇāmapi bhūyasīāmavasthāāṃ śrutismṛtyoḥ prakṛtivikārabhāvaprasiddheḥ
viyadadhikaraṇe hi gauṇyasaṃbhavāt iti pūrvapakṣasūtratvāt gauṇījamaśrutiḥ asaṃbhavāt iti vyākhyātam pratijñāhāyā ca tatra siddhātobhihitaḥ iha tu siddhātasūtratvāt gauṇyā jamaśruterasaṃbhavāt iti vyākhyātam
tadaurodhea tu ihāpi gauṇī jamaśrutiḥ asaṃbhavāt iti vyācakṣāṇaiḥ pratijñāhāirupekṣitā syāt tatprākśruteśca itaśca ākāśādīāmiva prāṇāāmapi mukhyaiva jamaśrutiḥ yat jāyate ityekaṃ jamavācipadaṃ
prāṇeṣu prākśrutaṃ sat uttareṣvākāśādiṣvauvartate etasmājjāyate prāṇaḥ ityatra ākāśādiṣu mukhyaṃ jameti pratiṣṭhāpitam tatsāmāyātprāṇeṣvapi mukhyameva jama bhavitumarhati a hi ekasmiprakaraṇe ekasmiṃśca vākye
ekaḥ śabdaḥ sakṛduccarito bahubhiḥ saṃbadhyamāaḥ kvacimukhyaḥ kvacidgauṇa ityadhyavasātuṃ śakyam vairūpyaprasaṅgāt tathā sa prāṇamasṛjata prāṇācchraddhām ityatrāpi prāṇeṣu śrutaḥ sṛjatiḥ pareṣvapyutpattimatsu śraddhādiṣvauṣajyate
yatrāpi paścācchruta utpattivacaaḥ śabdaḥ pūrvaiḥ saṃbadhyate tatrāpyeṣa eva yāyaḥ yathā sarvāṇi bhūtāi vyuccarati ityayamate paṭhito vyuccaratiśabdaḥ pūrvairapi prāṇādibhiḥ saṃbadhyate tatpūrvakatvādvācaḥ
yadyapi tattejosṛjata ityetasmiprakaraṇe prāṇāāmutpattira paṭhyate tejobaāāmeva trayāṇāṃ bhūtāāmutpattiśravaṇāt tathāpi brahmaprakṛtikatejobaapūrvakatvābhidhāādvākprāṇamaasām tatsāmāyācca sarveṣāmeva prāṇāāṃ brahmaprabhavatvaṃ siddhaṃ bhavati tathā hi asmieva prakaraṇe
tejobaapūrvakatvaṃ vākprāṇamaasāmāmāyate aamayaṃ hi somya maa āpomayaḥ prāṇastejomayī vāk iti tatra yadi tāvamukhyamevaiṣāmaādimayatvam tato vartata eva brahmaprabhavatvam atha bhāktam tathāpi
brahmakartṛkāyāṃ āmarūpavyākriyāyāṃ śravaṇāt yeāśrutaṃ śrutaṃ bhavati iti copakramāt aitadātmyamidaṃ sarvam iti copasaṃhārāt śrutyataraprasiddheśca brahmakāryatvaprapañcaārthameva maaādīāmaādimayatvavacaamiti gamyate tasmādapi prāṇāāṃ brahmavikāratvasiddhiḥ sapta
gaterviśeṣitatvācca saptagatyadhikaraṇam utpattiviṣayaḥ śrutivipratiṣedhaḥ prāṇāāṃ parihṛtaḥ saṃkhyāviṣaya idāīṃ parihriyate tatra mukhyaṃ prāṇamupariṣṭādvakṣyati saṃprati tu kati itare prāṇā iti saṃpradhārayati śrutivipratipatteścātra
viśayaḥ kvacitsapta prāṇāḥ saṃkīrtyate sapta prāṇāḥ prabhavati tasmāt iti kvacidaṣṭau prāṇā grahatvea guṇea saṃkīrtyate aṣṭau grahā aṣṭāvatigrahāḥ iti kvaciava sapta
vai śīrṣaṇyāḥ prāṇā dvāvavāñcau iti kvaciddaśa ava vai puruṣe prāṇā ābhirdaśamī iti kvacidekādaśa daśeme puruṣe prāṇā ātmaikādaśaḥ iti kvaciddvādaśa sarveṣāṃ
sparśāāṃ tvagekāyaam ityatra kvacittrayodaśa cakṣuśca draṣṭavyaṃ ca ityatra evaṃ hi vipratipaāḥ prāṇeyattāṃ prati śrutayaḥ kiṃ tāvatprāptam saptaiva prāṇā iti kutaḥ
gateḥ yatastāvatovagamyate sapta prāṇāḥ prabhavati tasmāt ityevaṃvidhāsu śrutiṣu viśeṣitāścaite sapta vai śīrṣaṇyāḥ prāṇāḥ ityatra au prāṇā guhāśayā ihitāḥ sapta sapta
iti vīpsā śrūyate sā saptabhyotiriktāprāṇāgamayatīti aiṣa doṣaḥ puruṣabhedābhiprāyeyaṃ vīpsā pratipuruṣaṃ sapta sapta prāṇā iti a tattvabhedābhiprāyā sapta sapta ayeye prāṇā
iti avaṣṭatvādikāpi saṃkhyā prāṇeṣu udāhṛtā kathaṃ saptaiva syuḥ satyamudāhṛtā virodhāttvayatamā saṃkhyā adhyavasātavyā tatra stokakalpaāurodhātsaptasaṃkhyādhyavasāam vṛttibhedāpekṣaṃ ca saṃkhyātaraśravaṇamiti mayate atrocyate hastādayastu
sthiteto aivam hastādayastvapare saptabhyotiriktāḥ prāṇāḥ śrūyate hasto vai grahaḥ sa karmaṇātigraheṇa gṛhīto hastābhyāṃ hi karma karoti ityevamādyāsu śrutiṣu sthite ca
saptatvātireke saptatvamatarbhāvācchakyate saṃbhāvayitum hīādhikasaṃkhyāvipratipattau hi adhikā saṃkhyā saṃgrāhyā bhavati tasyāṃ hīā atarbhavati a tu hīāyāmadhikā ataśca aivaṃ matavyam stokakalpaāurodhātsaptaiva prāṇāḥ
syuriti uttarasaṃkhyāurodhāttu ekādaśaiva te prāṇāḥ syuḥ tathā ca udāhṛtā śrutiḥ daśeme puruṣe prāṇā ātmaikādaśaḥ iti ātmaśabdea ca atra ataḥkaraṇaṃ parigṛhyate
karaṇādhikārāt avekādaśatvādapyadhike dvādaśatrayodaśatve udāhṛte satyamudāhṛte a tvekādaśabhyaḥ kāryajātebhyodhikaṃ kāryajātamasti yadarthamadhikaṃ karaṇaṃ kalpyeta śabdasparśarūparasagadhaviṣayāḥ pañca buddhibhedāḥ tadarthāi pañca buddhīdriyāṇi vacaādāaviharaṇotsargāadāḥ pañca
karmabhedāḥ tadarthāi ca pañca karmedriyāṇi sarvārthaviṣayaṃ traikālyavṛtti maastu ekam aekavṛttikam tadeva vṛttibhedāt kvacidbhiavadvyapadiśyate mao buddhirahaṃkāraścittaṃ ca iti tathā ca śrutiḥ
kāmādyā āāvidhā vṛttīraukramyāha etatsarvaṃ maa eva iti api ca saptaiva śīrṣaṇyāprāṇāabhimayamāasya catvāra eva prāṇā abhimatāḥ syuḥ sthāabhedāddhyete catvāraḥ sataḥ sapta
gaṇyate dve śrotre dve cakṣuṣī dve āsike ekā vāk iti a ca tāvatāmeva vṛttibhedā itare prāṇā iti śakyate vaktum hastādivṛttīāmatyatavijātīyatvāt
tathā ava vai puruṣe prāṇā ābhirdaśamī ityatrāpi dehacchidrabhedābhiprāyeṇaiva daśa prāṇā ucyate a prāṇatattvabhedābhiprāyeṇa ābhirdaśamī iti vacaāt a hi ābhirāma kaścitprāṇaḥ
prasiddhosti mukhyasya tu prāṇasya bhavati ābhirapyekaṃ viśeṣāyataamiti ato ābhirdaśamī ityucyate kvacidupāsaārthaṃ katicitprāṇā gaṇyate kvacitpradarśaārtham tadevaṃ vicitre prāṇeyattāmāe sati kva kiṃ
param āmāamiti vivektavyam kāryajātavaśāttvekādaśatvāmāaṃ prāṇaviṣayaṃ pramāṇamiti sthitam iyamaparā sūtradvayayojaā saptaiva prāṇāḥ syuḥ yataḥ saptāāmeva gatiḥ śrūyate tamutkrāmataṃ prāṇoūtkrāmati prāṇamaūtkrāmataṃ sarve
prāṇā aūtkrāmati ityatra au sarvaśabdotra paṭhyate tatkathaṃ saptāāmeva gatiḥ pratijñāyata iti viśeṣitatvādityāha saptaiva hi prāṇāścakṣurādayastvakparyatā viśeṣitā iha prakṛtāḥ sa yatraiva
cākṣuṣaḥ puruṣaḥ parāṅparyāvartatethārūpajño bhavati ekībhavati a paśyatītyāhuḥ ityevamādiā aukramaṇea prakṛtagāmī ca sarvaśabdo bhavati yathā sarve brāhmaṇā bhojayitavyā iti ye imatritāḥ
prakṛtā brāhmaṇāsta eva sarvaśabdeocyate āye evamihāpi ye prakṛtāḥ sapta prāṇāsta eva sarvaśabdeocyate āya iti avatra vijñāamaṣṭamamaukrātam kathaṃ saptāāmevāukramaṇam aiṣa doṣaḥ
maovijñāayostattvābhedādvṛttibhedepi saptatvopapatteḥ tasmātsaptaiva prāṇā iti evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ hastādayastvapare saptabhyotiriktāḥ prāṇāḥ pratīyate hasto vai grahaḥ ityādiśrutiṣu grahatvaṃ ca badhaabhāvaḥ gṛhyate
badhyate kṣetrajñaḥ aea grahasaṃjñakea badhaeeti sa ca kṣetrajño aikasmieva śarīre badhyate śarīrātareṣvapi tulyatvādbadhaasya tasmāccharīrātarasaṃcāri idaṃ grahasaṃjñakaṃ badhaam ityarthāduktaṃ bhavati tathā
ca smṛtiḥ puryaṣṭakea liṅgea prāṇādyea sa yujyate tea baddhasya vai badho mokṣo muktasya tea ca iti prāṅmokṣāt grahasaṃjñakea badhaea aviyogaṃ
darśayati ātharvaṇe ca viṣayedriyāukramaṇe cakṣuśca draṣṭavyaṃ ca ityatra tulyavaddhastādīīdriyāṇi saviṣayāṇyaukrāmati hastau cādātavyaṃ copasthaścāadayitavyaṃ ca pāyuśca visarjayitavyaṃ ca pādau ca gatavyaṃ
ca iti tathā daśeme puruṣe prāṇā ātmaikādaśaste yadāsmāccharīrāmartyādutkrāmatyatha rodayati ityekādaśāāṃ prāṇāāmutkrātiṃ darśayati sarvaśabdopi ca prāṇaśabdea saṃbadhyamāośeṣāprāṇāabhidadhāo a prakaraṇavaśea saptasvevāvasthāpayituṃ śakyate
prakaraṇācchabdasya balīyastvāt sarve brāhmaṇā bhojayitavyāḥ ityatrāpi sarveṣāmeva avaivartiāṃ brāhmaṇāāṃ grahaṇaṃ yāyyam sarvaśabdasāmarthyāt sarvabhojaāsaṃbhavāttu tatra imatritamātraviṣayā sarvaśabdasya vṛttirāśritā iha tu a
kiṃcitsarvaśabdārthasaṃkocae kāraṇamasti tasmātsarvaśabdea atra aśeṣāṇāṃ prāṇāāṃ parigrahaḥ pradarśaārthaṃ ca saptāāmaukramaṇamityaavadyam tasmādekādaśaiva prāṇāḥ śabdataḥ kāryataśceti siddham aṇavaśca prāṇāṇutvādhikaraṇam adhuā prāṇāāmeva svabhāvātaramabhyuccioti
aṇavaścaite prakṛtāḥ prāṇāḥ pratipattavyāḥ aṇutvaṃ caiṣāṃ saukṣmyaparicchedau a paramāṇutulyatvam kṛtsadehavyāpikāryāupapattiprasaṅgāt sūkṣmā ete prāṇāḥ sthūlāścetsyuḥ maraṇakāle śarīrāirgacchataḥ bilādahiriva upalabhyera mriyamāṇasya pārśvasthaiḥ
paricchiāścaite prāṇāḥ sarvagatāścetsyuḥ utkrātigatyāgatiśrutivyākopaḥ syāt tadguṇasāratvaṃ ca jīvasya a sidhyet sarvagatāāmapi vṛttilābhaḥ śarīradeśe syāditi cet a vṛttimātrasya karaṇatvopapatteḥ yadeva hi
upalabdhisādhaam vṛttiḥ ayadvā tasyaiva aḥ karaṇatvam saṃjñāmātre vivādaḥ iti karaṇāāṃ vyāpitvakalpaā irarthikā tasmātsūkṣmāḥ paricchiāśca prāṇā ityadhyavasyāmaḥ śreṣṭhaśca prāṇaśraiṣṭhyādhikaraṇam mukhyaśca prāṇa
itaraprāṇavadbrahmavikāraḥ ityatidiśati tacca aviśeṣeṇaiva sarvaprāṇāāṃ brahmavikāratvam ākhyātam etasmājjāyate prāṇo maaḥ sarvedriyāṇi ca iti sedriyamaovyatirekeṇa prāṇasyotpattiśravaṇāt sa prāṇamasṛjata ityādiśravaṇebhyaśca kimarthaḥ puaratideśaḥ
adhikāśaṅkāvāraṇārthaḥ āsadāsīye hi brahmapradhāe sūkte matravarṇo bhavati a mṛtyurāsīdamṛtaṃ a tarhi a rātryā aha āsītpraketaḥ āīdavātaṃ svadhayā tadekaṃ tasmāddhāyaaparaḥ kiṃcaāsa
iti āīt iti prāṇakarmopādāāt prāgutpatteḥ satamiva prāṇaṃ sūcayati tasmādajaḥ prāṇa iti jāyate kasyacimatiḥ tāmatideśeāpaudati āīcchabdopi a prāgutpatteḥ prāṇasadbhāvaṃ sūcayati avātam
iti viśeṣaṇāt aprāṇo hyamaāḥ śubhraḥ iti ca mūlaprakṛteḥ prāṇādisamastaviśeṣarahitatvasya darśitatvāt tasmātkāraṇasadbhāvapradarśaārtha evāyam āīcchabda iti śreṣṭhaḥ iti ca mukhyaṃ prāṇamabhidadhāti prāṇo
vāva jyeṣṭhaśca śreṣṭhaśca iti śrutiirdeśāt jyeṣṭhaśca prāṇaḥ śukraiṣekakālādārabhya tasya vṛttilābhāt a cettasya tadāīṃ vṛttilābhaḥ syāt yoau iṣiktaṃ śukraṃ pūyeta a
saṃbhavedvā śrotrādīāṃ tu karṇaśaṣkulyādisthāavibhāgaiṣpattau vṛttilābhāa jyeṣṭhatvam śreṣṭhaśca prāṇaḥ guṇādhikyāt a vai śakṣyāmastvadṛte jīvitum iti śruteḥ a vāyukriye pṛthagupadeśāt vāyukriyādhikaraṇam sa
puarmukhyaḥ prāṇaḥ kiṃsvarūpa iti idāīṃ jijñāsyate tatra prāptaṃ tāvat śruteḥ vāyuḥ prāṇa iti evaṃ hi śrūyate yaḥ prāṇaḥ sa vāyuḥ
sa eṣa vāyuḥ pañcavidhaḥ prāṇopāo vyāa udāaḥ samāaḥ iti athavā tatrātarīyābhiprāyāt samastakaraṇavṛttiḥ prāṇa iti prāptam evaṃ hi tatrātarīyā ācakṣate sāmāyā
karaṇavṛttiḥ prāṇādyā vāyavaḥ pañceti atrocyate a vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ āpi karaṇavyāpāraḥ kutaḥ pṛthagupadeśāt vāyostāvat prāṇasya pṛthagupadeśo bhavati prāṇa eva brahmaṇaścaturthaḥ pādaḥ
sa vāyuā jyotiṣā bhāti ca tapati ca iti a hi vāyureva sa vāyoḥ pṛthagupadiśyeta tathā karaṇavṛtterapi pṛthagupadeśo bhavati vāgādīi karaṇāyaukramya
tatra tatra pṛthakprāṇasyāukramaṇāt vṛttivṛttimatorabhedāt a hi karaṇavyāpāra eva sa karaṇebhyaḥ pṛthagupadiśyeta tathā etasmājjāyate prāṇo maaḥ sarvedriyāṇi ca khaṃ vāyuḥ ityevamādayopi
vāyoḥ karaṇebhyaśca prāṇasya pṛthagupadeśā ausartavyāḥ a ca samastāāṃ karaṇāāmekā vṛttiḥ saṃbhavati pratyekamekaikavṛttitvāt samudāyasya ca akārakatvāt au pañjaracālaayāyea etadbhaviṣyati yathā ekapañjaravartia
ekādaśapakṣiṇaḥ pratyekaṃ pratiiyatavyāpārāḥ sataḥ saṃbhūya ekaṃ pañjaraṃ cālayati evamekaśarīravartia ekādaśaprāṇāḥ pratyekaṃ pratiiyatavṛttayaḥ sataḥ saṃbhūya ekāṃ prāṇākhyāṃ vṛttiṃ pratilapsyata iti etyucyate
yuktaṃ tatra pratyekavṛttibhiravātaravyāpāraiḥ pañjaracālaāurūpairevopetāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ saṃbhūya ekaṃ pañjaraṃ cālayeyuriti tathā dṛṣṭatvāt iha tu śravaṇādyavātaravyāpāropetāḥ prāṇā a saṃbhūya prāṇyuriti yuktam pramāṇābhāvāt
atyatavijātīyatvācca śravaṇādibhyaḥ prāṇaasya tathā prāṇasya śreṣṭhatvādyuddhoṣaṇam guṇabhāvopagamaśca taṃ prati vāgādīām a karaṇavṛttimātre prāṇevakalpate tasmādayo vāyukriyābhyāṃ prāṇaḥ kathaṃ tarhīyaṃ śrutiḥ yaḥ
prāṇaḥ sa vāyuḥ iti ucyate vāyurevāyam adhyātmamāpaaḥ pañcavyūho viśeṣātmaāvatiṣṭhamāaḥ prāṇo āma bhaṇyate a tattvātaram āpi vāyumātram ataścobhe api bhedābhedaśrutī a
virudhyete syādetat prāṇopi tarhi jīvavat asmi śarīre svātatryaṃ prāpoti śreṣṭhatvāt guṇabhāvopagamācca taṃ prati vāgādīāmidriyāṇām tathā hi aekavidhā vibhūtiḥ prāṇasya śrāvyate
supteṣu vāgādiṣu prāṇa evaiko jāgarti prāṇa evaiko mṛtyuā aāptaḥ prāṇaḥ saṃvargo vāgādī saṃvṛṅkte prāṇa itarāprāṇārakṣati māteva putrā iti tasmātprāṇasyāpi jīvavat
svātatryaprasaṅgaḥ taṃ pariharati cakṣurādivattu tatsahaśiṣṭyādibhyaḥ tuśabdaḥ prāṇasya jīvavat svātatryaṃ vyāvartayati yathā cakṣurādīi rājaprakṛtivat jīvasya kartṛtvaṃ bhoktṛtvaṃ ca prati upakaraṇāi a
svatatrāṇi tathā mukhyopi prāṇaḥ rājamatrivat jīvasya sarvārthakaratvea upakaraṇabhūtaḥ a svatatraḥ kutaḥ tatsahaśiṣṭyādibhyaḥ taiścakṣurādibhiḥ sahaiva prāṇaḥ śiṣyate prāṇasaṃvādādiṣu samāadharmaṇāṃ ca saha
śāsaaṃ yuktaṃ bṛhadrathaṃtarādivat ādiśabdea saṃhatatvācetaatvādī prāṇasya svātatryairākaraṇahetū darśayati syādetat yadi cakṣurādivat prāṇasya jīvaṃ prati karaṇabhāvobhyupagamyeta viṣayātaraṃ rūpādivat prasajyeta rūpālocaādibhirvṛttibhiryathāsvaṃ cakṣurādīāṃ
jīvaṃ prati karaṇabhāvo bhavati api ca ekādaśaiva kāryajātāi rūpālocaādīi parigaṇitāi yadarthamekādaśa prāṇāḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ a tu dvādaśamaparaṃ kāryajātamavagamyate yadarthamayaṃ dvādaśaḥ prāṇaḥ
pratijñāyata iti ata uttaraṃ paṭhati akaraṇatvācca a doṣastathāhi darśayati a tāvadviṣayātaraprasaṅgo doṣaḥ akaraṇatvātprāṇasya a hi cakṣurādivat prāṇasya viṣayaparicchedea karaṇatvamabhyupagamyate a
ca asya etāvatā kāryābhāva eva kasmāt tathā hi śrutiḥ prāṇātareṣvasaṃbhāvyamāaṃ mukhyaprāṇasya vaiśeṣikaṃ kāryaṃ darśayati prāṇasaṃvādādiṣu atha ha prāṇā ahaṃ śreyasi
vyūdire ityupakramya yasmiva utkrāte śarīraṃ pāpiṣṭhataramiva dṛśyeta sa vaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ iti ca upayasya pratyekaṃ vāgādyutkramaṇea tadvṛttimātrahīaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ jīvaaṃ darśayitvā prāṇoccikramiṣāyāṃ
vāgādiśaithilyāpattiṃ śarīrapātaprasaṅgaṃ ca darśayatī śrutiḥ prāṇaimittāṃ śarīredriyasthitiṃ darśayati tāvariṣṭhaḥ prāṇa uvāca mā mohamāpadyathāhamevaitatpañcadhātmāaṃ pravibhajyaitadbāṇamavaṣṭabhya vidhārayāmi iti ca etamevārthaṃ śrutirāha prāṇea
rakṣaavaraṃ kulāyam iti ca supteṣu cakṣurādiṣu prāṇaimittāṃ śarīrarakṣāṃ darśayati yasmātkasmāccāṅgātprāṇa utkrāmati tadeva tacchuṣyati iti tea yadaśāti yatpibati teetarāprāṇāavati iti ca
prāṇaimittāṃ śarīredriyapuṣṭiṃ darśayati kasmivahamutkrāta utkrāto bhaviṣyāmi kasmivā pratiṣṭhite pratiṣṭhāsyāmi iti sa prāṇamasṛjata iti ca prāṇaimitte jīvasyotkrātipratiṣṭhe darśayati pañcavṛttirmaovadvyapadiśyate itaścāsti mukhyasya
prāṇasya vaiśeṣikaṃ kāryam yatkāraṇaṃ pañcavṛttirayaṃ vyapadiśyate śrutiṣu prāṇopāo vyāa udāaḥ samāaḥ iti vṛttibhedaścāyaṃ kāryabhedāpekṣaḥ prāṇaḥ prāgvṛttiḥ ucchvāsādikarmā apāaḥ avāgvṛttiriśvāsādikarmā vyāaḥ
tayoḥ saṃdhau vartamāo vīryavatkarmahetuḥ udāaḥ ūrdhvavṛttirutkrātyādihetuḥ samāaḥ samaṃ sarveṣvaṅgeṣu yoarasāayati ityevaṃ pañcavṛttiḥ prāṇaḥ maovat yathā maasaḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ evaṃ prāṇasyāpītyarthaḥ
śrotrādiimittāḥ śabdādiviṣayā maasaḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ prasiddhāḥ a tu kāmaḥ saṃkalpaḥ bṛ u ityādyāḥ paripaṭhitā gṛhyera pañcasaṃkhyātirekāt avatrāpi śrotrādiirapekṣā bhūtabhaviṣyadādiviṣayā aparā
maaso vṛttirastīti samāaḥ pañcasaṃkhyātirekaḥ evaṃ tarhi paramatamapratiṣiddhamaumataṃ bhavati iti yāyāt ihāpi yogaśāstraprasiddhā maasaḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ parigṛhyate pramāṇaviparyayavikalpaidrāsmṛtayaḥ āma bahuvṛttitvamātreṇa vā
maaḥ prāṇasya idarśaam iti draṣṭavyam jīvopakaraṇatvam api prāṇasya pañcavṛttitvāt maovat iti vā yojayitavyam aṇuśca śreṣṭhāṇutvādhikaraṇam aṇuścāyaṃ mukhyaḥ prāṇaḥ pratyetavyaḥ itaraprāṇavat
aṇutvaṃ ca ihāpi saukṣmyaparicchedau a paramāṇutulyatvam pañcabhirvṛttibhiḥ kṛtsaśarīravyāpitvāt sūkṣmaḥ prāṇaḥ utkrātau pārśvasthea aupalabhyamāatvāt paricchiaśca utkrātigatyāgatiśrutibhyaḥ au vibhutvamapi prāṇasya samāmāyate samaḥ
pluṣiṇā samo maśakea samo āgea sama ebhistribhirlokaiḥ samoea sarveṇa ityevamādiṣu pradeśeṣu taducyate ādhidaivikea samaṣṭivyaṣṭirūpeṇa hairaṇyagarbheṇa prāṇātmaaiva etadvibhutvamāmāyate a ādhyātmikea api
ca samaḥ pluṣiṇā ityādiā sāmyavacaea pratiprāṇivartiaḥ prāṇasya pariccheda eva pradarśyate tasmādadoṣaḥ jyotirādyadhiṣṭhāaṃ tu tadāmaaāt jyotirādyadhikaraṇam te puaḥ prakṛtāḥ prāṇāḥ kiṃ
svamahimaiva svasmai svasmai kāryāya prabhavati āhosviddevatādhiṣṭhitāḥ prabhavati iti vicāryate tatra prāptaṃ tāvat yathāsvaṃ kāryaśaktiyogāt svamahimaiva prāṇāḥ pravarteraiti api ca devatādhiṣṭhitāāṃ
prāṇāāṃ pravṛttāvabhyugamyamāāyāṃ tāsāmevādhiṣṭhātrīṇāṃ devatāāṃ bhoktṛtvaprasaṅgāt śārīrasya bhoktṛtvaṃ pralīyeta ataḥ svamahimaiva eṣāṃ pravṛttiriti evaṃ prāpte idamucyate jyotirādyadhiṣṭhāaṃ tu iti tuśabdea pūrvapakṣo
vyāvartyate jyotirādibhiragyādyabhimāiībhirdevatābhiradhiṣṭhitaṃ vāgādikaraṇajātaṃ svakāryeṣu pravartata iti pratijāīte hetuṃ ca vyācaṣṭhe tadāmaaāditi tathā hi āmaati agirvāgbhūtvā mukhaṃ prāviśat ityādi ageścāyaṃ vāgbhāvo
mukhapraveśaśca devatātmaā adhiṣṭhātṛtvamaṅgīkṛtya ucyate a hi devatāsaṃbadhaṃ pratyākhyāya ageḥ vāci mukhe vā kaścidviśeṣasaṃbadho dṛśyate tathā vāyuḥ prāṇo bhūtvā āsike prāviśat
ityevamādyapi yojayitavyam tathā ayatrāpi vāgeva brahmaṇaścaturthaḥ pādaḥ sogiā jyotiṣā bhāti ca tapati ca ityevamādiā vāgādīām agyādijyotiṣṭvādivacaea etamevārthaṃ draḍhayati sa vai
