ca dehātarapratipattau gatiḥ śrāvyate tamutkrāmataṃ prāṇoūtkrāmati prāṇamaūtkrāmataṃ sarve prāṇā aūtkrāmati ityādiśrutibhiḥ sā ca prāṇāāṃ gatirāśrayamatareṇa saṃbhavatītyataḥ prāṇagatiprayuktā tadāśrayabhūtāāmapāmapi bhūtātaropasṛṣṭāāṃ gatirarthādavagamyate
a hi irāśrayāḥ prāṇāḥ kvacidgacchati tiṣṭhati vā jīvato darśaāt aṃgyādigatiśruteriti cea bhāktatvāt syādetat aiva prāṇā dehātarapratipattau saha jīvea gacchati agyādigatiśruteḥ
tathā hi śrutiḥ maraṇakāle vāgādayaḥ prāṇā agyādīdevāgacchatīti darśayati yatrāsya puruṣasya mṛtasyāgiṃ vāgapyeti vātaṃ prāṇaḥ ityādiā iti cet a bhāktatvāt vāgādīāmagyādigatiśrutirgauṇī
lomasu keśeṣu ca adarśaāt oṣadhīrlomāi vaaspatīkeśāḥ iti hi tatrāmāyate a hi lomāi keśāścotplutya oṣadhīrvaaspatīṃśca gacchatīti saṃbhavati a ca jīvasya prāṇopādhipratyākhyāe
gamaamavakalpate āpi prāṇairviā dehātare upabhoga upapadyate vispaṣṭaṃ ca prāṇāāṃ saha jīvea gamaamayatra śrāvitam ato vāgādyadhiṣṭhātrīṇāmagyādidevatāāṃ vāgādyupakāriṇīāṃ maraṇakāle upakāraivṛttimātramapekṣya vāgādayogyādīgacchatītyupacaryate prathameśravaṇāditi
cea tā eva hyupapatteḥ syādetat kathaṃ puaḥpañcamyāmāhutāvāpaḥ puruṣavacaso bhavati ityetat irdhārayituṃ pāryate yāvatā aiva prathamegāvapāṃ śravaṇamasti iha hi dyulokaprabhṛtayaḥ pañcāgyaḥ
pañcāāmāhutīāmādhāratveādhītāḥ teṣāṃ ca pramukheasau vāva loko gautamāgiḥ ityupayasyatasmietasmiagau devāḥ śraddhāṃ juhvati iti śraddhā homyadravyatvea āveditā a tatra āpo homyadravyatayā śrutāḥ
yadi āma parjayādiṣūttareṣu caturṣvagiṣvapāṃ homyadravyatā parikalpyeta parikalpyatāṃ āma teṣu hotavyatayopāttāāṃ somādīāmabbahulatvopapatteḥ prathame tvagau śrutāṃ śraddhāṃ parityajya aśrutā āpaḥ parikalpyata iti
sāhasametat śraddhā ca āma pratyayaviśeṣaḥ prasiddhisāmarthyāt tasmādayuktaḥ pañcamyāmāhutāvapāṃ puruṣabhāva iti cet aiṣa doṣaḥ hi yataḥ tatrāpi prathamegau tā evāpaḥ śraddhāśabdeābhipreyate
kutaḥ upapatteḥ evaṃ hyādimadhyāvasāasaṃgāāt aākulametadekavākyamupapadyate itarathā puaḥ pañcamyāmāhutau apāṃ puruṣavacastvaprakāre pṛṣṭe prativacaāvasare prathamāhutisthāe yadyaapo homyadravyaṃ śraddhāṃ āmāvatārayet tataḥ ayathā praśoyathā
prativacaamityekavākyatā a syātiti tu pañcamyāmāhutāvāpaḥ puruṣavacaso bhavati iti ca upasaṃhara etadeva darśayati śraddhākāryaṃ ca somavṛṣṭyādi sthūlībhavadabbahulaṃ lakṣyate sā ca śraddhāyā
aptve yuktiḥ kāraṇāurūpaṃ hi kāryaṃ bhavati a ca śraddhākhyaḥ pratyayaḥ maaso jīvasya vā dharmaḥ sa dharmiṇo iṣkṛṣya homāyopādātuṃ śakyate paśvādibhya
iva hṛdayādīi iti āpa eva śraddhāśabdā bhaveyuḥ śraddhāśabdaścāpsūpapadyate vaidikaprayogadarśaāt śraddhā vā āpaḥ iti tautvaṃ śraddhāsārūpyaṃ gacchati āpo dehabījabhūtā ityataḥ śraddhāśabdāḥ
syuḥ yathā siṃhaparākramo araḥ siṃhaśabdo bhavati śraddhāpūrvakakarmasamavāyācca apsu śraddhāśabda upapadyate mañcaśabda iva puruṣeṣu śraddhāhetutvācca śraddhāśabdopapattiḥāpo hāsmai śraddhāṃ saṃamate puṇyāya karmaṇe
iti śruteḥ aśrutatvāditi ceeṣṭādikāriṇāṃ pratīteḥ athāpi syāt praśaprativacaābhyāṃ āma āpaḥ śraddhādikrameṇa pañcamyāmāhutau puruṣākāraṃ pratipadyera a tu tatsaṃpariṣvaktā jīvā raṃheyuḥ aśrutatvāt
a hyatra apāmiva jīvāāṃ śrāvayitā kaścicchabdosti tasmātraṃhati saṃpariṣvaktaḥ ityayuktam iti cet aiṣa doṣaḥ kutaḥ iṣṭādikāriṇāṃ pratīteḥ atha ya ime grāma
iṣṭāpūrte dattamityupāsate te dhūmamabhisaṃbhavati ityupakramya iṣṭādikāriṇāṃ dhūmādiā pitṛyāṇea pathā cadraprāptiṃ kathayatiākāśāccadramasam eṣa somo rājā iti ta evehāpi pratīyatetasmietasmiagau devāḥ śraddhāṃ
juhvati tasyā āhuteḥ somo rājā saṃbhavati iti śrutisāmāyāt teṣāṃ ca agihotradarśapūrṇamāsādikarmasādhaabhūtā dadhipayaḥprabhṛtayo dravadravyabhūyastvātpratyakṣameva āpaḥ sati tā āhavaīye hutāḥ sūkṣmā āhutyopūrvarūpāḥ
satyaḥ tāiṣṭādikāriṇa āśrayati teṣāṃ ca śarīraṃ aidhaea vidhāeātyegāvṛtvijo juhvati asau svargāya lokāya svāhā iti tatastāḥ śraddhāpūrvakakarmasamavāyiya āhutimayya āpopūrvarūpāḥ satyaḥ tāiṣṭādikāriṇo
jīvāpariveṣṭya amuṃ lokaṃ phaladāāya ayatīti yat tadatra juhotiā abhidhīyate śraddhāṃ juhvatīti tathā ca agihotre ṣaṭpraśīirvacaarūpeṇa vākyaśeṣeṇate vā ete āhutī hute
utkrāmataḥ ityevamādiā agihotrāhutyoḥ phalārambhāya lokātaraprāptirdarśitā tasmādāhutīmayībhiradbhiḥ saṃpariṣvaktā jīvā raṃhati svakarmaphalopabhogāyeti śliṣyate kathaṃ puaridamiṣṭādikāriṇāṃ svakarmaphalopabhogāya raṃhaṇaṃ pratijñāyate yāvatā teṣāṃ dhūmapratīkea vartmaā
cadramasamadhirūḍhāāmaabhāvaṃ darśayati eṣa somo rājā taddevāāmaaṃ taṃ tevā bhakṣayati itite cadraṃ prāpyāaṃ bhavati tāṃstatra devā yathā somaṃ rājāamāpyāyasvāpakṣīyasvetyevametāṃstatra bhakṣayati iti
ca samāaviṣayaṃ śrutyataram a ca vyāghrādibhiriva devairbhakṣyamāṇāāmupabhogaḥ saṃbhavatīti ata uttaraṃ paṭhati bhāktaṃ vāātmavittvāttathāhi darśayati vāśabdaścoditadoṣavyāvartaārthaḥ bhāktameṣāmaatvam a mukhyam mukhye hyaatvesvargakāmo
yajeta ityevaṃjātīyakādhikāraśrutiruparudhyeta cadramaṇḍale cediṣṭādikāriṇāmupabhogo a syāt kimarthamadhikāriṇa iṣṭādi āyāsabahulaṃ karma kuryuḥ aaśabdaścopabhogahetutvasāmāyāt aaepyupacaryamāṇo dṛśyate yathā viśoaṃ rājñāṃ paśavoaṃ viśāmiti tasmādiṣṭastrīputramitrabhṛtyādibhiriva
guṇabhāvopagatairiṣṭādikāribhiryatsukhaviharaṇaṃ devāām tadevaiṣāṃ bhakṣaṇamabhipretam a modakādivaccarvaṇaṃ igaraṇaṃ vāa ha vai devā aśati a pibatyetadevāmṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā tṛpyati iti ca devāāṃ carvaṇādivyāpāraṃ
vārayati teṣāṃ ca iṣṭādikāriṇāṃ devāprati guṇabhāvopagatāāmapyupabhoga upapadyate rājopajīviāmiva parijaāām aātmavittvācca iṣṭādikāriṇāṃ devopabhogyabhāva upapadyate tathā hi śrutiraātmavidāṃ devopabhogyatāṃ darśayati atha yoyāṃ
devatāmupāsteyosāvayohamasmīti a sa veda yathā paśurevaṃ sa devāām iti sa cāsmiapi loke iṣṭādibhiḥ karmabhiḥ prīṇayapaśuvaddevāāmupakaroti amuṣmiapi loke tadupajīvī tadādiṣṭaṃ phalamupabhuñjāaḥ
paśuvadeva devāāmupakarotīti gamyate aātmavittvāt tathā hi darśayati ityasya aparā vyākhyā aātmavido hyete kevalakarmiṇa iṣṭādikāriṇaḥ a jñāakarmasamuccayāuṣṭhāyiaḥ pañcāgividyāmiha ātmavidyetyupacarati prakaraṇāt pañcāgividyāvihīatvāccedamiṣṭādikāriṇāṃ
guṇavādeāatvamudbhāvyate pañcāgivijñāapraśaṃsāyai pañcāgividyeha vidhitsitā vākyatātparyāvagamāt tathā hi śrutyataraṃ cadramaṇḍale bhogasadbhāvaṃ darśayati sa somaloke vibhūtimaubhūya puarāvartate iti tathā ayadapi śrutyataramatha ye
śataṃ pitṛṇāṃ jitalokāāmāadāḥ sa ekaḥ karma devāāmāado ye karmaṇā devatvamabhisaṃpadyate iti iṣṭādikāriṇāṃ devaiḥ saha saṃvasatāṃ bhogaprāptiṃ darśayati evaṃ bhāktatvādaabhāvavacaasya iṣṭādikāriṇotra
jīvā raṃhatīti pratīyate tasmātraṃhati saṃpariṣvaktaḥ iti yuktamevoktam kṛtātyaye uśayavā dṛṣṭasmṛtibhyāṃ yathetamaevañ ca kṛtātyayādhikaraṇam iṣṭādikāriṇāṃ dhūmādiā vartmaā cadramaṇḍalam adhirūḍhāāṃ bhuktabhogāāṃ tataḥ
pratyavaroha āmāyate tasmi yāvat saṃpātamuṣitvāthaitam evādhvāaṃ puar ivartate yathetam ity ārabhya yāvat ramaṇīyacaraṇā brāhmaṇādiyoim āpadyate kapūyacaraṇāḥ śvādiyoim iti tatredaṃ vicāryate
kiṃ irauśayā bhuktakṛtsakarmāṇo varohati āhosvit sāuśayā iti kiṃ tāvat prāptam irauśayā iti kutaḥ yāvat saṃpātam iti viśeṣaṇāt saṃpātaśabdeātra karmāśaya ucyate
saṃpatati aea asmāl lokāt amuṃ lokaṃ phalopabhogāyeti yāvat saṃpātam uṣitvā iti ca kṛtsasya tasya kṛtasya tatraiva bhuktatāṃ darśayati teṣāṃ yadā
tat paryavaiti iti ca śrutyatareṇaiva evārthaḥ pradarśyate syād etat yāvad amuṣmiṃl loke upabhoktavyaṃ karma tāvad upabhuṅkta iti kalpayiṣyāmīti aivaṃ kalpayituṃ

aparā śrutiḥ yatkiṃca ity aviśeṣaparāmarśea kṛtsasyeha kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ tatra kṣayitatāṃ darśayati api ca prāyaṇam aārabdhaphalasya karmaṇo bhivyañjakam prākprāyaṇāt ārabdhaphalea karmaṇā
pratibaddhasyābhivyaktyaupapatteḥ tac ca aviśeṣād yāvat kiṃcid aārabdhaphalaṃ tasya sarvasyābhivyañjakam a hi sādhāraṇe imitte aimittikam asādhāraṇaṃ bhavitum arhati a hy aviśiṣṭe
pradīpasaṃidhau ghaṭo bhivyajyate a paṭa ity upapadyate tasmā irauśayā avarohatīty evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ kṛtātyaye uśayavā iti yea karmabṛdea cadramasam ārūḍhāḥ
phalopabhogāya tasmi upabhogea kṣayite teṣāṃ yad ammayaṃ śarīraṃ cadramasy upabhogāyārabdham tat upabhogakṣayadarśaaśokāgisaṃparkāt pravilīyate savitṛkiraṇasaṃparkādivahimakarakāḥ hutabhugarciḥsaṃparkād iva ca ghṛtakāṭhiyam tataḥ kṛtātyaye

ya iha ramaṇīyacaraṇā abhyāśo ha yatte ramaṇīyāṃ yoim āpadyera brāhmaṇayoiṃ vā kṣatriyayoiṃ vā vaiśyayoiṃ vātha ya iha kapūyacaraṇā abhyāśo ha
yatte kapūyāṃ yoim āpadyerañ śvayoiṃ vā sūkarayoiṃ vā cāṇḍālayoiṃ vā iti caraṇaśabdeāuśayaḥ sūcyata iti varṇayiṣyati dṛṣṭaś cāyaṃ jamaaiva pratiprāṇyuccāvacarūpa upabhogaḥ
pravibhajyamāa ākasmikatvāsaṃbhavād auśayasadbhāvaṃ sūcayati abhyudayapratyavāyayoḥ sukṛtaduṣkṛtahetutvasya sāmāyataḥ śāstreṇāvagamitatvāt smṛtir api varṇā āśramāś ca svakarmaiṣṭhāḥ pretya karmaphalam aubhūya tataḥ śeṣeṇa viśiṣṭadeśajātikularūpāyuḥśrutavṛttavittasukhamedhaso
jama pratipadyate iti sāuśayāām evāvarohaṃ darśayati kaḥ puar auśayo āmeti kecit tāvad āhuḥ svargārthasya karmaṇo bhuktaphalasyāvaśeṣaḥ kaścid auśayo āma bhāṇḍāusārisehavat
yathā hi sehabhāṇḍaṃ ricyamāaṃ a sarvātmaā ricyate bhāṇḍāusāry eva kaścit sehaśeṣo vatiṣṭhate tathā auśayo pīti au kāryavirodhitvād adṛṣṭasya a bhuktaphalasyāvaśeṣāvasthāaṃ
