kila kaścit sevakaḥ sakalaiḥ sevopakaraṇaiḥ rājakulam upasṛptaś cirapravāsāt parikṣīṇabahūpakaraṇaś chatrapādukādimātrāvaśeṣo a rājakule vasthātuṃ śakoti evam auśayamātraparigraho a cadramaṇḍale vasthātuṃ śakotīti
a caitadyuktam iva eva a hi svargārthasya karmaṇo bhuktaphalasyāvaśeṣāuvṛttir upapadyate kāryavirodhitvāt ity uktam av etad apy uktam a svargaphalasya karmaṇo
ikhilasya bhuktaphalatvaṃ bhaviṣyatīti tad etad apeśalam svargārthaṃ kila karma svargasthasyaiva svargaphalaṃ ikhilaṃ a jaayati svargacyutasyāpi kaṃcit phalaleśaṃ jaayatīti a śabdapramāṇakāām
īdṛśī kalpaā avakalpate sehabhāṇḍe tu sehaleśāuvṛttir dṛṣṭatvād upapadyate tathā sevakasyopakaraṇaleśāuvṛttiś ca dṛśyate a tv iha tathā svargaphalasya karmaṇo leśāuvṛttir dṛśyate
āpi kalpayituṃ śakyate svargaphalatvaśāstravirodhāt avaśyaṃ caitad evaṃ vijñeyam a svargaphalasyeṣṭādeḥ karmaṇo bhāṇḍāusārisehavad ekadeśo uvartamāo uśaya iti yadi hi yea sukṛtea
karmaṇā iṣṭādiā svargam avabhūva tasyaiva kaścid ekadeśo uśayaḥ kalpyeta tato ramaṇīya evaiko uśayaḥ syāt a viparītaḥ tatreyam auśayavibhāgaśrutir uparudhyeta tad
ya iha ramaṇīyacaraṇāḥ atha ya iha kapūyacaraṇāḥ iti tasmād āmuṣmikaphale karmajāte upabhukte vaśiṣṭam aihikaphalaṃ karmātarajātam auśayaḥ tadvato varohatīti yad uktam
yat kiṃca ity aviśeṣaparāmarśāt sarvasyeha kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ phalopabhogeātaṃ prāpya irauśayā avarohatīti aitad evam auśayasadbhāvasyāvagamitatvāt yat kiṃcid iha kṛtam āmuṣmikaphalaṃ karma
ārabdhabhogam tat sarvaṃ phalopabhogea kṣapayitvā iti gamyate yad apy uktam prāyaṇam aviśeṣād aārabdhaphalaṃ kṛtsam eva karmābhivyaakti tatra keacit karmaṇāmuṣimalloke phalam
ārabhyate keacid asmi ity ayaṃ vibhāgo a saṃbhavatīti tadapyauśayasadbhāvapratipādaeaiva pratyuktam api ca kea hetuā prāyaṇamaārabdhaphalasya karmaṇobhivyañjakaṃ pratijñāyata iti vaktavyam ārabdhaphalea
karmaṇā pratibaddhasyetarasya vṛttyudbhavāupapatteḥ tadupaśamāt prāyaṇakāle vṛttyudbhavo bhavatīti yadyucyeta tato vaktavyam yathaiva tarhi pākprāyaṇāt ārabdhaphalea karmaṇā pratibaddhasya itarasya vṛttyudbhavāupapattiḥ evaṃ prāyaṇakālepi
viruddhaphalasyāekasya karmaṇo yugapatphalārambhāsaṃbhavāt balavatā pratibaddhasya durbalasya vṛttyudbhavāupapattiriti a hi aārabdhaphalatvasāmāyea jātyataropabhogyaphalamapyaekaṃ karma ekasmiprāyaṇe yugapadabhivyaktaṃ sat ekāṃ jātimārabhata iti śakyaṃ vaktum
pratiiyataphalatvavirodhāt āpi kasyacitkarmaṇaḥ prāyaṇebhivyaktiḥ kasyaciduccheda iti śakyate vaktum aikātikaphalatvavirodhāt a hi prāyaścittādibhirhetubhirviā karmaṇāmucchedaḥ saṃbhāvyate smṛtirapi viruddhaphalea karmaṇā pratibaddhasya karmātarasya ciramavasthāaṃ
darśayati kadācitsukṛtaṃ karma kūṭasthamiha tiṣṭhati majjamāasya saṃsāre yāvadduḥkhādvimucyate ityevaṃjātīyākā yadi ca kṛtsamaārabdhaphalaṃ karma ekasmiprāyaṇebhivyaktaṃ sat ekāṃ jātimārabheta tataḥ svargaarakatiryagyoiṣvadhikārāavagamāt dharmādharmāutpattau
imittābhāvāt ottarā jātirupapadyeta brahmahatyādīāṃ ca ekaikasya karmaṇoekajamaimittatvaṃ smaryamāṇamuparudhyeta a ca dharmādharmayoḥ svarūpaphalasādhaādisamadhigame śāstrādatiriktaṃ kāraṇaṃ śakyaṃ saṃbhāvayitum a ca dṛṣṭaphalasya karmaṇaḥ
kārīryādeḥ prāyaṇamabhivyañjakaṃ saṃbhavatīti avyāpikāpīyaṃ prāyaṇasyābhivyañjakatvakalpaā pradīpopayāsopi karmabalābalapradarśaeaiva pratiītaḥ sthūlasūkṣmarūpābhivyaktivaccedaṃ draṣṭavyam yathā hi pradīpaḥ samāepi saṃidhāe sthūlaṃ rūpamabhivyaakti a sūkṣmam evaṃ
prāyaṇaṃ samāepyaārabdhaphalasya karmajātasya prāptāvasaratve balavataḥ karmaṇo vṛttimudbhāvayati a durbalasyeti tasmācchrutismṛtiyāyavirodhādaśliṣṭoyamaśeṣakarmābhivyaktyabhyupagamaḥ śeṣakarmasadbhāveirmokṣaprasaṅga ityayamapyasthāe saṃbhramaḥ samyagdarśaādaśeṣakarmakṣayaśruteḥ tasmāt sthitametadeva auśayavatovarohatīti te ca avarohato
yathetamaevaṃ ca avarohati yathetamiti yathāgatamityarthaḥ aevamiti tadviparyayeṇetyarthaḥ dhūmākāśayoḥ pitṛyāṇedhvayupāttayoravarohe saṃkīrtaāt yathetaṃśabdācca yathāgatamiti pratīyate rātryādyasaṃkīrtaādabhrādyupasaṃkhyāācca viparyayopi pratīyate caraṇāditi ceopalakṣaṇārtheti kārṣṇājiiḥ athāpi
syāt yā śrutirauśayasadbhāvapratipādaāyodāhṛtā tadya iha ramaṇīyacaraṇāḥ iti sā khalu caraṇāt yoyāpattiṃ darśayati āuśayāt ayaccaraṇam ayouśayaḥ caraṇaṃ cāritram ācāraḥ śīlamityaarthātaram auśayastu
bhuktaphalātkarmaṇotiriktaṃ karma abhipretam śrutiśca karmacaraṇe bhedea vyapadiśati yathākārī yathācārī tathā bhavati itiyāyaavadyāi karmāṇi tāi sevitavyāi o itarāṇi yāyasmāksucaritāi tāi tvayopāsyāi
iti ca tasmāt caraṇādyoyāpattiśruteḥ āuśayasiddhiḥ iti cet aiṣa doṣaḥ yatouśayopalakṣaṇārthaiva eṣā caraṇaśrutiriti kārṣṇājiirācāryo mayate āarthakyamiti cea tad apekṣatvāt syādetat kasmātpuaścaraṇaśabdea
śrautaṃ śīlaṃ vihāya lākṣaṇikaḥ auśayaḥ pratyāyyate au śīlasyaiva śrautasya vihitapratiṣiddhasya sādhvasādhurūpasya śubhāśubhayoyāpattiḥ phalaṃ bhaviṣyati avaśyaṃ ca śīlasyāpi kiṃcitphalamabhyupagatavyam ayathā hyāarthakyameva
śīlasya prasajyeta iti cet aiṣa doṣaḥ kutaḥ tadapekṣatvāt iṣṭādi hi karmajātaṃ caraṇāpekṣam a hi sadācārahīaḥ kaścidadhikṛtaḥ syāt ācārahīaṃ a puati
vedāḥ ityādismṛtibhyaḥ puruṣārthatvepyācārasya a āarthakyam iṣṭādau hi karmajāte phalamārabhamāṇe tadapekṣa evācārastatraiva kaṃcidatiśayamārapsyate karma ca sarvārthakāri iti śrutismṛtiprasiddhiḥ tasmātkarmaiva śīlopalakṣitamauśayabhūtaṃ yoyāpattau
kāraṇamiti kārṣṇājiermatam a hi karmaṇi saṃbhavati śīlāt yoyāpattiryuktā a hi padbhyāṃ palāyituṃ pārayamāṇo jāubhyāṃ raṃhitumarhati iti sukṛtaduṣkṛte eveti tu bādariḥ
bādaris tv ācāryaḥ sukṛtaduṣkṛte eva caraṇaśabdea pratyāyyete iti mayate caraṇam auṣṭhāa karmety aarthātaram tathā hi aviśeṣeṇa karmamātre caratiḥ prayujyamāo dṛśyate
yo hi iṣṭādilakṣaṇaṃ puṇyaṃ karma karoti taṃ laukikā ācakṣate dharmaṃ caraty eṣa mahātmeti ācāro pi ca dharmaviśeṣa eva bhedavyapadeśas tu
karmacaraṇayor brāhmaṇaparivrājakayāyeāpy upapadyate tasmāt ramaṇīyacaraṇāḥ praśastakarmāṇaḥ kapūyacaraṇā iditakarmāṇaḥ iti irṇayaḥ aiṣṭādikāriṇāmapi ca śrutam aiṣṭādikāryadhikaraṇam iṣṭādikāriṇaścadramasaṃ gacchatītyuktam ye tvitareiṣṭādikāriṇaḥ tepi kiṃ
cadramasaṃ gacchati uta a gacchatīti cityate tatra tāvadāha iṣṭādikāriṇa eva cadramasaṃ gacchatītyetat a kasmāt yatoiṣṭādikāriṇāmapi cadramaṇḍalaṃ gatavyatvea śrutam tathā hi
aviśeṣeṇa kauṣītakiaḥ samāmaati ye vai ke cāsmāllokātprayati cadramasameva te sarve gacchati iti dehārambhopi ca puarjāyamāāāṃ a atareṇa cadraprāptim avakalpatepañcamyāmāhutau ityāhutisaṃkhyāiyamāt
tasmātsarva eva cadramasamāsīdeyuḥ iṣṭādikāriṇāmitareṣāṃ ca samāagatitvaṃ a yuktamiti cet a itareṣāṃ cadramaṇḍale bhogābhāvāt saṃyamae tvaubhūyetareṣāmārohāvarohau tadgatidarśaāt tuśabdaḥ pakṣaṃ vyāvartayati aitadasti
sarve cadramasaṃ gacchatīti kasmāt bhogāyaiva hi cadrārohaṇam a iṣprayojaam āpi pratyavarohāyaiva yathā kaścidvṛkṣamārohati puṣpaphalopādāāya a iṣprayojaam āpi pataāyaiva bhogaśca aiṣṭādikāriṇāṃ
cadramasi āstītyuktam tasmādiṣṭādikāriṇa eva cadramasamārohati etare te tu saṃyamaaṃ yamālayamavagāhya svaduṣkṛtāurūpā yāmīryātaā aubhūya puareva imaṃ lokaṃ pratyavarohati evaṃbhūtau teṣāmārohāvarohau bhavataḥ
kutaḥ tadgatidarśaāt tathā hi yamavacaasarūpā śrutiḥ prayatām aiṣṭādikāriṇāṃ yamavaśyatāṃ darśayati a sāṃparāyaḥ pratibhāti bālaṃ pramādyataṃ vittamohea mūḍham ayaṃ loko āsti
para iti māī puaḥ puarvaśamāpadyate me itivaivasvataṃ saṃgamaaṃ jaāām ityevaṃjātīyakaṃ ca bahveva yamavaśyatāprāptiliṅgaṃ bhavati smarati ca api ca mauvyāsaprabhṛtayaḥ śiṣṭāḥ
saṃyamae pure yamāyattaṃ kapūyakarmavipākaṃ smarati āciketopākhyāādiṣu api ca sapta api ca sapta arakā rauravapramukhā duṣkṛtaphalopabhogabhūmitvea smaryate paurāṇikaiḥ tāaiṣṭādikāriṇaḥ prāpuvati kutaste
cadraṃ prāpuyuḥ ityabhiprāyaḥ au viruddhamidam yamāyattā yātaāḥ pāpakarmāṇoubhavatīti yāvatā teṣu rauravādiṣu aye citraguptādayo āādhiṣṭhātāraḥ smaryata iti etyāha tatrāpi ca tadvyāpārādavirodhaḥ
teṣvapi saptasu arakeṣu tasyaiva yamasyādhiṣṭhātṛtvavyāpārābhyupagamādavirodhaḥ yamaprayuktā eva hi te citraguptādayodhiṣṭhātāraḥ smaryate vidyākarmaṇoriti tu prakṛtatvāt pañcāgividyāyāmvettha yathāsau loko a saṃpūryate ityasya
praśasya prativacaāvasare śrūyate athaitayoḥ pathora katareṇacaa tāīmāi kṣudrāṇyasakṛdāvartīi bhūtāi bhavati jāyasva mriyastvetyetattṛtīyaṃ sthāaṃ teāsau loke a saṃpūryate iti tatra etayoḥ
pathoriti vidyākarmaṇorityetat kasmāt prakṛtatvāt vidyākarmaṇī hi devayāapitṛyāṇayoḥ pathoḥ pratipade prakṛte tadya itthaṃ viduḥ iti vidyā tayā pratipattavyo devayāaḥ pathāḥ prakīrtitaḥiṣṭāpūrte
dattam iti karma tea pratipattavyaḥ pitṛyāṇaḥ pathāḥ prakīrtitaḥ tatprakriyāyāmathaitayoḥ pathora katareṇacaa iti śrutam etaduktaṃ bhavati ye a vidyāsādhaea devayāe pathyadhikṛtāḥ
āpi karmaṇā pitṛyāṇe teṣām eṣa kṣudrajatulakṣaṇosakṛdāvartī tṛtīyaḥ pathā bhavatīti tasmādapi a aiṣṭādikāribhiścadramāḥ prāpyate syādetat tepi cadrabimbamāruhya tatovaruhya kṣudrajatutvaṃ pratipatsyata iti
tadapi āsti ārohāarthakyāt api ca sarveṣu prayatsu cadralokaṃ prāpuvatsu asau lokaḥ prayadbhiḥ saṃpūryeta ityataḥ praśaviruddhaṃ prativacaaṃ prasajyeta tathā hi prativacaaṃ
dātavyam yathā asau loko a saṃpūryate avarohābhyupagamādasaṃpūraṇopapattiriti cet a aśrutatvāt satyam avarohādapyasaṃpūraṇamupapadyate śrutistu tṛtīyasthāasaṃkīrtaea asaṃpūraṇaṃ darśayati etattṛtīyaṃ sthāaṃ teāsau loko
a saṃpūryate iti tea aārohādeva asaṃpūraṇamiti yuktam avarohasyeṣṭādikāriṣvapyaviśiṣṭatve sati tṛtīyasthāoktyāarthakyaprasaṅgāt tuśabdastu śākhātarīyavākyaprabhavāmaśeṣagamaāśaṅkāmucchiatti evaṃ sati adhikṛtāpekṣaḥ śākhātarīye vākye sarvaśabdovatiṣṭhate ye vai
kecidadhikṛtā asmāllokātprayati cadramasameva te sarve gacchatīti yatpuaruktam dehalābhopapattaye sarve cadramasaṃ gatumarhatipañcamyāmāhutau ityāhutisaṃkhyāiyamāditi tatpratyucyate a tṛtīye tathopalabdheḥ a tṛtīye sthāe dehalābhāya
pañcasaṃkhyāiyama āhutīāmādartavyaḥ kutaḥ tathopalabdheḥ tathā hi atareṇaivāhutisaṃkhyāiyamaṃ varṇitea prakāreṇa tṛtīyasthāaprāptirupalabhyate jāyasva mriyasvetyetattṛtīyaṃ sthāam iti api capañcamyāmāhutāvāpaḥ puruṣavacaso bhavati iti mauṣyaśarīrahetutvea
āhutisaṃkhyā kīrtyate a kīṭapataṅgādiśarīrahetutvea puruṣaśabdasya mauṣyajātivacaatvāt api ca pañcamyāmāhutāvapāṃ puruṣavacastvamupadiśyate a apañcamyāmāhutau puruṣavacastvaṃ pratiṣidhyate vākyasya dvyarthatādoṣāt tatra yeṣāmārohāvarohau saṃbhavataḥ teṣāṃ
pañcamyāmāhutau deha udbhaviṣyati ayeṣāṃ tu viaivāhutisaṃkhyayā bhūtātaropasṛṣṭābhiradbhirdeha ārapsyate smaryatepi ca loke api ca smaryate loke droṇadhṛṣṭadyumaprabhṛtīāṃ sītādraupadīprabhṛtīāṃ ca ayoijatvam tatra
droṇādīāṃ yoṣidviṣayā ekā āhutirāsti dhṛṣṭadyumādīāṃ tu yoṣitpuruṣaviṣaye dve apyāhutī a staḥ yathā ca tatra āhutisaṃkhyāiyamāādaro bhavati evamayatrāpi bhaviṣyati balākāpi atareṇaiva
retaḥsekaṃ garbhaṃ dhatta iti lokarūḍhiḥ darśaācca api ca caturvidhe bhūtagrāme jarāyujāṇḍajasvedajodbhijjalakṣaṇe svedajodbhijjayoḥ atareṇaiva grāmyadharmam utpattidarśaāt āhutisaṃkhyāādaro bhavati evamayatrāpi bhaviṣyati auteṣāṃ
khalveṣāṃ bhūtāāṃ trīṇyeva bījāi bhavati āṇḍajaṃ jīvajamudbhijjam ityatra trividha eva bhūtagrāmaḥ śrūyate kathaṃ caturvidhatvaṃ bhūtagrāmasya pratijñātamiti atrocyate tṛtīyaśabdāvarodhaḥ saṃśokajasya āṇḍajaṃ
jīvajamudbhijjam ityatra tṛtīyeodbhijjaśabdeaiva svedajopasaṃgrahaḥ kṛtaḥ pratyetavyaḥ ubhayorapi svedajodbhijjayoḥ bhūmyudakodbhedaprabhavatvasya tulyatvāt sthāvarodbhedāttu vilakṣaṇo jaṅgamodbheda ityayatra svedajodbhijjayorbhedavāda ityavirodhaḥ sābhāvyāpattirupapatteḥ sābhāvyāpattyadhikaraṇam iṣṭādikāriṇaścadramasamāruhya tasmiyāvatsaṃpātamuṣitvā
tataḥ sāuśayā avarohatītyuktam athāvarohaprakāraḥ parīkṣyate tatreyamavarohaśrutirbhavati athaitamevādhvāaṃ puarivartate yathetamākāśamākāśādvāyuṃ vāyurbhūtvā dhūmo bhavati dhūmo bhūtvābhraṃ bhavatyabhraṃ bhūtvā megho bhavati megho bhūtvā
pravarṣati iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kimākāśādisvarūpamevāvarohataḥ pratipadyate kiṃ vā ākāśādisāmyamiti tatra prāptaṃ tāvat ākāśādisvarūpameva pratipadyata iti kutaḥ evaṃ hi śrutir bhavati
itarathā lakṣaṇā syāt śrutilakṣaṇāviśaye ca śrutir yāyyā a lakṣaṇā tathā cavāyur bhūtvā dhūmo bhavati ity evamādīy akṣaraṇi tattatsvarūpāpattau āñjasyea avakalpate
tasmādākāśādisvarūpapratipattiriti evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ ākāśādisāmyaṃ pratipadyata iti cadramaṇḍale yat ammayaṃ śarīramupabhogārthamārabdham tat upabhogakṣaye sati pravilīyamāaṃ sūkṣmam ākāśasamaṃ bhavati tato vāyor
vaśameti tato dhūmādibhiḥ saṃpṛcyata iti tad etaducyate yathetam ākāśamākāśād vāyum ityevamādiā kuta etat upapatteḥ evaṃ hi etad upapadyate a hi
ayasyāyabhāvo mukhya upapadyate ākāśasvarūpapratipattau ca vāyvādikrameṇāvaroho opapadyate vibhutvāc ca ākāśea ityasaṃbaddhatvāt a tatsādṛśyāpatter ayaḥ tatsaṃbadho ghaṭate śrutyasaṃbhave ca lakṣaṇāśrayaṇaṃ yāyyam
eva ata ākāśāditulyatāpattir eva atra ākāśādibhāva ity upacaryate āticireṇa viśeṣāt āticirādhikaraṇam tatra akāśādipratipattau prāgvrīhyādibhāvāpatteḥ bhavati viśayaḥ kiṃ dīrghaṃ dīrghaṃ kālaṃ
pūrvapūrvasādṛśyeāvasthāyottarottarasādṛśyaṃ gacchati utālpamalpamiti tatrāiyamaḥ iyamakāriṇaḥ śāstrasyābhāvādityevaṃ prāpte idamāha āticireṇeti alpamalpaṃ kālamākāśādibhāveāvasthāya varṣadhārābhiḥ saha imāṃ bhuvamāpatati kuta etat viśeṣadarśaāt tathā hi
vrīhyādibhāvāpatteraataraṃ viśiaṣṭi ato vai khalu duriṣprapataram iti takāra ekaśchādasyāṃ prakriyāyāṃ lupto matavyaḥ duriṣprapatataraṃ duriṣkramataram duḥkhataramasmādvrīhyādibhāvāiḥsaraṇaṃ bhavatītyarthaḥ tat atra duḥkhaṃ iṣprapataaṃ
pradarśaya pūrveṣu sukhaṃ iṣprapataaṃ darśayati sukhaduḥkhatāviśeṣaścāyaṃ iṣprapataasya kālālpatvadīrghatvaimittaḥ tasmiavadhau śarīrāiṣpatterupabhogāsaṃbhavāt tasmādvrīhyādibhāvāpatteḥ prāk alpeaiva kāleāvarohaḥ syāditi ayādhiṣṭhiteṣu pūrvavadabhilāpāt ayādhiṣṭhitādhikaraṇam tasmievāvarohe pravarṣaṇāataraṃ
paṭhyate ta iha vrīhiyavā oṣadhivaaspatayastilamāṣā iti jāyate iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kimasmiavadhau sthāvarajātyāpaāḥ sthāvarasukhaduḥkhabhājouśayio bhavati āhosvitkṣetrajñātarādhiṣṭhiteṣu sthāvaraśarīreṣu saṃśleṣamātraṃ gacchatīti kiṃ tāvatprāptam
sthāvarajātyāpaāstatsukhaduḥkhabhājouśayio bhavatīti kuta etat jaermukhyārthatvopapatteḥ sthāvarabhāvasya ca śrutismṛtyorupabhogasthāatvaprasiddheḥ paśuhiṃsādiyogācca iṣṭādeḥ karmajātasyāiṣṭaphalatvopapatteḥ tasmāmukhyamevedamauśayiāṃ vrīhyādijama śvādijamavat yathāśvayoiṃ vā sūkarayoiṃ vā cāṇḍālayoiṃ vā
iti mukhyamevāuśayiāṃ śvādijama tatsukhaduḥkhāvitaṃ bhavati evaṃ vrīhyādijamāpīti evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ ayairjīvairadhiṣṭhiteṣu vrīhyādiṣu saṃsargamātramauśayiaḥ pratipadyate a tatsukhaduḥkhabhājo bhavati pūrvavat yathā vāyudhūmādibhāvouśayiāṃ
tatsaṃśleṣamātram evaṃ vrīhyādibhāvopi jātisthāvaraiḥ saṃśleṣamātram kuta etat tadvadevehāpyabhilāpāt kobhilāpasya tadvadbhāvaḥ karmavyāpāramatareṇa saṃkīrtaam yathā ākāśādiṣu pravarṣaṇāteṣu a kiṃcitkarmavyāpāraṃ parāmṛśati evaṃ vrīhyādijamayapi
tasmāāstyatra sukhaduḥkhabhāktvamauśayiām yatra tu sukhaduḥkhabhāktvamabhipraiti parāmṛśati tatra karmavyāpāram ramaṇīyacaraṇāḥ kapūyacaraṇāḥ iti api ca mukhyeuśayiāṃ vrīhyādijamai vrīhyādiṣu lūyamāeṣu kaṇḍyamāeṣu pacyamāeṣu bhakṣyamāṇeṣu
ca tadabhimāiouśayiaḥ pravaseyuḥ yo hi jīvo yaccharīramabhimayate sa tasmipīḍyamāe pravasati iti prasiddham tatra vrīhyādibhāvādretaḥsigbhāvouśayiāṃ ābhilapyeta ataḥ saṃsargamātramauśayiāmayādhiṣṭhiteṣu vrīhyādiṣu bhavati etea
jaermukhyārthatvaṃ pratibrūyāt upabhogasthāatvaṃ ca sthāvarabhāvasya a ca vayamupabhogasthāatvaṃ sthāvarabhāvasyāvajāīmahe bhavatvayeṣāṃ jatūāmapuṇyasāmarthyea sthāvarabhāvamupagatāām etat upabhogasthāam cadramasastu avarohatouśayio a sthāvarabhāvamupabhuñjata ityācakṣmahe aśuddham
iti ce a śabdāt yat puar uktam paśuhiṃsādiyogād aśuddham ādhvarikaṃ karma tasyāiṣṭam api phalam avakalpata ity ato mukhyam evāuśayiāṃ vrīhyādijama
astu tatra gauṇī kalpaā aarthiketi tat parihriyate a śāstrahetutvād dharmādharmavijñāasya ayaṃ dharmaḥ ayam adharma iti śāstram eva vijñāe kāraṇam atīdriyatvāt
tayoḥ aiyatadeśakālaimittatvāc ca yasmi deśe kāle imitte ca yo dharmo uṣṭhīyate sa eva deśakālaimittātareṣv adharmo bhavati tea a śāstrādṛte dharmādharmaviṣayaṃ
vijñāaṃ kasyacid asti śāstrāc ca hiṃsāugrahādyātmako jyotiṣṭomo dharma ity avadhāritaḥ sa katham aśuddha iti śakyate vaktum au a hiṃsyāt sarvā
bhūtāi iti śāstram eva bhūtaviṣayāṃ hiṃsām adharma ity avagamayati bāḍham utsargas tu saḥ apavādo yaṃ ca agīṣomīyaṃ paśum ālabheta iti
utsargāpavādayoś ca vyavasthitaviṣayatvam tasmād viśuddhaṃ karma vaidikam śiṣṭair auṣṭhīyamāatvāt aidyamāatvāc ca tea a tasya pratirūpaṃ phalam jātisthāvaratvam a ca śvādijamavad
api vrīhyādijama bhavitum arhati tad dhi kapūyacaraṇāadhikṛtya ucyate aivam iha vaiśeṣikaḥ kaścid adhikāro sti ataś cadrasthalas khalitāām auśayiāṃ vrīhyādisaṃśleṣamātraṃ tadbhāva
ity upacaryate retaḥsigyogotha itaśca vrīhyādisaṃśleṣamātraṃ tadbhāvaḥ yatkāraṇaṃ vrīhyādibhāvasyāataramauśayiāṃ retaḥsigbhāva āmāyate yo yo hyaamatti yo retaḥ siñcati tadbhūya eva bhavati iti
a cātra mukhyo retaḥsigbhāvaḥ saṃbhavati cirajāto hi prāptayauvao retaḥsigbhavati kathamiva aupacaritaṃ tadbhāvam adyamāāāugatouśayī pratipadyate tatra tāvadavaśyaṃ retaḥsigyoga eva retaḥsigbhāvobhyupagatavyaḥ tadvat
vrīhyādibhāvopi vrīhyādiyoga evetyavirodhaḥ yoeḥ śarīram atha retaḥsigbhāvasyāataraṃ yoau iṣikte retasi yoeradhi śarīram auśayiām auśayaphalopabhogāya jāyata ityāha śāstram tadya iha ramaṇīyacaraṇāḥ
ityādi tasmādapyavagamyate āvarohe brāhyādibhāvāvasare taccharīrameva sukhaduḥkhāvitaṃ bhavatīti tasmāt vrīhyādisaṃśleṣamātramauśayiāṃ tajjameti siddham iti śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācāryasya śrīgovidabhagavatpūjyapādaśiṣyasya śrīmacchaṃkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīrakamīmāṃsāsūtrabhāṣye tṛtīyādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ
murat tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ sadhye sṛṣṭirāha hi saṃdhyādhikaraṇam saṃdhye sṛṣṭiriti saṃdhyamiti svapasthāamācaṣṭe vede prayogadarśaāt saṃdhyaṃ tṛtīysvapasthāam iti dvayorlokasthāayoḥ prabodhasaṃprasādasthāayorvā saṃdhau
bhavatīti saṃdhyam tasmisaṃdhye sthāe tathyarūpaiva sṛṣṭirbhavitumarhati kutaḥ yataḥ pramāṇabhūtā śrutirevamāha atha rathāathayogāpathaḥ sṛjate ityādisa hi kartā iti ca upasaṃhārāt evamevāvagamyate
irmātāraṃ caike putrādayaśca api ca eke śākhiaḥ asmieva saṃdhye sthāe kāmāāṃ irmātāramātmāamāmaati ya eṣa supteṣu jāgarti kāmaṃ kāmaṃ puruṣo irmimāṇaḥ
iti putrādayaśca tatra kāmā abhipreyate kāmyata iti au kāmaśabdeecchāviśeṣo evocyera aśatāyuṣaḥ putrapautrāvṛṇīṣva iti prakṛtya atekāmāāṃ tvā kāmabhājaṃ karomi iti prakṛteṣu
tatra tatra putrādiṣu kāmaśabdasya prayuktatvāt prājñaṃ caiaṃ irmātāraṃ prakaraṇavākyaśeṣābhyāṃ pratīmaḥ prājñasya hīdaṃ prakaraṇam ayatra dharmādayatrādharmāt ityādi tadviṣaya eva ca vākyaśeṣopi
tadeva śukraṃ tadbrahma tadevāmṛtamucyate tasimallokāḥ śritāḥ sarve tadu ātyeti kaścaa iti prājñakartṛkā ca sṛṣṭistathyarūpā samadhigatā jāgaritāśrayā tathā svapāśrayāpi sṛṣṭirbhavitumarhati tathā
ca śrutiḥ atho khalvāhurjāgaritadeśa evāsyaiṣa iti yāyeva jāgratpaśyati tāi suptaḥ iti svapajāgaritayoḥ samāayāyatāṃ śrāvayati tasmāttathyarūpaiva saṃdhye sṛṣṭiriti evaṃ prāpte pratyāha
māyāmātraṃ tu kārtsyeāabhivyaktasvarūpatvāt tuśabdaḥ pakṣaṃ vyāvartayati aitadasti yaduktam saṃdhye sṛṣṭiḥ pāramārthikīti māyaiva saṃdhye sṛṣṭiḥ a paramārthagadhopyasti kutaḥ kārtsyeāabhivyaktasvarūpatvāt a hi
kārtsyea paramārthavastudharmeṇa abhivyaktasvarūpaḥ svapaḥ kiṃ puaratra kārtsyamabhipretam deśakālaimittasaṃpattiḥ abādhaśca a hi paramārthavastuviṣayāṇi deśakālaimittāi abādhaśca svape saṃbhāvyate a tāvatsvape rathādīāmucito deśaḥ
saṃbhavati a hi saṃvṛte dehadeśe rathādayovakāśaṃ labhera syādetat bahirdehāt svapaṃ drakṣyati deśātaritadravyagrahaṇāt darśayati ca śrutiḥ bahirdehātsvapam bahiṣkulāyādamṛtaścaritvā sa īyatemṛto yatra
kāmam iti sthitigatipratyayabhedaśca a aiṣkrāte jatau sāmañjasyamaśuvīta iti etyucyate a hi suptasya jatoḥ kṣaṇamātreṇa yojaaśatātaritaṃ deśaṃ paryetuṃ viparyetuṃ ca tataḥ
sāmarthyaṃ saṃbhāvyate kvacicca pratyāgamaavarjitaṃ svapaṃ śrāvayati kuruṣvahamadya śayāo idrayābhiplutaḥ svape pañcālāabhigataśca asmipratibuddhaśca iti dehāccedapeyāt pañcāleṣveva pratibudhyeta tāasāvabhigata iti kuruṣveva tu
pratibudhyate yea ca ayaṃ dehea deśātaramaśuvāo mayate tamaye pārśvasthāḥ śayaadeśa eva paśyati yathābhūtāi ca ayaṃ deśātarāṇi svape paśyati a tāi
tathābhūtāyeva bhavati paridhāvaṃścetpaśyet jāgradvat vastubhūtamarthamākalayet darśayati ca śrutiratareva dehe svapam sa yatraitatsvapyayā carati ityupakramyasve śarīre yathākāmaṃ parivartate iti ataśca śrutyupapattivirodhādbahiṣkulāyaśrutiḥ
gauṇī vyākhyātavyā bahiriva kulāyāt amṛtaścaritveti yo hi vasaapi śarīre a tea prayojaaṃ karoti sa bahiriva śarīrādbhavati iti sthitigatipratyayabhedopyevaṃ sati vipralambha
evābhyupagatavyaḥ kālavisaṃvādopi ca svape bhavati rajayāṃ supto vāsaraṃ bhārate varṣe mayate tathā muhūrtamātravartii svape kadācit bahū varṣapūgā ativāhayati imittāyapi ca
svape a buddhaye karmaṇe vā ucitāi vidyate karaṇopasaṃhārāddhi āsya aśvarathādigrahaṇāya cakṣurādīi sati rathādiirvartaepi kutosya imeṣamātreṇa sāmarthyaṃ dārūṇi vā bādhyate caite
rathāśvādayaḥ svapadṛṣṭāḥ prabodhe svapa eva ca ete sulabhabādhā bhavati ādyatayorvyabhicāradarśaāt rathoyamiti hi kadācitsvape irdhāritaḥ kṣaṇea mauṣyaḥ saṃpadyate mauṣyoyamiti irdhāritaḥ kṣaṇea
vṛkṣaḥ spaṣṭaṃ cābhāvaṃ rathādīāṃ svape śrāvayati śāstram a tatra rathā a rathayogā a pathāo bhavati ityādi tasmāmāyāmātraṃ svapadarśaam sūcakaśca hi
śruterācakṣate ca tadvidaḥ māyāmātratvāttarhi a kaścitsvape paramārthagadhostīti etyucyate sūcakaśca hi svapo bhavati bhaviṣyatoḥ sādhvasādhuoḥ tathā hi śrūyate yadā karmasu kāmyeṣu
striyaṃ svapeṣu paśyati samṛddhiṃ tatra jāīyāttasmisvapaidarśae iti tathāpuruṣaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ kṛṣṇadataṃ paśyati sa eaṃ hati ityevamādibhiḥ svapairacirajīvitvamāvedyata iti śrāvayati ācakṣate ca
svapādhyāyavidaḥ kuñjarārohaṇādīi svape dhayāi kharayāādīyadhayāi iti matradevatādravyaviśeṣaimittāśca kecitsvapāḥ satyārthagadhio bhavatīti mayate tatrāpi bhavatu āma sūcyamāasya vastuaḥ satyatvam sūcakasya tu strīdarśaāderbhavatyeva
vaitathyam bādhyamāatvādityabhiprāyaḥ tasmādupapaaṃ svapasya māyāmātratvam yaduktam āha hi iti tadevaṃ sati bhāktaṃ vyākhyātavyam yathālāṅgalaṃ gavādīudvahati iti imittamātratvādevamucyate a tu pratyakṣameva
lāṅgalaṃ gavādīudvahati evaṃ imittamātratvāt supto rathādīsṛjatesa hi kartā iti ca ucyate a tu pratyakṣameva supto rathādīsṛjati imittatvaṃ tu asya rathādipratibhāaimittamodatrāsādidarśaāttaimittabhūtayoḥ
sukṛtaduṣkṛtayoḥ kartṛtveeti vaktavyam api ca jāgarite viṣayedriyasaṃyogāt ādityādijyotirvyatikarācca ātmaaḥ svayaṃjyotiṣṭvaṃ durvivecaamiti tadvivecaāya svapa upayastaḥ tatra yadi rathādisṛṣṭivacaaṃ śrutyā īyeta tataḥ
svayaṃjyotiṣṭvaṃ a irṇītaṃ syāt tasmādrathādyabhāvavacaaṃ śrutyā rathādisṛṣṭivacaaṃ tu bhaktyeti vyākhyeyam etea irmāṇaśravaṇaṃ vyākhyātam yadapyuktam prājñameaṃ irmātāramāmaati iti tadapyasat śrutyataresvayaṃ vihatya
svayaṃ irmāya svea bhāsā svea jyotiṣā prasvapiti iti jīvavyāpāraśravaṇāt ihāpiya eṣa supteṣu jāgarti iti prasiddhāuvādājjīva evāyaṃ kāmāāṃ irmātā saṃkīrtyate tasya
tu vākyaśeṣeṇatadeva śukraṃ tadbrahma iti jīvabhāvaṃ vyāvartya brahmabhāva upadiśyate tattvamasi ityādivat iti a brahmaprakaraṇaṃ virudhyate a cāsmābhiḥ svapepi prājñavyāpāraḥ pratiṣidhyate
tasya sarveśvaratvāt sarvāsvapyavasthāsvadhiṣṭhātṛtvopapatteḥ pāramārthikastu āyaṃ saṃdhyāśrayaḥ sargaḥ viyadādisargavat ityetāvatpratipādyate a ca viyadādisargasyāpyātyatikaṃ satyatvamasti pratipāditaṃ hitadaayatvamārambhaṇaśabdādibhyaḥ ityatra samastasya prapañcasya māyāmātratvam prāk
tu brahmātmatvadarśaāt viyadādiprapañco vyavasthitarūpo bhavati saṃdhyāśrayastu prapañcaḥ pratidiaṃ bādhyate ityato vaiśeṣikamidaṃ saṃdhyasya māyāmātratvamuditam parābhidhyāāttu tirohitaṃ tato hyasya badhaviparyayau athāpi syāt
parasyaiva tāvadātmaoṃśaḥ jīvaḥ ageriva visphuliṅgaḥ tatraivaṃ sati yathā agivisphuliṅgayoḥ samāe dahaaprakāśaaśaktī bhavataḥ evaṃ jīveśvarayorapi jñāaiśvaryaśaktī tataśca jīvasya jñāaiśvaryavaśāt sāṃkalpikī svape
rathādisṛṣṭirbhaviṣyatīti atrocyate satyapi jīveśvarayoraṃśāṃśibhāve pratyakṣameva jīvasyeśvaraviparītadharmatvam kiṃ puarjīvasya īśvarasamāadharmatvaṃ āstyeva a āstyeva vidyamāamapi tat tirohitam avidyādivyavadhāāt tatpuastirohitaṃ sat parameśvaramabhidhyāyato yatamāasya
jatorvidhūtadhvātasya timiratiraskṛteva dṛkśaktiḥ auṣadhavīryāt īśvaraprasādāt saṃsiddhasya kasyacidevāvirbhavati a svabhāvata eva sarveṣāṃ jatūām kutaḥ tato hi īśvarāddhetoḥ asya jīvasya badhamokṣau bhavataḥ
īśvarasvarūpāparijñāāt badhaḥ tatsvarūpaparijñāāttu mokṣaḥ tathā ca śrutiḥ jñātvā devaṃ sarvapāśāpahāiḥ kṣīṇaiḥ kleśairjamamṛtyuprahāṇiḥ tasyābhidhyāāttṛtīyaṃ dehabhede viśvaiśvaryaṃ kevala āptakāmaḥ ityevamādyā dehayogādvā sopi
kasmātpuarjīvaḥ paramātmāṃśa eva sa tiraskṛtajñāaiśvaryo bhavati yuktaṃ tu jñāaiśvaryayoratiraskṛtatvam visphuliṅgasyeva dahaaprakāśaayoḥ iti ucyate satyamevaitat sopi tu jīvasya jñāaiśvaryatirobhāvaḥ dehayogāt dehedriyamaobuddhiviṣayavedaādiyogāt
bhavati asti ca atropamā yathā agerdahaaprakāśaasaṃpaasyāpyaraṇigatasya dahaaprakāśae tirohite bhavataḥ yathā vā bhasmacchaasya evamavidyāpratyupasthāpitaāmarūpakṛtadehādyupādhiyogāt tadavivekabhramakṛto jīvasya jñāaiśvaryatirobhāvaḥ vāśabdo jīvasya īśvarāt ayatvaśaṅkāvyāvṛttyarthaḥ
avaya eva jīvaḥ īśvarādastu tiraskṛtajñāaiśvaryatvāt kiṃ dehayogakalpaayā etyucyate a hi ayatvaṃ jīvasya īśvarādupapadyate seyaṃ devataikṣata ityupakramyaaea jīveātmaāupraviśya ityātmaśabdea jīvasya parāmarśāttatsatyaṃ
sa ātmā tattvamasi śvetaketo iti ca jīvāya upadiśati īśvarātmatvam ataḥ aaya eva īśvarājjīvaḥ sa dehayogāttirohitajñāaiśvaryo bhavati ataśca a sāṃkalpikī jīvasya
svape rathādisṛṣṭirghaṭate yadi ca sāṃkalpikī svape rathādisṛṣṭiḥ syāt aivāiṣṭaṃ kaścitsvapaṃ paśyet a hi kaścidaiṣṭaṃ saṃkalpayate yatpuaruktam jāgaritadeśaśrutiḥ svapasya satyatvaṃ khyāpayatīti
a tatsāmyavacaaṃ satyatvābhiprāyam svayaṃjyotiṣṭvavirodhāt śrutyaiva ca svape rathādyabhāvasya darśitatvāt jāgaritaprabhavavāsaāirmitatvāttu svapasya tattulyairbhāsatvābhiprāyaṃ tat tasmādupapaaṃ svapasya māyāmātratvam tadabhāvo āḍīṣu tacchruterātmai ca
tadabhāvādhikaraṇam svapāvasthā parīkṣitā suṣuptāvasthedāīṃ parīkṣyate tatraitāḥ suṣuptaviṣayāḥ śrutayo bhavati kvacic chrūyate tad yatraitat suptaḥ samastaḥ saṃprasaaḥ svapaṃ a vijāātyāsu tadā
āḍīṣu sṛpto bhavati iti ayatra tu āḍīr evāukramya śrūyate tābhiḥ pratyavasṛpya purītati śete iti tathāyatra āḍīr evāukramya tāsu tadā bhavati
yadā suptaḥ svapaṃ a kaṃcaa paśyaty athāsmi prāṇa evaikadhā bhavati iti tathāyatra ya eṣotarhṛdaya ākāśas tasmiñ śete iti tathāyatra satā
somya tadā saṃpao bhavati svamapīto bhavati iti tathā prājñeātmaā saṃpariṣvakto a bāhyaṃ kiṃcaa veda ātaram iti ca tatra saṃśayaḥ kim
etāi āḍyadīi parasparairapekṣatayā bhiāi suṣuptisthāāi āhosvit parasparāpekṣatayā ekaṃ suṣuptisthāam iti kiṃ tāvat prāptam bhiāīti kutaḥ ekārthatvāt a hi ekārthāāṃ kvacit
parasparāpekṣatvaṃ dṛśyate vrīhiyavādīām āḍyādīāṃ ca ekārthatā suṣuptau dṛśyateāḍīṣu sṛpto bhavatipurītati śete iti ca tatra tatra saptamīirdeśasya tulyatvāt au aivaṃ sati
saptamīirdeśo dṛśyate satā somya tadā saṃpao bhavati iti aiṣa doṣaḥ tatrāpi saptamyarthasya gamyamāatvāt vākyaśeṣo hi tatra āyataaiṣī jīvaḥ sat upasarpatītyāha
ayatrāyataamalabdhvā prāṇam evopaśrayate iti prāṇaśabdea tatra prakṛtasya sata upādāāt āyataaṃ ca saptamyarthaḥ saptamīirdeśopi tatra vākyaśeṣe dṛśyate sati saṃpadya a viduḥ
sati saṃpadyāmahe iti sarvatra ca viśeṣavijñāoparamalakṣaṇaṃ suṣuptaṃ a viśiṣyate tasmādekārthatvāt āḍyādīāṃ vikalpea kadācit kiṃcitsthāaṃ svāpāyopasarpati iti evaṃ prāpte pratipādyate tadabhāvo
āḍīṣv ātmai ceti tadabhāva iti tasya prakṛtasya svapadarśaasya abhāvaḥ suṣuptam ity arthaḥ āḍīṣv ātmai ceti samuccayea etāi āḍyādīi svāpāyopasarpati a
vikalpea ity arthaḥ kutaḥ tacchruteḥ tathā hi sarveṣām eva āḍyādīāṃ tatra tatra suṣuptisthāatvaṃ śrūyate tac ca samuccaye saṃgṛhītaṃ bhavati vikalpe
hyeṣām pakṣe bādhaḥ syāt au ekārthatvādvikalpo āḍyādīāṃ vrīhiyavādivat ityuktam etyucyate a hi ekavibhaktiirdeśamātreṇa ekārthatvaṃ vikalpaśca āpatati āārthatvasamuccayayor apy ekavibhaktiirdeśadarśaāt prāsāde
śete paryaṅke śete ityevamādiṣu tathā ihāpi āḍīṣu purītati brahmaṇi ca svapitīti upapadyate samuccayaḥ tathā ca śrutiḥ tāsu tadā bhavati yadā
suptaḥ svapaṃ a kaṃcaa paśyatyathāsmiprāṇa evaikadhā bhavati iti samuccayaṃ āḍīāṃ prāṇasya ca suṣuptau śrāvayati ekavākyopādāāt prāṇasya ca brahmatvaṃ samadhigatam prāṇastathāugamāt
ityatra yatrāpi irapekṣā iva āḍīḥ suṣuptisthāatvea śrāvayati āsu tadā āḍīṣu sṛpto bhavati iti tatrāpi pradeśātaraprasiddhasya brahmaṇopratiṣedhāt āḍīdvāreṇa brahmaṇyevāvatiṣṭhata iti pratīyate
a caivamapi āḍīṣu saptamī virudhyate āḍībhirapi brahmopasarpa sṛpta eva āḍīṣu bhavati yo hi gaṅgayā sāgaraṃ gacchati gata eva sa gaṅgāyāṃ
bhavati bhavati ca atra raśmiāḍīdvārātmakasya brahmalokamārgasya vivakṣitatvāt āḍīstutyarthaṃ sṛptisaṃkīrtaam āḍīṣu sṛpto bhavati ityuktvātaṃ a kaścaa pāpmā spṛśati iti bruva āḍīḥ
praśaṃsati bravīti ca pāpmasparśābhāve hetumtejasā hi tadā saṃpao bhavati iti tejasā āḍīgatea pittākhyea abhivyāptakaraṇo a bāhyā viṣayāīkṣata ityarthaḥ athavā tejaseti
brahmaṇa evāyaṃ irdeśaḥ śrutyatarebrahmaiva teja eva iti tejaḥśabdasya brahmaṇi prayuktatvāt brahmaṇā hi tadā saṃpao bhavati āḍīdvāreṇa atas taṃ a kaścaa
pāpmā spṛśatīty arthaḥ brahmasaṃpattiśca pāpmasparśābhāve hetuḥ samadhigataḥsarve pāpmāoto ivartatepahatapāpmā hyeṣa brahmalokaḥ ityādiśrutibhyaḥ evaṃ ca sati pradeśātaraprasiddhea brahmaṇā suṣuptisthāeāugato āḍīāṃ samuccayaḥ
samadhigato bhavati tathā purītatopi brahmaprakriyāyāṃ saṃkīrtaāt tadauguṇameva suṣuptisthāatvaṃ jñāyate ya eṣotarhṛdaya ākāśastasmiñśete iti hṛdayākāśe suṣuptisthāe prakṛte idamucyate purītati śete iti
purītaditi hṛdayapariveṣṭaamucyate tadatarvartiyapi hṛdayākāśe śayāaḥ śakyatepurītati śete iti vaktum prākāraparikṣiptepi hi pure vartamāaḥ prākāre vartata ityucyate hṛdayākāśasya ca brahmatvaṃ samadhigatamdahara
uttarebhyaḥ ityatra tathā āḍīpurītatsamuccayopitābhiḥ pratyavasṛpya purītati śete ityekavākyopādāāt avagamyate satprājñayośca prasiddhameva brahmatvam evametāsu śrutiṣu trīṇyeva suṣuptisthāāi saṃkīrtitāi āḍyaḥ purītat brahma
ceti tatrāpi dvāramātraṃ āḍyaḥ purītacca brahmaiva tu ekam aapāyi suṣuptisthāam api ca āḍyaḥ purītadvā jīvasyopādhyādhāra eva bhavati tatrāsya karaṇāi vartata
iti a hi upādhisaṃbadhamatareṇa svata eva jīvasyādhāraḥ kaścitsaṃbhavati brahmāvyatirekeṇa svamahimapratiṣṭhitatvāt brahmādhāratvam apy asya suṣupte aiva ādhārādheyabhedābhiprāyeṇa ucyate kathaṃ tarhi tādātmyābhiprāyeṇa
yata āha satā somya tadā saṃpao bhavati svamapīto bhavati iti svaśabdea ātmā abhilapyate svarūpamāpaaḥ supto bhavatītyarthaḥ api ca a kadācijjīvasya
brahmaṇā saṃpattirāsti svarūpasyāapāyitvāt svapajāgaritayostūpādhisaṃparkavaśāt pararūpāpattimivāpekṣya tadupaśamātsuṣupteḥ svarūpāpattirvivakṣyate svam apīto bhavati iti ataś ca suptāvasthāyāṃ kadācit satā saṃpadyate kadācia saṃpadyate ityayuktam
api ca sthāavikalpābhyupagamepi viśeṣavijñāopaśamalakṣaṇaṃ tāvatsuṣuptaṃ a kvacidviśiṣyate tatra sati saṃpaastāvat ekatvāt a vijāātīti yuktamtatkea kaṃ vijāīyāt iti śruteḥ āḍīṣu purītati
ca śayāasya a kiṃcit avijñāe kāraṇaṃ śakyaṃ vijñātum bhedaviṣayatvātyatra vā ayadiva syāttatrāyoyatpaśyet iti śruteḥ au bhedaviṣayasyāpyatidūrādikāraṇamavijñāe syāt bāḍhamevaṃ syāt yadi
jīvaḥ svataḥ paricchiobhyupagamyeta yathā viṣṇumitraḥ pravāsī svagṛhā a paśyatīti a tu jīvasyopādhivyatirekeṇa paricchedo vidyate upādhigatamevātidūrādikāraṇam avijñāe iti yadyucyeta tathāpyupādherupaśātatvāt satyeva
saṃpaaḥ a vijāātīti yuktam a ca vayamiha tulyavat āḍyādisamuccayaṃ pratipādayāmaḥ a hi āḍyaḥ suptisthāaṃ purītacca ityaea vijñāea kiṃcitprayojaamasti a hyetadvijñāapratibaddhaṃ
kiṃcitphalaṃ śrūyate āpyetadvijñāaṃ phalavataḥ kasyacidaṅgamupadiśyate brahma tu aapāyi suptisthāam ityetatpratipādayāmaḥ tea tu vijñāea prayojaamasti jīvasya brahmātmatvāvadhāraṇaṃ svapajāgaritavyavahāravimuktatvāvadhāraṇaṃ ca tasmādātmaiva suptisthāam
ataḥ prabodhosmāt yasmācca ātmaiva suptisthāam ata eva ca kāraṇāt ityavadeva asmādātmaaḥ prabodhaḥ svāpādhikāre śiṣyatekuta etadāgāt ityasya praśasya prativacaāvasare yathāgeḥ kṣudrā
visphuliṅgā vyuccaratyevamevāsmādātmaaḥ sarve prāṇāḥ ityādiāsata āgamya a viduḥ sata āgacchāmahe iti ca vikalpyamāeṣu tu suṣuptisthāeṣu kadāciāḍībhyaḥ pratibudhyate kadācitpurītataḥ kadācidātmaaḥ ityaśāsiṣyat
tasmādapyātmaiva suptisthāamiti sa eva tu karmāusmṛtiśabdavidhibhyaḥ karmāusmṛtiśabdavidhyadhikaraṇam tasyāḥ puaḥ satsaṃpatteḥ pratibudhyamāaḥ kiṃ ya eva satsaṃpaaḥ sa eva pratibudhyate uta sa
vā ayo vā iti cityate tatra prāptaṃ tāvat aiyama iti kutaḥ yadā hi jalarāśau kaścijjalabiduḥ prakṣipyate jalarāśireva sa tadā bhavati
puaruddharaṇe ca sa eva jalabidurbhavati iti duḥsaṃpādam tadvat suptaḥ pareṇaikatvamāpaaḥ saṃprasīdatīti a sa eva puarutthātumarhati tasmāt sa eva īśvaro vā
ayo vā jīvaḥ pratibudhyate iti evaṃ prāpte idamāha sa eva tu jīvaḥ suptaḥ svāsthyaṃ gataḥ puaruttiṣṭhati āyaḥ kasmāt karmāusmṛtiśabdavidhibhyaḥ vibhajya
hetuṃ darśayiṣyāmi karmaśeṣāuṣṭhāadarśaāttāvatsa evotthātumarhati āyaḥ tathā hi pūrvedyurauṣṭhitasya karmaṇaḥ aparedyuḥ śeṣamautiṣṭhadṛśyate a cāyea sāmikṛtasya karmaṇaḥ ayaḥ śeṣakriyāyāṃ pravartitumutsahate atiprasaṅgāt tasmādeka
eva pūrvedyuraparedyuśca ekasya karmaṇaḥ karteti gamyate itaśca sa evottiṣṭhati yatkāraṇam atītehai ahamadodrākṣamiti pūrvāubhūtasya paścātsmaraṇam ayasyotthāe opapadyate a hyayadṛṣṭam ayousmartumarhati sohamasmīti
ca ātmāusmaraṇamātmātarotthāe āvakalpate śabdebhyaśca tasyaivotthāamavagamyate tathā hi puaḥ pratiyāyaṃ pratiyoyādravati buddhātāyaivaimāḥ sarvāḥ prajā aharahargacchatya etaṃ brahmalokaṃ a vidatita iha vyāghro
vā siṃho vā vṛko vā varāho vā kīṭo vā pataṅgo vā daṃśo vā maśako vā yadyadbhavati tadābhavati ityevamādayaḥ śabdāḥ svāpaprabodhādhikārapaṭhitā
a ātmātarotthāe sāmañjasyam īyuḥ karmavidyāvidhibhyaścaivamevāvagamyate ayathā hi karmavidyāvidhayoarthakāḥ syuḥ ayotthāapakṣe hi suptamātro mucyata ityāpadyeta evaṃ cetsyāt vada kiṃ kālātaraphalea karmaṇā
vidyayā vā kṛtaṃ syāt api ca ayotthāapakṣe yadi tāvaccharīrātare vyavaharamāṇo jīva uttiṣṭhet tatratyavyavahāralopaprasaṅgaḥ syāt atha tatra supta uttiṣṭhet kalpaāarthakyaṃ syāt
yo hi yasmi śarīre suptaḥ saḥ tasmi ottiṣṭhati ayasmi śarīre suptaḥ ayasmiuttiṣṭhatīti kosyāṃ kalpaāyāṃ lābhaḥ syāt atha mukta uttiṣṭhet atavāmokṣa
āpadyeta ivṛttāvidyasya ca puarutthāamaupapaam etea īśvarasyotthāaṃ pratyuktam ityaivṛttāvidyatvāt akṛtābhyāgamakṛtavipraṇāśau ca durivārāvayotthāapakṣe syātām tasmātsa evottiṣṭhati āya iti yatpuaruktam yathā jalarāśau prakṣipto
jalabiduroddhartuṃ śakyate evaṃ sati saṃpao jīvo otpatitumarhatīti tatparihriyate yuktaṃ tatra vivekakāraṇābhāvāt jalabidorauddharaṇam iha tu vidyate vivekakāraṇam karma ca avidyā ca
iti vaiṣamyam dṛśyate ca durvivecayorapyasmajjātīyaiḥ kṣīrodakayoḥ saṃsṛṣṭayoḥ haṃsea vivecaam api ca a jīvo āma kaścitparasmādayo vidyate yo jalabiduriva jalarāśeḥ sato
vivicyeta sadeva tu upādhisaṃparkājjīva ityupacaryate ityasakṛtprapañcitam evaṃ sati yāvadekopādhigatā badhāuvṛttiḥ tāvadekajīvavyavahāraḥ upādhyataragatāyāṃ tu badhāuvṛttau jīvātaravyavahāraḥ sa evāyamupādhiḥ svāpaprabodhayoḥ bījāṅkurayāyea ityataḥ
sa eva jīvaḥ pratibudhyata iti yuktam mugdhe rdhasampattiḥ pariśeṣāt mugdhādhikaraṇam asti mugdho āma yaṃ mūrchita iti laukikāḥ kathayati sa tu
kimavastha iti parīkṣāyām ucyate tisras tāvad avasthāḥ śarīrasthasya jīvasya prasiddhāḥ jāgaritaṃ svapaḥ suṣuptam iti caturthī śarīrād apasṛptiḥ a tu pañcamī
kācid avasthā jīvasya śrutau smṛtau vā prasiddhā asti tasmāc catasṛṇām evāvasthāām ayatamāvasthā mūrchā iti evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ a tāva mugdho
jāgaritāvastho bhavitum arhati a hy ayam idriyair viṣayā īkṣate syād etat iṣukārayāyea mugdho bhaviṣyati yathā iṣukāro jāgrad api iṣvāsaktamaastayā āyā
viṣayā īkṣate evaṃ mugdho musalasaṃpātādijaitaduḥkhāubhavavyagramaastayā jāgrad api āyā viṣayā īkṣata iti a acetayamāatvāt iṣukāro hi vyāpṛtamaā bravīti iṣum evāham etāvataṃ
kālam upalabhamāo bhūvam iti mugdhas tu labdhasaṃjño bravīti adhe tamasy aham etāvataṃ kālaṃ prakṣipto bhūvam a kiṃci mayā cetitam iti
jāgrataś caikaviṣayaviṣaktacetaso pi deho vidhriyate mugdhasya tu deho dharaṇyāṃ patati tasmā a jāgarti āpi svapā paśyati iḥsaṃjñakatvāt āpi mṛtaḥ prāṇoṣmaṇorbhāvāt
mugdhe hi jatau mṛtoyaṃ syāa vā mṛta iti saṃśayāāḥ ūṣmāsti āstīti hṛdayadeśamālabhate iścayārtham prāṇosti āstīti ca āsikādeśam yadi prāṇoṣmaṇorastitvaṃ āvagacchati
tato mṛtoyamityadhyavasāya dahaāyāraṇyaṃ ayati atha tu prāṇamūṣmāṇaṃ vā pratipadyate tato āyaṃ mṛta ityadhyavasāya saṃjñālābhāya bhiṣajyati puarutthāācca a diṣṭaṃ gataḥ a
hi yamaṃ gataḥ yamarāṣṭrātpratyāgacchati astu tarhi suṣuptaḥ iḥsaṃjñatvāt amṛtatvācca a vailakṣaṇyāt mugdhaḥ kadācicciramapi occhvasiti savepathurasya deho bhavati bhayāakaṃ ca vadaam
visphārite etre suṣuptastu prasaavadaastulyakālaṃ puaḥ puarucchvasiti imīlite asya etre bhavataḥ a cāsya deho vepate pāṇipeṣaṇamātreṇa ca suṣuptamutthāpayati a tu mugdhaṃ
mudgaraghāteāpi imittabhedaśca bhavati mohasvāpayoḥ musalasaṃpātādiimittatvāmohasya śramaimittatvācca svāpasya a ca lokesti prasiddhiḥ mugdhaḥ supta iti pariśeṣādardhasaṃpattirmugdhatetyavagacchāmaḥ iḥsaṃjñatvāt saṃpaaḥ itarasmācca vailakṣaṇyādasaṃpaaḥ iti
kathaṃ puarardhasaṃpattirmugdhateti śakyate vaktum yāvatā suptaṃ prati tāvaduktaṃ śrutyā satā somya tadā saṃpao bhavati itiatra steosteo bhavatiaitaṃ setumahorātre tarato a
jarā a mṛtyura śoko a sukṛtaṃ a duṣkṛtam ityādi jīve hi sukṛtaduṣkṛtayoḥ prāptiḥ sukhitvaduḥkhitvapratyayotpādaea bhavati a ca sukhitvapratyayo duḥkhitvapratyayo vā
suṣupte vidyate mugdhepi tau pratyayau aiva vidyete tasmāt upādhyupaśamāt suṣuptavamugdhepi kṛtsasaṃpattireva bhavitumarhati ārdhasaṃpattiriti atrocyate a brūmaḥ mugdherdhasaṃpattirjīvasya brahmaṇā bhavatīti kiṃ
tarhi ardhea suṣuptapakṣasya bhavati mugdhatvam ardheāvasthātarapakṣasya iti brūmaḥ darśite ca mohasya svāpea sāmyavaiṣamye dvāraṃ caitat maraṇasya yadāsya sāvaśeṣaṃ karma bhavati
tadā vāṅmaase pratyāgacchataḥ yadā tu iravaśeṣaṃ karma bhavati tadā prāṇoṣmāṇāvapagacchataḥ tasmād ardhasaṃpattiṃ brahmavida icchati yat tūktam a pañcamī kācidavasthā prasiddhāstīti
aiṣa doṣaḥ kādācitkīyamavastheti a prasiddhā syāt prasiddhā caiṣā lokāyurvedayoḥ ardhasaṃpattyabhyupagamācca a pañcamī gaṇyata ityaavadyam a sthāatopi parasyobhayaliṅgaṃ sarvatra hi ubhayaliṅgādhikaraṇam
yea brahmaṇā suṣuptyādiṣu jīva upādhyupaśamātsaṃpadyate tasyedāīṃ svarūpaṃ śrutivaśea irdhāryate satyubhayaliṅgāḥ śrutayo brahmaviṣayāḥ sarvakarmā sarvakāmaḥ sarvagadhaḥ sarvarasaḥ ityevamādyāḥ saviśeṣaliṅgāḥasthūlamaaṇvahrasvamadīrgham ityevamādyāśca irviśeṣaliṅgāḥ
kimāsu śrutiṣu ubhayaliṅgaṃ brahma pratipattavyam uttāyataraliṅgam yadāpyayataraliṅgam tadāpi saviśeṣam uta irviśeṣam iti mīmāṃsyate tatra ubhayaliṅgaśrutyaugrahāt ubhayaliṅgameva brahma ityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ
a tāvatsvata eva parasya brahmaṇa ubhayaliṅgatvamupapadyate a hi ekaṃ vastu svata eva rūpādiviśeṣopetaṃ tadviparītaṃ ca ityavadhārayituṃ śakyam virodhāt astu tarhi
sthāataḥ pṛthivyādyupādhiyogāditi tadapi opapadyate a hi upādhiyogādapyayādṛśasya vastuoyādṛśaḥ svabhāvaḥ saṃbhavati a hi svacchaḥ sa sphaṭikaḥ alaktakādyupādhiyogādasvaccho bhavati bhramamātratvādasvacchatābhiiveśasya upādhīāṃ ca
avidyāpratyupasthāpitatvāt ataśca ayataraliṅgaparigrahepi samastaviśeṣarahitaṃ irvikalpakameva brahma pratipattavyam a tadviparītam sarvatra hi brahmasvarūpapratipādaapareṣu vākyeṣuaśabdamasparśamarūpamavyayam ityevamādiṣu apāstasamastaviśeṣameva brahma upadiśyate a bhedāditi cea
pratyekamatadvacaāt athāpi syāt yaduktam irvikalpamekaliṅgameva brahma āsya svataḥ sthāato vā ubhayaliṅgatvamastīti taopapadyate kasmāt bhedāt bhiā hi pratividyaṃ brahmaṇa ākārā upadiśyate
catuṣpāt brahma ṣoḍaśakalaṃ brahma vāmaītvādilakṣaṇaṃ brahma trailokyaśarīravaiśvāaraśabdoditaṃ brahma ityevaṃjātīyakāḥ tasmāt saviśeṣatvamapi brahmaṇobhyupagatavyam au uktaṃ obhayaliṅgatvaṃ brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhavatīti ayamapyavirodhaḥ upādhikṛtatvādākārabhedasya ayathā
hi irviṣayameva bhedaśāstraṃ prasajyeta iti cet eti brūmaḥ kasmāt pratyekamatadvacaāt pratyupādhibhedaṃ hi abhedameva brahmaṇaḥ śrāvayati śāstram yaścāyamasyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ tejomayomṛtamayaḥ puruṣo
yaścāyamadhyātmaṃ śārīrastejomayomṛtamayaḥ puruṣoyameva sa yoyamātmā ityādi ataśca a bhiākārayogo brahmaṇaḥ śāstrīya iti śakyate vaktum bhedasya upāsaārthatvāt abhede tātparyāt api caivameke
api caivaṃ bhedadarśaaidāpūrvakam abhedadarśaameva eke śākhiaḥ samāmaati maasaivedamāptavyaṃ eha āāsti kiṃcaa mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyumāpoti ya iha āeva paśyati iti tathāyepi
bhoktā bhogyaṃ preritāraṃ ca matvā sarvaṃ proktaṃ trividhaṃ brahma me tat iti samastasya bhogyabhoktṛiyatṛlakṣaṇasya prapañcasya brahmaikasvabhāvatāmadhīyate kathaṃ puaḥ ākāravadupadeśiīṣu aākāropadeśiīṣu
ca brahmaviṣayāsu śrutiṣu satīṣu aākārameva brahma avadhāryate a puarviparītam ityata uttaraṃ paṭhati arūpavadeva hi tatpradhāatvāt rūpādyākārarahitameva hi brahma avadhārayitavyam a
rūpādimat kasmāt tatpradhāatvātasthūlamaaṇvahrasvamadīrghamaśabdamasparśamarūpamavyayamākāśo vai āma āmarūpayorirvahitā te yadatarā tadbrahmadivyo hyamūrtaḥ puruṣaḥ sabāhyābhyataro hyajaḥtadetadbrahmāpūrvamaaparamaataramabāhyamayamātmā brahma sarvāubhūḥ ityevamādīi vākyāi iṣprapañcabrahmātmatattvapradhāāi a arthātarapradhāāi
ityetatpratiṣṭhāpitamtattu samavayāt ityatra tasmādevaṃjātīyakeṣu vākyeṣu yathāśrutaṃ irākārameva brahma avadhārayitavyam itarāṇi tu ākāravadbrahmaviṣayāṇi vākyāi a tatpradhāāi upāsaāvidhipradhāāi hi tāi teṣvasati virodhe
yathāśrutamāśrayitavyam sati tu virodhe tatpradhāāi atatpradhāebhyo balīyāṃsi bhavati ityeṣa viigamaāyāṃ hetuḥ yea ubhayīṣvapi śrutiṣu satīṣu aākārameva brahma avadhāryate a puarviparītamiti
kā tarhyākāravadviṣayāṇāṃ śrutīāṃ gatiḥ ityata āha prakāśavaccāvaiyarthyāt yathā prakāśaḥ sauraścādramaso vā viyadvyāpya avatiṣṭhamāaḥ aṅgulyādyupādhisaṃbadhāt teṣu ṛjuvakrādibhāvaṃ pratipadyamāeṣu tadbhāvamiva pratipadyate evaṃ
brahmāpi pṛthivyādyupādhisaṃbadhāt tadākāratāmiva pratipadyate tadālambao brahmaṇa ākāraviśeṣopadeśa upāsaārtho a virudhyate evam avaiyarthyam ākāravadbrahmaviṣayāṇāmapi vākyāāṃ bhaviṣyati a hi vedavākyāāṃ kasyacidarthavattvam kasyacidaarthavattvamiti
yuktaṃ pratipattum pramāṇatvāviśeṣāt avevamapi yatpurastātpratijñātam opādhiyogādapyubhayaliṅgatvaṃ brahmaṇostīti tadvirudhyate eti brūmaḥ upādhiimittasya vastudharmatvāupapatteḥ upādhīāṃ ca avidyāpratyupasthāpitatvāt satyāmeva ca aisargikyāmavidyāyāṃ lokavedavyavahārāvatāra iti
tatra tatra avocāma āha ca tamātram āha ca śrutiḥ caitayamātraṃ vilakṣaṇarūpātararahitaṃ irviśeṣaṃ brahma sa yathā saidhavaghaoatarobāhyaḥ kṛtso rasaghaa evaivaṃ vā
areyamātmāatarobāhyaḥ kṛtsaḥ prajñāaghaa eva iti etaduktaṃ bhavati āsya ātmaotarbahirvā caitayādayadrūpamasti caitayameva tu irataramasya svarūpam yathā saidhavaghaasyātarbahiśca lavaṇarasa eva irataro bhavati
a rasātaram tathaiveti darśayati cātho api smaryate darśayati ca śrutiḥ pararūpapratiṣedheaiva brahma irviśeṣatvāt athāta ādeśo eti etiayadeva tadviditādatho aviditādadhiyato vāco
ivartate aprāpya maasā saha ityevamādyā bāṣkaliā ca bādhvaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ sa avacaeaiva brahma provāceti śrūyate sa hovācādhīhi bho iti sa tūṣṇīṃ
babhūva taṃ ha dvitīye tṛtīye vā vacaa uvāca brūmaḥ khalu tvaṃ tu a vijāāsi upaśātoyamātmā iti tathā smṛtiṣvapi parapratiṣedheaivopadiśyate jñeyaṃ
yattatpravakṣyāmi yajjñātvāmṛtamaśute aādimatparaṃ brahma a sattaāsaducyate ityevamādyāsu tathā viśvarūpadharo ārāyaṇo āradamuvāceti smaryate māyā hyeṣā mayā sṛṣṭā yamāṃ paśyasi ārada sarvabhūtaguṇairyuktaṃ
aivaṃ māṃ jñātumarhasi iti ata eva copamā sūryakādivat yata eva ca ayamātmā caitayarūpo irviśeṣo vāṅmaasātītaḥ parapratiṣedhopadeśyaḥ ata eva ca asyopādhiimittāmapāramārthikīṃ
viśeṣavattāmabhipretya jalasūryakādivadityupamā upādīyate mokṣaśāstreṣu yathā hyayaṃ jyotirātmā vivasvāapo bhiā bahudhaikougaccha upādhiā kriyate bhedarūpo devaḥ kṣetreṣvevamajoyamātmā itieka eva hi bhūtātmā bhūte
bhūte vyavasthitaḥ ekadhā bahudhā caiva dṛśyate jalacadravat iti caivamādiṣu atra pratyavasthīyate ambuvadagrahaṇāttu a tathātvam a jalasūryakāditulyatvamihopapadyate tadvadagrahaṇāt sūryādibhyo hi mūrtebhyaḥ
pṛthagbhūtaṃ viprakṛṣṭadeśaṃ mūrtaṃ jalaṃ gṛhyate tatra yuktaḥ sūryādipratibimbodayaḥ a tu ātmā mūrtaḥ a cāsmātpṛthagbhūtā viprakṛṣṭadeśāścopādhayaḥ sarvagatatvāt sarvāayatvācca tasmādayuktoyaṃ dṛṣṭāta iti
atra pratividhīyate vṛddhihrāsabhāktvamatarbhāvādubhayasāmañjasyādevam yukta eva tu ayaṃ dṛṣṭātaḥ vivakṣitāṃśasaṃbhavāt a hi dṛṣṭātadārṣṭātikayoḥ kvacit kaṃcit vivakṣitamaṃśaṃ muktvā sarvasārūpyaṃ keacit darśayituṃ śakyate
sarvasārūpye hi dṛ darśaācca darśayati ca śrutiḥ parasyaiva brahmaṇo dehādiṣūpādhiṣvataraupraveśam puraścakre dvipadaḥ puraścakre catuṣpadaḥ puraḥ sa pakṣī bhūtvā puraḥ puruṣa
āviśat itiaea jīveātmaāupraviśya iti ca tasmādyuktametatata eva copamā sūryakādivat iti tasmāt irvikalpakaikaliṅgameva brahma a ubhayaliṅgaṃ viparītaliṅgaṃ vā iti siddham atra
kecit dve adhikaraṇe kalpayati prathamaṃ tāvat kiṃ pratyastamitāśeṣaprapañcamekākāraṃ brahma uta prapañcavadaekākāropetamiti dvitīyaṃ tu pratyastamitaprapañcatve kiṃ sallakṣaṇaṃ brahma uta bodhalakṣaṇam uta
ubhayalakṣaṇamiti atra vayaṃ vadāmaḥ sarvathāpyāarthakyamadhikaraṇātarārambhasyeti yadi tāvadaekaliṅgatvaṃ parasya brahmaṇo irākartavyamityayaṃ prayāsaḥ tat pūrveṇaivaa sthāatopi ityaeādhikaraṇea irākṛtamiti uttaramadhikaraṇamprakāśavacca ityetadvyarthameva bhavet a
ca sallakṣaṇameva brahma a bodhalakṣaṇam iti śakyaṃ vaktumvijñāaghaa eva ityādiśrutivaiyarthyaprasaṅgāt kathaṃ vā irastacaitayaṃ brahma cetaasya jīvasyātmatveopadiśyeta āpi bodhalakṣaṇameva brahma a
sallakṣaṇam iti śakyaṃ vaktumastītyevopalabdhavyaḥ ityādiśrutivaiyarthyaprasaṅgāt kathaṃ vā irastasattāko bodhobhyupagamyeta āpyubhayalakṣaṇameva brahma iti śakyaṃ vaktum pūrvābhyupagamavirodhaprasaṅgāt sattāvyāvṛttea ca bodhea bodhavyāvṛttayā ca
sattayā upetaṃ brahma pratijāāasya tadeva pūrvādhikaraṇapratiṣiddhaṃ saprapañcatvaṃ prasajyeta śrutatvādadoṣa iti cet a ekasya aekasvabhāvatvāupapatteḥ atha sattaiṣa bodhaḥ bodha eva ca
sattā āayoḥ parasparavyāvṛttirastīti yadyucyeta tathāpi kiṃ sallakṣaṇaṃ brahma uta bodhalakṣaṇam utobhayalakṣaṇam ityayaṃ vikalpo irālambaa eva syāt sūtrāṇi tvekādhikaraṇatveaivāsmābhirītāi api ca
brahmaviṣayāsu śrutiṣu ākāravadaākārapratipādaea vipratipaāsu aākāre brahmaṇi parigṛhīte avaśyaṃ vaktavyā itarāsāṃ śrutīāṃ gatiḥ tādarthyeaprakāśavacca ityādīi sūtrāṇyarthavattarāṇi saṃpadyate yadapyāhuḥ ākāravādiyopi śrutayaḥ prapañcavilayamukhea
aākārapratipattyarthā eva a pṛthagarthā iti tadapi a samīcīamiva lakṣyate katham ye hi paravidyādhikāre kecitprapañcā ucyate yathā yuktā hyasya harayaḥ śatā
daśeti ayaṃ vai harayoyaṃ vai daśa ca sahasrāṇi bahūi cāatāi ca ityevamādayaḥ te bhavatu pravilayārthāḥtadetadbrahmāpūrvamaaparamaataramabāhyam ityupasaṃhārāt ye puarupāsaāvidhāādhikāre prapañcā ucyate
yathā maomayaḥ prāṇaśarīro bhārūpaḥ ityevamādayaḥ a teṣāṃ pravilayārthatvaṃ yāyyamsa kratuṃ kurvīta ityevaṃjātīyakea prakṛteaiva upāsaavidhiā teṣāṃ saṃbadhāt śrutyā ca evaṃjātīyakāāṃ guṇāāmupāsaārthatvevakalpamāe
a lakṣaṇayā pravilayārthatvamavakalpate sarveṣāṃ ca sādhāraṇe pravilayārthatve satiarūpavadeva hi tatpradhāatvāt iti viigamaakāraṇavacaam aavakāśaṃ syāt phalamapyeṣāṃ yathopadeśaṃ kvacidduritakṣayaḥ kvacidaiśvairyaprāptiḥ kvacitkramamuktirityavagamyata eva
ityataḥ pārthagarthyameva upāsaāvākyāāṃ brahmavākyāāṃ ca yāyyam a ekavākyatvam kathaṃ ca eṣāmekavākyatotprekṣyata iti vaktavyam ekaiyogapratīteḥ prayājadarśapūrṇamāsavākyavaditi cet a brahmavākyeṣu iyogābhāvāt vastumātraparyavasāyīi
hi brahmavākyāi a iyogopadeśīi ityetadvistareṇa pratiṣṭhāpitamtattu samavayāt ityatra kiṃviṣayaścātra iyogobhipreyata iti vaktavyam puruṣo hi iyujyamāaḥkuru iti svavyāpāre kasmiṃściiyujyate au dvaitaprapañcapravilayo
iyogaviṣayo bhaviṣyati apravilāpite hi dvaitaprapañce brahmatattvābodho a bhavatītyato brahmatattvāvabodhapratyaīkabhūto dvaitaprapañcaḥ pravilāpyaḥ yathā svargakāmasya yāgouṣṭhātavya upadiśyate evamapavargakāmasya prapañcapravilayaḥ yathā ca tamasi
vyavasthitaṃ ghaṭāditattvamavabubhutsamāea tatpratyaīkabhūtaṃ tamaḥ pravilāpyate evaṃ brahmatattvamavabubhutsamāea tatpratyaīkabhūtaḥ prapañcaḥ pravilāpayitavyaḥ brahmasvabhāvo hi prapañcaḥ a prapañcasvabhāvaṃ brahma tea āmarūpaprapañcapravilāpaea brahmatattvāvabodho bhavati
iti atra vayaṃ pṛcchāmaḥ koyaṃ prapañcapravilayo āma kimagipratāpasaṃparkāt ghṛtakāṭhiyapravilaya iva prapañcapravilayaḥ kartavyaḥ āhosvidekasmiṃścadre timirakṛtāekacadraprapañcavat avidyākṛto brahmaṇi āmarūpaprapañco vidyayā pravilāpayitavyaḥ iti
tatra yadi tāvadvidyamāoyaṃ prapañcaḥ dehādilakṣaṇa ādhyātmikaḥ bāhyaśca pṛthivyādilakṣaṇaḥ pravilāpayitavya ityucyeta sa puruṣamātreṇāśakyaḥ pravilāpayitumiti tatpravilayopadeśośakyaviṣaya eva syāt ekea ca ādimuktea pṛthivyādipravilayaḥ
kṛta iti idāīṃ pṛthivyādiśūyaṃ jagadabhaviṣyat atha avidyādhyasto brahmaṇyekasmi ayaṃ prapañco vidyayā pravilāpyata iti brūyāt tato brahmaiva avidyādhyastaprapañcapratyākhyāea āvedayitavyam ekamevādvitīyaṃ brahmatatsatyaṃ
sa ātmā tattvamasi iti tasmiāvedite vidyā svayamevotpadyate tayā ca avidyā bādhyate tataśca avidyādhyastaḥ sakaloyaṃ āmarūpaprapañcaḥ svapaprapañcavat pravilīyate aāvedite tu brahmaṇibrahmavijñāaṃ
kuru prapañcapravilayaṃ ca iti śatakṛtvopyukte a brahmavijñāaṃ prapañcapravilayo vā jāyeta avāvedite brahmaṇi tadvijñāaviṣayaḥ prapañcavilayaviṣayo vā iyogaḥ syāt a iṣprapañcabrahmātmatvāvedaeaiva ubhayasiddheḥ
rajjusvarūpaprakāśaeaiva hi tatsvarūpavijñāam avidyādhyastasarpādiprapañcapravilayaśca bhavati a ca kṛtameva puaḥ kriyate iyojyopi ca prapañcāvasthāyāṃ yovagamyate jīvo āma sa prapañcapakṣasyaiva vā syāt
brahmapakṣasyaiva vā prathame vikalpe iṣprapañcabrahmatattvapratipādaea pṛthivyādivat jīvasyāpi pravilāpitatvāt kasya prapañcavilaye iyoga ucyeta kasya vā iyogaiṣṭhatayā mokṣovāptavya ucyeta dvitīyepi brahmaiva aiyojyasvabhāvaṃ
jīvasya svarūpam jīvatvaṃ tu avidyākṛtameva iti pratipādite brahmaṇi iyojyābhāvāt iyogābhāva eva draṣṭavyādiśabdā api paravidyādhikārapaṭhitāḥ tattvābhimukhīkaraṇapradhāāḥ a tattvāvabodhavidhipradhāā bhavati lokepi idaṃ
paśya idamākarṇayeti ca evaṃjātīyakeṣu irdeśeṣu praṇidhāamātraṃ kurvityucyate a sākṣājjñāameva kurviti jñeyābhimukhasyāpi jñāaṃ kadācijjāyate kadācia jāyate tasmāt taṃ prati jñāaviṣaya eva
darśayitavyo jñāpayitukāmea tasmidarśite svayameva yathāviṣayaṃ yathāpramāṇaṃ ca jñāamutpadyate a ca pramāṇātareṇa ayathāprasiddherthe ayathājñāaṃ iyuktasyāpyupapadyate yadi puariyuktohamiti ayathā jñāaṃ kuryāt a
tu tat jñāam kiṃ tarhi māasī sā kriyā svayameva cedayathotpadyeta bhrātireva syāt jñāaṃ tu pramāṇajayaṃ yathābhūtaviṣayaṃ ca a tat iyogaśateāpi
kārayituṃ śakyate a ca pratiṣedhaśateāpi vārayituṃ śakyate a hi tat puruṣatatram vastutatrameva hi tat atopi iyogābhāvaḥ kiṃcāyat iyogaiṣṭhatayaiva paryavasyatyāmāye yadabhyupagatam
aiyojyabrahmātmatvaṃ jīvasya tat apramāṇakameva syāt atha śāstrameva aiyojyabrahmātmatvamācakṣīta tadavabodhe ca puruṣaṃ iyuñjīta tato brahmaśāstrasyaikasya dvyarthaparatā viruddhārthaparatā ca prasajyeyātām iyogaparatāyāṃ ca
śrutahāiḥ aśrutakalpaā karmaphalavamokṣasyādṛṣṭaphalatvam aityatvaṃ ca ityevamādayo doṣā a keacitparihartuṃ śakyāḥ tasmādavagatiiṣṭhāy eva brahmavākyāi a iyogaiṣṭhāi ataś ca ekaiyogapratīter ekavākyatety ayuktam
abhyupagamyamāepi ca brahmavākyeṣu iyogasadbhāve tadekatvaṃ iṣprapañcopadeśeṣu saprapañcopadeśeṣu ca asiddham a hi śabdātarādibhiḥ pramāṇairiyogabhedevagamyamāe sarvatra eko iyoga iti śakyamāśrayitum prayājadarśapūrṇamāsavākyeṣu tu
adhikārāṃśeābhedāt yuktamekatvam a tviha saguṇairguṇacodaāsu kaścidekatvakaroṃśosti a hi bhārūpatvādayo guṇāḥ prapañcapravilayopakāriṇaḥ āpi prapañcavilayo bhārūpatvādiguṇopakārī parasparavirodhitvāt a hi kṛtsaprapañcapravilāpaaṃ prapañcaikadeśāpekṣaṇaṃ ca
ekasmidharmiṇi yuktaṃ samāveśayitum tasmāt asmadukta eva vibhāgaḥ ākāravadaākāropadeśāāṃ yuktatara iti prakṛtaitāvattvaṃ hi pratiṣedhati tato bravīti ca bhūyaḥ prakṛtaitāvattvādhikaraṇam dve vāva
brahmaṇo rūpe mūrtaṃ caivāmūrtaṃ ca ityupakramya pañcamahābhūtāi dvairāśyea pravibhajya amūrtarasasya ca puruṣaśabdoditasya māhārajaādīi rūpāṇi darśayitvā puaḥ paṭhyate athāta ādeśo eti
eti a hyetasmāditi etyayatparamasti iti tatra kosya pratiṣedhasya viṣaya iti jijñāsāmahe a hyatra idaṃ taditi viśeṣitaṃ kiṃcitpratiṣedhyamupalabhyate itiśabdea tu atra
pratiṣedhyaṃ kimapi samarpyateeti eti iti itiparatvāt añprayogasya itiśabdaścāyaṃ saṃihitālambaaḥ evaṃśabdasamāavṛttiḥ prayujyamāo dṛśyate iti ha smopādhyāyaḥ kathayati ityevamādiṣu saṃihitaṃ cātra prakaraṇasāmarthyādrūpadvayaṃ
saprapañcaṃ brahmaṇaḥ tacca brahma yasya te dve rūpe tatra aḥ saṃśaya upajāyate kimayaṃ pratiṣedho rūpe rūpavacca ubhayamapi pratiṣedhati āhosvidekataram yadāpyekataram
tadāpi kiṃ brahma pratiṣedhati rūpe pariśiaṣṭi āhosvidrūpe pratiṣedhati brahma pariśiaṣṭi iti tatra prakṛtatvāviśeṣādubhayamapi pratiṣedhatītyāśaṅkāmahe dvau caitau pratiṣedhau dviḥ etiśabdaprayogāt tayorekea
saprapañcaṃ brahmaṇo rūpaṃ pratiṣidhyate apareṇa rūpavadbrahma iti bhavati matiḥ athavā brahmaiva rūpavat pratiṣidhyate taddhi vāṅmaasātītatvādasaṃbhāvyamāasadbhāvaṃ pratiṣedhārham a tu rūpaprapañcaḥ pratyakṣādigocaratvāt
pratiṣedhārhaḥ abhyāsastvādarārthaḥ ityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ a tāvadubhayapratiṣedha upapadyate śūyavādaprasaṅgāt kaṃciddhi paramārthamālambya aparamārthaḥ pratiṣidhyate yathā rajjvādiṣu sarpādayaḥ tacca pariśiṣyamāṇe kasmiṃścidbhāve avakalpate
kṛtsapratiṣedhe tu koyo bhāvaḥ pariśiṣyeta apariśiṣyamāṇe cāyasmi ya itaraḥ pratiṣeddhumārabhyate pratiṣeddhumaśakyatvāt tasyaiva paramārthatvāpatteḥ pratiṣedhāupapattiḥ āpi brahmapratiṣedha upapadyate brahma te bravāṇi
ityādyupakramavirodhātasaeva sa bhavati asadbrahmeti veda cet ityādiidāvirodhātastītyevopalabdhavyaḥ ityādyavadhāraṇavirodhāt sarvavedātavyākopaprasaṅgācca vāṅmaasātītatvamapi brahmaṇo a abhāvābhiprāyeṇābhidhīyate a hi mahatā parikarabadheabrahmavidāpoti paramsatyaṃ jñāamaataṃ brahma
ityevamādiā vedāteṣu brahma pratipādya tasyaiva puaḥ abhāvobhilapyetaprakṣālaāddhi paṅkasya dūrādasparśaaṃ varam iti hi yāyaḥ pratipādaaprakriyā tu eṣā yato vāco ivartate aprāpya
maasā saha iti etaduktaṃ bhavati vāṅmaasātītamaviṣayātaḥpātipratyagātmabhūtaṃ ityaśuddhabuddhamuktasvabhāvaṃ brahmeti tasmādbrahmaṇo rūpaprapañcaṃ pratiṣedhati pariśiaṣṭi brahma ityavagatavyam tadetaducyate prakṛtaitāvattvaṃ hi pratiṣedhatīti prakṛtaṃ yadetāvat
iyattāparicchiaṃ mūrtāmūrtalakṣaṇaṃ brahmaṇo rūpaṃ tadeṣa śabdaḥ pratiṣedhati taddhi prakṛtaṃ prapañcitaṃ ca pūrvasmigrathe adhidaivatamadhyātmaṃ ca tajjaitameva ca vāsaālakṣaṇamaparaṃ rūpam amūrtarasabhūtaṃ puruṣaśabdoditaṃ
liṅgātmavyapāśrayaṃ māhārajaādyupamābhirdarśitam amūrtarasasya puruṣasya cakṣurgrāhyarūpayogitvāupapatteḥ tadetat saprapañcaṃ brahmaṇo rūpaṃ saṃihitālambaea itikaraṇea pratiṣedhakaṃ añaṃ prati upaīyata iti gamyate brahma tu rūpaviśeṣaṇatvea
ṣaṣṭhyā irdiṣṭaṃ pūrvasmigrathe a svapradhāatvea prapañcite ca tadīye rūpadvaye rūpavataḥ svarūpajijñāsāyām idamupakrātam athāta ādeśo eti eti iti tatra kalpitarūpapratyākhyāea brahmaṇaḥ
svarūpāvedaamiti irṇīyate tadāspadaṃ hi idaṃ samastaṃ kāryameti eti iti pratiṣiddham yuktaṃ ca kāryasya vācārambhaṇaśabdādibhyosattvamiti eti etīti pratiṣedhaam a tu brahmaṇaḥ
sarvakalpaāmūlatvāt a ca atra iyamāśaṅkā kartavyā kathaṃ hi śāstraṃ svayameva brahmaṇo rūpadvayaṃ darśayitvā svayameva puaḥ pratiṣedhati prakṣālaāddhi paṅkasya dūrādasparśaaṃ varam
iti yataḥ edaṃ śāstraṃ pratipādyatvea brahmaṇo rūpadvayaṃ irdiśati lokaprasiddhaṃ tu idaṃ rūpadvayaṃ brahmaṇi kalpitaṃ parāmṛśati pratiṣedhyatvāya śuddhabrahmasvarūpapratipādaāya ca iti iravadyam
dvau ca etau pratiṣedhau yathāsaṃkhyayāyea dve api mūrtāmūrte pratiṣedhataḥ yadvā pūrvaḥ pratiṣedho bhūtarāśiṃ pratiṣedhati uttaro vāsaārāśim athavāeti eti iti vīpsā
iyam iti iti yāvatkiṃcit utprekṣyate tatsarvaṃ a bhavatītyarthaḥ parigaṇitapratiṣedhe hi kriyamāṇe yadi aitadbrahma kimayadbrahma bhavediti jijñāsā syāt vīpsāyāṃ tu satyāṃ
samastasya viṣayajātasya pratiṣedhāt aviṣayaḥ pratyagātmā brahmeti jijñāsā ivartate tasmāt prapañcameva brahmaṇi kalpitaṃ pratiṣedhati pariśiaṣṭi brahma iti irṇayaḥ itaśca eṣa eva
irṇayaḥ yataḥ tataḥ prapañcapratiṣedhāt bhūyo brahma bravīti ayatparamasti iti abhāvāvasāe hi pratiṣedhe kriyamāṇe kimayatparamastīti brūyāt tatraiṣā akṣarayojaā eti eti iti
brahma ādiśya tameva ādeśaṃ puarirvakti eti eti ityasya korthaḥ a hi etasmādbrahmaṇo vyatiriktamastītyataḥeti eti ityucyate a puaḥ svayameva āsti ityarthaḥ
tacca darśayati ayatparam apratiṣiddhaṃ brahma astīti yadā puarevamakṣarāṇi yojyate a hi etasmātiti aiti a iti prapañcapratiṣedharūpāt ādeśaāt ayatparamādeśaaṃ brahmaṇaḥ astīti
tadātato bravīti ca bhūyaḥ ityetat āmadheyaviṣayaṃ yojayitavyam atha āmadheysatyasya satyamiti prāṇā vai satyaṃ teṣām eṣa satyam iti hi bravīti iti
tacca brahmāvasāe pratiṣedhe samañjasaṃ bhavati abhāvāvasāe tu pratiṣedhe kimsatyasya satyam ityucyeta tasmādbrahmāvasāaḥ ayaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ ābhāvāvasāaḥ ityadhyavasyāmaḥ tadavyaktamāha hi yattat pratiṣiddhātprapañcajātādayat
paraṃ brahma tadasti cet kasmāa gṛhyata iti ucyate tat avyaktamaidriyagrāhyam sarvadṛśyasākṣitvāt āha hi evaṃ śrutiḥ a cakṣuṣā gṛhyate āpi vācā
āyairdevaistapasā karmaṇā vāsa eṣa eti etyātmāgṛhyo a hi gṛhyateyattadadreśyamagrāhyamyadā hyevaiṣa etasmiadṛśyeātmyeirukteilayae ityādyā smṛtirapi avyaktoyamacityoyamavikāryoyamucyate ityādyā api ca saṃrādhae pratyakṣāumāābhyām api
ca eamātmāaṃ irastasamastaprapañcamavyaktaṃ saṃrādhaakāle paśyati yogaaḥ saṃrādhaaṃ ca bhaktidhyāapraṇidhāādyauṣṭhāam kathaṃ puaravagamyate saṃrādhaakāle paśyatīti pratyakṣāumāābhyām śrutismṛtibhyāmityarthaḥ tathā hi śrutiḥ parāñci khāi
vyatṛṇatsvayaṃbhūstasmātparāṅ paśyati ātarātma kaściddhīraḥ pratyagātmāam aikṣad āvṛttacakṣuramṛtatvam iccha iti jñāaprasādea viśuddhasattvastatas tu taṃ paśyate iṣkalaṃ dhyāyamāaḥ iti caivamādyā smṛtir api
ye viidrā jitaśvāsāḥ saṃtuṣṭāḥ saṃyatedriyāḥ jyotiḥ paśyati yuñjāās tasmai yogātmae amaḥ yogias taṃ prapaśyati bhagavataṃ saātaam iti caivamādyā au saṃrādhyasaṃrādhakabhāvābhyupagamāt
parāparātmaor ayatvaṃ syād iti ety ucyate prakāśādivac cāvaiśeṣyaṃ prakāśaś ca karmaṇy abhyāsāt yathā prakāśākāśasavitṛprabhṛtayaḥ aṅgulikarakodakaprabhṛtiṣu karmasu upādhibhūteṣu saviśeṣā ivāvabhāsate a
ca svābhāvikīm aviśeṣātmatāṃ jahati evam upādhiimitta evāyam ātmabhedaḥ svatas tu aikātmyam eva tathā hi vedāteṣu abhyāsea asakṛt jīvaprājñayor abhedaḥ pratipādyate
atoatea tathā hi liṅgam ataśca svābhāvikatvādabhedasya avidyākṛtatvācca bhedasya vidyayā avidyāṃ vidhūya jīvaḥ pareṇa aatea prājñea ātmaā ekatāṃ gacchati tathā hi
liṅgam sa yo ha vai tatparamaṃ brahma veda brahmaiva bhavatibrahmaiva sabrahmāpyeti ityādi ubhayavyapadeśāttvahikuṇḍalavat tasmieva saṃrādhyasaṃrādhakabhāve matātaramupayasyati svamataviśuddhaye kvacit jīvaprājñayorbhedo vyapadiśyate
tatastu taṃ paśyate iṣkalaṃ dhyāyamāaḥ iti dhyātṛdhyātavyatvea draṣṭṛdraṣṭavyatvea caparātparaṃ puruṣamupaiti divyam iti gatṛgatavyatveayaḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāyataro yamayati iti iyatṛiyatavyatvea ca kvacittu
tayorevābhedo vyapadiśyate tattvamasiahaṃ brahmāsmieṣa ta ātmā sarvātaraḥeṣa ta ātmātaryāmyamṛtaḥ iti tatraivamubhayavyapadeśe sati yadyabheda eva ekātato gṛhyate bhedavyapadeśo irālambaa eva syāt
ata ubhayavyapadeśadarśaāt ahikuṇḍalavadatra tattvaṃ bhavitumarhati yathā ahirityabhedaḥ kuṇḍalābhogaprāṃśutvādīīti ca bhedaḥ evamihāpīti prakāśāśrayavadvā tejastvāt athavā prakāśāśrayavadetatpratipattavyam yathā prakāśaḥ sāvitraḥ tadāśrayaśca savitā
ātyatabhiau ubhayorapi tejastvāviśeṣāt atha ca bhedavyapadeśabhājau bhavataḥ evamihāpīti pūrvavadvā yathā vā pūrvamupayastam prakāśādivaccāvaiśeṣyam iti tathaiva etadbhavitumarhati tathā hi avidyākṛtatvādbadhasya vidyayā
mokṣa upapadyate yadi puaḥ paramārthata eva baddhaḥ kaścidātmā ahikuṇḍalayāyea parasya ātmaaḥ saṃsthāabhūtaḥ prakāśāśrayayāyea ca ekadeśabhūtobhyupagamyeta tataḥ pāramārthikasya badhasya tiraskartumaśakyatvāt mokṣaśāstravaiyarthyaṃ
prasajyeta a cātra ubhāvapi bhedābhedau śrutiḥ tulyavadvyapadiśati abhedameva hi pratipādyatvea irdiśati bhedaṃ tu pūrvaprasiddhamevāuvadati arthātaravivakṣayā tasmātprakāśādivaccāvaiśeṣyamityeṣa eva siddhātaḥ pratiṣedhācca itaśca
eṣa eva siddhātaḥ yatkāraṇaṃ parasmādātmaoyaṃ cetaaṃ pratiṣedhati śāstram āyotosti draṣṭā ityevamādiathāta ādeśo eti etitadetadbrahmāpūrvamaaparamaataramabāhyam iti ca brahmavyatiriktaprapañcairākaraṇāt brahmamātrapariśeṣācca eṣa eva
siddhāta iti gamyate yadetat irastasamastaprapañcaṃ brahma irdhāritam asmātparam ayattattvamasti āstīti śrutivipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ kāiciddhi vākyāi āpāteaiva pratibhāsamāāi brahmaṇopi param ayattattvaṃ pratipādayatīva
teṣāṃ hi parihāramabhidhātumayamupakramaḥ kriyate paramataḥ setūmāasambadhabhedavyapadeśebhyaḥ param ato brahmaṇaḥ ayattattvaṃ bhavitumarhati kutaḥ setuvyapadeśāt umāavyapadeśāt saṃbadhavyapadeśāt bhedavyapadeśācca setuvyapadeśastāvat atha ya ātmā
sa seturvidhṛtiḥ ityātmaśabdābhihitasya brahmaṇaḥ setutvaṃ saṃkīrtayati setuśabdaśca hi loke jalasaṃtāavicchedakare mṛddārvādipracaye prasiddhaḥ iha ca setuśabdaḥ ātmai prayukta iti laukikasetoriva ātmasetorayasya
vastuostitvaṃ gamayatisetu tītrvā iti ca taratiśabdaprayogāt yathā laukikaṃ setuṃ tītrvā jāṅgalamasetuṃ prāpoti evamātmāaṃ setuṃ tītrvā aātmāamasetuṃ prāpotīti gamyate umāavyapadeśaśca bhavati
tadetadbrahma catuṣpāt aṣṭāśaphaṃ ṣoḍaśakalamiti yacca loke umitam etāvadidamiti paricchiaṃ kārṣāpaṇādi tatoyadvastvastīti prasiddham tathā brahmaṇopyumāāt tatoyea vastuā bhavitavyamiti gamyate tathā saṃbadhavyapadeśo
bhavati satā somya tadā saṃpao bhavati iti śārīra ātmāprājñeātmaā saṃpariṣvaktaḥ iti ca mitāāṃ ca mitea saṃbadho dṛṣṭaḥ yathā arāṇāṃ agareṇa
jīvāāṃ ca brahmaṇā saṃbadhaṃ vyapadiśati suṣuptau ataḥ tataḥ paramayadamitamastīti gamyate bhedavyapadeśaśca eamarthaṃ gamayati tathā hi atha ya eṣotarāditye hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣo
dṛśyate ityādityādhāramīśvaraṃ vyapadiśya tato bhedea akṣyādhāramīśvaraṃ vyapadiśati atha ya eṣokṣiṇi puruṣo dṛśyate iti atideśaṃ ca asya amuā rūpādiṣu karoti tasyaitasya
tadeva rūpaṃ yadamuṣya rūpaṃ yāvamuṣya geṣṇau tau geṣṇau yaāma taāma iti sāvadhikaṃ ca īśvaratvamubhayorvyapadiśati ye cāmuṣmātparāñco lokāsteṣāṃ ceṣṭe devakāmāāṃ ca
ityekasyaye caitasmādarvāñco lokāsteṣāṃ ceṣṭe mauṣyakāmāāṃ ca ityekasya yathā idaṃ māgadhasya rājyam idaṃ vaidehasyeti evametebhyaḥ setvādivyapadeśebhyo brahmaṇaḥ paramastīti evaṃ prāpte pratipādyate
sāmāyāttu tuśabdea pradarśitāṃ prāptiṃ iruṇaddhi a brahmaṇoyat kiṃcidbhavitumarhati pramāṇābhāvāt a hyayasyāstitve kiṃcitpramāṇamupalabhāmahe sarvasya hi jaimato vastujātasya jamādi brahmaṇo bhavatīti irdhāritam
aayatvaṃ ca kāraṇāt kāryasya a ca brahmavyatiriktaṃ kiṃcit ajaṃ saṃbhavatisadeva somyedamagra āsīdekamevādvitīyam ityavadhāraṇāt ekavijñāea ca sarvavijñāapratijñāāt a brahmavyatiriktavastvastitvamavakalpate au setvādivyapadeśāḥ
brahmavyatiriktaṃ tattvaṃ sūcayatītyuktam etyucyate setuvyapadeśastāvat a brahmaṇo bāhyasya sadbhāvaṃ pratipādayituṃ kṣamate seturātmeti hi āha a ataḥ paramastīti tatra parasmi asati
setutvaṃ āvakalpata iti paraṃ kimapi kalpyeta a caitat yāyyam haṭho hi aprasiddhakalpaā api ca setuvyapadeśādātmao laukikasetuidarśaea sabāhyavastutāṃ prasañjayatā mṛddārumayatāpi prāsaṅkṣyata
a caitayāyyam ajatvādiśrutivirodhāt setusāmāyāttu setuśabda ātmai prayukta iti śliṣyate jagatastamaryādāāṃ ca vidhārakatvaṃ setusāmāyamātmaaḥ ataḥ seturiva setuḥ iti prakṛta ātmā stūyatesetuṃ
tītrvā ityapi taratiḥ atikramāsaṃbhavāt prāpotyartha eva vartate yathā vyākaraṇaṃ tīrṇa iti prāptaḥ ucyate a atikrātaḥ tadvat buddhyarthaḥ pādavat yadapyuktam umāavyapadeśādasti
paramiti tatrābhidhīyate umāavyapadeśopi a brahmavyatiriktavastvastitvapratipattyarthaḥ kimarthastarhi buddhyarthaḥ upāsaārtha iti yāvat catuṣpādaṣṭāśaphaṃ ṣoḍaśakalamityevaṃrūpā buddhiḥ kathaṃ u āma brahmaṇi sthirā syāditi vikāradvāreṇa
brahmaṇa umāakalpaaiva kriyate a hi avikāreate brahmaṇi sarvaiḥ puṃbhiḥ śakyā buddhiḥ sthāpayitum madamadhyamottamabuddhitvāt puṃsāmiti pādavat yathā maaākāśayoradhyātmamadhidaivataṃ ca brahmapratīkayorāmātayoḥ catvāro
vāgādayo maaḥsaṃbadhiaḥ pādāḥ kalpyate catvāraśca agyādaya ākāśasaṃbadhiaḥ ādhyāāya tadvat athavā pādavaditi yathā kārṣāpaṇe pādavibhāgo vyavahāraprācuryāya kalpyate a hi sakaleaiva kārṣāpaṇea
sarvadā sarve jaā vyavahartumīśate krayavikraye parimāṇāiyamāt tadvadityarthaḥ sthāaviśeṣātprakāśādivat iha sūtre dvayorapi saṃbadhabhedavyapadeśayoḥ parihārobhidhīyate yadapyuktam saṃbadhavyapadeśāt bhedavyapadeśācca paramataḥ syāditi tadapyasat yata
ekasyāpi sthāaviśeṣāpekṣayā etau vyapadeśāvupapadyete saṃbadhavyapadeśe tāvadayamarthaḥ buddhyādyupādhisthāaviśeṣayogādudbhūtasya viśeṣavijñāasya upādhyupaśame ya upaśamaḥ sa paramātmaā saṃbadhaḥ ityupādhyapekṣayā upacaryate a parimitatvāpekṣayā tathā bhedavyapadeśopi
brahmaṇa upādhibhedāpekṣayaiva upacaryate a svarūpabhedāpekṣayā prakāśādivaditi upamopādāam yathā ekasya prakāśasya sauryasya cādramasasya vā upādhiyogādupajātaviśeṣasya upādhyupaśamātsaṃbadhavyapadeśo bhavati upādhibhedācca bhedavyapadeśaḥ yathā vā
sūcīpāśākāśādiṣūpādhyapekṣayaivaitau saṃbadhabhedavyapadeśau bhavataḥ tadvat upapatteśca upapadyate ca atra īdṛśa eva saṃbadhaḥ āyādṛśaḥ svamapīto bhavati iti hi svarūpasaṃbadhameamāmaati svarūpasya ca aapāyitvāt
a araagarayāyea saṃbadho ghaṭate upādhikṛtasvarūpatirobhāvāttusvamapīto bhavati ityupapadyate tathā bhedopi āyādṛśaḥ saṃbhavati bahutaraśrutiprasiddhaikeśvaratvavirodhāt tathā ca śrutirekasyāpyākāśasya sthāakṛtaṃ bhedavyapadeśamupapādayati yoyaṃ bahirdhā puruṣādākāśaḥyoyamataḥ
puruṣa ākāśaḥyoyamatarhṛdaya ākāśaḥ iti tathāyapratiṣedhāt evaṃ setvādivyapadeśā parapakṣahetūumathya saṃprati svapakṣaṃ hetvatareṇopasaṃharati tathāyapratiṣedhāpi a brahmaṇaḥ paraṃ vastvataramastīti gamyate tathā hi sa
evādhastāt ahamevādhastātātmaivādhastātsarvaṃ taṃ parādādyoyatrātmaaḥ sarvaṃ vedabrahmaivedaṃ sarvamātmaivedaṃ sarvameha āāsti kiṃcaayasmātparaṃ āparamasti kiṃcittadetadbrahmāpūrvamaaparamaataramabāhyam ityevamādīi vākyāi svaprakaraṇasthāi ayārthatvea pariṇetumaśakyāi brahmavyatiriktaṃ vastvataraṃ vārayati
sarvātaraśruteśca a paramātmaoyaḥ atarātmā astītyavagamyate aea sarvagatatvamāyāmaśabdādibhyaḥ aea setvādivyapadeśairākaraṇea ayapratiṣedhasamāśrayaṇea ca sarvagatatvamapyātmaaḥ siddhaṃ bhavati ayathā hi taa sidhyet setvādivyapadeśeṣu hi
mukhyeṣvaṅgīkriyamāṇeṣu pariccheda ātmaaḥ prasajyeta setvādīāmevamātmakatvāt tathā ayapratiṣedhepyasati vastu vastvatarādvyāvartata iti pariccheda eva ātmaaḥ prasajyeta sarvagatatvaṃ ca asya āyāmaśabdādibhyovagamyate āyāmaśabdaḥ vyāptivacaaḥ
śabdaḥyāvāvā ayamākāśastāvāeṣotarhṛdaya ākāśaḥākāśavatsarvagataśca ityaḥjyāyādivaḥjyāyāākāśāt ityaḥ sarvagataḥ sthāṇuracaloyaṃ saātaaḥ ityevamādayo hi śrutismṛtiyāyāḥ sarvagatatvamātmaovabodhayati phalamata upapatteḥ phalādhikaraṇam tasyaiva brahmaṇo vyāvahārikyām īśitrīśitavyavibhāgāvasthāyām ayamayaḥ
svabhāvo varṇyate yadetat iṣṭāiṣṭavyāmiśralakṣaṇaṃ karmaphalaṃ saṃsāragocaraṃ trividhaṃ prasiddhaṃ jatūām kimetat karmaṇo bhavati āhosvidīśvarāditi bhavati vicāraṇā tatra tāvatpratipādyate phalam ataḥ īśvarāt
bhavitumarhati kutaḥ upapatteḥ sa hi sarvādhyakṣaḥ sṛṣṭisthitisaṃhārā vicitrā vidadhat deśakālaviśeṣābhijñatvāt karmiṇāṃ karmāurūpaṃ phalaṃ saṃpādayatītyupapadyate karmaṇastu aukṣaṇaviāśiaḥ kālātarabhāvi phalaṃ bhavatītyaupapaam abhāvādbhāvāutpatteḥ
syādetat karma viaśyat svakālameva svāurūpaṃ phalaṃ jaayitvā viaśyati tatphalaṃ kālātaritaṃ kartrā bhokṣyata iti tadapi a pariśudhyati prāgbhoktṛsaṃbadhāt phalatvāupapatteḥ yatkālaṃ hi
yat sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ vā ātmaā bhujyate tasyaiva loke phalatvaṃ prasiddham a hi asaṃbaddhasyātmaā sukhasya duḥkhasya vā phalatvaṃ pratiyati laukikāḥ athocyeta
mā bhūtkarmāataraṃ phalotpādaḥ karmakāryādapūrvātphalamutpatsyata iti tadapi opapadyate apūrvasyācetaasya kāṣṭhaloṣṭasamasya cetaeāpravartitasya pravṛttyaupapatteḥ tadastitve eva pramāṇābhāvāt arthāpattiḥ pramāṇamiti cet a īśvarasiddherarthāpattikṣayāt śrutatvācca
a kevalam upapattereva īśvaraṃ phalahetuṃ kalpayāmaḥ kiṃ tarhi śrutatvādapi īśvarameva phalahetuṃ mayāmahe tathā ca śrutirbhavati sa vā eṣa mahāaja ātmāādo
vasudāaḥ ityevaṃjātīyakā dharmaṃ jaimiirata eva jaimiistvācāryo dharmaṃ phalasya dātāraṃ mayate ata eva hetoḥ śruteḥ upapatteśca śrūyate tāvadayamarthaḥsvargakāmo yajeta ityevamādiṣu vākyeṣu
tatra ca vidhiśruterviṣayabhāvopagamāt yāgaḥ svargasyotpādaka iti gamyate ayathā hi aauṣṭhātṛko yāga āpadyeta tatra asya upadeśavaiyarthyaṃ syāt au aukṣaṇaviāśiaḥ karmaṇaḥ phalaṃ
opapadyata iti parityaktoyaṃ pakṣaḥ aiṣa doṣaḥ śrutiprāmāṇyāt śrutiścet pramāṇam yathāyaṃ karmaphalasaṃbadhaḥ śruta upapadyate tathā kalpayitavyaḥ a ca autpādya kimapyapūrvaṃ karma
viaśyat kālātaritaṃ phalaṃ dātuṃ śakoti ataḥ karmaṇo vā sūkṣmā kāciduttarāvasthā phalasya vā pūrvāvasthā apūrvaṃ āma astīti tarkyate upapadyate ca ayamarthaṃ
uktea prakāreṇa īśvarastu phalaṃ dadātītyaupapaam avicitrasya kāraṇasya vicitrakāryāupapatteḥ vaiṣamyaairghṛṇyaprasaṅgāt tadauṣṭhāavaiyarthyāpatteśca tasmāt dharmādeva phalamiti pūrvaṃ tu bādarāyaṇo hetuvyapadeśāt bādarāyaṇastvācāryaḥ pūrvoktameva īśvaraṃ
phalahetuṃ mayate kevalātkarmaṇaḥ apūrvādvā kevalāt phalamityayaṃ pakṣaḥ tuśabdea vyāvartyate karmāpekṣāt apūrvāpekṣādvā yathā tathāstu īśvarātphalamiti siddhātaḥ kutaḥ hetuvyapadeśāt dharmādharmayorapi hi kārayitṛtvea
īśvaro hetuḥ vyapadiśyate phalasya ca dātṛtvea eṣa hyeva sādhu karma kārayati taṃ yamebhyo lokebhya uiīṣate eṣa u evāsādhu karma kārayati
taṃ yamadho iīṣate iti smaryate ca ayamartho bhagavadgītāsu yo yo yāṃ yāṃ tauṃ bhaktaḥ śraddhayārcitumicchati tasya tasyācalāṃ śraddhāṃ tāmeva vidadhāmyaham
sa tayā śraddhayā yuktastasyārādhaamīhate labhate ca tataḥ kāmā mayaiva vihitāhitā iti sarvavedāteṣu ca īśvarahetukā eva sṛṣṭayo vyapadiśyate tadeva ca īśvarasya
phalahetutvam yat svakarmāurūpāḥ prajāḥ sṛjati vicitrakāryāupapattyādayopi doṣāḥ kṛtaprayatāpekṣatvādīśvarasya a prasajyate iti śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācāryasya śrīgovidabhagavatpūjyapādaśiṣyasya śrīmacchaṃkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīrakamīmāṃsāsūtrabhāṣye tṛtīyādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ
tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ sarvavedātapratyayaṃ codaādyaviśeṣāt sarvavedātapratyayādhikaraṇam sarvavedātapratyayāi vijñāāi tasmi tasmi vedāte tāi tāyeva bhavitumarhati kutaḥ codaādyaviśeṣāt ādigrahaṇea śākhātarādhikaraṇasiddhātasūtroditā abhedahetava ihākṛṣyate saṃyogarūpacodaākhyāviśeṣādityarthaḥ
yathā ekasmiagihotre śākhābhedepi puruṣaprayatastādṛśa eva codyate juhuyāditi evamyo ha vai jyeṣṭhaṃ ca śreṣṭhaṃ ca veda iti vājasaeyiāṃ chadogāāṃ ca tādṛśyeva
codaā prayojaasaṃyogopyaviśiṣṭa eva jyeṣṭhaśca śreṣṭhaśca svāāṃ bhavati iti rūpamapyubhayatra tadeva vijñāasya yaduta jyeṣṭhaśreṣṭhādiviśeṣaṇāvitaṃ prāṇatattvam yathā ca dravyadevate yāgasya rūpam evaṃ
vijñeyaṃ rūpaṃ vijñāasya tea hi tat rūpyate samākhyāpi saiva prāṇavidyeti tasmāt sarvavedātapratyayatvaṃ vijñāāām evaṃ pañcāgividyā vaiśvāaravidyā śāṇḍilyavidyetyevamādiṣvapi yojayitavyam ye tu
āmarūpādayo bhedahetvābhāsāḥ te prathama eva kāṇḍea āmā syādacodaābhidhāatvāt ityārabhya parihṛtāḥ ihāpi kaṃcidviśeṣamāśaṅkya pariharati bhedāeti ceaikasyāmapi syādetat sarvavedātapratyayatvaṃ vijñāāāṃ guṇabhedāt opapadyate
tathā hi vājasaeyiaḥ pañcāgividyāṃ prastutya ṣaṣṭhamaparamagimāmaati tasyāgirevāgirbhavati ityādiā chadogāstu taṃ a āmaati pañcasaṃkhyayaiva ca te upasaṃharati atha ha ya etāevaṃ
pañcāgīveda iti yeṣāṃ ca sa guṇosti yeṣāṃ ca āsti kathamubhayeṣāmekā vidyopapadyeta a ca atra guṇopasaṃhāraḥ śakyate pratyetum pañcasaṃkhyāvirodhāt tathā prāṇasaṃvāde
śreṣṭhāt ayā caturaḥ prāṇā vākcakṣuḥśrotramaāṃsi chadogā āmaati vājasaeyiastu pañcamamapyāmaati reto vai prajāpatiḥ prajāyate ha prajayā paśubhirya evaṃ veda iti āvāpodvāpabhedācca
vedyabhedo bhavati vedyabhedācca vidyābhedaḥ dravyadevatābhedādivayāgasyeti cet aiṣa doṣaḥ yata ekasyāmapi vidyāyāmevaṃjātīyako guṇabheda upapadyate yadyapi ṣaṣṭhasyāgerupasaṃhāro a saṃbhavati tathāpi dyuprabhṛtīāṃ pañcāāmagīām
ubhayatra pratyabhijñāyamāatvāt a vidyābhedo bhavitumarhati a hi ṣoḍaśigrahaṇāgrahaṇayoratirātro bhidyate paṭhyatepi ca ṣaṣṭhogiḥ chadogaiḥ taṃ pretaṃ diṣṭamitogaya eva harati iti vājasaeyiastu
sāṃpādikeṣu pañcasvagiṣu auvṛttāyāḥ samiddhūmādikalpaāyā ivṛttayetasyāgirevāgirbhavati samitsamit ityādi samāmaati sa ityāuvādaḥ athāpyupāsaārtha eṣa vādaḥ tathāpi sa guṇaḥ śakyate chadogairapyupasaṃhartum a ca
atra pañcasaṃkhyāvirodha āśaṅkyaḥ sāṃpādikāgyabhiprāyā hi eṣā pañcasaṃkhyā ityāuvādabhūtā a vidhisamavāyiī ityadoṣaḥ evaṃ prāṇasaṃvādādiṣvapi adhikasya guṇasya itaratropasaṃhāro a virudhyate a ca
