āadādayo dharmā brahmasvarūpapratipādaāyaiva ucyamāāḥ arthasāmāyāt pratipādyasya brahmaṇo dharmiṇa ekatvāt sarve sarvatra pratīyeraiti vaiṣamyam pratipattimātraprayojaā hi te iti ādhyāāya prayojaābhāvāt ādhyāādhikaraṇam
kāṭhake hi paṭhyate idriyebhyaḥ parā hyarthā arthebhyaśca paraṃ maaḥ maasastu parā buddhiḥ ityārabhyapuruṣāa paraṃ kiṃcitsā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ iti
tatra saṃśayaḥ kimime sarva eva arthādayaḥ tatastataḥ paratvea pratipādyate uta puruṣa eva ebhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ paraḥ pratipādyata iti tatra tāvat sarveṣāmevaiṣāṃ
paratvea pratipādaamiti bhavati matiḥ tathāhi śrūyate idamasmātparam idamasmātparamiti au bahuṣvartheṣu paratvea pratipipādayiṣiteṣu vākyabhedaḥ syāt aiṣa doṣaḥ vākyabahutvopapatteḥ bahūyeva hi etāi
vākyāi prabhavati bahūarthā paratvopetā pratipādayitum tasmāt pratyekameṣāṃ paratvapratipādaamityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ puruṣa eva hi ebhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ paraḥ pratipādyata iti yuktam a
pratyekameṣāṃ paratvapratipādaam kasmāt prayojaābhāvāt a hi itareṣu paratvea pratipaeṣu kiṃcitprayojaaṃ dṛśyate śrūyate vā puruṣe tu idriyādibhyaḥ parasmi sarvāarthavrātātīte pratipae dṛśyate
prayojaam mokṣasiddhiḥ tathā ca śrutiḥ icāyya tamṛtyumukhātpramucyate iti api ca parapratiṣedhea kāṣṭhāśabdea ca puruṣaviṣayamādaraṃ darśaya puruṣapratipattyarthaiva pūrvāparapravāhoktiriti darśayati ādhyāāyeti ādhyāapūrvakāya
samyagdarśaāyetyarthaḥ samyagdarśaārthameva hi iha ādhyāamupadiśyate a tu ādhyāameva svapradhāam ātmaśabdācca itaśca puruṣapratipattyarthaiva iyamidriyādipravāhoktiḥ yatkāraṇameṣa sarveṣu bhūteṣu gūḍhotmā a prakāśate dṛśyate
tvagryayā buddhyā sūkṣmayā sūkṣmadarśibhiḥ iti prakṛtaṃ puruṣam ātmetyāha ataśca aātmatvamitareṣāṃ vivakṣitamiti gamyate tasyaiva ca durvijñāatāṃ saṃskṛtamatigamyatāṃ ca darśayati tadvijñāāyaiva ca
yacchedvāṅmaasī prājñaḥ iti ādhyāaṃ vidadhāti tat vyākhyātamāumāikamapyekeṣām ityatra evam aekaprakāra āśayātiśayaḥ śruteḥ puruṣe lakṣyate etareṣu api casodhvaaḥ pāramāpoti tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ
padam ityukte kiṃ tat adhvaaḥ pāraṃ viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padamityasyāmākāṅkṣāyām idriyādyaukramaṇāt paramapadapratipattyartha evāyam āmāya ityavasīyate ātmagṛhītiritaravaduttarāt ātmagṛhītyadhikaraṇam aitareyake śrūyate ātmā vā
idameka evāgra āsīāyatkiṃcaa miṣatsa īkṣata lokā u sṛjā itisa imāṃl lokā asṛjatāmbho marīcīrmaramāpaḥ ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ para evātmā iha
ātmaśabdeābhilapyate uta ayaḥ kaścid iti kiṃ tāvat prāptam a paramātmā iha ātmaśabdābhilapyo bhavitum arhatīti kasmāt vākyāvayadarśaāt au vākyāvayaḥ sutarāṃ paramātmaviṣayo
dṛśyate prāg utpatteḥ ātmaikatvāvadhāraṇāt īkṣaṇapūrvakasraṣṭṛtvavacaāc ca ety ucyate lokasṛṣṭivacaāt paramātmai hi sraṣṭari parigṛhyamāṇe mahābhūtasṛṣṭiḥ ādau vaktavyā lokasṛṣṭis tu iha ādāv
ucyate lokāś ca mahābhūtasaṃiveśaviśeṣāḥ tathā ca ambhaḥprabhṛtī lokatveaiva irbravīti adombhaḥ pareṇa divam ityādiā lokasṛṣṭiś ca parameśvarādhiṣṭhitea apareṇa keacid īśvareṇa kriyata
iti śrutismṛtyor upalabhyate tathā hi śrutir bhavati ātmaivedam agra āsīt puruṣavidhaḥ ityādyā smṛtir api sa vai śarīrī prathamaḥ sa vai
puruṣa ucyate ādikartā sa bhūtāāṃ brahmāgre samavartata iti aitareyiṇo pi athāto retasaḥ sṛṣṭiḥ prajāpate reto devāḥ ity atra pūrvasmi prakaraṇe
prajāpatikartṛkāṃ vicitrāṃ sṛṣṭim āmaati ātmaśabdo pi tasmi prayujyamāo dṛśyate ātmaivedam agra āsīt puruṣavidhaḥ ity atra ekatvāvadhāraṇam api prāg utpatteḥ svavikārāpekṣam
upapadyate īkṣaṇam api tasya cetaatvābhyupagamād upapaam api ca tābhyo gām āayat tābhyo śvam āayat tābhyaḥ puruṣam āayat tā abruva ity
evaṃjātīyako bhūyā vyāpāraviśeṣaḥ laukikeṣu viśeṣavatsu ātmasu prasiddhaḥ ihāugamyate tasmāt viśeṣavā eva kaścid iha ātmā syād ity evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ para
eva ātmā iha ātmaśabdea gṛhyate itaravat yathā itareṣu sṛṣṭiśravaṇeṣu tasmād vā etasmād ātmaa ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ ity evamādiṣu parasyātmao grahaṇam yathā
ca itarasmi laukikātmaśabdaprayoge pratyagātmaiva mukhya ātmaśabdea gṛhyate tathā ihāpi bhavitum arhati yatra tu ātmaivedam agra āsīt ity evamādau puruṣavidhaḥ ityevamādi
viśeṣaṇātaraṃ śrūyate bhavet tatra viśeṣavata ātmao grahaṇam atra puaḥ paramātmagrahaṇāuguṇam eva viśeṣaṇam api uttaram upalabhyate sa īkṣata lokā u sṛjā
itisa imāṃ llokā asṛjata ityevamādi tasmāt tasyaiva grahaṇam iti yāyyam avayāditi cetsyādavadhāraṇāt vākyāvayadarśaāt a paramātmagrahaṇamiti puaḥ yaduktam tatparihartavyamiti atrocyate syādavadhāraṇāditi
bhavedupapaaṃ paramātmao grahaṇam kasmāt avadhāraṇāt paramātmagrahaṇe hi prāgutpatterātmaikatvāvadhāraṇamāñjasamavakalpate ayathā hi aāñjasaṃ tatparikalpyeta lokasṛṣṭivacaaṃ tu śrutyataraprasiddhamahābhūtasṛṣṭyaataramiti yojayiṣyāmi yathātattejosṛjata ityetat śrutyataraprasiddhaviyadvāyusṛṣṭyaataramiti ayūyujam
evamihāpi śrutyataraprasiddho hi samāaviṣayo viśeṣaḥ śrutyatareṣu upasaṃhartavyo bhavati yopi ayaṃ vyāpāraviśeṣāugamaḥtābhyo gāmāayat ityevamādiḥ sopi vivakṣitārthāvadhāraṇāuguṇyeaiva grahītavyaḥ a hyayaṃ sakalaḥ kathāprabadho
vivakṣita iti śakyate vaktum tatpratipattau puruṣārthābhāvāt brahmātmatvaṃ tu iha vivakṣitam tathā hi ambhaḥprabhṛtīāṃ lokāāṃ lokapālāāṃ cāgyādīāṃ sṛṣṭiṃ śiṣṭvā karaṇāi karaṇāyataaṃ
ca śarīramupadiśya sa eva sraṣṭākathaṃ vidaṃ madṛte syāt iti vīkṣya idaṃ śarīraṃ praviveśeti darśayati sa etameva sīmāaṃ vidāryaitayā dvārā prāpadyata
iti puaścayadi vācābhivyāhṛtaṃ yadi prāṇeābhiprāṇitam ityevamādiā karaṇavyāpāravivecaapūrvakamatha koham iti vīkṣyasa etameva puruṣaṃ brahma tatamamapaśyat iti brahmātmatvadarśaamavadhārayati tathopariṣṭāt eṣa brahmaiṣa idraḥ
ityādiā samastaṃ bhedajātaṃ saha mahābhūtairaukramyasarvaṃ tatprajñāetraṃ prajñāe pratiṣṭhitaṃ prajñāetro lokaḥ prajñā pratiṣṭhā prajñāaṃ brahma iti brahmātmatvadarśaameva avadhārayati tasmāt iha ātmagṛhītirityaapavādam
aparā yojaā ātmagṛhītiritaravaduttarāt vājasaeyakekatama ātmeti yoyaṃ vijñāamayaḥ prāṇeṣu hṛdyatarjyotiḥ puruṣaḥ ityātmaśabdeopakramya tasyaiva sarvasaṅgaviirmuktatvapratipādaea brahmātmatāmavadhārayati tathā hi upasaṃharati sa vā eṣa
mahāaja ātmājaromaromṛtobhayo brahma iti chādogye tusadeva somyedamagra āsīdekamevādvitīyam iti atareṇaivātmaśabdam upakramya udarkesa ātmā tattvamasi iti tādātmyamupadiśati tatra saṃśayaḥ tulyārthatvaṃ kimaayorāmāayoḥ
syāt atulyārthatvaṃ veti atulyārthatvamiti tāvat prāptam atulyatvādāmāayoḥ a hi āmāavaiṣamye sati arthasāmyaṃ yuktaṃ pratipattum āmāatatratvādarthaparigrahasya vājasaeyake ca ātmaśabdopakramāt ātmatattvopadeśa iti
gamyate chādogye tu upakramaviparyayāt upadeśaviparyayaḥ au chadogāāmapi astyudarke tādātmyopadeśa ityuktam satyamuktam upakramatatratvādupasaṃhārasya tādātmyasaṃpattiḥ sā iti mayate tathā prāpte abhidhīyate ātmagṛhītiḥsadeva
somyedamagra āsīt ityatra cchadogāāmapi bhavitumarhati itaravat yathākatama ātmā ityatra vājasaeyiāmātmagṛhītiḥ tathaiva kasmāt uttarāt tādātmyopadeśātavayāditi cedavadhāraṇāt yaduktam upakramāvayāt upakrame ca ātmaśabdaśravaṇābhāvāt
a ātmagṛhītiriti tasya kaḥ parihāra iti cet sobhidhīyate syādavadhāraṇāditi bhavedupapaā iha ātmagṛhītiḥ avadhāraṇāt tathā hi yeāśrutaṃ śrutaṃ bhavatyamataṃ matamavijñātaṃ vijñātam
ityekavijñāea sarvavijñāamavadhārya tatsaṃpipādayiṣayāsadeva ityāha tacca ātmagṛhītau satyāṃ saṃpadyate ayathā hi yoyaṃ mukhya ātmā sa a vijñāta iti aiva sarvavijñāaṃ saṃpadyeta
tathā prāgutpatteḥ ekatvādhāraṇam jīvasya ca ātmaśabdea parāmarśaḥ svāpāvasthāyāṃ ca tatsvabhāvasaṃpattikathaam paricodaāpūrvakaṃ ca puaḥ puaḥtattvamasi ityavadhāraṇam iti ca sarvametat tādātmyapratipādaāyāmeva avakalpate
a tādātmyasaṃpādaāyām a ca atra upakramatatratvopayāso yāyyaḥ a hi upakrame ātmatvasaṃkīrtaam aātmatvasaṃkīrtaaṃ vā asti sāmāyopakramaśca a vākyaśeṣagatea viśeṣeṇa virudhyate viśeṣākaṅkṣitvātsāmāyasya
sacchabdārthopi ca paryālocyamāaḥ a mukhyādātmaoyaḥ saṃbhavati atoyasya vastujātasya ārambhaṇaśabdādibhyoṛtatvopapatteḥ āmāavaiṣamyamapi āvaśyamarthavaiṣamyamāvahatiāhara pātrampātramāhara ityevamādiṣu arthasāmyepi taddarśaāt tasmāt evaṃjātīyakeṣu vākyeṣu pratipādaaprakārabhedepi pratipādyārthābheda
iti siddham kāryākhyāādapūrvam kāryākhyāādhikaraṇam chadogā vājasaeyiaśca prāṇasaṃvāde śvādimaryādaṃ prāṇasya aamāmāya tasyaiva āpo vāsa āmaati aataraṃ ca cchadogā āmaati tasmādvā etadaśiṣyataḥ
purastāccopariṣṭāccādbhiḥ paridadhati iti vājasaeyiaścāmaati tadvidvāṃsaḥ śrotriyā aśiṣyata ācāmatyaśitvā cācāmatyetameva tadaamaagaṃ kurvato mayate tasmādevaṃvidaśiṣyaācāmedaśitvā cācāmedetameva tadaamaagaṃ kurute iti tatra ca ācamaam
aagatācitaaṃ ca prāṇasya pratīyate tatkimubhayamapi vidhīyate uta ācamaameva ua aagatācitaameveti vicāryate kiṃ tāvatprāptam ubhayamapi vidhīyata iti kutaḥ ubhayasyāpyavagamyamāatvāt ubhayamapi ca
etat apūrvatvāt vidhyarham athavā ācamaameva vidhīyate vispaṣṭā hi tasmividhivibhaktiḥ tasmādevaṃvidaśiṣyaācāmedaśitvā cācāmet iti tasyaiva stutyartham aagatāsaṃkīrtaamityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ a ācamaasya vidheyatvamupapadyate
kāryākhyāāt prāptameva hi idaṃ kāryatvea ācamaaṃ prāyatyārthaṃ smṛtiprasiddham avākhyāyate au iyaṃ śrutiḥ tasyāḥ smṛtermūlaṃ syāt etyucyate viṣayaāātvāt sāmāyaviṣayā hi smṛtiḥ
puruṣamātrasaṃbaddhaṃ prāyatyārthamācamaaṃ prāpayati śrutistu prāṇavidyāprakaraṇapaṭhitā tadviṣayameva ācamaaṃ vidadhatī vidadhyāt a ca bhiaviṣayayoḥ śrutismṛtyoḥ mūlamūlibhāvovakalpate a ca iyaṃ śrutiḥ prāṇavidyāsaṃyogi apūrvamācamaaṃ
vidhāsyatīti śakyamāśrayitum pūrvasyaiva puruṣamātrasaṃyogia ācamaasya iha pratyabhijñāyamāatvāt ata eva ca obhayavidhāam ubhayavidhāe ca vākyaṃ bhidyeta tasmāt prāptameva aśiśiṣatāmaśitavatāṃ ca ubhayata
ācamaam aūdyaetameva tadaamaagaṃ kurvato mayate iti prāṇasya aagatākaraṇasaṃkalpaḥ aea vākyea ācamaīyāsv apsu prāṇavidyāsaṃbadhitvea apūrva upadiśyate a ca ayamaagatāvādaḥ ācamaastutyartha iti
yāyyam ācamaasyāvidheyatvāt svayaṃ ca aagatāsaṃkalpasya vidheyatvapratīteḥ a ca evaṃ sati ekasya ācamaasya ubhayārthatā abhyupagatā bhavati prāyatyārthatā paridhāārthatā ceti kriyātaratvābhyupagamāt kriyātarameva
hi ācamaaṃ āma prāyatyārthaṃ puruṣasya abhyupagamyate tadīyāsu tu apsu vāsaḥsaṃkalpaaṃ āma kriyātarameva paridhāārthaṃ prāṇasya abhyupagamyata ityaavadyam api cayadidaṃ kiṃcā śvabhya
ā kṛmibhya ā kīṭapataṃgebhyastatteam ityatra tāvat a sarvāābhyavahāraścodyata iti śakyaṃ vaktum aśabdatvādaśakyatvācca sarvaṃ tu prāṇasyāamiti iyamaadṛṣṭiścodyate tatsāhacaryāccaāpo vāsaḥ ityatrāpi a

tasmāt vāsovijñāameva iha vidhīyate a ācamaamiti yāyyam samāa evaṃ cābhedāt samāādhikaraṇam vājasaeyiśākhāyām agirahasye śāṇḍilyaāmāṅkitā vidyā vijñātā tatra ca guṇāḥ śrūyate
sa ātmāamupāsīta maomayaṃ prāṇaśarīraṃ bhārūpam ityevamādayaḥ tasyāmeva śākhāyāṃ bṛhadāraṇyake puaḥ paṭhyate maomayoyaṃ puruṣo bhāḥsatyastasmiatarhṛdaye yathā vrīhirvā yavo vā sa eṣa
sarvasyeśāaḥ sarvasyādhipatiḥ sarvamidaṃ praśāsti yadidaṃ kiṃca iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kimiyam ekā vidyā agirahasyabṛhadāraṇyakayoḥ guṇopasaṃhāraśca uta dve ime vidye guṇāupasaṃhāraśceti kiṃ
tāvatprāptam vidyābhedaḥ guṇavyavasthā ceti kutaḥ pauaruktyaprasaṅgāt bhiāsu hi śākhāsu adhyetṛveditṛbhedāt pauaruktyaparihāramālocya vidyaikatvamadhyavasāya ekatrātiriktā guṇā itaratropasaṃhriyate prāṇasaṃvādādiṣu ityuktam ekasyāṃ puaḥ śākhāyām
adhyetṛveditṛbhedābhāvāt aśakyaparihāre pauaruktye a viprakraṣṭadeśasthā ekā vidyā bhavitumarhati a ca atra ekamāmāaṃ vidyāvidhāārtham aparaṃ guṇavidhāārtham iti vibhāgaḥ saṃbhavati tadā hi
atiriktā eva guṇā itaratretaratra ca āmāyera a samāāḥ samāā api tu ubhayatrāmāyate maomayatvādayaḥ tasmāt āyoyaguṇopasaṃhāra ityevaṃ prāpte brūmahe yathā bhiāsu

a ca vidyamāe rūpābhede vidyābhedamadhyavasātuṃ śakumaḥ āpi vidyābhede guṇavyavasthāam au pauaruktyaprasaṅgāt vidyābhedodhyavasitaḥ etyucyate arthavibhāgopapatteḥ ekaṃ hi āmāaṃ vidyāvidhāārtham aparaṃ guṇavidhāārtham

doṣaḥ tadbaleaiva pradeśātarapaṭhitavidyāpratyabhijñāāt samāaguṇāmāea hi viprakṛṣṭadeśāṃ śāṇḍilyavidyāṃ pratyabhijñāpya tasyām īśāatvādi upadiśyate ayathā hi kathaṃ tasyām ayaṃ guṇavidhirabhidhīyate api ca aprāptāṃśopadeśea
arthavati vākye saṃjāte prāptāṃśaparāmarśasya ityāuvādatayāpi upapadyamāatvāt a tadbalea pratyabhijñā upekṣituṃ śakyate tasmādatra samāāyāmapi śākhāyāṃ vidyaikatvaṃ guṇopasaṃhāraścetyupapaam sambadhādevamayatrāpi saṃbadhādhikaraṇam bṛhadāraṇyakesatyaṃ brahma
ityupakramya tadyattatsatyamasausa ādityo ya eṣa etasmimaṇḍale puruṣo yaścāyaṃ dakṣiṇekṣapuruṣaḥ iti tasyaiva satyasya brahmaṇaḥ adhidaivatamadhyātmaṃ ca āyataaviśeṣamupadiśya vyāhṛtiśarīratvaṃ ca saṃpādya dve

yathā śāṇḍilyavidyāyāṃ vibhāgeāpyadhītāyāṃ guṇopasaṃhāra uktaḥ evamayatrāpi evaṃjātīyake viṣaye bhavitumarhati ekavidyābhisaṃbadhāt ekā hi iyaṃ satyavidyā adhidaivatam adhyātmaṃ ca adhītā upakramābhedāt vyatiṣaktapāṭhācca
kathaṃ tasyāmudito dharmaḥ tasyāmeva a syāt yo hyācārye kaścidaugamaādirācāraścoditaḥ sa grāmagateraṇyagate ca tulyavadeva bhavati tasmāt ubhayorapyupaiṣadoḥ ubhayatra prāptiriti evaṃ prāpte

prayogadarśaāt tasmāt cālaaṃ vidhūaamabhidhīyate cālaaṃ tu sukṛtaduṣkṛtayoḥ kaṃcitkālaṃ phalapratibadhaāt ityevaṃ prāpayya prativaktavyam hāāveva eṣa vidhūaaśabdo vartitumarhati upāyaaśabdaśeṣatvāt a hi paraparigrahabhūtayoḥ
sukṛtaduṣkṛtayoḥ aprahīṇayoḥ parairupāyaaṃ saṃbhavati yadyapi idaṃ parakīyayoḥ sukṛtaduṣkṛtayoḥ parairupāyaaṃ a āñjasaṃ saṃbhāvyate tathāpi tatsaṃkīrtaāttāvat tadāuguṇyea hāameva vidhūaaṃ āmeti irṇetuṃ śakyate
kvacidapi ca idaṃ vidhūaasaṃidhāvupāyaaṃ śrūyamāṇaṃ kuśācchadastutyupagāavat vidhūaaśrutyā sarvatrāpekṣyamāṇaṃ sārvatrikaṃ irṇayakāraṇaṃ saṃpadyate a ca cālaaṃ dhvajāgravat sukṛtaduṣkṛtayormukhyaṃ saṃbhavati adravyatvāt aśvaśca romāṇi
vidhūvāaḥ tyaja rajaḥ sahaiva tea romāṇyapi jīrṇāi śātayati aśva iva romāṇi vidhūya pāpam iti ca brāhmaṇam aekārthatvābhyupagamācca dhātūāṃ a smaraṇavirodhaḥ
taduktamiti vyākhyātam sāmparāye tartavyābhāvāttathā hyaye sāṃparāyādhikaraṇam devayāea pathā paryaṅkasthaṃ brahma abhiprasthitasya vyadhvai sukṛtaduṣkṛtayorviyogaṃ kauṣītakiaḥ paryaṅkavidyāyāmāmaati sa etaṃ devayāaṃ pathāamāsādyāgilokamāgacchati ityupakramyasa
āgacchati virajāṃ adīṃ tāṃ maasaivātyeti tatsukṛtaduṣkṛte vidhūute iti tat kiṃ yathāśrutaṃ vyadhvayeva viyogavacaaṃ pratipattavyam āhosvit ādāveva dehādapasarpaṇe iti vicāraṇāyām śrutiprāmāṇyāt
yathāśruti pratipattiprasaktau paṭhati sāṃparāya iti sāṃparāye gamaa eva dehādapasarpaṇe idaṃ vidyāsāmarthyātsukṛtaduṣkṛtahāaṃ bhavati iti pratijāīte hetuṃ ca ācaṣṭe tartavyābhāvāditi a hi
viduṣaḥ saṃparetasya vidyayā brahma saṃprepsataḥ atarāle sukṛtaduṣkṛtābhyāṃ kiṃcitprāptavyamasti yadarthaṃ katicitkṣaṇāakṣīṇe te kalpeyātām vidyāviruddhaphalatvācca vidyāsāmarthyea tayoḥ kṣayaḥ sa ca yadaiva vidyā
phalābhimukhī tadaiva bhavitumarhati tasmāt prāgeva sa ayaṃ sukṛtaduṣkṛtakṣayaḥ paścātpaṭhyate tathā hi ayepi śākhiaḥ tāṇḍiaḥ śāṭyāyaiaśca prāgavasthāyāmeva sukṛtaduṣkṛtahāamāmaati aśva iva romāṇi
vidhūya pāpam ititasya putrā dāyamupayati suhṛdaḥ sādhukṛtyāṃ dviṣataḥ pāpakṛtyām iti ca chadata ubhayāvirodhāt yadi ca dehādapasṛptasya devayāea pathā prasthitasya ardhapathe
sukṛtaduṣkṛtakṣayobhyupagamyeta tataḥ patite dehe yamaiyamavidyābhyāsātmakasya sukṛtaduṣkṛtakṣayahetoḥ puruṣayatasya icchātouṣṭhāāupapatteḥ aupapattireva taddhetukasya sukṛtaduṣkṛtakṣayasya syāt tasmāt pūrvameva sādhakāvasthāyāṃ chadatouṣṭhāaṃ tasya syāt tatpūrvakaṃ ca
sukṛtaduṣkṛtahāam iti draṣṭavyam evaṃ imittaaimittikayorupapattiḥ tāṇḍiśāṭyāyaiśrutyośca saṃgatiriti gaterarthavattvamubhayathāyathā hi virodhaḥ gaterarthavattvādhikaraṇam kvacit puṇyapāpāhāasaṃidhau devayāaḥ pathāḥ śrūyate kvacia tatra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ
hāāvaviśeṣeṇaiva devayāaḥ pathāḥ saṃipatet uta vibhāgea kvacitsaṃipatet kvacieti yathā tāvat hāāvaviśeṣeṇaiva upāyaāuvṛttiruktā evaṃ devayāāuvṛttirapi bhavitumarhatītyasyāṃ prāptau ācakṣmahe gateḥ devayāasya pathaḥ
arthavattvam ubhayathā vibhāgea bhavitumarhati kvacidarthavatī gatiḥ kvacieti a aviśeṣeṇa ayathā hi aviśeṣeṇaiva etasyāṃ gatāvaṅgīkriyamāṇāyāṃ virodhaḥ syāt puṇyapāpe vidhūya irañjaaḥ paramaṃ
sāmyamupaiti ityasyāṃ śrutau deśātaraprāpaṇī gatirvirudhyeta kathaṃ hi irañjaogatā deśātaraṃ gacchet gatavyaṃ ca paramaṃ sāmyaṃ a deśātaraprāptyāyattam ityāarthakyamevātra gatermayāmahe upapaastallakṣaṇārthopalabdherlokavat upapaaścāyam
ubhayathābhāvaḥ kvacidarthavatī gatiḥ kvacieti tallakṣaṇārthopalabdheḥ gatikāraṇabhūtorthaḥ paryaṅkavidyādiṣu saguṇeṣu upāsaeṣu upalabhyate tatra hi paryaṅkārohaṇam paryaṅkasthea brahmaṇā saha saṃvadaam viśiṣṭagadhādiprāptiśca ityevamādi bahudeśātaraprāptyāyattaṃ
phalaṃ śrūyate tatra arthavatī gatiḥ a tu samyagdarśae tallakṣaṇārthopalabdhirasti a hi ātmaikatvadarśiāmāptakāmāām ihaiva dagdhāśeṣakleśabījāām ārabdhabhogakarmāśayakṣapaṇavyatirekeṇa apekṣitavyaṃ kiṃcidasti tatra aarthikā gatiḥ
lokavacca eṣa vibhāgo draṣṭavyaḥ yathā loke grāmaprāptau deśātaraprāpaṇaḥ pathā apekṣyate a ārogyaprāptau evamihāpīti bhūyaśca eaṃ vibhāgaṃ caturthādhyāye ipuṇataramupapādayiṣyāmaḥ aiyamaḥ sarvāsāmavirodhaḥ
śabdāumāābhyām aiyamādhikaraṇam saguṇāsu vidyāsu gatirarthavatī a irguṇāyāṃ paramātmavidyāyām ityuktam saguṇāsvapi vidyāsu kāsucidgatiḥ śrūyate yathā paryaṅkavidyāyām upakosalavidyāyāṃ pañcāgividyāyāṃ daharavidyāyām iti a
ayāsu yathā madhuvidyāyāṃ śāṇḍilyavidyāyāṃ ṣoḍaśakalavidyāyāṃ vaiśvāaravidyāyām iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ yāsveṣā gatiḥ śrūyate tāsveva iyamyeta uta aiyamea sarvābhireva evaṃjātīyakābhirvidyābhirabhisaṃbadhyeteti kiṃ
tāvatprāptam iyama iti yatraiva śrūyate tatraiva bhavitumarhati prakaraṇasya iyāmakatvāt yadyayatra aśrūyamāṇāpi gatiḥ vidyātaraṃ gacchet śrutyādīāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ hīyeta sarvasya sarvārthatvaprasaṅgāt api
ca arcirādikā ekaiva gatiḥ upakosalavidyāyāṃ pañcāgividyāyāṃ ca tulyavatpaṭhyate tat sarvārthatvearthakaṃ puarvacaaṃ syāt tasmāiyama ityevaṃ prāpte paṭhati aiyama iti sarvāsāmeva abhyudayaprāptiphalāāṃ
saguṇāāṃ vidyāām aviśeṣeṇa eṣā devayāākhyā gatirbhavitumarhati au aiyamābhyupagame prakaraṇavirodha uktaḥ aiṣosti virodhaḥ śabdāumāābhyāṃ śrutismṛtibhyāmityarthaḥ tathā hi śrutiḥ tadya itthaṃ viduḥ
iti pañcāgividyāvatāṃ devayāaṃ pathāamavatārayatīye cemeraṇye śraddhā tapa ityupāsate iti vidyātaraśīliāmapi pañcāgividyāvidbhiḥ samāamārgatāṃ gamayati kathaṃ puaravagamyate vidyātaraśīliāmiyaṃ gatiriti au śraddhātapaḥparāyaṇāāmeva syāt
tamātraśravaṇāt aiṣa doṣaḥ a hi kevalābhyāṃ śraddhātapobhyām atareṇa vidyābalam eṣā gatirlabhyate vidyayā tadārohati yatra kāmāḥ parāgatāḥ a tatra dakṣiṇā yati
āvidvāṃsastapasviaḥ iti śrutyatarāt tasmāt iha śraddhātapobhyāṃ vidyātaropalakṣaṇam vājasaeyiastu pañcāgividyādhikāredhīyate ya evametadvidurye cāmī araṇye śraddhāṃ satyamupāsate iti tatra śraddhālavo ye satyaṃ
brahmopāsate iti vyākhyeyam satyaśabdasya brahmaṇi asakṛtprayuktatvāt pañcāgividyāvidāṃ ca itthaṃvittayaiva upāttatvāt vidyātaraparāyaṇāāmeva etadupādāaṃ yāyyamatha ya etau pathāau a viduste kīṭāḥ pataṅgā
yadidaṃ dadaśūkam iti ca mārgadvayabhraṣṭāāṃ kaṣṭāmadhogatiṃ gamayatī śrutiḥ devayāapitṛyāṇayoreva eā atarbhāvayati tatrāpi vidyāviśeṣādeṣāṃ devayāapratipattiḥ smṛtirapi śuklakṛṣṇe gatī hyete jagataḥ śāśvate
mate ekayā yātyaāvṛttimayayāvartate puaḥ iti yatpuaḥ devayāasya patho dvirāmāam upakosalavidyāyāṃ pañcāgividyāyāṃ ca tat ubhayatrāpi aucitaārtham tasmādaiyamaḥ yāvadadhikāram avasthitir ādhikārikāṇām yāvadadhikārādhikaraṇam
viduṣo vartamāadehapātāataraṃ dehātaram utpadyate a vā iti cityate au vidyāyāḥ sādhaabhūtāyāḥ saṃpattau kaivalyairvṛttiḥ syāt a veti eyaṃ citā upapadyate a
hi pākasādhaasaṃpattau odao bhavet a veti citā saṃbhavati āpi bhuñjāaḥ tṛpyet a veti cityate upapaā tu iyaṃ citā brahmavidām api
keṣāṃcit itihāsapurāṇayor dehātarotpattidarśaāt tathā hi apātaratamā āma vedācāryaḥ purāṇarṣiḥ viṣṇuiyogāt kalidvāparayoḥ saṃdhau kṛṣṇadvaipāyaaḥ saṃbabhūveti smarati vasiṣṭhaś ca brahmaṇo māasaḥ putraḥ
sa imiśāpādapagatapūrvadehaḥ puar brahmādeśā mitrāvaruṇābhyāṃ saṃbabhūveti bhṛgvādīām api brahmaṇa eva māasaputrāṇāṃ vāruṇe yajñe puar utpattiḥ smaryate saatkumāropi brahmaṇa eva māasaḥ
putraḥ svayaṃ rudrāya varapradāāt skadatvea prādurbabhūva evam eva dakṣaāradaprabhṛtīāṃ bhūyasī dehātarotpattiḥ kathyate tea tea imittea smṛtau śrutāv api matrārthavādayoḥ prāyeṇopalakṣyate
te ca kecit patite pūrvadehe dehātaram ādadate kecit tu sthita eva tasmi yogaiśvaryavaśāt aekadehādāayāyea sarve ca ete samadhigatasakalavedārthāḥ smaryate tat
eteṣāṃ dehātarotpattidarśaāt prāptaṃ brahmavidyāyāḥ pākṣikaṃ mokṣahetutvam ahetutvaṃ veti ata uttaram ucyate a teṣām apātaratamaḥprabhṛtīāṃ vedapravartaādiṣu lokasthitihetuṣv adhikāreṣu iyuktāām adhikāratatratvāt sthiteḥ
yathāsau bhagavā savitā sahasrayugaparyataṃ jagato dhikāraṃ caritvā tadavasāe udayāstamayavarjitaṃ kaivalyam aubhavati atha tata ūrdhva udetya aivodetā āstametaikala eva madhye sthātā
iti śruteḥ yathā ca vartamāā brahmavidaḥ ārabdhabhogakṣaye kaivalyam aubhavati tasya tāvad eva ciraṃ yāva a vimokṣye tha saṃpatsye iti śruteḥ
evam apātaratamaḥprabhṛtayo pīśvarāḥ parameśvareṇa teṣu teṣv adhikāreṣu iyuktāḥ sataḥ saty api samyagdarśae kaivalyahetau akṣīṇakarmāṇo yāvad adhikāram avatiṣṭhate tadavasāe ca apavṛjyata
ity aviruddham sakṛtpravṛttam eva hi te phalād āāya karmāśayam ativāhayataḥ svātatryeṇaiva gṛhād iva gṛhātaram ayam ayaṃ dehaṃ saṃcarataḥ svādhikārairvartaāya aparimuṣitasmṛtaya
eva dehedriyaprakṛtivaśitvāt irmāya dehā yugapat krameṇa vā adhitiṣṭhati a ca ete jātismarā ity ucyate ta evaite iti smṛtiprasiddheḥ yathā hi
sulabhā āma brahmavādiī jaakea vivaditukāmā vyudasya svaṃ deham jāakaṃ deham āviśya vyudya tea paścāt svam eva deham āviveśa iti smaryate
yadi hi upayukte sakṛtpravṛtte karmaṇi karmātaraṃ dehātarārambhakāraṇam āvirbhavet tataḥ ayad apy adagdhabījaṃ karmātaraṃ tadvad eva prasajyeteti brahmavidyāyāḥ pākṣikaṃ mokṣahetutvam ahetutvaṃ
vā śaṅkyeta a tu iyam āśaṅkā yuktā jñāāt karmabījadāhasya śrutismṛtiprasiddhatvāt tathā hi śrutiḥ bhidyate hṛdayagrathiś chidyate sarvasaṃśayāḥ kṣīyate cāsya karmāṇi
tasmi dṛṣṭe parāvare iti smṛtilambhe sarvagrathīāṃ vipramokṣaḥ iti caivamādyā smṛtirapi yathaidhāṃsi samiddho gir bhasmasāt kuruterjua jñāāgiḥ sarvakarmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute tathā
iti bījāy agyupadagdhāi a rohati yathā puaḥ jñāadagdhais tathā kleśair ātmā saṃpadyate puaḥ MBh iti caivamādyā a ca avidyādikleśadāhe sati
kleśabījasya karmāśayasya ekadeśadāhaḥ ekadeśaprarohaś ca ity upapadyate a hi agidagdhasya śālibījasya ekadeśapraroho dṛśyate pravṛttaphalasya tu karmāśayasya mukteṣor iva vegakṣayāt ivṛttiḥ
tasya tāvad eva ciram iti śarīrapātāvadhikṣepakaraṇāt tasmād upapaā yāvadadhikāram ādhikārikāṇām avasthitiḥ a ca jñāaphalasya aaikātikatā tathā ca śrutiḥ aviśeṣeṇaiva sarveṣāṃ
jñāā mokṣaṃ darśayati tad yo yo devāāṃ praty abudhyata sa eva tad abhavat tatharṣīṇāṃ tathā mauṣyāṇām iti jñāātareṣu ca aiśvaryādiphaleṣv
āsaktāḥ syur maharṣayaḥ te paścād aiśvaryakṣayadarśaea irviṇṇāḥ paramātmajñāe pariiṣṭhāya kaivalyaṃ prāpur ity upapadyate brahmaṇā saha te sarve saṃprāpte pratisaṃcare parasyāte
kṛtātmāaḥ praviśati paraṃ padam iti smaraṇāt pratyakṣaphalatvāc ca jñāasya phalavirahāśaṅkāupapattiḥ karmaphale hi svargādāv aubhavāārūḍhe syād āśaṅkā bhaved vā a veti
aubhavārūḍhaṃ tu jñāaphalam yat sāṃkṣād aparokṣād brahma iti śruteḥ tat tvam asi iti siddhavadupadeśāt a hi tattvamasi ityasya vākyasya arthaḥ
tat tvaṃ mṛto bhaviṣyasīti evaṃ pariṇetuṃ śakyaḥ taddhaitat paśya ṛṣir vāmadevaḥ pratipede haṃ maur abhavaṃ sūryaś ca iti ca samyagdarśaakālam
eva tatphalaṃ sarvātmatvaṃ darśayati tasmāt aikātikī viduṣaḥ kaivalyasiddhiḥ akṣaradhiyāṃ tvavarodhaḥ sāmāyatadbhāvābhyāmaupasadavattaduktam akṣaradhyadhikaraṇam vājasaeyake śrūyate etadvai tadakṣaraṃ gārgi brāhmaṇā abhivadatyasthūlamaaṇvahrasvamadīrghamalohitamaseham ityādi
tathā ātharvaṇe śrūyate atha parā yayā tadakṣaramadhigamyate yattadadreśyamagrāhyamagotramavarṇam ityādi tathaiva ayatrāpi viśeṣairākaraṇadvāreṇa akṣaraṃ paraṃ brahma śrāvyate tatra ca kvacit kecit
atiriktā viśeṣāḥ pratiṣidhyate tāsāṃ viśeṣapratiṣedhabuddhīāṃ kiṃ sarvāsāṃ sarvatra prāptiḥ uta vyavastheti saṃśaye śrutivibhāgāt vyavasthāprāptau ucyate akṣaraviṣayāstu viśeṣapratiṣedhabuddhayaḥ sarvāḥ sarvatrāvaroddhavyāḥ sāmāyatadbhāvābhyām
samāo hi sarvatra viśeṣairākaraṇarūpo brahmapratipādaaprakāraḥ tadeva ca sarvatra pratipādyaṃ brahma abhiaṃ pratyabhijñāyate tatra kimiti ayatra kṛtā buddhayaḥ ayatra a syuḥ
tathā caāadādayaḥ pradhāasya ityatra vyākhyātam tatra vidhirūpāṇi viśeṣaṇāi cititāi iha pratiṣedharūpāṇīti viśeṣaḥ prapañcārthaścāyaṃ citābhedaḥ aupasadavaditi idarśaam yathā jāmadagyehīe puroḍāśiīṣūpasatsu coditāsu
puroḍāśapradāamatrāṇāmagerverhotraṃ veradhvaram ityevamādīām udgātṛvedotpaāāmapi adhvaryubhirabhisaṃbadho bhavati adhvaryukartṛkatvātpuroḍāśapradāasya pradhāatatratvāccāṅgāām evamihāpi akṣaratatratvāt tadviśeṣaṇāāṃ yatra kvacidapyutpaāām akṣareṇa sarvatrābhisaṃbadha ityarthaḥ taduktaṃ prathame kāṇḍe guṇamukhyavyatikrame
tadarthatvāmukhyea vedasaṃyogaḥ ityatra iyadāmaaāt iyadadhikaraṇam dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyā samāaṃ vṛkṣaṃ pariṣasvajāte tayorayaḥ pippalaṃ svādvattyaaśaayo abhicākaśīti ityadhyātmādhikāre matramātharvaṇikāḥ śvetāśvatarāśca paṭhati
tathā kaṭhāḥ ṛtaṃ pibatau sukṛtasya loke guhāṃ praviṣṭau parame parārdhye chāyātapau brahmavido vadati pañcāgayo ye ca triṇāciketāḥ iti kimatra vidyaikatvam
uta vidyāāātvamiti saṃśayaḥ kiṃ tāvatprāptam vidyāāātvamiti kutaḥ viśeṣadarśaāt dvā suparṇā ityatra hi ekasya bhoktṛtvaṃ dṛśyate ekasya ca abhoktṛtvaṃ dṛśyateṛtaṃ pibatau
ityatra ubhayorapi bhoktṛtvameva dṛśyate tat vedyarūpaṃ bhidyamāaṃ vidyāṃ bhidyādityevaṃ prāpte bravīti vidyaikatvamiti kutaḥ yataḥ ubhayorapyaayormatrayoḥ iyattāparicchiaṃ dvitvopetaṃ vedyaṃ rūpam abhiam
āmaati au darśito rūpabhedaḥ etyucyate ubhāvapyetau matrau jīvadvitīyamīśvaraṃ pratipādayataḥ ārthātaramdvā suparṇā ityatra tāvat aaśaayo abhicākaśīti ityaśaāyādyatītaḥ paramātmā pratipādyate vākyaśeṣepi ca
sa eva pratipādyamāo dṛśyatejuṣṭaṃ yadā paśyatyayamīśamasya mahimāam itiṛtaṃ pibatau ityatra tu jīve pibati aśaāyādyatītaḥ paramātmāpi sāhacaryāt chatriyāyea pibatītyupacaryate paramātmaprakaraṇaṃ hi
etat ayatra dharmādayatrādharmāt ityupakramāt tadviṣaya eva ca atrāpi vākyaśeṣo bhavati yaḥ seturījāāāmakṣaraṃ brahma yatparam itiguhāṃ praviṣṭāvātmāau hi ityatra ca etatprapañcitam
tasmāāsti vedyabhedaḥ tasmācca vidyaikatvam api ca triṣvapyeteṣu vedāteṣu paurvāparyālocae paramātmavidyaiva avagamyate tādātmyavivakṣayaiva jīvopādāam ārthātaravivakṣayā a ca paramātmavidyāyāṃ bhedābhedavicārāvatārostītyuktam tasmātprapañcārtha eva
eṣa prayogaḥ tasmāccādhikadharmopasaṃhāra iti atarā bhūtagrāmavat svātmaaḥ ataratvādhikaraṇam yatsākṣādaparokṣādbrahma ya ātmā sarvātaraḥ ityevaṃ dviḥ uṣastakaholapraśayoḥ airataryeṇa vājasaeyiaḥ samāmaati tatra saṃśayaḥ
vidyaikatvaṃ vā syāt vidyāāātvaṃ veti vidyāāātvamiti tāvatprāptam abhyāsasāmarthyāt ayathā hi aūāatiriktārthe dvirāmāam aarthakameva syāt tasmāt yathā abhyāsātkarmabhedaḥ evamabhyāsādvidyābheda ityevaṃ prāpte
pratyāha atarā āmāāviśeṣāt svātmaaḥ vidyaikatvamiti sarvātaro hi svātmā ubhayatrāpyaviśiṣṭaḥ pṛcchayate pratyucyate ca a hi dvāvātmāau ekasmidehe sarvātarau saṃbhavataḥ tadā hi
ekasya āñjasaṃ sarvātaratvamavakalpeta ekasya tu bhūtagrāmavat aiva sarvātaratvaṃ syāt yathā ca pañcabhūtasamūhe dehe pṛthivyā āpotarāḥ adbhyastejotaramiti satyapyāpekṣiketaratve aiva mukhyaṃ sarvātaratvaṃ
bhavati tathehāpītyarthaḥ athavā bhūtagrāmavaditi śrutyataraṃ idarśayati yathā eko devāḥ sarvabhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarvavyāpī sarvabhūtātarātmā ityasmimatre samasteṣu bhūtagrāmeṣveka eva sarvātara ātmā āmāyate
evamaayorapi brāhmaṇayorityarthaḥ tasmāt vedyaikyāt vidyaikatvamiti ayathā bhedāupapattiriti ceopadeśātaravat atha yaduktam aabhyupagamyamāe vidyābhede āmāabhedāupapattiriti tatparihartavyam atrocyate āyaṃ doṣaḥ upadeśātaravadupapatteḥ yathā tāṇḍiāmupaiṣadi
ṣaṣṭhe prapāṭhake sa ātmā tattvamasi śvetaketo iti avakṛtvopyupadeśe a vidyābhedo bhavati evamihāpi bhaviṣyati kathaṃ ca avakṛtvopyupadeśe vidyābhedo a bhavati upakramopasaṃhārābhyāmekārthatāvagamāt
bhūya eva mā bhagavāvijñāpayatu iti ca ekasyaivārthasya puaḥ puaḥ pratipipādayiṣitatvea upakṣepāt āśaṅkātarairākaraṇea ca asakṛdupadeśopapatteḥ evamihāpi praśarūpābhedātatoyadārtam iti ca parisamāptyaviśeṣāt upakramopasaṃhārau
tāvadekārthaviṣayau dṛśyeteyadeva sākṣādaparokṣādbrahma iti dvitīye praśe evakāraṃ prayuñjāaḥ pūrvapraśagatamevārtham uttaratrāukṛṣyamāṇaṃ darśayati pūrvasmiṃśca brāhmaṇe kāryakaraṇavyatiriktasya ātmaaḥ sadbhāvaḥ kathyate uttarasmiṃstu tasyaiva aśaāyādisaṃsāradharmātītatvaṃ
viśeṣaḥ kathyate ityekārthatopapattiḥ tasmāt ekā vidyeti vyatihāro viśiṃṣati hītaravat vyatihārādhikaraṇam yathā tadyohaṃ sosau yosau soham ityādityapuruṣaṃ prakṛtyaitareyiṇaḥ samāmaati tathā jābālāḥ
tvaṃ vā ahamasmi bhagavo devatehaṃ vai tvamasi iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kimiha vyatihāreṇa ubhayarūpā matiḥ kartavyā uta ekarūpaiveti ekarūpaiveti tāvadāha a
hi atra ātmaa īśvareṇaikatvaṃ muktvā ayatkiṃciccitayitavyamasti yadi caivaṃ citayitavyaviśeṣaḥ parikalpyeta saṃsāriṇaśca īśvarātmatvam īśvarasya saṃsāryātmatvamiti tatra saṃsāriṇastāvadīśvarātmatve utkarṣo bhavet īśvarasya tu
saṃsāryātmatve ikarṣaḥ kṛtaḥ syāt tasmādaikarūpyameva mateḥ vyatihārāmāyastu ekatvadṛḍhīkārārtha ityevaṃ prāpte pratyāha vyatihāroyam ādhyāāyāmāyate itaravat yathā itare guṇāḥ sarvātmatvaprabhṛtayaḥ ādhyāāya āmāyate
tadvat tathā hi viśiṃṣati samāmātāraḥ ubhayoccāraṇea tvamahamasmyahaṃ ca tvamasi iti tacca ubhayarūpāyāṃ matau kartavyāyām arthavadbhavati ayathā hi idaṃ viśeṣeṇobhayāmam aarthakaṃ
syāt ekeaiva kṛtatvāt au ubhayāmāasya arthaviśeṣe parikalpyamāe devatāyāḥ saṃsāryātmatvāpatteḥ ikarṣaḥ prasajyetetyuktam aiṣa doṣaḥ aikātmyasyaiva aea prakāreṇāucityamāatvāt au evaṃ sati sa
eva ekatvadṛḍhīkāra āpadyeta a vayamekatvadṛḍhīkāraṃ vārayāmaḥ kiṃ tarhi vyatihāreṇa iha dvirūpā matiḥ kartavyā vacaaprāmāṇyāt aikarūpetyetāvat upapādayāmaḥ phalatastu ekatvamapi dṛḍhībhavati yathā
ādhyāārthepi satyakāmādiguṇopadeśe tadguṇa īśvaraḥ prasidhyati tadvat tasmādayamādhyātavyo vyatihāraḥ samāe ca viṣaye upasaṃhartavyo bhavatīti saiva hi satyādayaḥ satyādyadhikaraṇam sa yo haitaṃ
mahadyakṣaṃ prathamajaṃ veda satyaṃ brahma ityādiā vājasaeyake satyavidyāṃ saāmākṣaropāsaāṃ vidhāya aataramāmāyate tadyattatsatyamasau sa ādityo ya eṣa etasmimaṇḍale puruṣo yaścāyaṃ dakṣiṇekṣapuruṣaḥ
ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ dve ete satyavidye kiṃ vā ekaiveti dve iti tāvatprāptam bhedea hi phalasaṃyogo bhavati jayatīmāllokā iti purastāthati
pāpmāaṃ jahāti ca ityupariṣṭāt prakṛtākarṣaṇaṃ tu upāsyaikatvādityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ ekaiveyaṃ satyavidyeti kutaḥ tad yat tat satyam iti prakṛtākarṣaṇāt au vidyābhedepi
prakṛtākarṣaṇam upāsyaikatvādupapadyata ityuktam aitadevam yatra tu vispaṣṭāt kāraṇātarāt vidyābhedaḥ pratīyate tatra etadevaṃ syāt atra tu ubhayathā saṃbhavetadyattatsatyam iti prakṛtākarṣaṇāt pūrvavidyāsaṃbaddhameva
satyam uttaratra ākṛṣyata iti ekavidyātvaiścayaḥ yatpuaruktam phalātaraśravaṇādvidyātaramiti atrocyate tasyopaiṣadahaḥ aham iti ca aṅgātaropadeśasya stāvakamidaṃ phalātaraśravaṇamityadoṣaḥ api ca arthavādādeva phale kalpayitavye
sati vidyaikatve ca avayaveṣu śrūyamāṇāi bahūyapi phalāi avayaviyāmeva vidyāyām upasaṃhartavyāi bhavati tasmātsaiveyam ekā satyavidyā tea tea viśeṣeṇopetā āmātā ityataḥ sarva
eva satyādayo guṇā ekasmiprayoge upasaṃhartavyāḥ kecitpuarasmisūtre idaṃ ca vājasaeyakamakṣyādityapuruṣaviṣayaṃ vākyam chādogye caatha ya eṣotarāditye hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣo dṛśyateya eṣokṣiṇi puruṣo dṛśyate
iti udāhṛtya saiveyam akṣyādityapuruṣaviṣayā vidyā ubhayatra ekaiveti kṛtvā satyādīguṇā vājasaeyibhyaśchadogāāmupasaṃhāryā mayate taa sādhu lakṣyate chādogye hi karmasaṃbadhiī udgīthavyapāśrayā vidyā vijñāyate
tatra hi ādimadhyāvasāeṣu karmasaṃbadhicihāi bhavati iyamevargagiḥ sāma ityupakrametasyarkca sāma ca geṣṇau tasmādudgīthaḥ iti madhyeya evaṃ vidvāsāma gāyati ityupasaṃhāre aivaṃ vājasaeyake
kiṃcit karmasaṃbadhi ciham asti tatra prakramabhedāt vidyābhede sati guṇavyavasthaiva yukteti kāmādītaratra tatra cāyataādibhyaḥ kāmādyadhikaraṇam atha yad idam asmi brahmapure daharaṃ
puṇḍarīkaṃ veśma daharo smi atarākāśaḥ iti prastutya chadogā adhīyate eṣa ātmāpahatapāpmā vijaro vimṛtyur viśoko vijighatso pipāsaḥ satyakāmaḥ satyasaṃkalpaḥ ityādi tathā
vājasaeyiaḥ sa vā eṣa mahā aja ātmā yo yaṃ vijñāamayaḥ prāṇeṣu ya eṣo tar hṛdaya ākāśas tasmiñ śete sarvasya vaśī
ityādi tatra vidyaikatvaṃ parasparaguṇayogaś ca kiṃ vā eti saṃśaye vidyaikatvam iti tatredam ucyate kāmādīti satyakāmādītyarthaḥ yathā devadatto dattaḥ satyabhāmā bhāmeti
Mahābhāṣya yad etat chādogye hṛdayākāśasya satyakāmatvādiguṇajātam upalabhyate taditaratra vājasaeyake sa vā eṣa mahā aja ātmā ity atra saṃbadhyeta yac ca
vājasaeyake vaśitvādi upalabhyate tad api itaratra chādogye eṣa ātmāpahatapāpmā ity atra saṃbadhyeta kutaḥ āyataādisāmāyāt samāaṃ hi ubhayatrāpi hṛdayam āyataam samāaś
ca vedya īśvaraḥ samāaṃ ca tasya setutvaṃ lokāsaṃbhedapprayojaam ityevamādi bahusāmāyaṃ dṛśyate au viśeṣopi dṛśyate chādogye hṛdayākāśasya guṇayogaḥ vājasaeyake tu ākāśāśrayasya
brahmaṇa iti a dahara uttarebhyaḥ ity atra cchādogyepi ākāśaśabdaṃ brahmaiveti pratiṣṭhāpitatvāt ayaṃ tu atra vidyate viśeṣaḥ saguṇā hi brahmavidyā chādogye
upadiśyate atha ya ihātmāama uvidya vrajaty etāṃś ca satyākāmā ityātmavat kāmāāmapi vedyatvaśravaṇāt vājasaeyake tu irguṇameva brahma upadiśyamāaṃ dṛśyate atha urdhvaṃ
vimokṣāya brūhiasaṅgo hyayaṃ puruṣaḥ ityādipraśaprativacaasamavayāt vaśitvādi tu stutyarthameva guṇajātaṃ vājasaeyake saṃkīrtyate tathā ca upariṣṭātsa eṣa eti etyātmā ityādiā irguṇam eva
brahma upasaṃharati guṇavatastu brahmaṇa ekatvāt vibhūtipradarśaāya ayaṃ guṇopasaṃhāraḥ sūtritaḥ opāsaāya iti draṣṭavyam ādarādalopaḥ ādarādhikaraṇam chādogye vaiśvāaravidyāṃ prakṛtya śrūyate tadyadbhaktaṃ prathamamāgacchettaddhomīyaṃ
sa yāṃ prathamāmāhutiṃ juhuyāttāṃ juhuyātprāṇāya svāhā ityādi tatra pañca prāṇāhutayo vihitāḥ tāsu ca parastādagihotraśabdaḥ prayuktaḥya etadevaṃ vidvāagihotraṃ juhoti itiyatheha kṣudhitā
bālā mātaraṃ paryupāsate evaṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāyagihotramupāsate iti ca tatredaṃ vicāryate kiṃ bhojaalope lopaḥ prāṇāgihotrasya uta alopa ititadyadbhaktam iti bhaktāgamaasaṃyogaśravaṇāt bhaktāgamaasya
ca bhojaārthatvāt bhojaalope lopaḥ prāṇāgihotrasyetyevaṃ prāpte a lupyeteti tāvadāha kasmāt ādarāt tathā hi vaiśvāaravidyāyāmeva jābālāāṃ śrutiḥ pūrvotithibhyośīyāt yathā ha vai
svayamahutvāgihotraṃ parasya juhuyādevaṃ tat iti atithibhojaasya prāthamyaṃ iditvā svāmibhojaaṃ prathamaṃ prāpayatī prāṇāgihotre ādaraṃ karoti yā hi a prāthamyalopaṃ sahate atarāṃ
sā prāthamyavatogihotrasya lopaṃ saheteti mayate au bhojaārthabhaktāgamaasaṃyogādbhojaalope lopaḥ prāpitaḥ a tasya dravyaviśeṣavidhāārthatvāt prākṛte hi agihotre payaḥprabhṛtīāṃ dravyāṇāṃ iyatatvāt ihāpi agihotraśabdāt
kauṇḍapāyiāmayaavat taddharmaprāptau satyām bhaktadravyatāguṇaviśeṣavidhāārtham idaṃ vākyamtadyadbhaktam iti ato guṇalope a mukhyasyetyevaṃ prāptam bhojaalopepi adbhirvā ayea vā dravyeṇāviruddhea pratiidhāayāyea prāṇāgihotrasyāuṣṭhāamiti ata
uttaraṃ paṭhati upasthitetastadvacaāt upasthite bhojae ataḥ tasmādeva bhojaadravyāt prathamopaipatitāt prāṇāgihotraṃ irvartayitavyam kasmāt tadvacaāt tathā hi tadyadbhaktaṃ prathamamāgacchettaddhomīyam iti siddhavadbhaktopaipātaparāmarśea parārthadravyasādhyatāṃ
prāṇāhutīāṃ vidadhāti tāḥ aprayojakalakṣaṇāpaāḥ satyaḥ kathaṃ bhojaalope dravyātaraṃ pratiidhāpayeyuḥ a ca atra prākṛtāgihotradharmaprāptirasti kuṇḍapāyiāmayae himāsamagihotraṃ juhoti iti vidhyuddeśagatogihotraśabdaḥ tadvadbhāvaṃ vidhāpayediti
yuktā taddharmaprāptiḥ iha puaḥ arthavādagatogihotraśabdaḥ a tadvadbhāvaṃ vidhāpayitumarhati taddharmaprāptau ca abhyupagamyamāāyām agyuddharaṇādayopi prāpyera a ca asti saṃbhavaḥ agyuddharaṇaṃ tāvat homādhikaraṇabhāvāya
a ca ayam agau homaḥ bhojaārthatāvyāghātaprasaṅgāt bhojaārthopaītadravyasaṃbadhācca āsya eva eṣa homaḥ tathā ca jābālaśrutiḥpūrvotithibhyośīyāt iti āsyādhārāmeva imāṃ homairvṛttiṃ darśayati ata
eva ca ihāpi sāṃpādikāyevāgihotrāṅgāi darśayati ura eva vedirlomāi barhirhṛdayaṃ gārhapatyo maovāhāryapacaa āsyamāhavaīyaḥ iti vediśrutiścātra sthaṇḍilamātropalakṣaṇārthā draṣṭavyā mukhyāgihotre vedyabhāvāt tadaṅgāāṃ ca
iha saṃpipādayiṣitatvāt bhojaeaiva ca kṛtakālea saṃyogāt a agihotrakālāvarodhasaṃbhavaḥ evamayepi upasthāādayo dharmāḥ kecitkathaṃcit virudhyate tasmādbhojaapakṣa eva ete matradravyadevatāsaṃyogāt pañca homā irvartayitavyāḥ
yattu ādaradarśaavacaam tat bhojaapakṣe prāthamyavidhāārtham a hyasti vacaasya atibhāraḥ a tu aea asya ityatā śakyate darśayitum tasmāt bhojaalope lopa eva
prāṇāgihotrasyeti tairdhāraṇāiyamastaddṛṣṭeḥ pṛthagghyapratibadhaḥ phalam tairdhāraṇādhikaraṇam sati karmāṅgavyapāśrayāṇi vijñāāi omityetadakṣaramudgīthamupāsīta ityevamādīi kiṃ tāi ityāyeva syuḥ karmasu parṇamayītvādivat uta aityāi godohaādivaditi vicārayāmaḥ
kiṃ tāvatprāptam ityāīti kutaḥ prayogavacaaparigrahāt aārabhyādhītāyapi hi etāi udgīthādidvāreṇa kratusaṃbadhāt kratuprayogavacaeaiva aṅgātaravat saṃspṛśyate yattu eṣāṃ svavākyeṣu phalaśravaṇam āpayitā ha vai
kāmāāṃ bhavati ityādi tadvartamāāpadeśarūpatvādarthavādamātrameva apāpaślokaśravaṇādivat a phalapradhāam tasmāt yathāyasya parṇamayī juhūrbhavati a sa pāpaṃ ślokaṃ śrṛṇoti ityevamādīām aprakaraṇapaṭhitāāmapi juhvādidvāreṇa kratupraveśāt
prakaraṇapaṭhitavat ityatā evamudgīthādyupāsaāāmapītyevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ tairdhāraṇāiyama iti yāyetāi udgīthādikarmaguṇayāthātmyairdhāraṇāi rasatamaḥ āptiḥ samṛddhiḥ mukhyaprāṇaḥ ādityaḥ ityevamādīi aitāi ityavat karmasu iyamyera kutaḥ
taddṛṣṭeḥ tathā hi aityatvamevaṃjātīyakāāṃ darśayati śrutiḥ teobhau kuruto yaścaitadevaṃ veda yaśca a veda ityaviduṣopi kriyābhyaujñāāt prastāvādidevatāvijñāavihīāāmapi prastotrādīāṃ yājaādhyavasāadarśaāt prastotaryā devatā
prastāvamavāyattā tāṃ cedavidvāprastoṣyasitāṃ cedavidvāudgāsyasitāṃ cedavidvāpratihariṣyasi iti ca api ca evaṃjātīyakasya karmavyapāśrayasya vijñāasya pṛthageva karmaṇaḥ phalam upalabhyate karmaphalasiddhyapratibadhaḥ tatsamṛddhiḥ atiśayaviśeṣaḥ kaścit
teobhau kuruto yaścaitadevaṃ veda yaśca a veda āā tu vidyā cāvidyā ca yadeva vidyayā karoti śraddhayopaiṣadā tadeva vīryavattaraṃ bhavati iti
tatraāā tu iti vidvadavidvatprayogayoḥ pṛthakkaraṇātvīryavattaram iti ca tarappratyayaprayogāt vidyāhīamapi vīryavaditi gamyate tacca aityatve vidyāyā upapadyate ityatve tu kathaṃ tadvihīaṃ karma
vīryavadityaujñāyeta sarvāṅgopasaṃhāre hi vīryavatkarmeti sthitiḥ tathā lokasāmādiṣu pratiiyatāi pratyupāsaaṃ phalāi śiṣyate kalpate hāsmai lokā ūrdhvāścāvṛttāśca ityevamādīi a cedaṃ phalaśravaṇam arthavādamātraṃ
yuktaṃ pratipattum tathā hi guṇavāda āpadyeta phalopadeśe tu mukhyavādopapattiḥ prayājādiṣu tu itikartavyatākāṅkṣasya kratoḥ prakṛtatvāt tādarthye sati yuktaṃ phalaśruterarthavādatvam tathā aārabhyādhīteṣvapi
parṇamayītvādiṣu a hi parṇamayītvādīāmakriyātmakāām āśrayamatareṇa phalasaṃbadhovakalpate godohaādīāṃ hi prakṛtāppraṇayaādyāśrayalābhādupapaaḥ phalavidhiḥ tathā bailvādīāmapi prakṛtayūpādyāśrayalābhādupapaaḥ phalavidhiḥ a tu parṇamayītvādiṣu evaṃvidhaḥ kaścidāśrayaḥ prakṛtosti
vākyeaiva tu juhvādyāśrayatāṃ vivakṣitvā phalepi vidhiṃ vivakṣato vākyabhedaḥ syāt upāsaāāṃ tu kriyātmakatvāt viśiṣṭavidhāopapatteḥ udgīthādyāśrayāṇāṃ phale vidhāaṃ a virudhyate tasmāt yathā
kratvāśrayāṇyapi godohaādīi phalasaṃyogādaityāi evamudgīthādyupāsaāyapi iti draṣṭavyam ata eva ca kalpasūtrakārā aivaṃjātīyakāyupāsaāi kratuṣu kalpayāṃcakruḥ pradāavadeva taduktam pradāādhikaraṇam vājasaeyakevadiṣyāmyevāhamiti vāgdadhre ityatra adhyātmaṃ
vāgādīāṃ prāṇaḥ śreṣṭhovadhāritaḥ adhidaivatamagyādīāṃ vāyuḥ tathā chādogyevāyurvāva saṃvargaḥ ityatra adhidaivatam agyādīāṃ vāyuḥ saṃvargovadhāritaḥ prāṇo vāva saṃvargaḥ ityatra adhyātmaṃ vāgādīāṃ prāṇaḥ
tatra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ pṛthagevemau vāyuprāṇāvupagatavyau syātām uta apṛthagiti apṛthagiti tāvatprāptam tattvābhedāt a hi abhie tattve pṛthagaucitaaṃ yāyyam darśayati ca śrutiḥ
adhyātmamadhidaivataṃ ca tattvābhedam agirvāgbhūtvā mukhaṃ prāviśat ityārabhya tathāta ete sarva eva samāḥ sarveatāḥ iti ādhyātmikāāṃ prāṇāām ādhidaivikīṃ vibhūtimātmabhūtāṃ darśayati tathā
ayatrāpi tatra tatra adhyātmamadhidaivataṃ ca bahudhā tattvābhedadarśaaṃ bhavati kvaciccayaḥ prāṇaḥ sa vāyuḥ iti spaṣṭameva vāyuṃ prāṇaṃ ca ekaṃ karoti tathā
udāhṛtepi vājasaeyibrāhmaṇeyataścodeti sūryaḥ ityasmi upasaṃhāraślokeprāṇādvā eṣa udeti prāṇestameti iti prāṇeaiva upasaṃhara ekatvaṃ darśayatitasmādekameva vrataṃ caretprāṇyāccaivāpāyācca iti ca prāṇavrateaiva ekeopasaṃhara etadeva
draḍhayati tathā chādogyepi parastātmahātmaaścaturo deva ekaḥ kaḥ sa jagāra bhuvaasya gopāḥ ityekameva saṃvargaṃ gayamati a bravīti eka eva eṣāṃ caturṇāṃ
saṃvargaḥ aparopareṣāmiti tasmādapṛthaktvamupagamaasyetyevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ pṛthageva vāyuprāṇāvupagatavyāviti kasmāt pṛthagupadeśāt ādhyāārtho hi ayam adhyātmādhidaivavibhāgopadeśaḥ saḥ asatyādhyāapṛthaktve aarthaka eva syāt au uktam
apṛthagaucitaaṃ tattvābhedāditi aiṣa doṣaḥ tattvābhedepyavasthābhedāt upadeśabhedavaśea aucitaabhedopapatteḥ ślokopayāsasya ca tattvābhedābhiprāyeṇāpi upapadyamāasya pūrvoditadhyeyabhedairākaraṇasāmarthyābhāvātsa yathaiṣāṃ prāṇāāṃ madhyamaḥ prāṇa evametāsāṃ devatāāṃ vāyuḥ iti
ca upamāopameyakaraṇāt etea vratopayāso vyākhyātaḥ ekameva vratam iti ca evakāraḥ vāgādivrataivartaea prāṇavratapratipattyarthaḥ bhagavratāi hi vāgādīyuktāitāi mṛtyuḥ śramo bhūtvopayeme iti śruteḥ
a vāyuvrataivṛttyarthaḥathāto vratamīmāṃsā iti prastutya tulyavat vāyuprāṇayorabhagavratatvasya irdhāritatvātekameva vrataṃ caret iti ca uktvāteo etasyai devatāyai sāyujyaṃ salokatāṃ jayati iti vāyuprāptiṃ
phalaṃ bruva vāyuvratamaivartitaṃ darśayati devatetyatra vāyuḥ syāt aparicchiātmakatvasya propsatatvāt purastātprayogācca saiṣāastamitā devatā yadvāyuḥ iti tathātau vā etau dvau saṃvargau vāyureva
deveṣu prāṇaḥ prāṇeṣu iti bhedea vyapadiśatite vā ete pañcāye pañcāye daśa satastatkṛtam iti ca bhedeaiva upasaṃharati tasmātpṛthageva upagamaam pradāavat yathāidrāya
rājñe puroḍāśamekādaśakapālamidrāyādhirājāyedrāya svarājñe ityasyāṃ tripuroḍāśiyāmiṣṭausarveṣāmabhigamayaavadyatyachaṃbaṭkāram ityato vacaāt idrābhedācca sahapradāāśaṅkāyām rājādiguṇabhedāt yājyāuvākyāvyatyāsavidhāācca yathāyāsameva devatāpṛthaktvātpradāapṛthaktvaṃ bhavati evaṃ tattvābhedepi ādhyeyāṃśapṛthaktvāt ādhyāapṛthaktvamityarthaḥ taduktaṃ saṃkarṣe
āā vā devatā pṛthagjñāāt iti tatra tu dravyadevatābhedāt yāgabhedo vidyate aivamiha vidyābhedosti upakramopasaṃhārābhyām adhyātmādhidaivopadeśeṣu ekavidyāvidhāapratīteḥ vidyaikyepi tu adhyātmādhidaivabhedāt pravṛttibhedo bhavati
agihotra iva sāyaṃprātaḥkālabhedāt ityetāvadabhipretya pradāavadityuktam liṅgabhūyastvāt tad dhi balīyastād api liṅgabhūyastvādhikaraṇam vājasaeyiogirahasyeaiva vā idamagre sadāsīt ityetasmibrāhmaṇe maodhikṛtya adhīyate tatṣaṭtriṃśataṃ sahasrāṇyapaśyadātmaogīarkāmaomayāmaaścitaḥ
ityādi tathaivavākcitaḥ prāṇacitaścakṣuścitaḥ śrotracitaḥ karmacitogicitaḥ iti pṛthagagī āmaati sāṃpādikā teṣu saṃśayaḥ kimete maaścidādayaḥ kriyāupraveśiaḥ taccheṣabhūtāḥ uta svatatrāḥ kevalavidyātmakā iti tatra
prakaraṇāt kriyāupraveśe prāpte svātatryaṃ tāvatpratijāīte liṅgabhūyastvāditi bhūyāṃsi hi liṅgāi asmibrāhmaṇe kevalavidyātmakatvameṣāmupodbalayati dṛśyate tadyatkiṃcemāi bhūtāi maasā saṃkalpayati teṣāmeva sā kṛtiḥ ititāhaitāevaṃvide
sarvadā sarvāṇi bhūtāi civatyapi svapate iti ca evaṃjātīyakāi taddhi liṅgaṃ prakaraṇādbalīyaḥ tadapyuktaṃ pūrvasmikāṇḍe śrutiliṅgavākyaprakaraṇasthāasamākhyāāṃ samavāye pāradaurbalyamarthaviprakarṣāt iti pūrvavikalpaḥ prakaraṇāt syāt
kriyā māasavat aitadyuktam svatatrā etegayaḥ aayaśeṣabhūtā iti pūrvasya kriyāmayasya ageḥ prakaraṇāt tadviṣaya eva ayaṃ vikalpaviśeṣopadeśaḥ syāt a svatatraḥ au prakaraṇālliṅgaṃ
balīyaḥ satyamevametat liṅgamapi tu evaṃjātīyakaṃ a prakaraṇādbalīyo bhavati ayārthadarśaaṃ hi etat sāṃpādikāgipraśaṃsārūpatvāt ayārthadarśaaṃ ca asatyāmayasyāṃ prāptau guṇavādeāpyupapadyamāaṃ a prakaraṇaṃ bādhitumutsahate
tasmāt sāṃpādikā apyetegayaḥ prakaraṇātikrayāupraveśia eva syuḥ māasavat yathā daśarātrasya daśamehai avivākye pṛthivyā pātreṇa samudrasya somasya prajāpataye devatāyai gṛhyamāṇasya grahaṇāsādaahavaāharaṇopahvāabhakṣaṇāi māasāyeva
āmāyate sa ca māasopi grahakalpaḥ kriyāprakaraṇāt kriyāśeṣa eva bhavati evamayamapyagikalpa ityarthaḥ atideśācca atideśaśca eṣāmagīāṃ kriyāupraveśamupodbalayati ṣaṭtriṃśatsahasrāṇyagayorkāsteṣāmekaika eva tāvāyāvāasau pūrvaḥ iti
sati hi sāmāye atideśaḥ pravartate tataśca pūrveṇa iṣṭakācitea kriyāupraveśiā agiā sāṃpādikāagīatidiśa kriyāupraveśameva eṣāṃ dyotayati vidyaiva tu irdhāraṇāt tuśabdaḥ pakṣaṃ vyāvartayati
vidyātmakā eva ete svatatrā maaścidādayogayaḥ syuḥ a kriyāśeṣabhūtāḥ tathā hi irdhārayati te haite vidyācita eva itividyayā haivaita evaṃvidaścitā bhavati iti
ca darśaācca dṛśyate ca eteṣāṃ svātatrye liṅgam tatpurastāddarśitam liṅgabhūyastvāt ityatra au liṅgamapi asatyāmayasyāṃ prāptau asādhakaṃ kasyacidarthasyeti apāsya tat prakaraṇasāmarthyāt kriyāśeṣatvamadhyavasitam
ityata uttaraṃ paṭhati śrutyādibalīyastvācca a bādhaḥ aivaṃ prakaraṇasāmarthyātikrayāśeṣatvamadhyavasāya svātatryapakṣo bādhitavyaḥ śrutyāderbalīyastvāt balīyāṃsi hi prakaraṇāt śrutiliṅgavākyāīti sthitaṃ śrutiliṅgasūtre tāi ca iha
svātatryapakṣaṃ sādhayati dṛśyate katham śrutistāvat te haite vidyācita eva iti tathā liṅgam sarvadā sarvāṇi bhūtāi civatyapi svapate iti tathā vākyamapi
vidyayā haivaita evaṃvidaścitā bhavati itividyācita eva iti hi sāvadhāraṇāṃ iyaṃ śrutiḥ kriyāupraveśemīṣāmabhyupagamyamāe pīḍitā syāt au abāhyasādhaatvābhiprāyamidamavadhāraṇaṃ bhaviṣyati etyucyate tadabhiprāyatāyāṃ hividyācitaḥ
iti iyatā svarūpasaṃkīrtaeaiva kṛtatvāt aarthakamavadhāraṇaṃ bhavet svarūpameva hi eṣām abāhyasādhaatvamiti abāhyasādhaatvepi tu māasagrahavat kriyāupraveśaśaṅkāyāṃ taivṛttiphalam avadhāraṇam arthavadbhaviṣyati tathāsvapate jāgrate caivaṃvide
sarvadā sarvāṇi bhūtāyetāagīṃścivati iti sātatyadarśaam eṣāṃ svātatryevakalpate yathā sāṃpādike vākprāṇamayegihotreprāṇaṃ tadā vāci juhoti vācaṃ tadā prāṇe juhoti iti ca uktvā
ucyate ete aate amṛte āhutī jāgracca svapaṃśca satataṃ juhoti iti tadvat kriyāupraveśe tu kriyāprayogasya alpakālatvāt a sātatyea eṣāṃ prayogaḥ kalpeta
a ca idamarthavādamātramiti yāyyam yatra hi vispaṣṭo vidhāyako liṅādiḥ upalabhyate yuktaṃ tatra saṃkīrtaamātrasyārthavādatvam iha tu vispaṣṭavidhyatarāupalabdheḥ saṃkīrtaādeva eṣāṃ vijñāavidhāaṃ kalpaīyam
tacca yathāsaṃkīrtaameva kalpayituṃ śakyata iti sātatyadarśaāt tathābhūtameva kalpyate tataśca sāmarthyādeṣāṃ svātatryasiddhiḥ eteatadyatkiṃcemāi bhūtāi maasā saṃkalpayati teṣāmeva sā kṛtiḥ ityādi vyākhyātam
tathā vākyamapievaṃvide iti puruṣaviśeṣasaṃbadhameva eṣāmācakṣāṇaṃ a kratusaṃbadhaṃ mṛṣyate tasmāt svātatryapakṣa eva jyāyāiti aubadhādibhyaḥ prajñātarapṛthaktvavaddṛṣṭaśca taduktam itaśca prakaraṇamupamṛdya svātatryaṃ maaścidādīāṃ pratipattavyam
yat kriyāvayavā maaādivyāpāreṣvaubadhāti te maasaivādhīyata maasācīyata maasaiva grahā agṛhyata maasāstuvamaasāśaṃsayatkiṃca yajñe karma kriyeta yatkiṃca yajñiyaṃ karma maasaiva teṣu tamaomayeṣu maaścitsu
maomayameva kriyate ityādiā saṃpatphalo hi ayamaubadhaḥ a ca pratyakṣāḥ kriyāvayavāḥ sataḥ saṃpadā lipsitavyāḥ a ca atra udgīthādyupāsaavat kriyāṅgasaṃbadhāt tadaupraveśitvamāśaṅkitavyam śrutivairūpyāt
a hi atra kriyāṅgaṃ kiṃcidādāya tasmi ado āmādhyavasitavyamiti vadati ṣaṭtriṃśatsahasrāṇi tu maovṛttibhedā ādāya teṣvagitvaṃ grahādīṃśca kalpayati puruṣayajñādivat saṃkhyā ca iyaṃ
puruṣāyuṣasyāhaḥsudṛṣṭā satī tatsaṃbadhiīṣu maovṛttiṣvāropyata iti draṣṭavyam evamaubadhātsvātatryaṃ maaścidādīām ādiśabdāt atideśādyapi yathāsaṃbhavaṃ yojayitavyam tathā hi teṣāmekaika eva tāvāyāvāasau pūrvaḥ iti kriyāmayasyāgermāhātmyaṃ
jñāamayāāmekaikasya atidiśa kriyāyāmaādaraṃ darśayati a ca satyeva kriyāsaṃbadhe vikalpaḥ pūrveṇottareṣāmiti śakyaṃ vaktum a hi yea vyāpāreṇa āhavaīyadhāraṇādiā pūrvaḥ kriyāyāmupakaroti tea
uttare upakartuṃ śakuvati yattu pūrvapakṣepyatideśa upodbalaka ityuktam sati hi sāmāyetideśaḥ pravartata iti tat asmatpakṣepyagitvasāmāyeātideśasaṃbhavātpratyuktam asti hi sāṃpādikāāmapyagīāmagitvamiti śrutyādīi ca kāraṇāi
darśitāi evamaubadhādibhyaḥ kāraṇebhyaḥ svātatryaṃ maaścidādīām prajñātarapṛthaktvavat yathā prajñātarāṇi śāṇḍilyavidyāprabhṛtīi svea svea aubadhea aubadhyamāāi pṛthageva karmabhyaḥ prajñātarebhyaśca svatatrāṇi bhavati evamiti dṛṣṭaśca
aveṣṭeḥ rājasūyaprakaraṇapaṭhitāyāḥ prakaraṇādutkarṣaḥ varṇatrayāubadhāt rājayajñatvācca rājasūyasya taduktaṃ prathame kāṇḍe kratvarthāyāmiti cea varṇatrayasaṃyogāt iti a sāmāyādapyupalabdhermṛtyuvaa hi lokāpattiḥ yaduktaṃ māasavaditi tatpratyucyate
a māasagrahasāmāyādapi maaścidādīāṃ kriyāśeṣatvaṃ kalpyam pūrvoktebhyaḥ śrutyādihetubhyaḥ kevalapuruṣārthatvopalabdheḥ a hi kiṃcit kasyacit keacit sāmāyaṃ a saṃbhavati a ca tāvatā yathāsvaṃ
vaiṣamyaṃ ivartate mṛtyuvat yathāsa vā eṣa eva mṛtyurya eṣa etasmimaṇḍale puruṣaḥ itiagirvai mṛtyuḥ iti ca agyādityapuruṣayoḥ samāepi mṛtyuśabdaprayoge a atyatasāmyāpattiḥ
yathā caasau vāva loko gautamāgistasyāditya eva samit ityatra a samidādisāmāyāt lokasyāgibhāvāpattiḥ tadvat pareṇa ca śabdasya tādvidhyaṃ bhūyastvāttvaubadhaḥ parastādapiayaṃ vāva loka
eṣogiścitaḥ ityasmi aatare brāhmaṇe tādvidhyaṃ kevalavidyāvidhitvam śabdasya prayojaaṃ lakṣyate a śuddhakarmāṅgavidhitvam tatra hi vidyayā tadārohati yatra kāmāḥ parāgatāḥ a tatra
dakṣiṇā yati āvidvāṃsastapasvaiḥ ityaea ślokea kevalaṃ karma ida vidyāṃ ca praśaṃsa idaṃ gamayati tathā purastādapiyadetamaṇḍalaṃ tapati ityasmibrāhmaṇe vidyāpradhāatvameva lakṣyate somṛto
bhavati mṛtyurhyasyātmā bhavati iti vidyāphaleaiva upasaṃhārāt a karmapradhāatā tatsāmāyāt ihāpi tathātvam bhūyāṃstu agyavayavāḥ saṃpādayitavyā vidyāyām ityetasmātkāraṇāt agiā aubadhyate vidyā a
karmāṅgatvāt tasmāt maaścidādīāṃ kevalavidyātmakatvasiddhiḥ eka ātmaaḥ śarīre bhāvāt śarīrebhāvādhikaraṇam iha dehavyatiriktasya ātmaaḥ sadbhāvaḥ samarthyate badhamokṣādhikārasiddhaye a hi asati dehavyatirikta ātmai
paralokaphalāścodaā upapadyera kasya vā brahmātmatvamupadiśyeta au śāstrapramukha eva prathame pāde śāstraphalopabhogayogyasya dehavyatiriktasya ātmaostitvamuktam satyamuktaṃ bhāṣyakṛtā a tu tatrātmāstitve sūtramasti iha
tu svayameva sūtrakṛtā tadastitvamākṣepapuraḥsaraṃ pratiṣṭhāpitam ita eva ca ākṛṣya ācāryeṇa śabarasvāmiā pramāṇalakṣaṇe varṇitam ata eva ca bhagavatā upavarṣeṇa prathame tatre
ātmāstitvābhidhāaprasaktau śārīrake vakṣyāma ityuddhāraḥ kṛtaḥ iha ca idaṃ codaālakṣaṇeṣu upāsaeṣu vicāryamāṇeṣu ātmāstitvaṃ vicāryate kṛtsaśāstraśeṣatvapradarśaāya api ca pūrvasmiadhikaraṇe prakaraṇotkarṣābhyupagamea maaścidādīāṃ puruṣārthatvaṃ
varṇitam kosau puruṣaḥ yadarthā ete maaścidādayaḥ ity asyāṃ prasaktau idaṃ dehavyatiriktasya ātmao stitvam ucyate tadastitvākṣepārtham idam ādimaṃ sūtram ākṣepapūrvikā hi
parihāroktiḥ vivakṣite rthe sthūṇāikhaaayāyea dṛḍhāṃ buddhim utpādayed iti atra eke dehamātrātmadarśio lokāyatikāḥ dehavyatiriktasya ātmao bhāvaṃ mayamāāḥ samastavyasteṣu bāhyeṣu pṛthivyādiṣv adṛṣṭam
api caitayaṃ śarīrākārapariṇateṣu bhūteṣu syād iti saṃbhāvayatas tebhyaś caitayam madaśaktivat vijñāam caitayaviśiṣṭaḥ kāyaḥ puruṣaḥ iti ca āhuḥ a svargagamaāya apavargagamaāya
vā samartho dehavyatirikta ātmā asti yatkṛtaṃ caitayaṃ dehe syāt deha eva tu cetaaś ca ātmā ca iti pratijāate hetuṃ ca
ācakṣate śarīre bhāvād iti yad dhi yasmi sati bhavati asati ca a bhavati tat taddharmatveādhyavasīyate yathā agidharmāv auṣṇyaprakāśau prāṇaceṣṭācaitayasmṛtyādayaś ca
ātmadharmatveābhimatā ātmavādiām te pi atareva dehe upalabhyamāāḥ bahiś ca aupalabhyamāāḥ asiddhe dehavyatirikte dharmiṇi dehadharmā eva bhavitum arhati tasmād avyatireko dehād
ātmaa iti evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ vyatirekas tadbhāvābhāvitvā a tūpalabdhivat a tv etad asti yad uktam avyatireko dehādātmaa iti vyatireka eva
asya dehād bhavitum arhati tadbhāvābhāvitvāt yadi dehabhāve bhāvāt dehadharmatvam ātmadharmāṇāṃ mayeta tato dehabhāve apy abhāvād ataddharmatvam evaiṣāṃ kiṃ a mayeta
dehadharmavailakṣaṇyāt ye hi dehadharmā rūpādayas te yāvad dehaṃ bhavati prāṇaceṣṭādayas tu saty api dehe mṛtāvasthāyāṃ a bhavati dehadharmāś ca rūpādayaḥ
parair apy upalabhyate a tv ātmadharmāś caitayasmṛtyādayaḥ api ca sati hi tāvad dehe jīvadavasthāyām eṣāṃ bhāvaḥ śakyate iścetuṃ a tv
asaty abhāvaḥ patite api kadācid asmi dehe jīvadavasthāyām eṣāṃ bhāvaḥ śakyate iścetuṃ a tv asatyabhāvaḥ patite api kadācid asmi dehe
dehātarasaṃcāreṇātmadharmā auvartera saṃśayamātreṇpi parapakṣaḥ pratiṣidhyate kimātmakaṃ ca puar idaṃ caitayaṃ mayate yasya bhūtebhya utpattim icchatīti paraḥ paryauyoktavyaḥ a hi bhūtacatuṭayavyatirekeṇa
lokāyatikaḥ kiṃcit tattvaṃ pratyeti yadaubhavaaṃ bhūtabhautikāām tac caitayam iti cet tarhi viṣayatvāt teṣāṃ a taddharmatvam auvīta svātmai kriyāvirodhāt a hy
agir uṣṇaḥ sa svātmāaṃ dahati a hi aṭaḥ śikṣitaḥ sa svaskadham adhirokati a hi bhūtabhautikadharmeṇa satā caitayea bhūtabhautikāi viyīkriyera a
hi rūpādibhiḥ svarūpaṃ pararūpaṃ vā viṣayīkriyate viṣayīkriyate tu bāhyādhyātmikāi bhūtabhautikāi caitayea ataś ca yathaivāsyā bhūtabhautikaviṣayāyā upalabdher bhāvo abhyupagamyate evaṃ vyatireko
apy asyās tebhyo abhyupagatavyaḥ upalabdhisvarūpa eva ca a ātmety ātmao dehavyatiriktatvam ityatvaṃ copalabdher aikarūpyāt yat tūktaṃ śarīre bhāvāc charīradharma upalabdhir
iti tadvarṇitea prakāreṇa pratyuktam api ca satsu pradīpādiṣūpakaraṇeṣūpalabdhir bhavaty asatsu a bhavati a caitāvatā pradīpādidharma evopalabdhir bhavati evaṃ sati deha
upalabdhir bhavaty asati ca a bhavatīti a dehadhearmo bhavitum arhati upakaraṇatvamātreṇāpi pradīpādivad dehopayogopapatteḥ a cātyataṃ dehasyopalabdhāv upayogo api dṛśyate iśceṣṭo
apy asmi dehe svape āāvidhopalabdhidarśaāt tasmād aavadyaṃ dehavyatiriktasyātmao astitvam iti triṃśam aikātmyādhikaraṇam aṅgāvabaddhās tu a śākhāsu hi prativedam aṅgāvabaddhādhikaraṇam samāptā
prāsaṅgikī kathā saṃprati prakṛtāmevāuvartāmaheomityetadakṣaramudgīthamupāsītalokeṣu pañcavidhaṃ sāmopāsītaukthamukthamiti vai prajā vadati tadidamevokthamiyameva pṛthivīayaṃ vāva lokaḥeṣogiścitaḥ ityevamādyā ye udgīthādikarmāṅgāvabaddhāḥ pratyayāḥ prativedaṃ śākhābhedeṣu vihitāḥ
te tacchākhāgateṣveva udgīthādiṣu bhaveyuḥ athavā sarvaśākhāgateṣu iti viśayaḥ pratiśākhaṃ ca svarādibhedāt udgīthādibhedāupādāya ayamupayāsaḥ kiṃ tāvatprāptam svaśākhāgateṣveva udgīthādiṣu vidhīyeraiti kutaḥ saṃidhāāt
udgīthamupasīta iti hi sāmāyavihitāāṃ viśeṣākāṅkṣāyāṃ saṃikṛṣṭeaiva svaśākhāgatea viśeṣeṇa ākāṅkṣādiivṛtteḥ tadatilaṅghaea śākhātaravihitaviśeṣopādāe kāraṇaṃ āsti tasmātpratiśākhaṃ vyavasthetyevaṃ prāpte bravīti aṅgāvabaddhāstviti tuśabdaḥ pakṣaṃ
vyāvartayati aite prativedaṃ svaśākhāsveva vyavatiṣṭhera api tu sarvaśākhāsvauvartera kutaḥ udgīthādiśrutyaviśeṣāt svaśākhāvyavasthāyāṃ hiudgīthamupāsīta iti sāmāyaśrutiraviśeṣapravṛttā satī saṃidhāavaśea viśeṣe vyavasthāpyamāā pīḍitā syāt
a caitayāyyam saṃidhāāddhi śrutirbalīyasī a ca sāmāyāśrayaḥ pratyayo opapadyate tasmāt svarādibhede satyapi udgīthatvādyaviśeṣāt sarvaśākhāgateṣveva udgīthādiṣu evaṃjātīyakāḥ pratyayāḥ syuḥ matrādivadvāvirodhaḥ athavā
aivātra virodhaḥ śaṅkitavyaḥ kathamayaśākhāgateṣu udgīthādiṣu ayaśākhāvihitāḥ pratyayā bhaveyuriti matrādivat avirodhopapatteḥ tathā hi matrāṇāṃ karmaṇāṃ guṇāāṃ ca śākhātarotpaāāmapi śākhātare upasaṃgraho dṛśyate
yeṣāmapi hi śākhiāmkuṭarurasi ityaśmādāamatro āmātaḥ teṣāmapi asau viiyogo dṛśyate kukkuṭosītyaśmāamādatte kuṭarurasīti vā iti yeṣāmapi samidādayaḥ prayājā āmātāḥ teṣāmapi teṣu guṇavidhirāmāyate
ṛtavo vai prayājāḥ samāatra hotavyāḥ iti tathā yeṣāmapiajogīṣomīyaḥ iti jātiviśeṣopadeśo āsti teṣāmapi tadviṣayo matravarṇa upalabhyate chāgasya vapāyā medasoubrūhi iti tathā
vedātarotpaāāmapiagerverhotraṃ veradhvaram ityevamādimatrāṇāṃ vedātare parigraho dṛṣṭaḥ tathā bahvṛcapaṭhitasya sūktasyayo jāta eva prathamo maasvā ityasyaadhvaryave sajaīyaṃ śasyam ityatra parigraho dṛṣṭaḥ tasmāt
yathā āśrayāṇāṃ karmāṅgāāṃ sarvatrāuvṛttiḥ evam āśritāāmapi pratyayāām ityavirodhaḥ bhūmaḥ kratuvajjyāyastvaṃ tathā hi darśayati bhūmajyāyastvādhikaraṇam prācīaśāla aupamayavaḥ ityasyāmākhyāyikāyāṃ vyastasya samastasya ca
vaiśvāarasya upāsaaṃ śrūyate vyastopāsaaṃ tāvat aupamayava kaṃ tvamātmāamupāssa iti divameva bhagavo rājaiti hovācaiṣa vai sutejā ātmā vaiśvāaro yaṃ tvamātmāamupāsse ityādi
tathā samastopāsaamapi tasya ha vā etasyātmao vaiśvāarasya mūrdhaiva sutejāścakṣurviśvarūpaḥ prāṇaḥ pṛthagvartmātmā saṃdeho bahulo vastireva rayiḥ pṛthivyeva pādau ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ
kimiha ubhayathāpi upāsaaṃ syāt vyastasya samastasya ca uta samastasyaiveti kiṃ tāvatprāptam pratyavayavaṃ sutejaḥ prabhṛtiṣuupāsse iti kriyāpadaśravaṇāttasmāttava sutaṃ prasutamāsutaṃ kule dṛśyate
ityādiphalabhedaśravaṇācca vyastāyapyupāsaāi syuḥ iti prāptam tatobhidhīyate bhūmaḥ padārthopacayātmakasya samastasya vaiśvāaropāsaasya jyāyastvaṃ prādhāyea asmivākye vivakṣitaṃ bhavitumarhati a pratyekam avayavopāsaāāmapi kratuvat yathā
kratuṣu darśapūrṇamāsaprabhṛtiṣu sāmastyea sāṅgapradhāaprayoga eva eko vivakṣyate a vyastāāmapi prayogaḥ prayājādīām āpyekadeśāṅgayuktasya pradhāasya tadvat kuta etat bhūmaiva jyāyāiti tathā hi
śrutiḥ bhūmo jyāyastvaṃ darśayati ekavākyatāvagamāt ekaṃ hi idaṃ vākyaṃ vaiśvāaravidyāviṣayaṃ paurvāparyālocaātpratīyate tathā hi prācīaśālaprabhṛtaya uddālakāvasāāḥ ṣaṭ ṛṣayaḥ vaiśvāaravidyāyāṃ pariiṣṭhāmapratipadyamāāḥ aśvapatiṃ
kaikeyaṃ rājāamabhyājagmuḥ ityupakramya ekaikasya ṛṣerupāsyaṃ dyuprabhṛtīāmekaikaṃ śrāvayitvāmūrdhā tveṣa ātmaa iti hovāca ityādiā mūrdhādibhāvaṃ teṣāṃ vidadhātimūrdhā te vyapatiṣyadyamāṃ āgamiṣyaḥ ityādiā ca
vyastopāsaamapavadati puaśca vyastopāsaaṃ vyāvartya samastopāsaamevāuvartyasa sarveṣu lokeṣu sarveṣu bhūteṣu sarveṣvātmasvaamatti iti bhūmāśrayameva phalaṃ darśayati yattu pratyekaṃ sutejaḥprabhṛtiṣu phalabhedaśravaṇam tat evaṃ
sati aṅgaphalāi pradhāa evābhyuccioti iti draṣṭavyam tathāupāsse ityapi pratyavayavamākhyātaśravaṇaṃ parābhiprāyāuvādārtham a vyastopāsaavidhāārtham tasmātsamastopāsaapakṣa eva śreyāiti kecittu atra samastopāsaapakṣaṃ jyāyāṃsaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya
jyāyastvavacaādeva kila vyastopāsaapakṣamapi sūtrakāroumayata iti kalpayati tadayuktamekavākyatāvagatau satyāṃ vākyabhedakalpaasyāyāyyatvāt mūrdhā te vyapatiṣyat iti ca evamādiidāvirodhāt spaṣṭe ca upasaṃhārasthe samastopāsaāvagame tadabhāvasya
pūrvapakṣe vaktumaśakyatvāt sautrasya ca jyāyastvavacaasya pramāṇavattvābhiprāyeṇāpi upapadyamāatvāt āā śabdādibhedāt śabdādibhedādhikaraṇam pūrvasmiadhikaraṇe satyāmapi sutejaḥprabhṛtīāṃ phalabhedaśrutau samastasyopāsaaṃ jyāya ityuktam ataḥ prāptā buddhiḥ
ayāyapi bhiaśrutīyupāsaāi samasya upāsiṣyate iti api ca aiva vedyābhede vidyābhedo vijñātuṃ śakyate vedyaṃ hi rūpaṃ vidyāyāḥ dravyadaivatamiva yāgasya vedyaśca eka
eva īśvaraḥ śrutiāātvepyavagamyate maomayaḥ prāṇaśarīraḥkaṃ brahma khaṃ brahmasatyakāmaḥ satyasaṃkalpaḥ ityevamādiṣu tathāeka eva prāṇaḥprāṇo vāva saṃvargaḥprāṇo vāva jyeṣṭhaśca śreṣṭhaścaprāṇo ha pitā
prāṇo mātā ityevamādiṣu vedyaikatvācca vidyaikatvam śrutiāātvamapi asmipakṣe guṇātaraparatvāt a aarthakam tasmāt svaparaśākhāvihitam ekavedyavyapāśrayaṃ guṇajātamupasaṃhartavyaṃ vidyākārtsyāya ityevaṃ prāpte pratipādyate āeti vedyābhedepi
evaṃjātīyakā vidyā bhiā bhavitumarhati kutaḥ śabdādibhedāt bhavati hi śabdabhedaḥ vedaupāsītasa kratuṃ kurvīta ityevamādiḥ śabdabhedaśca karmabhedahetuḥ samadhigataḥ purastātśabdātare karmabhedaḥ kṛtāubadhatvāt iti
ādigrahaṇāt guṇādayopi yathāsaṃbhavaṃ bhedahetavo yojayitavyāḥ auveda ityādiṣu śabdabheda eva avagamyate ayajati ityādivat arthabhedaḥ sarveṣāmevaiṣāṃ maovṛttyarthatvābhedāt arthātarāsaṃbhavācca tat kathaṃ śabdabhedādvidyābheda iti
aiṣa doṣaḥ maovṛttyarthatvābhedepi aubadhabhedādvedyabhede sati vidyābhedopapatteḥ ekasyāpīśvarasya upāsyasya pratiprakaraṇaṃ vyāvṛttā guṇāḥ śiṣyate tathā ekasyāpi prāṇasya tatra tatra upāsyasya abhedepi ayādṛgguṇoyatropāsitavyaḥ
ayādṛgguṇaścāyatra ityevamaubadhabhedādvidhibhede sati vidyābhedo vijñāyate a ca atra eko vidyāvidhiḥ itare guṇavidhaya iti śakyaṃ vaktum viigamaāyāṃ hetvabhāvāt aekatvācca pratiprakaraṇaṃ guṇāāṃ
prāptavidyāuvādea vidhāāupapatteḥ a ca asmipakṣe samāāḥ sataḥ satyakāmādayo guṇā asakṛcchrāvayitavyāḥ pratiprakaraṇaṃ ca idaṃkāmeedamupāsitavyam idaṃkāmea ca idam iti airākāṅkṣyāvagamāt aikavākyatāpattiḥ a
ca atra vaiśvāaravidyāyāmiva samastacodaā aparā asti yadbalea pratiprakaraṇavartīyavayavopāsaāi bhūtvā ekavākyatām iyuḥ vedyaikatvaimitte ca vidyaikatve sarvatra iraṅkuśe pratijñāyamāe samastaguṇopasaṃhārośakyaḥ pratijñāyeta tasmāt
suṣṭhu ucyate āā śabdādibhedāditi sthite ca etasmiadhikaraṇe sarvavedātapratyayamityādi draṣṭavyam vikalpoviśiṣṭaphalatvāt vikalpādhikaraṇam sthite vidyābhede vicāryate kimāsāmicchayā samuccayo vikalpo vā syāt athavā
vikalpa eva iyameeti tatra sthitatvāt tāvadvidyābhedasya a samuccayaiyame kiṃcitkāraṇamasti au bhiāāmapyagihotradarśapūrṇamāsādīāṃ samuccayaiyamo dṛśyate aiṣa doṣaḥ ityatāśrutirhi tatra kāraṇam aivaṃ vidyāāṃ
kāciityatāśrutirasti tasmāa samuccayaiyamaḥ āpi vikalpaiyamaḥ vidyātarādhikṛtasya vidyātarāpratiṣedhāt pāriśeṣyāt yāthākāmyamāpadyate au aviśiṣṭaphalatvādāsāṃ vikalpo yāyyaḥ tathā hi maomayaḥ prāṇaśarīraḥkaṃ brahma khaṃ brahmasatyakāmaḥ
satyasaṃkalpaḥ ityevamādyāḥ tulyavat īśvaratvaprāptiphalā lakṣyate aiṣa doṣaḥ samāaphaleṣvapi svargādisādhaeṣu karmasu yāthākāmyadarśaāt tasmāt yāthākāmyaprāptau ucyate vikalpa eva āsāṃ bhavitumarhati a samuccayaḥ
kasmāt aviśiṣṭaphalatvāt aviśiṣṭaṃ hi āsāṃ phalamupāsyaviṣayasākṣātkaraṇam ekea ca upāsaea sākṣātkṛte upāsye viṣaye īśvarādau dvitīyamaarthakam api ca asaṃbhava eva sākṣātkaraṇasya samuccayapakṣe
cittavikṣepahetutvāt sākṣātkaraṇasādhyaṃ ca vidyāphalaṃ darśayati śrutayaḥ yasya syādaddhā a vicikitsāsti itidevo bhūtvā devāapyeti iti ca evamādyāḥ smṛtayaśca sadā tadbhāvabhāvitaḥ ityevamādyāḥ
tasmāt aviśiṣṭaphalāāṃ vidyāāmayatamāmādāya tatparaḥ syāt yāvadupāsyaviṣayasākṣātkaraṇea tatphalaṃ prāptamiti kāmyāstu yathākāmaṃ samuccīyeraa vā pūrvahetvabhāvāt kāmyādhikaraṇam aviśiṣṭaphalatvādityasya pratyudāharaṇam yāsu puaḥ kāmyāsu vidyāsusa
ya etamevaṃ vāyuṃ diśāṃ vatsaṃ veda a putrarodaṃ roditisa yo āma brahmetyupāste yāvaāmo gataṃ tatrāsya yathākāmacāro bhavati iti caivamādyāsu kriyāvat
adṛṣṭeātmaā ātmīyaṃ phalaṃ sādhayatīṣu sākṣātkaraṇāpekṣā āsti tā yathākāmaṃ samuccīyera a vā samuccīyera pūrvahetvabhāvāt pūrvasya aviśiṣṭaphalatvādityasya vikalpahetoḥ abhāvāt aṅgeṣu yathāśrayabhāvaḥ yathāśrayabhāvādhikaraṇam
karmāṅgeṣu udgīthādiṣu ye āśritāḥ pratyayā vedatrayavihitāḥ kiṃ te samuccīyera kiṃ vā yathākāmaṃ syuriti saṃśaye yathāśrayabhāva ityāha yathaiva eṣāmāśrayāḥ stotrādayaḥ saṃbhūya
bhavati evaṃ pratyayā api āśrayatatratvātpratyayāām śiṣṭeśca yathā vā āśrayāḥ stotrādayaḥ triṣu vedeṣu śiṣyate evamāśritā api pratyayāḥ opadeśakṛtopi kaścidviśeṣaḥ aṅgāāṃ tadāśrayāṇāṃ
ca pratyayāāmityarthaḥ samāhārāt hotṛṣadaāddhaivāpi durudgītamausamāharati iti ca praṇavodgīthaikatvavijñāamāhātmyāt udgātā svakarmaṇyutpaaṃ kṣataṃ hautrātkarmaṇaḥ pratisamādadhāti iti bruva vedātaroditasya pratyayasya vedātaroditapadārthasaṃbadhasāmāyāt sarvavedoditapratyayopasaṃhāraṃ sūcayati
iti liṅgadarśaam guṇasādhāraṇyaśruteśca vidyāguṇaṃ ca vidyāśrayaṃ satam oṃkāraṃ vedatrayasādhāraṇaṃ śrāvayati teeyaṃ trayī vidyā vartata omityāśrāvayatyomiti śaṃsatyomityudgāyati iti ca tataśca āśrayasādhāraṇyāt
āśritasādhāraṇyamiti liṅgadarśaameva athavā guṇasādhāraṇyaśruteśceti yadīme karmaguṇā udgīthādayaḥ sarve sarvaprayogasādhāraṇā a syuḥ a syāt tataḥ tadāśrayāṇāṃ pratyayāāṃ sahabhāvaḥ te tu udgīthādayaḥ
sarvāṅgagrāhiṇā prayogavacaea sarve sarvaprayogasādhāraṇāḥ śrāvyate tataśca āśrayasahabhāvātpratyayasahabhāva iti a vā tatsahabhāvāśruteḥ a veti pakṣavyāvartaam a yathāśrayabhāva āśritāāmupāsaāāṃ bhavitumarhati kutaḥ tatsahabhāvāśruteḥ
yathā hi trivedavihitāāmaṅgāāṃ stotrādīāṃ sahabhāvaḥ śrūyate grahaṃ vā gṛhītvā camasaṃ voīya stotramupākaroti stutamauśaṃsati prastotaḥ sāma gāya hotaretadyaja ityādiā aivamupāsaāāṃ sahabhāvaśrutirasti
au prayogavacaa eṣāṃ sahabhāvaṃ prāpayet eti brūmaḥ puruṣārthatvādupāsaāām prayogavacao hi kratvarthāāmudgīthādīāṃ sahabhāvaṃ prāpayet udgīthādyupāsaāi tu kratvarthāśrayāṇyapi godohaādivat puruṣārthāītyavocāmapṛthagghyapratibadhaḥ phalam ityatra
ayameva ca upadeśāśrayo viśeṣaḥ aṅgāāṃ tadālambaāāṃ ca upāsaāām yadekeṣāṃ kratvarthatvam ekeṣāṃ puruṣārthatvamiti paraṃ ca liṅgadvayam akāraṇamupāsaasahabhāvasya śrutiyāyābhāvāt a ca pratiprayogam
āśrayakārtsyopasaṃhārādāśritāāmapi tathātvaṃ vijñātuṃ śakyam atatprayuktatvādupāsaāām āśrayatatrāṇyapi hi upāsaāi kāmam āśrayābhāve mā bhūva a tvāśrayasahabhāvea sahabhāvaiyamamarhati tatsahabhāvāśrutereva tasmāt yathākāmameva upāsaāyauṣṭhīyera darśaācca
darśayati ca śrutirasahabhāvaṃ pratyayāām evaṃviddha vai brahmā yajñaṃ yajamāaṃ sarvāṃścartvijobhirakṣati iti sarvapratyayopasaṃhāre hi sarve sarvavida iti a vijñāavatā brahmaṇā paripālyatvamitareṣāṃ
saṃkīrtyeta tasmāt yathākāmamupāsaāāṃ samuccayo vikalpo veti iti śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācāryasya śrīgovidabhagavatpūjyapādaśiṣyasya śrīmacchaṃkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīrakamīmāṃsāsūtrabhāṣye tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ puruṣārtho taḥ
śabdād iti bādarāyaṇaḥ puruṣārthādhikaraṇam puruṣārtho ta iti asmād vedātavihitād ātmajñāāt svatatrāt puruṣārthaḥ sidhyatīti bādarāyaṇa ācāryo mayate kuta etad avagamyate śabdād
ityāha tathā hi tarati śokamātmavit sa yo ha vai tat paramaṃ brahma veda brahmaiva bhavati brahmavid āpoti param ācāryavā puruṣo
veda tasya tāvad eva ciraṃ yāva a vimokṣye tha saṃpatsye ya ātmāpahatapāpmā ityupakramya sa sarvāṃśca lokā āpoti sarvāṃś ca kāmā
yas tam ātmāam auvidya vijāāti iti ātmā vā are draṣṭavyaḥ ity upakramya etāvad are khalv amṛtatvam iti evaṃjātīyakā śrutiḥ kevalāyā
vidyāyāḥ puruṣārthahetutvaṃ śrāvayati athātra pratyavatiṣṭhate śeṣatvāt puruṣārthavādo yathā yeṣv iti jaimiiḥ kartṛtvea ātmaaḥ karmaśeṣatvāt tadvijñāam api vrīhiprokṣaṇādivat viṣayadvāreṇa karmasaṃbadhy eva
ity ataḥ tasmi avagataprayojae ātmajñāe yā phalaśrutiḥ sā arthavādaḥ iti jaimiir ācāryo mayate yathā ayeṣu dravyasaṃskārakarmasu yasya parṇamayī juhūr bhavati
a sa pāpaṃ ślokaṃ śrṛṇoti yadāṅkte cakṣureva bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte yatprayājāūyājā ijyate varma vā etadyajñasya kriyate varma yajamāāya bhrātṛvyābhibhūtyai ityevaṃjātīyakā phalaśrutiḥ
arthavādaḥ tadvat kathaṃ puaḥ asya aārabhyādhītasya ātmajñāasya prakaraṇādīāmayatameāpi hetuā viā kratupraveśa āśaṅkyate kartṛdvāreṇa vākyāt tadvijñāasya kratusaṃbadha iti cet a vākyādviiyogāupapatteḥ
avyabhicāriṇā hi keaciddvāreṇa aārabhyādhītāāmapi vākyaimittaḥ kratusaṃbadhovakalpate kartā tu vyabhicāri dvāram laukikavaidikakarmasādhāraṇyāt tasmāa taddvāreṇa ātmajñāasya kratusaṃbadhasiddhiriti a vyatirekavijñāasya vaidikebhyaḥ karmabhyoyatra aupayogāt
a hi dehavyatiriktātmajñāaṃ laukikeṣu karmasu upayujyate sarvathā dṛṣṭārthapravṛttyupapatteḥ vaidikeṣu tu dehapātottarakālaphaleṣu dehavyatiriktātmajñāamatareṇa pravṛttiḥ opapadyata iti upayujyate vyatirekavijñāam au apahatapāpmatvādiviśeṣaṇāt asaṃsāryātmaviṣayam
aupaiṣadaṃ darśaaṃ a pravṛttyaṅgaṃ syāt a priyādisaṃsūcitasya saṃsāriṇa eva ātmao draṣṭavyatvopadeśāt apahatapāpmatvādi viśeṣaṇaṃ tu stutyarthaṃ bhaviṣyati au tatra tatra prasādhitametat
adhikamasaṃsāri brahma jagatkāraṇam tadeva ca saṃsāriṇa ātmaaḥ pāramārthikaṃ svarūpam upaiṣatsu upadiśyata iti satyaṃ prasādhitam tasyaiva tu sthūṇāikhaaavat phaladvāreṇa ākṣepasamādhāe kriyete
dārḍhyāya ācāradarśaāt jaako ha vaideho bahudakṣiṇea yajñeeje yakṣyamāṇo vai bhagavato ham asmi ity evamādīi brahmavidām api ayapareṣu vākyeṣu karmasaṃbadhadarśaāi bhavati
tathā uddālakādīām api putrāuśāsaādidarśaāt gārhasthyasaṃbadho vagamyate kevalāc cet jñāāt puruṣārthasiddhiḥ syāt kimartham aekāyāsasamavitāi karmāṇi te kuryuḥ atke cemadhu videta kimarthaṃ
parvataṃ vrajet iti yāyāt tacchruteḥ yadeva vidyayā karoti śraddhayopaiṣadā tadeva vīryavattaraṃ bhavati iti ca karmaśeṣatvaśravaṇāt vidyāyā a kevalāyāḥ puruṣārthahetutvam samavārambhaṇāt
taṃ vidyākarmaṇī samavārabhete iti ca vidyākarmaṇoḥ phalārambhe sāhityadarśaāt a svātatryaṃ vidyāyāḥ tadvato vidhāāt ācāryakulādvedamadhītya yathāvidhāaṃ guroḥ karmātiśeṣeṇābhisamāvṛtya kuṭumbe śucau deśe
svādhyāyamadhīyāaḥ iti ca evaṃjātīyakā śrutiḥ samastavedārthavijñāavataḥ karmādhikāraṃ darśayati tasmādapi a vijñāasya svātatryeṇa phalahetutvam au atra adhītya ityadhyayaamātraṃ vedasya śrūyate a
arthavijñāam aiṣa doṣaḥ dṛṣṭārthatvāt vedādhyayaam arthāvabodhaparyatamiti sthitam iyamācca kurvaeveha karmāṇi jijīviṣecchataṃ samāḥ evaṃ tvayi āyathetosti a karma lipyate are iti
tathā etadvai jarāmaryaṃ satraṃ yadagihotraṃ jarayā vā hyevāsmāmucyate mṛtyuā vā ityevaṃjātīyakāt iyamādapi karmaśeṣatvameva vidyāyā iti evaṃ prāpte pratividhatte adhikopadeśāttu bādarāyaṇasyaivaṃ
taddarśaāt tuśabdāt pakṣo viparivartate yaduktam śeṣatvātpuruṣārthavādaḥ iti tat opapadyate kasmāt adhikopadeśāt yadi saṃsāryeva ātmā śārīraḥ kartā bhoktā ca śarīramātravyatirekeṇa vedāteṣu
upadiṣṭaḥ syāt tato varṇitea prakāreṇa phalaśruterarthavādatvaṃ syāt adhikastāvat śārīrādātmaaḥ asaṃsārī īśvaraḥ kartṛtvādisaṃsāridharmarahitopahatapāpmatvādiviśeṣaṇaḥ paramātmā vedyatveopadiśyate vedāteṣu a ca tadvijñāaṃ karmaṇāṃ pravartakaṃ
bhavati pratyuta karmāṇyucchiatti iti vakṣyati upamardaṃ ca ityatra tasmāt puruṣārthotaḥ śabdāt iti yamataṃ bhagavato bādarāyaṇasya tat tathaiva tiṣṭhati a śeṣatvaprabhṛtibhirhetvābhāsaiścālayituṃ
śakyate tathā hi tamadhikaṃ śārīrāt īśvaramātmāaṃ darśayati śrutayaḥ yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvavit bhīṣāsmādvātaḥ pavate mahadbhayaṃ vajramudyatam etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsae gārgi
tadaikṣata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti tattejosṛjata ityevamādyāḥ yattu priyādisaṃsūcitasya saṃsāriṇa eva ātmao vedyatayā aukarṣaṇam ātmaastu kāmāya sarvaṃ priyaṃ bhavati ātmā vā
are draṣṭavyaḥ yaḥ prāṇea prāṇiti sa ta ātmā sarvātaraḥ ya eṣokṣiṇi puruṣo dṛśyate ityupakramya etaṃ tveva te bhūyouvyākhyāsyāmi iti caivamādi
tadapi asya mahato bhūtasya iḥśvasitametadyadṛgvedaḥ yośaāyāpipāse śokaṃ mohaṃ jarāṃ mṛtyumatyeti paraṃ jyotirupasaṃpadya svea rūpeṇābhiiṣpadyate sa uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ ityevamādibhirvākyaśeṣaiḥ satyāmeva adhikopadidikṣāyām
atyatābhedābhiprāyamityavirodhaḥ pārameśvarameva hi śārīrasya pāramārthikaṃ svarūpam upādhikṛtaṃ tu śārīratvam tattvamasi āyadatosti draṣṭṛ ityādiśrutibhyaḥ sarvaṃ ca etat vistareṇāsmābhiḥ purastāt tatra tatra
varṇitam tulyaṃ tu darśaam yattūktam ācāradarśaātkarmaśeṣo vidyeti atra brūmaḥ tulyamācāradarśaam akarmaśeṣatvepi vidyāyāḥ tathā hi śrutirbhavati etaddha sma vai tadvidvāṃsa āhuṛrṣayaḥ
kāvaṣeyāḥ kimarthā vayamadhyeṣyāmahe kimarthā vayaṃ yakṣyāmahe etaddha sma vai tatpūrve vidvāṃsogihotraṃ a juhavāṃcakrire etaṃ vai tamātmāaṃ viditvā brāhmaṇāḥ putraiṣaṇāyāśca vittaiṣaṇāyāśca
lokaiṣaṇāyāśca vyutthāyātha bhikṣācaryaṃ carati ityevaṃjātīyakā yājñavalkyādīām api brahmavidām akarmaiṣṭhatvaṃ dṛśyate etāvadare khalvamṛtatvamiti hoktvā yājñavalkyaḥ pravavrāja ityādiśrutibhyaḥ api ca yakṣyamāṇo vai
bhagavatohamasmi ityetat liṅgadarśaaṃ vaiśvāaravidyāviṣayam saṃbhavati ca sopādhikāyāṃ brahmavidyāyāṃ karmasāhityadarśaam a tu atrāpi karmāṅgatvamasti prakaraṇādyabhāvāt yatpuaruktam tacchruteḥ iti atra brūmaḥ asārvatrikī
yadeva vidyayā karoti ityeṣā śrutira sarvavidyāviṣayā prakṛtavidyābhisaṃbadhāt prakṛtā ca udgīthavidyā omityetadakṣaramudgīthamupāsīta ityatra vibhāgaḥ śatavat yadapyuktam taṃ vidyākarmaṇī samavārabhete ityetat samavārambhavacaam
asvātatrye vidyāyā liṅgamiti tat pratyucyate vibhāgotra draṣṭavyaḥ vidyā ayaṃ puruṣamavārabhate karma ayamiti śatavat yathā śatam ābhyāṃ dīyatāmityukte vibhajya dīyate pañcāśadekasmai
pañcāśadaparasmai tadvat a ca idaṃ samavārambhavacaaṃ mumukṣuviṣayam iti u kāmayamāaḥ iti saṃsāriviṣayatvopasaṃhārāt athākāmayamāaḥ iti ca mumukṣoḥ pṛthagupakramāt tatra saṃsāriviṣaye vidyā
vihitā pratiṣiddhā ca parigṛhyate viśeṣābhāvāt karmāpi vihitaṃ pratiṣiddhaṃ ca yathāprāptāuvāditvāt evaṃ sati avibhāgeāpi idaṃ samavārambhavacaamavakalpate yaccaitat tadvato vidhāāt iti ata
uttaraṃ paṭhati adhyayaamātravataḥ ācāryakulādvedamadhītya ityatra adhyayaamātrasya śravaṇāt adhyayaamātrakṣavata eva karmavidhirityadhyavasyāmaḥ au evaṃ sati avidyatvāt aadhikāraḥ karmasu prasajyeta aiṣa doṣaḥ a
vayam adhyayaaprabhavaṃ karmāvabodhaam adhikārakāraṇaṃ vārayāmaḥ kiṃ tarhi aupaiṣadamātmajñāam svātatryeṇaiva prayojaavat pratīyamāam a karmādhikārakāraṇatāṃ pratipadyate ityetatpratipādayāmaḥ yathā ca a kratvatarajñāaṃ kratvatarādhikāreṇa
apekṣyate evametadapi draṣṭavyamiti yadapyuktam iyamācca iti atrābhidhīyate āviśeṣāt kurvaeveha karmāṇi jijīviṣet ityevamādiṣu iyamaśravaṇeṣu a viduṣa iti viśeṣosti aviśeṣeṇa iyamavidhāāt stutayeumatirvā
kurvaeveha karmāṇi ityatra aparo viśeṣa ākhyāyate yadyapi atra prakaraṇasāmarthyāt vidvāeva kurva iti saṃbadhyeta tathāpi vidyāstutaye karmāujñāam etaddraṣṭavyam a karma lipyate
are iti hi vakṣyati etaduktaṃ bhavati yāvajjīvaṃ karma kurvatyapi tvayi viduṣi puruṣe a karma lepāya bhavati vidyāsāmarthyāditi tadevaṃ vidyā stūyate
kāmakāreṇa caike api ca eke vidvāṃsaḥ pratyakṣīkṛtavidyāphalāḥ sataḥ tadavaṣṭambhāt phalātarasādhaeṣu prajādiṣu prayojaābhāvaṃ parāmṛśati kāmakāreṇa iti śrutirbhavati vājasaeyiām etaddha sma vai
tatpūrve vidvāṃs upamardaṃ ca api ca karmādhikārahetoḥ kriyākārakaphalalakṣaṇasya samastasya prapañcasya avidyākṛtasya vidyāsāmarthyāt svarūpopamardamāmaati yatra tvasya sarvamātmaivābhūttatkea kaṃ paśyettatkea kaṃ jighret
ityādiā vedātoditātmajñāapūrvikāṃ tu karmādhikārasiddhiṃ pratyāśāsāasya karmādhikārocchittireva prasajyeta tasmādapi svātatryaṃ vidyāyāḥ ūrdhvaretaḥsu ca śabde hi ūrdhvaretaḥsu ca āśrameṣu vidyā śrūyate a
ca tatra karmāṅgatvaṃ vidyāyā upapadyate karmābhāvāt a hi agihotrādīi vaidikāi karmāṇi teṣāṃ sati syādetat ūrdhvaretasa āśramā a śrūyate veda iti
tadapi āsti tepi hi vaidikeṣu śabdeṣvavagamyate trayo dharmaskadhāḥ ye cemeraṇye śraddhā tapa ityupāsate tapaḥśraddhe ye hyupavasatyaraṇye etameva pravrājio lokamicchataḥ pravrajati
brahmacaryādeva pravrajet ityevamādiṣu pratipaāpratipaagārhasthyāām apākṛtāapākṛtarṇatrayāṇāṃ ca ūrdhvaretastvaṃ śrutismṛtiprasiddham tasmādapi svātatryaṃ vidyāyāḥ parāmarśaṃ jaimiiracodaā cāpavadati hi parāmarśādhikaraṇam trayo dharmaskadhāḥ ityādayo ye
śabdā ūrdhvaretasāmāśramāṇāṃ sadbhāvāya udāhṛtāḥ a te tatpratipādaāya prabhavati yataḥ parāmarśam eṣu śabdeṣvāśramātarāṇāṃ jaimiirācāryo mayate a vidhim kutaḥ a hi atra
liṅādīāmayatamaścodaāśabdosti arthātaraparatvaṃ ca eṣu pratyekamupalabhyate trayo dharmaskadhāḥ ityatra tāvat yajñodhyayaaṃ dāamiti prathamastapa eva dvitīyo brahmacāryācāryakulavāsī tṛtīyotyatamātmāamācāryakulevasādayasarva ete puṇyalokā bhavati iti
parāmarśapūrvakamāśramāṇāmaātyatikaphalatvaṃ saṃkīrtya ātyatikaphalatayā brahmasaṃsthatā stūyate brahmasaṃsthomṛtatvameti iti au parāmarśepi āśramā gamyata eva satyaṃ gamyate smṛtyācārābhyāṃ tu teṣāṃ prasiddhiḥ a pratyakṣaśruteḥ
ataśca pratyakṣaśrutivirodhe sati aādaraṇīyāste bhaviṣyati aadhikṛtaviṣayā vā au gārhasthyamapi sahaivordhvaretobhiḥ parāmṛṣṭam yajñodhyayaaṃ dāamiti prathamaḥ iti satyamevam tathāpi tu gṛhasthaṃ pratyeva
agihotrādīāṃ karmaṇāṃ vidhāāt śrutiprasiddhameva hi tadastitvam tasmātstutyartha eva ayaṃ parāmarśaḥ a codaārthaḥ api ca apavadati hi pratyakṣā śrutirāśramātaram vīrahā vā
eṣa devāāṃ yogimudvāsayate ācāryāya priyaṃ dhaamāhṛtya prajātatuṃ mā vyavacchetsīḥ āputrasya lokostīti tatsarve paśavo viduḥ ityevamādyā tathā ye cemeraṇye śraddhā tapa
ityupāsate tapaḥśraddhe ye hyupavasatyaraṇye iti ca devayāopadeśaḥ a āśramātaropadeśaḥ saṃdigdhaṃ ca āśramātarābhidhāam tapa eva dvitīyaḥ ityevamādiṣu tathā etameva pravrājio lokamicchataḥ
pravrajati iti lokasaṃstavoyam a pārivrājyavidhiḥ au brahmacaryādeva pravrajet iti vispaṣṭamidaṃ pratyakṣaṃ pārivrājyavidhāaṃ jābālāām satyamevametat aapekṣya tu etāṃ śrutim ayaṃ vicāra
iti draṣṭavyam auṣṭheyaṃ bādarāyaṇaḥ sāmyaśruteḥ auṣṭheyam āśramātaraṃ bādarāyaṇa ācāryo mayate vedeśravaṇādagihotrādīāṃ ca avaśyāuṣṭheyatvāt tadvirodhādaadhikṛtāuṣṭheyamāśramātaram iti hi imāṃ matiṃ irākaroti gārhasthyavadeva
āśramātaramapi aicchatā pratipattavyamiti mayamāaḥ kutaḥ sāmyaśruteḥ samā hi gārhasthyeāśramātarasya parāmarśaśrutirdṛśyate trayo dharmaskadhāḥ ityādyā yathā iha śrutyataravihitameva gārhasthyaṃ parāmṛṣṭam evamāśramātaramapīti pratipattavyam
yathā ca śāstrātaraprāptayoreva ivītaprācīāvītayoḥ parāmarśa upavītavidhipare vākye tasmāt tulyamauṣṭheyatvaṃ gārhasthyea āśramātarasya tathā etameva pravrājio lokamicchataḥ pravrajati ityasya vedāuvacaādibhiḥ samabhivyāhāraḥ ye
cemeraṇye śraddhā tapa ityupāsate ityasya ca pañcāgividyayā yattūktam tapa eva dvitīyaḥ ityādiṣvāśramātarābhidhāaṃ saṃdigdhamiti aiṣa doṣaḥ iścayakāraṇasadbhāvāt trayo dharmaskadhāḥ iti hi
dharmaskadhatritvaṃ pratijñātam a ca yajñādayo bhūyāṃso dharmā utpattibhiāḥ sataḥ ayatrāśramasaṃbadhāt tritvetarbhāvayituṃ śakyate tatra yajñādiliṅgo gṛhāśrama eko dharmaskadho irdiṣṭaḥ brahmacārīti ca
spaṣṭa āśramairdeśaḥ tapa ityapi koyastapaḥpradhāādāśramāt dharmaskadhobhyupagamyeta ye cemeraṇye iti ca araṇyaliṅgāt śraddhātapobhyāmāśramagṛhītiḥ tasmāt parāmarśepyauṣṭheyamāśramātaram vidhirvā dhāraṇavat vidhirvā ayamāśramātarasya a parāmarśamātram
au vidhitvābhyupagame ekavākyatāpratītiruparudhyeta pratīyate caṃ atra ekavākyatā puṇyalokaphalāstrayo dharmaskadhāḥ brahmasaṃsthatā tvamṛtatvaphaleti satyametat satīmapi tu ekavākyatāpratītiṃ parityajya vidhirevābhyupagatavyaḥ apūrvatvāt vidhyatarasyādarśaāt vispaṣṭāccāśramātarapratyayāt
guṇavādakalpaayā ekavākyatvayojaāupapatteḥ dhāraṇavat yathā adhastātsamidhaṃ dhārayaaudravedupari hi devebhyo dhārayati ityatra satyāmapyadhodhāraṇea ekavākyatāpratītau vidhīyata eva uparidhāraṇam apūrvatvāt tathā ca uktaṃ śeṣalakṣaṇe
vidhistu dhāraṇepūrvatvāt iti tadvat ihāpi āśramaparāmarśaśrutiḥ vidhireveti kalpyate yadāpi parāmarśa evāyamāśramātarāṇām tadāpi brahmasaṃsthatā tāvat saṃstavasāmarthyādavaśyaṃ vidheyā abhyupagatavyā sā ca kiṃ
caturṣvāśrameṣu yasya kasya cit āhosvitparivrājakasyaiveti vivektavyam yadi ca brahmacaryāteṣvāśrameṣu parāmṛśyamāeṣu parivrājakopi parāmṛṣṭaḥ tataścaturṇāmapyāśramāṇāṃ parāmṛṣṭatvāviśeṣāt aāśramitvāupapatteśca yaḥ kaściccaturṣvāśrameṣu brahmasaṃstho bhaviṣyati atha
a parāmṛṣṭaḥ tataḥ pariśiṣyamāṇaḥ parivrāḍeva brahmasaṃstha iti setsyati tatra tapaḥśabdea vaikhāasagrāhiṇā parāmṛṣṭaḥ parivrāḍapi iti kecit tadayuktam a hi satyāṃ gatau
vāaprasthaviśeṣaṇea parivrājako grahaṇamarhati yathā atra brahmacārigṛhamedhiau asādhāraṇeaiva svea svea viśeṣaṇea viśeṣitau evaṃ bhikṣuvaikhāasāvapīti yuktam tapaśca asādhāraṇo dharmo vāaprasthāāṃ kāyakleśapradhāatvāt tapaḥśabdasya
tatra rūḍheḥ bhikṣostu dharma idriyasaṃyamādiḥ lakṣaṇayaiva tapaḥśabdeābhilapyeta catuṣṭvea ca prasiddhā āśramāḥ tritvea parāmṛśyata ityayāyyam api ca bhedavyapadeśotra bhavati traya ete
puṇyalokabhājaḥ ekomṛtatvabhāgiti pṛthaktve ca bhedavyapadeśovakalpate a hyevaṃ bhavati devadattayajñadattau madaprajñau ayatarastvaayormahāprajña iti bhavati tvevam devadattayajñadattau madaprajñau viṣṇumitras tu mahāprajña iti
tasmāt pūrve traya āśramiṇaḥ puṇyalokabhājaḥ pariśiṣyamāṇaḥ parivrāṭ amṛtatvabhāk kathaṃ puaḥ brahmasaṃsthaśabdo yogātpravartamāaḥ sarvatra saṃbhava parivrājaka evāvatiṣṭheta rūḍhyabhyupagame ca āśramamātrādamṛtatvaprāpterjñāāarthakyaprasaṅga iti
atrocyate brahmasaṃstha iti hi brahmaṇi parisamāptiḥ aayavyāpāratārūpaṃ taiṣṭhatvamabhidhīyate tacca trayāṇāmāśramāṇāṃ a saṃbhavati svāśramavihitakarmāauṣṭhāe pratyavāyaśravaṇāt parivrājakasya tu sarvakarmasaṃyāsāt pratyavāyo a saṃbhavati
aauṣṭhāaimittaḥ śamadamādistu tadīyo dharmo brahmasaṃsthāyā upodbalakaḥ a virodhī brahmaiṣṭhatvameva hi tasya śamadamādyupabṛṃhitaṃ svāśramavihitaṃ karma yajñādīi ca itareṣām tadvyatikrame ca tasya
pratyavāyaḥ tathā ca yāsa iti brahmā brahmā hi paraḥ paro hi brahmā tāi vā etāyavarāṇi tapāṃsi yāsa evātyarecayat vedātavijñāasuiścitārthāḥ saṃyāsayogādyatayaḥ
śuddhasattvāḥ ityādyāḥ śrutayaḥ smṛtayaśca tadbuddhayastadātmāastaiṣṭhāstatparāyaṇāḥ ityādyāḥ brahmasaṃsthasya karmābhāvaṃ darśayati tasmāt parivrājakasya āśramamātrādamṛtatvaprāpterjñāāarthakyaprasaṅga ityeṣopi doṣo āvatarati tadevaṃ parāmarśepi itareṣāmāśramāṇām pārivrājyaṃ tāvadbrahmasaṃsthatālakṣaṇaṃ
labhyetaiva aapekṣyaiva jābālaśrutimāśramātaravidhāyiīm ayamācāryeṇa vicāraḥ pravartitaḥ vidyata eva tu āśramātaravidhiśrutiḥ pratyakṣā brahmacaryaṃ samāpya gṛhī bhavedgṛhī bhūtvā vaī bhavedvaī bhūtvā pravrajet
yadi vetarathā brahmacaryādeva pravrajedgṛhādvā vaādvā iti a ca iyaṃ śrutiḥ aadhikṛtaviṣayā śakyā vaktum aviśeṣaśravaṇāt pṛthagvidhāācca aadhikṛtāām atha pua reva vratī
vāvratī vā sātako vāsātako votsaāgiraagiko vā ityādiā brahmajñāaparipākāṅgatvācca pārivrājyasya a aadhikṛtaviṣayatvam tacca darśayati atha parivrāḍvivarṇavāsā muṇḍoparigrahaḥ śuciradrohī bhaikṣāṇo brahmabhūyāya bhavati
iti tasmātsiddhā ūrdhvaretasāmāśramāḥ siddhaṃ ca ūrdhvaretaḥsu vidhāādvidyāyāḥ svātatryamiti stutimātramupādāāditi ceāpūrvatvāt stutimātrādhikaraṇam sa eṣa rasāāṃ rasatamaḥ paramaḥ parārdhyoṣṭamo yadudgīthaḥ iyamevargagiḥ sāma
