prajñāṃ kurvīta soveṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ iti ca evamādiśravaṇeṣu saṃśayaḥ kiṃ sakṛtpratyayaḥ kartavyaḥ āhosvit āvṛttyeti kiṃ tāvatprāptam sakṛtpratyayaḥ syāt prayājādivat tāvatā
śāstrasya kṛtārthatvāt aśrūyamāṇāyāṃ hi āvṛttau kriyamāṇāyām aśāstrārthaḥ kṛto bhavet au asakṛdupadeśā udāhṛtāḥ śrotavyo matavyo ididhyāsitavyaḥ ityevamādayaḥ evamapi yāvacchabdamāvartayet sakṛcchravaṇaṃ sakṛmaaaṃ
sakṛididhyāsaaṃ ceti ātiriktam sakṛdupadeśeṣu tu veda upāsīta ityevamādiṣu aāvṛttirityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ pratyayāvṛttiḥ kartavyā kutaḥ asakṛdupadeśāt śrotavyo matavyo ididhyāsitavyaḥ ityevaṃjātīyako hi
asakṛdupadeśaḥ pratyayāvṛttiṃ sūcayati au uktam yāvacchabdameva āvartayet ādhikamiti a darśaaparyavasāatvādeṣām darśaaparyavasāāi hi śravaṇādīyāvartyamāāi dṛṣṭārthāi bhavati yathā avaghātādīi taṇḍulādiiṣpattiparyavasāāi hi tadvat
api ca upāsaaṃ ididhyāsaaṃ ca ityatarṇītāvṛttiguṇaiva kriyā abhidhīyate tathā hi loke gurumupāste rājāamupāste iti ca yastātparyeṇa gurvādīauvartate sa evamucyate tathā
dhyāyati proṣitaāthā patim iti yā iratarasmaraṇā patiṃ prati sotkaṇṭhā sā evamabhidhīyate vidyupāstyośca vedāteṣu avyatirekeṇa prayogo dṛśyate kvacit vidiopakramya upāsiopasaṃharati yathā
yastadveda yatsa veda sa mayaitaduktaḥ ityatra au ma etāṃ bhagavo devatāṃ śādhi yāṃ devatāmupāsse iti kvacicca upāsiopakramya vidiopasaṃharati yathā mao
brahmetyupāsīta ityatra bhāti ca tapati ca kīrtyā yaśasā brahmavarcasea ya evaṃ veda iti tasmātsakṛdupadeśeṣvapi āvṛttisiddhiḥ asakṛdupadeśastu āvṛtteḥ sūcakaḥ liṅgācca liṅgamapi
pratyayāvṛttiṃ pratyāyayati tathā hi udgīthavijñāaṃ prastutya āditya udgīthaḥ ityetat ekaputratādoṣeṇāpodya raśmīṃstvaṃ paryāvartayāt iti raśmibahutvavijñāaṃ bahuputratāyai vidadhat siddhavatpratyayāvṛttiṃ darśayati tatsāmāyāt sarvapratyayeṣvāvṛttisiddhiḥ
atrāha bhavatu āma sādhyaphaleṣu pratyayeṣvāvṛttiḥ teṣvāvṛttisādhyasyātiśayasya saṃbhavāt yastu parabrahmaviṣayaḥ pratyayo ityaśuddhabuddhamuktasvabhāvameva ātmabhūtaṃ paraṃ brahma samarpayati tatra kimarthā āvṛttiriti sakṛcchrutau ca
brahmātmatvapratītyaupapatterāvṛttyabhyupagama iti cet a āvṛttāvapi tadaupapatteḥ yadi hi tattvamasi ityevaṃjātīyakaṃ vākyaṃ sakṛcchrūyamāṇaṃ brahmātmatvapratītiṃ otpādayet tatastadeva āvartyamāamutpādayiṣyatīti kā pratyāśā syāt athocyeta
a kevalaṃ vākyaṃ kaṃcidarthaṃ sākṣātkartuṃ śakoti ato yuktyapekṣaṃ vākyamaubhāvayiṣyati brahmātmatvamiti tathāpyāvṛttyāarthakyameva sāpi hi yuktiḥ sakṛtpravṛttaiva svamarthamaubhāvayiṣyati athāpi syāt yuktyā vākyea
ca sāmāyaviṣayameva vijñāaṃ kriyate a viśeṣaviṣayam yathā asti me hṛdaye śūlam ityato vākyāt gātrakampādiliṅgācca śūlasadbhāvasāmāyameva paraḥ pratipadyate a viśeṣamaubhavati yathā
sa eva śūlī viśeṣāubhavaśca avidyāyā ivartakaḥ tadarthā āvṛttiriti cet a asakṛdapi tāvamātre kriyamāṇe viśeṣavijñāotpattyasaṃbhavāt a hi sakṛtprayuktābhyāṃ śāstrayuktibhyāmaavagato viśeṣaḥ śatakṛtvopi
prayujyamāābhyāmavagatuṃ śakyate tasmāt yadi śāstrayuktibhyāṃ viśeṣaḥ pratipādyeta yadi vā sāmāyameva ubhayathāpi sakṛtpravṛtte eva te svakāryaṃ kuruta iti āvṛttyaupayogaḥ a ca
sakṛtprayukte śāstrayuktī kasyacidapyaubhavaṃ otpādayata iti śakyate iyatum vicitraprajñatvātpratipattṛṇām api ca aekāṃśopete laukike padārthe sāmāyaviśeṣavati ekeāvadhāea ekamaṃśamavadhārayati apareṇa aparam iti syādapyabhyāsopayogaḥ
yathā dīrghaprapāṭhakagrahaṇādiṣu a tu irviśeṣe brahmaṇi sāmāyaviśeṣarahite caitayamātrātmake pramotpattāvabhyāsāpekṣā yukteti atrocyate bhavedāvṛttyāarthakyaṃ taṃ prati yaḥ tattvamasi iti sakṛduktameva brahmātmatvamaubhavituṃ śakuyāt
yastu a śakoti taṃ prati upayujyata eva āvṛttiḥ tathā hi cchādogye tattvamasi śvetaketo ityupadiśya bhūya eva mā bhagavāvijñāpayatu iti puaḥ
puaḥ paricodyamāaḥ tattadāśaṅkākāraṇaṃ irākṛtya tattvamasi ityevāsakṛdupadiśati tathā ca śrotavyo matavyo ididhyāsitavyaḥ ityādi darśitam au uktam sakṛcchrutaṃ cet tattvamasivākyaṃ svamarthamaubhāvayituṃ a
śakoti tata āvartyamāamapi aiva śakṣyatīti aiṣa doṣaḥ a hi dṛṣṭeupapaaṃ āma dṛśyate hi sakṛcchrutādvākyāt madapratītaṃ vākyārthaṃ āvartayataḥ tattadābhāsavyudāsea samyakpratipadyamāāḥ api
ca tattvamasi ityetadvākyaṃ tvaṃpadārthasya tatpadārthabhāvamācaṣṭe tatpadea ca prakṛtaṃ sat brahma īkṣitṛ jagato jamādikāraṇamabhidhīyate satyaṃ jñāamaataṃ brahma vijñāamāadaṃ brahma adṛṣṭaṃ draṣṭṛ
avijñātaṃ vijñātṛ ajamajaramamaram asthūlamaaṇvahrasvamadīrgham ityādiśāstrasiddham tatra ajādiśabdairjamādayo bhāvavikārā ivartitāḥ asthūlādiśabdaiśca sthaulyādayo dravyadharmāḥ vijñāādiśabdaiśca caitayaprakāśātmakatvamuktam eṣa vyāvṛttasarvasaṃsāradharmakoubhavātmako brahmasaṃjñakastatpadārtho vedātābhiyuktāāṃ prasiddhaḥ tathā
tvaṃpadārthopi pratyagātmā śrotā dehādārabhya pratyagātmatayā saṃbhāvyamāaḥ caitayaparyatatveāvadhāritaḥ tatra yeṣām etau padārthau ajñāasaṃśayaviparyayapratibaddhau teṣāṃ tattvamasi ityetadvākyaṃ svārthe pramāṃ otpādayituṃ śakoti padārthajñāapūrvakatvādvākyārthajñāasya
ityataḥ tāprati eṣṭavyaḥ padārthavivekaprayojaaḥ śāstrayuktyabhyāsaḥ yadyapi ca pratipattavya ātmā iraṃśaḥ tathāpi adhyāropitaṃ tasmi bahvaṃśatvaṃ dehedriyamaobuddhiviṣayavedaādilakṣaṇam tatra ekea avadhāea ekamaṃśamapohati apareṇa
aparam iti yujyate tatra kramavatī pratipattiḥ tattu pūrvarūpameva ātmapratipatteḥ yeṣāṃ puaḥ ipuṇamatīāṃ a ajñāasaṃśayaviparyayalakṣaṇaḥ padārthaviṣayaḥ pratibadhosti te śakuvati sakṛduktameva tattvamasivākyārtham
aubhavitumiti tāprati āvṛttyāarthakyamiṣṭameva sakṛdutpaaiva hi ātmapratipattiḥ avidyāṃ ivartayatīti ātra kaścidapi kramobhyupagamyate satyamevaṃ yujyeta yadi kasyacit evaṃ pratipattirbhavet balavatī hi ātmao
duḥkhitvādipratipattiḥ ato a duḥkhitvādyabhāvaṃ kaścitpratipadyata iti cet a dehādyabhimāavat duḥkhitvādyabhimāasya mithyābhimāatvopapatteḥ pratyakṣaṃ hi dehe chidyamāe dahyamāe vā ahaṃ chidye dahye
iti ca mithyābhimāo dṛṣṭaḥ tathā bāhyatareṣvapi putramitrādiṣu saṃtapyamāeṣu ahameva saṃtapye ityadhyāropo dṛṣṭaḥ tathā duḥkhitvādyabhimāopi syāt dehādivadeva caitayādbahirupalabhyamāatvādduḥkhitvādīām suṣuptādiṣu ca aauvṛtteḥ
caitayasya tu suṣuptepi auvṛttimāmaati yadvai taa paśyati paśyavai taa paśyati ityādiā tasmāt sarvaduḥkhaviirmuktaikacaitayātmakohamityeṣa ātmāubhavaḥ a ca evam ātmāamaubhavataḥ kiṃcidayatkṛtyamavaśiṣyate tathā
ca śrutiḥ kiṃ prajayā kariṣyāmo yeṣāṃ oyamātmāyaṃ lokaḥ ityātmavidaḥ kartavyābhāvaṃ darśayati smṛtirapi yastvātmaratireva syādātmatṛptaśca māavaḥ ātmayeva ca saṃtuṣṭastasya kāryaṃ a
vidyate iti yasya tu a eṣoubhavo drāgiva jāyate taṃ prati aubhavārtha eva āvṛttyabhyupagamaḥ tatrāpi a tattvamasivākyārthāt pracyāvya āvṛttau pravartayet a
hi varaghātāya kayāmudvāhayati iyuktasya ca asmiadhikṛtohaṃ kartā mayedaṃ kartavyam ityavaśyaṃ brahmapratyayādviparītapratyaya utpadyate yastu svayameva madamatiḥ apratibhāāt taṃ vākyārthaṃ jihāset tasya
etasmieva vākyārthe sthirīkāra āvṛttyādivācoyuktyā abhyupeyate tasmāt parabrahmaviṣayepi pratyaye tadupāyopadeśeṣvāvṛttisiddhiḥ ātmeti tūpagacchati grāhayati ca ātmatvopāsaādhikaraṇam yaḥ śāstroktaviśeṣaṇaḥ paramātmā sa kim aham
iti grahītavyaḥ kiṃ vā madaya iti etad vicārayati kathaṃ puar ātmaśabde pratyagātmaviṣaye śrūyamāṇe saṃśaya iti ucyate ayam ātmaśabdo mukhyaḥ śakyatebhyupagatum
sati jīveśvarayor abhedasaṃbhave itarathā tu gauṇoyam abhyupagatavyaḥ iti mayate kiṃ tāvat prāptam a aham iti grāhyaḥ a hi apahatapāpmatvādiguṇo viparītaguṇatvea
śakyate grahītum viparītaguṇo vā apahatapāpmatvādiguṇatvea apahatapāpmatvādiguṇaś ca parameśvaraḥ tadviparītaguṇas tu śārīraḥ īśvarasya ca saṃsāryātmatve īśvarābhāvaprasaṅgaḥ tataḥ śāstrāarthakyam saṃsāriṇopi īśvarātmatve adhikāryabhāvāc
chāstrāarthakyam eva pratyakṣādivirodhaś ca ayatvepi tādātmyadarśaaṃ śāstrāt kartavyam pratimādiṣv iva viṣṇvādidarśaam iti cet kāmam evaṃ bhavatu a tu saṃsāriṇo mukhya
ātmā īśvara ity etat aḥ prāpayitavyam evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ ātmety eva parameśvaraḥ pratipattavyaḥ tathā hi parameśvaraprakriyāyāṃ jābālā ātmatveaiva etam upagacchati
tvaṃ vā aham asmi bhagavo devatehaṃ vai tvam asi devate iti tathā ayepi ahaṃ brahmāsmi ity evamādaya ātmatvopagamā draṣṭavyāḥ grāhayati
ca ātmatveaiva īśvaraṃ vedātavākyāi eṣa ta ātmā sarvātaraḥ eṣa ta ātmātaryāmy amṛtaḥ tat satyaṃ sa ātmā tat tvam asi ityevamādīi
yad uktam pratīkadarśaam idaṃ viṣṇupratimāyāyea bhaviṣyatīti tad ayuktam gauṇatvaprasaṅgāt vākyavairūpyāc ca yatra hi pratīkadṛṣṭir abhipreyate sakṛd eva tatra vacaaṃ bhavati
yathā mao brahma ādityo brahma ityādi iha puaḥ tvam aham asmi ahaṃ ca tvam asīty āha ataḥ pratīkaśrutivairūpyāt abhedapratipattiḥ bhedadṛṣṭyapavādāc
ca tathā hi atha yoyāṃ devatām upāsteyosāv ayoham asmīti a sa veda mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpoti ya iha āeva paśyati
sarvaṃ taṃ parādādyoyatrātmaaḥ sarvaṃ veda ityevamādyā bhūyasī śrutiḥ bhedadarśaam apavadati yat tūktam a viruddhaguṇayor ayoyātmatvasaṃbhava iti āyaṃ doṣaḥ viruddhaguṇatāyā mithyātvopapatteḥ
yat puar uktam īśvarābhāvaprasaṅga iti tad asat śāstraprāmāṇyāt aabhyupagamāc ca a hi īśvarasya saṃsāryātmatvaṃ pratipādyata ityabhyupagacchāmaḥ kiṃtarhi saṃsāriṇaḥ saṃsāritvāpohea īśvarātmatvaṃ
pratipipādayiṣitam iti evaṃ ca sati advaiteśvarasya apahatapāpmatvādiguṇatā viparītaguṇatā tu itarasya mithyeti vyavatiṣṭhate yad apy uktam adhikāryabhāvaḥ pratyakṣādivirodhaś ceti tad apy
asat prākprabodhāt saṃsāritvābhyupagamāt tadviṣayatvāc ca pratyakṣādivyavahārasya yatra tv asya sarvam ātmaivābhūt tat kea kaṃ paśyet ityādiā hi prabodhe pratyakṣādyabhāvaṃ darśayati
pratyakṣādyabhāve śruter apy abhāvaprasaṅga iti cet a iṣṭatvāt atra pitāpitā bhavati ity upakramya vedā avedāḥ iti vacaāt iṣyata eva asmābhiḥ
śruter apy abhāvaḥ prabodhe kasya puar ayam aprabodha iti cet yas tvaṃ pṛcchasi tasya te iti vadāmaḥ au aham īśvara
evoktaḥ śrutyā yady evaṃ pratibuddhosi āsti kasyacid aprabodhaḥ yopi doṣaś codyate kaiś cid avidyayā kila ātmaaḥ sadvitīyatvāt advaitāupapattir iti sopi
etea pratyuktaḥ tasmāt ātmety eva īśvare mao dadhīta a pratīke a hi saḥ pratīkādhikaraṇam mao brahmety upāsītety adhyātmam athādhidaivatam ākāśo
brahmeti tathā ādityo brahmety ādeśaḥ sa yo āma brahmetyupāste ityevamādiṣu pratīkopāsaeṣu saṃśayaḥ kiṃ teṣvapi ātmagrahaḥ kartavyaḥ a veti kiṃ tāvatprāptam
teṣvapi ātmagraha eva yuktaḥ kartum kasmāt brahmaṇaḥ śrutiṣu ātmatvea prasiddhatvāt pratīkāāmapi brahmavikāratvādbrahmatve sati ātmatvopapatterityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ a pratīkeṣvātmamatiṃ badhīyāt a
hi sa upāsakaḥ pratīkāi vyastāi ātmatvea ākalayet yatpuaḥ brahmavikāratvātpratīkāāṃ brahmatvaṃ tataśca ātmatvamiti tadasat pratīkābhāvaprasaṅgāt vikārasvarūpopamardea hi āmādijātasya brahmatvameva āśritaṃ bhavati
svarūpopamarde ca āmādīāṃ kutaḥ pratīkatvam ātmagraho vā a ca brahmaṇa ātmatvāt brahmadṛṣṭyupadeśeṣvātmadṛṣṭiḥ kalpyā kartṛtvādyairākaraṇāt kartṛtvādisarvasaṃsāradharmairākaraṇea hi brahmaṇa ātmatvopadeśaḥ tadairākaraṇea ca
upāsaavidhāam ataśca upāsakasya pratīkaiḥ samatvāt ātmagraho opapadyate a hi rucakasvastikayoḥ itaretarātmatvamasti suvarṇātmaeva tu brahmātmaā ekatve pratīkābhāvaprasaṅgamavocāma ato a pratīkeṣvātmadṛṣṭiḥ kriyate
brahmadṛṣṭirutkarṣāt brahmadṛṣṭyadhikaraṇam teṣveva udāharaṇeṣvayaḥ saṃśayaḥ kimādityādidṛṣṭayo brahmaṇyadhyasitavyāḥ kiṃ vā brahmadṛṣṭirādityādiṣviti kutaḥ saṃśayaḥ sāmāādhikaraṇye kāraṇāavadhāraṇāt atra hi brahmaśabdasya ādityādiśabdaiḥ sāmāādhikaraṇyamupalabhyate ādityo
brahma prāṇo brahma vidyudbrahma ityādisamāavibhaktiirdeśāt a ca atra āñjasaṃ sāmāādhikaraṇyamavakalpate arthātaravacaatvādbrahmādityādiśabdāām a hi bhavati gauraśva iti sāmāādhikaraṇyam au prakṛtivikārabhāvādbrahmādityādīāṃ mṛccharāvādivatsāmāādhikaraṇyaṃ
syāt etyucyate vikārapravilayo hyevaṃ prakṛtisāmāādhikaraṇyātsyāt tataśca pratīkābhāvaprasaṅgamavocāma paramātmavākyaṃ cedaṃ tadāīṃ syāt tataścopāsaādhikāro bādhyeta parimitavikāropādāaṃ ca vyartham tasmāt brāhmaṇogirvaiśvāaraḥ ityādivat ayataratrāyataradṛṣṭyadhyāse
sati kva kiṃdṛṣṭiradhyasyatāmiti saṃśayaḥ tatra aiyamaḥ iyamakāriṇaḥ śāstrasyābhāvādityevaṃ prāptam athavā ādityādidṛṣṭaya eva brahmaṇi kartavyā ityevaṃ prāptam evaṃ hi ādityādidṛṣṭibhiḥ brahma
upāsitaṃ bhavati brahmopāsaaṃ ca phalavaditi śāstramaryādā tasmāt a brahmadṛṣṭirādityādiṣvityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ brahmadṛṣṭireva ādityādiṣu syāditi kasmāt utkarṣāt evam utkarṣeṇa ādityādayo dṛṣṭā
bhavati utkṛṣṭadṛṣṭesteṣvadhyāsāt tathā ca laukiko yāyougato bhavati utkṛṣṭadṛṣṭirhi ikṛṣṭedhyasitavyeti laukiko yāyaḥ yathā rājadṛṣṭiḥ kṣattari sa ca ausartavyaḥ viparyaye pratyavāyaprasaṅgāt a
hi kṣattṛdṛṣṭiparigṛhīto rājā ikarṣaṃ īyamāaḥ śreyase syāt au śāstraprāmāṇyādaāśaṅkaīyotra pratyavāyaprasaṅgaḥ a ca laukikea yāyea śāstrīyā dṛṣṭiriyatuṃ yukteti atrocyate irdhārite śāstrārthe
etadevaṃ syāt saṃdigdhe tu tasmi tairṇayaṃ prati laukikopi yāya āśrīyamāṇo a virudhyate tea ca utkṛṣṭadṛṣṭyadhyāse śāstrārthevadhāryamāṇe ikṛṣṭadṛṣṭimadhyasyapratyaveyāditi śliṣyate prāthamyācca ādityādiśabdāāṃ
mukhyārthatvam avirodhāt grahītavyam taiḥ svārthavṛttibhiravaruddhāyāṃ buddhau paścādavatarato brahmaśabdasya mukhyayā vṛttyā sāmāādhikaraṇyāsaṃbhavāt brahmadṛṣṭividhāārthataiva avatiṣṭhate itiparatvādapi brahmaśabdasya eṣa evārtho yāyyaḥ tathā hi
brahmetyādeśaḥ brahmetyupāsīta brahmetyupāste iti ca sarvatretiparaṃ brahmaśabdamuccārayati śuddhāṃstu ādityādiśabdā tataśca yathā śuktikāṃ rajatamiti pratyetītyatra śuktivacaa eva śuktikāśabdaḥ rajataśabdastu rajatapratītilakṣaṇārthaḥ pratyetyeva
hi kevalaṃ rajatamiti a tu tatra rajatamasti evamatrāpi ādityādībrahmeti pratīyāditi gamyate vākyaśeṣopi ca dvitīyāirdeśea ādityādīeva upāstikriyayā vyāpyamāādarśayati sa ya etadevaṃ
vidvāādityaṃ brahmetyupāste yo vācaṃ brahmetyupāste yaḥ saṃkalpaṃ brahmetyupāste iti ca yattūktam brahmopāsaamevātra ādaraṇīyaṃ phalavattvāyeti tadayuktam uktea yāyea ādityādīāmeva upāsyatvāvagamāt phalaṃ
tu atithyādyupāsaa iva ādityādyupāsaepi brahmaiva dāsyati sarvādhyakṣatvāt varṇitaṃ caitat phalamata upapatteḥ ityatra īdṛśaṃ ca atra brahmaṇa upāsyatvam yatpratīkeṣu taddṛṣṭyadhyāropaṇam pratimādiṣv
iva viṣṇvādīām ādityādimatayaścāṅga upapatteḥ ādityādimatyadhikaraṇam ya evāsau tapati tamudgīthamupāsīta lokeṣu pañcavidhaṃ sāmopāsīta vāci saptavidhaṃ sāmopāsīta iyamevargagiḥ sāma ityevamādiṣu aṅgāvabaddheṣūpāsaeṣu saṃśayaḥ
kimādityādiṣu udgīthādidṛṣṭayo vidhīyate kiṃ vā udgīthādiṣveva ādityādidṛṣṭaya iti tatra aiyamaḥ iyamakāraṇābhāvāt iti prāptam a hi atra brahmaṇa iva kasyacidutkarṣaviśeṣovadhāryate brahma
hi samastajagatkāraṇatvāt apahatapāpmatvādiguṇayogācca ādityādibhya utkṛṣṭamiti śakyamavadhārayitum a tu ādityodgīthādīāṃ vikāratvāviśeṣāt kiṃcidutkarṣaviśeṣāvadhāraṇe kāraṇamasti athavā iyameaiva udgīthādimataya ādityādiṣu adhyasyera kasmāt karmātmakatvādudgīthādīām karmaṇaśca
phalaprāptiprasiddheḥ udgīthādimatibhirupāsyamāā ādityādayaḥ karmātmakāḥ sataḥ phalahetavo bhaviṣyati tathā ca iyamevargagiḥ sāma ityatra tadetadetasyāmṛcyadhyūḍhaṃ sāma iti ṛkśabdea pṛthivīṃ irdiśati sāmaśabdeāgim tacca
pṛthivyagyoḥ ṛksāmadṛṣṭicikīrṣāyāmavakalpate a ṛksāmayoḥ pṛthivyagidṛṣṭicikīrṣāyām kṣattari hi rājadṛṣṭikaraṇāt rājaśabda upacaryate a rājai kṣattṛśabdaḥ api ca lokeṣu pañcavidhaṃ sāmopāsīta iti adhikaraṇairdeśāt
lokeṣu sāma adhyasitavyamiti pratīyate etadgāyatraṃ prāṇeṣu protam iti ca etadeva darśayati prathamairdiṣṭeṣu ca ādityādiṣu caramairdiṣṭaṃ brahmādhyastam ādityo brahmetyādeśaḥ ityādiṣu prathamairdiṣṭāśca
pṛthivyādayaḥ caramairdiṣṭā hiṃkārādayaḥ pṛthivī hiṃkāraḥ ityādiśrutiṣu ataḥ aaṅgeṣvādityādiṣu aṅgamatikṣepa ityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ ādityādimataya eva aṅgeṣu udgīthādiṣu kṣipyera kutaḥ upapatteḥ upapadyate
hi evam apūrvasaṃikarṣāt ādityādimatibhiḥ saṃskriyamāṇeṣu udgīthādiṣu karmasamṛddhiḥ yadeva vidyayā karoti śraddhayopaiṣadā tadeva vīryavattaraṃ bhavati iti ca vidyāyāḥ karmasamṛddhihetutvaṃ darśayati bhavatu
karmasamṛddhiphaleṣvevam svatatraphaleṣu tu katham ya etadevaṃ vidvāllokeṣu pañcavidhaṃ sāmopāste ityādiṣu teṣvapi adhikṛtādhikārāt prakṛtāpūrvasaṃikarṣeṇaiva phalakalpaā yuktā godohaādiiyamavat phalātmakatvācca ādityādīām udgīthādibhyaḥ karmātmakebhyaḥ
utkarṣopapattiḥ ādityādiprāptilakṣaṇaṃ hi karmaphalaṃ śiṣyate śrutiṣu api ca omityetadakṣaramudgīthamupāsīta khalvetasyaivākṣarasyopavyākhyāaṃ bhavati iti ca udgīthameva upāsyatveopakramya ādityādimatīrvidadhāti yattūktam udgīthādimatibhirupāsyamāā ādityādayaḥ karmabhūyaṃ
bhūtvā phalaṃ kariṣyatīti tadayuktam svayamevopāsaasya karmatvāt phalavattvopapatteḥ ādityādibhāveāpi ca dṛśyamāāāmudgīthādīāṃ karmātmakatvāapāyāt tadetadetasyāmṛcyadhyūḍhaṃ sāma iti tu lākṣaṇika eva pṛthivyagyoḥ ṛksāmaśabdaprayogaḥ lakṣaṇā
ca yathāsaṃbhavaṃ saṃikṛṣṭea viprakṛṣṭea vā svārthasaṃbadhea pravartate tatra yadyapi ṛksāmayoḥ pṛthivyagidṛṣṭicikīrṣā tathāpi prasiddhayoḥ ṛksāmayorbhedeāukīrtaāt pṛthivyagyośca saṃidhāāt tayoreva eṣa ṛksāmaśabdaprayogaḥ ṛksāmasaṃbadhāditi
iścīyate kṣattṛśabdopi hi kutaścitkāraṇādrājāamupasarpa a ivārayituṃ pāryate iyamevark iti ca yathākṣarayāsam ṛca eva pṛthivītvamavadhārayati pṛthivyā hi ṛktvevadhāryamāṇe iyamṛgevetyakṣarayāsaḥ syāt ya
evaṃ vidvāsāma gāyati iti ca aṅgāśrayamavavijñāamupasaṃharati a pṛthivyādyāśrayam tathā lokeṣu pañcavidhaṃ sāmopāsīta iti yadyapi saptamīirdiṣṭā lokāḥ tathāpi sāmyeva te adhyasyera
dvitīyāirdeśea sāma upāsyatvāvagamāt sāmai hi lokeṣvadhyasyamāeṣu sāma lokātmaopāsitaṃ bhavati ayathā puaḥ lokāḥ sāmātmaāupāsitāḥ syuḥ etea etadgāyatraṃ prāṇeṣu protam ityādi vyākhyātam
yatrāpi tulyo dvitīyāirdeśaḥ atha khalvamumādityaṃ saptavidhaṃ sāmopāsīta iti tatrāpi samastasya khalu sāma upāsaaṃ sādhu itiṃ tu pañcavidhasya atha saptavidhasya iti
ca sāma eva upāsyatvopakramāt tasmieva ādityādyadhyāsaḥ etasmādeva ca sāma upāsyatvāvagamāt pṛthivī hiṃkāraḥ ityādiirdeśaviparyayepi hiṃkārādiṣveva pṛthivyādidṛṣṭiḥ tasmāt aaṅgāśrayā ādityādimatayaḥ aṅgeṣūdgīthādiṣu kṣipyeraiti
siddham āsīaḥ sambhavāt āsīādhikaraṇam karmāṅgasaṃbaddheṣu tāvat upāsaeṣu karmatatratvāt a āsaādicitā āpi samyagdarśae vastutatratvādvijñāasya itareṣu tu upāsaeṣu kim aiyamea tiṣṭha āsīaḥ
śayāo vā pravarteta uta iyamea āsīa eveti citayati tatra māasatvāvadupāsaasya aiyamaḥ śarīrasthiterityevaṃ prāpte bravīti āsīa evopāsīteti kutaḥ saṃbhavāt upāsaaṃ āma
samāapratyayapravāhakaraṇam a ca tat gacchato dhāvato vā saṃbhavati gatyādīāṃ cittavikṣepakaratvāt tiṣṭhatopi dehadhāraṇe vyāpṛtaṃ mao a sūkṣmavastuirīkṣaṇakṣamaṃ bhavati śayāasyāpi akasmādeva idrayā
abhibhūyate āsīasya tu evaṃjātīyako bhūyādoṣaḥ suparihara iti saṃbhavati tasyopāsaam dhyāācca api ca dhyāyatyartha eṣaḥ yat samāapratyayapravāhakaraṇam dhyāyatiś ca praśithilāṅgaceṣṭeṣu pratiṣṭhitadṛṣṭiṣu
ekaviṣayākṣiptacitteṣu upacaryamāṇo dṛśyate dhyāyati bakaḥ dhyāyati proṣitabadhur iti āsīaś ca aāyāso bhavati tasmād api āsīakarmopāsaam acalatvaṃ cāpekṣya api ca dhyāyatīva
pṛthivī ityatra pṛthivyādiṣu acalatvamevāpekṣya dhyāyativādo bhavati tacca liṅgam upāsaasya āsīakarmatve smarati ca smaraty api ca śiṣṭā upāsaāṅgatvea āsaam śucau deśe
pratiṣṭhāpya sthiram āsaamātmaaḥ ityādiā ata eva padmakādīām āsaaviśeṣāṇām upadeśo yogaśāstre yatraikāgratā tatrāviśeṣāt ekāgratādhikaraṇam digdeśakāleṣu saṃśayaḥ kimasti kaściiyamaḥ āsti veti prāyeṇa
vaidikeṣvārambheṣu digādiiyamadarśaāt syādihāpi kaściiyama iti yasya matiḥ taṃ pratyāha digdeśakāleṣu arthalakṣaṇa eva iyamaḥ yatraiva asya diśi deśe kāle vā maasaḥ
saukaryeṇaikāgratā bhavati tatraivopāsīta prācīdikpūrvāhṇaprācīapravaṇādivat viśeṣāśravaṇāt ekāgratāyā iṣṭāyāḥ sarvatrāviśeṣāt au viśeṣamapi kecidāmaati same śucau śarkarāvahivālukāvivarjite śabdajalāśrayādibhiḥ maoukūle a tu cakṣupīḍae guhāivātāśrayaṇe
prayojayet iti yatheti ucyate satyamasti evaṃjātīyako iyamaḥ sati tvetasmi tadgateṣu viśeṣeṣvaiyama iti suhṛdbhūtvā ācārya ācaṣṭe maoukūle iti caiṣā śrutiḥ yatraikāgratā
tatraivaityetadeva darśayati āprāyaṇāttatrāpi hi dṛṣṭam āprāyaṇādhikaraṇam āvṛttiḥ sarvopāsaeṣvādartavyeti sthitamādyedhikaraṇe tatra yāi tāvat samyagdarśaārthāyupāsaāi tāi avaghātādivat kāryaparyavasāāīti jñātameva eṣāmāvṛttiṃparimāṇam a hi
samyagdarśae kārye iṣpae yatātaraṃ kiṃcicchāsituṃ śakyam aiyojyabrahmātmatvapratipatteḥ śāstrasyāviṣayatvāt yāi puaḥ abhyudayaphalāi teṣveṣā citā kiṃ kiyataṃcitkālaṃ pratyayamāvartya uparamet uta yāvajjīvamāvartayediti kiṃ
tāvatprāptam kiyataṃcitkālaṃ pratyayamabhyasya utsṛjet āvṛttiviśiṣṭasyopāsaaśabdārthasya kṛtatvādityevaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ ā prāyaṇādeva āvartayetpratyayam atyapratyayavaśādadṛṣṭaphalaprāpteḥ karmāṇyapi hi jamātaropabhogyaṃ phalamārabhamāṇāi tadaurūpaṃ bhāvaāvijñāaṃ prāyaṇakāle ākṣipati
savijñāo bhavati savijñāamevāvavakrāmati yaccittasteaiṣa prāṇamāyāti prāṇastejasā yuktaḥ sahātmaā yathāsaṃkalpitaṃ lokaṃ ayati iti caivamādiśrutibhyaḥ tṛṇajalūkāidarśaācca pratyayāstvete svarūpāuvṛttiṃ muktvā kimayat prāyaṇakālabhāvi bhāvaāvijñāamapekṣera
tasmāt ye pratipattavyaphalabhāvaātmakāḥ pratyayāḥ teṣu ā prāyaṇāt āvṛttiḥ tathā ca śrutiḥ sa yāvatkraturayamasmāllokātpraiti iti prāyaṇakālepi pratyayāuvṛttiṃ darśayati smṛtirapi yaṃ yaṃ
vāpi smarabhāvaṃ tyajatyate kalebaram taṃ tamevaiti kautaya sadā tadbhāvabhāvitaḥ iti prayāṇakāle maasācalea iti ca sotavelāyāmetattrayaṃ pratipadyeta iti ca maraṇavelāyāmapi kartavyaśeṣaṃ
śrāvayati tadadhigama uttarapūrvāghayoraśleṣaviāśau tadvyapadeśāt tadadhigamādhikaraṇam gatastṛtīyaśeṣaḥ athedāīṃ brahmavidyāphalaṃ prati citā pratāyate brahmādhigame sati tadviparītaphalaṃ duritaṃ kṣīyate a kṣīyate veti saṃśayaḥ
kiṃ tāvatprāptam phalārthatvātkarmaṇaḥ phalamadattvā a saṃbhāvyate kṣayaḥ phaladāyiī hi asya śaktiḥ śrutyā samadhigatā yadi tat atareṇaiva phalopabhogamapavṛjyeta śrutiḥ kadarthitā syāt
smarati ca a hi karma kṣīyate iti avevaṃ sati prāyaścittopadeśoarthakaḥ prāpoti aiṣa doṣaḥ prāyaścittāāṃ aimittikatvopapatteḥ gṛhadāheṣṭyādivat api ca prāyaścittāāṃ doṣasaṃyogea
vidhāādbhavedapi doṣakṣapaṇārthatā a tvevaṃ brahmavidyāyāṃ vidhāamasti av aabhyupagamyamāe brahmavidaḥ karmakṣaye tatphalasyāvaśyabhoktavyatvād airmokṣaḥ syāt ety ucyate deśakālaimittāpekṣo mokṣaḥ karmaphalavat bhaviṣyati tasmā
a brahmādhigame duritaivṛttir ity evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ tadadhigame brahmādhigame sati uttarapūrvayor aghayor aśleṣaviāśau bhavataḥ uttarasya aśleṣaḥ pūrvasya viāśaḥ kasmāt tadvyapadeśāt
tathā hi brahmavidyāprakriyāyāṃ saṃbhāvyamāasaṃbadhasya āgāmio duritasyāabhisaṃbadhaṃ viduṣo vyapadiśati yathā puṣkarapalāśa āpo a śliṣyata evamevaṃvidi pāpaṃ karma a śliṣyate iti tathā
viāśam api pūrvopacitasya duritasya vyapadiśati tad yatheṣīkātūlamagau protaṃ pradūyetaivaṃ hāsya sarve pāpmāaḥ pradūyate iti ayam aparaḥ karmakṣayavyapadeśo bhavati bhidyate hṛdayagradhiś
chidyate sarvasaṃśayāḥ kṣīyate cāsya karmāṇi tasmidṛṣṭe parāvare iti yaduktam aupabhuktaphalasya karmaṇaḥ kṣayakalpaāyāṃ śāstraṃ kadarthitaṃ syāditi aiṣa doṣaḥ a hi vayaṃ
karmaṇaḥ phaladāyiīṃ śaktimavajāīmahe vidyata eva sā sā tu vidyādiā kāraṇātareṇa pratibadhyata iti vadāmaḥ śaktisadbhāvamātre ca śāstraṃ vyāpriyate a pratibadhāpratibadhayor api
a hi karma kṣīyate ity etad api smaraṇam autsargikam a hi bhogād ṛte karma kṣīyate tadarthatvād iti iṣyata eva tu
prāyaścittādiā tasya kṣayaḥ sarvaṃ pāpmāaṃ tarati tarati brahmahatyām yośvamedhea yajate ya u caiam evaṃ veda ityādi śrutismṛtibhyaḥ yat tūktam aimittikāi
prāyaścittāi bhaviṣyatīti tadasat doṣasaṃyogea codyamāāāmeṣāṃ doṣairghātaphalasaṃbhave phalātarakalpaāupapatteḥ yatpuaretaduktam a prāyaścittavat doṣakṣayoddeśea vidyāvidhāamastīti atra brūmaḥ saguṇāsu tāvadvidyāsu vidyata eva vidhāam tāsu
ca vākyaśeṣe aiśvaryaprāptiḥ pāpaivṛttiśca vidyāvata ucyate tayoścāvivakṣākāraṇaṃ āsti ityataḥ pāpmaprahāṇapūrvakaiśvaryaprāptiḥ tāsāṃ phalamiti iścīyate irguṇāyāṃ tu vidyāyāṃ yadyapi vidhāaṃ āsti tathāpi
akartrātmatvabodhātkarmapradāhasiddhiḥ aśleṣa iti ca āgāmiṣu karmasu kartṛtvameva a pratipadyate brahmavid iti darśayati atikrāteṣu tu yadyapi mithyājñāātkartṛtvaṃ pratipeda iva tathāpi vidyāsāmarthyāmithyājñāaivṛtteḥ
tāyapi pravilīyata ityāha viāśa iti pūrvasiddhakartṛtvabhoktṛtvaviparītaṃ hi triṣvapi kāleṣvakartṛtvābhoktṛtvasvarūpaṃ brahmāhamasmi etaḥ pūrvamapi kartā bhoktā vā ahamāsam edāīm āpi bhaviṣyatkāle iti
brahmavid avagacchati evam eva ca mokṣa upapadyate ayathā hi aādikālapravṛttāāṃ karmaṇāṃ kṣayābhāve mokṣābhāvaḥ syāt a ca deśakālaimittāpekṣo mokṣaḥ karmaphalavat bhavitumarhati
aityatvaprasaṅgāt parokṣatvāupapatteśca jñāaphalasya tasmāt brahmādhigame duritakṣaya iti sthitam itarasyāpyevamasaṃśleṣaḥ pāte tu itarāsaṃśleṣādhikaraṇam pūrvasmiadhikaraṇe badhahetoraghasya svābhāvikasya aśleṣaviāśau jñāaimittau śāstravyapadeśāirūpitau dharmasya puaḥ
śāstrīyatvāt śāstrīyeṇa jñāea avirodha ityāśaṅkya tairākaraṇāya pūrvādhikaraṇayāyātideśaḥ kriyate itarasyāpi puṇyasya karmaṇaḥ evam aghavat asaṃśleṣo viāśaśca jñāavato bhavataḥ kutaḥ tasyāpi svaphalahetutvea
jñāaphalapratibadhitvaprasaṅgāt ubhe u haivaiṣa ete tarati ityādiśrutiṣu ca duṣkṛtavatsukṛtasyāpi praṇāśavyapadeśāt akartrātmatvabodhaimittasya ca karmakṣayasya sukṛtaduṣkṛtayostulyatvāt kṣīyate cāsya karmāṇi iti ca aviśeṣaśruteḥ
yatrāpi kevala eva pāpmaśabdaḥ paṭhyate tatrāpi teaiva puṇyamapyākalitamiti draṣṭavyam jñāāpekṣayā ikṛṣṭaphalatvāt asti ca śrutau puṇyepi pāpmaśabdaḥ aiaṃ setumahorātre tarataḥ ityatra
saha duṣkṛtea sukṛtamapyaukramya sarve pāpmāoto ivartate ityaviśeṣeṇaiva prakṛte puṇye pāpmaśabdaprayogāt pāte tu iti tuśabdovadhāraṇārthaḥ evaṃ dharmādharmayorbadhahetvoḥ vidyāsāmarthyādaśleṣaviāśasiddheḥ avaśyaṃbhāviī viduṣaḥ śarīrapāte
muktirityavadhārayati aārabdhakārye eva tu pūrve tadavadheḥ aārabdhādhikaraṇam pūrvayor adhikaraṇayor jñāaimittaḥ sukṛtaduṣkṛtayor viāśo vadhāritaḥ sa kim aviśeṣeṇa ārabdhakāryayor aārabdhakāryayoś ca bhavati
uta viśeṣeṇāārabdhakāryayor eveti vicāryate tatra ubhe u haivaiṣa ete tarati ity evamādiśrutiṣv aviśeṣaśravaṇād aviśeṣeṇaiva kṣaya ity evaṃ prāpte pratyāha aārabdhakārye
eva tv iti apravṛttaphale eva pūrve jamātarasaṃcite asmi api ca jamai prāgjñāotpatteḥ saṃcite sukṛtaduṣkṛte jñāādhigamāt kṣīyete a tu ārabdhakārye sāmibhuktaphale
yābhyām etat brahmajñāāyataaṃ jama irmitam kuta etat tasya tāvad eva ciraṃ yāva a vimokṣye tha saṃpatsye iti śarīrapātāv adhikaraṇāt kṣemaprāpteḥ
itarathā hi jñāād aśeṣakarmakṣaye sati sthitihetvabhāvāt jñāaprāptyaataram eva kṣemam aśuvīta tatra śarīrapātapratīkṣāṃ a ācakṣīta au vastubaleaiva ayam akartrātmāvabodhaḥ karmāṇi kṣapaya
kathaṃ kāicit kṣapayet kāicic copekṣeta a hi samāe gibījasaṃparke keṣāṃcid bījaśaktiḥ kṣīyate keṣāṃci a kṣīyate iti śakyam aṅgīkartum iti ucyate
a tāvad aāśritya ārabdhakāryaṃ karmāśayaṃ jñāotpattir upapadyate āśrite ca tasmi kulālacakravat pravṛttavegasya atarāle pratibadhāsaṃbhavāt bhavati vegakṣayapratipālaam akartrātmabodho pi hi mithyājñāabādhaea
karmāṇy ucchiatti bādhitam api tu mithyājñāaṃ dvicadrajñāavat saṃskāravaśāt kaṃcit kālam auvartata eva api ca aivātra vivaditavyam brahmavidā kaṃcit kālaṃ śarīraṃ
dhriyate a vā dhriyata iti kathaṃ hi ekasya svahṛdayapratyayaṃ brahmavedaaṃ dehadhāraṇaṃ ca apareṇa pratikṣeptuṃ śakyeta śrutismṛtiṣu ca sthitaprajñalakṣaṇairdeśea etad eva
irucyate tasmād aārabdhakāryayor eva sukṛtaduṣkṛtayor vidyāsāmarthyāt kṣaya iti irṇayaḥ agihotrādi tu tatkāryāyaiva taddarśaāt agihotrādyadhikaraṇam puṇyasyāpyaśleṣaviāśayoraghayāyotidiṣṭaḥ sotideśaḥ sarvapuṇyaviṣaya ityāśaṅkya prativakti agihotrādi
tviti tuśabda āśaṅkāmapaudati yaityaṃ karma vaidikamagihotrādi tat tatkāryāyaiva bhavati jñāasya yatkāryaṃ tadeva asyāpi kāryamityarthaḥ kutaḥ tametaṃ vedāuvacaea brāhmaṇā vividiṣati yajñea
dāea ityādidarśaāt au jñāakarmaṇorvilakṣaṇakāryatvātkāryaikatvāupapattiḥ aiṣa doṣaḥ jvaramaraṇakāryayorapi dadhiviṣayoḥ guḍamatrasaṃyuktayostṛptipuṣṭikāryadarśaāt tadvat karmaṇopi jñāasaṃyuktasya mokṣakāryopapatteḥ au aārabhyo mokṣaḥ kathamasya karmakāryatvamucyate aiṣa doṣaḥ
ārādupakārakatvātkarmaṇaḥ jñāasyaiva hi prāpakaṃ sat karma praṇāḍyā mokṣakāraṇamityupacaryate ata eva ca atikrātaviṣayametatkāryaikatvābhidhāam a hi brahmavida āgāmyagihotrādi saṃbhavati aiyojyabrahmātmatvapratipatteḥ śāstrasyāviṣayatvāt saguṇāsu
tu vidyāsu kartṛtvāativṛtteḥ saṃbhavati āgāmyapi agihotrādi tasyāpi irabhisaṃdhiaḥ kāryātarābhāvādvidyāsaṃgatyupapattiḥ kiṃviṣayaṃ puaridam aśleṣaviāśavacaam kiṃviṣayaṃ vā ado viiyogavacaam ekeṣāṃ śākhiām tasya putrā
dāyamupayati suhṛdaḥ sādhukṛtyāṃ dviṣataḥ pāpakṛtyām iti ata uttaraṃ paṭhati atoyāpi hyekeṣāmubhayoḥ atogihotrāderityātkarmaṇaḥ ayāpi hyasti sādhukṛtyā yā phalamabhisaṃdhāya kriyate tasyā eṣa
viiyoga uktaḥ ekeṣāṃ śākhiām suhṛdaḥ sādhukṛtyāmupayati iti tasyā eva ca idam aghavadaśleṣaviāśairūpaṇam itarasyāpyevamasaṃśleṣa iti tathājātīyakasya kāmyasya karmaṇo vidyāṃ pratyaupakārakatve saṃpratipattiḥ
ubhayorapi jaimiibādarāyaṇayorācāryayoḥ yad eva vidyayeti hi vidyājñāasādhaatvādhikaraṇam samadhigatametadaatarādhikaraṇe ityamagihotrādikaṃ karma mumukṣuṇā mokṣaprayojaoddeśea kṛtamupāttaduritakṣayahetudvāreṇa sattvaśuddhikāraṇatāṃ pratipadyamāaṃ mokṣaprayojaabrahmādhigamaimittatvea brahmavidyayā saha ekakāryaṃ bhavatīti
tatra agihotrādi karmāṅgavyapāśrayavidyāsaṃyuktaṃ kevalaṃ cāsti ya evaṃ vidvāyajati ya evaṃ vidvāñjuhoti ya evaṃ vidvāñśaṃsati ya evaṃ vidvāgāyati tasmādevaṃvidameva brahmāṇaṃ kurvīta
teobhau kuruto yaścaitadevaṃ veda yaśca a veda ityādivacaebhyo vidyāsaṃyuktamasti kevalamapyasti tatredaṃ vicāryate kiṃ vidyāsaṃyuktameva agihotrādikaṃ karma mumukṣorvidyāhetutvea tayā saha ekakāryatvaṃ
pratipadyate a kevalam uta vidyāsaṃyuktaṃ kevalaṃ ca aviśeṣeṇeti kutaḥ saṃśayaḥ tametamātmāaṃ yajñea vividiṣati iti yajñādīāmaviśeṣeṇa ātmavedaāṅgatvea śravaṇāt vidyāsaṃyuktasya ca agihotrāderviśiṣṭatvāvagamāt
kiṃ tāvatprāptam vidyāsaṃyuktameva karma agihotrādi ātmavidyāśeṣatvaṃ pratipadyate a vidyāhīam vidyopetasya viśiṣṭatvāvagamādvidyāvihīāt yadahareva juhoti tadahaḥ puarmṛtyumapajayatyevaṃ vidvā ityādiśrutibhyaḥ buddhyā yukto yayā
pārtha karmabadhaṃ prahāsyasi dūreṇa hyavaraṃ karma buddhiyogāddhaaṃjaya ityādismṛtibhyaśca ityevaṃ prāpte pratipādyate yadeva vidyayeti hi satyametat vidyāsaṃyuktaṃ karma agihotrādikaṃ vidyāvihīātkarmaṇogihotrādviśiṣṭam vidvāiva
brāhmaṇo vidyāvihīādbrāhmaṇāt tathāpi ātyatamaapekṣaṃ vidyāvihīaṃ karma agihotrādikam kasmāt tametamātmāaṃ yajñea vividiṣati ityaviśeṣeṇa agihotrādervidyāhetutvea śrutatvāt au vidyāsaṃyuktasya agihotrādervidyāvihīādviśiṣṭatvāvagamāt vidyāvihīamagihotrādi ātmavidyāhetutveāapekṣameveti yuktam
aitadevam vidyāsahāyasyāgihotrādervidyāimittea sāmarthyātiśayea yogāt ātmajñāaṃ prati kaścitkāraṇatvātiśayo bhaviṣyati a tathā vidyāvihīasya iti yuktaṃ kalpayitum a tu yajñea vividiṣati ityatrāviśeṣeṇātmajñāāṅgatvea śrutasyāgihotrāderaaṅgatvaṃ
śakyamabhyupagatum tathā hi śrutiḥ yadeva vidyayā karoti śraddhayopaiṣadā tadeva vīryavattaraṃ bhavati iti vidyāsaṃyuktasya karmaṇogihotrādeḥ vīryavattaratvābhidhāea svakāryaṃ prati kaṃcidatiśayaṃ bruvāṇā vidyāvihīasya
tasyaiva tatprayojaaṃ prati vīryavattvaṃ darśayati karmaṇaśca vīryavattvaṃ tat yatsvaprayojaasādhaasahatvam tasmādvidyāsaṃyuktaṃ ityamagihotrādi vidyāvihīaṃ ca ubhayamapi mumukṣuṇā mokṣaprayojaoddeśea iha jamai jamātare ca
prāgjñāotpatteḥ kṛtaṃ yata tadyathāsāmarthyaṃ brahmādhigamapratibadhakāraṇopāttaduritakṣayahetutvadvāreṇa brahmādhigamakāraṇatvaṃ pratipadyamāaṃ śravaṇamaaaśraddhātātparyādyataraṅgakāraṇāpekṣaṃ brahmavidyayā saha ekakāryaṃ bhavatīti sthitam bhogea tvitare kṣapayitvā sampadyate itarakṣapaṇādhikaraṇam aārabdhakāryayoḥ puṇyapāpayorvidyāsāmarthyātkṣaya
uktaḥ itare tu ārabdhakārye puṇyapāpe upabhogea kṣapayitvā brahma saṃpadyate tasya tāvadeva ciraṃ yāvaa vimokṣyetha saṃpatsye iti brahmaiva sabrahmāpyeti iti ca
evamādiśrutibhyaḥ au satyapi samyagdarśae yathā prāgdehapātādbhedadarśaaṃ dvicadradarśaayāyeāuvṛttam evaṃ paścādapyuuvarteta a imittābhavāt upabhogaśeṣakṣapaṇaṃ hi tatrāuvṛttiimittam a ca tādṛśamatra kiṃcidasti au aparaḥ
karmāśayobhiavamupabhogamārapsyate a tasya dagdhabījatvāt mithyājñāāvaṣṭambhaṃ hi karmātaraṃ dehapāta upabhogātaramārabheta tacca mithyājñāaṃ samyagjñāea dagdham ityataḥ sādhvetat ārabdhakāryakṣaye viduṣaḥ kaivalyamavaśyaṃ bhavatīti iti
śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācāryasya śrīgovidabhagavatpūjyapādaśiṣyasya śrīmacchaṃkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīrakamīmāṃsāsūtrabhāṣye caturthādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ murat caturthodhyāyaḥ dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ vāṅmaasi darśaācchabdācca vāgadhikaraṇam asti prāyaṇaviṣayā śrutiḥ asya somya
puruṣasya prayato vāṅmaasi saṃpadyate maaḥ prāṇe prāṇastejasi tejaḥ parasyāṃ devatāyām iti kimiha vāca eva vṛttimattyā maasi saṃpattirucyate uta vāgvṛtteriti viśayaḥ
tatra vāgeva tāvat maasi saṃpadyata iti prāptam tathā hi śrutiraugṛhītā bhavati itarathā lakṣaṇā syāt śrutilakṣaṇāviśaye ca śrutiryāyyā a lakṣaṇā tasmāt
vāca eva ayaṃ maasi pralaya iti evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ vāgvṛttirmaasi saṃpadyata iti kathaṃ vāgvṛttiriti vyākhyāyate yāvatā vāṅmaasi ityeva ācāryaḥ paṭhati
satyametat paṭhiṣyati tu parastāt avibhāgo vacaāt iti tasmādatra vṛttyupaśamamātraṃ vivakṣatīti gamyate tattvapralayavivakṣāyāṃ tu sarvatraiva avibhāgasāmyāt kiṃ paratraiva viśiṃṣyāt avibhāgaḥ iti
tasmādatra vṛttyupasaṃhāravivakṣā vāgvṛttiḥ pūrvamupasaṃhriyate maovṛttāvavasthitāyāmityarthaḥ kasmāt darśaāt dṛśyate hi vāgvṛtteḥ pūrvopasaṃhāro maovṛttau vidyamāāyām a tu vāca eva vṛttimattyā maasyupasaṃhāraḥ keacidapi
draṣṭuṃ śakyate au śrutisāmarthyāt vāca evāyaṃ maasyapyayo yukta ityuktam etyāha atatprakṛtitvāt yasya hi yata utpattiḥ tasya tatra pralayo yāyyaḥ mṛdīva
śarāvasya a ca maaso vāgutpadyata iti kiṃcaa pramāṇamasti vṛttyudbhavābhibhavau tu aprakṛtisamāśrayāvapi dṛśyete pārthivebhyo hi idhaebhyaḥ taijasasyāgervṛttirudbhavati apsu ca upaśāmyati kathaṃ
tarhi asmipakṣe śabdaḥ vāṅmaasi saṃpadyate iti ata āha śabdācceti śabdopyasmipakṣevakalpate vṛttivṛttimatorabhedopacārādityarthaḥ ata eva ca sarvāṇyau tasmādupaśātatejāḥ puarbhavamidriyairmaasi saṃpadyamāaiḥ ityatra aviśeṣeṇa
sarveṣāmevedriyāṇāṃ maasi saṃpattiḥ śrūyate tatrāpi ata eva vāca iva cakṣurādīāmapi savṛttike maasyavasthite vṛttilopadarśaāt tattvapralayāsaṃbhavāt śabdopapatteśca vṛttidvāreṇaiva sarvāṇīdriyāṇi maouvartate sarveṣāṃ karaṇāāṃ
maasyupasaṃhārāviśeṣe sati vācaḥ pṛthaggrahaṇam vāṅmaasi saṃpadyate ityudāharaṇāurodhea tamaaḥ prāṇa uttarāt maodhikaraṇam samadhigatametat vāṅmaasi saṃpadyate ityatra vṛttisaṃpattivivakṣeti atha yaduttaraṃ vākyam maaḥ
prāṇe iti kimatrāpi vṛttisaṃpattireva vivakṣyate uta vṛttimatsaṃpattiḥ iti vicikitsāyām vṛttimatsaṃpattireva atra iti prāptam śrutyaugrahāt tatprakṛtitvopapatteśca tathā hi aamayaṃ hi somya
maa āpomayaḥ prāṇaḥ ityaayoi maa āmaati abyoiṃ ca prāṇam āpaścāamasṛjata iti śrutiḥ ataśca yamaaḥ prāṇe pralīyate aameva tadapsu pralīyate aaṃ
hi maaḥ āpaśca prāṇaḥ prakṛtivikārābhedāditi evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ tadapi āgṛhītabāhyedriyavṛtti mao vṛttidvāreṇaiva prāṇe pralīyata iti uttarādvākyādavagatavyam tathā hi suṣupsormumūrṣośca prāṇavṛttau
parispadātmikāyāmavasthitāyām maovṛttīāmupaśamo dṛśyate a ca maasaḥ svarūpāpyayaḥ prāṇe saṃbhavati atatprakṛtitvāt au darśitaṃ maasaḥ prāṇaprakṛtitvam aitatsāram a hi īdṛśea prāṇāḍikea tatprakṛtitvea
maaḥ prāṇe saṃpattumarhati evamapi hi ae maaḥ saṃpadyeta apsu cāam apsveva ca prāṇaḥ a hyetasmiapi pakṣe prāṇabhāvapariṇatābhyodbhyo mao jāyata iti
kiṃcaa pramāṇamasti tasmāt a maasaḥ prāṇe svarūpāpyayaḥ vṛttyapyayepi tu śabdovakalpate vṛttivṛttimatorabhedopacārāt iti darśitam sodhyakṣe tadupagamādibhyaḥ adhyakṣādhikaraṇam sthitametat yasya yato otpattiḥ
tasya tasmivṛttipralayaḥ a svarūpapralaya iti idamidāīm prāṇastejasi ityatra cityate kiṃ yathāśruti prāṇasya tejasyeva vṛttyupasaṃhāraḥ kiṃ vā dehedriyapañjarādhyakṣe jīva iti tatra
śruteraatiśaṅkyatvāt prāṇasya tejasyeva saṃpattiḥ syāt aśrutakalpaāyā ayāyyatvāt ityevaṃ prāpte pratipadyate sodhyakṣa iti sa prakṛtaḥ prāṇaḥ adhyakṣe avidyākarmapūrvaprajñopādhike vijñāātmai avatiṣṭhate tatpradhāā
prāṇavṛttirbhavatītyarthaḥ kutaḥ tadupagamādibhyaḥ evamevemamātmāamatakāle sarve prāṇā abhisamāyati yatraitadūrdhvoṃcchvāsī bhavati iti hi śrutyataram adhyakṣopagāmiaḥ sarvāprāṇā aviśeṣeṇa darśayati viśeṣeṇa ca tamutkrāmataṃ prāṇoūtkrāmati
iti pañcavṛtteḥ prāṇasya adhyakṣāugāmitāṃ darśayati tadauvṛttitāṃ ca itareṣām prāṇamaūtkrāmataṃ sarve prāṇā aūtkrāmati iti savijñāo bhavati iti ca adhyakṣasya atarvijñāavattvapradarśaea tasmi
apītakaraṇagrāmasya prāṇasya avasthāaṃ gamayati au prāṇastejasi iti śrūyate kathaṃ prāṇodhyakṣe ityadhikāvāpaḥ kriyate aiṣa doṣaḥ adhyakṣapradhāatvādutkramaṇādivyavahārasya śrutyataragatasyāpi ca viśeṣasyāpekṣaṇīyatvāt kathaṃ tarhi
prāṇastejasi iti śrutirityata āha bhūtaṣu tacchruteḥ sa prāṇasaṃpṛktodhyakṣaḥ tejaḥsahacariteṣu bhūteṣu dehabījabhūteṣu sūkṣmeṣu avatiṣṭhata ityavagatavyam prāṇastejasi iti śruteḥ au ca iyaṃ
śrutiḥ prāṇasya tejasi sthitiṃ darśayati a prāṇasaṃpṛktasyādhyakṣasya aiṣa doṣaḥ sodhyakṣe iti adhyakṣasyāpyatarāla upasaṃkhyātatvāt yopi hi srughāmathurāṃ gatvā mathurāyāḥ pāṭaliputraṃ vrajati
sopi srughātpāṭaliputraṃ yātīti śakyate vaditum tasmāt prāṇastejasi iti prāṇasaṃpṛktasyādhyakṣasyaiva etat tejaḥsahacariteṣu bhūteṣvavasthāam kathaṃ tejaḥsahacariteṣu bhūteṣvityucyate yāvatā ekameva tejaḥ śrūyate prāṇastejasi
iti ata āha aikasmidarśayato hi a ekasmieva tejasi śarīrātaraprepsāvelāyāṃ jīvo vatiṣṭhate kāryasya śarīrasyāekātmakatvadarśaāt darśayataś ca etam arthaṃ praśaprativacae āpaḥ puruṣavacasaḥ
iti tadvyākhyātam tryātmakatvāt tu bhūyastvāt ity atra śrutismṛtī ca etam arthaṃ darśayataḥ śrutiḥ pṛthvīmaya āpomayo vāyumaya ākāśamayas tejomayaḥ ityādyā smṛtir
api aṇvyo mātrāviāśiyo daśārdhāāṃ tu yāḥ smṛtāḥ tābhiḥ sārdham idaṃ sarvaṃ saṃbhavaty aupūrvaśaḥ ityādyā au ca upasaṃhṛteṣu vāgādiṣu karaṇeṣu śarīrātaraprepsāvelāyām
kvāyaṃ tadā puruṣo bhavati ity upakramya śrutyataraṃ karmāśrayatāṃ irūpayati tau ha yadūcatuḥ karma haiva tadūcaturatha ha yatpraśaśaṃsatuḥ karma haiva tatpraśaśaṃsatuḥ
iti atrocyate tatra karmaprayuktasya grahātigrahasaṃjñakasya idriyaviṣayātmakasya badhaasya pravṛttir iti karmāśrayatoktā iha puaḥ bhūtopādāād dehātarotpattir iti bhūtāśrayatvam uktam praśaṃsāśabdād api tatra
prādhāyamātraṃ karmaṇaḥ pradarśitam a tv āśrayātaraṃ ivāritam tasmād avirodhaḥ samāā cāsṛtyupakramādamṛtatvaṃ cāupoṣya āsṛtyupakramādhikaraṇam seyamutkrātiḥ kiṃ vidvadaviduṣoḥ samāā kiṃ vā viśeṣavatī
iti viśayāāāṃ viśeṣavatīti tāvatprāptam bhūtāśrayaviśiṣṭā hyeṣā puarbhavāya ca bhūtāyāśrīyate a ca viduṣaḥ puarbhavaḥ saṃbhavati amṛtatvaṃ hi vidvāaśute iti sthitiḥ tasmādaviduṣa
eva eṣā utkrātiḥ au vidyāprakaraṇe samāmāāt viduṣa eva eṣā bhavet a svāpādivat yathāprāptāukīrtaāt yathā hi yatraitatpuruṣaḥ svapiti āma aśiśiṣati āma
pipāsati āma iti ca sarvaprāṇisādhāraṇā eva svāpādayoukīrtyate vidyāprakaraṇepi pratipipādayiṣitavastupratipādaāuguṇyea a tu viduṣo viśeṣavato vidhitsyate evam iyamapi utkrātiḥ mahājaagataivāukīrtyate yasyāṃ parasyāṃ
devatāyāṃ puruṣasya prayataḥ tejaḥ saṃpadyate sa ātmā tattvamasi ityetatpratipādayitum pratiṣiddhā ca eṣā viduṣaḥ a tasya prāṇā utkrāmati iti tasmāt aviduṣa
evaiṣeti evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ samāā caiṣā utkrātiḥ vāṅmaasi ityādyā vidvadaviduṣoḥ āsṛtyupakramāt bhavitumarhati aviśeṣaśravaṇāt avidvā dehabījabhūtāi bhūtasūkṣmāṇyāśritya karmaprayukto dehagrahaṇamaubhava saṃsarati vidvāṃstu
jñāaprakāśitaṃ mokṣaāḍīdvāramāśrayate tadetat āsṛtyupakramāt ityuktam au amṛtatvaṃ viduṣā prāptavyam a ca taddeśātarāyattam tatra kuto bhūtāśrayatvaṃ sṛtyupakramo veti atrocyate aupoṣya ca
idam adagdhvā atyatamavidyādīkleśā aparavidyāsāmarthyāt āpekṣikamamṛtatvaṃ prepsate saṃbhavati tatra sṛtyupakramaḥ bhūtāśrayatvaṃ ca a hi irāśrayāṇāṃ prāṇāāṃ gatirupapadyate tasmādadoṣaḥ tadāpīteḥ saṃsāravyapadeśāt saṃsāravyapadeśādhikaraṇam
tejaḥ parasyāṃ devatāyām ityatra prakaraṇasāmarthyāt tat yathā prakṛtaṃ tejaḥ sādhyakṣaṃ saprāṇaṃ sakaraṇagrāmaṃ bhūtātarasahitaṃ prayataḥ puṃsaḥ parasyāṃ devatāyāṃ saṃpadyata ityetaduktaṃ bhavati
kīdṛśī puariyaṃ saṃpattiḥ syāditi cityate tatra ātyatika eva tāvat svarūpapravilaya iti prāptam tatprakṛtitvopapatteḥ sarvasya hi jaimato vastujātasya prakṛtiḥ parā devateti
pratiṣṭhāpitam tasmāt ātyatikī iyamavibhāgāpattiriti evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ tat tejaādi bhūtasūkṣmaṃ śrotrādikaraṇāśrayabhūtam āpīteḥ āsaṃsāramokṣāt samyagjñāaimittāt avatiṣṭhate yoimaye prapadyate śarīratvāya dehiaḥ sthāṇumayeusaṃyati
yathākarma yathāśrutam ityādisaṃsāravyapadeśāt ayathā hi sarvaḥ prāyaṇasamaya eva upādhipratyastamayādatyataṃ brahma saṃpadyeta tatra vidhiśāstramaarthakaṃ syāt vidyāśāstraṃ ca mithyājñāaimittaśca badho a samyagjñāādṛte
visraṃsitumarhati tasmāt tatprakṛtitvepi suṣuptipralayavat bījabhāvāvaśeṣaiva eṣā satsaṃpattiriti sūkṣmaṃ pramāṇataśca tathopalabdheḥ tacca itarabhūtasahitaṃ tejo jīvasya asmāccharīrātpravasata āśrayabhūtaṃ svarūpataḥ parimāṇataśca sūkṣmaṃ bhavitumarhati
tathā hi āḍīiṣkramaṇaśravaṇādibhyosya saukṣmyamupalabhyate tatra tautvātsaṃcāropapattiḥ svacchatvācca apratighātopapattiḥ ata eva ca dehāirgacchat pārśvasthairopalabhyate opamardeātaḥ ata eva ca sūkṣmatvāt āsya sthūlasya
śarīrasyopamardea dāhādiimittea itaratsūkṣmaṃ śarīramupamṛdyate asyaiva copapattereṣa ūṣmā asyaiva ca sūkṣmasya śarīrasya eṣa ūṣmā yametasmiñjīvaccharīre saṃsparśeoṣmāṇaṃ vijāati tathā hi mṛtāvasthāyām avasthitepi
dehe vidyamāeṣvapi ca rūpādiṣu dehaguṇeṣu a ūṣmā upalabhyate jīvadavasthāyāmeva tu upalabhyate ityata upapadyate prasiddhaśarīravyatiriktavyapāśraya eva eṣa ūṣmeti tathā ca śrutiḥ
uṣṇa eva jīviṣyañśīto mariṣya iti pratiṣedhāditi cea śārīrāt pratiṣedhādhikaraṇam amṛtatvaṃ cāupoṣya ityato viśeṣaṇāt ātyatikemṛtatve gatyutkrātyorabhāvobhyupagataḥ tatrāpi keacitkāraṇea utkrātimāśaṅkya pratiṣedhati athākāmayamāo
yokāmo iṣkāma āptakāma ātmakāmo bhavati a tasya prāṇā utkrāmati brahmaiva sabrahmāpyeti iti ataḥ paravidyāviṣayātpratiṣedhāt a parabrahmavido dehāt prāṇāām utkrātir astīti
cet ety ucyate yataḥ śārīrād ātmaa eṣa utkrātipratiṣedhaḥ prāṇāām a śarīrāt kathamavagamyate a tasmātprāṇā utkrāmati iti śākhātare pañcamīprayogāt saṃbadhasāmāyaviṣayā hi
ṣaṣṭhī śākhātaragatayā pañcamyā saṃbadhaviśeṣe vyavasthāpyate tasmāt iti ca prādhāyāt abhyudayaiḥśreyasādhikṛto dehī saṃbadhyate a dehaḥ a tasmāduccikramiṣorjīvāt prāṇā apakrāmati sahaiva tea
bhavati ityarthaḥ saprāṇasya ca pravasato bhavatyutkrātirdehāditi evaṃ prāpte pratyucyate spaṣṭo hyekeṣām aitadasti yad uktam parabrahmavido pi dehāt asty utkrātiḥ utkrātipratiṣedhasya
dehyapādāatvād iti yato dehāpādāa eva utkrātipratiṣedha ekeṣāṃ samāmātṛṇāṃ spaṣṭa upalabhyate tathā hi ārtabhāgapraśe yatrāyaṃ puruṣo mriyata udasmāt prāṇāḥ krāmatyāho eti
ity atra eti hovāca yājñavalkyaḥ ity autkrātipakṣaṃ parigṛhya a tarhy ayam autkrāteṣu prāṇeṣu mṛtaḥ ity asyāmāśaṅkāyām atraiva samavaīyate iti pravilayaṃ
prāṇāāṃ pratijñāya tatsiddhaye sa ucchvayatyādhmāyatyādhmāto mṛtaḥ śete iti saśabdaparāmṛṣṭasya prakṛtasya utkrātyavadheḥ ucchvayaādīi samāmaati dehasya ca etāi syuḥ a dehiaḥ tatsāmāyāt
a tasmātprāṇā utkrāmatyatraiva samavaīyate ityatrāpi abhedopacāreṇa dehāpādāasyaiva utkramaṇasya pratiṣedhaḥ yadyapi prādhāyaṃ dehiaḥ iti vyākhyeyam yeṣāṃ pañcamīpāṭhaḥ yeṣāṃ tu ṣaṣṭhīpāṭhaḥ teṣāṃ
vidvatsaṃbadhiī utkrātiḥ pratiṣidhyata iti prāptotkrātipratiṣedhārthatvāt asya vākyasya dehāpādāaiva sā pratiṣiddhā bhavati dehād utkrātiḥ prāptā a dehiaḥ api ca cakṣuṣṭo vā
mūrdho vāyebhyo vā śarīradeśebhyastamutkrāmataṃ prāṇoūtkrāmati prāṇamaūtkrāmataṃ sarve prāṇā aūtkrāmati ityevamavidvadviṣaye saprapañcamutkramaṇaṃ saṃsāragamaaṃ ca darśayitvā iti u kāmayamāaḥ iti upasaṃhṛtya avidvatkathām
athākāmayamāaḥ iti vyapadiśya vidvāṃsam yadi tadviṣayepyutkrātimeva prāpayet asamañjasa eva vyapadeśaḥ syāt tasmāt avidvadviṣaye prāptayorgatyutkrātyoḥ vidvadviṣaye pratiṣedhaḥ ityevameva vyākhyeyam vyapadeśārthavattvāya a
ca brahmavidaḥ sarvagatabrahmātmabhūtasya prakṣīṇakāmakarmaṇaḥ utkrātiḥ gatir vā upapadyate imittābhāvāt atra brahma samaśute iti ca evaṃjātīyakāḥ śrutayo gatyutkrātyor abhāvaṃ sūcayati smaryate
ca smaryatepi ca mahābhārate gatyutkrātyorabhāvaḥ sarvabhūtātmabhūtasya samyagbhūtāi paśyataḥ devā api mārge muhyatyapadasya padaiṣiṇaḥ iti au gatir api brahmavidaḥ sarvagatabrahmātmabhūtasya smaryate
śukaḥ kila vaiyāsakirmumukṣurādityamaṇḍalamabhipratasthe pitrā cāugamyāhūto bho iti pratiśuśrāva iti a saśarīrasyaiva ayaṃ yogabalea viśiṣṭadeśaprāptipūrvakaḥ śarīrotsarga iti draṣṭavyam sarvabhūtadṛśyatvādyupayāsāt a hi
aśarīraṃ gacchataṃ sarvabhūtāi draṣṭuṃ śakuyuḥ tathā ca tatraivopasaṃhṛtam śukastu mārutācchīghrāṃ gatiṃ kṛtvātarikṣagaḥ darśayitvā prabhāvaṃ svaṃ sarvabhūtagatobhavat iti tasmādabhāvaḥ parabrahmavido gatyutkrātyoḥ
gatiśrutīāṃ tu viṣayamupariṣṭādvyākhyāsyāmaḥ tāi pare tathā hymāha vāgādilayādhikaraṇam tāi puaḥ prāṇaśabdoditāi idriyāṇi bhūtāi ca parabrahmavidaḥ tasmi eva parasmi ātmai pralīyate
kasmāt tathā hi āha śrutiḥ evamevāsya paridraṣṭurimāḥ ṣoḍaśa kalāḥ puruṣāyaṇāḥ puruṣaṃ prāpyāstaṃ gacchati iti au gatāḥ kalāḥ pañcadaśa pratiṣṭhāḥ iti
vidvadviṣayaivāparā śrutiḥ parasmādātmaoyatrāpi kalāāṃ pralayam āha sma a sā khalu vyavahārāpekṣā pārthivādyāḥ kalāḥ pṛthivyādīreva svaprakṛtīrapiyatīti itarā tu vidvatpratipattyapekṣā kṛtsaṃ kalājātaṃ
parabrahmavido brahmaiva saṃpadyata iti tasmādadoṣaḥ avibhāgo vacaāt avibhāgādhikaraṇam sa puarviduṣaḥ kalāpralayaḥ kim itareṣāmiva sāvaśeṣo bhavati āhosviiravaśeṣa iti tatra pralayasāmāyāt śaktyavaśeṣatāprasaktau
bravīti avibhāgāpattireveti kutaḥ vacaāt tathā hi kalāpralayamuktvā vakti bhidyete tāsāṃ āmarūpe puruṣa ityevaṃ procyate sa eṣokalomṛto bhavati iti avidyāimittāāṃ ca
kalāāṃ a vidyāimitte pralaye sāvaśeṣatvopapattiḥ tasmādavibhāga eveti tadokograjvalaaṃ tatprakāśitadvāro vidyāsāmarthyāttaccheṣagatyausmṛtiyogācca hārdāugṛhītaḥ śatādhikayā tadokodhikaraṇam samāptā prāsaṅgikī paravidyāgatā citā saṃprati tu aparavidyāviṣayāmeva
citāmauvartayati samāā ca āsṛtyupakramāt vidvadaviduṣorutkrātiḥ ityuktam tam idāīṃ sṛtyupakramaṃ darśayati tasya upasaṃhṛtavāgādikalāpasyoccikramiṣato vijñāātmaaḥ okaḥ āyataaṃ hṛdayam sa etāstejomātrāḥ samabhyādadāo hṛdayamevāvavakrāmati
iti śruteḥ tadagraprajvalaapūrvikā cakṣurādisthāāpādāā ca utkrātiḥ śrūyate tasya haitasya hṛdayasyāgraṃ pradyotate tea pradyoteaiṣa ātmā iṣkrāmati cakṣuṣṭo vā mūrdho vāyebhyo vā
śarīradeśebhyaḥ iti sā kimaiyameaiva vidvadaviduṣorbhavati athāsti kaścidviduṣo viśeṣaiyamaḥ iti vicikitsāyām śrutyaviśeṣādaiyamaprāptau ācaṣṭe samāepi hi vidvadaviduṣorhṛdayāgrapradyotae tatprakāśitadvāratve ca mūrdhasthāādeva vidvāiṣkrāmati sthāātarebhyastu

iti raśmyausārī raśmyadhikaraṇam asti hārdavidyā atha yadidamasmibrahmapure daharaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ veśma ityupakramya vihitā tatprakriyāyām atha yā etā hṛdayasya āḍyaḥ ityupakramya saprapañcaṃ
āḍīraśmisaṃbadhamuktvā uktam atha yatraitadasmāccharīrādutkrāmatyathaitaireva raśmibhirūrdhvamākramate iti puaścoktam tayordhvamāyaamṛtatvameti iti tasmāt śatādhikayā āḍyā iṣkrāma raśmyausārī iṣkrāmatīti gamyate tat kim aviśeṣeṇaiva ahai

ca śrutestu arthaṃ vakṣyati ātivāhikāstalliṅgāt iti au ca yatra kāle tvaāvṛttimāvṛttiṃ caiva yogiaḥ prayātā yāti taṃ kālaṃ vakṣyāmi bharatarṣabha iti

agirjyotirahaḥ śuklaḥ ṣaṇmāsā uttarāyaṇam dhūmo rātristathā kṛṣṇaḥ ṣaṇmāsā dakṣiṇāyaam iti ca śrautāvetau devayāapitṛyāṇau pratyabhijñāyete smṛtāvapīti ucyate taṃ kālaṃ vakṣyāmi iti

sa brahmalokam iti kauṣītakiāṃ devayāaḥ pathāḥ paṭhyate tatra arciragilokaśabdau tāvat ekārthau jvalaavacaatvāditi ātra saṃiveśakramaḥ kaścidaveṣyaḥ vāyustu arcirādau vartmai katamasmisthāe iveśayitavya
iti ucyate terciṣamevābhisaṃbhavatyarciṣoharaha āpūryamāṇapakṣamāpūryamāṇapakṣādyāṣaḍudaṅṅeti māsāṃstāmāsebhyaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ saṃvatsarādādityam ityatra saṃvatsarātparāñcam ādityādarvāñcaṃ vāyumabhisaṃbhavati kasmāt aviśeṣaviśeṣābhyām tathā hi sa vāyulokam ityatra aviśeṣopadiṣṭasya vāyoḥ
śrutyatareṇa viśeṣopadeśo dṛśyate yadā vai puruṣosmāllokātpraiti sa vāyumāgacchati tasmai sa tatra vijihīte yathā rathacakrasya khaṃ tea sa ūrdhvamākramate sa ādityamāgacchati

devayāaṃ pathāam āsādyāgilokam āgacchati sa vāyulokaṃ sa varuṇalokam iti ucyate kevalo tra pāṭhaḥ paurvāparyeṇāvasthitaḥ ātra kramavacaaḥ kaścic chabdo sti padārthopadarśaamātraṃ
hy atra kriyate etaṃ etaṃ ca āgacchatīti itaratra puaḥ vāyuprattea rathacakramātreṇa cchidreṇa ūrdhvam ākramya ādityam āgacchatīti avagamyate kramaḥ tasmāt sūktam
aviśeṣaviśeṣābhyām iti vājasaeyias tu māsebhyo devalokaṃ devalokād ādityam iti samāmaati tatra ādityāataryāya devalokādvāyumabhisaṃbhaveyuḥ vāyumabdāt iti tu cchadogaśrutyapekṣayoktam chādogyavājasaeyakayostu ekatra devaloko
a vidyate paratra saṃvatsaraḥ tatra śrutidvayapratyayāt ubhāvapi ubhayatra grathayitavyau tatrāpi māsasaṃbadhātsaṃvatsaraḥ pūrvaḥ paścimo devaloka iti vivektavyam taḍito dhi varuṇaḥ sambadhāt
taḍidadhikaraṇam ādityāc cadramasaṃ cadramaso vidyutam ity asyā vidyuta upariṣṭāt sa varuṇalokam ity ayaṃ varuṇaḥ saṃbadhyeta asti hi saṃbadho vidyudvaruṇayoḥ yadā
hi viśālā vidyutas tīvrastaitairghoṣā jīmūtodareṣu praṛtyati atha āpaḥ prapatati vidyotate staayati varṣiṣyati vā iti ca brāhmaṇam apāṃ ca adhipatir varuṇa
iti śrutismṛtiprasiddhiḥ varuṇād adhi idraprajāpatī sthāātarābhāvāt pāṭhasāmarthyāc ca āgatukatvād api varuṇādīām ate eva iveśaḥ vaiśeṣikasthāābhāvāt vidyuc ca atyā arcir ādau
vartmai ātivāhikāstalliṅgāt ātivāhikādhikaraṇam teṣv eva arcirādiṣu saṃśayaḥ kim etāi mārgacihāi uta bhogabhūmayaḥ athavā etāro gatṛṇām iti tatra mārgalakṣaṇabhūtā arcirādaya iti
tāvat prāptam tatsvarūpatvād upadeśasya yathā hi loke kaścid grāmaṃ agaraṃ vā pratiṣṭhāsamāo uśiṣyate gaccha itas tvam amuṃ giriṃ tato yagrodhaṃ
tato adīṃ tato grāmaṃ tato agaraṃ vā prāpsyasīti evam ihāpi arciṣo har aha āpūryamāṇapakṣam ityādy āha atha vā bhogabhūmaya iti
prāptam tathā hi lokaśabdea agyādī aubadhāti agilokam āgacchati ityādi lokaśabdaś ca prāṇiāṃ bhogāyataeṣu bhāṣyate mauṣyalokaḥ pitṛloko devalokaḥ iti ca tathā
ca brāhmaṇam ahorātreṣu te lokeṣu sajjate ityādi tasmā ātivāhikā arcirādayaḥ acetaatvād apy eṣām ātivāhikatvāupapattiḥ cetaā hi loke rājaiyuktāḥ puruṣā durgeṣu
mārgeṣv ativāhyā ativāhayatīti evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ ātivāhikā evaite bhavitum arhati kutaḥ talliṅgāt tathā hi cadramaso vidyutaṃ tatpuruṣo māavaḥ sa etā
brahma gamayati iti siddhavad gamayitṛtvaṃ darśayati tadvacaaṃ tadviṣayam evopakṣīṇam iti cet a prāptamāavatvaivṛttiparatvād viśeṣaṇasya yady arcirādiṣu puruṣā gamayitāraḥ prāptāḥ te
ca māavāḥ tato yuktaṃ taivṛttyarthaṃ puruṣaviśeṣaṇam amāava iti au talliṅgamātram agamakam yāyābhāvāt aiṣa doṣaḥ ubhayavyāmohāt tatsiddheḥ ye tāvad arcirādimārgagāḥ te
dehaviyogāt saṃpiṇḍitakaraṇagrāmā iti asvatatrāḥ arcirādīām apy acetaatvād asvātatryam ity ataḥ arcirādyabhimāiaś cetaā devatāviśeṣā atiyātrāyāṃ iyuktā iti gamyate loke pi hi
mattamūrchitādayaḥ saṃpiṇḍitakaraṇāḥ paraprayuktavartmāo bhavati aavasthitatvād apy arcirādīāṃ a mārgalakṣaṇatvopapattiḥ a hi rātrau pretasya ahaḥsvarūpābhisaṃbhava upapadyate a ca pratipālaam astīty uktaṃ
purastāt dhruvatvāt tu devatātmaāṃ āyaṃ doṣo bhavati arcirādiśabdatā ca eṣām arcirādyabhimāād upapadyate arciṣo haḥ ityādiirdeśas tu ātivāhikatve pi a virudhyate
arciṣā hetuā ahar abhisaṃbhavati ahā hetuā āpūryamāṇapakṣam iti tathā ca loke prasiddheṣv apy ātivāhikeṣu evaṃjātīyaka upadeśo dṛśyate gaccha tvam ito
balavarmāṇaṃ tato jayasiṃhaṃ tataḥ kṛṣṇaguptam iti api ca upakrame te rcir abhisaṃbhavati iti saṃbadhamātram uktam a saṃbadhaviśeṣaḥ kaścit upasaṃhāre tu
sa etā brahma gamayati iti saṃbadhaviśeṣaḥ ativāhyātivāhakatvalakṣaṇa uktaḥ tea sa evopakrame pīti irdhāryate saṃpiṇḍitakaraṇatvād eva ca gatṛṇāṃ a tatra bhogasaṃbhavaḥ
lokaśabdas tu aupabhuñjāeṣv api gatṛṣu gamayituṃ śakyate ayeṣāṃ tallokavāsiāṃ bhogabhūmitvāt ataḥ agisvāmikaṃ lokaṃ prāptaḥ agiā ativāhyate vāyusvāmikaṃ prāpto vāyuā iti
yojayitavyam kathaṃ puar ātivāhikatvapakṣe varuṇādiṣu tatsaṃbhavaḥ vidyuto hy adhi varuṇādaya upakṣiptāḥ vidyutas tv aataram ā brahmaprāpteḥ amāavasyaiva puruṣasya gamayitṛtvaṃ śrutam
ity ata uttaraṃ paṭhati vaidyuteaiva tatastacchruteḥ tato vidyudabhisaṃbhavaādūrdhvaṃ vidyudaataravartiaivāmāavea puruṣeṇa varuṇalokādiṣvativāhyamāā brahmalokaṃ gacchatītyavagatavyam tāvaidyutātpuruṣomāavaḥ sa etya brahmalokaṃ gamayati iti tasyaiva
gamayitṛtvaśruteḥ varuṇādayastu tasyaiva apratibadhakaraṇea sāhāyyāuṣṭhāea vā keacit augrāhakā ityavagatavyam tasmātsādhūktam ātivāhikā devatātmāorcirādaya iti kāryaṃ bādarir asya gatyupapatteḥ kāryādhikaraṇam sa eā
brahma gamayati ity atra vicikitsyate kiṃ kāryam aparaṃ brahma gamayati āhosvit param evāvikṛtaṃ mukhyaṃ brahmeti kutaḥ saṃśayaḥ brahmaśabdaprayogāt gatiśruteśca tatra
kāryameva saguṇamaparaṃ brahma eāgamayatyamāavaḥ puruṣa iti bādarirācāryo mayate kutaḥ asya gatyupapatteḥ asya hi kāryabrahmaṇo gatavyatvam upapadyate pradeśavattvāt a tu parasmi
brahmaṇi gatṛtvaṃ gatavyatvaṃ gatir vā avakalpate sarvagatatvātpratyagātmatvācca gatṛṇām viśeṣitatvācca brahmalokāgamayati te teṣu brahmalokeṣu parāḥ parāvato vasati iti ca śrutyatare viśeṣitatvāt
kāryabrahmaviṣayaiva gatiriti gamyate a hi bahuvacaea viśeṣaṇaṃ parasmibrahmaṇyavakalpate kārye tu avasthābhedopapatteḥ saṃbhavati bahuvacaam lokaśrutirapi vikāragocarāyāmeva saṃiveśaviśiṣṭāyāṃ bhogabhūmāvāñjasī gauṇī tvayatra brahmaiva
loka eṣa samrāṭ ityādiṣu adhikaraṇādhikartavyairdeśopi parasmibrahmaṇi aāñjasaḥ syāt tasmāt kāryaviṣayamevedaṃ ayaam au kāryaviṣayepi brahmaśabdo opapadyate samavaye hi samastasya jagato jamādikāraṇaṃ
brahmeti sthāpitam ityatrocyate sāmīpyātu tadvyapadeśaḥ tuśabda āśaṅkāvyāvṛttyarthaḥ parabrahmasāmīpyāt aparasya brahmaṇaḥ tasmiapi brahmaśabdaprayogo a virudhyate parameva hi brahma viśuddhopādhisaṃbadhaṃ kvacitkaiścidvikāradharmairmaomayatvādibhiḥ upāsaāya
upadiśyamāam aparamiti sthitiḥ au kāryaprāptau aāvṛttiśravaṇaṃ a ghaṭate a hi parasmādbrahmaṇoyatra kvaciityatāṃ saṃbhāvayati darśayati ca devayāea pathā prasthitāāmaāvṛttim etea pratipadyamāā
imaṃ māavamāvartaṃ āvartate iti teṣāmiha a puarāvṛttirasti tayordhvamāyaamṛtatvameti iti ca atra brūmaḥ kāryātyaye tadadhyakṣeṇa sahātaḥ paramabhidhāāt kāryabrahmalokapralayapratyupasthāe sati tatraiva utpaasamyagdarśaāḥ
sataḥ tadadhyakṣeṇa hiraṇyagarbheṇa saha ataḥ para pariśuddhaṃ viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ pratipadyate itītthaṃ kramamuktiḥ aāvṛttyādiśrutyabhidhāebhyobhyupagatavyā a hyañjasaiva gatipūrvikā paraprāptiḥ saṃbhavatītyupapāditam smṛteś
ca smṛtirapyetamarthamaujāāti brahmaṇā saha te sarve saṃprāpte pratisaṃcare parasyāte kṛtātmāaḥ praviśati paraṃ padam iti tasmātkāryabrahmaviṣayā eva gatiśrutayaḥ iti siddhātaḥ kaṃ
puaḥ pūrvapakṣamāśaṅkya ayaṃ siddhātaḥ pratiṣṭhāpitaḥ kāryaṃ bādariḥ ityādieti sa idāīṃ sūtrair evopadarśyate paraṃ jaimiir mukhyatvāt jaimiistvācāryaḥ sa eābrahma gamayati ityatra
parameva brahma prāpayatīti mayate kutaḥ mukhyatvāt paraṃ hi brahma brahmaśabdasya mukhyamālambaam gauṇamaparam mukhyagauṇayośca mukhye saṃpratyayo bhavati darśaācca tayordhvamāyaamṛtatvameti iti ca
gatipūrvakamamṛtatvaṃ darśayati amṛtatvaṃ ca parasmibrahmaṇyupapadyate a kārye viāśitvātkāryasya atha yatrāyatpaśyati tadalpaṃ tamartyam iti pravacaāt paraviṣayaiva ca eṣā gatiḥ kaṭhavallīṣu paṭhyate
a hi tatra vidyātaraprakramosti ayatra dharmādayatrādharmāt iti parasyaiva brahmaṇaḥ prakrātatvāt a ca kārye pratipattyabhisadhiḥ api ca prajāpateḥ sabhāṃ veśma prapadye
iti āyaṃ kāryaviṣayaḥ pratipattyabhisaṃdhiḥ āmarūpayor irvahitā te yad atarā tad brahma iti kāryavilakṣaṇasya parasyaiva brahmaṇaḥ prakṛtatvāt yaśohaṃ bhavāmi brāhmaṇāām iti
ca sarvātmatveopakramaṇāt a tasya pratimā asti yasya āma mahadyaśaḥ iti ca parasyaiva brahmaṇo yaśoāmatvaprasiddheḥ sā ceyaṃ veśmapratipattirgatipūrvikā hārdavidyāyāmuditā tadaparājitā pūrbrahmaṇaḥ
prabhuvimitaṃ hiraṇmayam ityatra paderapi ca gatyarthatvāt mārgāpekṣatā avasīyate tasmātparabrahmaviṣayā gatiśrutaya iti pakṣātaram tāvetau dvau pakṣāvācāryeṇa sūtritau gatyupapattyādibhirekaḥ mukhyatvādibhiraparaḥ tatra gatyupapattyādayaḥ
prabhavati mukhyatvādīābhāsayitum a tu mukhyatvādayo gatyupapattyādī iti ādya eva siddhāto vyākhyātaḥ dvitīyastu pūrvapakṣaḥ a hyasatyapi saṃbhave mukhyasyaivārthasya grahaṇamiti kaścidājñāpayitā vidyate
paravidyāprakaraṇepi ca tatstutyarthaṃ vidyātarāśrayagatyaukīrtaamupapadyate viṣvaṅṅayā utkramaṇe bhavati itivat prajāpateḥ sabhāṃ veśma prapadye iti tu pūrvavākyavicchedea kāryepi pratipattyabhisaṃdhira virudhyate saguṇepi ca
brahmaṇi sarvātmatvasaṃkīrtaam sarvakarmā sarvakāmaḥ ityādivat avakalpate tasmādaparaviṣayā eva gatiśrutayaḥ kecitpuaḥ pūrvāṇi pūrvapakṣasūtrāṇi bhavati uttarāṇi siddhātasūtrāṇi ityetāṃ vyavasthāmaurudhyamāāḥ paraviṣayā eva gatiśrutīḥ
pratiṣṭhāpayati tat aupapaam gatavyatvāupapatterbrahmaṇaḥ yatsarvagataṃ sarvātaraṃ sarvātmakaṃ ca paraṃ brahma ākāśavatsarvagataśca ityaḥ yatsākṣādaparokṣādbrahma ya ātmā sarvātaraḥ ātmaivedaṃ sarvam brahmaivedaṃ viśvamidaṃ
variṣṭham ityādiśrutiirdhāritaviśeṣam tasya gatavyatā a kadācidapyupapadyate a hi gatameva gamyate ayo hyayadgacchatīti prasiddhaṃ loke au loke gatasyāpi gatavyatā deśātaraviśiṣṭasya dṛṣṭā
yathā pṛthivīstha eva pṛthivīṃ deśātaradvāreṇa gacchati tathā aayatvepi bālasya kālātaraviśiṣṭaṃ vārdhakaṃ svātmabhūtameva gatavyaṃ dṛṣṭam tadvat brahmaṇopi sarvaśaktyupetatvāt kathaṃcit gatavyatā syāditi
a pratiṣiddhasarvaviśeṣatvādbrahmaṇaḥ iṣkalaṃ iṣkriyaṃ śātaṃ iravadyaṃ irañjaam asthūlamaaṇvahrasvamadīrgham sa bāhyābhyataro hyajaḥ sa vā eṣa mahāaja ātmājaromaromṛtobhayo brahma sa eṣa eti
etyātmā ityādiśrutismṛtiyāyebhyo a deśakālādiviśeṣayogaḥ paramātmai kalpayituṃ śakyate yea bhūpradeśavayovasthāyāyeāsya gatavyatā syāt bhūvayasostu pradeśāvasthādiviśeṣayogādupapadyate deśakālaviśiṣṭā gatavyatā jagadutpattisthitipralayahetutvaśruteraekaśaktitvaṃ brahmaṇa iti cet a
viśeṣairākaraṇaśrutīāmaayārthatvāt utpattyādiśrutīāmapi samāamaayārthatvamiti cet a tāsāmekatvapratipādaaparatvāt mṛdādidṛṣṭātairhi sato brahmaṇa ekasya satyatvaṃ vikārasya ca aṛtatvaṃ pratipādayat śāstraṃ otpattyādiparaṃ bhavitumarhati kasmāt puar
utpattyādiśrutīāṃ viśeṣairākaraṇaśrutiśeṣatvam a puaritaraśeṣatvamitarāsāmiti ucyate viśeṣairākaraṇaśrutīāṃ irākāṅkṣārthatvāt a hi ātmaa ekatvaityatvaśuddhatvādyavagatau satyāṃ bhūyaḥ kācidākāṅkṣā upajāyate puruṣārthasamāptibuddhyutpatteḥ tatra ko mohaḥ kaḥ
śoka ekatvamaupaśyataḥ abhayaṃ vai jaaka prāptosi vidvāa bibheti kutaścaa etha vāva a tapati kimahsādhu ākaravam kimahaṃ pāpamakaravam ityādiśrutibhyaḥ tathaiva ca
viduṣāṃ tuṣṭyaubhavādidarśaāt vikārāṛtābhisaṃdhyapavādācca mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyumāpoti ya iha āeva paśyati iti ato a viśeṣairākaraṇaśrutīāmayaśeṣatvamavagatuṃ śakyam aivamutpattyādiśrutīāṃ irākāṅkṣārthapratipādaasāmarthyamasti pratyakṣaṃ tu tāsāmayārthatvaṃ
samaugamyate tathā hi tatraitacchuṅgamutpatitaṃ somya vijāīhi edamamūlaṃ bhaviṣyati ityupayasya udarke sata evaikasya jagamūlasya vijñeyatvaṃ darśayati yato vā imāi bhūtāi jāyate
yea jātāi jīvati yatprayatyabhisaṃviśati tadvijijñāsasva tadbrahma iti ca evamutpattyādiśrutīām aikātmyāvagamaparatvāt āekaśaktiyogo brahmaṇaḥ ataśca gatavyatvāupapattiḥ a tasya prāṇā utkrāmati brahmaiva sabrahmāpyeti
iti ca parasmibrahmaṇi gatiṃ ivārayati tadvyakhyātam spaṣṭo hyekeṣām ityatra gatikalpaāyāṃ ca gatā jīvo gatavyasya brahmaṇaḥ avayavaḥ vikāraḥ ayo vā tataḥ
syāt atyatatādātmye gamaāupapatteḥ yadyevam tataḥ kiṃ syāt ata ucyate yadyekadeśaḥ tea ekadeśio ityaprāptatvāt a puarbrahmagamaamupapadyate ekadeśaikadeśitvakalpaā ca brahmaṇyaupapaā iravayavatvaprasiddheḥ vikārapakṣepyetattulyam

eva jīvo brahmaṇaḥ soṇuḥ vyāpī madhyamaparimāṇo vā bhavitumarhati vyāpitve gamaāupapattiḥ madhyamaparimāṇatve ca aityatvaprasaṅgaḥ aṇutve kṛtsaśarīravedaāupapattiḥ pratiṣiddhe ca aṇutvamadhyamaparimāṇatve vistareṇa purastāt
parasmācca ayatve jīvasya tattvamasi ityādiśāstrabādhaprasaṅgaḥ vikārāvayavapakṣayorapi samāoyaṃ doṣaḥ vikārāvayavayostadvatoayatvāt adoṣa iti cet a mukhyaikatvāupapatteḥ sarveṣu ca eteṣu pakṣeṣu airmokṣaprasaṅgaḥ saṃsāryātmatvāivṛtteḥ
ivṛttau vā svarūpaāśaprasaṅgaḥ brahmātmatvāabhyupagamācca yat tu kaiścij jalpyate ityāi aimittikāi ca karmāṇyauṣṭhīyate pratyavāyāutpattaye kāmyāi pratiṣiddhāi ca parihriyate svargaarakāavāptaye sāṃpratadehopabhogyāi ca
karmāṇyupabhogeaiva kṣipyate ityato vartamāadehapātādūrdhvaṃ dehātarapratisaṃdhāakāraṇābhāvāt svarūpāvasthāalakṣaṇaṃ kaivalyaṃ viāpi brahmātmatayā evaṃvṛttasya setsyatīti tadasat pramāṇābhāvāt a hyetat śāstreṇa keacitpratipāditam mokṣārthī itthaṃ samācarediti
svamaīṣayā tu etattarkitam yasmātkarmaimittaḥ saṃsāraḥ tasmāimittābhāvāa bhaviṣyatīti a ca etat tarkayituṃ śakyate imittābhāvasya durjñāatvāt bahūi hi karmāṇi jātyatarasaṃcitāi iṣṭāiṣṭavipākāi ekaikasya
jatoḥ saṃbhāvyate teṣāṃ viruddhaphalāāṃ yugapadupabhogāsaṃbhavāt kāicillabdhāvasarāṇi idaṃ jama irmimate kāicittu deśakālaimittapratīkṣāṇyāsate ityataḥ teṣāmavaśiṣṭāāṃ sāṃprateopabhogea kṣapaṇāsaṃbhavāt a yathāvarṇitacaritasyāpi vartamāadehapāte dehātaraimittābhāvaḥ śakyate
iścetum karmaśeṣasadbhāvasiddhiśca tadya iha ramaṇīyacaraṇāḥ tataḥ śeṣeṇa ityādiśrutismṛtibhyaḥ syādetat ityaaimittikāi teṣāṃ kṣepakāṇi bhaviṣyatīti tat a virodhābhāvāt sati hi virodhe kṣepyakṣepakabhāvo
bhavati a ca jamātarasaṃcitāāṃ sukṛtāāṃ ityaaimittikairasti virodhaḥ śuddhirūpatvāviśeṣāt duritāāṃ tu aśuddhirūpatvāt sati virodhe bhavatu kṣapaṇam a tu tāvatā dehātaraimittābhāvasiddhiḥ sukṛtaimittatvopapatteḥ
duritasyāpyaśeṣakṣapaṇāavagamāt a ca ityaaimittikāuṣṭhāāt pratyavāyāutpattimātram a puaḥ phalātarotpattiḥ iti pramāṇamasti phalātarasyāpyauiṣpādiaḥ saṃbhavāt smarati hi āpastambaḥ tadyathā āmre phalārthe imitte chāyāgadhāvaūtpadyete
evaṃ dharmaṃ caryamāṇam arthā aūtpadyate iti a ca asati samyagdarśae sarvātmaā kāmyapratiṣiddhavarjaaṃ jamaprāyaṇātarāle keacitpratijñātuṃ śakyam suipuṇāāmapi sūkṣmāparādhadarśaāt saṃśayitavyaṃ tu bhavati
tathāpi imittābhāvasya durjñāatvameva a ca aabhyupagamyamāe jñāagamye brahmātmatve kartṛtvabhoktṛtvasvabhāvasya ātmaaḥ kaivalyamākāṅkṣituṃ śakyam agyauṣṇyavat svabhāvasyāparihāryatvāt syādetat kartṛtvabhoktṛtvakāryam aarthaḥ a tacchaktiḥ tea
śaktyavasthāepi kāryaparihārādupapao mokṣa iti tacca a śaktisadbhāve kāryaprasavasya durivāratvāt athāpi syāt a kevalā śaktiḥ kāryamārabhate aapekṣya ayāi imittāi ata ekākiī
sā sthitāpi āparādhyatīti tacca a imittāāmapi śaktilakṣaṇea saṃbadhea ityasaṃbaddhatvāt tasmāt kartṛtvabhoktṛtvasvabhāve sati ātmai asatyāṃ vidyāgamyāyāṃ brahmātmatāyām a kathaṃcaa mokṣaṃ prati
āśā asti śrutiśca āyaḥ pathā vidyateyaāya iti jñāādayaṃ mokṣamārgaṃ vārayati parasmād aayatvepi jīvasya sarvavyavahāralopaprasaṅgaḥ pratyakṣādipramāṇāpravṛtteriti cet a prākprabodhāt svapavyavahāravat tadupapatteḥ
śāstraṃ ca yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati taditara itaraṃ paśyati ityādiā aprabuddhaviṣaye pratyakṣādivyavahāramuktvā puaḥ prabuddhaviṣaye yatra tvasya sarvamātmaivābhūttatkea kaṃ paśyet
ityādiā tadabhāvaṃ darśayati tad evaṃ parabrahmavido gatavyādivijñāasya bādhitatvāt a kathaṃcaa gatir upapādayituṃ śakyā kiṃviṣayāḥ puargatiśrutaya iti ucyate saguṇavidyāviṣayā bhaviṣyati tathā
hi kvacitpañcāgividyāṃ prakṛtya gatirucyate kvacitparyaṅkavidyām kvacidvaiśvāaravidyām yatrāpi brahma prakṛtya gatirucyate yathā prāṇo brahma kaṃ brahma khaṃ brahma iti atha yadidamasmibrahmapure
daharaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ veśma iti ca tatrāpi vāmaītvādibhiḥ satyakāmādibhiśca guṇaiḥ saguṇasyaiva upāsyatvāt saṃbhavati gatiḥ a kvacitparabrahmaviṣayā gatiḥ śrāvyate yathā gatipratiṣedhaḥ śrāvitaḥ
a tasya prāṇā utkrāmati iti brahmavid āpoti param ityādiṣu tu satyapi āpotergatyarthatve varṇitea yāyea deśātaraprāptyasaṃbhavāt svarūpapratipattireveyam avidyādhyāropitaāmarūpapravilayāpekṣayā abhidhīyate brahmaiva sabrahmāpyeti
ityādivat iti draṣṭavyam api ca paraviṣayā gatirvyākhyāyamāā prarocaāya vā syāt aucitaāya vā tatra prarocaaṃ tāvat brahmavido a gatyuktyā kriyate svasaṃvedyeaiva
avyavahitea vidyāsamarpitea svāsthyea tatsiddheḥ a ca ityasiddhaiḥśreyasaivedaasya asādhyaphalasya vijñāasya gatyaucitae kācidapekṣā upapadyate tasmādaparaviṣayā gatiḥ tatra parāparabrahmavivekāavadhāraṇea aparasmibrahmaṇi vartamāā gatiśrutayaḥ parasmiadhyāropyate
kiṃ dve brahmaṇī paramaparaṃ ceti bāḍham etad vai satyakāma paraṃ cāparaṃ ca brahma yadoṃkāraḥ ityādidarśaāt kiṃ puaḥ paraṃ brahma kimaparamiti
ucyate yatra avidyākṛtaāmarūpādiviśeṣapratiṣedhāt asthūlādiśabdairbrahmopadiśyate tatparam tadeva yatra āmarūpādiviśeṣeṇa keacidviśiṣṭam upāsaāyopadiśyate maomayaḥ prāṇaśarīro bhārūpaḥ ityādiśabdaiḥ tad aparam au evam advitīyaśrutir uparudhyeta
a avidyākṛtaāmarūpopādhikatayā parihṛtatvāt tasya ca aparabrahmopāsaasya tatsaṃidhau śrūyamāṇam sa yadi pitṛlokakāmo bhavati ityādi jagadaiśvaryalakṣaṇaṃ saṃsāragocarameva phalaṃ bhavati aivartitatvādavidyāyāḥ tasya ca
deśaviśeṣāvabaddhatvāt tatprāptyarthaṃ gamaamaviruddham sarvagatatvepi ca ātmaaḥ ākāśasyeva ghaṭādigamae buddhyādyupādhigamae gamaaprasiddhiḥ ityavādiṣma tadguṇasāratvāt ityatra tasmāt kāryaṃ bādariḥ ityeṣa eva sthitaḥ pakṣaḥ
paraṃ jaimiiḥ iti tu pakṣātarapratibhāamātrapradarśaaṃ prajñāvikāsaāyeti draṣṭavyam apraṃtīkālambaāayatīti bādarāyaṇa ubhayathādoṣāttatkratuśca apratīkālambaādhikaraṇam sthitametat kāryaviṣayā gatiḥ a paraviṣayeti idamidāīṃ saṃdihyate kiṃ sarvāvikārālambaā
aviśeṣeṇaiva amāavaḥ puruṣaḥ prāpayati brahmalokam uta kāṃścideveti kiṃ tāvatprāptam sarveṣāmeva eṣāṃ viduṣām ayatra parasmādbrahmaṇaḥ gatiḥ syāt tathā hi aiyamaḥ sarvāsām
ityatra aviśeṣeṇaiva eṣā vidyātareṣvavatāriteti evaṃ prāpte pratyāha apratīkālambaāiti pratīkālambaāvarjayitvā sarvāayāvikārālambaā ayati brahmalokam iti bādarāyaṇa ācāryo mayate a hi evam ubhayathābhāvābhyupagame
kaściddoṣosti aiyamayāyasya pratīkavyatirikteṣvapyupāsaeṣūpapatteḥ tatkratuśca asya ubhayathābhāvasya samarthako heturdraṣṭavyaḥ yo hi brahmakratuḥ sa brāhmamaiśvaryamāsīdet iti śliṣyate taṃ yathā yathopāsate tadeva bhavati
iti śruteḥ a tu pratīkeṣu brahmakratutvamasti pratīkapradhāatvādupāsaasya au abrahmakraturapi brahma gacchatīti śrūyate yathā pañcāgividyāyām sa eābrahma gamayati iti bhavatu yatra
evam āhatyavāda upalabhyate tadabhāve tu autsargikeṇa tatkratuyāyea brahmakratūāmeva tatprāptiḥ a itareṣām iti gamyate viśeṣaṃ ca darśayati āmādiṣu pratīkopāsaeṣu pūrvasmātpūrvasmāt phalaviśeṣam
uttarasmiuttarasmi upāsae darśayati yāvaāmo gataṃ tatrāsya yathākāmacāro bhavati vāgvāva āmo bhūyasī yāvadvāco gataṃ tatrāsya yathākāmacāro bhavati mao vāva vāco bhūyaḥ
ityādiā sa ca ayaṃ phalaviśeṣaḥ pratīkatatratvādupāsaāām upapadyate brahmatatratve tu brahmaṇoviśiṣṭatvāt kathaṃ phalaviśeṣaḥ syāt tasmāt a pratīkālambaāām itaraistulyaphalatvamiti iti śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācāryasya śrīgovidabhagavatpūjyapādaśiṣyasya
śrīmacchaṃkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīrakamīmāṃsāsūtrabhāṣye caturthādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ murat caturthodhyāyaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ sampadyāvirbhāvaḥ svea śabdāt saṃpadyāvirbhāvādhikaraṇam kevaleaiva ātmaā āvirbhavati a dharmātareṇeti kutaḥ
svea rūpeṇābhiiṣpadyate iti svaśabdāt ayathā hi svaśabdea viśeṣaṇamaavaklṛptaṃ syāt au ātmīyābhiprāyaḥ svaśabdo bhaviṣyati a tasyāvacaīyatvāt yeaiva hi keacidrūpeṇābhiiṣpadyate tasyaiva ātmīyatvopapatteḥ
sveeti viśeṣaṇamaarthakaṃ syāt ātmavacaatāyāṃ tu arthavat kevaleaiva ātmarūpeṇābhiiṣpadyate a āgatukeāpararūpeṇāpīti kaḥ puarviśeṣaḥ pūrvāvasthāsu iha ca svarūpāapāyasāmye satītyata āha muktaḥ pratijñāāt
yotra abhiiṣpadyata ityuktaḥ sa sarvabadhaviirmuktaḥ śuddheaiva ātmaā avatiṣṭhate pūrvatra tuadho bhavatyapi roditīva viāśamevāpīto bhavatiiti ca avasthātrayakaluṣitea ātmaā ityayaṃ viśeṣaḥ kathaṃ
puaravagamyatemuktoyamidāīṃ bhavatīti pratijñāādityāha tathā hi etaṃ tveva te bhūyouvyākhyāsyāmi iti avasthātrayadoṣavihīam ātmāam vyākhyeyatvea pratijñāya aśarīraṃ vāva sataṃ a priyāpriye spṛśataḥ
iti ca upayasya svea rūpeṇābhiiṣpadyate sa uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ iti ca upasaṃharati tathā ākhyāyikopakramepi ya ātmāpahatapāpmā ityādi muktātmaviṣayameva pratijñāam phalatvaprasiddhirapi mokṣasya
badhaivṛttimātrāpekṣā a apūrvopajaāpekṣā yadapi abhiiṣpadyata ityutpattiparyāyatvam tadapi a apūrvāvasthāpekṣam yathā rogaivṛttau arogobhiiṣpadyata iti tadvat tasmādadoṣaḥ ātmā prakaraṇāt kathaṃ puarmukta ityucyate
yāvatā paraṃ jyotirupasaṃpadya iti kāryagocarameva eaṃ śrāvayati jyotiḥśabdasya bhautike jyotiṣi rūḍhatvāt a ca aativṛtto vikāraviṣayāt kaścimukto bhavitumarhati vikārasya ārtatvaprasiddheriti aiṣa
doṣaḥ yataḥ ātmaivātra jyotiḥśabdea āvedyate prakaraṇāt ya ātmāpahatapāpmā vijaro vimṛtyuḥ iti prakṛte parasmiātmai a akasmādbhautikaṃ jyotiḥ śakyaṃ grahītum prakṛtahāāprakṛtaprakriyāprasaṅgāt jyotiḥśabdastu
ātmayapi dṛśyate taddevā jyotiṣāṃ jyotiḥ iti prapañcitaṃ ca etat jyotirdarśaāt ityatra avibhāgea dṛṣṭatvāt avibhāgādhikaraṇam paraṃ jyotirupasaṃpadya svea rūpeṇābhiiṣpadyate yaḥ sa
kiṃ parasmādātmaaḥ pṛthageva bhavati uta avibhāgeaivāvatiṣṭhata iti vīkṣāyām sa tatra paryeti ityadhikaraṇādhikartavyairdeśāt jyotirupasaṃpadya iti ca kartṛkarmairdeśāt bhedeaivāvasthāamiti yasya matiḥ taṃ
vyutpādayati avibhakta eva pareṇa ātmaā muktovatiṣṭhate kutaḥ dṛṣṭatvāt tathā hi tattvamasi ahaṃ brahmāsmi yatra āyatpaśyati a tu taddvitīyamasti tatoyadvibhaktaṃ yatpaśyet
ityevamādīi vākyāyavibhāgeaiva paramātmāaṃ darśayati yathādarśaameva ca phalaṃ yuktam tatkratuyāyāt yathodakaṃ śuddhe śuddhamāsiktaṃ tādṛgeva bhavati evaṃ muervijāata ātmā bhavati gautama iti
ca evamādīi muktasvarūpairūpaṇaparāṇi vākyāyavibhāgameva darśayati adīsamudrādiidarśaāi ca bhedairdeśastu abhedepyupacaryate sa bhagavaḥ kasmipratiṣṭhita iti sve mahimi iti ātmaratirātmakrīḍaḥ iti ca evamādidarśaāt
brāhmeṇa jaimiirupayāsādibhyaḥ brāhmādhikaraṇam sthitametat svea rūpeṇa ityatra ātmamātrarūpeṇābhiiṣpadyate a āgatukeāpararūpeṇeti adhuā tu tadviśeṣabubhutsāyāmabhidhīyate svam asya rūpaṃ brāhmam apahatapāpmatvādisatyasaṃkalpatvāvasāaṃ tathā sarvajñatvaṃ
sarveśvaratvaṃ ca tea svarūpeṇābhiiṣpadyata iti jaimiirācāryo mayate kutaḥ upayāsādibhyastathātvāvagamāt tathā hi ya ātmāpahatapāpmā ityādiā satyakāmaḥ satyasaṃkalpaḥ ityevamatea upayāsea evamātmakatāmātmao bodhayati
tathā sa tatra paryeti jakṣatkrīḍaramamāṇaḥ iti aiśvaryarūpamāvedayati tasya sarveṣu lokeṣu kāmacāro bhavati iti ca sarvajñaḥ sarveśvaraḥ ityādivyapadeśāśca evamupapaā bhaviṣyatīti cititamātreṇa
tadātmakatvādityauḍulomiḥ yadyapi apahatapāpmatvādayo bhedeaiva dharmā irdiśyate tathāpi śabdavikalpajā eva ete pāpmādiivṛttimātraṃ hi tatra gamyate caitayameva tu asya ātmaaḥ svarūpamiti tamātreṇa
svarūpeṇa abhiiṣpattiryuktā tathā ca śrutiḥ evaṃ vā areyamātmāatarobāhyaḥ kṛtsaḥ prajñāaghaa eva ityevaṃjātīyakā augṛhītā bhaviṣyati satyakāmatvādayastu yadyapi vastusvarūpeṇaiva dharmā ucyate satyāḥ
kāmā asyeti tathāpi upādhisaṃbadhādhīatvātteṣāṃ a caitayavat svarūpatvasaṃbhavaḥ aekākāratvapratiṣedhāt pratiṣiddhaṃ hi brahmaṇoekākāratvam a sthāatopi parasyobhayaliṅgam ityatra ata eva ca jakṣaṇādisaṃkīrtaamapi duḥkhābhāvamātrābhiprāyaṃ
stutyartham ātmaratiḥ ityādivat a hi mukhyāyeva ratikrīḍāmithuāi ātmaimittāi śakyate varṇayitum dvitīyaviṣayatvātteṣām tasmāirastāśeṣaprapañcea prasaea avyapadeśyea bodhātmaā abhiiṣpadyata ityauḍulomirācāryo mayate evam apy

eva tu tacchruteḥ saṃkalpādhikaraṇam hārdavidyāyāṃ śrūyate sa yadi pitṛlokakāmo bhavati saṃkalpād evāsya pitaraḥ samuttiṣṭhati ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kiṃ saṃkalpa eva
kevalaḥ pitrādisamutthāe hetuḥ uta imittātarasahita iti tatra saty api saṃkalpād eva iti śravaṇe lokavat imittātarāpekṣatā yuktā yathā loke asmadādīāṃ saṃkalpāt
gamaādibhyaś ca hetubhyaḥ pitrādisaṃpattir bhavati evaṃ muktasyāpi syāt evaṃ dṛṣṭaviparītaṃ a kalpitaṃ bhaviṣyati saṃkalpād eva iti tu rājña iva saṃkalpitārthasiddhikarīṃ
sādhaātarasāmagrīṃ sulabhām apekṣya yokṣyate a ca saṃkalpamātrasamutthāāḥ pitrādayaḥ maorathavijṛmbhitavat cañcalatvāt puṣkalaṃ bhogaṃ samarpayituṃ paryāptāḥ syur iti evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ saṃkalpād
eva tu kevalāt pitrādisamutthāam iti kutaḥ tacchruteḥ saṃkalpād evāsya pitaraḥ samuttiṣṭhati ityādikā hi śrutir imittātarāpekṣāyāṃ pīḍyeta imittātaram api tu yadi
saṃkalpāuvidhāyy eva syāt bhavatu a tu prayatātarasaṃpādyaṃ imittātaram iṣyate prāk saṃpatteḥ vadhyasaṃkalpatvaprasaṅgāt a ca śrutyavagamye rthe lokavad iti sāmāyato dṛṣṭaṃ
kramate saṃkalpabalād eva ca eṣāṃ yāvat prayojaaṃ sthairyopapattiḥ prākṛtasaṃkalpavilakṣaṇatvā muktasaṃkalpasya ata eva cāayādhipatiḥ ata eva ca avadhyasaṃkalpatvāt aayādhipatir vidvā bhavati
āsyāyo dhipatir bhavatīty arthaḥ a hi prākṛto pi saṃkalpaya ayasvāmikatvam ātmaaḥ satyāṃ gatau saṃkalpayati śrutiś caitad darśayati atha ya ihātmāam
auvidya vrajaty etāṃś ca satyā kāmāṃs teṣāṃ sarveṣu lokeṣu kāmacāro bhavati iti abhāvaṃ bādarir āha hy evam abhāvādhikaraṇam saṃkalpād evāsya
pitaraḥ samuttiṣṭhati ity ataḥ śruteḥ maas tāvat saṃkalpasādhaaṃ siddham śarīredriyāṇi puaḥ prāptaiśvaryasya viduṣaḥ sati a vā sati iti samīkṣyate tatra
bādaris tāvad ācāryaḥ śarīrasyedriyāṇāṃ ca abhāvaṃ mahīyamāasya viduṣo mayate kasmāt evaṃ hi āha āmāyaḥ maasaitā kāmā paśya ramate ya ete
brahmaloke iti yadi maasā śarīredriyaiś ca vihareta maaseti viśeṣaṇaṃ a syāt tasmād abhāvaḥ śarīredriyāṇāṃ mokṣe bhāvaṃ jaimiir vikalpāmaaāt jaimiis tv
ācāryaḥ maovat śarīrasyāpi sedriyasya bhāvaṃ muktaṃ prati mayate yataḥ sa ekadhā bhavati tridhā bhavati ityādiā aekadhābhāvavikalpam āmaati a hi aekavidhatā
viā śarīrabhedea āñjasī syāt yady api irguṇāyāṃ bhūmavidyāyām ayam aekadhābhāvavikalpaḥ paṭhyate tathāpi vidyamāam evedaṃ saguṇāvasthāyām aiśvaryaṃ bhūmavidyāstutaye saṃkīrtyata ity ataḥ
saguṇavidyāphalabhāvea upatiṣṭhata iti ucyate dvādaśāhavad ubhayavidhaṃ bādarāyaṇo taḥ bādarāyaṇaḥ puar ācāryaḥ ata eva ubhayaliṅgaśrutidarśaāt ubhayavidhatvaṃ sādhu mayate yadā saśarīratāṃ saṃkalpayati
tadā saśarīro bhavati yadā tu aśarīratāṃ tadā aśarīra iti satyasaṃkalpatvāt saṃkalpavaicitryāc ca dvādaśāhavat yathā dvādaśāhaḥ satram ahīaś ca bhavati ubhayaliṅgaśrutidarśaāt
evamidam apīti tavabhāve sadhyavad upapatteḥ yadā taoḥ sedriyasya śarīrasya abhāvaḥ tadā yathā saṃdhye sthāe śarīredriyaviṣayeṣv avidyamāeṣv api upalabdhimātrā eva pitrādikāmā

evaṃ muktasyāpy upapadyate pradīpavad āveśas tathā hi darśayati pradīpādhikaraṇam bhāvaṃ jaimiirvikalpāmaaāt ity atra saśarīratvaṃ muktasyoktam tatra tridhābhāvādiṣu aekaśarīrasarge kiṃ irātmakāi
śarīrāṇi dāruyatravat sṛjyate kiṃ vā sātmakāy asmadādiśarīravat iti bhavati vīkṣā tatra ca ātmamaasoḥ bhedāupapatteḥ ekea śarīreṇa yogāt itarāṇi śarīrāṇi irātmakāi
ity evaṃ prāpte pratipadyate pradīpavad āveśa iti yathā pradīpa ekaḥ aekapradīpabhāvamāpadyate vikāraśaktiyogāt evamekopi sa vidvā aiśvaryayogādaekabhāvamāpadya sarvāṇi śarīrāṇyāviśati kutaḥ tathā
hi darśayati śāstramekasyāekabhāvam sa ekadhā bhavati tridhā bhavati pañcadhā saptadhā avadhā ityādi aitaddāruyatropamābhyupagamevakalpate āpi jīvātarāveśe a ca irātmakāāṃ śarīrāṇāṃ pravṛttiḥ
saṃbhavati yattu ātmamaasorbhedāupapatteḥ aekaśarīrayogāsaṃbhava iti aiṣa doṣaḥ ekamaouvartīi samaaskāy evāparāṇi śarīrāṇi satyasaṃkalpatvāt srakṣyati sṛṣṭeṣu ca teṣu upādhibhedāt ātmao pi bhedeādhiṣṭhātṛtvaṃ
yokṣyate eṣaiva ca yogaśāstreṣu yogiām aekaśarīrayogaprakriyā kathaṃ puaḥ muktasya aekaśarīrāveśādilakṣaṇam aiśvaryam abhyupagamyate yāvatā tat kea kaṃ vijāīyāt a tu taddvitīyam
asti tato yad vibhaktaṃ yad vijāīyāt salila eko draṣṭādvaito bhavati iti ca evaṃjātīyakā śrutiḥ viśeṣavijñāaṃ vārayati ity ata uttaraṃ paṭhati
svāpyayasampattyorayatarāpekṣamāviṣkṛtaṃ hi svāpyayaḥ suṣuptam svamapīto bhavati tasmādeaṃ svapitītyācakṣate iti śruteḥ saṃpattiḥ kaivalyam brahmaiva sabrahmāpyeti iti śruteḥ tayorayatarāmavasthāmapekṣya etat viśeṣasaṃjñābhāvavacaam kvacit
suṣuptāvasthāmapekṣyocyate kvacitkaivalyāvasthām kathamavagamyate yatastatraiva etadadhikāravaśāt āviṣkṛtam etebhyo bhūtebhyaḥ samutthāya tāyevāu viaśyati a pretya saṃjñāstīti yatra tvasya sarvamātmaivābhūt yatra supto a
kaṃcaa kāmaṃ kāmayate a kaṃcaa svapaṃ paśyati ityādiśrutibhyaḥ saguṇavidyāvipākasthāaṃ tu etat svargādivat avasthātaram yatraitadaiśvaryamupavarṇyate tasmādadoṣaḥ jagadvyāpāravarjaṃ prakaraṇādasaṃihitatvācca jagadvyāpārādhikaraṇam ye saguṇabrahmopāsaāt
sahaiva maasā īśvarasāyujyaṃ vrajati kiṃ teṣāṃ iravagrahamaiśvaryaṃ bhavati āhosvitsāvagrahamiti saṃśayaḥ kiṃ tāvatprāptam iraṅkuśameva eṣāmaiśvaryaṃ bhavitumarhati āpoti svārājyam sarvesmai devā balimāvahati
teṣāṃ sarveṣu lokeṣu kāmacāro bhavati ityādiśrutibhya iti evaṃ prāpte paṭhati jagadvyāpāravarjamiti jagadutpattyādivyāpāraṃ varjayitvā ayat aṇimādyātmakamaiśvaryaṃ muktāāṃ bhavitumarhati jagadvyāpārastu ityasiddhasyaiva īśvarasya
kutaḥ tasya tatra prakṛtatvāt asaṃihitatvāccetareṣām para eva hi īśvaro jagadvyapāredhikṛtaḥ tameva prakṛtya utpattyādyupadeśāt ityaśabdaibadhaatvācca tadaveṣaṇavijijñāsaapūrvakaṃ tu itareṣāmaṇimādyaiśvaryaṃ śrūyate teāsaṃihitāste jagadvyāpāre
samaaskatvādeva ca eteṣāmaaikamatye kasyacitsthityabhiprāyaḥ kasyacitsaṃhārābhiprāya ityevaṃ virodhopi kadācitsyāt atha kasyacit saṃkalpamau ayasya saṃkalpa ityavirodhaḥ samarthyeta tataḥ parameśvarākūtatatratvamevetareṣāmiti vyavatiṣṭhate pratyakṣopadeśāditi ceādhikārikamaṇḍalasthokteḥ
atha yaduktam āpoti svārājyam ityādipratyakṣopadeśāt iravagrahamaiśvaryaṃ viduṣāṃ yāyyamiti tatparihartavyam atrocyate āyaṃ doṣaḥ ādhikārikamaṇḍalasthokteḥ ādhikāriko yaḥ savitṛmaṇḍalādiṣu viśeṣāyataeṣvavasthitaḥ para īśvaraḥ tadāyattaiva
iyaṃ svārājyaprāptirucyate yatkāraṇam aataram āpoti maasaspatim ityāha yo hi sarvamaasāṃ patiḥ pūrvasiddha īśvaraḥ taṃ prāpotītyetaduktaṃ bhavati tadausāreṇaiva ca aataram vākpatiścakṣuṣpatiḥ
śrotrapatirvijñāapatiḥ ca bhavati ityāha evamayatrāpi yathāsaṃbhavaṃ ityasiddheśvarāyattameva itareṣāmaiśvaryaṃ yojayitavyam vikārāvarti ca tathā hi sthitimāha vikārāvartyapi ca ityamuktaṃ pārameśvaraṃ rūpam a
kevalaṃ vikāramātragocaraṃ savitṛmaṇḍalādyadhiṣṭhāam tathā hi asya dvirūpāṃ sthitimāha āmāyaḥ tāvāasya mahimā tato jyāyāśca puruṣaḥ pādosya sarvā bhūtāi tripādasyāmṛtaṃ divi ityevamādiḥ
a ca tat irvikārarūpam itarālambaāḥ prāpuvatīti śakyaṃ vaktum atatkratutvātteṣām ataśca yathaiva dvirūpe parameśvare irguṇaṃ rūpamaavāpya saguṇa evāvatiṣṭhate evaṃ saguṇepi iravagrahamaiśvaryamaavāpya
sāvagraha evāvatiṣṭhata iti draṣṭavyam darśayataścaivaṃ pratyakṣāumāe darśayataśca vikārāvartitvaṃ parasya jyotiṣaḥ śrutismṛtī a tatra sūryo bhāti a cadratārakaṃ emā vidyuto bhāti
kutoyamagiḥ iti a tadbhāsayate sūryo a śaśāṅko a pāvakaḥ iti ca tadevaṃ vikārāvartitvaṃ parasya jyotiṣaḥ prasiddhamityabhiprāyaḥ bhogamātrasāmyaliṅgāc ca itaś ca
a iraṅkuśaṃ vikārālambaāām aiśvaryam yasmāt bhogamātram eva eṣām aādisiddheeśvareṇa samāam iti śrūyate tam āhāpo vai khalu mīyate lokosau iti sa
yathaitāṃ devatāṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāy avaty evaṃ haivaṃvidaṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāy avati teo etasyai devatāyai sāyujyaṃ salokatāṃ jayati ityādibhedavyapadeśaliṅgebhyaḥ au evaṃ sati
sātiśayatvād atavattvam aiśvaryasya syāt tataś ca eṣām āvṛttiḥ prasajyeta ity ataḥ uttaraṃ bhagavā bādarāyaṇa ācāryaḥ paṭhati aāvṛttiḥ śabdād aāvṛttiḥ śabdāt
āḍīraśmisamavitea arcirādiparvaṇā devayāea pathā ye brahmalokaṃ śāstroktaviśeṣaṇaṃ gacchati yasmiaraś ca ha vai ṇyaścārṇavau brahmaloke tṛtīyasyām ito divi yasmiairaṃ madīyaṃ saraḥ
yasmi aśvatthaḥ somasavaaḥ yasmi aparājitā pūrbrahmaṇaḥ yasmiṃś ca prabhuvimitaṃ hiraṇmayaṃ veśma yaścāekadhā matrārthavādādipradeśeṣu prapañcyate te taṃ prāpya a cadralokād iva
bhuktabhogā āvartate kutaḥ tayordhvam āya amṛtatvam eti teṣāṃ a puar āvṛttiḥ etea pratipadyamāā imaṃ māavam āvartaṃ āvartate brahmalokam abhisaṃpadyate a
ca puar āvartate ityādiśabdebhyaḥ atavattvepi tu aiśvaryasya yathā aāvṛttiḥ tathā varṇitam kāryātyaye tad adhyakṣeṇa sahātaḥ param ity atra samyagdarśaavidhvastatamasāṃ tu
ityasiddhairvāṇaparāyaṇāāṃ siddhaiva aāvṛttiḥ tadāśrayaṇeaiva hi saguṇaśaraṇāām apy aāvṛttisiddhir iti aāvṛttiḥ śabdād aāvṛttiḥ śabdāt iti sūtrābhyāsaḥ śāstraparisamāptiṃ dyotayati iti śrīmatparamahaṃsaparivrājakācāryāsya śrīgovidabhagavatpūjyapādaśiṣyasya
śrīmacchaṃkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau śārīrakamīmāṃsāsūtrabhāṣye caturthādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ iti śrīmacchārīrakamīmāṃsāsūtrabhāṣyaṃ saṃpūrṇam murat
